NK_1.1–1.3	praṇamya hetum īśvaram munim kaṇādam anu atas padārtha dharma saṅgrahaḥ pravakṣyate mahā udayaḥ anādinidhanam devam jagat kāraṇam īśvaram prapadye satya saṅkalpam nitya vijñāna vigraham dhyāna eka tāna manasaḥ vigata pracārāḥ paśyanti yam kam api nirmalam advitīyam jñāna ātmane vighaṭita akhila bandhanāya tasmai namaḥ bhagavate puruṣottamāya 
NK_2.1	 śāstra ārambhe abhimatām devatām śāstrasya praṇetāram gurun ca ślokasya pūrva ardhena namasyati praṇamya iti karma ārambhe hi devatāḥ guravaḥ ca namaskriyante iti śiṣṭa ācāraḥ ayam phalam ca namaskārasya vighna upaśamaḥ na tāvat ayam aphalaḥ prekṣāvadbhiḥ anuṣṭhīyamāna tvāt anyaphalaḥ api na karma ārambhe niyamena anuṣṭīyeta avighnena prāripsita parisamāpteḥ tadānīm apekṣita tvāt phala antarasya anabhisaṃhita tvāt ca 
NK_3.1	 nanu kim namaskārāt eva vighna upaśamaḥ kim uta anyasmāt api bhavati na tāvat namaskārāt eva iti asti niyamaḥ asati api namaskāre nyāya mī māṃsā bhāṣyayoḥ parisamāpta tvāt yadi ca anyasmāt api tadā bhavati namaskārasya niyamena upādānam nirupapattikam atra ucyate namaskārāt eva vighna upaśamaḥ karma ārambhe sadbhiḥ niyamena tasya upādānāt na ca nyāya mīmāṃsā bhāṣya kārābhyām na kṛtaḥ namaskāraḥ kintu tatra anupanibaddhaḥ katham eṣā pratītiḥ iti ced kartuḥ śiṣṭa tayā eva astu vā tāvat aparaḥ prekṣāvān mleccha upi tāvat guru ārambhe karmaṇi na pravartate yāvat iṣṭām devatām na namasyati yat imau paramāstikau pakṣila śabara svāmīnau na anutiṣṭate iti asambhāvanam idam 
NK_4.1^1	 akṣara arthaḥ vyākriyate praṇamya iti prakarṣa vācinā apra aśabdena bhakti śraddhā atiśaya pūrvakam namaskāram ācaṣṭe sa hi dharma utpādakaḥ tirayati antarāya bījam na aparaḥ atas eva kṛta namaskārasya api kādambaryī ādeḥ aparisamāptiḥ viśiṣṭa namaskāra abhāvāt tad avaiśiṣti asya ca kāryya gamya tvāt atra eva ca namaskāraḥ kriyamāṇaḥ api kariṣyamāṇa padārtha dharma saṅgraha pravacana apekṣayā pūrva kāla bhāvi iti ktvā apratyayena abhidhīyate tad eka vākyatām āpādayitum na tu asya pūrva kālatā mātram anūdyate anuvāde vā prayojana abhāvāt hetum iti nirviśeṣaṇena hetu padena sarva utpattimatām nimittam pratijānīte īśvaram iti viśiṣṭa devatāyāḥ abhidhānam loke tad viṣaya tvena eva asya padasya prasiddheḥ loka prasiddha padārtha upasaṅgraha paratvāt ca asya śāstrasya munim iti śuddha ātma jñāna pradīpa kṣapita tamasam ati ugra tapasam sākṣāt aśeṣa tattva avabodha yuktam jīvanmuktam puruṣa viśeṣam āha ittham bhūtaḥ eva arthe muni śabdasya loke prayoga darśanāt 
NK_4.1^2	 kaṇādam iti tasya kāpotīm vṛttim anutiṣṭhataḥ rathyā nipatitān= taṇḍula kaṇān ādāya adāya ādāya pratyaham kṛtasya āhārasya āhāra nimittā sañjñā atas eva niravakāśaḥ kaṇān vā bhakṣyitvā iti upālambhaḥ tatra bhavatām idam hi tasya nāma iti tad śabda saṅkīrtanam kṛtam praśasta devena na tu iyam tad upanibandha vaiśiṣṭya khyāpanāya yuktiḥ abhihitā tad upanibandha vaiśiṣṭyasya manu ādi vākya vat mahā jana parigrahāt eva pratīteḥ na ca asya kaṇādaśāstra vaiṣṭya khyāpanena kiścid prayojanam asti tāvatā tad pūrvakasya granthasya vaiśiṣṭya siddhiḥ iti ced na avaśyam tat pūrvaka tvena sva granthasya vaiśiṣṭya siddhiḥ kartṛ doṣeṇā ayathārthasya api nibandhasya sambhāvana āspada tvāt sambhāvita prāmāṇye praśasta deve puruṣa doṣāṇām asambhavaḥ iti ced evam tarhi yathā kaṇāda darśinām tad śiṣyāṇām puruṣa pratyayāt eva tathā tva niścayāt tad upanibandhe pravṛttiḥ apareṣān ca puruṣa antara saṃvādāt evam praśasta deva kṛta upanibandhe api tad śiṣyāṇām apareṣān ca pravṛttiḥ bhaviṣyati iti na arthaḥ tad pūrvaka tva khyāpanena 
NK_5.1	 kimartham tarhi kaṇā darṣeḥ namaskāraḥ vighna upaśamāya iti uktam yathā īśvarasya namaskāraḥ saḥ api hi na tad pūrvaka tva khyāpanāya vyabhicārāt yā yasya iṣṭā devatā sa tām praṇamya sarva karmāṇi prastauti na karmaṇām tad pūrvaka tvena bhakti śraddhā mātra nibandhana tvāt namaskārasya yathā mīmāṃsā vārttika kṛtā namaskṛtaḥ soma arddha dharaḥ na ca tad pūrvikā mīmāṃsā iti asti pravādaḥ anu iti īśvara praṇāmāt anantara tām kaṇāda praṇāmasya parāmṛśati atas īśvaram ādau praṇamya iti īśvara praṇāmasya parāmarśaḥ atas īśvara praṇāmāt anu paścāt kaṇādam praṇamya iti arthaḥ 
NK_6.1^1	 sambandha prayojanayoḥ anabhidhāne śrotā na pravarttate prayojana adhigati pūrvaka tvāt sarva prekṣā vat pravṛtteḥ tasya apravṛttau ca śāstram kṛtam api na kṛtam syāt anupādeya tvāt atas śāstra ārambham samādadhānaḥ prekṣāvat pravṛtti aṅgam tasya sambandham prayojanan ca ādau ślokasya uttara arddhena kathayati padārtha dharma ityādi padārthāḥ dravya ādayaḥ ṣaṭ teṣām dharmāḥ sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa svabhāvāḥ saṅgṛhyante saṅkṣepeṇa abhidhīyante anena iti padārtha dharma saṅgrahaḥ pravakṣyate iti padārtha dharmāṇām saṅkṣepeṇa abhidhāyakaḥ ayam granthaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ mayā vakṣyate iti granthakarttuḥ pratijñā 
NK_6.1^2–7.1	 granthasya ca iyam prakṛṣṭa tā yat anyatra granthe vistareṇa itas tatas abhihitānām iha ekatra tāvatām eva padārtha dharmāṇām granthe saṅkṣepeṇa kathanam etat artham eva ca asya ārambhaḥ satsu api upanibandha antareṣu padārtha dharmāṇām saṅgrahaḥ padārtha dharma pratīti hetuḥ padārtha dharma pratītiḥ ca na puruṣa arthaḥ sukha duḥkha āpti hānyoḥ puruṣa prayojana tvāt tasmāt ayam apuruṣa artha hetu tvāt anupādeyaḥ eva iti āśaṅkya tasya puruṣa artha phala tām pratipādayitum uktam mahā udayaḥ iti mahān udayaḥ mahat phalam apavarga lakṣaṇam yasmāt saṅgrahāt asau mahā udayaḥ saṅgrahaḥ etena saṅgrahasya padārtha dharmaiḥ saha vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ tad pratipattyā ca mahā udayena saha sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sambandhaḥ darśitaḥ nanu bhoḥ kaḥ eṣa mahā udayaḥ nāma sa vāsanā kleṣa samucchedaḥ jñāna uparamaḥ iti eke tathā ca paṭhanti na pretya sañjñā asti iti tat ayuktam sarvatas priyatamasya ātmanaḥ samucchedāya prekṣāvat pravṛtti anupapatteḥ bandha viccheda paryyāyasya mukti śabdasya ātad artha tvāt ca 
NK_8.1	 nikhila vāsanā ucchede vigata vividha viṣaya ākāra upaplava viśuddha jñāna utpādaḥ mahā udayaḥ iti apare tat api ayuktam kāraṇa abhāvāt eva tad anupapatteḥ bhāvanā pracayaḥ hi tasya kāraṇam iṣyate sa ca sthira eka āśraya abhāvāt viśeṣa anādhāyakaḥ pratikṣaṇam apūrvavat upajāyamānaḥ niranvaya vināśī gagana laṅghana abhyāsa vadanāsādita prakarṣaḥ na sphuṭa ābha jñāna jananāya prabhavati iti anupapattiḥ eva tasya sa mala cit takṣaṇānām svābhāvikyāḥ sadṛśa ārambhaṇa śakteḥ asadṛśa ārambham pratyaśakteḥ ca akasmāt anucchedāt kiñca pūrve kṣaṇāḥ svarasa parinirvāṇāḥ ayam apūrvaḥ jātaḥ santānaḥ ca ekaḥ na vidyate bandha mokṣau ca eka adhikaraṇau na viṣaya bhedena vartete tat kasya iyam muktiḥ yaḥ etad artham prayatate yaḥ prāpya ca nivṛttaḥ bhavati 
NK_9.1	 prakṛti puruṣa viveka darśanāt uparatāyām prakṛtau puruṣasya sva rūpeṇa avasthānam mahā udayaḥ iti anye tat na pravṛtti svabhāvāyāḥ prakṛteḥ audāsīnya ayogāt puruṣa artha nibandhanā tasyāḥ pravṛttiḥ viveka khyātiḥ ca puruṣa arthaḥ tasyām san jātāyām sā nivartate kṛta kārya tvāt iti ced na tasyāḥ acetanāyāḥ vimṛśya kāritva abhāvāt yathā iyam kṛte api śabda ādi upalambhe punar tad artham pravartate tathā viveka khyātau kṛtāyām api punar tad artham pravarttiṣyate svabhāvasya anapeta tvāt dṛṣṭā mayā iti upekṣakaḥ ekaḥ dṛṣṭā aham iti uparamati anyā sati saṃyoge api tayoḥ prayojanam na asti sargasya 
NK_10.1–10.2	 nitya niratiśaya sukha abhivyaktiḥ muktiḥ iti apare tat api asāram agre nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt tasmāt ahita nivṛttiḥ ātyantikī mahā udayaḥ iti yuktam tasyāḥ sadbhāve kim pramāṇam duḥkha santatiḥ dharmiṇī atyantam ucchidyate santati tvāt pradīpa santati vat iti tārkkikāḥ tat ayuktam pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādi santānena vyabhicārāt aśarīram vāva santam priya apriye na spṛśataḥ ityādayaḥ vedāntāḥ pramāṇam iti tu vayam bhūta arthānām eṣām aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na pratyakṣeṇa anaikāntika tvāt atha matam bhūta artha pratipādakam vacanam anuvādakam syāt tatas ca apramāṇa tvam pramāṇa antara sāpekṣa tvāt pramāyām sādhakatama tva abhāvāt iti na siddhārtha pratipādaka tvam anuvādaka tvam pratyakṣasya api anuvādakatva prasaṅgāt kintu adhigata artha adhigantṛ tvam īdṛśaḥ ca vedāntānām arthaḥ yat ayam bhūtaḥ api pratyakṣa ādeḥ pramāṇa antarasya na viṣayaḥ kutas teṣām anuvādaka tā kutas ca sa apekṣa tvam smṛteḥ iva tebhyaḥ pūrva adhigama saṃsparśena artha pratīteḥ abhāvāt atas eva puruṣa vākyam api pramāṇam 
NK_11.1	 na hi tat api vaktṛ prāmāṇya utthāpanena artham pratipādayati kintu anapekṣita tad vyāpāram svayam eva utpatti mātram prati tad apekṣaṇāt svābhāvikī hi padānām padārtha para tā svābhāvikī ca padārthānām ākāṅkṣa ayogya tā sannidhimatām itaretara anvaya yogya tā tena yathā vede pramāṇa antara anapekṣaḥ śabdaḥ śabda sāmarthyāt eva artha pratyayaḥ evam loke api yaḥ eva laukikā te eva vaidikāḥ iti nyāyena ubhayatra api śabda śakteḥ aviśeṣāt vaktṛ prāmāṇya anusaraṇan tu svarūpa viparyāsa hetoḥ doṣasya abhāva avagamāya pratyakṣaḥ iva sva kāraṇa śuddheḥ anugamaḥ viparyāsa śaṅkā nirāsa arthaḥ iti eṣā diś vistaraḥ tu advaya siddhau draṣṭavyaḥ 
NK_12.1^1	 nanu kārye arthe śabdasya prāmāṇyam na svarūpe vṛddha vyavahāreṣu anvaya vyatirekābhyām kāryya anviteṣu padārtheṣu padānām śakti avagamāt atas vedāntānām na bhūta artha paratā iti ced vārtam idam svarūpa parasya api vākyasya loke prayoga darśanāt yathā pariṇāma surasam āmram pariṇati virasan ca panasam iti atra api pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ upadeśaḥ evam hi vākya arthaḥ pariṇama surasam āmram bhakṣaya pariṇati virasam panasam mā bhakṣaya iti na vaiyarthyāt surasatva pratītya eva svayam abhilāṣāt puruṣaḥ pravarttate virasa tva pratītya eva dveṣāt nivarttate kā tatra vastu sāmarthya bhāvinī upadeśa apekṣā aprāpte hi śāstram arthavat bhavati 
NK_12.1^2	 atha pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ abhisandhānena asya vākyasya prayogāt tādarthyam iti ced asti etasya pravṛtti nivṛtti artha tā kintu janaka tvāt na tu pratipādaka tvena pratipādaka tvam tu vākyasya bhūta artha viṣayam eva pratipādaka tvena ca pramāṇānām pramāṇyam na janakatvena tasmāt bhūta artha viṣayam eva vākyasya pramāṇyam yadi tu pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ abhisandhānena vākya prayogāt tayoḥ apratīyamānayoḥ api śabda artha tā āmra bhakṣaṇa uttara kālīnā tṛptiḥ dhātu sāmyan ca vākya arthau ayātām pratyakṣasya ca kāñcid artha kriyām abhisandhāya upalipsite viṣaye pravṛttasya artha kriyā api prameyā syāt janakatvena pravṛtti nivṛtti para tvam vedāntānām api vidyate tebhyaḥ svarūpa pratītau dhyāna abhyāsa ādi pravṛttasya vigata vividha vikalpa viśada ātma jñāna udaye sati apavargasya bhāvāt 
NK_12.1^3	 na ca idam āvaśyakam yat pravṛtti nivṛtti avadhikaḥ pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ iti tayoḥ puruṣa icchā pratibaddhayoḥ anutpāde api vastu pariccheda mātreṇa apekṣā buddheḥ paryyavasānāt na ca kāryyā anvitaḥ eva arthe padānām śaktiḥ ananvite api vyutpatti darśanāt yathā iha prabhinnakam alodare madhūni madhukaraḥ pibati iti varttamāna upadeśe prasiddha itara padārthaḥ a prasiddha madhukara padārthaḥ tu yam madhu pāna karttāram paśyati tam madhukara śabda vācya tvena pratyeti atra api asti pāramparyeṇa kārya anvayaḥ vākya prayoktuḥ pūrvam vṛddha vyavahārāt kāryyāṃnvitaḥ eva arthe madhukara padasya vyutpatti bhāvāt iti ced na aniścayāt vākya prayoktuḥ kim vṛddha vyavahārāt kāryya anvite arthe vyutpattiḥ abhūt kim uta prasiddha pada sā mānādhikaraṇyena upadeśāt vā svarūpe arthaḥ iti niścayaḥ na asti idam prathama tāyāḥ abhāvāt 
NK_12.1^4	 kiñca vākya prayoktuḥ anvate vyutpattiḥ śrotuḥ ca ananvite anya vyutpattyā ca anyaḥ na śabda artham pratyeti tatas ca madhukara śabdasya ananvita artha tvam anvita artha tvan ca puruṣa bhedena iti arddha vaiśaśa samāpatitam kriyā kāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ padārthānām anyonya sambandhaḥ na ākhyāta pada rahiteṣu siddhārtheṣu vedānta vākyeṣu bhavitum arhati iti ced na tāvat atra sarvatra kriyāyāḥ abhāvaḥ yatra tu na asti tatra api saṃsarga para tayā padaiḥ abhihitānām padārthanām eva yogyatā sannidhimatām anyonya ākāṅkṣā nibandhanaḥ sambandhaḥ tatha ca akāñcyām idānīm tribhuvana tilakaḥ rājāa iti atra api vākyarthaḥ gamyate eva athavā tatra śruta prayujyamānā asti bhavati kriyā nibandhanaḥ bhaviṣyati iti yat kiñcid etat 
NK_13.1–13.3	 dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām ṣaṇṇām padārthānām sādharmyam vaidharmya tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa hetuḥ prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ atra padārtha dharma pratijñānāt eva padārthānām api saṅgrahaḥ labhyate svātantryeṇa dharmāṇām saṅgraha abhāvāt nanu padārtha dharmāṇām saṅgraha paraḥ granthaḥ mahā udaya hetuḥ iti na upapadyate śabdasya artha pratipādanam antareṇa kāryya antara abhāvāt iti āśaṅkya padārtha dharma pratīti hetoḥ saṅgrahasya pāramparyyeṇa mahā udaya hetu tvam pratipādayan āha dravya guṇa ityādi 
NK_13.4^1	 yasya vastunaḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ yat svarūpaḥ tat tasya tattvam sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ sādharmyam asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ vaidharmya vaidharmye eva tattvam sādharmya vaidharmya tattvam tasya jñānam niḥśreyasa hetuḥ viṣaya sambhoga jam sukham tāvat kṣaṇa vināśi duḥkha bahulam svarga ādi pada prāpyam api sa prakṣayam sā atiśayañca tathā ca kasyacid svarga mātram aparasya svarga rājyam atas tat api satatam pracyuti śaṅkyā para samutkarṣa upatāpāt ca duḥkha krāntam na niścitam śreyaḥ ātyantikī duḥkha nivṛttiḥ asahya saṃvedana nikhila duḥkha uparama rūpa tvāt apunarāvṛtteḥ ca niścitam śreyaḥ tasya kāraṇam dravya ādi svarūpa jñānam 
NK_13.4^2	 etena tat pratyuktam yat uktam maṇḍanena viśeṣa guṇa nivṛtti lakṣaṇā mukti russhet apakṣāt na bhidyate iti viśeṣa guṇa ucchede hi satya ātmanaḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthānam na ucchedaḥ nitya tvāt na ca ayam apuruṣa arthaḥ samasta duḥkha uparamasya parama puruṣa artha tvāt samasta sukha abhāvāt apuruṣa artha tvam api asti iti ced na sukhasya api kṣayitayā bahula pratyanīka tayā ca sādhana prārthanā śata parikliṣṭa tayā ca sarvadā duḥkha krāntasya viṣa sampṛktasya iva madhunaḥ duḥkha pakṣe nikṣepāt keṣam sādharmya vaidharmya tattava parījñānam apavarga kāraṇam iti apekṣāyām dravya ādīnām iti sambandhaḥ 
NK_14.1	 dravyāṇi ca guṇāḥ ca sāmānye ca viśeṣāḥ ca samavāyaḥ ca iti vibhāga vacana anusārenā vigrahaḥ uddeśasya vibhāga vacanena samāna viṣaya tvāt ādau dravyasya uddeśaḥ sarva śraya tvena prādhānyāt guṇa an āñca karma apekṣayā bhūyas tvāt dravya anantaram abhidhānam niyamena guṇa anuvidhāyi tvāt karmaṇām guṇa anantaram uddeśaḥ karma anvita tvāt sāmānyasya karma anantaram abhidhānam pañca padārtha vṛtteḥ samavāyasya sarva ayasya sarva śeṣaṇa abhidhāne prāpte arthāt viśeṣāṇām madhye kathanam iti abhāvasya pṛthak anupadeśaḥ bhāva pāratantryāt na tu abhāvāt dravyāṇām iti sambandhe ṣaṣṭhī atra api sādharmya ādi jñānasya niḥśreyasa hetu tve kathite dravya ādi jñānasya api kathitam sadharmya vaidharmyayoḥ svātantryeṇa jñāna abhāvāt 
NK_15.1–15.2	 tat ca īśvara codanā abhivyaktāt dharmāt eva nanu yadi tattva jñānam niḥśreyasa hetuḥ tarhi dharmaḥ na kāraṇam tatas ca sūtra viṛdhaḥ yatas abhyudaya niḥśreyasa siddhiḥ sa dharmaḥ iti atas āha tat ca īśvara codanā abhivyaktāt dharmāt eva iti tat niḥśreyasam dharmāt eva bhavati dravya ādi tattva jñānam tu tasya kāraṇa tvena niḥśreyasa sādhanam iti abhiprāyaḥ tattvataḥ nirjñāteṣu bāhya ādhyātmikeṣu viṣayeṣu doṣa darśanāt viraktasya samīha anivṛttau= ātma jñasya tad arthāni karmāṇi akurvvataḥ tad parityāga sādhanāni ca śruti smṛti uditāni a saṅkalpita phalāni upādadānasya ātma jñānam abhyasyataḥ prakṛṣṭa vinivarttaka dharma upacaye sati paripakva ātma jñānasya ātyantika śarīra ādi viyogasya bhāvāt dṛṣṭaḥ hi viṣayāṇām ahikaṇṭaka ādīnām parityāgaḥ viśeṣa doṣa darśana pūrvaka abhisandhi kṛta nivarttaka ātma viśeṣa guṇāt prayatnāt tena śarīra ādīnām ātyantikaḥ parityāgaḥ api tad doṣa darśana pūrvaka abhisandhi kṛta nivarttaka ātma viśeṣa guṇa nimittaḥ vijñātaḥ iti mokṣa adhikāre vakṣyāmaḥ 
NK_16.1	 adharmaḥ api kevalaḥ na niḥśreyasam karoti yāvat īśvara icchayā na anugṛhyate tena idam uktam īśvara codanā abhivyaktāt dharmāt eva iti codyante preryyante sva kāryyaṣu pravartti ante anayā bhāvāḥ iti codanāīśvara codanāḥ īśvara icchā viśeṣeṇaḥ abhivyaktiḥ kāryya ārambham pratyābhimukhyam īśvara codanayā abhivyaktāt īśvara codana abhivyaktāt īśvara icchā viśeṣeṇa kāryya ārambha abhimukhīkṛtāt dharmāt eva tat niḥśreyasam bhavati iti vākya yojanā tat ca iti cakāraḥ dravya ādi sādharmya jñānena saha dharmasya niḥśreyasa hetu tvam samuccinoti 
NK_17.1–17.3	 atha ke dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ kiñca teṣām sādharmyam vaidharmyañca iti tatra dravyāṇi pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu ākāśa kāla diś ātma manāṃsi sāmānya viśeṣa saṃjñayā uktāni navā eva iti tad vyatirekeṇa anyasya sañjñāna bhidhānāt evam ṣaṣ padārtha jñānasya puruṣa artha āpāyika tvam pratītya teṣām pratyekam bheda jñāna artham paripṛcchati atha ke dravya ādayaḥ pada prthāḥ iti kāni dravyāṇi ke guṇāḥ kāni karmāṇi ityādi yojanīyam na ca avaśyam dharmiṇi jñāte dharmāḥ jñāyante iti tena dharmeṣvātha pṛthak praśnaḥ kiñca teṣām iti ādi atra api ca samuccaye 
NK_17.4	 uttaram āha tatra iti ādi teṣu dravya ādiṣu madhye dravyāṇi pṛthivī ādīni sāmānya viśeṣa sañjñayā sāmānya sañjñayā dravya sañjñayā viśeṣa sañjñayā pratyekam asādhāraṇa sañjñaya pṛthivī apteja ādi rūpayā uktāni sūtrakāreṇa pratipāditāni kim etāvanti āhosvit aparāṇi api santi iti atas āha navā eva iti nanu navānām lakṣaṇa abhidhāne sāmarthyāt apareṣām abhāvaḥ jñātaḥ vyartham nava eva iti na navasu lakṣiteṣu kim apareṣām asat tvāt uta satām api anupayogi tvāt na lakṣaṇam kṛtam iti saṃśayaḥ na nivartteta lakṣaṇasya vyavahāra mātra sāra tayā samāna asamāna jātīya vyavaccheda mātra sādhana tvena ca anya abhāva pratipādana asāmarthyāt tad artham avadhāranām kṛtam idam eva sāmānyena uddiṣṭānām viśeṣa sañjña abhidhānam tantra antare vibhāgaḥ iti nirddeśaḥ iti ca kathyate katham etat avagatam navā eva iti atas āha tad vyatirekeṇa ityādi tebhyaḥ navabhyaḥ vyatirekeṇa sarvajñena mahā ṛṣiṇā sarva artha upadeśāya pravṛttena anyasya daśam asya saṃjñā anabhidhānāt 
NK_18.1^1	 tamaḥ nāma rūpa saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthak tva paratva aparatva saṃyoga vibhāga paratvā paratva vega vat dravya antaram asti iti ced atra kaścid āha yadi tamaḥ dravyam rūpavat dravyasya sparśa avī abhicārāt sparśavat dravyasya mahataḥ pratighāta dharmaka tvāt tamasi sañcarataḥ pratibandhaḥ syāt mahā andhakāre ca bhū golakasya iva tad avayava bhūtāni khaṇḍa avaya vi dravyāṇi pratīyeran iti tat ayuktam yathā pradīpāt nirgaṃtaiḥ avayavaiḥ adṛṣṭa vaśāt anudbhūta sparśam anibiḍa avayavam apratīyamāna khaṇḍa avayavi dravya pravibhāgam apratighāti prabhā maṇḍala gṛha vyāpakam ārabhyate tathā tamaḥ paramāṇubhiḥ api tamaḥ dravyam 
NK_18.1^2	 tasmāt anyathā samādhīyate tamaḥ paramāṇavaḥ sparśavantaḥ tad rahitāḥ vā na tāvat sparśavantaḥ sparśavataḥ tad kāryya dravyasya kvacid api anupalambhāt adṛṣṭa vyāpāra abhāvāt sparśavat kārya dravya anārambhakāḥ iti ced rūpavantaḥ vāyu paramāṇavaḥ adṛṣṭa vyāpāra vaiguṇyāt rūpavat kāryyam na ārabhante iti kim na kalpyeta kim vā na kalpitam etat eka jātīyāt eva paramāṇoḥ adṛṣṭa upagrahāt caturdhā kāryyāṇi jāyante iti kāryya eka samadhigamyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ yathākāryyam unnīyate na tad vilakṣaṇāḥ pramāṇa abhāvāt iti ced asparśavat tvasya kāryya dravya anārambhaka tvena avyabhicāra upalambhāt 
NK_18.1^3	 kāryya darśanāt tad anuguṇam kāraṇam kalpyate na tu kāraṇa vaiguṇyena dṛṣṭa kāryi aviparyyāsaḥ yujyate jagat vaicitryasya api apahnava prasaṅgāt iti ced na vayam andhakārasya pratyarthinaḥ kintvā ārambhānupapatteḥ nīlima mātra pratīteḥ ca dravyam idam na bhavati iti brumaḥ tarhi bhāsām abhāvaḥ eva ayam pratīyeta na tasya nīla ākāreṇa pratibhāsā yogāt madhyandine api dūra gagana ābhoga vyāpinaḥ nīlimnaḥ ca pratīteḥ kiñca gṛhyamāṇe pratiyogini saṃyukta viśeṣaṇa tayā tad anya pratiṣedha mukhena abhāvaḥ gṛhyate na svatantraḥ tamasi ca gṛhyamāṇe na anyasya grahaṇam asti 
NK_18.1^4	 na ca pratiṣedha mukhaḥ pratyayaḥ tasmāt na abhāvaḥ ayam na ca āloka adarśana mātram eva etat bahirmukha tayā tam iti chāyā iti ca kṛṣṇa ākāra pratibhāsanāt tasmāt rūpa viśeṣaḥ ayam atyantam tejaḥ bhāve sati sarvu atas samāropitaḥ tamaḥ iti pratīyate divā ca ūrdhvam nayana golakasya nīlimāḥ avabhāsate iti vakṣyāmaḥ yadā tu niyata deśa adhikaraṇaḥ bhāsām abhāvaḥ tadā tāvat deśa samāropite nīlimni chāyā iti avagamaḥ atas eva dīrghā hrasvā mahanī alpīyasī chāyā iti abhimānaḥ tad deśa vyāpinaḥ nīlimnaḥ pratīteḥ abhāva pakṣe ca bhāva dharma adhyāraḥ api durupapādaḥ tat uktam 
NK_18.2–18.4	 na ca bhāsām abhāvasya tamaḥ tvam vṛddha sammatam chāyāyāḥ kārṣṇyam iti evam puraṇe bhū guṇa śruteḥ dūra āsanna pradīpa ādeḥ mahat alpa cala acalāḥ deha anuvarttinī chāyā na vastu tvāt vinā bhavet iti durupapādaḥ ca kvacid chāyāyām kṛṣṇa sarpa bhramaḥ calati pratyayaḥ api gacchati āvaraka dravye yatra yatra tejasaḥ abhāvaḥ tatra tatra rūpa upalabdhi kṛtaḥ evam paratva ādayaḥ api anyathā siddhāḥ 
NK_19.1–19.2	 tatra ca āloka abhāva vyañjanīya rūpa viśeṣe tamasya āloka anapekṣasya eva cakṣuṣaḥ sāmarthyam tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt yathā loka abhāvaḥ eva tvad mate nanu evam tarhi sūtra virodhaḥ dravya guṇa karma niṣpatti vaidharmya adbhā bhāvaḥ tamaḥ iti na virodhaḥ bhās abhāve sati tamasaḥ pratīteḥ bhābhāvaḥ tamaḥ iti uktam īśvaraḥ api buddhi guṇa tvāt ātmā eva na tu ṣaḍguṇa adhikaraṇaḥ caturddaśa guṇa adhikaraṇāt guṇa bhedena bhidyate mukta ātmabhiḥ vyabhicārāt 
NK_20.1–20.2^1	 guṇāḥ rūpa rasa gandha sparśa saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ ca iti kaṇṭha uktāḥ saptadaśa aca a śabda samuccitāḥ ca guru tva drava tva sneha saṃskāra adṛṣṭa śabdāḥ saptā eva iti evam caturviṃśatiḥ guṇāḥ guṇāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ kaṇṭha uktā sūtrakāreṇa sākṣāt uktāḥ rūpa rasa gandha sparśāḥ saṅkhyā parimāṇāni pṛthaktvam saṃyoga viyogau paratva aparatve buddhayaḥ sukha duḥkhe icchā dveṣau prayatnaḥ ca guṇāḥ iti prayatnaḥ ca iti aca aśabdena atra anuktā gunātvena loke prasiddhāḥ guru tva ādayaḥ sapta samuccitā evam caturviṃśatiḥ eva guṇāḥ ye tu śauryya audāryya kāruṇya dākṣiṇī augrī ādayaḥ te atra eva antarbhavanti śauryyaḥ balavataḥ api parasya parājayam pratyutsāhaḥ sa ca prayatna viśeṣaḥ eva satatam sat mārga anuvartinī buddhiḥ audāryyam 
NK_20.2^2	 para duḥkha prahāṇa icchā kāruṇyam tattva abhiniveśinī buddhiḥ dākṣiṇyam augryam ātmani utkarṣa pratyayaḥ iti evam ādiḥ adṛṣṭa śabdena dharma adharmayoḥ upasaṅgrahaḥ saṃskāraḥ iti sa ca vegasya bhāvanāyāḥ sthiti sthāpakasya ca abhidhānam nanu evam tarhi ādhikyam na saṃakāra tva jāti apekṣayā vega bhāvanā sthiti sthāpakānām eka tvāt evam tarhi na caturviṃśati tvam adṛṣṭa tva jāti apekṣayā dharma adharmayoḥ eka tvāt katham caturviṃśati tvam iti ced tat na asṛṣṭa tva jāti abhāvāt nirguṇaṣu asā dharma yogi tvena upacārāt caturviṃśatiḥ iti vyavahāraḥ 
NK_21.1–21.2	 utkṣepaṇa apakṣepaṇa ākuñcana prasāraṇa gamanāni pañca eva karmāṇi gamana grahaṇāt bhramaṇa recana syandana ūrddhva jvalana tiryyak patanana manonnamana ādayaḥ gamana viśeṣāḥ na jāti antarāṇi karmāṇi vibhajate utkṣepaṇa iti kiyanti tāni tatra āha pañca eva iti nanu bhramaṇa ādayaḥ api santi katham pañca eva iti avadhāraṇam atas āha gamana grahaṇāt iti gamana grahaṇāt pñca eva karmāṇi atra upapattim āha bhramaṇa recana syandana iti ādi yasmāt bhramaṇa ādayaḥ api gamana viśeṣāḥ gamana prabhedāḥ na jāti antarāṇi tasmāt gamana grahaṇena eteṣām api grahaṇāt pañca eva iti avadhāraṇam siddhyati iti arthaḥ 
NK_22.1–22.2^1	 sāmānyam dvividham param aparan ca anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam tatra param sattā mahā viṣaya tvāt sā ca anuvṛtteḥ eva hetu tvāt sāmānyam eva dravya tva ādi aparam alpa viṣaya tvāt tat ca vyāvṛtteḥ api hetu tvāt sāmānyam sat viśeṣa ākhyām api labhate sāmānyam kathayati sāmānyam dvividham iti dvaividhyam eva kathayati parama param ca iti caḥ avadhāraṇe param a param eva iti arthaḥ tasya svarūpam kathayati anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam iti atyanta vyāvṛttānām piṇḍānām yatas kāraṇāt anyonya svarūpa anugamaḥ pratīyate tad sāmānyam 
NK_22.1–22.2^2	 kim tat param sāmānyam iti āha param sattā iti atra yuktim āha saha aviṣaya tvāt iti dravya tva ādi apekṣayā bahu viṣaya tvāt iti arthaḥ sā ca anuvṛtteḥ eva hetu tvāt sāmānyam eva dravya tva ādikam tu sva āśrayasya vijātīyebhyaḥ api vyāvṛtteḥ api hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ api bhavati sattā tu sva āśrayasya anuvṛtteḥ eva hetuḥ tena sāmānyam eva yadi api eṣā sāmānya ādibhyaḥ vyāvarttate tathā api na tebhyaḥ sva āśrayam vyāvarttayitum śaknoti teṣām api svarūpa satām sat buddhi vedya tvāt vastu apekṣayā ca anuvṛtti hetu tvam vivakṣitam tena abhāvāt vyāvṛtti hetu tve api na doṣaḥ 
NK_23.1–23.2	 yad pramāṇena pratīyate tatra asti iti vyavahāraḥ lokānām viparyyaye tu na asti iti tena pramāṇa gamya eva sat tā iti kecid tat ayuktam pramāṇa utpatteḥ prāk vastumaḥ asattava prasaṅgāt asataḥ ca khara viṣāṇasya iva grāhya tva abhāvāt anyonya saṃśraya āpatteḥ ca asataḥ pramāṇasya agrāhaka tve sattāyāḥ pramāṇa grāhya tā lakṣaṇa tve ca grahakasya pramāṇasya api grahaka antara anusaraṇena anavasthā pātāt ca atha matam na brūmaḥ pramāṇa sambandhaḥ sat tā iti kintu pramāṇa sambandha yogyam vastu svarūpam eva sattā yaḥ api sattā sāmānyam icchati tena api padārtha svarūpam abhyupeyam niḥsvabhapve śaśaviṣāṇa ādau sattāyāḥ asamavāyāt evam ced tat eva astu kim anyayā sat tayā iti 
NK_24.1	 atra ucyate pratyekam padārtha svarūpāṇi bhinnāni katham tesu eka ākāra pratītiḥ eka śabda pravṛttiḥ ca ananteṣu sambandha grahaṇa abhāvāt atha teṣu ekam nimittam asti siddham naḥ samīhitam yathā dṛṣṭa eka gopiṇḍasya piṇḍa antare pūrvaṃrūpa anukāriṇī buddhiḥ udeti na evam mahīdharam upalabhya sarṣapam upalabhamānasya pūrva ākāra avabhāsaḥ asti iti kutas atra sāmānya kalpanā iti ced kim mahīdhara ādiṣu nikhila rūpa anugamaḥ na asti uta mātrayā api na vidyate yadi nikhila rūpa anugama abhāvāt teṣu sāmānya pratyākhyānam tarhi go tvam api pratyākhyeyam tayoḥ śābaleya bāhuleyayoḥ api sarvathā sādharmya abhāvāt atha mātrayā api svarūpa anugamaḥ na asti tat asiddham sarvu eṣām api teṣām abhāva vilakṣaṇena rūpeṇa tulya tā pratibhāsanāt iyān tu viśeṣaḥ gopiṇḍeṣu jhaṭiti tad jātīyatā buddhiḥ bhūyas avayava sāmānya anugamāt mahīdhara ādiṣu tu vilambinī stoka avayava sāmānya anugamena jāteḥ anudbhūta tvāt yathā maṇika darśnāt śarāve mṛd jāti buddhiḥ 
NK_24.2–24.3	 etena artha kriyā kāri tvam api sattvam pratyuktam asataḥ artha kriyāyāḥ abhāvāt artha kriyā yāñca satyām tasya sattvāt artha kriyāyāḥ ca artha kriyā apekṣayā sattvena anavasthāne sarvasya asattva prasaṅgāt ca dravya tva ādi aparam dravya tvam guṇa tvam karma tvañca aparam sattā apekṣayā alpa viṣaya tvāt iti arthaḥ tathā dravya tva ādi apekṣayā pṛthivī tva ādikam aparam tad apekṣayā ghaṭa tva ādikam aparam guṇa tva ādi apekṣayā rūpa tva ādikam aparam tad apekṣayā nīla tva ādikam karma tva ādi apekṣayā ca utkṣepaṇa tva ādikam vyākhyeyam 
NK_25.1^1	 jalam upalabhya vahnim upalamānasya tat iti anugama abhāvāt dravya tvam na asti iti kecid tad asāram dvayoḥ api tayoḥ sva prādhānyena pratīti sambhavāt sva prādhānya prādhānya aratītiḥ eva ca dravya tva pratītiḥ utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu api calana ātmaka tā pratītiḥ asti sā eva ca karma tva pratītiḥ rūpa ādiṣu tu kṛta samayasya anuvṛtti pratyaya sambhavāt guṇa tvasya apratyākhyānam vyakti grahaṇam iva samaya grahaṇam api pratīti kāraṇam brāhmaṇa tvasya iva yoni sambandha jñānam tatra api viśuddha brāhmaṇa santati jasya utpatti mātra anubaddham api brāhmaṇa tvam indriya pāta mātreṇa kṣatriya ādi vilakṣaṇa tayā na gṛhyate atyanta vyakti sausādṛśyena jāteḥ anudbhūta tvāt 
NK_25.1^2	 yadā tu mātā pitroḥ tad pūrveṣān ca vṛddha paramparayā viśuddha brāhmaṇa tvam avasitam tadā brāhmaṇaḥ ayam iti pratyakṣeṇa eva pratīyate yathā hi su vidita ratna parīkṣā śāstraḥ ratna jāti bhedam pratyakṣatas pratyeti na apāraḥ na ca tāvatā ratna jāti bhedaḥ na asti na ca tad pratyakṣam apratyakṣam yat ca uktam strīṇām svabhāva capalānām viśuddhiḥ durava bodhā eva iti tat asat abhiyuktsiḥ su rakṣitānām sukaraḥ tad avabodhaḥ kathitaḥ ca tāsām bahuvidhaḥ rakṣaṇa upāyaḥ iti āstam tāvat prasakta anuprasaṅgaḥ 
NK_26.1–26.2	 nitya dravya vṛttayaḥ antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ te khalu atyanta vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt viśeṣāḥ eva tat ca dravya tva ādikam sva viṣayasya vijātīyebhyaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ api vyavacchedasya api hetu tvāt viśeṣa ākhyām viśeṣa sañjñām api labhate na kevalam anuvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānya sañjñām labhate vyāvṛtteḥ api hetu tvāt viśeṣa sañjñām api labhate iti api śabdayoḥ arthaḥ kim uktam syāt dravya tva ādiṣu sāmānya śabdaḥ mukhyaḥ anuvṛtti hetu tvasya sāmānya lakṣaṇasya sambhavāt viśeṣa śabdaḥ ca bhāktaḥ sva āśrayaḥ viśiṣyate sarvatas atyantam vyavacchidyate yena sa viśeṣaḥ iti lakṣaṇasya atra abhāvāt idantu lakṣaṇam antya viśeṣeṣu asti 
NK_26.3	 nitya dravya vṛttayaḥ antayā viśeṣāḥ iti nitya dravyeṣu eva varttante eva ye te viśeṣāḥ iti nitya dravyeṣu eti dravya guṇa karma sāmānyānām vyavacchedaḥ dravya guṇa karmāṇi dravyeṣu eva varttante na nityeṣu eva iti sāmānyāni tu na dravyeṣu eva na nityeṣu eva varttantaḥ eva iti buddhi cabda ādīnām vyavacchedaḥ teṣām samasta nitya dravya prāpti abhāvāt nanu kim viśesāḥ viśeṣāḥ eva kim vā dravya tva ādi vat ubhaya rūpāḥ iti tatra āha te khalu iti khalu śabdaḥ niścaye nitya dravya vṛttayaḥ ye viśeṣāḥ te viśeṣāḥ eva niścitā na tu sāmānyāni api bhavanti iti arthaḥ atyantam sarvadā vyāvṛtteḥ eva sva āśrayasya itarasmāt vyavacchedasya eva hetu tvāt kāraṇa tvāt iti yathā ca idam tathā upariṣṭāt upapādanīyam 
NK_27.1–27.2	 ayutasiddhānām ādhāryya ādhāra bhūtānām yaḥ sambandhaḥ iha pratyaya hetuḥ sa samavāyaḥ samavāyasya svarūpam nirūpayati ayutasiddhānām iti yuta siddhiḥ pṛthak siddhiḥ pṛthak avasthitiḥ ubhayoḥ api sambandhinoḥ paraspara parihāreṇa pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvāt sā yayoḥ na asti tau= ayuta siddhau tayoḥ sambandhaḥ samavāyaḥ yathā tantu paṭayoḥ 
NK_27.3^1	 yadi api tantavaḥ paṭa vyatiriktāḥ paṭe na samavayanti tathā api ubhayoḥ paraspara parihāreṇa pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam na asti paṭasya tantuṣu eva āśrayi tvāt yatra tu dvayoḥ api sambandhinoḥ paraspara parihāreṇa vyatirikta ācrayā āśrayi tvam tatra yuta siddhiḥ yathā tvac indriya śarīrayoḥ śarīram hi tvac indriya parihāreṇa pṛthak āśraye sva avayave samāśritam tvac indriyam ca śarīra parihāreṇa pṛthak āśraye sva avayave samāśratam tena anayoḥ saṃyogaḥ na samavāyaḥ nityānāntu yuta siddhiḥ pṛthak avasthitiḥ pṛthak gamana yogya tā sā yayoḥ na asti tau= ayuta siddhau tayoḥ yaḥ sambandhaḥ sa samavāyaḥ yathā ākāśa dravya tvayoḥ iti 
NK_27.3^2	 ayuta siddhiyoḥ sambandhaḥ iti ucyamāne dharmasya sukhasya ca yaḥ kāryya kāraṇa bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ api samavāyaḥ prāpnoti tayoḥ ātma eka āśratayoḥ yuta siddhi abhāvāt tat artham ādhāryya ādhāra bhūtānām iti padam na tu ākāśa śakuni sambandha nivṛtti artham ayutasiddha padena eva tasya nivarttita tvāt evam api ākāśasya ākāśa padasya ca vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ samavāyaḥ syāt tad nivṛtti artham ihapratyaya hetuḥ iti vācya vācaka bhāve hi tasmāt śabdāt tat arthaḥ na vyavacchidyate tat artham ayutasiddhānām iti 
NK_28.1–28.2^1	 atra kecid ayuta siddha padam vikalpayanti kim yutau na siddhau āhosvit ayutau siddhau yadi yutau na siddhau kaḥ tayoḥ sambandhaḥ dharmaṇoḥ abhāvāt atha ayutau siddhau tathā api kaḥ sambandhaḥ apṛthak siddha tvāt eva bhinnayoḥ hi sambandhaḥ yathā kuṇḍa badarayoḥ iti tat apare na mṛṣyanti na hi asya ayam arthaḥ yutau na siddhau na niṣpannau= iti asatoḥ samavāya anabhyupagamāt na api asya ayam arthaḥ ayutau siddhau= eka ātmakau siddhau= iti eka ātmaka tve hi ekam eva vastu syāt na ubhayam paraspara ātmaka tva abhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt ubhaya rūpa tāyāḥ na ca tat ekam vastu parama arthaḥ paraspara vilakṣaṇena rūpeṇa tayoḥ ākārayoḥ pratibhāsanāt 
NK_28.1–28.2^2	 vilakṣaṇa ākāra buddhi vedya tvasya eva bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt anyathap bheda abheda vyavasthā anupapatteḥ tasmāt na svarūpa abhedaḥ api ayuta siddhiḥ kintu ayutasiddhāṇm iti paraspara parihāreṇa pṛthak āśraya an āśritānām iti arthaḥ tathā ca sati sambandhaḥ na anupapannaḥ svarūpa bhedasya sambhavāt bhinnayoḥ ca paraspara upaśleṣasya dahana ayaḥ piṇḍayoḥ iva vinā sambandhena asambhavāt iyān tu viśeṣaḥ vahniḥ utpatteḥ paścāt ayaḥ piṇḍena saha sambaddhyate iha tu sva kāraṇa sāmarthyāt upajamānam eva tatra sambaddhyate yathā chidi kriyā chedyena iti alam 
NK_29.1–29.2	 evam dharmaiḥ vinā dharmaṇām uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ nanu kim artham ṣaṣ eva padārthāḥ uddiṣṭā na apare teṣam eva bhāvāt tad anyeṣām abhāvāt ca tad abhāvaḥ ca sarvvaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt śaśa viṣāṇa vat ṣaṇṇām sāmānya lakṣaṇam vidhi pratyaya viṣaya tvam vyāvṛttantu lakṣaṇam yathā guṇa āśrayaḥ dravyam sāmānyavāna guṇaḥ saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapekṣaḥ na kāraṇam guṇaḥ eka dravyam aguṇam saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapelṣa kāraṇam karma anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam samānyam atyanta vyāvṛtti buddhi hetuḥ viśeṣaḥ ayutasiddhayoḥ āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ samavāyaḥ iti 
NK_29.3	 anuddiṣṭeṣu dharmaṣu dharmāḥ na śakyante vaktum atas dharmāṇam uddeśam prakramayitum saṅgatim pradarśayati evam iti evam pūrva uktena granthena dharmaiḥ vinā dharmān parityajya dharmaṇam uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ dharmaṇām saṃjñā mātreṇa saṅkīrttanam kṛtam idānīm dharmāḥ uddiśyante iti bhāvaḥ yadi api pūrvam dravya ādīnām vibhāgaḥ kṛtaḥ tathā api uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ iti uktam vibhāgasya nāmadheya saṅkīrttana mātreṇa uddeśe antarbhāvāt 
NK_30.1–30.5	 ṣaṇṇām api padārthānām sādharmyam astitatva abhidheya tva jñeya tvam āśrita tvañcāmi atra nitya dravyebhyaḥ dravya ādīnām pañcānām api samavāyi tvam aneka tvañca guṇa ādīnām pañcānām api nirguṇa tva niṣkriya tve yadi api dharmāḥ ṣaṭpadārthebhyaḥ na vyatiricyante kintu te eva anyonya apekṣayā dharmāḥ dharmiṇaḥ ca bhavanti iti tathā api teṣām dharma rūpa tayā parijñāna artham pṛthak uddeśam karoti ṣaṇṇām api iti astitvam svarūpattvam ṣaṇṇām api sādharman yasya yasya vastunaḥ yat yat svarūpam tat eva tasya astitvam adhidheya tvam api abhidhāna pratipādana yogya tvam tat ca vastunaḥ sva rūpam eva jñeya tvam jñāna grahaṇa yogya tvam tat api svarūpam eva bhāva bhāvasya sva rūpam eva avasthā bhedena jñeya tvam abhidheya tvañcā ucyate 
NK_30.6–30.7	 āśrita tvañca paratantra tayā upalabdhiḥ na samavāya lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ samavāye tat abhāvāt idañca āśrita tvam caturvvidheṣu paramāṇuṣu ākāśa kāla diś ātma manaḥsu na asti iti āha anyatra nitya dravyebhyaḥ iti ye tu dharmān tada vyatiriktān icchanti teṣām ekasmin samasta vastu vyāpini asti iti pratyaya hetau= astitve kalpite dravya ādiṣu sattā vaiyarthyam atha astitvam prativastu bhidyate tadā tad kalpam āvaii arthyam sattāyāḥ sva rūpa sattāyāḥ ca sat iti prayaya upapatteḥ yeṣāntu bhāva svarūpam eva astitvam na teṣām vyarthā sattā svarūpasya anuvṛtti pravyaya hetutva abhāvāt na api astitvam anarthakam niḥsvarūpe sattāyāḥ samavāya abhāvāt iti ubhayam upapadyate 
NK_30.8	 dravya ādīnām viśeṣa antānām sādharmyam sādharati samavāyi tvam samavāya lakṣaṇā vṛttiḥ aneka tvam paraspara bhinna tvam bhinna tvam ca itaretaravyāvṛttam svarūpam eva dravya ādīnām iti ukte samavāyaḥ api gṛhyeta gṛhyeta tad artham pañcānām iti uktam pañcānām iti ukte ca keṣām iti na jñāyate tad artham dravya ādīnām iti 
NK_31.1–31.2	 dravya ādīnām trayāṇām api sattā sambandhaḥ sāmānya viśeṣavat tvam avasamaya artha śabda abhidheya tvam dharma adharma kartṛ tvañca guṇānām samavāya antānām sādharmyam āha guṇa ādīnām iti nirguṇa tvam guṇa abhāva viśiṣṭa tvam niṣkriya tvam kriyā bhāva viśiṣṭa tvam yathā ca bhāvaḥ abhāvasya viśeṣaṇam sva viśiṣṭa pratyaya jananāt evam abhāvaḥ api tathā ca upanibaddham aghaṭam bhū talam iti bhāva abhāvayoḥ asambandhāt katham abhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇam iti ced asti tāvat ayam viśiṣṭa pratyayaḥ tat datśanāt sambandham api kalpayiṣyāmaḥ yadi sambaddham eva viśeṣaṇam manyase 
NK_31.3	 dravya ādīnām trayāṇām api sattā sambandhaḥ sat tayā sāmānyena saha sambandhaḥ samavāya rūpaḥ dravya guṇa karmaṇām sādharmyam yathā ca eteṣu sattā sambandhaḥ tathā upapāditam idantu iha nirūpyate kim sattā sambandhaḥ sataḥ asataḥ vā sataḥ ced prāk sattā sambandhāt san= ā iva asau= arthaḥ iti vyarthā sattā atha asataḥ sambandhaḥ khara viṣāṇa ādiṣu api sattā syāt nityeṣu tāvat rūpūrva aparabha anabhyupagamaḥ anityeṣu tu prāk asataḥ eva sattā kāraṃasāmārthyāt na ca khara viṣāṇa ādiṣu atiprasaṅgaḥ kasyacid sāmarthya abhāvāt 
NK_31.4–31.5	 anyat api sādharmyam dravya ādīnām trāṇām kathayati sāmānya viśeṣavat tvan ca iti anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt sāmānya viśeṣāḥ dravya tvāt ayastaḥ saha sambandhaḥ dravya ādīnām sa ca samavāyaḥ eva sva samaya artha śabda abhidheya tvan ca iti vaiśeṣikaḥ svayam vyavahārāya yaḥ saṅketaḥ kṛtaḥ asmin śāstre aartha śabdāt dravya guṇa karmāṇi pratipatta vyāni a iti tena dravya ādīni trīṇi nirupapadena arśabdena ucyante 
NK_31.6	 dharma adharma kartṛ tvan ca iti dharma adharma utpatti nimitta tvam trayāṇām tathā hi bhūmiḥ ekā eva dīyamāna apahriyamāṇā ca dharma adharmayoḥ kāraṇam ekaḥ saṃyogaḥ dvayoḥ kāraṇam yathā kapilā sparśaḥ nara asthi sparśaḥ ca evam karma api ubhaya kāraṇam yathā tīrtha gamanam śauṇḍika gṛha gamanan ca evam anyat api ūhyam dharma adharma karttṛ tvam iti tva pratyayena dharma adharma jananam prati teṣām nijā śaktiḥ ucyate nanu jātiḥ api tayoḥ kāraṇam na tasyāḥ sva āśraya vyavaccheda mātreṇa caritārtha tvāt 
NK_32.1–32.2	 kāryyatva anitya tve kāraṇavatām eva kāryyatva anitya tve kāraṇavatām eva yeṣām dravya ādīnām utpatti kāraṇam asti teṣām kāryya tvam anitya tvañca dharmaḥ na sarveṣām iti arthaḥ sva kāraṇe samavāyaḥ prāc asataḥ sattā samavāyaḥ vā kāryya tvam iti eke tat ayuktam pradhvaṃse tad abhāvāt tasmāt kāraṇa adhīnaḥ sva ātma lābhaḥ kāryya tvam iti lakṣaṇam vyāpaka tvāt prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāva upalakṣitāḥ vastunaḥ sattā eva anitya tvam iti kecid tat ayuktam apratīteḥ anityaḥ iti vināśī iti evam lokaḥ pratyeti na tu sattā viśiṣṭatām utpatti vināśa yogi tvam iti aparaḥ tat api asāram prāc abhāve utpatteḥ abhāvāt tasya api anitya tvena loke sampratipatteḥ tasmāt sva rūpa vinācaḥ eva anitya tvam iti yathā uktam anitya tvam vināśa ākhyam kriyā sāmānyam ucyate iti yadi api vināśaḥ vastu kāle na asti tathā api pramāṇa antar asiddha sadbhāvaḥ bhavati eva viśeṣaṇam anityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti pratyetuḥ eka tvāt tathā ca loke vināśi śarīram adhruvāḥ viṣayāḥ iti 
NK_33.1–33.2	 kāraṇatvañca anyatra pārimāṇḍalī ādibhyaḥ kāraṇatvañca anyatra pārimāṇḍalī ādibhyaḥ iti pārimāṇḍalyam iti vibhu tvam antyaḥ śabdaḥ manaḥ parimāṇam paratva aparatve dvi pṛthaktvam antya avayaviparimāṇañca ityādi grahyam etāni parityajya apareṣām dravya ādīnām trayāṇam kāraṇa tvam samavāyi asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam yadi api dravyasya na asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam na ca samavāyi kāraṇa tvam guṇa karmaṇoḥ tathā api nimitta kāraṇa vilakṣaṇa tayā idam sādharmyam uktam 
NK_34.1–34.2	 dravya āśrita tvañcā anyatra nitya dravyebhyaḥ dravya āśrita tvañcā anyatra nitya dravyebhyaḥ iti nanu āśrita tvam ṣaṇṇām iti uktam tena idam punar uktam na pusar uktam dravya upalakṣitasya āśrita tvasya atra vivakṣita tvāt iti kaścid tat ayuktam sāmānya ādīnām api dravya upalakṣitasya āśrita tvasya sambhavān na idam dravya ādi trayasya sādharmya kathanam syāt tasmāt ittham vyākhyeyam anyatra nitya dravyebhyaḥ iti dravya grahaṇam upalakṣaṇam tad vṛttayaḥ antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ te api gṛhyante nitya dravyāṇi tad gatān ca viśeṣān parityajya dravyaḥ eva āśrita tvam dravya ādīnām trayāṇām sādhyarmyam na apareṣam iti arthaḥ 
NK_35.1–35.2^1	 sāmānya ādīnām trayāṇām api sva ātma sattvam buddhi lakṣaṇa tvam akāryya tvam akāraṇa tvam asāmānya viśeṣavat tvam nitya tvam artha śabda an abhidheya tvañca iti samprati sāmānya ādīnām sādharmyam āha sāmānya ādīnām iti sva ātmava sattvam sva ātma sattvam svarūpam yat sāmānya ādīnām tat eva teṣām sattvam na sattā yogaḥ sattvam etena sāmānya ādīnām trayāṇām sāmānya rahita tvam sādharmyam uktam iti srthaḥ katham etat bādhaka sadbhāvāt sattāyām tāvat sattā na asti aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt viśeṣeṣu api sāmānya sadbhāve saṃśayasya api sambhavāt nirṇaya artham viśeṣa anusaraṇe api anavasthā eva samavāye api sattā abhyupagame tad vṛtti artham samavāya antara abhyupagamāt aniṣṭāpattiḥ eva dūṣaṇam 
NK_35.2^2	 go tva ādiṣu tu apara jātimat tvvena vyāptasya sattā saṃbandhasya tad nivṛtau nivṛtti siddhiḥ kutas tarhi sāmānya ādiṣu sat sat iti anugamaḥ sva rūpa sattva sādharmyeṇa satta adhya āropāt tarhi mithyā pratyayaḥ ayam kaḥ nāma āha na iti bhinna svabhāveṣu eka anugamaḥ mithyā eva svarūpa grahaṇantu na mithyā svarūpasya yathārtha tvāt dravya ādiṣu ādiṣu api sattādhyāra upakṛtaḥ eva astu pratyaya anugamaḥ na evam asati mukhye adhyāropasya asambhavāt na ca iyam sāmānya ādiṣu eva mukhyāḥ bādhaka sambhavāt dravya ādiṣu ca tad abhāvāt 
NK_35.3	 buddhi lakṣaṇa tvam iti buddhiḥ eva lakṣaṇam pramāṇam yeṣām te buddhi lakṣaṇāḥ vipratipannam prati sāmānya ādi sadbhāve buddhiḥ eva lakṣaṇam na anyat dravya ādi sadbhāve tu anyat api tat kāryyam pramāṇam syāt iti arthaḥ kaścid punar evam āha buddhi ap lakṣante pratīnte iti buddhi lakṣaṇāḥ tat ayuktam dravya ādeḥ api sva buddhi lakṣaṇa tvāt na idam vaidharmyam uktam syāt 
NK_35.4	 akāryya tvam kāraṇa anapekṣa svabhāva tvam tat ca sāmānye tāvat vyakteḥ pūrvam ūrddhvam vyakti kāle ca avasthiti grāhakeṇa kāraṇa abhāva upalabdhi sahakāriṇā bhūyas darśana ja saṃskāra nugṛhītena pratyakṣeṇa eva vyāpti vat gṛhyate samavāyasya api skāryya tvam pūrva apara sahabhāva an avaklṛpteḥ yadi hi paṭasya samavāyaḥ paṭāt pūrvam sambhavati asati sambandhini kasya asau sambandhaḥ syāt atha paṭena saha utpadyate tadā paṭasya anādhāra tvam prāpnoti atha paścāt bhavati tathā api paṭasya anādhāra tvam eva na ca kāryya tvam anādhāram yuktam tasmāt akṛtakaḥ samavāyaḥ viśeṣāṇa añcā kāryya tvam vastu tve sati dravya guṇa karma anya tvāt sāmānya sama vāta vat siddham 
NK_35.5	 akāraṇa tvam samavāyi asamavāyikāraṇa tva abhāvaḥ na tu nimitta kāraṇa tva pratiṣedhaḥ buddhi nimitta tva abhyupagamāt asāmānya viśeṣavat tvam apara jāti rahita tvam iti arthaḥ sāmānyeṣu sāmānyeṣu sāmānyat nāma na aparam sāmānyam asti tatra api sāmānya prāptā anavasthānāt viṣeṣa samavāyayoḥ tu sāmānya abhāve kathitaḥ eva nyāyaḥ katham tarhi sāmānyeṣu pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ sāmānyam sāmānyam iti aneka vyakti samavāya upādhi vaśāt viśeṣeṣu api eka śabda pravṛttiḥ atyanta vyāvṛtti buddhi janaka tvasi sarvatra sambhavāt nitya tvam vināśa rahita tvam tat api sāmānyasya vyakti utpāda vināśayoḥ avasthiti grāhiṇā bhūyas bhūyas pravṛttena nirupādhi pratyakṣeṇa vyāpti vat niścīyate samavāyasya tu sarvatra kāryya upalambhāt akṛtaka tvāt ca anumīyate artha śabda an abhidheya tvañcā iti sva samaya artha śabda an abhidheya tvam ca eteṣām sādharmyam caḥ samuccaye 
NK_36.1–36.2	 pṛthivī ādīnām navānām api dravya tva yogaḥ sva ātmani ārambhaka tvam guṇavattavam kāryya kāraṇa avirodhi tvam anya viśeṣavat tvam idānīm dravyaṇām eva sādharmyam nirūpayati pṛthivī ādīnām iti pṛthivī ādīnām eva dravya tvena sāmānyena yogaḥ sambandhaḥ sa kiyatām iti atas āha navānām api iti api śabdaḥ abhivyāpti arthaḥ etena dravya padārthasya itarebhyaḥ bheda lakṣaṇam uktam dravya śabdasya pravṛtti nimittan ca cintitam 
NK_36.3	 atra kaścid codayati dravya tva yogaḥ dravya tva samavāyaḥ sa ca pañca padārtha dharma tvāt katham dravya lakṣaṇam iti aparaḥ samādhatte yadi api sarvatra abhinnaḥ samavāyaḥ tathā api dravya tva upakṣaṇa bhesāt dravyasya lakṣaṇam dṛṣṭaḥ hi kalpita bhedasya api ākāśasya śrotra bhāvena artha kriyā bhedaḥ iti dvayam api etat asādhīyaḥ yathā ākāśam śrotram na evam yogaḥ dravyasya lakṣaṇam kintu dravya tvam eva tattva sambaddham lakṣaṇam na syāt iti yoga saṅkīrttanam liṅgasya dharmiṇī astitva kathanam tathā ca evam prayogaḥ pṛthivī ādikam itarebhyaḥ bhidyate dravya tvāt yeṣām itarebhyaḥ bhedaḥ na asti teṣām dravya tvam api na asti yathā rūpa ādīnām iti tasmāt asat codyama saduttaran ca 
NK_36.4	 anyat api dravyāṇām sādharmyam āha sva ātmani ārambhaka tvam iti sva ātmani ārambhaka tvam sva samevetakāryya janaka tvam iti arthaḥ guṇa tvam saha sambandhaḥ etat api ubhayam guṇa ādibhyaḥ dravyāṇām vaidharmyam anyatra asambhavāt kāryya kāraṇa avirodhi tvam guṇaḥ hi kvacid kāryyeṇa vināśyate yathā ādyaḥ śabdaḥ dvitīya śabdena kvacid kāraṇena vināśyate yathā antyaḥ śbdaḥ upāntyaśbdena kāryyeṇa vināśyate yathā uttara saṃyogena dravyāṇi tu na sva kāryyeṇa vināśyante na api sva kāraṇena iti kāryya kāraṇa avirodhīni nityānām kāraṇa vināśayoḥ abhācāt eva kāraṇena avināśaḥ anitya dravyāṇām kāraṇa vināśayoḥ sambhave api kāraṇena na vināśaḥ kintu anyena iti vivekaḥ tathā antya viśeṣavat tvam antya viśeṣa yogi tvam iti arthaḥ 
NK_37.1–37.4	 anāśrita tva nitya tve ca anyatra avaya vi dravyebhyaḥ pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavana ātma manasām aneka tva apara jātimat tve kṣiti jala jyotiḥ anila manasām kriyāvat tava mūrtta tva paratva aparatva vegavat tvāni anāśrita tvam kvacid api asama etatvam nitya tvam vināśa rahita tvañca dravyāṇām sādharmyam tat kim sarveṣām sādharmyam iti atas āha avayavi dravyebhyaḥ anyatra iti avayavi dravyāṇi parityajya antya viśeṣa vat tva āśrita tva nitya tvāni anyatra santi iti arthaḥ na kevakam pūrva uktāḥ pṛthivī ādīnām dharmāḥ kintu anāśrita tva nitya tve ca iti ca arthaḥ 
NK_37.5–37.6	 idānīm dravyāṇām eva paraspara sādharmyam vaidharmyañca pratipādan= āha pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavana ātma manasām iti aneka tvam pratyekam vyakti bhedaḥ apara jātima tvam iti pṛthivī tva ādi jāti sambandhi tvam kṣiti jala jyotiḥ anilam ansām kriyāvat tva mūrtta tva paratva aparatva vegavat tvāni iti kriyāvat tvam utkṣepaṇa ādi kriyā yogaḥ mūrtta tvam avacchinna āarimāṇa yogit tvam paratva aparatva vegavat tvāni paratva aparatva vega samavāyaḥ 
NK_37.7	 saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu abhūyaḥ tvayoḥ eva para apara vyavahāra hetu tvāt paratva aparatve na staḥ iti kecid tat na bhinna diś sambandhinoḥ sati api saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu abhūyaḥ tu asadbhāve sati api ca draṣṭuḥ śarīra apekṣayā sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ utpāde parāpara pratyaya abhāvāt ekasyām diśi avasthitayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ tathā prayayaḥ iti ced asti tarhi saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu abhūyaḥ tvābhyām viṣaya antaram viṣaya vailakṣaṇāyāḥ buddheḥ anutpādāt vegaḥ api guṇa antaram na kriyā santati mātram manda gatau vega pratīti abhāvāt kriyā akṣaṇānām āśu utpāda nimittaḥ vega vyavahāraḥ iti ced na alāta cakra ādiṣu kriyā akṣaṇānām nirantara utpāda vyayavatām pratyekam antara agrahaṇena aśu utpādasya pratyakṣeṇa apratīteḥ vega pratyayasya ca bhāvāt vyaktā ca loke kriyā vegayoḥ bheda avagatiḥ vegena gacchati iti pratīteḥ 
NK_38.1–38.2	 ākāśa kāla diś ātmanām sarva gata tvam parama mahat tvam sarva saṃyogi samāna deśa tvañca ākāśa kāla diś ātmanām sarva gata tvam iti ādi sarva śabdena atra prakṛta apekṣayā anantara uktāni mūrtta dravyāṇi parāmṛśyante sarva gata tvam sarvaiḥ mūttaiḥ saha saṃyogaḥ ākāśa ādīnām na tu sarvatra gamanam teṣām niṣkriya tvāt parama mahat tvam iyattā an avacchinna parimāṇa yogi tvam sarva saṃyogi samāna deśa tvam ca sarveṣām sā yoginām mūrtta dravyāṇām ākāśaḥ samānaḥ deśaḥ ekaḥ ādhāraḥ iti arthaḥ evam diś ādiṣu api vyākhyeyam yadi api ākāśa ādikām sarveṣām saṃyoginām ādhāraḥ na bhavati ādhāra bhāvena anavasthānāt tathā api sarva saṃyoga ādhāra tvāt sarva saṃyoginām ādhāra saṃyogaḥ asti iti uktam iha tu sarveṣām ādhāraḥ iti ucyate 
NK_39.1–39.2	 pṛthivī ādīnām pañcānām api bhūta tva indriya prakṛti tva bāhya ekaika indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇavat tvāni pṛthivī ādīnām ākāśa antānām itara vaidharmyeṇa sādharmyam kathayati pṛthivī ādīnām iti bhūta tvam bhūta śabda vācya tvam eka nimittam antareṇa anekeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu eka śabda pravṛttiḥ akṣa śabda vat yathā devanatva indriya tva bibhītaka tva sāmānya traya yogāt devana ādiṣcakṣa śabdaḥ sa aṅketikaḥ tathā pṛthivī tva ādi sāmānya vaśāt pṛthivī ādiṣu caturṣu bhūta śabda saṅketaḥ ākāśe tu vyakti nimittaḥ eva bhūtam bhūtam iti tad śabda anuviddhaḥ pratyayaḥ tad śabda vācya topa adhikṛtaḥ yathā devana ādiṣu ekaaḥ akṣaḥ iti pratyayaḥ 
NK_39.3	 indriya prakṛti tvam indriya svabhāvam na bhūta svabhāvāni indriyāṇi aprāpya kāri tvāt prāpya kāri tvam hi bhautikaḥ dharmaḥ yathā pradīpasya iti kecid tat ayuktam vyavahita artha anupalabdheḥ yadi indriyam aprāpya kāri kuḍya ādi vyavahitam api artham gṛhṇīya aprāpteḥ aviśeṣāt yogyatā bhāvāt vyavahita artha agrahaṇam iti ced indriyasya tāvat yogya tā viṣaya grahaṇa sāmarthyam asti eva tadānīm avyavahita artha grahaṇāt viṣayasya api yogya tā sahat tva aneka dravyavat tva rūpa viśeṣa ādi ātmikāḥ vyavadhāne api na nivṛttā eva ārjava avasthānam api tad avastham eva atha matam āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ api artha pratīti kāraṇam saṃyoga abhāvaḥ iva patana karmaṇi āvaraṇe satya āvaraṇa abhāvaḥ nivṛttaḥ iti pratīteḥ anutpattiḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt iti na etat sāram āvaraṇasya sparśavat dravya prāpti pratiṣedha artha tvena upalabdheḥ chatra ādikam hi patataḥ jalasya sāvitrasya ca tejasaḥ prāptim prātiṣedhati na tu svasya abhāva mātram nivarttayati 
NK_39.4^1	 tathā ca sati sulabham etat anumānam prāpta prakāśakam cakṣuḥ vyavahita artha aprakāśaka tvāt pradīpa vat bāhya indriya tvāt vā tvac indriya vat nanu evam tarhi viprakṛṣṭa artha grahaṇam kutas raśmi artha saṃnikarṣāt anudbhūta rūpa sparśāḥ na ayanāḥ raśmayaḥ dūre gatvā santam arthaḥ gṛhṇanti atas eva mahat aṇu prakāśaka tvāt kim indriyasya bhautika tvam na siddhyati pradīpasi eva raśmi dvāreṇa tat upapatteḥ yatra ca paśmayaḥ bhūyobhiḥ sva avayavaiḥ saha arthau= ayavinā tat avayavaiḥ ca saha sambaddhi ante tatra aśeṣa viśeṣāskanditasya arthasya grahaṇat sparṣṭam grahaṇam yatra tu avayavi mātreṇa sambandhaḥ tatra sāmānya mātra viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ grahaṇāt aspaṣṭam grahaṇam 
NK_39.4^2–39.5	 yat gacchati tat saṃnihita vyavahitau= arthau krameṇa prāpnoti tat katham śākhā candramasoḥ tulya kāla upalabdhiḥ iti ced indriya vṛtteḥ āśu sañcāri tvāt utpala patra śata vyatibheda vat krama agrahaṇa nimittaḥ ayam bhramaḥ na tu vāstavam yaugapadyam nanu prāpti pakṣe sa antarālaḥ ayam iti grahaṇam na syāt na anyathā tat upapatteḥ indriya sambandhasya atīndriya tvāt na tat abhāva akṛtau sāntara nirantara pratyayau kintu śarīra sambandha bhāva kṛtau yatra śarīra sambaddhasya arthasya grahaṇam tatra nirantaraḥ ayam iti pratyayaḥ yatra tu tad asambaddhasya grahaṇam tatra sāntaraḥ iti bāhya ekaika indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇavat tvāni iti bāhya ekaika indriyeṇa cakṣuḥ ādinā grāhyāḥ ye viśeṣa guṇāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ taiḥ tadvat tā pṛthivī ādīnām iti antaḥkaraṇa grāhya tvam api eṣam guṇānām asti tat aḥ ca ekaika indriya grāhya tvam asiddham tat artham bāhya grahaṇam ekaika grahaṇam svarūpa kathana artham 
NK_40.1–40.6	 caturṇām dravya ārambhaka tva sparśavat tve trayāṇām pratyakṣa tva rūpavat tva drava tvāni caturṇām dravya ārambhaka tva sparśavat tve caturṇām pṛthivī udkā anala anila anilānām dravya ārambhaka tvam dravyam prati samavāyi kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sa ca nijā śaktiḥ eva sparśavat tvam sparśa samavāyaḥ trayāṇām pratyakṣa tva rūpavat tva drava tvāni trayāṇām kṣiti udaka tejasām pratyakṣa tvam indriya ja jñāna pratibhāsamāna tā na tu mahatva ādi kāraṇa yogaḥ rūpavat tvam iti asya punar ukta tva prasaṅgāt nanu ātmanaḥ api pratyakṣa tvam asti satyam bāhya indriya apekṣayā trayāṇām pratyakṣa tvam iti uktam tathā rūpavat tvam rūpa samavāyaḥ dravya tvam dravāṇām bhāvaḥ drava tvam tañca guṇa antaram 
NK_41.1–41.5	 dvayoḥ guru tvam rasavat tvañca bhūtātmanām vaiśeṣika guṇavat tvam kṣiti udaka ātmanām caturdaśa guṇavat tvam ākāśa ātmanām kṣaṇika eka deśa vṛtti viśeṣa guṇavat tvam dvayoḥ guru tvam dvayoḥ pṛthivī udakayoḥ guru tvad nāma guṇa antaram tasya bhāvāt pṛthivyām udake ca guru śabda niveśaḥ rasavat tvañca rasa samavāyaḥ na kevalam tayoḥ guru tvam rasavat tvañca iti ca arthaḥ 
NK_41.6–41.8	 bhūtātmanām vaiśeṣika guṇavat tvam bhūtānām pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyu nabhasām ātmanām ca vaiśeṣika guṇa yogaḥ viśeṣaḥ vyavacchedaḥ viśeṣāya sva āśrayasya itarebhyaḥ vyavacchedāya prabhavanti iti vaiśeṣikāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ tad yogaḥ bhūtātmanām kṣiti udaka ātmanām caturdaśa guṇavat tvam kṣiteḥ udakasya ātmanām caturdaśa guṇa yogaḥ ākāśa ātmanān ca kṣaṇika eka deśa vṛttibhiḥ viśeṣa guṇaiḥ saha yogaḥ vidyate iti āha ākāśa ātmanām iti viśeṣa guṇāḥ pṛthivī ādīnām api tad nivṛtti atham eka deśa vṛtti grahaṇam ye ca te ākāśa ātmanām avyāpya vṛttayaḥ viśeṣa guṇāḥ teṣām āśutara vināśi tvan ca svarūpam asti iti kṣaṇika saṅkīrttanam kutam 
NK_42.1–42.3	 diś kālayoḥ pañca guṇavat tvam sarva utpattimatām nimitta kāraṇa tvan ca saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ pañca eva guṇa ādi śi kāle ca varttante iti āha diś kālayoḥ iti na kevalam anayoḥ pañca guṇavat tvam sādharmyam sarva utpattimatām nimitta kāraṇa tvan ca sādharmyam nanu diś kālau sarveṣām utpattimatām nimittam iti kutas etat pratyetavyam yadi sannidhi mātreṇa ākāśasya api kāraṇa tvam syāt atha tad vyapadeśāt saḥ api anaikāntikaḥ gṛhe jātaḥ goṣṭhe jātaḥ iti animitte api darśanāt atra ucyate asti tāvat tantu ādi pratiniyamāt paṭa ādi utpatti vat deśa viśeṣa niyamāt kāla viśeṣa niyamāt ca sarveṣām utpattiḥ yadi deśa kāla viśeṣau api na kāraṇam yatra kvacana hetuvaḥ kāryyam kuryyuḥ aviśeṣāt sarvadā sarvatra kārāṇa abhāvāt kāryya anutpattiḥ iti ced yatra deśe kāle ca kāraṇāni bhavanti tatra teṣām janaka tvam na anyatra iti abhyupetam viśiṣṭa deśa kālayoḥ aṅga tvam kāryya jananāya tayoḥ kāraṇaiḥ apekṣaṇīya tvāt idam eva ca deśasya kālasya ca nimitta tvam yat ekatra kāryya utpattiḥ anyatra anutpattiḥ iti 
NK_43.1–43.2	 kṣiti tejasoḥ naimittika drava tva yogaḥ kṣiti tejasoḥ naimittika drava tva yogaḥ nimittāt upajātam naimittikam naimitti kañca tat drava tvan ca iti naimittika drava tvam tena saha kṣiti tejasoḥ yogaḥ pārthivasya sarpiḥ ādeḥ taijasasya ca suvarṇa rajata ādeḥ agni saṃyogena vilayanāt guru tva vat pārthivam eva drava tvam dahyamāneṣu suvarṇa ādiṣu saṃyukta samavāyāt pratīyate iti kecid na pārthiva drava tvasya atyanta agni saṃyogena bhasmībhāva upalabdheḥ asya ca tad abhāvāt atas eva suvarṇa ādikam api pārthivam eva iti kasyacid pravādaḥ api pratyuktaḥ pārthiva tve sati sarpiḥ ādi vat atyanta vahni saṃyogena dravarva uccheda prasaṅgāt 
NK_43.3	 yat api idam uktam pārthivam suvarṇa ādikam saṃsiddhi ka drava tva abhāve sati guru tva adhikaraṇa tvāt loṣṭa ādi vat tat api asāram kintatra guru tvasya upalabdhiḥ tat guṇa tvāt uta anya guṇa tve api ghṛta ādiṣu api sneha vat sva āśraya pratyāsatti nimittāt iti saṃśayasya anivṛtteḥ yat api sādhana antaram para prakāśyamāna tvāt iti tat api anudbhūta rūpavat tvena api upapatteḥ asapdhanam diś mātram asmābhiḥ upadiṣṭam 
NK_44.1–44.3^1	 evam sarvatra sādharmyam viparyyayāt vaidharmyan ca vācyam iti anena eva nyapyena sarvatra padārtheṣu anyat api sādharmyam svayam vācyam viparyyayāt itara vyāvṛtteḥ vaidharmyam ca vācyam iti śiṣyān āha evam iti anuddiṣṭeṣu padārtheṣu na teṣām lakṣaṇāni pravarttante nirviṣaya tvāt alakṣiteṣu ca tattva prati iti abhāvaḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt atas padārtha vyutpādanāya pravṛttasya śāstrasya ubhayathā pravṛttiḥ uddeśaḥ lakṣaṇan ca parūkṣāya astu antyamaḥ yatra abhihite lakṣaṇe pravāda antara vyākṣepāt tattva niścayaḥ na bhavati tatra para pakṣa vyudāsa artham parīkṣā vidhiḥ adhikriyate yatra tu lakṣaṇa abhidhāna sāmarthyāt eva tattva niścayaḥ syāt tatra ayam vyarthaḥ na arthyate yaḥ api hi trividhām śāstrasya pravṛttim icchati tasya api prayojana ādīnām na asti parīkṣā tat kasya hetoḥ lakṣaṇa mātrāt eva te pratīyante iti 
NK_44.3^2	 evan ced artha prati iti anurodhāt śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ na tridhā eva iti nāmadheyena padārthānām abhidhānam uddeśaḥ uddiṣṭasya sva para jātīya vyāvarttakaḥ dharmaḥ lakṣaṇam lakṣitasya yathālakṣaṇam vicāraḥ parīkṣā uddiṣṭa vibhāgaḥ tu na vidha antaram uddeśa lakṣaṇena eva saṃgṛhīta tvāt tathā api pṛthak ucyeta etāni eva iti niyama artham viśeṣa lakṣaṇa pravṛtti arthan ca vibhakteṣu padārtheṣu teṣām viśeṣa lakṣaṇāni bhavanti anyathā tāni nirviṣayāṇi syuḥ tatra dravyāṇi dravya guṇa karma iti uddiṣṭāni dravyāṇi pṛthivī aptejaḥ iti vibhaktāni samprati teṣām viśeṣa lakṣaṇa artham prakaraṇam ārabhyate 
NK_45.1–45.5	 iha idānīm ekaikaśas vaidharmyam ucyate pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt pṛthivī rūpa rasa gandha sparśa saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva guru tva drava tva saṃkāravatī ete ca guṇa viniveśa adhikāre rūpa ādayaḥ guṇa viśeṣāḥ siddhāḥ cākṣuṣa vacanāt sāta sagkhyā ādayaḥ patana upadeśāt guru tvam iha idānīm iti pūrvam dvayoḥ bahūnām paraspara apekṣayā vaidharmyam uktam iha vakṣyamāṇe prakaraṇe samprati ekaikasya dravyasya vyāvarttakaḥ dharmaḥ kathyate ekaikaśas iti śaspratyaya antāt vīpsā atyanta bahu vyāpti pradarśana arthāḥ 
NK_45.6^1	 uddeśa krameṇa pṛthivyaḥ prathamam vaidharmyam āha pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt pṛthivī iti yaḥ hi pṛthivīm svarūpataḥ jāman api kutas cit vyāmohāt pṛthivī iti na vyavaharati tam prati viparyaya sambandha avyabhicāreṇa vyavahāra sādhana artham asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ kathyate pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt pṛthivī iti iyam pṛthivī iti vyavahartavyā pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt yat punar pṛthivī iti na vyavahriyate na tat pṛthivī tvena abhisambaddham yathā bādikam na ca iyam pṛthivī tvena nābhi sambaddhā tasmāt pṛthivī iti vyavahartavyā iti yaḥ vā pṛthivī iti loke śṛṇoti na jānāti ca tasyāḥ svarūpam kīdṛś iti tam prati tasyāḥ sva para jātīya vyāvṛtta svarūpa pratipādana artham asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ kathyate yā loke pṛthivī iti vyapadiśyate sā pṛthivī pṛthivī tva abhisambandhāt 
NK_45.6^2	 yathā āhodyota karaḥ samāna asamāna jātīya vyavacchedaḥ lakṣaṇa arthaḥ etena etat api pratyuktam yat uktam aparaiḥ prasiddhāḥ ced padārthāḥ na lakṣaṇīyāḥ aprasiddhāḥ natarāma śakya tvāt sva rūpeṇa avagatasya api vyavahāra viśeṣa pratipādana artham sāmānyena prasiddhasya viśeṣa avagama arthan ca lakṣaṇasya pravṛtteḥ nanu evam sati a navasthā lakṣya vat lakṣaṇasya api anyatas lakṣaṇīya tvāt iti ced na apratītau lakṣaṇasya apekṣi tvāt sarvatra ca apratītya bhāvāt tathā hi śirasā pādena gavām anubadhnanti vidvāṃsaḥ na punar etau api anyatas samīkṣante yaḥ tu sarvathā eva apratipannaḥ na tam pratyupadeśaḥ tasya bāla mūka ādi vat anadhikārāt 
NK_45.7–45.8	 gandhasacarita caturdaśa guṇavat tvam api pṛthivyāḥ itarebhyaḥ vaidharmyam iti pratipādayan= āha rūrasagandhā iti atra dvandva anantaram matuppratyaya yogāt pratyekam rūpa ādīnām pṛthivyā saha sambandhaḥ labhyate sūtrakārasya api ete guṇāḥ pṛthivyām abhimatāḥ iti āha ete ca iti guṇānām viniveśaḥ dravyeṣu vṛttiḥ sā pratipādya tvena adhikriyate asmin iti guṇa viniveśa adhikāraḥ dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ tasmin rūpa rasa gandha sparśāḥ pṛthivyām siddhaḥ sūtrakāreṇa pratipāditāḥ rūpa rasa gandha sparśavatī pṛthivī iti cākṣuṣa vacanāt sapta saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ saṅkhyā parimāṇāni pṛthaktvam saṃyoga vibhāgau paratva aparatve karma ca rūpi dravya samavāyāt cakṣuṣāṇi iti cākṣuṣa vacanāt rūpavatyām pṛthivyām saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ sapta siddhāḥ yadi te rūpa dravyeṣu na santi tad samavāyena teṣām pratyakṣa tvam sūtrakāreṇa na uktam syāt iti arthaḥ patana upadeśāt guru tvam iti saṃyoga vega prayatna abhāve guru tvāt patanam iti upadeśāt sūtrakāreṇa patana sambandhinyām pṛthivyām guru tvam asti iti arthāt kathitam vyadhikaraṇasya akaraṇa tvāt 
NK_46.1–46.2	 adbhiḥ sāmānya vacanāt drava tvam uttara karma vacanāt saṃskāraḥ iti kṣitau eva gandhaḥ rūpam aneka prakāram śukla ādi rasaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ madhura ādiḥ gandhaḥ dvividhaḥ surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ ca sparśaḥ aanuṣṇa aśīta tve sati pāka jaḥ adbhiḥ sāmānya vacanāt drava tvam sarpiḥ jatu madhūcchiṣṭānām pārthivānām agni saṃyogāt srava tvam adbhiḥ sāmānyam iti vacanāt pṛthivyām naimittikam drava tvam astiti uktam madhūcchiṣṭa śabdena sikthasi abhidhānam 
NK_46.3–46.4	 uttara karma vacanāt saṃskāraḥ iti nodanāt ādyam iṣoḥ karma tad karma kāritāt ca saṃskārāt tathā uttaram uttaran ca iti sūtrakāreṇa iṣau pārthiva dravye karma hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ iti darśayatā pṛthivyām vegaḥ asti iti jñāpitam avidyamānasya ahetu tvāt yathā ca ekaḥ eva saṃskāraḥ āpatanāt tathā upapādayiṣyāmaḥ kṣitau eva gandhaḥ ayam asya arthaḥ kevalaḥ eva ayam asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ iti sugandhi salilam sugandhiḥ samīraṇaḥ iti pratyayāt dravya antare api gandhaḥ asti iti ced na pārthiva dravya samavāyena tad guṇa upalabdheḥ katham eṣa niśśyaḥ iti ced tat abhāve anupalambhāt 
NK_47.1^1	 yadi api rūpam trayāṇam samānam tathā api avāntara bheda apekṣayā tat api pṛthivyāḥ eva vaidharmyam iti āha rūpam aneka prakārakam iti atra api kṣitau= eva iti anusandhānīyam śukla pīta ādi anekavidham rūpam kṣitau eva na anyatra iti arthaḥ ekasyām pṛthivī tva jātau nānā rūpāṇi vyakti bhedena samavayanti kvacid ekasyām api vyaktau= aneka prakāra rūpa samāveśaḥ yatra nānāvidha rūpa sambandhibhiḥ avayavaiḥ avayavi ārabhyate katham etat iti ced ucyate yathā avayavaiḥ avaya vi ārabdhaḥ tathā avayava rūpaiḥ avayavini rūpam ārabdhavyam avayaveṣu ca na śuklam eva rūpam asti na api śyāmam eva kintu śyāma śukla harita ādīni 
NK_47.1^2	 na ca teṣām eva rūpam eva ārabhate na aparāṇi iti asti niyamaḥ pratyekam anyatra sarveṣām api sāmarthya darśanāt na ca parasparam virodhena sarvāṇi api na ārabhantā iva iti yuktam citra rūpasya avayavinaḥ pratīteḥ a rūpasya dravyasya pratyakṣa tva abhāvāt ca na ca avayava rūpāṇi samuccitāni atra citra dhiyā pratīyante taiḥ eva avayavī pratyakṣaḥ iti kalpanāyām anyatra api tathā abhāva prasaṅgena avayavi rūpa uccheda prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt sambhūya taiḥ ārabhyate tat ca ārabhyamāṇām vividha kāraṇa svabhāva anugamāt śyāma śukla harita ātmakam eva syāt citram iti ca vyapad iśyate virodhāt ekam aneka svabhāvam ayuktam iti ced 
NK_47.1^3	 tathā ca prāvāduka pravādaḥ ekañca citrañcā iti etat tat ca citrataram tatas iti kaḥ virodhaḥ nīla ādīnām na tāvat itaretara abhāva ātmakaḥ bhāva svabhāva anugamāt anyonya saṃśrayāt teḥ ca svarūpa anya tvam virodhaḥ iti ced satyam asti eva tathā api citra ātmanaḥ rūpasya na ayukta tā vicitra kāraṇa sāmarthya bhāvinaḥ tasya sarva loka prasiddhena pratyakṣeṇa evaa upapādita tvāt acitre pārśve paṭasi eva tad āśrayasya citra rūpasya grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tasya ekatvāt iti ced na anvaya vyatirekābhyām samadhigata sāma arthyasya avayava nānā rūpa darśanasya api citra rūpa grahaṇa hetu tvāt tasya ca pārśva antare abhāvāt 
NK_47.1^4	 nanu evam tarhi nānā rūpaiḥ dvi aṇukaiḥ ārabdhe dravye na citra rūpa grahaṇam tat avayava rūpa grahaṇa abhāvāt kaḥ nam āha na tathā iti na hi parama sūkṣmasya vastunaḥ rūpam vivicya gṛhyate yasya tu vivicya gṛhyate tasya avayava rūpāṇi api gṛhyante yaḥ tu avyāpakāni bahūni citra rūpāṇi iti manyate tasya nīla pītābhyām ārabdham dvi tantuke rūpa anutpattiḥ ekaikasya avayava rūpasya anārambhaka tvāt atha matam tatra ābhābhyām ekam citram rūpam ārabhyate tat ānyatra api tathā syāt aviśeṣāt vivāda adhyāsitam citra dravyam eka rūpa dravya sambandhi dravya tvāt itara dravya vat tad gatam rūpam ekam avayavi yavi rūpa tvāt itara avaya vi dravya rūpa vat 
NK_48.1	 rasaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ iti atra api pūrvavat vyākhyānam yat gandhasya bheda nirūpaṇam tat pāramparyeṇa pṛthivyāḥ api svarūpa kathanam iti abhiprāyeṇa āha gandhaḥ dvividhaḥ iti tat eva dvaividhyam darśayati surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ ca iti asurabhiḥ iti surabhi gandha virddham pratidravya ādi samavetam pratikūla saṃvadenīyam gandha antaram na tu tat abhāvā mātram vidhi rūpeṇa sa atiśaya tayā ca saṃvedanāt upekṣaṇīyaḥ tu gandhaḥ anudbhūta surabhya surabhiprabhedaḥ eva iti pṛthak na ucyate athavā saḥ api asurabhiḥ eva surabhi gandhapdanyaḥ a surabhiḥ iti vyutpādanāt 
NK_48.2	 yathābhūtaḥ sparśaḥ asyāḥ vaidharmyam tathā darśayati sparśaḥ asyāḥ iti pāka jaḥ aparśaḥ pṛthivyāḥ vaidharmyam tasya sva rūpa kathanam anuṣṇa aśītaḥ iti yadi api aparśavat pāka jau rūpa rasau api asyāḥ vaidharmyam tathā api rūpa rasayoḥ pāka ja tvān abhidhānam anyathā api tayaḥ vaidharmyasya sambhavāt vaidharmya mātrasya eva pratipādanasya eva vivakṣita tvāt apratīyamāna pākeṣu stambha ādiṣu sparśasya pākaja tvam anumānāt stambha ādiṣu aparśaḥ pāka jaḥ pārthiva sparśa tvāt ghaṭa ādi sparśa vat ghaṭa ādi sparśasya api pākaja svam eka indriya grāhya tve sati tad guṇa tvāt tad gata rūpavat 
NK_49.1–49.3^1^1	 sā ca dvividhāḥ nityā ca anityā ca paramāṇu lakṣaṇā nityāḥ kāryya lakṣaṇā tu anityāḥ sā ca sthairyī ādi ava yavasanniveśa viśiṣṭā apara jāti bahutva upetā śayana āsana ādi aneka upakāra kārī ca avāntara bheda nirūpaṇa artham āha nityā ca anityā ca iti prakāra antara abhāva saṃsūcana arthau caśabdau kā nityā kā ca anitya iti āha paramāṇu lakṣaṇā nityā kārya lakṣaṇā tu anityā iti ubhayatra api lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ svabhāva arthaḥ paramāṇu svabhāvāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ sattve kim pramāṇam anumānam aṇu parimāṇa tāratamyam kvacid viśrāntam parimāṇa tāratamya tvāt mahat parimāṇa tāratamya vat yatra idam viśrāntam yatas param aṇuḥ nna asti saḥ paramāṇuḥ 
NK_49.1–49.3^1^2	 atas eva nityaḥ dravya tve satya nava yava tvāt ākāśa vat atha ayam sa avayavaḥ na tarhi paramāṇuḥ kāryya parimāṇa apekṣayā tad avayava parimāṇasya loke alpī alpīyaḥ tu apratīteḥ yaḥ ca tasya avayavaḥ saḥ paramāṇuḥ bhaviṣyati atha saḥ api na bhavati avayava antara sadbhāvāt evam tarhi anavasthā tatas ca avayavinām alpataratama ādi bhāvaḥ na syāt sarveṣām ananta kāraṇa janya tva aviśeṣeṇa parimāṇa prakarṣā prakarṣa hetvoḥ kāraṇa saṅkhyā bhūyaḥ tvayoḥ asambhavāt asti tāvat ayam parimāṇa bhedaḥ tasmāt aṇu parimāṇam kvacid niratiśayam iti siddhaḥ nityaḥ paramāṇu 
NK_49.3^2	 sa ca ekaḥ na ārambhakāḥ ekasya nityasya ca ārambhaka tve kāryyasya satata utpattiḥ syāt apekṣaṇīya abhāvāt avināśi tvan ca prasajyeta āśraya vināśasya avayavi bhāgasya ca vināhetoḥ abhavāt trayāṇām api ārambhaka tvam ayuktam iha mahat kāryya dravyasya utpattau sva parimāṇa apekṣayā alpa parimāṇasya kāryya dravyasya eva sāmarthya darśanāt tri aṇukam kāryya dravyeṇa eva janyate mahat parimāṇa tvāt ghaṭa vat evam trayāṇam ekasya ca ārambhaka tve pratikṣipte dvābhyām eva paramāṇubhyām ārabhyate yat tat dvi aṇukam iti siddham 
NK_49.3^3	 dvi aṇukaiḥ bahubhiḥ ārabhyate iti api niyamaḥ na dvābhyām tasya aṇu parimāṇa utpattau kāraṇa sadbhāvena aṇutva utpattau= ārambha vaiyarthyāt bahuṣu tu aniyamaḥ kadācid tribhiḥ āramhyate iti tri aṇukam iti ucyate kadācid ca turbhiḥ ārabhyate kadācid pañcabhiḥ iti yatheṣṭam kalpanā na ca kāryyasya vyartha tā yathā yathā kāraṇa saṅkhyā bāhulyam tathā tathā mahat parimāṇa tāratamyasya upalambhāt na ca evam sati dvi aṇukāṇm eva ghaṭa ārambhaka tva prasaktiḥ ghaṭasya bhaṅge alpataratama ādi bhāga darśanena tathā eva ārabhaka kalpanāt tat evam dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kriyate kāryya lakṣaṇā pṛthivī 
NK_49.4	 sā ca anityā kāraṇa vibhāgasya āśraya vināśasya ca hetoḥ sambhavāt kāryya lakṣaṇāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ anitya tvena saha dharma antaram samuccinvan āha sā ca iti atha airyyam niviḍa tvam ādi śabdāt praśithila tva ādi parigrahaḥ avayavānām sanniveśaḥ avayava saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ sthairyī ādayaḥ ca te avayava sanniveśāḥ ca taiḥ viśiṣṭāḥ apara jāti bahutva upetā go tva śva tva ādi jāti bhūyaḥ tu ayuktā iti arthaḥ paramāṇu ādiṣu apara jāve api adṛṣṭa vaśāt tathā tathā teṣām vyūhaḥ yathā yathā tad ārabdheṣu apara jātayaḥ vyajyante nanu adṛṣṭa kāri tā sarva bhāvānām sṛṣṭiḥ kāryya lakṣaṇā pṛthivī kāmartha kriyām puruṣasya janayati yena iyam adṛṣṭena kriyate iti atas āha śayana āsana iti śayana āsana ādayaḥ anekaḥ upakārāḥ tad kāriṇī kārya lakṣaṇa iti 
NK_50.1	 trividham ca asyāḥ kāryyam śarīra indriya viṣaya saṃjñakam śarīram dvividham yoni jam ayonijan ca tatra ayonijam anapekṣya śukra śoṇitam deva ṛṣīṇām śarīram dharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ jāyate kṣudra jantūnām yātanā śarīrāṇi adharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ jāyante śukra śoṇita sannipāta jam yoni jam tat dvividham jarāyu ja m aṇḍa jañca mānuṣa paśu mṛgāṇām jarāyu jam pakṣi sarīsṛpāṇām aṇḍa jam 
NK_50.2^1	 kāryya antaram tu asyāḥ samuccinoti trividham ca iti kāryatraividhyam eva darśayati trividham ca iti kāryatraividhyam eva darśayati śarīra ityādi śarīram indriyam viṣayaḥ iti saṃjñā yasya kāryasya tat tathā bhoktuḥ bhoga āyatanam śarīram mṛta śarīre tad yogya tvāt tad vyapadeśaḥ śrī ḥ āśrayam jñātuḥ aparokṣa pratīti sādhanam dravyam indriyam śarīra indriya vyatiriktam ātma upabhoga sādhanam dravyam viṣayaḥ śarīra bhedam kathayati yoni jam ayonijan ca iti śukra śoṇita sannipātaḥ yoniḥ tasmāt jātam yoni jam tad viparītam ayonijam tat eva darśapati tatra ayonijam iti tayoḥ yonija ayoni jayoḥ madhye ayonijam śarīram śukra śoṇitam anapekṣya jāyate keṣām iti atas āha deva ṛṣīṇām iti devān āñcaḥ ṛṣīṇāñca iti arthaḥ anvaya vyatireka avadhārita kāraṇa bhāvasya śukra śoṇitasyāḥ bhāve katham śarīrasya utpattiḥ iti atas āha dharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ iti viśiṣyate iti viśeṣaḥ dharmaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ dharma viśeṣḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ tad sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ iti 
NK_50.2^2	 ayam abhisandhiḥ śarīra ārambhe paramāṇavaḥ eva kāraṇam na tu śukra śoṇita sannipātaḥ kriyā vibhāga ādi nyāyena tayoḥ vināśe sati utpanna pāka jaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ ārambhāt na ca śukra śoṇita paramāṇūnām itara paramāṇūnām ca kaścid viśeṣaḥ pārthiva tva aviśeṣāt atra api kāryye jāti niyamasya adṛṣṭaḥ eva hetuḥ evan ced dharma viśeṣa anugṛhītebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ ayonija śrīra utpattiḥ nna anupapannāḥ nanu dṛṣṭaḥ tāvat sarvatra śarīra utpattau śukra śoṇitayoḥ pūrva kālatā niyamaḥ tena yathā grāva unmajjanābhyupagamaḥ tad sadṛśa grāva antara nimajjana grāhaka pramāṇa antara virodhāt anupapannaḥ tadvat ayonija śarīra abhyupagamaḥ api na evam śukra ādi nirapekṣasya api śalabha ādi śarīrasya darśanāt viśiṣṭa saṃsthānasya śarīrasya śukra ādi pūrva tā avagata iti ced satyam tathā api na niyama siddhiḥ kim adṛṣṭa viśeṣa abhāvāt asmad ādi śarīrasya śukra ādi pūrva tā kim vā viśiṣṭa saṃsthāna mātra anubandha kṛtā iti saṃdehāt etena bādhaka anumānam api paryyudaḥ tam tasya vyāpti saṃdehāt yat ca atra vaktavyam tad yogi pratyakṣa nirūpaṇa avasare vakṣyāmaḥ 
NK_50.3^1	 adharma viśeṣeṇa api ayonijam śarīram bhavati iti āha kṣudra jantūnām iti kṣudra jantavaḥ daṃśa maśaka ādayaḥ teṣām yātanā duḥkham iti yāvat tad artham śarīram yātanā śarīram tad adharma viśeṣa sahitebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ jāyate idantu iha loka prasiddham eva yoni jam śarīram āha śukra śoṇita sannipāta jam iti śukrañca śoṇitañca tayoḥ sannipātaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ tasmāt jātam yoni jam iti ucyate 
NK_50.3^2	 pituḥ śukram mātuḥ śoṇitam tayoḥ sannipāta anantaram jaṭhara analambandha āt chukra śoṇita ārambhakeṣu parama aṇuṣu kriyā vibhāga ādi nyāyena śukra śoṇita nivṛttau agni saṃyogāt paramāṇuṣu pūrvarūpa ādi vināśe sati samāna guṇa antara utpattau dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kalala śarīra utpattiḥ tatra antaḥkaraṇa praveśaḥ na tu śukra śoṇita avasthāyām śarīra āśraya tvāt manasaḥ tatra mātuḥ āhāra rasaḥ mātrayā saṃkrāmati adṛṣṭa vaśāt tatra punar jaṭhara anala sambandhāt kalala ārambhaka paramāṇuṣu kriyā vibhāga ādi nyāyena kalala śarīre naṣṭe samutpanna pāka jaiḥ kalala ārambhaka paramāṇubhiḥ adṛṣṭa vaśāt upajāta kriyaiḥ āhāra paramāṇubhiḥ samāna guṇaiḥ saha sambhūya śarīra antaram ārambhyate iti eṣā kalpanā śarīre pratyaham draṣṭavyā 
NK_50.3^3	 śrī ḥ abhede kim pramāṇam parimāṇa bhedaḥ su alpa parimāṇa avacchinne āśraye mahat parimāṇasya parisamāpti abhāvāt avasthā antara āpannam śarīram tad āśrayaḥ bhavati iti ced avasthā antaram āhāra avayava sahakāriṇaḥ śarīra avayavāḥ ārabheran śarīram va tad saha kṛtam ubhayathā api paṭa ādiṣu tantu ādi vat ante hīna adhika parimāṇa vat aneka śarīra upalambhaḥ syāt na ca evam tasmāt pūrvam pranaṣṭam aparañca śarīram upajātam vivāda adhyāsite parimāṇe bhinna āśraye hīna adhika parimāṇa tvāt ghaṭa śarāva parimāṇa vat vivāda adhyāsitam parimāṇam āśraya vināśāt eva vinaśyati parimāṇa tvāt mudgara abhihata vinaṣṭa parimāṇa vat pratyabhijñānāt śarīra eka tva siddhiḥ iti ced na tasya sādṛśya viṣaya tvena api upapatteḥ vyaktīnām avyavadhāna utpādanena antara agrahaṇasya ātyantika sādṛśyasya ca bhrānti hetoḥ sarvadā sambhave jvālā ādi vyakti vat na idam tat iti bādhaka anudaye api yukti dvāreṇa bādhaka sambhavāt 
NK_50.4	 tasya prakāram darśayati dvividham iti dve vidhe prakārau yasya tat dvividham iti vyākhyā jarāyuḥ iti garbhāśayasya abhidhānam tena veṣṭitam jāyate iti jarāyu jam aṇḍam bimbam tena veṣṭitam jāyate yat tat aṇḍa jam keṣām jarāyu jam keṣām ca aṇḍa jam iti atra āha mānuṣa iti ādi mānuṣāḥ asmad ādayaḥ paśavaḥ chāgāḥ agnīṣomīyam paśum ālabheta saptadaśa prājāpatyān paśūn ālabhetaḥ iti darśanāt mṛgāḥ kṛṣṇasāra ādayaḥ teṣām jarāyu jam śarīram idan ca upalakṣām api catuṣpadām jarāyuja tvāt pakṣiṇaḥ prasiddhāḥ sarīsṛpāḥ sarpāḥ teṣām aṇḍa jam śrīram etat api na niyama artham anyeṣām api matsya ādīnām aṇḍaja tvāt 
NK_51.1–51.2^1	 indriyam gandha vyañjakam sarva prāṇinām jala ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārabdham ghrāṇam indriya svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham āha indriyam iti sarva prāṇinām gandha vyañjakam gandha upalambhakam yat indriyam tat pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārabdham etāvatā niyamaḥ na labhyate yat etat eva gandham abhivyanakti na anyat pārthivam dravyam tat artham āha jala ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ārabdham ghrāṇam jala ādibhiḥ anabhibhūtaiḥ apratihata sāmarthyaiḥ avayavaiḥ adṛṣṭa vaśāditara vilakṣaṇam ārabdham etat atas viśiṣṭa utpādāt idam eva gandha abhivyakti samartham na anyat iti arthaḥ ghrāṇam iti tasya saṃjñā 
NK_51.2^2	 ātmā jighrti gandham upādatte anena iti kṛtvā tat sadbhāve gandha upalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam kriyāyāḥ karaṇa sādhya tvāt cakṣuḥ ādi vyāpāre ca tasyāḥ anutpādāt pārthiva tve api rūpa ādīṣu madhye gandhasya eva abhivyañjaka tvam pramāṇam kuṅkuma gangha abhivyañjaka ghṛta vat yathā ghṛtam sva gandha sahitam eva kuṅkuma gandham abhivyanakti tathā ghrāṇam api sva gandha sahitam eva indriyam atas na sva gandhasya grāhakam tena eva tasya agrahaṇāt yathā ghrāṇasya tathā rasana cakṣuḥ tvac indriyāṇām api vakṣyamāṇena dṛṣṭānta balena rūpa rasa sparśa saha kṛtānām eva indriya tva anumānāt na sva guṇa grahaṇam śrotrantu śabda guṇam indriyam atas tena eva śabda upalambhaḥ 
NK_52.1–52.2^1	 viṣayaḥ tu dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdhaḥ trividhaḥ mṛd pāṣāṇa sthāvara lakṣaṇaḥ tatra bhū pradeśāḥ prākāra iṣṭaka ādayaḥ mṛd prakārāḥ pāṣāṇāḥ upala maṇi vajra ādayaḥ sthāvarāḥ tṛṇa oṣadhi vṛkṣa gulma latā avatāna vanaspatayaḥ iti śarīra indriya āghyām viṣayasya sva rūpa viśeṣam atu aśabdena darśayan bhedam darśayati viṣayaḥ tu iti dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdhaḥ iti sādhāraṇa rūpa anuvādaḥ mṛd pāṣāṇa sthāvara lakṣaṇaḥ iti mṛd pāṣāṇa sthāvara ādi svabhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ teṣām madhye mṛdam sva rūpeṇa nirddhārayan= āha tatra iti tatra bhū pradeśāḥ bhū gola kalpa pradeśāh 
NK_52.1–52.2^2	 sthala nimna ādayaḥ prākāra iṣṭaka ādayaḥ sarve te mṛd prakārāḥ mṛd prabhedāḥ iti arthaḥ pāṣāṇabhedam āha pāṣāṇāḥ iti upalāḥ śilāhaḥ maṇayaḥ sūryya kānta ādayaḥ vajraḥ aśaniḥ hīrāḥ ca tṛṇa mulapādaḥ auṣadhayaḥ phala pāka antāḥ godhūma ādayaḥ ye sa puṣpa phalāḥ te vṛkṣāḥ kovidāra prabhṛtayaḥ gulamāḥ sa stūpāḥ vaṃśa ikṣu prabhṛtayaḥ latā prasiddhā eva avatanvantī satyavatānāḥ viṭapāḥ ketakī bījapūra ādayaḥ ye vinā puṣpam phalanti te vanaspatayaḥ udumbara ādayaḥ nanu svi icchā adhīna ceṣṭā virahaḥ sthāvara tvam tat tu mṛd pāṣāṇayoḥ api asti satyam tayoḥ rūpa antarasya api sambhavāt anena rūpeṇa abhidhānam na kṛtam 
NK_53.1–53.5^1	 aptvā abhisambandhāt āpaḥ rūpa rasa sparśa drava tva sneha saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva guru tva saṃskāravatyaḥ pūrvavat eṣām siddhiḥ śukla madhura śītāḥ eva rūpa rasa sparśāḥ apām lakṣaṇa artham āha aptvā abhisambandhāt āpaḥ iti atra api vyavahāra sādhanam samāna asamāna jātīya vyavacchedaḥ vā lakṣaṇa arthaḥ sarvam pūrvavat idantu iha vaktavyam svayam pratyakṣa adhigata padārtha bhedaḥ parasya lakṣaṇena pratipādayet apratipannasya apratipādaka tvāt bhedaḥ ca padārthānām anyonya abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ sa ca yasya abhāvaḥ yatra ca abhāvaḥ tad ubhaya grahaṇena gṛhyate anyathā tad svarūpa pratiniyamena niṣedha anupapattiḥ gauḥ aśvaḥ na bhavati iti tatra kim saṅkīrṇa svabhāvayoḥ ubhayoḥ grahaṇāt anyonya abhāva grahaṇam paraspara viviktayoḥ vā saṅkīrṇa grahaṇe tāvat ayam ayam na bhavati iti pratīti asambhavaḥ eva paraspara viviktayoḥ grahaṇāt abhāva pratītau= itaretara āśraya tvam viviktayoḥ grahaṇe satyabhāva grahaṇam abhāva grahaṇe ca vivikta grahaṇam abhāvaḥ eva vivekaḥ yatas 
NK_53.5^2	 atra ucyate bhinnayoḥ itaretarābhāvaḥ na tu itaretarābhāvaḥ bhedaḥ yat etat vastunaḥ prātyātmikam svarūpam saḥ eva bhedaḥ tat ca apara darśana anapekṣam indriya sannikarṣa mātrāt eva pratīyamānam pratyekam vilakṣaṇam eva saṃvedyate tathā hi gavārthī na aśva darśanāt pravarttate go śabdañca na smarati tatra aśve gavi ca svena svena ātmanā gṛhīte tad svarūpa niyamena anyonya abhāva pratītiḥ na anupapannāḥ na ca evam sati vācyam svarūpa bhedaḥ eva astu kim anyonya abhāvena iti tasya api pratiṣedha viṣayasya saṃvedanāt na kevalam ap tvam apām vaidharmyam sneha sahacaritam caturdaśa guṇavat tvam api itarebhyaḥ vaidharmyam iti pratipādayan= āha rūpa rasa iti atra dvandva anantaram amatup a pratyayaḥ karaṇīyaḥ 
NK_53.6	 pūrvavat eṣām siddhiḥ yathā pūrvam pṛthivyām sūtrakāra vacanāt eṣām rūpa ādīnām guṇānām siddhiḥ pratipattiḥ tathā apsu api iti arthaḥ tathā ca sūtram rūpa rasa sparśavatyaḥ āpaḥ dravāḥ snigdhāḥ ca iti saṅkhyā ādi pratipādakantu sādhāraṇam eva sūtram vaidharmya nirūpaṇa avasare pṛthivī ādi sādhāraṇānām rūpa ādīnām abhidhānam ayuktam iti āśaṅkya avāntara bhedena eṣām asādhāraṇa tvam pratipādayati śukla ityādi śuklam eva rūpam apām madhuraḥ eva rasaḥ śītaḥ eva sparśaḥ apsu rūpa antara pratītiḥ āśraya rūpa bhedāt katham etat iti ced tāsām eva uddhṛtya viyati vikṣiptānām dhava lima mātra pratītiḥ punar nipatitānām āśraya rūpa anuvidhānāt tāsu na madhuraḥ rasaḥ guḍa ādi vat apratibhāsanāt iti ced na kaṭu kaṣāya tikta lavaṇa amla vilakṣaṇasya rasasya saṃvedanāt guḍa ādi vat apratibhāsanantu mādhuryya atiśaya abhāvāt 
NK_54.1–54.3	 snehaḥ ambhasya iva sāṃsiddhi kañca drava tvam nirviśeṣaḥ eva snehaḥ apām vaidharmyam iti dhvanati snehaḥ ambhasya iva iti nanu ayam pṛthivyām api varttate yathā kṣīre taile sarpiṣi ca na sarvatra pāṣāṇa iṣṭakā śuka indhana ādiṣu asambhavāt yat tu kvacid kṣīra ādiṣu darśanam tad saṃyukta samavāyāt udaka gatasya eva yathā sāṃsiddhika drava tvasya kṣīra tailayoḥ svāśrasat nikarṣāt udaka dharma tvantu snehasya sarvatra tat anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt tathā ca anupadeśa prabhavānām taru tṛṇa ādīnām snigdha tā jāṅgala pradeśa prabhavānān ca rūkṣa tā tatra api satatam pariṣicyamāna mūlānām snigdha tvam tad virahiṇān ca tat na asti iti sāṃsiddhikan ca dravya tvam iti na kevalam snehaḥ avabhāva siddhan ca drava tvam ambhasya iva iti arthaḥ kṣīra tailayoḥ sva āśraya sannikarṣeṇa tad upalambhaḥ kvacid tayoḥ dhana tva upalambhāt 
NK_55.1–55.3	 tāḥ tu pūrvavat dvividhāḥ nitya aniti abhāvāt tāsām tu kāryyam trividham śarīra indriya viṣaya sañjñakam tatra śarīram ayonijam eva varuṇa loke pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt ca upabhoga samartham pṛthivyāḥ iva apām api avāntara bhedena dvaividhyam iti āha tāḥ tu iti paramāṇu svabhāvāḥ āpaḥ nityāḥ kāryya svabhāvāḥ tu anityāḥ kāryyan ca trividham atra api pūrvavat iti anaṣaṅgaḥ yathā pṛthivyāḥ śarīra indriya viṣaya saṃjñitam kāryyam trividham evam apām api iti 
NK_55.4	 tatra śarīram ayonijam eva pārthivam śarīram yoni jam ayonijan ca āpyam śarīram ayonijam eva iti viśeṣaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu māṇuṣam śarīram tāvat pārthivam gandha guṇa upalabdheḥ āpyam tu kva asti iti āha varuṇa lokaḥ iti idam śarīram apām āgamāt pratyetavyam drava tva eka svabhāva tvāt apām tadā ārabdham śarīram jala budbuda prāyam viśiṣṭa vyavahāra ayogyam katham upabhoga samartham syāt iti atas āha pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt upabhoga samartham pārthivānām avayavānām upaṣṭambhāt saṃyoga viśeṣāt āpyam śarīram upabhogāya samrtham syāt āpya śarīra utpattau pārthiva avayavāḥ nimitta kāraṇam teṣam saṃyogāt āpi a avayavānām drava tve pratiruddhe viśiṣṭam eva idam śarīram utpadyate na jala budbuda prāyam iti arthaḥ 
NK_55.5	 ye tu pañcabhūta samavāyi kāraṇam śarīram iti āsthiṣata teṣām agandham śarīram syāt kāraṇa gandhasya ekasya anārambhaka tvāt citra rūpa rasa sparśan ca prāpnoti kāraṇeṣu nānā rūparśa sambhavāt na ca evam dṛṣṭam tasmāt na pañcabhūta prakṛtikam bhū jala prakṛtikam api atas eva na syāt atas eva ca bhū jala anila prakṛtikam api na syāt bhū vāyu ākāśa prakṛtika tve aru upamarasam agandhan ca syāt bhū dahana anila prakṛtika tve ca agandhamarasam anala anila ākāśa prakṛtika tve ca agandhamara sama rūpam ca ityādi yathapsambhavam yojanīyam na ca pañcabhūta samavāyi kāraṇa tve śarīrasya ekatvam prāpnoti svabhāva bhedema bheda upapatteḥ mānuṣam śarīram pṛthivī ātmakam gandhavat tvāt paramaṇu lakṣaṇa pṛthivī vat udaka ādi dharma upalambhaḥ katham atra iti ced saṃyukta samavāyāt iti alam 
NK_56.1–56.3	 indriyam sarva prāṇinām rasa vyañjakam vijāti anabhibhūtaiḥ jala avayavaiḥ ārabdham rasanam viṣayaḥ tu sarit samudra hima karaka ādiḥ iti indriyam rasa vyañjakam sarva prāṇinām iti sarva prāṇinām rasa vyañjakam yat indriyam tad jala avayavaiḥ ārabdham tathā api kasmāt tat eva rasa vyañjakam syāt na anyat udaka dravyam iti āha vijāti anabhibhūtaiḥ iti vijātibhiḥ pārthiva avayavaiḥ ye anabhibhūtāḥ apratihata sāmarthyāḥ āpya avayavāḥ taiḥ itata dravya vilakṣaṇam ārabdham atas idam viśiṣṭa utpādāt rañjakam indriyam na dravya antaram tasya ittham utpatti abhāvāt iti arthaḥ etat ca nirama darśanāt eva kalpyate rasanā indriya sadbhāve rasa upalabdhar eva pramāṇam kriyāyāḥ karaṇa sādhya tvāt āpya tvam rūpa ādiṣu madhye rasasya eva abhivyañjaka tvāt mukha śoṣiṇām lālā ādi dravya vat viṣaya nirūpaṇa artham āha viṣayaḥ tu iti sarit samudrau hitam karakaḥ ghana upalam iti ādiḥ viṣayaḥ bhogya tvena bhoktuḥ bhoga sādhana tvāt
