NK_57.1–57.2	 tejaḥ tvā abhisambandhāt tejaḥ rūpa sparśa saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva drava tva saṃskāra vat pūrvavat eṣām siddhiḥ tatra śuklam bhāsvarañca rūpam uṣṇaḥ eva sparśaḥ tejaḥ tvā abhisambandhāt tejaḥ iti vyākhyānam pūrvavat tejaḥ tvam iva rūpa ādi ekādaśa guṇa yogaḥ api tasya vaidharmyam iti darśayati rūpa iti ādi pūrvavat eṣām siddhiḥ iti yathā sūtrakāra vacanāt rūpa ādīnām pṛthivyām siddhiḥ tathā tejasi api iti arthaḥ tathā ca sūtram tejaḥ rūpa sparśa vat saṅkhyā ādi pratipādakantu sādhāraṇam eva sūtram yādṛśam asya rūpam tat darśayati śuklam bhāsvarañca iti śuklam rūpam pṛthivī udakayoḥ api asti kintu na tat bhāsvaram sva para prakāśakam śuklam rūpam tejasi eva iti vaidharmyam yat tvasya lohitam kapilam vā rūpam kvacid pratīyate tat āśraya upādhi kṛtam nirāśrayasya sarvatra śukla tā mātra pratīteḥ yathā pradīpa prabhā maṇḍaladya saura candra ādi ālokasya ca uṣṇaḥ eva sparśaḥ iti pṛthivī udaka marutām anuṣṇa aśīta anuṣṇa aśīta sparśāḥ uṣṇaḥ eva tejasi sparśaḥ iti vaidharmyam 
NK_58.1–58.4	 tat api dvividham aṇu kāryya bhāvāt kāryyan ca śarīra ādi trayam śarīram ayonijam eva āditya loke pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt ca upabhoga samartham indriyam sarva prāṇinām rūpa vyañjaka m anya avayavān abhibhūtaiḥ tejaḥ avayavaiḥ ārabdham cakṣuḥ pṛthivī udaka vat tejasaḥ api dvaividhyam api śabdena sambhāvayan= āha tat api iti aṇu kārya bhāvāt kārya bhāvāt tejaḥ api dvividham iti kāryyan ca śarīra ādi trayam śarīram indriyam viṣayaḥ iti trayam tejasaḥ kāryyam śarīram ayonijam eva āditya loke nanu dahana ātma tvāt tejasam tadā ārabdham śarīram vahni puñja prāyam viśiṣṭa vyavahāra ayogya tvāt na upabhogāt tatra āha pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt ca iti pārthiva avayavānām nimitta bhūtānām upaṣṭambhāt saṃyoga viśeṣāt tejaḥ avayavāḥ upabhoga kṣamam viśiṣṭam eva śarīram ārabhante na vahni puñja prāyam iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NK_58.5	 indriyam sarva prāṇinām rūpa vyañjakam iti sarva prāṇinām rūpa vyañjakam yat indriyam tat tejaḥ avayavaiḥ ārabdham idam eva kutas rūpa vyañjakam indriyam syāt na anyat tejaḥ dravyam iti atra upapattiḥ anya avayavān abhibhūtaiḥ iti ye pārthiva udaka avayavaiḥ apratibaddha sāmarthyāḥ tejaḥ avayavāḥ taiḥ ārabdham cakṣuḥ atas idam viśiṣṭa utpādāt rūpa abhivyañjakam indriyam na anyāt tādṛśam tat utpadyate iti atra adṛṣṭam eva kāraṇam kāryya niyamaḥ eva pramāṇam taijasatvantu tasya rūpa ādiṣu madhye niyamena rūpasya abhivyañjaka tvāt pradīpa vat idam tu adṛṣṭa vaśāt anudbhūta rūpa sparśam tena na sva āśrayam dahati na api upalabhyate 
NK_59.1	 viṣaya sañjñakam caturvidham bhaumam divyam udaryyam ākarajan ca tatra bhaumam kāṣṭha indhana prabhavam ūrddhva jvalana svabhāvam pacana dahana svedana ādi samartham divyam ap indhanam saura vidyut ādi bhuktasya ahātasya rasa ādi pariṇām artham udaryyam ākāra jan ca suvarṇa ādi tatra saṃyukta samavāyāt rasa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti 
NK_59.2^1	 viṣaya sañjñakam caturvidham viṣayaḥ iti sañjñā yasya tat viṣaya sañjñakam tejaḥ kāryyam caturvidham cāturvidhyam eva darśayati bhaumam iti ādi tatra bhaumam iti tatra iti nirdhāraṇa arthaḥ bhūmau bhavam kāṣṭha indhana prabhavam kāṣṭha svabhāvam yat indhanam tasmāt prabhavati utpadyate nirāśrayasya anutpatteḥ kāṣṭha grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa artham tṛṇa tuṣa ādīnām api kāraṇa tvāt ūrdhva jvalana svabhāvakam ūrddhvam jvalanam kriyā viśeṣaḥ tat svabhāvakam tat dharmakam pacanasvedana ādi samartham pacanam pūrva guṇa vilakṣaṇam guṇa antara utpādanam svedanam stabdha tva nāśanam ādi śabdāt visphoṭa ādi janana lakṣaṇam dahanam tatra samartham iti artha kriyā upavarṇanam 
NK_59.2^2	 divyam abindhanam sauram vidyut ādi bhāvam tejaḥ abindhanam āpaḥ indhanam yasya iti vyutpattyā tat sauram vidyut ādi ādi śabdāt ulkāyāḥ avabodhaḥ bhuktasya āhārasya rasa ādi pariṇāma artham udaryam udare bhavam tejaḥ bhuktasya āhārasya rasa mala dhātu bhāvena pariṇāma prayojanam ākarajan ca suvarṇa ādi ākaraḥ sthāna viśeṣaḥ tasmin suvarṇa rajata ādi taijasam dravyam jāyate suvarṇa ādīnām taijasa tve tāvat āgamaḥ pramāṇam nyāyaḥ ca abhihitaḥ katham tarhi gandha rasayoḥ anuṣṇa aśīta sparśasya ca guru tvasya ca upalabdhiḥ atas āha tatra iti bhoginām adṛṣṭa vaśena bhūyasām pārthiva avayavānām upaṣṭambhāt anudbhūta rūpa sparśam piṇḍībhāva yogyam suvarṇa ādikam ārabhyate tatra pārthiva dravya samavetāḥ ime rasa ādayaḥ gṛhyante iti śabdaḥ samāptau 
NK_59.3^1	 anudbhūta rūpa sparśam suvarṇa ādikam iti na mṛṣyāmahe pratīyamāna rūpa sparśa vyatiriktasya dravya antarasya abhāvāt iti ced na stambhaḥ ayam kumbhaḥ ayam iti pratyeka vilakṣaṇa saṃsthāna saṃvedanāt rūpa ādi svabhāvasya ca sarvatra aviśeṣāt vāsanā bhedāt pratisañcayam saṃvitti bhedaḥ iti ced nīla ādi saṃvitti bhedaḥ api vāsanā kṛtaḥ eva astu na arthaḥ nīla ādi bhedena asati bāhya vastuni sva santāna mātra adhīna janmanaḥ vāsanā paripākasya kādācid katva anupapatteḥ tanmātra hetoḥ nīla ādi saṃvedanasya kādācid katva asambhavān nīla ādi bheda kalpanā iti ced stambha ādi saṃvitti bhedasya api bāhya vastu ananurodhinaḥ na kādācid ka tvam upapadyate iti rūpa ādi vyatiriktaḥ pratisañjayam vāsanā viśeṣa prabodha hetuḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ kalpanīyaḥ yena darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇam api siddhyati rūpa ādi mātre vastuni asya api asambhavaḥ teṣam ekaika indriya grahaṇa niyamāt api ca rūpa ādayaḥ paramāṇu svabhāvāḥ pratyekam atīndriyāḥ tad vyatiriktaḥ sajcayaḥ na asti iti bhavatām kaḥ arthaḥ darśana sparśana viṣayaḥ 
NK_59.3^2	 pratyekam atīndriyāḥ api paramāṇavaḥ manaskāra indriya ādiṣu satsu samartha utpannāḥ aindriyakāḥ bhāvanti iti ced na samartha utpāde api parama sūkṣma svarūpa anati vṛtteḥ samartha utpatti mātreṇa ca cākṣuṣa tve manaskāra indriyayoḥ api pratyakṣatā syāt aviśeṣāt atha matam pratyekam asthūlāḥ api paramāṇavaḥ keśa samūha vat saṃhatāḥ sthūla avabhāsa bhājaḥ bhavantaḥ cākṣuṣāḥ jāyante nirantara tayā ca eka svena adhyavasīyante iti ced kim eteṣu bahuṣu tadānīm ekaḥ sthūla ākāraḥ jāyate kim vā keśeṣu iva avidyamānaḥ samāropya pratīyate yadi ca jāyate sa naḥ avayavi iti atha avidyamānaḥ pratīyate bhrāntiḥ tarhi bhrāntiḥ ca abhrānti pratiyoginī iti kvacid ekaḥ sthūlaḥ satyaḥ abhyupeyaḥ na ca vijñane tasya satya tā yuktāḥ sthūlam aham asmi iti prati iti anudayāt aneka draṣṭṛ sādhāraṇa tva abhāva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt viṣayaḥ eva ayam ekaḥ sthūlaḥ sarvadā bhinna ākāreṇa pratibhāsanāt artha kriyā sampādanāt ca iti avayavi siddhiḥ 
NK_59.4^1	 nanu asati bādhake pratīti siddhaḥ tathā iti vyavahniyate avayavi sadbhāve tu bādhakam pramāṇam asti tathā hi pāṇau kampavati tad āśritam śarīram na kampate pāde vā kampamāne tad gatam śarīram na kampate iti ekasya viruddha dharma tā prasaṅgaḥ tad asaṅgatam pāṇau kampamāne śarīra kampā vaśyambhāva niyama abhāvāt yadā pāṇi mātram cālayitum kāraṇam bhavati tadā tanmātram calati na śarīram kāraṇa abhāvāt yadā tu śarīrasya api calana kāraṇam bhavet tadā śarīram calati eva na asya acalanam asti iti kutas virodhaḥ yadi hastaḥ calatina śarīram tadā avayava avayavinoḥ yuta siddhiḥ prasaṅgaḥ na evam pṛthak āśrayi tvam yuta siddhiḥ na cala acala tvam dravye calati guṇasya acalane api sayoḥ yuta siddhi abhāvāt pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam ca avayava avayavinoḥ bhinna tve api na asti iti na yuta siddha tā 
NK_59.4^2	 yat api anyat bādhakam uktam eka avāyava āvaraṇe tat samavetasya avayavinaḥ na grahaṇam anāvṛta avayava grahaṇe ca grahaṇam iti ekasya yugapad grahaṇam agrahaṇan ca prāpnutaḥ iti tat api asāram eka avayava āvaraṇe avayavi āvaraṇasya abhāvāt sa hi ekaḥ anekeṣu vā avayaviṣu varttamānaḥ katipaya avayava āvaraṇe api anāvṛta itara katipaya avayava grahaṇena gṛhyate tasya sarvatra abhinna tvāt tat tu bahutara avayava grahaṇa vat sthūla pratītiḥ na bhavati tad bhūtayaḥ avayava pracaya grahaṇasya parimāṇa prakarṣa pratīti hetoḥ abhāvāt yatra tu bhūyasām avayavānām āvaraṇam alpatara avayava grahaṇan ca tatra avayavinaḥ na grahaṇam yathā jala nimagnasya śiraḥ mātra darśanāt ekasmin avayave rakte tad deśaḥ avayavī raktaḥ avayava antare ca ārakte na raktaḥ iti ekasya rakta ārakta tva prasaṅgaḥ iti adūṣaṇam avirodhāt rāga dravya saṃyogaḥ rakta tvam arakta tvan va tad abhāvaḥ ubhayam ca ekasya bhavati eva saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti bhāvāt 
NK_60.1	 idam aparam avayavinaḥ pratyavayavam eka deśena vṛttiḥ kārtsnyena vā prakāra antara abhāvāt na tāvat eka deśena vṛttiḥ avayava vyatirekeṇa asya ekadeśa abhāvāt kārtsnyena vṛttau vā avayava antare vṛtti abhāvaḥ eka avayava saṃsarga avacchinne svarūpe avayava antarāṇām anavakāśāt tad svarūpa vyatirekeṇa ca asya svarūpa antara abhāvāt atra api nirūpyate yat varttate tad eka deśena varttate kārtsnyena ca iti kim idam sva siddham abhidhīyate para siddham vā svayam tavat kasyacid kvacid vṛttiḥ asiddhā śākyānām parasya api na eka deśa kārtsnyābhyām vṛttiḥ siddhāḥ tayoḥ avṛtti tvāt vṛttim pratyakāraṇa tvāt ca 
NK_60.2^1	 yat varttate tat svarūpeṇa āśraya āśrita bhāva lakṣaṇayā vṛttyā varttate na ca ekasya aneka saṃsargaḥ viruddhyate dṛṣṭaḥ hi citra jñāne nīla ākāra avacchinne pīta ādi ākāra saṃsargaḥ na ca tasya pratyākāram bhedaḥ ekasya aneka ākāra grahaṇa anupapttau bhavatām citra pratītyabhāva prasaṅgāt na api vijñāna eka tvāt ākārāṇām api eka tvam citra anubhava virodhāt yathā eka avayava avacchinne eka avayavi svabhāve avayava antara samāveśaḥ pratyakṣeṇa aneka avayava sambaddhasya tathā ekasya sthūlārmanaḥ saṃvedanāt ekasmin aneka saṃsargaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ na ekasya anekeṣu saṃsargaḥ iti ca vaidharmya mātram ekasya aneka saṃsarga avacchedasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt 
NK_60.2^2	 evam ca yat ekam tat ekatra eva varttate yathā ekam rūpam ekaḥ ca avayavi iti tathā yat aneka vṛtti tat anekam yathā aneka bhājana gatāni tāla phalāni aneka vṛttiḥ ca avayavī iti prasaṅga dvayam pratyākhyātam svatas paratas ca vyāpti asiddheḥ svatas tāvat ekam vijñānam anekeṣu viṣaya indriya manaskāreṣu svarūpa abhedena tad utpattyā varttate parasya api ekam sūtram abhedena anekeṣu maṇiṣu saṃyoga vṛttyā varttate tathā avayavi avayaveṣu samavāya vṛttyā varttiṣyate nāmā ca na bhaviṣyati 
NK_60.2^3	 sarvaḥ cāram prasaṅga hetuḥ āśrayam nighnan= ātmānam api hanti avayavi abhāve paramāṇu mātre jagati dharma dharmi dṛṣṭānta ādi pratīti asiddhau nirāśrayasya vṛtti abhāvāt atas na anena pratyakṣa siddhaḥ avayavī śakyaḥ nirākarttum pratyakṣa sāpekṣasya tasya tatas durbala tvāt bhrāntam pratyakṣam iti ced kutas etat bādhakena tad arthasya apākaraṇāt iti ced pratyakṣasya bhrānta tve bādhakasya pramāṇa tvam bādhaka prāmāṇye ca pratyakṣasya bhrānta tvam iti anyonya apekṣa tvam pratyakṣe tu na ayam nyāyaḥ tasya anapekṣa tvāt na ca artha kriyā saṃvādi sarva loka siddham spaṣṭa pratibhāsam bhrāntam iti yuktam nīla ādi pratyakṣasya api bhrānta tva prasaṅgāt iti bādhaka uddhāraḥ paramāṇavaḥ avayavi sadbhāva anumeyāḥ api santaḥ vyavaharttavyāḥ 
NK_60.3	 ṣaṭkena yugapad yogaḥ ekasya paramaṇoḥ ṣaṣ aṃśa tvam āpādayan paramāṇu sadbhāvam bādhataḥ iti ced kaḥ ayam yugapad yogaḥ nāma kim ekasya paramāṇoḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ saha yugapad utpādaḥ kim vā yugapad saṃyogaḥ yugapad utpādaḥ tāvat kāraṇa yaugapadya adhīnaḥ niraṃśasya api yadi bhavet kaḥ virodhaḥ atha yugapad saṃyogaḥ saḥ api na anupapannaḥ na hi aṃśa viṣayaḥ saṃyogaḥ dravyāṇām niraṃśasya api ākāśasya tat sadbhāvāt aṃśasya api aṃśa antara sadbhāve paramāṇu mātre saṃyoga sthitau tasya apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt ca kintu svarūpa viṣayaḥ evan ced sa aṃśa dravyasya iva niraṃśasya api paramāṇoḥ ekasya yugapad kāraṇa sambhave sati aneka saṃyoga adhikaraṇa tvam upapadyate eva iti na tad pratikṣepaḥ 
NK_61.1–61.4	 vāyu tvā abhisambandhāt vāyuḥ sparśa saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva saṃskātavān sparśaḥ asya anuṣṇa aśīta tve satya pāka jaḥ guṇa viniveśāt siddhaḥ urūpiṣu acākṣuṣa vacanāt sapta saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ tṛṇa karma vacanāt saṃskāraḥ sa ca ayam dvividhaḥ aṇu kāryya bhāvāt tatra kāryya lakṣaṇaḥ caturvidhaḥ śarīram indriyam viṣayaḥ prāṇaḥ iti 
NK_61.5–61.7	 tatṛ yonijam eva śarīram marutām loke pārthiva avayava upaṣṭambhāt ca upabhoga samartham indriyam sarva prāṇinām sparśa upalambhakam pṛthivī ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ vāyu avayavaiḥ ārambdham sarva śarīra vyāpi tvac indriyam pratyakṣam pṛthivī ādi trayam vyākhyāya apratyakṣa dravya vyākhyāna avasare nitya anitya ubhaya svabhāva dravya nirūpaṇasya prakṛta tvāt vāyum vyācaṣṭe vāyu tvā abhisambandhāt vāyuḥ iti vyākhyānam pūrvavat tasya guṇān kathayati sparśa ityādi atra api pūrvavat vyākhvā 
NK_61.8^1	 yādṛśaḥ sparśaḥ vāyau varttate tam darśayati sparśaḥ iti pṛthivīspāśaḥ pāka jaḥ paramāṇuṣu tad pūrvakaḥ ca sva kāryyeṣu asya vāyo sparśaḥ apākajaḥ iti atas vaidhyarmyam apākaja tvan ca asya pṛthivī anadhikaraṇa tvāt udaka tejaḥ speśa vat anuṣṇa aśīta tve sati iti udaka tejaḥ sparśābhyām vaidharmyam uktam ayañca dvitīya adhyāyāt vāyuḥ sparśavān iti sūtreṇa vāyau siddhaḥ iti āha guṇa viniveśāt iti arūpiṣu acākṣuṣa vacanāt sapta saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ rūpa rahiteṣu dravyeṣu saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ cākṣuṣāḥ na bhavanti iti abhidhānāt arūpiṣu saṅkhī ā ādīnām sadbhāvaḥ kathitaḥ anyathā tad varttinām teṣām apratyakṣatva abhidhānam asambaddham syāt 
NK_61.8^2–61.9	 tṛṇa karma vacanāt saṃskāraḥ iti tṛṇe karma vāyu saṃyogāt iti vacanāt vāyau saṃskāraḥ darśitaḥ vega rahita dravya saṃyogasya karma hetu tva anupalambhāt tasya bheda nirūpaṇa artham āha sa ca ayam iti sa ca iti smṛti utthāpitaḥ buddhi sannihitaḥ paścāt ayam iti pratyakṣa vat parāmṛśyate na kevalam pṛthivī āsayaḥ dvividhāḥ ayam api dvividhaḥ iti ca arthaḥ kāryya lakṣaṇaḥ caturvidhaḥ kāryya svabhāva eti arthaḥ cāturvidhyam katham iti atas āha śarīram indriyam viṣayaḥ prāṇaḥ iti teṣām madhye śarīram jātyā nirddhārayati tatra śarīram iti ayonijam eva na tu pārthiva śarīra vat yoni jam ayonijam api bhavati iti arthaḥ marutām loke iti sthāna saṅkīrttanam bhūyasām pārthiva avayavānām nimitta kāraṇa bhūtānām upaṣṭambhāt saṃyoga viśeṣāt sthiram saṃhata svabhāvam utpannam pārthiva śarīra vat upabhoga samartham 
NK_61.10	 indriyam sarva prāṇinām sparśa upalambhakam iti yat sarva prāṇinām sparśa upalambhakam indriyam tat pṛthivī ādi anabhibhūtaiḥ apratihata sāmarthyaiḥ vāyu avayavaiḥ ārabdham atas viśiṣṭa utpādāt indriyam syāt iti arthaḥ tasya sadbhāve tāvat sparśa upalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam vāyavīyatvañca asya rūpa ādiṣu madhye sparśasya eva abhivyañjaka tvāt aṅga saṅgi salila śaitya abhivyañjaka samīraṇa vat tat ca sarva śarīra vyāpi sarvatra tad kāryyasya sparśa upalambhasya bhāvāt tvac indriyam iti samākhyā tvaci sthitam indriyam tvad indriyam iti ucyate tad sthe tad upacārāt tvacā sarva indriya adhiṣṭhānāni vyāptāni satyām tvaci rūpa ādi grahaṇam asatyām agrahaṇam iti tvac indriyam sarva artham na tu sparśa mātra grāhakam iti ced tat ayuktam andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅgāt tad tad adhiṣṭhāna bhedena tasyāḥ śakti bheda abhyupagame prakāra antareṇa indriya bheda abhyupagamaḥ 
NK_62.1–62.2^1	 viṣayaḥ tu upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna bhūtaḥ sparśa śabda dhṛti kampa liṅgaḥ tiryyak gamana svabhāvaḥ megha ādi preṇa dhāraṇa dhāraṇa ādi samarthaḥ viṣaya vyavasthā niyama nirūpaṇa artham āha viṣayaḥ tu iti upalabhyamāna sparśasya adhiṣṭhāna bhūtaḥ āśrayaḥ yaḥ sa viṣayaḥ iti kim asya astitve pramāṇam pratyākṣam eva tvac indriya vyāpāreṇa vāyuḥ vātī iti aparokṣa jñāna utpatteḥ iti kaścid tat na aparśa vyatiriktasya vastu antarasya asaṃvedanāt aparokṣa jñane tu ṣarśaḥ eva pratibhāti na anyat yat api vāyuḥ vātī iti jñānam tad abhyāsa pāṭava atiśayāt vyāpti smaraṇa ādi anapekṣam sparśena anumānam cakṣuṣā iva vṛkṣa ādi gata kriyā upalambhāt śīta uṣṇa sparśa bheda tītau vāyu pratyabhijñānam api tad āśraya upanāyaka dravya anumānāt eva 
NK_62.2^2	 tvac indriyeṇa tu śīta uṣṇa sparśābhyām anyasya na pratibhāsaḥ asti spārśana pratyakṣaḥ vāyuḥ upalabhyamāna sparśa adhiṣṭhāna tvāt ghaṭa vat iti anumānam śaśa ādiṣu paśutvena śṛṅga anumāna vat anupalabdhitam dravyasya spārśana tvam cākṣuṣa tvena vyāptam avagatam ghaṭa ādiṣu cākṣuṣa tvasya ca vāyau= abhāvaḥ tena atra śakyam spārśana tva nivṛtti anumānam etat atas tasya apratyakṣasya sadbhāve anumānam upanyasyati sparśa śabda dhṛti kampa liṅgaḥ iti sparśaḥ ca śabdaḥ ca dhṛtiḥ ca kampaḥ ca liṅgāni yasya iti bahuvrīhiḥ 
NK_62.3	 yaḥ ayam rūpa ādi rahitaḥ sparśaḥ pratīyate sa kvacid āśritaḥ sparśa tvāditara sparśa vat na ca asya pṛthivī ā iva āśrayaḥ rūpa viprayogāt asti atra api anudbhūtam rūpam iti ced na upalabhyamānasya pārthivasya sparśasya upalabhyamāna rūpeṇa eva saha avyabhicāra upalambhāt na ca iha rūpasya asti upapalambhaḥ tasmāt na ayam pārthivaḥ sparśaḥ na ca udaka tejasoḥ ayam āśritaḥ anuṣṇa aśīta tvāt ghaṭa ādi sparśa vat na api amūrtteṣu ākāśa kāla diś ātmasu varttate sparśasya mūrtta avi abhicāra upalambhāt manasā añca sparśavat tve paramāṇūnām iva teṣam sajātīya dravya ārambhaka tvam syāt na ca evam tasmāt teṣām api na bhavati atas yatra ayam āśritaḥ sa vāyuḥ iti pariśeṣaḥ 
NK_62.4	 evam śabdaḥ api asya liṅgam yaḥ ayam parṇa ādiṣu akasmāt śuka śukā śabdaḥ śrūyate tasya ādyaḥ śabdaḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga jaḥ avibhajyamāna avayava dravya sambandhi tve satya ādi śabda tvāt daṇḍa āhata bherī śabda vat yaḥ ca asau sparśavām sa vāyuḥ ākāśa ādīnām sparśa abhāvāt pṛthivī udaka tejasām ca rūpavatām tad śabda hetu tve pratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt vibhāga ja śabda vyavaccheda artham avibhajyamāna avayava dravya sambandhi tve sati iti uktam 
NK_62.5	 evam antarikṣe parṇa ādīnām dhṛtiḥ avasthitiḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga kāryyā prayatna vega ādi kāraṇa abhāve sati dhṛti tvāt jala upari sthita parṇa ādi dhṛti vat yat ca tat sparśavat dravyam na tat pṛthivī ādi trayamapratyakṣa tvāt eva iti dravya antara siddhiḥ iṣoḥ pakṣiṇān ca sthiti vyavaccheda artham prayatna ādi kāraṇa abhāvaḥ iti 
NK_62.6–62.7	 tathā vṛkṣa ādīnām kampa viśeṣaḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga jaḥ viśiṣṭa kampa tvāt nadīpūrā āha tevetasa ādi vana kampa vat bhūkampena vyabhicāraḥ iti ced na tasya anya hetutva avagamāt sparśavat dravya saṃyoga je tu viśiṣṭa kampa tvam eva pramāṇam iti avyabhicāraḥ nanu yat eva dravyam sparśena anumitam tat eva śabda ādibhiḥ api anumīyate na tu pratiliṅgam dravya antara anumitiḥ kim iha pramāṇam yena etat uvyate sparśa śabda dhṛti kampa liṅgaḥ vāyuḥ iti idam pramāṇam sparśa anumita dravya kāryya tvena eva śabda ādīnām upapattau sambhavantyām dravya antara kalpanā vaiyarthyam iti evam vyavasthite vāyau tad dharmam darśayati tiryyak gamana svabhāvaḥ iti tiryyak gamanam svabhāvaḥ yasya iti mebhā ādi preraṇe itas tatas nayane dhāraṇe guru tva pratibandhe ādi śabdāt gharṣaṇe samarthaḥ megha ādi ityādi padena yāna pātra ādi parigrahaḥ teṣam api vāyunā preryyamāṇa tvāt 
NK_63.1–63.2^1	 tasya apratyakṣasya api nānātvam sammūrcchanena anumīyate sammūrcchanam punar samāna javayoḥ vāyvoḥ viruddha diś kriyayauḥ sannipātaḥ saḥ api sāvayavinoḥ vāyvoḥ ūrddhva gamanena anumīyate tat api tṛṇa ādi gamanena iti anumīyamāneṣu ākāśa ātma ādiṣu eka aneka tva upalabdhau saṃśaye sati tad vyudāsā artham āha tasya apratyakṣasya api iti sammūrcchanam api na jñāyate sadartham āha sammūrcchanam iti viruddhāyām diśi kriyā yayoḥ tayoḥ samāna vegayoḥ sannipātaḥ paraspara gati pratibandha hetuḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ sammūrcchanam tena vāyoḥ nnānātvam anumīyate ekasya saṃyoga abhāvāt eka diś prasthitayoḥ yathākram gacchatoḥ sammūrcchana abhāvaḥ iti viruddha dikkriyayoḥ iti uktam viruddha dikkriyayoḥ bhinna dikkriyayoḥ iti arthaḥ asamāna vegayoḥ sammūrcchanam na bhavati ekena aparasya vijayāt tad artham samāna javayoḥ iti 
NK_63.2^2	 apratyakṣayoḥ yathā nānātvam apratyakṣam tathā saṃyogaḥ api iti sattva idam āha saḥ api iti sannipātaḥ api sāvayavinoḥ vāyvoḥ ūrddhva gamanena anumīyate vāyoḥ ūrddhva gamanam paraspara vyāhati pūrvakam anya kāraṇā sambhave sati tiryyak gati svabhāva dravya ūrddhva gati tvāt paraspara āhata jala taraṅga ūrddhva gamana vat avayavinoḥ iti vaktavye sāvayavinoḥ iti uktam avayavānām api avayavi tva vivakṣayā sthūla vāyu parigraha artham aṇu parimāṇasya tṛṇa ādi preraṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt ūrddhva gamanam api tayoḥ apratyakṣam iti tad pratipattau anumānam āha tṛṇa ādi gamanena anumīyate iti 
NK_64.1–64.2	 prāṇaḥ antar śarīre rasa mala dhātūnām preraṇa ādi hetuḥ ekaḥ san kriyā bhedāt apāna ādi saṃjñam labhate loke yoga śāstre ca viṣaya vāyoḥ bhedena prasiddhasya prāṇa ākhyasya svarūpam āha praṇaḥ antar śarīraḥ iti antar śarīre yaḥ vāyuḥ varttate sa prāṇaḥ iti ucyate tasya artha kriyām kathayati rasa mala dhātūnām preraṇa ādi hetuḥ iti rasaḥ iti bhukta pīta āhāreṣu pākaja utpatti krameṇa uptannasya dravya viśeṣasya grahaṇam malaḥ iti mūtra purīṣayoḥ abhidhānam dhātavaḥ tvac māṃsa asthi śoṇita ādayaḥ teṣām preraṇasya itaḥ tatas nayanasya ādi śabdāt vyūhanasya ca hetuḥ tasya ekatva aneka tva saṃśaye satyāha ekaḥ san iti nanu pañca vāyavaḥ śarīrāḥ śrūyante tatra āha kriyā bhedāt iti mūtra purīṣa roḥ adhonayanāt apānaḥ rasasya garbha nāḍīṣu vitananāt vyānaḥ anna pāna ādeḥ ūrddhvam nayanāt udānaḥ mukha nāsikābhyām niṣkramaṇāt prāṇaḥ āhāreṣu pāka artham udaryyasya vahneḥ samam sarvatra sayanāt samānaḥ iti na vāstavam eteṣām pañcatvam api tu kalpitam katham ekasmin āśraye mūrttānām samāveśa abhāvāt 
NK_65.1	 iha idānīm caturṇām mahābhūtānām sṛṣṭi saṃhāra vidhiḥ ucyate brāhmeṇa mānena varṣa śata ante varttamānasya brahmaṇaḥ apavarga kāle saṃsāre khinnānām sarva prāṇinām niśi viśrāma artham sakala bhuvana pateḥ maheśvarasya sañja hīrṣā samakālam śarīra indriya mahā bhūta upanibandhakānām sarva ātma gatānām adṛṣṭānām vṛtti nirodhe sati maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyoga ja karmabhyaḥ śarīra indriya kāraṇa aṇu vibhāgebhyaḥ tad saṃyoga nivṛttau teṣām āparamāṇu astaḥ vināśaḥ tathā pṛthivī udaka jvalana pavanām api mahābhūtānām anena eva krameṇa uttarasmin= uttarasmin sati pūrvasya pūrvasya vināśaḥ tatas pravibhaktaḥ paramāṇavaḥ avatiṣṭhante dharma adharma saṃskāra anuviddhāḥ ca ātmānaḥ tāvantam eva kālam 
NK_65.2–65.3^1	 utpattim anti catvāri dravyāṇi ākhyāya vistarāt teṣām karttṛ parīkṣā artham udyamaḥ kriyate adhunā pṛthivī ādīnām caturṇām utpatti vināśau nirūpayīṇau tayoḥ ca pratiprakaraṇam nirūpaṇe grantha vistaraḥ syāt iti samāna nyāyena ekatra nirūpaṇa artham prakaraṇam ārabhyate caturṇām iti sṛṣṭi saṃhārayoḥ utpatti vināśayoḥ vidhiḥ prakāraḥ kathyate yadi api ekatra caturṇām api sṛṣṭa saṃhārau kathyete tathā api na idam sādharmya abhidhānam pratyekam vilakṣaṇayoḥ eva tayoḥ upavarṇanāt mahābhūtānām iti ukte trayāṇām eva parigrahaḥ syāt kapiñjala anāla bheta iti vat bahutva saṃkhyāyāḥ tāvatā eva caritārtha tvāt atas caturṇām iti uktam 
NK_65.3^2	 caturṇām iti ukte ca anantara uktam eva vāyu kāryyam śarīram indriyam viṣayaḥ prāṇaḥ iti catuṣṭayam buddhau niviśate tad nivṛtti artham mahābhūtānām iti nanu evam tarhi dvi aṇukānām utpatti vināśau na pratijñātau syātām teṣām aṇu tvāt na evam vidhi śabda upādānāt yena prakāreṇa mahābhūtānām utpatti vināśau sa prakāraḥ kathyate iti uktam teṣān ca dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpattiḥ āparamāṇu antar ca vināśaḥ iti atas dvi aṇukānām api sṛṣṭi saṃhārau pratijñātau syātām artha pratipādana mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt 
NK_65.4	 paścāt uktam api saṃhāram prathamam kathayati brāhmeṇa mānena iti asmākam pañcadaśa nimeṣāḥ kāṣṭhā triṃśat kāṣṭhāḥ kalā pañcadaśa kalā nāḍikā triṃśat kalaḥ muhūrttaḥ triṃśātā muhūrttaiḥ ahorātraḥ pañcadaśa ahorātrāḥ pakṣaḥ dvau pakṣau māsaḥ dvau māsau= ṛtuḥ ṣaṭṛtavaḥ dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatdaraḥ ṛtu trayeṇa uttarāyaṇam ṛtu trayeṇa ca dakṣiṇāyanam uttarāyaṇan ca devānām dinam dakṣiṇāyanan ca devānām rātriḥ tathā bhūta ahorātra śata trayeṇa ṣaṣṭi adhikena varṣam dvādaśa sahasraiḥ ca varṣaiḥ caturyugam catur tuga sahasreṇa brahmaṇaḥ dinam ekam 
NK_65.5^1	 iti anena mānena varṣa śatasya ante avasāne varttamānasya brahmaṇaḥ apavarga kāle mukti kāle saṃsāre nānā sthāneṣu bhūyas bhūyas śarīra ādi parigraheṇa khinnānām garbhāsa ādividha duḥkhena duḥkhitānām prāṇinām niśi viśrāma artham kiyat kālam duḥkha upaśama artham sakala bhuvana pateḥ sarvatra avyāhata prabhāvasya maheśvarasya sañjihīrṣā saṃhāra icchā bhavati tad samāna kālam tad anantaram śarīra indriya mahā bhūta upanibandhakānām śarīra indriya mahābhūta ārambha kāṇām sarva ātma gatānām sarveṣava ātmasu samavetānām adṛṣṭāṇam vṛtti nirodhaḥ śakti pratibandhaḥ syāt 
NK_65.5^2	 tasmin sati anāgatānām śarīra indriya mahābhūtānām anutpattiḥ utpannānān ca vināśa artham maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyogebhyaḥ karmāṇi jāyante maheśvara icchā sañji hīrṣā akṣaṇāḥ aṇu iti paramāṇu parigrahaḥ maheśvarasya icchā ca ātmā aṇu saṃyogāḥ ca iti vigrahaḥ tebhyaḥ jātāni maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyoga jāni tebhyaḥ maheśvara icchā ātmā aṇu saṃyoga ja karmabhyaḥ śarīrāṇām indriyāṇām ye pāramparyeṇa kāraṇa bhūtāḥ uṇavaḥ teṣu vibhāgāḥ bhavanti vibhāgebhyaḥ teṣām aṇūnām saṃyoga nivṛttiḥ saṃyoga nivṛttau satyām teṣām āparamāṇu antaḥ vināśaḥ teṣām śarīra indriyāṇām dvi aṇuka ādi vināśa prakrameṇa tāvat vināśaḥ yāvat paramāṇuḥ iti 
NK_65.6^1	 prajām akāṇḍe saṃharan= ayamakāruṇikaḥ yat kiñcana kārī ca syāt iti yat kenacid uktam tatra iyam pratikriyā prāṇinām niśi viśrāma artham iti yat api etat uktam anantānām ātmanām ananteṣu adṛṣṭeṣu krameṇa paripacyamāneṣu kecid adṛṣṭa kṣayāt bhogāt uparamante bhujyante ca kecid apare tu bhoga abhimukhāḥ iti evam sarvatra viṣaya pravṛttau na śarīra ādīnām yugapad a bhāvaḥ ghaṭate iti tat anena parāhatam adṛṣṭānām vṛtti pratibandhaḥ iti brahmaṇaḥ apavarga kāle niśi iti uktam tatra sarva prāṇinām prabodha pratyasta maya sādharmyeṇa upacārāt mahābhūtānām api evam vināśaḥ iti āha tathā iti 
NK_65.6^2	 yathā śarīra indriyāṇām āparamāṇu antaḥ vināśaḥ tathā mahābhūtānām api anena eva krameṇa iti paramāṇu kriyā vibhāga ādi krameṇa uttarasmin uttarasmin sati pūrvasya pūrvasya vināśaḥ iti jale tiṣṭhati pūrvam pṛthivyāḥ vināśaḥ tejasi tiṣṭhati jalasya vāyau tiṣṭhati tejasaḥ iti arthaḥ tatas pravibhaktāḥ paramāṇavaḥ avatiṣṭhante dharma adharma bhāvanā ākhya saṃskāraiḥ anuviddhāḥ upagṛhītāḥ ca ātmānaḥ tāvantam eva kālam brahmaṇaḥ varṣatam eva avatiṣṭhante diś ādayaḥ api tiṣṭhanti nitya tvāt kintu ātmanām adṛṣṭa vaśāt paramāṇavaḥ punar na ārapsyante iti prādhānyāt aḍṛṣṭa vaśāt ātma paramāṇu avasthāna saṃkīrttanam 
NK_65*.1–65*.2	 tatas punar prāṇinām bhoga bhūtaye maheśvarasya aisṛkṣa anantaram sarvatma gata vṛtti labdha adṛṣṭa apekṣebhyaḥ tad saṃyogebhyaḥ pavana paramāṇuṣu karma utpattau teṣām paraspara saṃyogebhyaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa mahān vāyuḥ samutpannaḥ nabhasi dodhūyamānaḥ tiṣṭhati tad anantaram tasmin eva vāya avāpyebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ tena eva krameṇa mahān salilanidhiḥ utpannaḥ poplūyamānaḥ tiṣṭhati tad anantaram tasmin eva jalanidhau pārthivebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ mahā pṛthivī samutpannā saṃhata avatiṣṭhate tad anantanam tasmin eva mahā udadhau taijasobhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpannaḥ mahān tejaḥ rāśiḥ kenacid anabhibhūta tvāt dedīpyamānaḥ tiṣṭhati evaṃsam utpanneṣu caturṣu mahābhūteṣu maheśvarayā abhidhyāna mātrāt taijasebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu sahitebhyaḥ mahat aṇḍam ārabhyate tasmin catur vadana kamalam sarva loka pitāmaham brahmāṇam sakala bhuvana sahitam utpādya prajā sarge viniyuṅkte 
NK_65*.3^1	 evam saṃhāra kramam pratipādya sṛṣṭi kramam pratipādayam māha tatas punar iti yadi api tadā nīma ātmanām prāṇa sambandhaḥ na asti tathā api prāṇinaḥ iti uktam yogya tvāt teṣām bhoga bhūtaye sukha duḥkha anubhava utpattaye maheśvarasya sisṛkṣā sarjana icchā jāyate tad anantaram sarveṣu ātmasu gatāḥ adṛṣṭāḥ vṛvṛttim labhante yadi api yugapad utpadyamāna asaṃkhyeya kārya utpattau vyāpriyamāṇā diś ādi vat nitya tvāt ekā eva īśvara icchā kriyāśakti rūpā tathā api eṣā tad tad kāla viśeṣa sahakāri prāptau prāptau kadācid saṃhāra arthā bhavati kadācid sṛṣṭi arthā syāt yadā saṃhāra arthā tadā tad anurodhāt adṛṣṭānām vṛtti nirodhaḥ audāsīnya lakṣaṇaḥ jāyate yadā tu asau sṛṣṭi arthā bhavet tadā vṛtti lābhaḥ sva kāryya jananam prati vyāpāraḥ bhavati vṛttiḥ labdhāḥ yaiḥ te vṛtti labdhāḥ iti āhitāgni ādi tvāt niṣṭhāyāḥ pūrva nipātaḥ danta jātaḥ iti yathā sarva ātma gatāḥ ca vṛtti labdhāḥ ca adṛṣṭāḥ ca tān apekṣante ye tad saṃyogā ātma aṇu saṃyogāḥ tebhyaḥ pavana paramāṇuṣu karmāṇi utpadyante 
NK_65*.3^2	 pavana paramāṇavaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam labdha vṛtti adṛṣṭa vat ātma paramāṇu saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam adṛṣṭam nimitta kāraṇam evam karma utpattau teṣām pavana paramāṇūnām paraspara saṃyogāḥ jāyante tad saṃyogebhyaḥ ca dvi aṇukāni utpadyante tadanu tri aṇukāni iti anena krameṇa mahān vāyuḥ samutpadyamānaḥ nabhasi ākāśe dodhūyamānaḥ kvacid apratihata tvāt vega atiśaya yuktaḥ tiṣṭhati tad anantaram tasmin eva vāya avāpyebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ tena eva krameṇa dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa mahān salilanidhiḥ utpannaḥ poplūyamānaḥ pratirodhaka abhāvāt sarvatra plavamānaḥ tiṣṭhati tad anantaram jalanidheḥ utpatti anantaram tasmin eva jaladhau pārthivebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ mahā pṛthivī samutpannā saṃhatā sthira svabhāva avatiṣṭhate tad anantaram tasmin eva mahā udadhau taijasebhyaḥ aṇubhyaḥ dvi sṇuka ādi prakrameṇa utpannaḥ mahān tejaḥ rāśiḥ kenacid anabhibhūta tvāt dedīpyamānaḥ tiṣṭhati yadi api payaḥ pāvakayoḥ svābhāvikaḥ virodhaḥ tathā api adṛṣṭa vaśena ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ na anupapannaḥ 
NK_65*.4^1	 evam anantara uktena prakrameṇa utpanneṣu mahābhūteṣu maheśvarasya abhidhyāna mātrāt saṅkalpa mātrāt taijasebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu sahitebhyaḥ mahat aṇḍam mahat bimbam ārabhyate bimba aran bhe pārthivāḥ avayavāḥ upaṣṭambhākāḥ tena idam vahni puñja prāyam na abhūt tasmin aṇḍe catvāri vadana kamalāni yasya tam brahmāṇam sarva loka pitāmaham sarveṣām eva lokānām adyam puruṣam samaḥ taiḥ bhuvanauḥ saha ūrpādya prajānām sarge janane viniyuṅkte tvam idam kuru iti sa ca maheśvareṇa viniyuktaḥ brahma atiśaya jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryya sampannaḥ jñānan ca vairāgyan ca aiśvaryyañca jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryyāṇi atiśayena jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryyāṇi taiḥ sampannaḥ upacitaḥ jñāna atiśayāt prāṇinām dharma adharmau yathāvat pratyeti vairāgyāt na pakṣapātena pravarttate aiśvaryyāt karma phalam bhojayati 
NK_65*.4^2	 prāṇinām karma vipākam viditvā iti vividhena prakāreṇa pākaḥ vipākaḥ karmaṇām vipākaḥ karma vipākaḥ tam viditvā etāvat asya karma phalam bhaviṣyati iti jñātvā karma anurūpāṇi jñāna bhoga āyūṃṣi yeṣām tān sutān prajāpatīn dakṣa ādīn mānasān manaḥ saṅkalpa mātra prabhavān manu deva ṛṣi pitṛ gaṇān manūn devān ṛṣīn pitṛ gaṇān mukha bāhu ūru pādataḥ caturaḥ varṇān mukhāt brāhmaṇān bāhūbhyām kṣitriyān ūrubhyām vaiśyān padbhyām śūdrān anyāni ca uccāvacāni kṣudra kṣudratarāṇi ca bhūtāni sṛṣṭvā āśaya anurūpaiḥ āśete phala upabhoga kālam yāvat ātmani avatiṣṭhati iti āśayaḥ karma tad anurūpaiḥ dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryyaiḥ saṃyojayati yasya yathāvidham karma tad tad anurūpeṇa jñāna ādinā samyak yojayati mātrayā api anyathā na karoti iti arthaḥ 
NK_66.1–66.2^1	 sa ca maheśvareṇa viniyuktaḥ brahma atiśaya jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryya sampannaḥ prāṇinām karma vipākam viditvā karma anurūpa jñāna bhoga āyuṣaḥ sutān prajāpatīn mānasān manu deva ṛṣi pitṛ gaṇān mukha bāhu ūru pādataḥ caturaḥ varṇān anyāni ca uccāvacāni bhūtāni ca sṛṣṭvā āśaya anurūpaiḥ dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryyaiḥ saṃyojati iti yat khalu kecid evam ācacakṣire prekṣāvat pravṛttiḥ iṣṭa artha adhigamā syāt aniṣṭa parihāra arthāḥ vā na ca iṣṭā aniṣṭa prāpti parihārau= īśvare samasta avāpta kāme sambhavataḥ tena asya jagat nirmāṇe pravṛttiḥ anupapannāḥ tatra uttaram prāṇinām bhoga bhūtayaḥ iti para arthā sisṛkṣāyām pravṛtṭḥ na avārtha nibandhanā iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NK_66.1–66.2^2	 nanu evam tarhi sukha mayīm eva sṛṣṭim kuryyāt na duḥkha śabalām karuṇā pravṛtta tvāt iti atra eṣa parihāraḥ prāṇinām karma vipākam viditvā iti para artham pravṛttaḥ api na sukha mayīm eva karoti vicitra karma āśara sahāyasya saṛttṛ tvāt iti arthaḥ na ca evam sati karuṇā virodhaḥ duḥkha utpādasya api vairāgya janana dvāreṇa parama puruṣartha hetu tvāt yadi dharma adharmau= apekṣya karoti na asti svādhīnam karttṛ tvi anīśvara tā doṣaḥ iti asi apyam pratisamādhiḥ āśaya anurūpaiḥ dharma jñānavaiḥ āgya aiśvaryyaiḥ saṃyojayati sa hi sarva prāṇinām karma anurūpam phalam prayacchan katham anīśvaraḥ syāt iti bhāvaḥ na hi yogyatā anurūpapyeṇa bhṛtyānām phala viśeṣa pradaḥ prabhuḥ aprabhuḥ bhavati 
NK_66.3	 kalpa ādau= utpannānām prāṇinām sarva śabda artheṣu avyutpannānām saṅketasya aśakya karaṇa tvāt chābda vyavahāra anupapattiḥ iti codanāyām pratyavasthāna bījam idam mānasān iti yonija śarīraḥ hi mahatā garbha vāsa ādi duḥkha prabandhena vilupta saṃskāraḥ janma antara anubhūtasya sarvasya na smarati ṛṣayaḥ prajāpatayaḥ manavaḥ tu manasā ayonija śarīra viśiṣṭa adṛṣṭa sambandhenā abhraṣṭa saṃskārāḥ kalpa antara anubhūtam sarvam eva śabda artha vyavahāram supta pratibuddha vat pratisanda dhate pratisandadhānāḥ ca parasparam saṃvadantaḥ vyavaharanti teṣām vyavahārāt tad kāla varttinām prāṇinām vyutpattiḥ tad vyavahārāt ca anyeṣām iti upapadyate vyavahāra paramparayā śabda artha vyutpattiḥ iti arthaḥ 
NK_67.1^1	 kim punar īśvara sadbhāve pramāṇam āgamaḥ tāvat anumānan ca mahābhūta catuṣṭayam upalabdhimat pūrtvāt yat kāryyam tat upalabdha mad pūrvakam yathā ghaṭaḥ kāryyan ca mahābhūta catuṣṭayam tasmāt etat api upalabdhimat pūrvakam pramāṇena pūrva koṭi anupalabdheḥ asiddham pṛthivī ādiṣu kāryya tvam iti ced tat uktam sāvayava tvāt yat sa avayavam tat kāryyam yathā ghaṭaḥ sāvayavañca pṛthivī ādi tasmāt etat api kāryyam eva nanu vyāpti grahaṇāt anumānasya pravṛttiḥ kāryyatu abdhimat pūrvaka tvayoḥ ca vyāpti grahaṇam aśakyam ghaṭa ādiṣu karttṛ pratīti kāle eva aṅ kura ādiṣu utpadyamāneṣu tad abhāva pratīteḥ 
NK_67.1^2	 na ca aṅkura tva ādīnām api pakṣa tvam iti nyāyyam gṛhītāyām vyāptau anumāna pravṛtti kāle prativādi apekṣayā pakṣa ādi pravibhāgaḥ iha tu sarvadā eva pratipakṣa prāti iti ākrānta tvāt vyāpti grahaṇam eva na siddhyati iti uktam atra pratividhīyate ghaṭa ādiṣu kartṛ pūrvaka kārya tva pratītiḥ asti na aṅkuradiṣu iti evam dvaita upalambhe a pi vyāpti grahaṇa sambhave pṛthivī ādiṣu upalabdhimat pūrvaka kāryatva anumānam vartate yadi ca evam dvaita anupalambhāt vyāpti grahaṇa abhāvaḥ tadānīm mīmāṃsā bhāṣya kṛt abhimatam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam āditya gati anumānam api na siddhyati tatra api deva datta gati pūrvaka deśa antara prāpti grahaṇa kāle eva nakṣatra ādiṣu kevala deśa antara prāpti mātra upalambhāt 
NK_67.1^3	 atha teṣu deśa viprakarṣeṇa api gateḥ anupalabdhau sambhavantyām na tayā vyāpti grahaṇa hetoḥ nirupādhi pravṛttasya bhūyas darśanasya pratirodhaḥ tulya kakṣya tva abhāvāt evan ced atra api aśarīra tvena abhyupetasya karttuḥ sva rūpa vipra karṣeṇa api aṅkura ādiṣu apalambha sambhavān na tena nirupādhi pravṛttasya bhūyas darśanasya sāmarthyam upahanyate iti samānam api ca bhoḥ ! kim anumānena karttṛ mātram sādhyate pṛthivī ādi nirmāṇa samarthaḥ vā karttṛ mātra sādhane tāvat abhipretasya asiddhiḥ na hi asmad ādi sadṛśaḥ karttā abhopretaḥ bhavatām na ca tena idam pṛthivī ādi kāryyam arvāk dṛśā śakya nirmāṇam pṛthivī ādi nirmāṇa samarthaḥ tu karttā na siddhi ati ananvayāt anvaya balena hi dṛṣṭānta dṛṣṭa karttṛ sadṛśaḥ sidshyati iti 
NK_67.1^4	 na ayam prasaṅgaḥ karttṛ viśeṣasya aprasādhanāt vyāpti sāmarthyāt buddhimat pūrvaka tve sāmānye sādhyamāne pṛthivī ādi nirmāṇa sāmarthya lakṣaṇaḥ api viśeṣaḥ siddhyāti eva nirviśeṣasya sāmānyasya siddhi abhāvāt nanu mā siddhyatu sāmānyam iti ced na kāryya tvena saha tad vyāpteḥ apratikṣepa arha tvāt yadi hi vyāptam api na siddhyati dhūmāt api agni sāmānyam na siddhyeta agni viśeṣasya ananvitasya asiddheḥ nirviśeṣasya ca sāmānyasya anavasthānāt 
NK_67.2	 atha idam ucyate dvayam anumānasya svarūpam vyāptiḥ pakṣa dharma tā ca tatra vyāpti sāmarthyāt sāmānyam siddhyati pakṣa dharma tā balena ca abhipretaḥ viśeṣaḥ parvata ādi avacchinna vahni sva lakṣaṇa ātmā siddhyati anyathā pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ kva upayogaḥ kva ca anumānasya gṛhīta grāhiṇaḥ prāmāṇyam evan ced īśvara anumāne api tulyam anyatra abhiniveśāt atha matam siddhi ati anumāne viśeṣaḥ api yatra pramāṇa virodhaḥ na asti tathā hi dhūmāt parvata nitamba varti vahni viśeṣa siddhai kā nāma anupapattiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi deśa kāla ādi bhedaḥ sva lakṣaṇānām īśvara anumāne tu viśeṣaḥ na siddhyati pramāṇa virodhāt tathā hi na atra śarīra pūrvaka tvam sādhanīyam śrīre satya vaśyam indriya prāptau= atīndriya upādāna upakaraṇa ādikā śakti parijñāna asambhave sati karttṛ tva asambhavāt 
NK_67.3	 aśarīra pūrvaka tvan ca aśakya sādhanam sarvaḥ hi karttā kāraka svarūpam avadhārayati tatas icchati idam aham anena nirvarttayāmi iti tatas prayatate tadanu kāyam vyāpārayati tatas kāraṇāni adhitiṣṭhati tatas karoti anavadhārayan= aprayatamānaḥ kāyam avyāpārayan kāraṇāni anadhitiṣṭhat na karoti iti anvayatiḥ ekābhyām buddhi cat śarīram api kāryya utpattau upāya bhūtam nikhila upādhi prahāṇe vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa deva avadhāritam na śakyate prahātum vahniḥ iva indhana vikāra sāmarthyam dhūma anumāne tad parityāge ca buddhiḥ api parityajyatām prabhāva atiśayādeva śarīra vat abuddhimān eva ayam īśvaraḥ kariṣyati upādāna upakaraṇa ādi svarūpa anabhijñaḥ na śaknoti iti ced kutas etat tathā anupalambhāt iti ced phalitam mama api manoratha drumeṇa na tathā yāvat icchā prayatna vyavahita abuddhiḥ kāryya utpattau upayujyate yathā idam avyavahita vyāpāram śarīram 
NK_67.4	 evam tarhi kā gatiḥ atra buddhimat kartṛ pūrvakatva sāmānyasya agatiḥ eva ubhayoḥ api śarīritvā aśarīri tva viśeṣayoḥ anupapatteḥ nirviśeṣasya ca sāmānyasya sarvatra siddhi abhāvāt kim anumānasya dūṣaṇam na kiñcid puruṣaḥ eva ayam viśeṣa abhāvāt śaśa viṣāṇāyamāne sādhana anarhe sāmānye sādhanam prayuñjānaḥ nigṛhyate yathā kaścid niśitam kṛpāṇam acchedyam ākāśam prati vyāpārayan atha anumāna dūṣaṇam vinā na tuṣyati bhavān tadānīm idam aśarīri pūrvakatva anumānam vyapti grahaka pramāṇa bādhita tvāt kāla atyaya āt iṣṭam vyāpti balena ca abhipretam aśarīri tva viśeṣam virundhat viśeṣa viruddham tata sa ca viruddha avāntara viśeṣaḥ eva iti pūrva pakṣa saṅkṣepaḥ 
NK_68.1^1	 atra pratisamādhiḥ kim śarīri tvam eva karttṛ tvam uta paridṛṣṭa sāmarthya kāraka prayojaka tvam na tāvat śarīri tvam eva karttṛ tvam suṣuptasya udāsīnasya ca katvarttṛ prasaṅgāt kintu paridṛṭa sāmarthya kāraka prayojaka tvam tasmin sati kāryya utpatteḥ tad cārīrasya api nirvahati yathā sva śarīra preraṇāyām ātmanaḥ asti tatra api asya sva karma upārjitam tat eva śarīram iti ced satyam asti param preraṇa upāyaḥ na bhavati sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt preryyatayap asti iti ced īśvarasya api preryyaḥ paramāṇuḥ asti 
NK_68.1^2	 nanu sva śarīre preraṇāyāḥ icchā prayatnābhyām utpatteḥ icchā prayatnayoḥ ca sati śarīre bhāvāt asati abhāvāt asti tasya sva preraṇāyām icchā prayatna janana dvāreṇa upāya tvam iti ced na tasya icchā prayatnayoḥ upajananam pratyeva kāraṇa tvāt labdha ātmakayoḥ icchā prayatnayoḥ preraṇākaraṇa kāle tu tad anupāya bhūtam eva śarīram karma tvāt iti vyābhicāraḥ anapekṣita śarīra vyāpārasya icchā prayatna mātra sacivasya eva cetanasya kadācid acetana vyāpāram prati sāmarthya darśanāt buddhimat avyabhicāri tu kāryya tvam iti īśvara siddhiḥ 
NK_68.2	 icchā prayatna utpattau api śarīram apekṣaṇīyam iti ced apekṣatām yatra anayoḥ āgantuka tvam yatra punar imau svābhāvikau= āsāte satra āsya apekṣaṇam vyartham na ca buddhi icchā prayatnānām nitya tve kaścid virodhaḥ dṛṣṭā hi rūpa ādīnām guṇānām āśraya bhedena dvatī gatiḥ nitya tā anitya tā ca tathā buddhi ādīnām api bhaviṣyati iti sā iyam īśvara vāde vādi prativādinoḥ api parākāṣṭhā atas param prapañcaḥ 
NK_69.1	 ātma adhiṣṭhitāḥ paramāṇvaḥ pravartiṣyati iti ced na teṣām sva karma upārjita indriya gaṇa adhīna saṃvidām śarīra utpatteḥ pūrvam sarva viṣaya avabodha virahāt asti ātmanām api sarva viṣaya vyāpi sahaja caitanyam iti ced na sahajam śarīra sambandha bhājām tat kena viplatam yena idam sarvatra apūrvavat avabhāsayati śarīra āvaraṇa tirodhānāt tad ātmani eva samādhīyate na bahirmukham bhavati iti ced vyāpaka tvena tasya viṣaya saṃbandha anucchedena nitya tvena ca viṣaya prakāśa svabhāvasya anivṛttau kā tirodhāna vācaḥ yuktiḥ vṛtti pratibandhaḥ caitanyasya tirodhānam iti ced katham tarhi śarīriṇām viṣaya grahaṇam kvacid asya vṛttayaḥ na nirudhyante iti ced kutas ayam viśeṣaḥ indriya pratyāsatti viśeṣāt yadi evam indriya adhīnaḥ caitanyasya viṣayeṣu vṛtti lobhaḥ na sannidhi mātra nibandhanaḥ sati api vyāpaka tve sarva artheṣu pravṛtti abhāvāt indriya vaiyarthya prasaṅga āt ca iti sādhu uktam aśarīriṇām ātmanām na viṣaya avabodhaḥ iti 
NK_69.2–69.3^1	 tathā ca eke vadanti parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat svayabhūḥ tasmāt parān paśyati na antarātman iti anavabodhe ca teṣām na adhiṣṭhātāraḥ iti tebhyaḥ paraḥ sarva artha darśa sahaja jñāna mayaḥ karttṛ svabhāvaḥ kaḥ api adhiṣṭhātā kalpanīyaḥ cetanam adhiṣṭhātāram antareṇa acetanānām pravṛtti abhāvāt sa kim ekaḥ anekaḥ vā ekaḥ iti vadāmaḥ bahūnām asarvajña tve asmad ādi vat asāmarthyāt sarvajña tve tu ekasya eva sāmarthyāt apareṣām anupayogāt na ca sama pradhānānām bhūyasām sarva daikamatye hetuḥ asti iti kasācid anutpattiḥ api kāryyasya syāt ekabhiprāya anurodhena sarveṣām pravṛttau ekasya eva īśvara tvam na apareṣām maṭha pariṣadām iva kāryya utpatti amurodhena sarveṣām avirodhe pratyekam anīśvara tvam tat evam kāryya viśeṣeṇa siddhasya karttṛ viśeṣasya sarvajñtvāt na kutracid vastuni viśeṣa anupalambhaḥ asti 
NK_69.3^2	 atas na tad nibandhanam mithyājñānam mithyājjāna abhāve ca na tad mūlau rāga dveṣau tayoḥ abhāvāt na tad pūrvikā pravṛttiḥ pravṛtti abhāve cana tad sādhyau dharma adharmau tayoḥ abhāvāt tad jayoḥ api sukha duḥkhayoḥ abhāvaḥ sarvadā eva ca anubhava sadbhāvāt smṛti saṃskārau api na asāte iti aṣṭaguṇa adhikaraṇaḥ bhagavān īśvaraḥ iti kecid anye tu buddhie eva tasya avyāhatā kriyā śaktiḥ iti evam vadantaḥ icchā prayatnau api anaṅgīkurvāṇaḥ ṣaḍguṇa adhikaraṇaḥ ayam iti āhuḥ sa kim baddhaḥ muktaḥ vā na tāvat baddhaḥ bandhana samājñatasya bandha hetoḥ kleśa ādeḥ asambhavāt muktaḥ api na bhavati bandha viccheda paryāya tvāt mukteḥ nityam uktaḥ tu syāt yat āha tatrabhavān patañjaliḥ kleśa karma vipāśayaiḥ aparāmṛṣṭaḥ putuṣviśeṣaḥ īśvaraḥ iti 
NK_70.1–70.4	 ākāśa kāla diśām ekaika tvāt apara jāti abhāve pāribhāṣikyaḥ tisraḥ sañjñāḥ bhavanti ākāśaḥ kālaḥ diś iti tatra ākāśasya guṇāḥ śabda saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ ākāśa ādīnām trayāṇām saḍkṣepa artham ekena granthena vaidharmyam kathayati ākāśa kāla diśām iti ākāśasya kālasya diśaḥ ca ekaika tvāt āpara jātiḥ nna asti tasyāḥ vyakta ubheda adhiṣṭhāna tvāt apara jāti abhāve ca ākāśaḥ iti kālaḥ iti diś iti tisraḥ sañjñā pāribhāṣikyaḥ na pṛthivī ādi sañjñāvat apara jāti naimittikyaḥ iti arthaḥ sañjñā eva eṣām itara vaidharmyam yasyāḥ sañjñāyā vinā nimittena śṛṅga grāhikayā saṅkrta sā pāribhāṣikī yathā ayam devadattaḥ iti yasyāḥ punar nimittam upādāya saṅketaḥ sā naimittikī iti vivekaḥ samprati prayeka nirūpaṇa artham āha tatra ākāśasya guṇāḥ iti teṣām trayāṇām madhye ākāśasya guṇāḥ śabda saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ śabda ādi guṇa yogaḥ api ākāśasya vaidharmyam 
NK_71.1	 śbdaḥ pratyakṣa tve satya kāraṇa nuṇa pūrvaka tvāt arāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt āśrayāt danyatraḥ palabdheḥ ca na sparśavat viśeṣa guṇaḥ bāhya indriya pratyakṣa tvāt ātma antara grāhya tvāt ātmanta samavāyāt ahaṅkāranā vibhakta grahaṇāt ca na ātma guṇaḥ śrotra grāhya tvāt vaiśeṣika guṇa bhāvāt ca na diś kāla manasām pariśeṣāt guṇaḥ bhūtvā ākāśasya adhigameliṅgam 
NK_71.2	 nanu ākāśasya sadbhāve kim pramāṇam pratyakṣam eva viyati patati patattriṇi cakṣuḥ vyāpāreṇa iha ayam pakṣī prāptaḥ na iha iti niyata deśa adhikaraṇā pratītiḥ iti kecid tat ayuktam arūpasya dravyasya ca akṣṣa tvā abhāvāt yaḥ api ayam adhikaraṇa pratyayaḥ tatra vitata āloka maṇḍala vyatirekeṇa na dravya antaram pratibhāti atas ākāśasya sadbhāve pariśeṣa anumānam upanyasyan chabdasya dravya antara guṇa tvam niṣedhati śabdaḥ iti 
NK_71.3	 sva āśrayasya yat samavāyi kāraṇam tad guṇa pūrvakaḥ śabdaḥ na bhavati paṭa rūpa ādi vat āśraya utpatti anantaram anutpādāt atas sukha ādi vat sparśavataḥ viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati viśeṣa guṇa tva pratiṣedhe sāmānya guṇa tvam bhaviṣyati iti na aśaṅkanīyam sāmānya viśeṣavataḥ tasya bāhya eka indriya grāhya tvena rūpa ādi vat viśeṣa guṇa tva siddheḥ pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ sparśavat viśeṣa guṇāḥ atha ca akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ paramāṇoḥ akāryya tvāt tad vyavaccheda artham pratyakṣa tve sati iti kṛtam yāvat dravyam śabdaḥ bhavati satyā iva āśraye śaṅkḥdau tasya vināśāt atas api sukha ādi vat sparśavat viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati 
NK_71.4^1	 tatra api pārthvaparamāṇu rūpa ādibhiḥ eva vyabhicāraḥ teṣām satyā iva āśraye paramāṇau agni saṃyogena vināśāt tad artham pratyakṣa tve satī iti anuvarttanīyam hetu antarañca āha āśrayāt anyatra upalabdheḥ ca sparśavat viśeṣa guṇa tve ca śabdasya śaṅkha ādiḥ āśrayaḥ vācyaḥ sa ca tasmāt anyatra dūre karṇa śaṣkulī deśe samupalabhyate na ca anya guṇasya anyatra graṇam asti tasmāt na sparśavat viśeṣa guṇaḥ nanu śaṅkha ādi deśa sthitaḥ eva śabdaḥ gṛhyate indriyāṇām āsaṃsāra maṇḍala vyāpi tvāt iti ced na saṃnikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ aviśeṣeṇa upalabdhaḥ syāt vyāpaka tve api indriyāṇām puruṣarthena hetunā kṣobhyamāṇānām yat adhiṣṭhāna deśebhyaḥ viṣaya grahaṇa anuguṇa vṛttayaḥ nirgatā viṣayam viśnuvate tadā viṣaya grahaṇasya bhāvāt na avyavasthā iti ced 
NK_71.4^2	 viṣaya grahaṇa arthāni indriyāṇi viṣaya grahaṇañca vṛtti nibandhanam vṛttyaḥ eva indriyāṇi tad anyeṣām anupayogāt niḥpramāṇaka tvāt ca na ca śrotra vṛttiḥ viṣaya deśam gatvā artham upalabhate cākṣuṣa pratītau= iva śabde api diś sandeha anupapatti prasaṅgāt na api sva āśrayam parityajya guṇasya āgamanam asti na ca śaṅkha varttinā tena antarāle śabdaḥ ārabdhavyaḥ sparśavat viśeṣa guṇasya sva āśraya ārabdhe dravye viśeṣa guṇa antara ārambha darśanāt śaṅkha ārabdhasya ca dravyasya śaṅkha śrotrayoḥ antarāle anupalambhāt na ca aprāptasya grahaṇam asti atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt śaṅkha ādi guṇa tve śabdasya anupalabdhiḥ eva asti ca tad upalabdhiḥ sā eva tasya dravya antara guṇa tvam sādhayati yasmin antarāla vyāpini śabdasya śabda antara ārambha krameṇa śrotra pratyāsannasya grahaṇam syāt 
NK_72.1	 ātma guṇa niṣedha artham āha bāhyeidriya pratyakṣa tvāt iti śrotram tāvat bāhya indriyam niyamena bāhya artha prakāśaka tvāt śakṣuḥ vat tat grahyaḥ ca śabdaḥ tad pratīteḥ tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt yaḥ tu bāhya indriya agrāhyaḥ na asau= ātma guṇaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ tasmāt ayam api na tad guṇaḥ iti arthaḥ itas api śabdaḥ na ātma guṇaḥ ātma antapa grāhya tvāt aneka pratitṛsādhāraṇa tvāt iti arthaḥ yā khalu vīṇā veṇu ādi jā śabda vyaktiḥ santati dvāreṇa ekena puruṣeṇa pratīyate sā eva apareṇa api tad deśa varttinā pratīyate na tu evam sukha ādiḥ iti ātma guṇa vaidharmyānna ātma guṇaḥ ātmani asamavāyāt api śabdaḥ na ātma guṇaḥ rūpa ādi vat ātmani asamavāyaḥ tasya asiddhaḥ iti ced na rūpa ādi vat bahirmukha tayā pratīteḥ ātma guṇānān ca antara tvena avagamāt 
NK_72.2	 itas ca na ayam ātma guṇaḥ ahaṅkāreṇa aham iti pratyayena vibhaktasya vyadhikaraṇasya grahaṇāt yaḥ khalu ātma guṇaḥ saḥ ahaṅkāra samanādhikaraṇaḥ gṛhyate yathā sukhī aham duḥkhī aham iti na tu evam śabdasya grahaṇam atas na ātma guṇaḥ priya vāc aham iti vyapadeśaḥ asti iti ced satyam kin tu tad adhiṣṭhāna śīla tayā na tu tad guṇa adhikaraṇa tvena mṛdaṅga ādi śabdeṣu tathā prati iti abhāvāt 
NK_73.1	 astu tarhi diśaḥ kālasya manasaḥ guṇaḥ tatra āha śrotra grāhya tvāt iti kim rktam syāt ye diś kāla manasām ubhaya vapdi siddhāḥ saṃyoga ādayaḥ guṇāḥ te śrotra grāhyāḥ na bhavanti ayantu tat grāhyaḥ tasmāt na tad gṛhaḥ diś kāla manasām viśeṣa guṇaḥ na asti ayantu viśeṣa guṇaḥ itas api teṣām na bhavati iti āha vaiśeṣika guṇa bhāvāt ca iti śabdaḥ diś kāla manasām guṇaḥ na bhavati viśeṣa guṇa tvāt sukha ādi vat iti prayogaḥ 
NK_74.1	 nanu ekasmin arthe aneka sādhana upanyāsaḥ vyarthaḥ ekena eva tad artha paricchedasya kṛta tvāt iti ced kim eka pramāṇau= asite pramāṇa antara vaiyarthyam phala abhāvāt puruṣeṇa apekṣita tvāt vā na tāvat phalam na asti pūva vat uttaratra api tad artha ti iti bhāvāt na api puruṣasya anapekṣā sarvatra yatra atiśaya viṣaya mādhuryyāt pratyanubhāvam sukha utpattiḥ tatra dṛṣṭe api punar punar darśana ākāṅkṣā bhavati eva yathā atyanta priya putra ādau yatra tvan apekṣā tatra api pūrvavat uttarasya api kāraṇa sadbhāve sati pravṛttasya na vaiyarthyam tad viṣaya paricchedena eva arthena arthavat tvāt piṣṭa peṣaṇe tu aśakta bhaṅga tā prāptau phakam eva na bhavati anyat api pramāṇam viṣaya pariccheda mātram eva artha kriyāyāḥ viṣaya sādhya tvāt eka paricchenne dvītīyasya sādhakatama tva abhāvaḥ iti ced na sva kāryye tasya eva sādhakatama tvāt anyathā dhārāvāhikam jñānam apramāṇam syāt viṣayasya anatirekāt pratijñānañca kālakṣaṇānām ati sūkṣmāṇām apratibhāsānāt na ca evam sati a navasthā upayoga abhāve sati virāma ādityakam 
NK_75.1	 nanu yadi nāma pṛthivī ādi dravya aṣṭaka guṇaḥ śabdaḥ na bhavati tathā api ākāśasya sadbhāve kim āyātam tatra āha pariśeṣāt iti guṇaḥ śabdaḥ guṇaḥ ca guṇinā vinā na bhavati na ca eṣa pṛthivī ādīnām guṇaḥ dravya antarañca na asti tasmāt yasya ayam guṇaḥ tadākāṣam iti pariśeṣāt ākāśasya adhigame pratipattau liṅgam iti artha nirddeśaḥ prayogaḥ punar evam dravya antara guṇaḥ śabdaḥ guṇa tve sati pṛthivī ādi aṣṭa dravya an āśrita tvāt yaḥ tu dravya as tara guṇaḥ na bhavati na asau guṇa tve sati pṛthivī ādi aṣṭa dravyān āśritaḥ yathā rūpa ādiḥ iti vyatirekī 
NK_75*.1–75*.4	 śabda liṅga aviṣa īśāt eka tvam siddham tad anuvidhānāt eka pṛthaktvam vibhava vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam śabda kāraṇa tva vacanāt saṃyoga vibhāgau iti atas guṇavat tvāt anāśrita tvāt ca dravyam samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇa abhāvāt ca nityam sarva prāṇinām ca śabda upalabdhau namittam śrotra bhāvena śrotram punar śravaṇa vivara sañjñakaḥ nabhaḥ deśaḥ śabda nimitta upabhoga prāpaka dharma adharma upanibaddhaḥ tasya ca nitya tve sati upanibandhaka vaikalyāt bādhiryyam iti 
NK_75*.5	 sadbhāva pratipādakāt eva pramāṇāt ākāśasya śabda guṇa tvam tāvat pratītam samprati saṅkhyā ādi guṇa tva pratipādana arhram āha śabda liṅga aviśeṣāt iti śabdaḥ hi liṅgam ākāśasya śabdaḥ ca sarvatra aviśiṣṭaḥ ekaḥ iti eka rūpam eva ākāśam ṣddhyati bheda pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāvāt iti arthaḥ nanu śabdaḥ api tāratara ādi rūpeṇa vividhaḥ eva satyam na tu tena rūpeṇa asya liṅgatā kintu guṇa tvena tat ca aviśiṣṭam na āśraya bheda avagamāya prabhavati eka smāt api āśrayāt kāraṇa bhedena tāratara ādi bhedasya śabdasya utpatti avirodhāt 
NK_75*.6	 tad anuvidhānāt ekāṛthaktvam iti ekatva anuvidhānāt eka pṛthaktvam asti ca ākāśe bheda pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāvāt sarva siddham eka tvam tena pṛthaktvam api siddham iti arthaḥ kecid vastunaḥ nijam svarūpam eva eka tvam na tu saṅkhyā viśeṣaḥ iti āhuḥ teṣām ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti saha prayoga anupapattiḥ paryyātvāt ye api padārthānām svābhāvikam eka pṛthaktvam iti āhuḥ teṣām api pratiyogi anusandhāna rahitasya ekatva vikalpa vat pṛthaktu a vikalpaḥ api prāpnoti na ca evam syāt ayam asmāt pṛthak iti pṛthaktvasya vikalpanāt tasmāt na tayoḥ ekatvam 
NK_75*.7	 vibhava vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam iti dravya tvāt āvākāśasya parimāṇa yogi tve siddhe vibhavavān mahān ākāśaḥ iti sūtra kāra vacanāt parama mahat tvam ākāśe siddham yat vibhu tat parama mahat yathā ātmā vibhu ca ākāśam tasmāt etat api parama mahat vibhu tvam sarva gata tvam tad ākāśasya kutas siddham iti ced sarvatra śabda utpādāt tadi ākāśam vyāpakam na bhavati tadā sarvatra śabda utpattiḥ nna syāt samavāyi kāraṇa abhāve kāryya utpatti abhāvāt divi bhuvi antarikṣe ca upajātāḥ śabdāḥ rka artha samavetāḥ śabda tvāt śrūyamāṇa ādya śabda vat śrūyamāṇa ādya śabdayoḥ ca eka artha samavāyaḥ kāryya kāraṇa bhāvena pratyeyavyaḥ vyadhikaraṇasya asamavāyikāraṇa tva abhāvāt 
NK_75*.8–75*.9	 śabda kāraṇa tva vacanāt saṃyoga bhāgau iti saṃyogāt vibhāgāt śabdāt ca śabdasya niṣpattiḥ iti sūtreṇa ākāśa guṇam śabdam prati saṃyoga vibhāgau kāraṇam iti uktam tena ākāśe saṃyoga vibhāgau siddhau vyadhikaraṇasya asamavāyikāraṇa tva abhāvāt atas guṇavat tvāt anāśrita tvāt ca dravyam yatas ākāśam guṇavat atas guṇava tvāt dravyam ghaṭa ādi vat na kevalam guṇavat tvāt ākāśam dravyam anāśrita tvāt ca dravyam paramāṇu vat samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇa abhāvāt ca nityam iti samāna jātīyam samavāyi kāraṇam asamāna jātī yam asamavāyi kāraṇam nimitta kāraṇañca teṣām abhāvāt nityam 
NK_75*.10–75*.11^1	 sarva prāṇinām śabda upalabdhau nimittam iti nanu evam sarveṣām sarva śabda upalabdhiḥ ākāśasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt atas āha śrotra bhāvena iti kim punar śro traṃtatra āha śrotram punar iti śrūyate anena iti śravaṇam śravaṇañca tad vivarañcā iti śravaṇa vivaram tat eva saṃjñā yasya nabhaḥ deśasya sa nabhaḥ deśaḥ śrotra tad pidhāne śabdasya anupakambhāt tasya viśeṣaṇam āha śabda nimitta ityādinā śabda nimittaḥ upabhogaḥ sukha duḥkha anubhavaḥ tasya prapakābhyām dharma adharmābhyām upanibaddhaḥ saha kṛtaḥ iti 
NK_75*.11^2	 ayam arthaḥ yasya bāhya ekaika indriya grāhya viśeṣa guṇa grāhakam yat indriyam tad tad guṇakam yathā rūpa grāhakam cakṣu rūpa adhikaraṇam śrotrañca tathābhūtasya śabdasya grāhakam tasmāt tat api śabda guṇakam śbdaḥ ca ākāśa guṇaḥ iti nirṇītam tena ākāśam eva tāvat śotram tat ca vyāpakam api na sarvatra śabdam upalambhayati praṇinām adṛṣṭa vaśena karṇa śaṣkulī adhiṣṭhāna niyatasya eva tasyensriya tvāt yathā sarva gata tve api ātmanaḥ deha pradeśe jñātṛ tvam na anyatra śarīrasya upabhortha tvāt anyathā tasya vaiyarthyāt nanu evam api badhirasya śabda upalabdhiḥ syāt karṇa śaṣkulī sadbhāvāt atra āha tasi ca iti tasya ākāśasya nitya tve api upanibandhakayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ sahakāri bhūtayoḥ vaikalyāt abhāvāt bādhiryyam iti śabdaḥ samāptau 
NK_76.1–76.2	 kālaḥ parāpara vyatikara yaugapadya ayaugapadi acira kṣipra pratyaya liṅgaḥ teṣām viṣayeṣu pūrva pratyaya vilakṣaṇānām utpattau= anya nimitta abhāvāt yat atra nimittam sa kālaḥ sarvat kāryyaṇāñca utpatti sthiti vināśa hetuḥ tad vyapadeśāt kṣaṇa lava nimeṣa kāṣṭhākalā muhūrttayāmāhorātra arddha māsa māsaṛtu ayana saṃvatsara yuga kalpa manvantara pralayam apralaya vyavahāra hetuḥ ca 
NK_76.3–76.4	 kālasya nirūpaṇa artham āha kālaḥ iti diś viśeṣa apekṣayā yaḥ paraḥ tasmin aparaḥ iti pratyayaḥ yaḥ ca aparaḥ tasmin paraḥ iti pratyayaḥ para aparayoḥ vyatikaraḥ vyatyayaḥ tathā ca yugapad pratyayaḥ ayugapad pratyayat ca kṣipra pratyayaḥ cira pratyayaḥ ca kālaliṅgam nanu kālasya apratyakṣa tvāt tena saha yugapad ādi pratyayānām vyāpti grahaṇa abhāvāt kutas liṅga tvam atas āha teṣām iti teṣām yugapad a ādi pratyayānām viṣayeṣu dravya ādiṣu pūrva pratyaya vilakṣaṇa ānāna dravya ādi pratyaya vilakṣaṇānām utpattau= anyasya nimittasya abhāvāt etat uktam bhāvati dravya ādiṣu viṣayeṣu pūrva apara ādi pratyayāḥ jāyante na ca eṣām dravya ādayaḥ nimittam tad pratyaya vilakṣaṇa tvāt na ca nimittam antareṇa kāryyasya utpattiḥ asti tasmāt yat atra nimittam kālaḥ iti āditya parivarttana alpīyaḥ tu anibandhanaḥ yuvastha vipiṇḍābhyām parāpara vyavahāraḥ iti eke tat ayuktam āditya parivarttanasya yuvasthavirayoḥ sambandha abhāvāt asamgaddhasya nimitta tve ca atiprasaṅgāt 
NK_77.1^1	 sahabhāvaḥ yaugadyam iti apare tat api asaṅgatam kāla anabhyupagama saha artha abhāvāt kasyāñcid kriyāyām bhāvānām anya upratiyogi tvam saha arthaḥ iti ced na anutpanna sthita niruddhānām anya pratiyogi tva abhāvāt sahabhavatāñca pratiyogi tve kālasya apratyākhyānam eva iti uktam evam ayugapad a ādi pratyayāḥ api samarthanīyāḥ kālasya abhedāt katham pratyaya bhedaḥ iti ced sāmagridāt vastu dvayasya utpāda sadbhāvayoḥ yat ekena jñānena grahaṇaṃatat sahakāriṇā kālena parāpara pratyayau janyete bhūyasām utpāsa vyāpārayoḥ eka grahaṇa sahakāriṇā yugapad pratyayaḥ kāryyasya utpāda vināśayoḥ antarvartinām kriyā akṣaṇānām bhūyastyālpīyaḥ tu agrahaṇa sahakāriṇā cira kṣipra pratyayau iti yathāsambhavam vācyam nanu tad tad nibandhanaḥ eva astu pratyaya bhedaḥ kṛtam kālena na asti tasmin vastu utpāda abhāvāt na tāvat atyanta sataḥ gaganasya utpādaḥ na api atyanta asataḥ nara viṣāṇasya kintu prāc asataḥ 
NK_77.1^2	 kāla asattve ca abhāva viśeṣaṇasya prāc śabda arthasya abhāvāt na ayam viśeṣaḥ siddhyati iti na kasyacid utpattiḥ syāt apratyakṣeṇa kālena katham viśiṣṭā pratītiḥ iti ced tatra āha kaścid viśiṣṭa pratyayasya utpattā visdriya vat kāraṇa tvam kālasya na tu daṇḍa vat viśeṣaṇa tvam iti tat api asāram bodha eka svabhāvasya jñānasya viṣaya sambandham antareṇa viśeṣaṇa antara abhāvāt tasmāt anyathā ucyate yuvastha viratoḥ śarīra avasthā bhedena tad kāraṇa tayā kāla saṃyoge anumite sati paścāt tayoḥ kāla viśiṣṭa tā avagatiḥ pratyetuḥ eka tvāt pramāṇa antara upanītasya api viśeṣaṇa tva avirodhāt yathā surabhi candanam iti yathā vā mīmāṃsakānām aghaṭam bhū talam iti ghaṭa ādiṣu tu mūrtta dravya tvena avasthā ābhena vā śarīra vat kāla sambandhe anumite tad viśiṣṭaḥ yugapad ādi pratyayaḥ jātaḥ paścāt kāryya tva ādi vipratipannam pratikāla liṅga tvam iti anavadyam 
NK_77.2	 sarva kāryyāṇāñca utpatti vināśa hetuḥ atra yuktim āha tad vyapadeśāt iti tena kālena utpatti ādīnām vyapadeṣīnām vyapadeśāt utpatti kālaḥ vināśa kālaḥ iti ādi vyapadeśāt kālasya tatra hetu tvam iti arthaḥ kāryya antaram api tasya kathayati kṣaṇalava ityādi nimeṣasya caturthaḥ bhāgaḥ kṣaṇaḥ kṣaṇa dvayana lavaḥ akṣi pakṣma karma upalakṣita kālaḥ nimeṣaḥ ityādi gaṇi tathā astra anusāreṇa pratyetavyam 
NK_78.1–78.5	 tasya guṇāḥ saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt eka tvam siddham radanu vidhānāt pṛthaktvam kāreṇe kālaḥ iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam kāraṇa paratva ādi vacanāt saṃyogaḥ tad vināśaka tvāt vibhāgaḥ iti tasya ākāśa vat dravya tva nitya tve siddhe kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt añjasā eka tve api sarva kāryyāṇām prārambha kripa abhinirvrptti sthiti nirodha upābhedāt maṇi vat pācaka vat vā nānātva upacāraḥ iti evam dhrmmiṇi siddhe tasya guṇān kathayati tasya guṇāḥ iti 
NK_78.6^1	 kālasya sravya tvāt saṅkhyā ādi yoge siddhe tad viśeṣa pratipādana artham āha kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt iti kālasya liṅgānām yugapad a ādi pratyayānām aviśeṣāt eka tvam kālasya bhede pramāṇa antara abhāvāt iti arthaḥ nanu yugapad a ādi pratyaya bhedaḥ eva tad abheda pratipādakaḥ na evam kāla abhede api sahakāri bhedāt pratyaya bheda upapatteḥ tad anuvidhānāt pṛthaktvam iti eka tvasya pṛthaktvā anuvidhānam sāharyyam iyamaḥ tena ekatvāt pṛthaktva siddhiḥ kāraṇe kālaḥ iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam iti anena kāraṇe kālakhāḥ iti sutram lakṣayati 
NK_78.6^2–78.7	 yugapad ādi prayayānām kāraṇe kāla ākhyā kāla sañjjā iti sūtra arthaḥ tena vyāpakaḥ kālaḥ labhyate yugapad ādi pratyayānām sarvatra bhāvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ kāraṇa paratvāt iti vacanāt saṃyogaḥ iti kāraṇa para tvāt kāraṇa aparatvāt ca paratva aparatve iti sūtre kāraṇa paratva va śabdena kāla piṇḍa saṃyogaḥ abhihitaḥ tena asya saṃyoga guṇa tvam siddham tad vināśaka tvāt vibhāgaḥ iti tasya saṃyogasya kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam vināśe vibhāgaḥ vināśakaḥ sarvatra āśraya vināśa abhāvāt atas kāle vibhāga siddhiḥ vyadhikaraṇasya vibhāgasya avināśaka tvāt tasya ākāśa vat dravya tva nitya tve siddhe yathā guṇavat tvāt anāśrita tvāt ca ākāśam dravyam tathā kālaḥ api yathā samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇa abhāvāt ca nityam ākāśam tathā kālaḥ api 
NK_78.8	 tadi ekaḥ kālaḥ katham tatra aneka vyapadeśaḥ iti āha kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt iti kāla liṅgānām parāpara ādi pratyayānām aviśeṣāt bheda apratipādaka tvāt añjasā mukhyayā vṛttyā kālasya ekatve siddhe nānā tva upacārāt nānātva vyapadeśaḥ kutas sarveṣām kāryyāṇām ārambhaḥ upakramaḥ kriyāyāḥ abhinirvṛttiḥ kriyāyāḥ parisamāptiḥ sthitiḥ svarūpa avasthānam nirodhaḥ vināśaḥ eṣām upādhīnām bhedāt nānātva vyapadeśaḥ yathā ekaḥ maṇiḥ sphaṭika ādiḥ nīla ādi upādhi bhedāt nīlaḥ iti pītaḥ iti vyapadiśyate tathā kālaḥ api aikaḥ eva upādhi bhedāt ārambha kāla iti kriyā abhivyakti kāle iti kriyā abhivyakti kāle iti kriyā sthiti kālaḥ iti nirodha kālaḥ iti vyapadiśyate iti arthaḥ maṇeḥ upādhi dambandhaḥ na vāstavaḥ kālasya tu kriyā sambandhaḥ vāstavaḥ iti pratipādayitum dṛṣṭānta antaram āha pācaka vat vā iti yathā ekasya puruṣasya pacana ādi kriyā rogāt pācakaḥ iri pāṭhakaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ tathā kālasya api na tu prārambha ādi kriyā eva kālaḥ vilakṣaṇa buddhi vedya tvāt iti 
NK_79.1–79.2	 diś pūrva apara ādi pratyaya liṅgāḥ mūrtta dravyam avadhi kṛtvā mūrtteṣu eva dravyeṣu etasma ādi dam pūrveṇa dakṣiṇena paścimena uttareṇa pūrva dakṣiṇena pūrva dakṣiṇena daksiṇa apareṇa apara uttareṇa uttara pūrveṇa ca adhastāt upariṣṭāt ca iti daśa pratyayāḥ yatas bhavanti sā diś iti anya nimitta asambhavāt tasyāḥ tu guṇāḥ saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ kāla vat ete siddhāḥ 
NK_79.3^1	 yugapad a ādi pratyaya liṅga tvam iva kālasya pūrva apara ādi pratyaya liṅga tvam diśaḥ vaidharmyam iti pratipādan= āha diś pūrva apara ādi pratyaya liṅga iti pūrvam iti aparam ityādi pratyayaḥ liṅgam yasyāḥ diśaḥ sā tathā uktā etat eva darśayati mūrtta dravyam ityādinā amūrttasya dravyasya na avadhi tvam na api pūrva apara ādi pratyaya viṣaya tvam asti anavacchinna parimāṇa tvāt atas idam uktam mūrtta dravyam avadhim kṛtvā mūptteṣu eva dravyeṣu idam asmāt pūrveṇa ityādi pratyayāḥ yatas bhavanti sā diś iti etasmāt idam pūrvam iti asmin eva arthe pūrveṇa iti nirddeśaḥ prātipadikā arthe tṛtīya upasaṅkhyānāt nanu pūrva apara ādi pratyayānām kāryya tvāt kāraṇam anumīyate tat tu diś eva iti kutas niścayaḥ tatra āha anya nimittā san bhavāt iti na tāvat pūrva apara ādi pratyayānām dravya mātram nimittam yathā kathañcat avasthite dravye teṣām utpatti prasaṅgāt paraspara apekṣayā dravyayoḥ utpatti nimit tve api saḥ eva doṣaḥ ubhaya abhāva pravaprasaṅgaḥ ca adhikaḥ 
NK_79.3^2	 kriyā guṇa ādi nimitta tve ca samāna guṇa kriyā ādiṣu pratyaya viśeṣaḥ na syāt tena yat eṣām nimittam sā diś iti yatra etamāt idam iti pañcamī prayujyate anyathā sā api nirviṣayā syāt avadhau= iyam pañcamī iti ced satyam kintu avadhi tvam diś apekṣayā na tu dravya mātrasya sarvatra aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt tasyāḥ apratyakṣa tve api kāla vat viśiṣṭa pratyaya hetu tvam vācyam guṇavat tvam dravya lakṣaṇam tat asyām asti iti pratipādayan āha tasyāḥ tu guṇāḥ ityādi kāla vat ete siddhāḥ yathā kāla liṅga aviśeṣāt kālasya ekatvam siddham tathā diś liṅga avaśeṣāt diḥ eka tvam yathā tad anuvidhānāt kāle pṛthaktvam atathā diśi yathā a kāraṇe kālaḥ iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam tathā kāraṇe diś iti vacanāt diśaḥ parama mahat parimāṇam sarvatra tad kāryyasya pūva apara ādi pratyayasya bhāvāt yathā kāraṇa para tvāt kāraṇa aparatvāt ca kālasya saṃyoga guṇava tvam pratipāditam tathā diśaḥ api yathā saṃyoga vināśaka tvāt kāle vibhāgaḥ siddhaḥ tathā diśi iti atideśa arthaḥ 
NK_80.1	 diś liṅga aviśeṣāt añjasā eka tve api siśaḥ parama mahā ṛṣibhiḥ śruti smṛti loka saṃvyavahāra artham merum pradakṣiṇam āvarttamānasya bhagavataḥ savituḥ ye saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ lokapāla parigṛhīta dikrpradeśānām anvarthāḥ prācya ādi bhedena daśavidhāḥ sañjñāḥ kṛtāḥ tatas bhaktyā daśa diśaḥ siddhāḥ tāsām eva devatā parigraha vaśāt punar daśa sañjñāḥ bhavanti māhendrī vaiśvānarī yāmyāḥ nairṛtī vāruṇī kauberī aiśānī brāhmī nāgī ca iti 
NK_80.2	 nanu diś liṅga aviśeṣaḥ na siddhaḥ pūrva apara ādi pratyayānām para sparataḥ bhedāt tathā ca sati dibho bhedaḥ iti yuktam na ekasmimm eva arthe yugapad vastu antarā apekṣayā pūrva apara ādi pratyaya utpatteḥ diś bhede hi yat pūrvam na tatra paścima pratyayaḥ bhavet sarva didsambandhaḥ tasya asti iti ced tarhi sarva artheṣu sarva apekṣayā sarveṣām sarve pratyayāḥ prasajyeran na ca evam tasmāt ekā diś pratyaya bhedaḥ tu upādhi bhedāt 
NK_80.3^1	 prathama āditya saṃyogasya tad ā ārjava avasthitasya ca dravyasya antarāle pūk iti vyavahāraḥ madhyāhna saṃyogasya tad ā ārjava avasthitasya ca antarāle dakṣiṇā iti astamaya saṃyogasya tad ā ārjava avasthitasya ca dravyasya antarāle paścimā iti yatra āditya saṃyogaḥ na dṛśyate tatra madhyāhna saṃyoga praguṇa avasthita drāpa īkṣayā uttara vyavahāraḥ tāsām antarāleṣu pūrva dakṣiṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ iti upapadyate pratīti bhedaḥ āditya saṃyoga nibandhanaḥ eva astu pratyayaḥ na tasya mūrtta dravya saṃyoga abhāvāt asambaddhasya ca pratyaya hetutva asambhavāt etat eva darśayati diś liṅga aviśeṣāt iti diśaḥ eka tve sthite api mahā ṛṣibhiḥ prācī ādi bhedena daśavidhāḥ sañjñāḥ kṛtāḥ kīdṛśyaḥ tāḥ anvarthāḥ anugataḥ arthaḥ yāsām iti sā anvarthāḥ keṣām arthaḥ tāsu anugataḥ lokapālaiḥ indra ādadibhiḥ parigṛhītānām diś pradeśānām 
NK_80.3^2	 savituḥ ye saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ teṣām iti adhyāhāraḥ tathā hi prathamam asya amañcati savitā iti prācī avāgañcati iti avācī udagañcati iti udīcī kim viśiṣṭasya savituḥ merum pradakṣiṇam āvarttamānasya merum pradikṣiṇam paribhramataḥ kimartham sañjñāḥ kṛtāḥ śrutiḥ ca smṛtiḥ ca lokaḥ ca teṣām saṃvyavahāra artham samyak vyavahāra artham śrautaḥ vyavahāraḥ na pratīcīśirāḥ śayīta ityādiḥ smārttaḥ vyavahāraḥ āyuṣyam praṅmukhaḥ bhuṅkte iti ādiḥ loka vyavahāraḥ pūrvam gaccha dakṣiṇam avalokayā ityādiḥ yatas dāśa sañjñā kṛtāḥ tatas bhaktyā upacāreṇa daśa diśaḥ siddhāḥ vyavasthitāḥ māhendri ādi saṃjñāḥ tu na artha antara viṣayāḥ kintu tāsām eva nimitta antara vaśāt pravarttante iti āha tāsām eva ityādi mahā indrasya iyam iti māhendrī vaiśvānarasya iyam vaiśvānarī ityādi sarvatra nirvacanīyam 
NK_81.1–81.2^1^1	 ātma tva abhisambandhāt ātmā tasya saukṣmyāt apratyakṣa tve sati karaṇaiḥ śabda ādi upalabdhi anumitaiḥ śrotra ādibhiḥ samadhigamaḥ kriyate vā asya ādīnām iva karaṇānām karttṛ prayojya tva darśanāt śabda ādināt śabda ādiṣu prasiddhyā ca prasādhakaḥ anumīyate yasya tattva jñanam niḥśreyasāya ghaṭate viparyyaya jñānam saṃsāra hetuḥ yad arthāni ca bhūtāni tad pratipādana artham āha ātma tva abhisaṃbandhāt ātmā iti ātma tvam nāma sāmamnyam tad abhisambandhāt ātmā iti vyavahāraḥ iti arthaḥ idam asya itarebhyaḥ vaidharmyam 
NK_81.1–81.2^1^2	 nanu dṛśyasya sattvam tad ākāra saṃvedanena vyāptam na ca ātma ākāram kasyacid saṃvedanam asti atas vyāpaka anupalabdhyā tasya sattvam eva nirākriyate kutas dharma nirūpaṇam iti āśaṅkya tad sadbhāve bādhakam pramāṇam na asti pratyakṣa anupalabdheḥ anyathā siddha tvāt sādhakañca pramāṇam anumānam asti iti pratipādayan āha tasya iti pratyakṣa upalabdhi yogya tā virahaḥ saukṣmyam tasmāt apratyakṣasya ātmanaḥ karaṇaiḥ śabda ādi upalabdhayaḥ karaṇa sādhyāḥ kriyā tvāt chidi kriyāvat iti anumitaiḥ śrotra ādibhiḥ samadhigamaḥ kriyate kutas iti āha vā asya ādīnām karaṇānām karttṛ prayojya tva darśanāt 
NK_81.2^2	 yat karaṇam tat kenacid kartrā prayujyate kārye vyāpātyate yathā vā asya ādikam vardhakiṇā karaṇañca śrotra ādikam tasmāt kenacid kartrā prayoktavyam yaḥ eṣām prayoktā saḥ ātmā ākāśasya śrotrasya yadi api ātmanā saha sākṣāt sambandhaḥ na asti vibhu tvāt tathā api ātmanā tasya prayojya tvam antaḥkaraṇa adhiṣṭhānat vāreṇa yathā hastena sandaṃśa saṃyoginā tad saṃyuktasya ayaḥ piṇḍasya saṃyogaḥ karaṇa tvañca śrotra ādīnām niyata arthasya grāhaka tvāt pradīpa vat yadi api ātmā aham mama iti sva karmaā upārjita kārya kāraṇa sambandha upādhi kṛta karttrptva svāmi tva rūpa sambhinnaḥ manasā saṃvedyate tatḥpi atra aprakṣa tva vācaḥ yuktiḥ bāhya indriya abhiprāyeṇa śabda ādiṣu prasiddhyā ca prasādhakaḥ anumīyate śabda ādiṣu viṣayeṣu yā prasiddhiḥ jñānam tatra api prasādhakaḥ jñātā anumīyate jñānam ca kvacid āśritam kriyā tvāt chidi kriyā vat yatra idam āśritam saḥ ātmanā 
NK_81.3^1	 atha idam svayam eva jānāti na para āśritam iti ced kim idam nityam pratikṣaṇa vināśi vā yadi nityam sañjñābheda mātram atha kṣaṇikam cira anubhūtasya na smaraṇam pratipattṛ bhedāt yat tu kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt pūrvakṣaṇa anubhūtasya uttareṇa smaraṇam yaypunar pitrā anubhūtasya putreṇa asmaraṇam tatra pitṛ putra jñānayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhāvāt śarīrayoḥ ca tathābhūtayoḥ acetana tvāt tat ayuktam ātma abhāve kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya aniścayāt kāraṇa vijñāna kāle kārya jñānam anāgatam tad kāle ca kāraṇam atītam na ca tābhyām anyaḥ kaścid ekaḥ draṣṭā asti iti kaḥ tayoḥ krama bhāvinoḥ kāryya kāraṇa bhāvam pratīyāt 
NK_81.3^2	 atha katam sva ātma grāhiṇī pūrvā buddhiḥ sva ātma avyatiriktam svasya kāraṇa tvam ati rūpam gocarayati uttarā api buddhiḥ sva rūpa viṣayā tat avyatiriktam ātmīyam kāryya tvam api gṛhṇāti tābhyāñca pratyekam upāttam kāraṇa tvam kāryya tvam ca tad ubhaya janita eka vāsanā bala bhuvā vikalpena adhyavasīyate iti ced aho kusrpṣṭi kalpanā pūrva uttapa dhiyau sva ātma mātra niyate kutas tasyāḥ kāraṇam aham asyāḥ ca asmi kāryyam iti pratīyetām paraspara vārttā anabhijña tvāt tābhyām agṛhītam ca kutas adhyavasyati tasya anubhava anusāri tvāt 
NK_82.1–82.3^1^1	 na śarīra indriya manasām ajña tvāt na śarīrasya caitanyam ghaṭa ādi dbhūta kāryya tvāt mṛte ca asambhavāt na indriyāṇām karaṇa tvāt upahateṣu viṣayāsān nidhye ca anusmṛti darśanāt bhavatu para āśritam jñānam tat adhikaraṇantu śarīram indriyam manaḥ vā bhaviṣyati tatra āha na śarīra indriya manasām iti uttara vākya sthitam caitanyan iti padam iha samvaddhyate śarīra indriya manasām caitanyam na bhavati kutas tatra āha ajña tvāt iti jñānam prati samavāyi kāraṇa tva abhāvāt iti arthaḥ nanu etat api sādhya aviśiṣṭam iti āśaṅkhyāhāḥ na śarīrasya iti 
NK_82.1–82.3^1^2	 caitanyam śarīrasya na bhavati ghaṭāvat śarīrasya bhūta kāryya tvāt yat bhūta kāryam na tad cetanam yathā ghaṭaḥ bhūtakāryyañca śarīram tasmāt etat api acetanam yukti antarāha mṛte ca asambhavāt iti mṛte śarīre caitanyasya asambhavāt iti anena ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvam vivakṣitam caitanyam śarīrasya viśeṣa guṇaḥ na bhavati ayāvat sravya bhāvi tvāt saṃyoga vat atas eva tad kāraṇāni api acetanāni teṣām caitanye kāryye api caitanyam syāt ekasmin śarīre jñātṛ bahutvañca prāpnoti tatas ca eka abhiprāyeṇa pravṛtti niyama abhāva ādi doṣaḥ 
NK_82.3^2	 nedriyāṇam karaṇa tvāt iti indriyāṇi acetanāni karaṇa tvāt daṇḍa vat hetu antarañca samuccinoti upahateṣu iti vinaṣṭeṣu api indriyeṣu pūrva anubhūtaḥ arthaḥ smaryyate na ca anubhavitari vinaṣṭe smaraṇam yuktam tasmāt na indriya guṇaḥ jñānam na ca viṣayasya pūrva anubhūtasya asāt nidhye api smṛtiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ bāhya indriyāṇām prāpya kāri tvāt tasmāt smṛtiḥ tāvat na indriyāṇām tad abhāvāt anubhāvaḥ api na syāt anyasya anubhave anyasya asmaraṇāt iti arthāḥ atas eva viṣayasya api na caitanyam naṣṭe viṣaye tad smaraṇā yogāt itas api na tasya caitanyam tad deśa ijñānasya tad janyasya ca sukha ādeḥ ananubhavāt buddhi pūrvvaka ceṣṭā viśeṣa abhāvāt ca na ca indriya caitanye viṣaya caitanye ca rūpam aham adrākṣam rasam anvabhavam sparśam spṛśāmi gandham ghrāsyāmi iti rūpa ādi pratyayānām eka kartṛ tva pratipatti sambhavaḥ rūpa ādīnām cakṣupādīnāñca bhedāt 
NK_83.1–83.2	 na api manasaḥ karaṇa antara anapekṣi tve yugapad āloca smṛti prasaṅgāt svayam karaṇa bhāvāt ca pariśeṣāt ātma kāryya tvāt tena ātmā samadhigamyate astu tarhi manaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam tasya sarva viṣaya tve nitya tve ca pratisandhāna ādi upapatteḥ tatra āha na api manasaḥ iti jñātṛ manaḥ yadi cakṣuḥ ādi vyatiriktam kāraṇa antaram apekṣya rūpa ādīn pratyeti sañjñā bheda mātre vivādaḥ yat apekṣaṇīyam tat manaḥ yat ca jñāna adhikaraṇam manaḥ saḥ asmākam ātmā iti atha na apekṣate karaṇa antaram tadā rūpa rasa ādiṣu indriya sambaddheṣu yugapad a ālocanāni prasajyante kāraṇa yaugapadyāt karaṇa antara apeṣāyām tu tasya aṇu tve sarva indriyeṣu sānnidhi ugapad a ālocana anutpattiḥ tathā antaḥkaraṇa abhāve yugapad smaraṇāni syuḥ apekṣaṇīya abhāvāt karaṇa apekṣāyām tu tad saṃyogasya yugapada sāmarthyāt krameṇa smṛti utpattiḥ 
NK_83.3–83.4	 yat tu uktam kenacid ekasya nityasya krama yauga padtābhyām akaraṇam iti tat ayuktam yugapad karaṇa asambhavāt uttara kālam akaraṇañca kartta vya ābhāt na ca etāvatā tasyāḥ sattvaḥ artha kriyā kāritva vyatiriktasya sattvayā iṣṭa tvāt itas api manaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam na bhavati manasaḥ svayam karaṇa tvāt iti āha svayam karaṇa bhāvāt ca iti manaḥ cetanam na bhavati karaṇa tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat iti asiddham manasaḥ karaṇa tvam karttṛ tva abhyupagamāt iti ced manasā karttṛ tve rūpa ādi pratītau cakṣuḥ ādi vat sukha ādi pratītau karaṇa antaram mṛgyam kriyāyāḥ karaṇam antareṇa anupajananāt tathā sati ca sañjñābheda mātram karttuḥ karaṇasya ca ubhayoḥ api siddha tvāt 
NK_83.5	 itas api acetanam manaḥ mūrtta tvāt loṣṭa vat yadi śarīra indriya manasām guṇaḥ jñānam na bhavati tathā api ātma siddhau kim āyātam tatra āha pariśeṣāt iti jñānam tāvat kāryya tvāt kasyacid samavāyi kāraṇasya kāryyam śarīra indriya manasā añca tad āśraya tvam pratiṣiddham na ca anyeṣām vakṣyamāṇena nyāyena jñāna kāraṇa tva prasaktiḥ asti atas pariśeṣāt ātma kāryyam jñānam ātma kāryya tvāt ca tana jñānena ātmā samadhigamyate iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
NK_83.6	 nanu sarvam etat asambaddham kṣaṇika tvena āśraya āśrayi bhāva abhāvāt tathā hi sattvam artha kriyā kāritvam tat ca krama yaugapadyābhyām vyāptam kramākramān ātmakasya prakāra antarasya asambhavāt aneka artha kriyāṇām aneka kālatā hi kramaḥ yaugapadyam ca eka kāla tā na ca eka an ekābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ asti paraspara viruddhayoḥ eka pratiṣedhasya itara vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt akṣaṇika tve tu na krama sambhavaḥ samarthasya kṣepā yogāt asamarthasya kāla antare api ajanaka tvam svabhāvasya anivṛtteḥ kramavat mahakāri lābhāt krameṇa karaṇam tasya iti ced 
NK_84.1	 atra vadanti yadi sahakāriṇaḥ bhāva atiśayam na janayanti na apekṣaṇīyāḥ akiñcatkara tvāt janayanti ced sa kim bhāva vyatiriktaḥ avyatiriktaḥ vā vyatirikta pakṣe tāvat atiśayāt eva āgantukāt anvaya vyatirekābhyām kārya utpattiḥ iti akṣaṇikasya na hetu tvam sati api tasmin= abhāvāt sahakāri kṛta āśaya sahitasya tasya janaka tvam iti ced atiśayasya atiśaya anārambhe kīdṛśī sahāyate ārambhe ca anavasthāyāḥ kā pratikriyā sahakāri janyaḥ atiśayaḥ sa ca akṣaṇikasya iti api subhāṣitam anupakāryya anupakārakayoḥ sambandha abhāvat bhāvāt abhinnaḥ atiśayaḥ saha kāribhiḥ kriyate iti api na pekṣalam bhāvasya pūrva utpannasya punar utpatti abhāvāt praktanaḥ hi bhāvaḥ anatiśaya ātmā nivarttate anyaḥ ca atiśaya ātmā jāyate iti ced kṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ 
NK_84.2	 nanu kṣaṇikasya api saha kāribhiḥ kim kriyate na kiñcid kimartham tarhi tena te apekṣyante kaḥ vai brūte apekṣyante iti pratyekam eva hi kārya jananāya samarthāḥ antyau= sthā bhāvinaḥ kṣaṇāḥ kā teṣām paraspara apekṣā yat tu tadānīm parasparam pratyāsīdanti tad upasarpaṇa kāraṇasya avaśyambhāva niyamāt na tu sambhūya kārya karaṇāya tad kāle ca upasarpaṇa hetu niyamaḥ teṣām vastu svābhāvyāt 
NK_84.3^1	 pratyekam samarthāḥ hetavaḥ pratyekam ekaikam eva kāryam janayeyuḥ kim iti ekam aneke kurvvanti atra api amīṣām kāraṇāni praṣṭavyāni yā ani amūni eka artha nirvarttana śīlāni prabhāvyanti vayam tu yathādṛṣṭasya vastu svabhāvasya vaktāraḥ na paryyanuyogam arhāmaḥ kāryyam ekena eva kṛtam kim apare kurvvanti iti ced na kṛtam kurvvanti kintu ekena kriyamāṇam apare api kurvvanti yatra ekam eva samartham tatra apareṣām tatra apareṣām kaḥ upayogaḥ iti ced satyam na te prekṣā pūrva kāriṇaḥ yat evam vimṛśya udāsate 
NK_84.3^2	 ekam kāryyam anekasmāt utpadyate iti durghaṭam idam kāraṇa bhedasya kādasya kāryya bheda hetu tvāt iti ced na evam sāmagrī bhedāt hi kāryya bhedaḥ na sahakāri bhedāt eka kāryya kāri tā eva sahakāritā tasmāt kṣaṇika tve na kramavatām bhāvānām krameṇa kāryya karaṇam ghaṭate durghaṭā tu akṣaṇikasya artha kriyā iti yugapad karaṇam api durghaṭam tāvat kāryya karaṇa samarthasya svabhāvasya uttara kālam api nirvṛteḥ kṛtasya karaṇam na asti karttavyañcā asya na vidyate nikhilasya kāryya kalāpasya sakṛt eva kṛta tvāt atas kṣaṇa antare na karoti iti ced tarhi ayam tadānīmasan= eva samasta artha kriyā virahāt tat evam vyāpakayoḥ krama yaugapadyayoḥ anupalambhāt akṣaṇikān nivarttamānam sattvam kṣaṇike vyavatiṣṭhate tathā ca sati sulabham kṣaṇikatva anumānam yat sat tat kṣaṇikam santi ca dvādaśa āyatanāni iti 
NK_85.1^1	 atra ucyate na sattvāt kṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ tasya vipakṣa vyāvṛtti anavagamāt yad kramyaugapadya rahitam tat asat yathā vāji viṣāṇam krama yaugapadya rahitañcākṣaṇikam iti bādhakena akṣaṇikāt krama yauga padya vyāvṛttyā sattva vyatireka pratītiḥ iti ced na akṣaṇikasya apratītau sattvasya tatas vyāvṛtti pratīti asaṃbhavāt yathā pratīyamāne jale tatra vahni dhūmayoḥ abhāva pratītiḥ evam akṣaṇike dṛśyamāne krama yaugapadya abhāvāt sattva abhāvaḥ pratyetavyaḥ na ca akṣaṇikaḥ nāma kaścid asti bhavatām yathā apratīyamāne api piśāce tatas anya vyāvṛttiḥ pratīyate stambhaḥ piśācaḥ na bhavati iti tadvat etat api bhaviṣyati iti ced na vyāvṛtteḥ anupalabdhi pramāṇa eka bocara tvāt tad vivikta itara padārtha upalabdhi svabhāvayoḥ ca anupalabdheḥ pratiyogi upalabdhim antareṇa avāt 
NK_85.1^2	 na ca sva rūpa viprakṛṣṭa tve piśācasya tatas anya vyāvṛtti pratīti sambhavaḥ katham tarhi stambhaḥ piśācaḥ na bhāvati iti pratītiḥ iti ced na ayam saṃsarga pratiṣedhaḥ kintu tādātmya pratiṣedhaḥ ayam sa ca atambha ātma tayā prasañjatasya piśācasya dṛśyava abhyanujñānāt pravarttate na anyathā yathā uktam tādātmyena yāvān niṣedhaḥ sa sarvaḥ api upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tva abhyupagamena kriyate iti tatra stambha svarūpa eka niyatā stambha pratītiḥ tad anātma vyavaccheda kāraṇam yadi stambhaḥ piśācaḥ bhavet tena api ātmanā jñātaḥ syāt na ca jñānam stambha tva vat piśāca ātmaka tvam api gṛhṇāti tasmāt ayam piśācaḥ na bhavati iti 
NK_85.2^1	 atha matam na nīla ādi vyatiriktaḥ akṣaṇikaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ vā kaścid asti kintu prāktana buddhi vedyaḥ nīla ādi kṣaṇaḥ adhunātana buddhi vedyān nīlakṣaṇāt abhedena āropyamāṇaḥ akṣaṇikaḥ iti ucyate bhedena vyavasthāpyamānaḥ tu kṣaṇikaḥ iti tatra nīla ādiṣu eva iyam kramākrama vyāvṛttyā sattva abhāva pratītiḥ yadipūrva upalabdhaḥ kṣaṇaḥ eva ayam upalabhyate tadā sampratitanīm artha kriyām prāk eva kuryyāt prāktanīm vā samprati eva na punar krameṇa kuryāt ekasya kāraka tva ākāraka tva virodhāt na api sarvam pūrvam eva karoti samprati artha kriyā rahitasya asattva prasaṅgāt iti atra api kim evam sattvasya hetoḥ vāstavaḥ vipakṣaḥ darśitaḥ kalpanā samāropitaḥ vā samarthitaḥ na tāvat vāstavaḥ vipakṣaḥ nīla ādīnām akṣaṇikasya āvāstava tvāt yena ca rūpeṇa te vastumantar tena ca artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ eva iti na vipakṣatā 
NK_85.2^2	 kalpanā samāropitaḥ tu vipakṣaḥ na vastu sādhanasya anumānasya aṅgam tasya alīka tvāt sarve eva ayam anumāna anumeya vyavahāraḥ buddhi ārūḍhena dharma dharmya ādi bhāvena iti ced na hetu hetvābhāsa vyavasthā anupapatteḥ kalpanā mātra āropitasya pakṣa ādi bhāvasya sarvatra sulabha tvāt tasmāt anumānāt vāstavīm artha gatim icchatā liṅgasya trairūpya viniścaya artham dhūma anumāna vat sarvatra pramāṇa siddhaḥ pakṣa ādi bhāvaḥ darśayitavyaḥ na kalpanā mātreṇa na ca akṣaṇikaḥ tathābhūtaḥ asti iti vyatireka asiddhiḥ tat asiddhau= anvayasya api asiddhiḥ tad pūrva āditya sādhāraṇa tvam hetoḥ api ca bādhakena akṣaṇikāt sattva vyatitekaḥ prasādhitaḥ kṣaṇika tva sattvayoḥ anvayaḥ kutas siddhyati 
NK_85.2^3	 na ca tatra vipakṣa vyāvṛtti mātreṇa hetu tvam asādhāraṇasya api hetu tva prasaṅgāt kevala vyatireki anumānañca avayam aniṣṭam akṣaṇike sattvam na bhavati iti avasthāpite arthāt kṣaṇikāśrayam sattvam iti anvaya siddhiḥ iti ced na tāvat arthāt iti sattvasya hetoḥ parāmarśaḥ asiddha anvayasya tasya adya api hetu tva abhāvāt bādhakam eva tu ubhaya vyāpāram pramāṇa antaram vyāptim prasādhayat dvādaśa āyataneṣu eva prasādhayet nirvviṣayāyāḥ vyāpteḥ pratyetum aśakyatvāt dvādaśa āyatana vyatiriktasya ca arthasya abhāvāt teṣu ca anvaya pratītau kṣaṇika tvasya api pratītiḥ sambandhi pratītinā antarīyaka tvāt sambandha pratīteḥ iti sattva vaiyarthyam 
NK_85.2^4	 pakṣe sāmānyena vyāpti grahaṇam viśeṣe sattvasya hetu tvam iti ced na nirviśeṣasya sāmānyasya prātiteḥ abhāvāt viśeṣa pariniṣṭhayoḥ ca kṣaṇika tva sattva sāmānyayoḥ pratīyamānayoḥ nīla ādi gatam kṣaṇika tvam pratītam iti sūktam sattva vaiyarthyam iti bādhakā dakṣaṇika tva vṛtti asattva vyāvṛttyoḥ vyāpti grahaṇam sattvāt tu vastu ātma ka kṣaṇika tva pratītiḥ iti ced na vyāvartti a bhedena kalpita bhedayoḥ vyāvrpttyoḥ tādātmya abhāvāt tādātmyañca anumāna aṅgam uktam vastu ātmanoḥ kṣaṇika tva sattvayoḥ tādātmyāt tad ātmaka tvena adhyavasitayoḥ api vyāvṛttyoḥ tādātmyam iti ced na vastunoḥ tādātmyasya anyatas aprasiddhau vā bādhakasya api vaiyarthyam na ca vyāvṛttyoḥ pratibandha niścaye vastu siddhiḥ asti vastu avastunoḥ bhedāt asambandhāt ca 
NK_86.1^1	 yat apktayum dharma uttareṇa ghaṭe bādhakena vyāptim prasādhya śabde sattvāt kṣaṇika tva prasādhanam iti ubhayoḥ api sarthaka tvam viṣaya bhedāt iti tatra api idam uttaram ghaṭaḥ iva śabde api bādhakasya pravṛtti avirodhāt pramāṇa antara anusaraṇam aphalam iti na ca akṣaṇikasya artha kriyā anupapattiḥ sahakāri sāhitye sati kāryya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ hi bhāvaḥ na anapekṣa kāraka svarūpaḥ tasya yathā anvaya vyatireka avagata sāmarthyāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ sannipatanti tathā kāryya utpattiḥ iti upapadyate sthirasya api krameṇa karaṇam aneka kāraṇa adhīnasya kāryyasya ekasmāt utpatti abhāvāt na ca sahakāri sāpekṣi tve sati tad kṛtāt eva atiśayāt kāryya utpatteḥ bhāvaḥ na kārakaḥ iti yuktam bhāva svarūpa anugamena kāryya utpāda darśanāt akāraka tve hi yava bījasya kṣiti udaka saṃnidhau śarībījāt yava aṅkuraḥ api syāt niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt 
NK_86.1^2	 na api sahakāriṇaḥ bhāvasya svarūpa atiśayam ādadhati kintu sahakāriṇaḥ eva te atiśayaḥ punar etasya sahakāri sāhityam anatiśayaḥ api tad abhāvaḥ eva tasmin sati tatas kāryyasya bhāvāt asatyabhāvāt janakājana kakṣaṇa bheda abhyupagamaḥ tu sarvadā avasthāna grāhi pratyakṣa bādhitaḥ su sadṛśa kṣaṇānām āvyavadhāna utpādena antarāgrahaṇāt avasthāna bhramaḥ ayam iti ced sthite kṣaṇika tve pratyakṣasya bhrānta tā tad bhrānta tve ca kṣaṇika tva sthitiḥ iti anyonya apekṣatā na ca yadi asya utpatti kāraṇam vināśa kāraṇañca anvaya vyatirekābhyām avagatam tayoḥ abhāve tasya ūrpatti vināśa kalpanā yuktāḥ nirhetukaḥ vināśaḥ bījam api bījasya kāraṇam iti ca asiddham
