NK_86.1^3	 aṅkura janakam bījam bīja kṛtam na bhavati bīja tvāt śāli stambha m ūrddha sthita bīja vat nirbhāgam vastu tasya kāraka tvam akāraka tvañca iti aṃśau= anupapannau iti ced yat kiñcid etat yathā vahnet ahim prati kāraka tvam akāraka tvañca snānam prati na ca tābhyām asya svarūpa bhedaḥ tathā ekasya eva bhavasya saha kāri bhāvāt kāraka tvam akāraka tvañca tad abhāvāt katham anyasya sannidhau= anyasya kāraka tvam kāraka tve api kasyacid eva na sarvasya iti ced atra vastu svabhāvāḥ paryyanuyoktavyāḥ 
NK_86.2^1	 vayantu yatra yeṣām anvaya vyatirekābhyām sāmarthyam avagacchāmaḥ tatra teṣām eva sāmagrībhāvam abhyupagacchantaḥ na upālambham arhāmaḥ tvad pakṣe api kṣiti udaka bījānām eva aṅkura utpattau sahakāritā na apareṣām tatra api vastu svabhāvāt aparaḥ kaḥ hetuḥ pratyekam eva bīja ādayaḥ samarthāḥ na paraspara sahakāriṇaḥ iti ced kimartham tarhi kṛṣī balaḥ parikarṣitāyām bhūmau bījam āvapati udakañcāsiñcati paraspara ādhipatyena tebhyaḥ pratyekam aṅkura janana yogyakṣaṇa upajananāya iti ced yadi aṅkura janana yogyakṣaṇa upajananāya bījam sva hetubhyaḥ samartham upajātam kim avani salilābhyām atha asamartham tathā api tayoḥ akiñcitkaraḥ sannidhiḥ svabhāvasya aparityāgāt kṣiti udakābhyām bījasya sva santāna varttinya samartha kṣaṇa antara ārambhaṇa śaktiḥ niruddhyate iti ced 
NK_86.2^2	 astu tasmāt asamartha kṣaṇa anutpattiḥ samartha kṣaṇa utpattiḥ tu duelabhā kāraṇa abhāvāt na ca svabhāva bhūtāyāḥ śakteḥ asti nirodhaḥ bhāvasya api nirodha prasaṅgāt sa hetukaḥ ca vināśaḥ prāpnoti viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa utpādana śakti ādhānañca bījasya aśakyam kṣiṇika tvāt svabhāva vyatirikta śakti utpādane ca utpanna utpādana prasaṅgāt tasmāt asamarthasya utpādavataḥ na kadācid kriyā samarthasya utpāda anantaram eva karaṇam iti dvayī gatiḥ na tu artha antara sāhitye sati karaṇam tasya anupayogāt atha matam ekasmāt kāryya anutpatteḥ bbahubhyaḥ ca tad urpatti darśanāt sahitānām eva sāmarthyam iti kim iti evam vadadbhyaḥ asmabhyam krudhyati bhavan tat evam akṣaṇikasya api artha kriyā upapatteḥ anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ 
NK_86.3	 yat api uktam kṛtakānām bhāvānām avaśyambhāvī vināśaḥ tena api śakyam kṣaṇika tvam anumātum tathā hi yadi eṣām dhruva bhāvī tatra teṣām kāraṇa antara apekṣā na asti yathā śara kṛpāṇa ādīnām loha maya tve dhruva bhāvī ca kṛtakānām vināśaḥ iti anumānam vināśasya hetu antarāyatta tām pratikṣipati ye hi hetu antara sā apekṣāḥ na te dhruva bhāvinaḥ yathā vāsasi rāga ādayaḥ tathā yadi bhāvāḥ api sva hetubhyaḥ vināśam prati hetu antaram apekṣante tadā hetu antarasya pratibandha vaikalyayoḥ api sambhavāt kaścid kṛtakaḥ api na vinaśyet sva hetoḥ tu vinaśvara svabhāvāḥ jāyamānāḥ utpatti anantaram eva vinaśyanti iti siddham kṣaṇikḥ tvam 
NK_86.4	 api ca bhāvasya avinaśvara svabhāva tve vināśaḥ aśakya karaṇaḥ vahneḥ iva śītimā vinaśvara svabhāva tve na arthaḥ hetubhiḥ na ca bhāvāt abhinnasya vināśasya hetu antara janya tā kāraṇa bhedasya bheda hetu tvāt bhinnasya hetu antarāt utpāde ca bhāvasya upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ anya utpādāt anya svarūpa pracyuteḥ abhāvāt ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti ca bhāvakarttṛkaḥ vyapadeśaḥ na syāt kintu a bhāvaḥ jātaḥ iti vyapadiśyeta tathā ca sati ghaṭaḥ kim abhūt iti vārttā praśne tasya nivṛttau prastutāyām a prastutam eva kathitam syāt tasmāt bhāva svabhāvaḥ eva vināśaḥ iti 
NK_87.1^1	 atra ucyate ed pannaḥ bhāvaḥ kim eka kṣaṇa avasthāyī kim vā kṣaṇa antare api avatiṣṭhate kṣaṇa antara avasthiti pakṣe tāvat kṣaṇika tva vyāhatiḥ aneka kāla avasthānāt eka kṣaṇa avasthāyi tve tu tasya kṣaṇa antare sthiti abhāvaḥ iti na bhāva abhāvatoḥ eka tvam kāla bhedāt atha matam na brūmaḥ bhāvaḥ svasya eva abhāvaḥ kintu dvitīya kṣaṇaḥ pūrva kṣaṇasya abhāvaḥ iti tat api asāram pūrva aparakṣaṇayoḥ vyakti bhede api sva rūpa virodhasya abhāvāt yathā ghaṭaḥ bhinna santati varttinā ghaṭa antareṇa saha tiṣṭhati evam eka santati varttinā api saha tiṣṭhet dvitīya kṣaṇa grāhi pramāṇa antarasya tad svarūpa vidhi carita arthasya prathama kṣaṇe niṣedhe pramāṇa tva abhāvāt abhāvaḥ tu bhāva pratiṣedha ātmā eva ghaṭaḥ na asti iti prati iti udayāt 
NK_87.1^2	 tatas tasya utpattiḥ bhāvasya nivṛttiḥ tasya avasthānam bhāvasya anavasthitiḥ tasya upalambhaḥ bhāvasya anupalambhaḥ iti yuktam paraspara virodhāt evañca sati na bhāvasya kṣaṇika tvam paścāt bhāvinaḥ tad abhāvasya hetu antara sā apekṣasya bhāva anantaryya niyama abhāvāt tathā ca dṛśyate ghaṭasya utpannasya cireṇa eva vināśaḥ mudgara abhighātāt bhāva ātmakaḥ ghaṭa vināśaḥ mudgara abhighātāt tu kapāla santāna utpādaḥ syāt iti asaṅgatam sva santāna pratibaddhāyāḥ sadṛśa ārambhaṇa śakteḥ apratighāte vilakṣaṇa samtāna utpatti asambhavāt mudgara āghātena tasyāḥ pratihatau ca bhāva pratighāte kaḥ pradveṣaḥ na ca kāraṇa kāryya tve bhāva vat abhāvasya api vastu tva prasaktiḥ tasya pratiṣedha svabhāvasya pratyakṣa ādi siddha tvāt 
NK_87.2^1	 īdṛśan ca asya svarūpam yat ayam kṛtakaḥ api bhāva vat na vinaśyati naṣṭasya anupalambhāt pramāṇa adhigatasya vastu svabhāvasya para sādharmyeṇa nirākaraṇe jagat vaicitryasya api nirākaraṇam anya utpāde katham anyasya svarūpa pracyutiḥ iti aparyyanuyojyam vastu svābhāvyāt ghaṭaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ iti ca vyapadeśaḥ tad avayava kriyā ādi nyāyena abhāvorpattyā eva atas eva ayam tasya eva abhāvaḥ na sarvasya na ca asya samavāyi kāraṇam kiñcid tad abhāva at na asamavāyi kāraṇam kva kāryyam anādhāram dṛṣṭam idam eva dṛśyate tāvat na hi ayam ghaṭe samavaiti tasya abhāvāt na api bhū tale anya dharma tvāt katham tarhi niyata deśaḥ pratīyate pratiyogi niyamāt ayam asya svabhāvaḥ yat saṃyukta pratiṣedhe saṃyukta vat pratibhāti samaveta pratiṣedhe samaveta vat pratibhāti 
NK_87.2^2	 viśeṣaṇam api ittham eva na punar asya saṃyoga samavāyau tayoḥ bhāva dharma tvāt tat evam siddhaḥ abhāvaḥ bhāvi rodhī na asti iti buddhi vedyaḥ arthaḥ yad kṛtaḥ dahana tu hinayoḥ api virodhaḥ dahana abhāvaḥ tuhine tuhina abhāvaḥ ca dahane iti anayoḥ virodhaḥ na sva rūpeṇa vidheḥ vidhi antara virodha abhāvāt yat ca ghruva bhāvi tvāt abhāvasya hetu antarā anapekṣā iti uktam tat api savituḥ udaya astamayābhyām anaikāntikam tayoḥ anapekāa tve hi kāla bhedaḥ na syāt eka sāmagrī pratibandhe api saḥ eva doṣaḥ niyataḥ hi vāsasi rāga hetuḥ niyata kālaḥ ca tasya tad kāla asannidhi mātreṇa rāgasya anutpādaḥ siddhyati anantāḥ tu vināśa hetavaḥ aniyata kālāḥ ca teṣām sarvadā sarveṣām pratibandhasya aśakya tvāt kaścid ekaḥ nipatati eva kāla antare sa ca nipatitaḥ kṣaṇena eva bhāvam vināśayati iti upapadyate kṛtaka tve api ghruvaḥ vināśaḥ 
NK_88.1	 sarvañca etakṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhanam kāla atyaya apadiṣṭam pratyabhijñā pratyakṣeṇa pratītasya punar pratīteḥ nanu eṣa pratyayaḥ na bhāvasya pūrvva aparaka avasthānam śaknoti pratipādayitum na hi etat ekam vijñānam kāraṇa abhāvāt indriyam sannihita viṣayam na pūrva kāla tvam avagāhate saṃskāraḥ api pūrva anubhavat mā tad viṣaye niyataḥ na apara kāla tām parispṛśati na ca tābhyām anyat ubhaya viṣayam kiñcid ekam asti yat etat vijñānam prasuvīta itas api na etat ekam vijñānam svabhāva bhedāt idam iti hi pratyakṣa tā tat iti hi parokṣa tvam pratyakṣatā aparokṣa tve ca paraspara virodhinī na ekasya yujyete tasmāt grahaṇa smaraṇa ātmake dve ime saṃvittī bhinna viṣaye 
NK_88.2^1	 atra brūmaḥ pratīyate tāvat etasmāt vijñānāt pūrva apara kāla avacchinnam ekam vastu tattvam tat asya viṣayaḥ na bhavati iti saṃvitti viruddham graṇa smāraṇe ca na ekam viṣayam ālambete tasmāt ekam eva idam vijñānam iti pratīti sāmarthyāt ubhaya viṣayam āstheyam pratīyamāna kāryya utpattaye ca apratīyamānam api kāraṇam kalpayanti vidvāṃsaḥ na tu kāraṇā pratītyā viśadam api kāryyam apahnuvate jagat vaicitryasya api apahnava prasaṅgāt tena yadi api pratyekam indriya saṃskārau= asamarthau kāraṇa sāmarthyāt ubhaya viṣayam prāpsyati ca pratyakṣatām viṣaya indriya sāmarthya anuvidhānāt na ca yatra ekaikam asam artham tatra militānām api teṣām asāmarthyam pratyekam akurvatām api kṣiti udaka bīja ādīnām anyonya sannidhi bhājām aṅkura ādi janana upalabdheḥ yatra vilakṣaṇā sāmagrī tatra kāryyam api vilakṣaṇam eva ayāt iti su pratītam tena asya sannihita asat nihita viṣaya tā lakṣaṇe pratyakṣatā aparokṣate na virotsyete atas eva ca indriya sannikarṣa abhāve api pūrva kāla pratyakṣa tā eva indriya ja jñāna viṣaya tvāt tanmātra anubandhi tvāt ca pratyakṣatāyāḥ 
NK_88.2^2	 asannihitam api paricchindat indriyam pūrva kāla tām eva paricchinatti na bhaviṣyat kāla tām tatra saṃskārasya sahakāriṇaḥ abhāvāt na ca ekasya ubhaya kālatāyām kācid anupapattiḥ yena asya ubhaya kālatām saṅkalayataḥ kalpanā tvam dṛṣṭaḥ hi ekasya anekena viśeṣaṇena sambandhaḥ tathā caitrasya chatra pustakābhyām yugapad chatra pustaka sambandhe krameṇa kāla dvaya sambandhe ca na kaścid viśeṣaḥ ekasya ubhaya śeṣaṇa avaccheda pratīteḥ ubhayatra aviśeṣāt tat evam deśa kāla avasthā bheda anugatam ekam vastu tattva madhya vasantī prayabhijñā bhāvānām pratikṣaṇam utpāda vināśau tirayati iti bhrāntā iyam pratītiḥ iti ced na bādhaka abhāvāt kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhanam eva bādhakam iti ced pratyakṣa bādhe satya bādhita viṣaya tvāt anumāna udayaḥ udite ca tasmin pratyakṣa bādhaḥ iti anyonya āśraya tvam pratyakṣe na ayam vidhiḥ tasya anapekṣa tvāt jvālā ādiṣu sāmānya viśayam pratyakṣam viśeṣa viṣayañca anumānam iti avirodhāt na pratyakṣenumāna utpatti niṣedhaḥ iti alam 
NK_89.1^1	 yaḥ api ati prauḍhimnā pratyakṣa siddham kṣaṇa bhaṅgam āha tasya anubhava abhāvaḥ eva uttaram nīlam etat iti hi pratipattiḥ na tu kṣaṇikam etat iti nīlatva avyatirekiṇī kṣaṇika tā tasyāḥ pṛthgartha kriyāyāḥ abhāvāt atas nīlatve gṛhyamāṇe kṣaṇika tvam api gṛhyate su sadṛśa kṣaṇa bheda agrahaṇāt tathā na adhyavasīyate iti ced aho aparaḥ prajñā prakarṣaḥ yat ayam anubhavam api vyākhyāya kathayati yat na adhyavasitam tat gṛhītam iti mṛgatṛṣṇikeyam pratyakṣa bala utpannāt adhyavasāyāt anyasya pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa tva vyasthā nibandhanasya anabhyupagamāt yasmin= adhyavasīyamāne yat niyamena na adhyavasīyate nīla pītayoḥ iva tayoḥ tādātmya abhidhānam api pralāpaḥ 
NK_89.1^2	 kṣaṇikam prathakṣam jñānam sva samāna kāla varttinīm arthasya sattām paricchindat tad kāla asambaddha tām vyavacchindat tad kāla abhāva vyabhicāriṇam kāla antara sambandham api vyavacchindat tad eka kṣiṇa avasthāyi tvam kṣaṇika tvam gṛhṇāti iti ced kāśa kuśa avalambana prāyam idam sva ātmānam eva na grphṇāti vijñānam kutas sva samāvakāla tām arthasya gṛhṇāti gṛhṇātu vā tathā api pūrvam ayam na āsīt paścāt ca na bhaviṣyati iti atra pratyakṣam ajāgarūkam pūrva apara kāla agrahaṇāt varttamāna kāla tva paricchede ca ātad kāla vyavacchedaḥ yuktaḥ bhāvayoḥ virodhān na tu kālantara sambandha vyavacchedaḥ maṇi sūtra vat ekasya aneka sambandha avirodhāt prapañcitaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ asmābhiḥ tattva prabodhe tattva saṃvādinyān ca iti na atra pratanyate 
NK_89.2	 kiñca sarva bhāva kṣaṇika tva abhyupagame kasya saṃsāraḥ jñāna santānasya iti ced na santāni vyatiriktasya santānasya abhāvāt atha matam na ekasya aneka śarīra ādi yogaḥ saṃsāraḥ kim tarhi jñāna santāna avicchedaḥ sa ca kṣaṇika tve api na anupapannaḥ tat api asāram garbha ādi jñānasya prāk bhavīya jñāna kṛta tve pramāṇa abhāvāt na hi samāna jātīyāt eva arthasya utpattiḥ vijātīyāt api agneḥ dhūmasya utpatti sambhavāt atha matam yasya anvaya vyatirekau= atiśayañca yat anuvidhatte tat tasya samāna jātīyam upādānañca iti sthitiḥ jñānañca bodha ātmaka tvam atiśayam bibhartti tat ca pṛthivī ādi bhūteṣu na asti tasmāt yasya ayam atiśayaḥ tat asya samāna jātīyam upādāna kāraṇam iti sthite garbha jñānam jñāna antara pūrvakam siddhyati kāraṇa vyabhicāre kāryyasyā kasmika tva prasaṅgāt iti 
NK_89.3	 tat api asāram adahana svabhāvebhyaḥ dāru nirmathana ādibhyaḥ vahneḥ dāha atiśaya utpatti vat abodha ātmakebhyaḥ api cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ bodha ātmaka tva atiśaya utpatti sambhave bodha ātmaka kāraṇa kalpa nāna vakāśāt atas na prāktana janma siddhiḥ bhaviṣyati janmāntaram iti api na siddhyati maraṇe śarīra antya jñānena jñāna antaram pratisandhātavyam iti atra pramāṇa abhāvāt yadi atra avikala kāraṇa avastham tat tatrajanayati eva yathā vikala janana avastham bījam aṅkuram prati avikala jñāna janana avastham ca antyam jñānam iti pramāṇam asti iti ced na jvālā ādīnām antyakṣaṇena vyabhicārāt sneha vartti kṣaya ādinā antya jvālākṣaṇasya kāraṇa avasthā vaikalyāt avikala tvam na asti iti ced antya jñānasya api maraṇa pīḍayā pīḍitasya avikala kāraṇa avastha tvam asiddham iti su vyāhṛtam kṣaṇika tve para loka abhāvaḥ iti uparamyate 
NK_90.1	 śarīra sama vāyinībhyāñca hita ahita prāpti parihāra yogyābhyām pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām rathakarmaṇā sārathi vat prayatnavān vigrahasya adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate prāṇa ādibhiḥ ca iti katham śarīra parigṛhīte vāyau vikṛta karma darśanāt bhastrā ādhmāpayitā iva nimeṣa unmeṣa karmaṇā niyatena dāru yantra prayoktā iva dehasya vṛddhi kṣata bhagra saṃrohaṇa ādi nimitta tvāt gṛhapatiḥ iva 
NK_90.2^1	 ātma siddhau pramāṇa antaram api āha śarīra samavāyinībhyām iti pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām prayatnavān vigrahasya śarīrasya adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate latā ādi nivṛtti pravṛtti vyavaccheda artham śarīra samavāyinībhyām iti uktam srotaḥ prerita mṛta śarīra pravṛtti nivṛtti vyavaccheda arthan ca hita ahita prāpti parihā yogyābhyām iti hitam sukham ahitam duḥkhm tayoḥ prāpti parihārau hitasya prāpti rahitasya parihāraḥ tatra yogyābhyām samarthābhyām iti buddhi pūrvaka ceṣṭā parigrahaḥ rathakarmaṇā sārathi vat iti dṛṣṭānta kathanam sādhana upādāna parivarjana dvāreṇa hita ahita prāpti parihāra samarthā ceṣṭā prayatna pūrvikā viśiṣṭa kriyā tvāt ratha kriyā vat śarīram vā prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam viśiṣṭa kriyā āśraya tvāt ratha vat uprāṇa ādibhiḥ ca iti praṇādibhiḥ ca prayatnavān adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate iti anuṣañjanīyam prāṇa ādibhiḥ iti anena praṇāpāna nimeṣa unmeṣa jīvana manaḥ gati indriya antara vikārāḥ sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ ca ātmanaḥ liṅgāni iti sūtra ukta samasta liṅga parigrahaḥ 
NK_90.2^2	 katham iti praśna pūrvakam prāṇa apānayoḥ liṅga tvam darśayati śarīra parigṛhītaḥ iti vāyuḥ tiryyak gamana svabhāvaḥ śarīra parigṛhīte ca vāyau prāṇa apāna ākhye vikṛtam svabhāva viparītam karma ūrdhva gamanam adhas gamanañca dṛśyate tasmāt prayatnavān vigrahasya adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate yaḥ tathā vāyum prerayati anyathā asya vikṛtattva asambhavāt bhastrā ādhmāpayitā iva iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ śarīram prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam icchā pūrvaka vi kṛta vāyu āśraya tvāt bhastrā vat śarīra parigṛhīta iti anena icchā pūrvaka tvam darśitam tena hi dvi vāyuka ādibhiḥ nnānā ekāntikam nimeṣa unmeṣa karmaṇā niyatena dāru yantra prayotkā iva iti akṣi pakṣmaṇoḥ saṃyoga nimittam karma nimeṣaḥ vibhāga artham ca karma unmeṣaḥ tena karmaṇā dāru yantra prayoktā iva vigrahasya prayatnavān adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate vāyu vaśena api dāru yantrasya nimeṣa unmeṣau syātām tad nivṛtti artham niyatena iti anena icchā adhīna tvam darśayati śarīram prayatna vat adhiṣṭhitam icchā adhīna nimeṣa unmeṣa vat avayogi tvāt dāru yantra vat 
NK_90.3	 jīvana liṅgakam anumānam kathayati dehasya iti vṛddhiḥ prasiddhā eva kṣatasya bhagrasya ca saṃrohaṇam punar saṅghaṭanam tayoḥ nimitta tvāt gṛhapatiḥ iva prayatnavān adhiṣṭhātā anumīyate śarīrasya vṛddhi kṣata saṃrohaṇam ca prayatnavatā kṛtam vṛddhi kṣata bhagra saṃrohaṇa tvāt gṛha vṛddhi kṣata bhagra saṃrohaṇa vat vṛkṣa ādi gatena vṛddhi ādinā vyabhicāraḥ iti ced na tasya api īśvara kṛta tvāt na tu vṛkṣa ādayaḥ sa ātmakāḥ buddhi ādi utpādana samarthasya viśiṣṭa ātma sambandhasya abhāvāt 
NK_91.1–91.3^1^1	 abhimata viśaya grāhaka karaṇa sambandha nimittena manaḥ karmaṇā gṛha koṇeṣu pelaka prerakaḥ iva dārakaḥ nayana viśaya ālocana anantaram rasa anusmṛti krameṇa rasana vikriyā darśanāt aneka gavākṣa antargata prekṣaka vat ubhaya darśī kaścid ekaḥ vijñāyate sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnaiḥ ca guṇaiḥ guṇī anumīyate manaḥ gati liṅgakam anumānam upanyasyati abhimata ityādi abhimataḥ viṣayaḥ jighṛkṣitaḥ arthaḥ tasya yat grāhakam karaṇam cakṣuḥ ādi tena yaḥ manasaḥ sambandhaḥ tasya nimittena manaḥ karmaṇā 
NK_91.1–91.3^1^2	 gṛhe koṇeṣu koṣṭheṣu bhūmau ropitam pelakam prati hasta sthitasya pelakasya prerakaḥ dārakaḥ iva prayatnavān manaḥ prerakaḥ anumīyate prayatnavatā preryyam manaḥ abhimata viṣaya sambadha nimitta kriyā āśraya tvāt dāraka hasta pelaka vat vāyu ādi preritasya anabhimatena api sambandhaḥ bhavati etad artham abhimata viṣaya iti uktam indriya antara vikāram darśayati nayana viṣaya iti nayana viṣayasya rūpasya ālocanāt grahaṇāt anantaram rasasya anusmaraṇa krameṇa rasanā indriya antarasya vikāraḥ dṛśyate tasmāt ubhayoḥ gavākṣakayoḥ antargataḥ prekṣakaḥ iva dvābhyām indriyābhyām rūpa rasayoḥ darśī kaścid ekaḥ anumīyate 
NK_91.3^2	 kim uktam syāt kasyacid iṣṭa phalasya rūpam dṛṣṭvā tad sahacaritasya pūrva anubhūtasya rasasya smaraṇāt tatra icchā bhavati tatas api prayatnaḥ ātma manassaṃyoga apekṣaḥ rasanā indriya vikriyām karoti sā danta udaka saṃplava anumitāḥ rasanā indriya vikriyāḥ indriya caitasye na syāt pratyekam niyatābhyām cakṣū rasanābhyām rūpa rasayoḥ sāhacaryya apratītau rūpa darśanena rasa smṛti abhāvāt asti ca ayam vikāraḥ tasmāt indriya vyatiriktaḥ kaḥ api asti ubhaya darśī yaḥ rūpam dṛṣṭvā rasasya smarati śarīram eva ca ubhaya darśi bhaviṣyati iti ced na bāla vṛddha śarīrayoḥ parimāṇa bhedena anya tve siddhe bāla avasthā anubhūtasya vṛddha avasthāyām asmaraṇa prasaṅgāt 
NK_91.4^1	 na kevalam pūrva uktaiḥ haitubhiḥ sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ guṇī anumīyate sukha ādīni dravya āśritāni guṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vat yaḥ asau guṇī saḥ ātmā iti nanu śarīra āśritāḥ eva sukha ādayaḥ tatra āha te ca na śarīra indriya guṇāḥ iti na pratijñā mātreṇa kasyacid arthasya siddhiḥ asti iti anena abhiprāyeṇa āha kasmāt iti kāraṇam āha ahaṅkāreṇa eka vākyatā bhāvāt iti ahaṅkāreṇa aham iti pratyayena eka vākya tvam eka adhikaraṇa tvam sukha ādīnām aham sukhī aham duḥkhī iti ahaṅkāta pratyaya viṣayasya sukha ādi avacchedyasya pratīteḥ aham pratyayaḥ ca na śarīra ālambanaḥ para śarīre abhāva prasaṅgāt sva śarīre eva ayam pratyayaḥ bhavati iti ced na aviśeṣāt 
NK_91.4^2	 śarīra ālambanaḥ ahaṃpratyayaḥ sva śarīra vat para śarīram api ced pratyakṣam tatra yathā sthūla tva ādi pratyayaḥ sva śarīre para śarīre api bhavati evam aham iti pratyayaḥ api syāt svarūpasya ubhayatra aviśeṣāt sva sambandhitā kṛte tu vīśeṣe tad kṛtaḥ eva ayam pratyayaḥ na svarūpa ālambanaḥ tad ālambana tve ca antarmukha tayā api na bhavet atas eva ayam na indriya avalambanaḥ indriyāṇām atīndriya tvāt asya ca liṅga śabda ādi anapekṣasya pratyakṣa pratyaya tvāt tasmāt sukha ādayaḥ api na śarīra indriya viḍayāḥ kiñca yaḥ anubhavitā tasya eva smaraṇam abhilāṣaḥ sukha sādhana parigrahaḥ sukha utpattiḥ duḥkheṣu dveḍaḥ iti sarva śarīriṇām pratyātma saṃvedanīyam anubhava smaraṇe ca na śarīra indriyāṇām iti uktam tatas api sukha ādayaḥ na tad viṣayāḥ 
NK_92.1–92.2^1	 te ca na śarīra indriya guṇāḥ kasmāt aṅkāreṇa eka vākyatā bhāvāt pradeśa vṛtti tvāt ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt bāhya indriya apratyakṣa tvāt ca tathā ahaṃśabdena api pṛthivī ādi śabda vyatirekāt iti yukti anyarañca āha pradeśa vṛtti tvāt iti dṛśyate pradeśa vṛtti tvam sukha ādīnām pāde me sukham śirasi me vedanā iti pratyayāt tatas ca śarīra indriya guṇa tva abhāvaḥ tad viśeṣa guṇānām vyāpya vṛtti tva avi abhicārāt sukha ādayaḥ śarīra indriya viśeṣa guṇāḥ na bhavanti avyāpya vṛtti tvāt ye tu śarīra indriya viśeṣa guṇāḥ te vyāpya vṛttayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ yathā rūpa ādayaḥ na ca tathā sukha ādayaḥ vyāpya vṛttayaḥ tasmāt na śarīra indriya guṇāḥ iti vyatirekī karṇa śaṣkulī avacchinnasya nabhaḥ deśasya śrotra indriya bhāvam āpannasya yaḥ śabdaḥ guṇaḥ bhavati sa tad vivara vyāpī iti avyabhicāraḥ 
NK_92.2^2	 itas api na śarīra guṇāḥ sukha ādayaḥ bhavanti ayādat dravya bhāvi tvāt vyatirekeṇa rūpa ādayaḥ eva nidarśanam indriya guṇa pratiṣedhe tu na ayam hetuḥ śrotra guṇena śabdena anaikāntika tva prasaṅgāt itas api na śarīra indriya guṇāḥ sukha ādayaḥ bāhya indriya apratyakṣa tvāt śarīra indriya guṇānām dvayī gatiḥ apratyakṣatā guru tva ādīnām bāhya indriya pratyakṣatā rūpa ādīnām vidhā antarantu sukha ādayaḥ tasmāt na tad guṇāḥ iti śarīra indriya guṇa tve pratiṣiddhe pariśeṣāt taiḥ ātmā anumīyate iti sthitiḥ 
NK_92.3	 nanu sukham suḥkhañcā imau vikārau= iti nityasya ātmanaḥ na sambhavataḥ bhavataḥ ced saḥ api carmma vat anityaḥ syāt na tayoḥ utpāda vināśābhyām tad anyasya ātmanaḥ svarūpa pracyuteḥ abhāvāt nityasya hi sva rūpa vināśaḥ svarūpa antara utpādaḥ ca vikāraḥ na iṣyate guṇa nivṛttiḥ guṇa antara utpādaḥ ca aviruddhaḥ eva atha asya nityasya sukha duḥkhābhyām kim kriyate sva viṣayaḥ anubhavaḥ sukha duḥkha anubhave satyasya atiśayān atiśaya rahitasya kaḥ upakāraḥ ayam eva tasya upakāraḥ apam eva ca atiśayaḥ yasmin sati sukhduḥ kha bhoktṛ tvam tathā ahaṃśabdena api iti yathā sukha ādibhiḥ ātmā anumīyate tathā ahaṃśabdena api anumīyate ahaṃśabdaḥ leke vede ca abhiyuktaiḥ prayujyamānaḥ na tāvat nirabhidheyaḥ na ca svarūpam abhidheyam yuktam sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt yathā uktam na ātmānam abhidhatte hi kaścid śabdaḥ kadācana 
NK_92.4	 tasmāt yaḥ asya abhidheyaḥ saḥ ātmā iti nanu ayam pṛthivī ādīnām eva vācakaḥ bhaviṣyati tatra āha pṛthivī ādi śabda vyatirekāt iti yaḥ yasya arthasya vācakaḥ sa tad śabdena samāna adhikaraṇaḥ dṛḍṭaḥ yathā dravyam pṛthivī iti pṛthivī iti ahaṃśabdasya tu pṛthivī ādi vācakaiḥ śabdaiḥ saha vyatirekaḥ samāna adhikaraṇa tva abhāvaḥ aham pṛthivī aham udakam iti prayoga abhāvāt tasmāt na ayam pṛthivī ādi viṣayaḥ nanu śarīra viṣayaḥ eva ayam dṛśyate sthūlaḥ aham iti na aham jānāmi aham smārāmīti prayogāt śarīrasya ca jñāna smṛti adhikaraṇa tvam niṣiddham tasmāt ātma upakāraka tvena lakṣaṇayā śarīre tasya prayogaḥ yathā bhṛtye aham eva ayam iti vyapadeśaḥ 
NK_93.1–93.2^1^1	 tasya guṇāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma saṃskāra saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ ātma liṅga adhikāre buddhi ādayaḥ prayatna antāḥ siddhāḥ dharma adharmau ātma antara guṇānām akāraṇa tva vacanāt saṃskāraḥ smṛti utpattau kāraṇa vacanāt vyavasthā vacanāt saṅkhyā evam vyavasthite satya ātmanaḥ guṇān kathayati tasya guṇāḥ ityādinā buddhi ādīnām ātmani sadbhāve sūtrakāra anumatim darśayati ātma liṅga adhikāre buddhi ādayaḥ prayatna antāḥ siddhāḥ iti ātma liṅga adhikāraḥ iti prāṇa apāna ādi sūtram lakṣayati 
NK_93.1–93.2^1^2	 dharma adharmau= ātma antara guṇānām akāraṇa tvāt iti vacanāt siddhau dātari varttamānaḥ dāna dharmaḥ pratigrahītari varttamānam pratigraha dharmam janayati iti kasyacid matam pratiṣedhayatā sūtra kṛta uktam ātma antara guṇānām ātma antara guṇeṣu akāraṇa tvāt iti asya ayam arthaḥ ātma antara guṇa āmām sukha ādīnām ātma antara guṇeṣu sukha ādiṣu kāraṇa tva abhāvāt dharma adharmayoḥ anyatra varttamānayoḥ anyatra ārambhaka tvam ayuktam iti etena dharma adharmayoḥ ātma guṇa tvam kathitam anyathā tayoḥ sukha ādi sādharmya kathanena anārambhaka tva samartha nam asambaddham syāt 
NK_93.2^2	 saṃskāraḥ smṛti utpattau iti ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga aviśeṣāt saṃskārāt ca smṛtiḥ iti sūtram lakṣayati pūrva anubhūtaḥ arthaḥ smaryyate na tatra anubhavaḥ kāraṇam cira vinaṣṭa tvāt na api anubhava abhāvaḥ kāraṇam abhāvasya niratiśaya tvena smṛteḥ paṭu manda ādi bheda anupapatteḥ abhyāsa vaiyarthyāt ca tasmāt anubhavena ātmani kaścid atiśayaḥ kṛtaḥ yatas smaraṇam syāt iti saṃskāra kalpanā ye tu vinaṣṭam api anubhavam eva smṛteḥ kāraṇam āhuḥ teṣām vinaṣṭam eva jyotiṣṭoma ādikam svarga ādi phalasya sādhanam bhaviṣyati iti adṛṣṭasya api ucchedaḥ syāt vyavasthā vacanāt saṃkhyā iti nānā ātmānaḥ vyavasthātaḥ iti sūtreṇa ātma nā ānātva pratipādanāt bahu tva saṅkhyā siddhā iti arthaḥ 
NK_93.3^1	 atha kā iyaṃa vyavasthā nānā deha bhāvinām jñāna sukha ādīnām apratisandhānam aikārmye hi yathā bāla avasthāyām anubhūtam vṛddha avasthāyām anusamdhīyate mama sukham āsīt mama duḥkham āsīt iti evam deha antara anubhūtam api anusandhīyeta anubhavituḥ eka tvāt na ca evam asti atas pratiśarīram nānā ātmānaḥ yathā sarvatra ekasya ākāśasya śrotra sve karṇa śaṣkulī a ādi upādhi bhedāt śabda upalabdhi vyavasthā tathā ātmā eka tve api deha bhedāt anubhava ādi vyavasthā iti ced 
NK_93.3^2	 viṣamaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ prati puruṣam vyavasthitābhyām dharmābhyām upagṛhītānām śabda upalabdhi hetūnām karṇa śaṣkulīnām vyavasthānādyuktā tad adhiṣṭhāna niyamena śabda grahaṇa vyavasthā aikātmye tu dharma adharmayoḥ avya vastḥnāt śarīra vyavasthā abhāve kim kṛtā sukha duḥkha ādi utpatti vyavasthā manassambandhasya api sādhāraṇa tvāt yasya tu nānā ātmānaḥ tasya sarveṣām ārmanām sarva gata tvena sarva śarīra sambandhe api na sādhāraṇaḥ bhogaḥ yasya karmaṇā yat śarīram ārabdham tasya eva tad ubhoga āyatanam na sarvasya karma api yasya śarīreṇa tasya eva tat bhavati na aparasya evam śarīra antara niyaṃḥ karma antara niyamāt iti anādiḥ 
NK_94.1^1	 atha matam eka tve api paramātmanaḥ jīva ātmanām paraspara bhedāt vyavasthā iti tat asat paramātmanaḥ jīva ātmanām bhede advaita siddhānta kṣatiḥ anena jīvena ātmanā anupraviśya nāma rūpe vyākaravāṇi iti jīva paramātmanoḥ tādātmya śruti virodhaḥ ca avidyā kṛtaḥ jīva paramātmanoḥ bhedaḥ iti ced kasya iyam avidyā kim brahmaṇaḥ kim uta jīvānām na tāvat brahmaṇaḥ asti avidyā yogaḥ śuddha buddha svabhāva tvāt jīvāśraya avidyā iti ca anyonya āśraya doṣa parāhatam svidyākṛtaḥ jīva bhedaḥ jīva āśraya avidyā iti bīja aṅkura vat anādiḥ avidyā jīva prabhedaḥ iti ced 
NK_94.1^2–94.3^1	 bīja aṅkura vyakti bheda vat avidyā jīvayoḥ pāramārthika tva abhāvāt anupapannam vyakti bhedena ca bīja aṅkurayoḥ anyonya kāraṇa tā jīvaḥ tu sarvāsu bhava koṭiṣu ekaḥ eva mānuṣa paśa pakṣī ādi yoniṣu pratyagra jātasya śiśoḥ jāti sāmyāt āhāra viśeṣa abhilāṣeṇa tāsu tāsu jātiṣu janma antara kṛtasya tad tadāra viśeṣa abhyāsasya anumāna paramparayā tasya anādi śarīra yoga pratīteḥ tatra avidyā kṛtaḥ jīvva bhedāt ca avidyā iti asaṅgatiḥ 
NK_94.1^2–94.3^2	 brahma vat jīvasya api anādi nidhana tvena brahma pratibimba tā tasmāt tam eva bhāntam anubhāti sarvam tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti śruti prāmāṇyāt anādinidhanam brahma tattvam eva idam sarva deheṣu kāśate iti vācyam tathā sati ca anupapannā vyavasthā iti sūktam nānā ātmānaḥ vyavasthātaḥ iti abheda śrutayaḥ tu gauṇa arthāḥ iti eṣā diś na ca nānā ātma pakṣe sarveṣām krameṇa muktāvante saṃsāra ucchedaḥ aparimitānām antya nyūna atirikta tva ayogāt yathā āhuḥ vārttikakāra miśrāḥ atas eva ca vidvatsu mucyamāneṣu santatam brahmāṇḍa loka jīvānām ananta tvāt aśūnyatā antya nyūna arikta tve yujyate parimāṇa vat vastuni aparimeye tu nūnam teṣām asambhavaḥ iti 
NK_95.1–95.2^1	 pṛthaktvam api atas eva tathā ca ātma iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam sannikarṣa ja tvāt sukha ādīnām saṃyogaḥ tad vināśaka tvāt vibhāgaḥ iti pṛthaktvam api atas eva nānā ātmānaḥ vyavasthātaḥ iti vacanāt eva pṛthaktvam siddham saṅkhyā anuvidhāyi tvāt pṛthaktu asya iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā ca ātmā iti vacanāt parama mahat parimāṇam iti vibhavavān mahān ākāśa tathā ca ātmā iti sūtrakāra vacanāt ākāśa vat ātmanaḥ api vibhu tvāt parama mahat parimāṇam siddham iti arthaḥ vibhu tvañca ātmanaḥ vahneḥ ūrdhva jvalanāt vāyoḥ tiryyak gama nāt avagatam te hi adṛṣṭa kārite na ca tad āśrayeṇa asambaddham adṛṣṭam tayoḥ bhavitum arhati atiprasaṅgāt na ca ātma samavetasya adṛṣṭasya sākṣāt dravya antara sambandhaḥ ghaṭataḥ iti sva āśraya sambandha dvāreṇa tasya sambandhaḥ iti āyātam tatas samasta mūrtta dravya sambandha lakṣaṇam ātmanaḥ vibhu tvam siddhyati svabhāvataḥ eva vahneḥ ūrdhva jvalanam na adṛṣṭa vaśāt iti ced 
NK_95.2^2	 kaḥ ayam svabhāvaḥ nāma yadi vahni tvam uta dāhaka tvam rūpa viśeṣaḥ vā tapta ayaḥ piṇḍe vahneḥ api syāt atha indhana viśeṣa prabhava tvam svabhāvaḥ iti anindhana prabhavasya vidyut ādi prabhavasya ca ūrdhva jvalanam na syāt atha atīndriyaḥ kaḥ api svabhāvaḥ kāsucid vyaktiṣu asti yāsām ūrdhva jvajvalanam dṛśyate iti puruṣa guṇe kaḥ pradbeṣaḥ yasya hi karmaṇaḥ guru tva drava tva vegāḥ na kāraṇam tasya ātma viśeṣa guṇāt utpādaḥ yathā pāṇi karmaṇaḥ puruṣa prayatnāt ūrdhva jvalana tiryyak gamana ādīnām sarkkaṇām guru tva ādayaḥ na kāraṇam abhāvāt tad tad kāryyaviparīta tvāt ca tasmāt eṣām api ātma viśeṣa guṇāt eva utpādaḥ nyāyyaḥ ūrdhva jvalana tiryyak pavanāni ātma viśeṣa guṇa kṛtāni guṇa tva ādi kāraṇa abhāve sati karma tvāt puruṣa prayatna japāṇi karma vat 
NK_95.3	 sannikarṣa ja tvāt sukha ādīnām saṃyogaḥ sukha ādīnām ātma guṇānām manaḥ saṃyoga ja tvāt ātmani saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ vyadhikaraṇasya asamavāyikāraṇa tva abhāvāt tad vināśaka tvāt vibhāgaḥ iti tasya saṃyogasya vināśaka tvāt vibhāgaḥ siddhaḥ ātma manasoḥ nitya tvena āśraya vināśasya vināśa hetoḥ abhāvāt iti arthaḥ nanu ātmani nitye sthite nitya ātma darśinaḥ sukha tṛṣṇā pariplutasya sukha sādhaneṣu rāgaḥ duḥkha sādhaneṣu dveṣaḥ tābhyām pravṛtti nivṛttī tatas dharma adharmau tatas saṃsāraḥ iti anirmokṣaḥ nairātmye tu aham eva na asmi kasya sukham duḥkham iti anāsthayā sarvatra rāga dveṣa rahitasya pravṛtti ādeḥ abhāve sati apavargaḥ ghaṭataḥ iti ced na nitya ātma darśane api viṣaya doṣa darśanāt vairāgya utpatti dvāreṇa tasya ūrpattiḥ iti alam 
NK_96.1–96.3^1	 manaḥ tu ayogān manaḥ sati api ātma indriya arthān nidhye jñāna sukha ādīnām abhūtvā utpatti darśanāt karaṇa antaram anumīyate śrotra ādi avyāpāre smṛti uḥ patti darśanāt bāhya indriyaiḥ agṛhīta ssukha ādi grāhya antara bhāvāt ca pradhāna tvāt prathamam ātmānam ākhyāya tad anantaram manaḥ nirūpaṇa artham āha manaḥ tu ayogāt manaḥ iti vyākhyānam pūrvavat manaḥ tvam nāma sāmānyam ṃnovyaktīnām bhede sthite satya numā iyam yā hi samāna guṇa kāryyāḥ vyaktayaḥ tāsu aparam sāmānyam dṛāṭam yathā ghaṭa ādiṣu samāna guṇa kāryyāḥ ca manaḥ vyaktayaḥ tasmāt tāsu apara sāmānya yogaḥ asiddhe manasi tasya dharma nirūpaṇam anyāyyam iti matvā tasya sadbhāve pramāṇam āha sati api ātma indriya artha sānnidhye iti 
NK_96.3^2	 ātmanaḥ tāvat sarva gata tvāt sarva indriyaiḥ yugapad sambandhaḥ asti eva indriyāṇām api sannihitaiḥ arthaiḥ sannikarṣaḥ bhavati tathā api ekasmin viṣaye pratīyamāne viṣaya antare jñāna sukha ādayaḥ na bhavanti tad uparamāt ca bhavanti iti dṛśyate tad darśanāt ātmrndriya artha sannikarṣebhyaḥ karaṇa antaram animīyate yasya sannidhānāt jñāna sukha ādīm utpattiḥ asannidhānāt ca anutpattiḥ ātma indriya artha sannikarṣāḥ kāryya utpattau karaṇa antara sāpekṣāḥ sati api sadbhāve kāryya anutpādaka tvāt tantu ādi vat yat ca tat aprkṣaṇīyam tat manaḥ eka artha upalabdhi kāle anupalabhyamānasya api artha antarasya indriya sannikarṣaḥ asti iti kim pramāṇam indriya adhiṣṭhāna sannidhiḥ eva rūpa upalabdhi kāle gandha ādayaḥ api ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ san nikṛṣyante tad adhiṣṭhāna sannihita tvāt upalabhyamāna gandha ādi vat 
NK_96.4^1	 pramāṇa antaram api āha śrotra ādi avyāpāre smṛti utpatti darśanāt iti smṛtiḥ tāvat indriya jāḥ jñāna tvāt gandha ādi jñāna vat na ca asyāḥ śrotra ādīni karaṇāni badhira ādīnām śrotra ādi vyāpāra abhāve tasyāḥ utpatti darśanāt tasmāt yat asyāḥ karaṇam indriyam tat manaḥ na kevalam pūrvasmāt kāraṇāt karaṇa antara anumānam bāhya indriyaiḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ agṛhītānām sukha ādīnām rūpa ādi apekṣayā grāhya antara bhāvāt ca tad anumānam iti āha bāhya indriyaiḥ iti sukha ādi pratītiḥ indriya jāḥ aparokṣa pratīti tvāt rūpa ādi pratīti vat yat ca tat indriyam tat manaḥ cakṣuḥ ādīnām tatra vyāpāra abhāvāt abhinna kāraṇa tvāt jñāna ātmakāḥ sukha ādayaḥ sva saṃvedanāḥ na karaṇa antareṇa gṛhyante iti ced na jñāna svabhāva tve sukha duḥkhayoḥ aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt paraspara bhede ca na tayoḥ jñāna ātmaka tā bodha ākārasya ubhaya sādhāraṇa tve api sukha duḥkha ākārayoḥ paraspara vyāvṛtta tvāt 
NK_96.4^2	 na ca anayoḥ vijñāna abhinna āhrtu jatvam jñānasya arthāt utpatteḥ tasmāt ca vāsanā sahāyāt sukha duḥkhayoḥ utpādāt anyathā upekṣā jñāna abhāva prasaṅgāt na ca sva saṃvedanam vijñānam iti api siddham ekasya karma karaṇa ādi bhāve dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt sva prakāśaḥ pradīpaḥ asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ced na evam saḥ api hi puruṣeṇa jñāyate jñāpyate ca cakṣuṣā jñānañca tasya kriyā na tu svayam karaṇam karttā karma kriyā ca bhavati yathā ātma vādinām sva pratītau= ātmanā yugapad karma karttṛ bhāvaḥ tathā jñānasya api karaṇa ādi bhāvaḥ iti ced na avirodhāt jñāna kriyā viṣaya tvam karma tvam ātmanaḥ tasyām eva ca svātantryāt karttṛ tvam na svātantrya viṣaya tvayoḥ asti virodhaḥ karaṇa tvam kriyā tvantu siddha sādhya tvābhyām ekasya paraspara viruddham kāraṇa karaṇayoḥ eka tva abhāvāt evam para prayojya tā karaṇa tvam itarā prayojya tvam ca karttṛ tvam iti anayoḥ api virodhaḥ vidhi pratiṣedha svabhāva tvāt iti atas na eṣām ekatra sambhadaḥ yuktaḥ 
NK_97.1	 atha matam na jñānasya karaṇa ādi bhāvaḥ sva saṃvedana arthaḥ kintu sva prakāśa svabhāvasya tasya utpattiḥ eva sva saṃvedanam iti atra api nirūpyate kim tad arthasya prakāśaḥ svasya vā yadi arthasya prakāśaḥ tad utpatteḥ arthasya saṃvedanam syāt na tu svasya iti svasya asaṃvedya tā doṣaḥ atha idam svasya prakāśaḥ tat eva prakāśyam prakāśaḥ ca iti kriyā karaṇayoḥ eka tvam tad avastham na ca sva utpattiḥ eva sva ātmani kriyā iti api nidarśanam asti yat api sva saṃvedana siddhau pramāṇam uktam yat yat āyatta prakāśam tat tasmin prakāśamāne prakāśate yathā pradīpa āyatta prakāśaḥ ghaṭaḥ jñāna āyatta prakāśāḥ ca rūpa ādayaḥ iti tatra api yadi jñānam eva artha prakāśaḥ abhimataḥ tadā tad āyatta prakāśāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti asiddham anaikānti kañca indriyaṇa atha ca jñāna janyaḥ artha prakāśaḥ na jñānam eva artha prakāśaḥ tadā dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ jñāna janakasya pradīpasya artha prakāśaka tva abhāvāt etena etat api pratyuktam 
NK_97.2–97.3	 apratyakṣa upalambhasya na artha dṛṣṭaḥ prasiddhi ati iti na hi jñānasya pratyakṣatā arthasya darśanam kintu vijñānasya utpattiḥ tatra asaṃvidite api jñāne tad upatti mātra eṇa eva arthasya saṃvedanam siddhyati katham antasya utpattiḥ anyasya saṃvedanam iti ced kim kurmaḥ vastu svabhāva tvāt na ca evam sati sarvasya saṃvedanam tasya sva kāraṇa sāmagrī niyamāt pratiniyata artha saṃvitti svabhāvasya pratiniyata pratipattṛ saṃvedyasya eva ca utpādāt 
NK_97.4	 apare punar evam āhuḥ jñāna saṃsargāt viṣaye prakāśamāne prakāśa svabhāva tvāt pradīpa vat vijñānam prakāśate prakāśa āśraya tvāt pradīpa varti vat ātmā api prakāśate iti tripuṭī pratyakṣa ta iti tat api asat ghaṭaḥ ayam iti etasmin pratīyamāne jñātṛ jñānayoḥ apratibhāsanāt yatra tu anayoḥ pratibhāsaḥ ghaṭam aham jānāmi iti tatra utpanne jñāne jñātṛ jñāna viśiṣṭasya arthasya mānasa pratyakṣa tā na tu jñātṛ jñānayoḥ cākṣuṣa jñāne pratibhāsaḥ tayoḥ api cākṣuṣa tva prasaṅgāt 
NK_98.1–98.2	 tasya guṇāḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva saṃskārāḥ prayatna jñāna ayaugapadya vacanāt pratiśarīram eka tvam siddham pṛthaktvam api atas eva tad abhāva vacanāt aṇu parimāṇam apasarpaṇa upasarpaṇa vacanāt saṃyoga vibhāgau mūrta tvāt paratva aparatve saṃskāraḥ ca asparśavat tvāt dravya anārambhaka tvam kriyāvat tvāt mūrtta tvam sādhāraṇa vigraha vat tva prasaṅgāt ajñtvam karaṇa bhāvāt para artham guṇavat tvāt dravyam prayatna adṛṣṭa parigraha vaśāt āśu sañcāri ca iti iti praśasta pāda bhāṣye dravya pārthaḥ 
NK_98.3^1	 tat evam siddhe manasi tasya guṇān pratipādayati tasya guṇāḥ ityādinā saṅkhī ā ādi aṣṭaguṇa yogaḥ api manasaḥ vaidharmyam saṅkhyā sadbhāvam kathayati prayatna ityādinā pratiśarīram ekam manaḥ āhosvit anekam iti saṃśaye sati sūtra kṛta uktam prayatna ayaugapadyāt jñāna ayaugapadyāt ca pratiśarīram ekam manaḥ iti tena prati śarīram eka tvam siddham iti manaḥ bahutve hi ātma manaḥ saṃyogānām bahu tvāt yugapad jñānāni prayatnāḥ ca bhaveyuḥ dṛśyate ca kramaḥ jñānānām eka upalambha vyāsaktena viṣaya antara anupalambhāt nivṛtta vyāsaṅgena ca upalambhāt iti uktam evam prayatnānām api krama utpādaḥ eva ekatra prayatamānasya anyatra vyāpāra abhāvāt samāpta kriyasya ca bhāvāt tasmāt ekam manaḥ tasya ekatve khalu eka rva ekadā saṃyogaḥ iti ekam eva jñānam ekaḥ ca prayatnaḥ iti upapadyate yasya kvacid yugapad abhimānaḥ tad alāta cakra vat āśu bhāvāt na tu tāttvikam yaugapadyam ekatra dṛṣṭena kāryya krameṇa anyatra api karaṇasya tasya eva sāmarthya anumānāt 
NK_98.3^2	 nanu evam tarhi dvau= imau= arthau puṣpitāḥ taravaḥ iti aneka artha pratibhāsaḥ kutas kutas ca sva śarīrasya saha preraṇa dhāraṇe na artham ūha ālambanasya eka jñānasya apratiṣedhāt buddhi bhedaḥ eva na tu tathā pratibhāsaḥ sarvāsām eva tāsām eka eka artha niyata tvāt evam śarīrasya preraṇa dhāraṇe ca prayatna viśeṣāt ekasmāt eva bhavataḥ yathā aneka viṣayam ekam jñānam tathā tad kāraṇau= icchā prayatnau= api iti na kiñcid durupapādam pṛthaka tvam api atas eva iti saṅkhyā anuvidhānāt eva pṛthaktvam api siddham iti arthaḥ tad abhāva vacanāt aṇu parimāṇam vibhavavān mahān ākāśaḥ tathā ca ātmā iti abhidhāya sūtrakāreṇa tad abhāvāt aṇu manaḥ iti uktam tasmāt aṇu parimāṇam manaḥ iti siddham nitya dravya gatasya vibhava abhāvasya aṇu parimāṇa tva avi abhicārāt vibhava abhāvaḥ ca asya yugapad jñāna anupapattya eva samadhigataḥ manasaḥ vibhu tve tasya yugapad samaḥ ta indriya sambandhāt cakṣuḥ ādi sannikṛṣṭeṣu rūpa ādiṣu jñāna yaugapadyam syāt 
NK_98.4^1	 atha katham eka indriya grāhyeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu manaḥ dhiṣṭhitena cakṣuṣā yugapad sannikṛṣṭeṣu jñānāni yugapad na bhavanti ātma indriya artha sannikarṣāṇām yaugapadyāt na bhavanti tāvadanena ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya ekasya yugapad anekasya jñānasya utpādana sāmarthya abhāvaḥ kalpyate iti ced samānam etat vibhu tve api manasaḥ tasmāt avibhu tve api tasya yukti antaram vācyam tat ucyate vibhu tvāt ātma manasoḥ paraspara saṃyoga abhāve satya ātma guṇānām jñāna sukha ādīnām anutpattiḥ asamavāyikāraṇa abhāvāt 
NK_98.4^2	 ātma artha saṃyogasya hi asamavāyikāraṇa tve artha deśe jñāna utpattiḥ syāt asamavāyi kāraṇa avyavadhānena pradeśa vṛttīnām guṇānām utpādāt ātma indriya saṃyogasya asamavāyikāraṇa tve api śabda jñāna anutpattiḥ ākāśa ātmakena śrotreṇa ātmanaḥ saṃyoga abhāvāt na ca bahis deśe pratyayaḥ na api śabda jñāna anutpādaḥ tasmāt ātma artha saṃyogasya ātma indriya saṃyogasya ca asamavāyi kāraṇa tve pratiṣiddhe pariśeṣāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam vyavatiṣṭhate tat ca manasaḥ vyāpaka tve na sambhavati iti anutpattiḥ eva jñāna sukha ādīnām asti ca teṣām utpādaḥ saḥ eva manasaḥ vibhu tvam nivarttayati iti 
NK_98.5^1	 apasarpaṇa upasarpaṇa vacanāt saṃyoga vibhāgau iti apasarpaṇam upasarpaṇam aśīta pīta saṃyogāḥ kāya antara saṃyogāḥ ca adṛṣṭa kāritāni iti sūtreṇa manasaḥ pūrva śarīrāt apasarpaṇam śarīra antare ca upasarpaṇañca adṛṣṭa kāritam iti uktam tasmāt asya saṃyoga vibhāgau siddhau mūrtta tvāt paratva aparatve saṃskāraḥ ca vibhava abhāvāt tāvat mūrtta tvam siddham tasmāt ghaṭa ādi vat paratva aparatva vega āha siddhāḥ asparśavat tvāt dravya anārambhaka tvam asparśavat tvam manasaḥ śarīra anya tve sati sarva viṣaya jñāna utpādaka tvāt ātma vat siddham tasmāt ca ātma vat eva sajātīya dravya anārambhaka tvam kriyāvat tvāt mūrtta tvam iti aṇu tva pratipādanāt mūrtta tve siddhe api vispaṣṭa artham etat uktam 
NK_98.5^2–98.7	 sādhāraṇa vigraha vat tva prasaṅgāt ajña tvam yadi jñātṛ manaḥ bhavet śarīram idam sādhāraṇam upaghoga āyatanam syāt na ca evam eka abhiprāya anurodhena tasya sarvadā pravṛtti nivṛtti darśanāt tasmāt ajñam manaḥ caitanye niṣiddhe api prakramāt punar etat uktam ajña tve siddhe satyāha karaṇa bhāvāt para artham iti para artham parasya upabhoga sādhanam iti arthaḥ guṇavat tvāt dravyam pṛthivī ādi vat prayatna adṛṣṭa parigraha vaśāt āśu sañcāri ca iti draṣṭavyam icchā dveṣa pūrvakeṇa jīvana pūrvakeṇa ca prayatnena parigṛhītam sthānāt sthāna antaram āśu sañcarati tathā adṛṣṭena parigṛhītam maraṇāt śarīra antaram āśu sañcarati iti draṣṭavyam iti śabdaḥ parisamāptau viśuddha vividha nyāya mauktika prakara ākaraḥ sevyatām dravya jaladhiḥ sphuṭa siddhānta vidrumaḥ iti bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhara kṛtau padārtha praveśaka nyāya kanda līṭīkāyām dravya padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_99.1–99.4	 rūpa ādīnām guṇānām sarveṣām guṇa tva abhisambandhaḥ dravya āśrita tvam nirguṇa tvam niṣkriya tvam ūm namaḥ jalada nīlāya śeṣa paryaṅka śāyine lakṣmī kaṇṭha graha ānanda niḥṣyandāya muradviṣe dravya padārtham vyākhyāya guṇānām nirūpaṇa artham āha rūpa ādīnām guṇānām iti guṇa tvam nāma sāmānyam tena abhisambandhaḥ guṇānām iti paraspara sādharmya kathanam itara padārtha vaidharmya kathanam api etat guṇa tvam rūpa ādiṣu ratna tvam iva upadeśa sahakāriṇā pratyakṣeṇa eva gṛhyate yat tu prathamam asya karma ādi vilakṣaṇa tayā na grahaṇam tad āśraya pāratantryasya ātyantika sādṛśyasya sambhavāt rūpa ādīnām guṇānām iti sva rūpa mātra kathanam sarveṣām iti abhivyāptippradarśana artham dravya āśrita tvam dravya upasarjana tvam etat ca dharma mātra kathanam na tu vaoidharmya abhidhānam dravya karma ādiṣu api sambhavāt 
NK_99.5–99.7	 evam nirguṇa tvam guṇa rahita tvam guṇānām svarūpam teṣām sva ātmani guṇa antara anārambhaka tvāt tad anārambhaka tvañca rūpa ādiṣu rūpa ādiṣu rūpa ādi antarā anupalabdheḥ anavasthānāt ca evam sati ekam rūpa manpuḥ śbdaḥ ityādi vyavahāraḥ upacārāt saṅkhyā ādikam rūpadyāśrayā na bhavati guṇa tvāt rūpa ādi vat svarūpa antaram kathayati niṣkriya tvam iti dravye gacchati rūpa ādikam api gacchati iti ced na vegavat vāyu saṃyogena vyoma ādiṣu kriyāyāḥ abhāvāt śākhā ādiṣu ca bhāvāt anvaya vyatirekābhyām mūrtta tva kriyāvat tvayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau mūrtti abhāvena rūpa ādiṣu kriyāyāḥ nivṛtti saddheḥ katham tarhi teṣu gamana pratītiḥ āśraya kriyayā yathā eva sattāyām na hi sattā sva āśrayeṇa saha gacchati ekasya gamane viśvasya gamana prasaṅgāt iti 
NK_100.1–100.6	 rūpa sagandha sparśa paratva aparatva guru tva drava sneha vegāḥ mūrtta guṇāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma bhāvanā śabdāḥ amurtta guṇāḥ saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyaḥ vibhāgāḥ ubhaya guṇāḥ saṃyoga vibhāga dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādayaḥ aneka āśritāḥ śeṣāḥ tu ekaika vṛttayaḥ rūpa rasa gandha sparśa sneha sāṃsiddhi ka drava tva buddhi sukha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma bhāvanā śabdāḥ vaiśeṣa eka guṇāḥ 
NK_100.7–100.11	 saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva guru tva naimittika drava tva vegāḥ sāmānya guṇāḥ śabda sparśa rūpa para gandhāḥ bāhya ekaika indriya grāhyāḥ saṅkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva drava tva sneha vegāḥ dvindriya grāhyāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnāḥ tu antaḥkaraṇa grāhyāḥ samprati parasparam eva teṣām sādharmyam vaidharmyañca pratipādayan= āha rūpa ityādi ete mūrttānām eva guṇāḥ na amūrttānām tathā hi rūpa sparśa paratva aparatva vegāḥ pṛthivī ādiṣu triṣu vāyau rūpa varjam rūpa sparśa varjam manasi rasa guru tve pṛthivī udakayoḥ drava tvam pṛthivī udaka tejassu snehaḥ ambhasi gandhaḥ pṛthivyām 
NK_100.12–100.14	 amūrtta guṇān kathayati buddhi sukha duḥkha ityādi buddhi ādayaḥ bhāvanā antāḥ ātma guṇāḥ ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ ubhaya guṇāḥ mūrtta amūrtta guṇāḥ saṃyoga vibhāga dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādayaḥ aneka āśritāḥ ekā saṃyoga vyaktiḥ ekā ca vibhāga vyaktiḥ ubhayoḥ dravyayoḥ varttate iti aneka āśrita tvam evam dvi tva pṛthaktva vyaktyoḥ api ādi śabda gṛhītāḥ tu tritva tripṛthaktva ādi vyaktayaḥ yathāsambhavam bahuṣu āśritāḥ aneka śabdaḥ ca aekaḥ na bhavati a iti vyutpattyā dvayoḥ bahuṣu api sādhāraṇaḥ 
NK_100.15–100.16	 śeṣāḥ tu ekaika vṛttayaḥ aśeṣāḥa rūpa ādi vyaktayaḥ ekasyām eva vyaktau varttante na punar ekā rūpa vyaktiḥ saṃyoga vat ubhayatra vyāsajya varttate iti arthaḥ viśeṣa guṇān nirūpayati rūpa rasa gandhā ityādi viśeṣaḥ vyavacchedaḥ tasmai prabhavanti ye guṇāḥ te vaiśeṣikāḥ guṇāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ te hi sva āśraya m itarasmāt vyavacchindanti na saṃkhyā ādayaḥ teṣām svatas viśeṣa abhāvāt yasya teṣām viṣeṣaḥ saḥ āśraya viśeṣa kṛtaḥ eva iti boddhavyam 
NK_100.17–100.20	 saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ sāmānya guṇāḥ sāmānyāya sva āśraya sādharmyāya guṇāḥ na sva āśraya viśeṣāya iti arthaḥ nanu aṇu parimāṇam paramāṇūnām vyavasthāpakam na tasya jāti antara paramāṇu sādhāraṇa tvāt sāṃsiddhika drava tvam apām vaiśeṣika guṇaḥ eva tena naimittika grahaṇam śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāḥ bāhya ekaika indriya grāhyāḥ bāhyāni indriyāṇi cakṣuḥ ādīni bāhya artha prakāśaka tvāt taiḥ pratyekam rūpa ādayaḥ gṛhyante saṅkhī ā ādayaḥ vega antāḥ dvi indriya grāhyāḥ cakṣu sparśana grāhyāḥ yathā cakṣuṣā asnigdhaḥ ayam a iti pratītiḥ evam tvac indriyeṇa api bhavati iti saṅkhī ā ādi vat snehaḥ api tad ubhaya grāhyaḥ buddhi ādayaḥ prayatna antāḥ antaḥkaraṇa grāhyāḥ manasā pratīyante iti arthaḥ 
NK_100.21	 buddhiḥ anumeyāḥ na antaḥkaraṇena gṛhyate iti kecid tat ayuktam liṅga abhāvāt na tāvat artha mātram liṅgam tasya vyabhicārāt jñātaḥ arthaḥ liṅgam ced jñāna sambandhaḥ jñāta tā yā asau jñāma karma tā sā pratīyamāne jñāne na pratīyate sambandhi pratītinā antarīyaka tvāt sambandha pratīteḥ iti katham radviśeṣaṇa arthaḥ liṅgam syāt liṅga vat liṅga viśeṣaṇasya api jñāyamānasya eva anumāna hetutvāt atha manyase ajñānena sva utpatti anantaram arthe jñāta tā nāma kācid avasthā janyate pākena iva taṇḍuleṣu pakva tā sā ca artha dharma tvāt arthena saha pratīyate a iti tat api asāram ananubhavāt yathā hi taṇḍulānāmrvaudanī bhāvaḥ pakva tā anubhūyate na evam arthasya jñāta tā yā ca iyam aparokṣa rūpa tā hāna ādi vyahāra yogya tā ca tasya sā api hi jñāna sambadhaḥ na dharma antaram yathā ca arthe jñāyamāne jñāta tā tathā jñāta tāyām api jñāyamānāyām jñāta tā antaram iti anavasthā atha iyam sva prakāśāḥ jñāne kaḥ pradveṣaḥ 
NK_100.22	 vastutas tri kāla viśiṣṭaḥ api arthaḥ jñānena pratīyamānaḥ varttamāna kāla avacchinnaḥ pratīyate yā ca tri kālasya varttamāna kāla avacchinna ācasthā sā jñāta tā jñāna kṛta tvāt tasya liṅgam iti kaścid tat api na kiścid varttamāna avacchinna tā hi varttamāna kāla viśiṣṭa tā sā ca arthasya svābhāvikī na jñānena kriyate kintu pratīyate 
NK_100.23	 yaḥ api hi viṣaya saṃvedana anumeyam jñānam icchati saḥ api evam paryanuyojyaḥ kim viṣaya saṃvedanam ātmani samavaiti viṣaye vā na tāvat viṣaye tad caitanya pratiṣedhāt atha ātmani samavaiti tatas kim anyat vijñānam yat asya anumeyam asya kāraṇam jñātṛ vyāpāra lakṣaṇam tat iti ced tat kim nityam anityam vaḥ yadi anityam tad utpattau= api kāraṇam vācyam viṣaya indriya ādi sahakārī jñānamaḥ saṃyogaḥ tasya kāraṇam iti ced sā eva sāmagrī viṣaya saṃvedana utpattau= astu kim antar gaḍunā tena atha tat nityam kādācid kaviṣya indriya saṃnikarṣa ādi sahakāri kādācid kam viṣaya saṃvedanam karoti iti abhyupagaḥ tat asya api āgantuka kāraṇa kalāpau= eva viṣaya saṃvedana utpatti sidhau taskalpanā vaiyarthyam viṣaya saṃvedanāt eva artha avabodhasya tad pūrvakasya vyavahārasya ca siddheḥ 
NK_101.1	 atha ucyate viṣaya indriya ādi jatyam vijñānam katham ātmani eva samavaiti yadi ātmā sahaja jñāna mayaḥ na syāt tasya acetana tve hi kāraṇa tva aviśeṣāt indriya ādiṣu api jñāna samavāyaḥ bhavet iti tatra svabhāva niyamāt eva niyama upapatteḥ yathā tantūnām apaṭa ātmaka tve api tantu tva jāti niyamāt teṣu samavāyaḥ na turya ādiṣu tat vat acit ātmake api ātmani ātma tva jāti niyamāt jñāna samavāyasya niyamaḥ bhaviṣyati 
NK_101.2	 etena etat api pratyuktam yat āhuḥ eke asva saṃvedanam ātmanaḥ nijam caitanyam a iti saṃsāra avasthāyām api tasya avabhāsa prasaṅgāt avidyayā vā tasya tirodhānam iti ced kim brahmaṇaḥ api avidyā kā ca nitye sva prakāśe tirodhāna vācaḥ yuktiḥ na ca tirohite tasmin= anyasya pratibhānam asti atasya bhāsā sarvam idam bhāti a iti śruteḥ bhāsate ced sarvasya muktiḥ vidyā virbhāve satya vidyā vilayāt atha iyam na vilīyate na tarhi vidyā prakāśaḥ tasyāḥ vilaya hetuḥ iti anirmokṣaḥ nirbhāgasya eka deśena pratibhā na manāśaṅkanīyam 
NK_102.1–102.5	 guru tva dharma adharma bhāvanā hi atīndriyāḥ apākaja rūpa rasa gandha sparśa parimāṇa eka tva eka pṛthaktva guru tva drava tva sneha vegāḥ kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ guru tva dharma adharma bhāvanāḥ atīndriyāḥ na kenacid indriyeṇa gṛhyante iti arthaḥ apākaja rūpa dayaḥ vigāntāḥ kāraṇa guṇa rūrvakāḥ sva āśrayasya yat samavāyi kāraṇam tasya ye guṇāḥ tad pūrvakāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ tantu rūpa ādi ḥ ūrvakāḥ paṭa rūpa ādayaḥ niyamena tad dharma anuvidhānāt atat pūrvaka tve hi paṭe yat kiñcid guṇa antaram syāt niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt etena ekam eva sarvatra śuklam rūpam pratyabhijñānāt iti pratyuktam taratama ādi bhāva anupapatti prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt sāmānya viḍayā pratyabhijñā 
NK_102.6	 pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ pākāt vahni saṃyogāt jāyante na tu paramāṇu samavāyi kāraṇa āśrita rūpa ādi rūevakāḥ atas tad nivṛtti artham apāka ja grahaṇam siddhāyām urpattau kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam akāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam ca iti nirūpaṇīyam jala ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām ca utpattiḥ eva na asti iti na vyabhicāraḥ eṣām ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakatva abhidhānam svarūpa kathanam na tu avadhāraṇa artham naimittika drava tva vegayoḥ akāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvasya api sambhavāt kāraṇa guṇa pūrvaka tvam anayoḥ vegavat ārabdha jala avaya vi samavetayoḥ draṣṭavyam 
NK_103.1–103.3	 buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma bhāvanā śabdāḥ akāraṇa guṇa purvakāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma bhāvanā aśbda tūla parimāṇa uttara saṃyoga naimittika dravya tva paratva aparatva pāka jāḥ saṃyoga jāḥ buddhi ādayaḥ śabda antāḥ akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakāḥ sva āśrayasya yat samavāyi kāraṇam tad guṇa pūrvakāḥ na bhavanti nitya guṇa tvāt 
NK_103.4	 buddhi ādayaḥ saṃyoga jāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma bhāvanāḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyoga jāḥ śabdaḥ bherī ākāśa saṃyoga jaḥ tūla parimāṇam pracaya ākhya saṃyoga jam uttara saṃyogaḥ saṃtoga jaḥ sa yogaḥ abhimataḥ naimittika drava tvam vahni saṃyoga jam paratva aparatve diś kāla piṇḍa saṃyoga je pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa rasa gandha sparśāḥ vahni saṃyoga jāḥ iti vivekaḥ 
NK_104.1–104.7	 saṃyoga vibhāga vegāḥ karma jāḥ śabda uttara vibhāgau vibhāga jau paratva aparatva dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādayaḥ buddhi apekṣāḥ rūpa rasa gandha anuṣṇa sparśa śabda parimāṇa eka tva eka pṛthaktva snehāḥ samāna jāti ārambhakāḥ saṃyoga vibhāga vegāḥ karma jāḥ ādyau saṃyoga vibhāgau karma jau akāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ api śabda uttara vibhāgau vibhāga jau ādyaḥ śabdaḥ vibhāgāt api jāyate uttaraḥ vibhāgaḥ vibhāgāt eva jāyate iti vivekaḥ paratva aparatva dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādayaḥ buddhi apekṣāḥ eṣām urpattau nimitta kāraṇam buddhiḥ ādi śabdāt tritva tripṛthaktva ādi parigrahaḥ 
NK_104.8	 rupādayaḥ sneha antāḥ samāna jāti ārambhakāḥ kāraṇa rūpāt kārya rūpam rasāt rasaḥ gandhāt gandhaḥ sparśāt sparśaḥ snehāt snehaḥ mahat tvāt mahat tvam ityādi yojyam śabdaḥ tu sva āśraye eva śabda antara ārambhakaḥ atra ca kāraṇa tva mātram vivakṣitam na tu asamavāyi sāraṇa tvam anyathā vijātīyānām pāka jānām nimitta kāraṇasya uṣṇa sparśa vyavacchedaḥ asaṅga tā arthaḥ syāt nanu evam tarhi katham rūpa ādīnām jñāna kāraṇa tvam na tad vyatirekeṇa samāna jātīya ambhaka tvasya abhipreta tvāt 
NK_105.1–105.3	 sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa praytnāḥ ca asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ saṃyoga vibhāga saṅkhyā guru tva drava tva uṣṇa sparśa jñāna dharma adharma saṃskārāḥ samāna asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ sukha ādayaḥ asamāna jāti ārambhakāḥ sukham icchāyāḥ kāraṇam duḥkham dveṣasya icchā dveṣau prayatnasya saḥ api karmaṇaḥ putra sakham pirasi sukham janayati anyathā tasya pramoda anupapattiḥ iti ced tad asāram putrasya hi mukha prasāda ādinā sukha utpattim anumāya paścāt pitari sukham jāyate tatra asya putrasya sukham na kāranpam tasya etāvantam kālam anavasthānāt kintu laiṅgikī tad viṣayā pratītiḥ kāraṇam iti prakriyā 
NK_105.4	 saṃyoga ādayaḥ saṃskāra antāḥ samāna samāna jāti ārambhbhakāḥ saṃyogāt samāna jātīyaḥ uttara saṃyogaḥ vijātīyam dvi tūlake mahat parimāṇam vibhāgāt vibhāgaḥ śabdaḥ ca kāraṇa gata eka tva saṅkhyātaḥ kārya varttinī eka tva saṅkhyā dvi tva bahutva saṅkhyābhyām ca aṇu tva mahat tve guru tvāt guru tva antaram patanam ca drava tvāt drava tva antaram ayandana kriyā ca uṣṇa sparśāt uṣṇa sparśaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ ca jñānāt jñāna antaram saṃskāraḥ ca dharmāt dharmaḥ sukhm ca adharmāt adharma antaram duḥkham ca saṃskārāt saṃskāraḥ smaraṇam ca 
NK_106.1–106.5	 buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa bhāvanā śabdāḥ avāśraya samaveta ārambhakāḥ rupa rasa gandha sparśa parimāṇa sneha prayatnāḥ paratra ārambhakāḥ sa yoga vibhāga saṅkhyā eka pṛthaktva guru tva drava tva vega dharma adhrmāḥ tu ubhayatra ārambhakāḥ buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa bhāvanā śabdāḥ sva āśraya samaveta ārambhakāḥ sukha ādayaḥ tāvat yatra svayam vartante tatra eva kāryam janayanti buddhiḥ tu dvi tva ādikam paratra ārambhamāṇā api ātma viśeṣa guṇaṃjanayantī sva āśraya samavetam eva janayati na anyatra rūpa rasa gandha sparśa parimāṇa sneha prayatnāḥ paratra ārambhakāḥ avayaveṣu vartamānāḥ rūpāsayaḥ yathāsambhavam avayavini rūpa ādikam ārambha ante ātmani samavetaḥ prayatnaḥ hasta ādiṣu kriyā hetuḥ 
NK_106.6	 saṃyoga ādayaḥ ubhayatra ārambhakāḥ sva āśraye tat anyatra ca ārambhakāḥ tantuṣu vartamānaḥ saṃyogaḥ teṣu eva paṭam ārabhate viṣaya indriya saṃyogaḥ ca ātmāni jñānam vaṃśalayoḥ vibhāgaḥ anya krākāśe śabdam ākāśe śabdam ārabhate vaṃśa dala ākāśa vibhāgaḥ ca sva āśrayaḥ ākāśe avayava varttinī eka tva saṅkhyāḥ avayavinī eka tva saṅkhyām ārabhate avāśraye ca dvi tva ādi saṅkhyām atha avayaveṣu eka pṛthaktvam avayavinī eka pṛthaktvam sva āśrayeṣu dvi pṛthaktva ādikam iti kāraṇa gatāḥ ca gurutva drava tva vegāḥ kāryeṣu gurutva drava tvavrgān ārabhante sva āśrayeṣu kriyām dharma adharmau= ātmani sukha duḥkhe paratra ca agni ādau jvalana ādi kriyām 
NK_107.1–107.5	 guru tva drava tva vega prayatna dharma adharma saṃyoga viśeṣāḥ kriyā hetavaḥ rūpa rasa gandha anuṣṇa sparśa saṅkhyā parimāṇa eka pṛthaktva sneha śabdānāmasamavāyi kāraṇa tvam buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma adharma bhāvanānām nimitta kāraṇa tvam saṃyoga vibhāga uṣṇa sparśa guru tva drava tva vegānām ubhayathā kāraṇa tvam guru tva ādayaḥ kriyā hetavaḥ guru tvāt patanam drava tvāt syadanam vega ādiṣoḥ uttara karmāṇi prayatnāt śarīra ādi kriyā dharma adharmābhyām agni ādi kriyā viśiṣyate iti viśeṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ saṃyogaḥ nodana abhighāta lakṣaṇaḥ saḥ api kriyā hetuḥ iti vakṣyate 
NK_107.6^1	 rūpa ādayaḥ śabda antāḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam samavāyi kāraṇa pratyāsannam avadhṛta sāmarthyam asamavāyi kāraṇam pratyāsattiḥ ca samavāyi kāraṇa samavāyaḥ samavāyi kāraṇa eka artha samavāyaḥ ca sukha ādīnām sanavāyi kāraṇam ātmā tatra samavāyāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ teṣām asamavāyi kāraṇam nanu evam tarhi dharma adharmayoḥ api asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam syāt na tayoḥ samasta ātma viśeṣa guṇa utpattau sāmarthya anavadhāraṇāt tathā hi dharma adarma duḥkhayoḥ anutpattiḥ adharmāt ca dharma sukhayoḥ anutpādaḥ evam jñāna ādīnām api pratyekam vyabhicāraḥ deśanīyaḥ sarvatra avadhṛta sāmarthyaḥ tu jñātṛ manaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti etāvatā viśeṣeṇa tasya eva asamavāyokāraṇa tvam 
NK_107.6^2	 tathā paṭa rūpasya samavāyi kāraṇena paṭena saha ekasmin= arthe tantau samavāyāt tantu rūpam paṭa rūpasya asamavāyi kāraṇam na rasa ādayaḥ tasyava tad utpattau= anvaya vyatirekābhyām sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt evam rasa ādiṣu api yojyam uṣṇa sparśasya pākaja ārambhe nimitta kāraṇa tvam api asti tad artham anuṣṇasya grahaṇam rūpa rasa gandha anuṣṇa sparśa parimāṇa snehānām samavāyaḥ kāraṇa eka artha samavāya ādāyāt asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam kāraṇa varttinām eṣām kārya māna jātīya ārambhaka tvāt śabdasya samavāyi kāraṇa samavāyāt asamavāyikāraṇa tā ākāśa āśritena ākāśe eva śabda antara ārambhāt saṅkhyā pṛthaktvayoḥ ubhayathā kāraṇa tvam kāraṇa varttinoḥ tayoḥ kārye yathāsaṅkhyam ekatva eka pṛthaktva ārambhaka tvāt sva āśraye dvi tvat vipṛthaktva jamaka tvāt 
NK_107.7–107.8	 buddhi ādīnām nimitta kāraṇa tvam teṣām nimitta kāraṇa tvam eva iti arthaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga uṣṇa sparśa guru drava tva vegānām ubhayathā kāraṇa tvam asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam nimitta kāraṇa tvam ca iti arthaḥ tathā hi bherī daṇḍa saṃyogaḥ śabda utpattau nimittam bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam evam vaṃśa dala vibhāgaḥ nimittam vaṃśa dala ākāśa vibhāgaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam uṣṇa sparśaḥ uṣṇa sparśasya asamavāyi kāraṇam pāka jānām nimitta kāraṇam guru tvam sva āśraye patanasya asamavāyi kāraṇam nodana abhighāta kriyā utpattau nimitta kāraṇam evam drava tva vegayoḥ api yojyam 
NK_108.1–108.4^1	 paratva aparatva dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādīnām akāraṇa tvam saṃyoga vibhāga śabda ātma viśeṣa guṇānām pradeśa vṛtti tvam paratva aparatva ādīnām akāraṇa tvam na etānya samavāyi kāraṇam na api nimitta kāraṇam dvi tvat vipṛthaktva ādinām ityādi padena tripṛthaktvānām paramāṇu parimāṇa parama mahat parimāṇayoḥ ca parigrahaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga śabda ātma viśeṣa guṇānām pradeṣa vṛtti tvam iti pradeśa vṛttayaḥ avyāpya vṛttayaḥ sva āśraye varttante na varttante ca iti arthaḥ nanu etat ayuktam yugapad ekasya ekatra bhāva abhāva virodhāt na anupapannam pramaṇena tathā abhāva pratītiḥ tathā hi mahataḥ vṛkṣasya puruṣeṇa saha agre saṃyogaḥ mūle ca tad abhāvaḥ pratīyate mūle vṛkṣa upalambhe api saṃyogasya sarvaiḥ anupalambhāt agre ca upalambhāt na ca mūla grayoḥ eva saṃyoga tad abhāvau tad pradeśa avacchedena vṛkṣe eva puruṣasya bhāva abhāva pratīteḥ yadi pradeśasya saṃyogaḥ na pradeśinaḥ tadā pradeśasya api sva pradeśa apekṣayā pradeśi tvāt niṣpradeśe paramāṇu mātre saṃyogaḥ syāt tad vṛttiḥ tu saṃyogaḥ na pratyakṣaḥ iti saṃyoga pratīti abhāvaḥ eva paryavasyati 
NK_108.4^2	 yathā ca rūpa ādi bhede api ekaḥ avayavī na bhidyate tathā saṃyogaḥ sat asat bhāvābhyām tad abhāvābhyām api ubhayatra api tad eka tvasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt yadi api ubhaya āśrayaḥ saṃyogasya ūḥ upalabdhau= upalabhyate eva tathā api tasya rūpa ādi vat gṛhyamāṇā akhila avayava avacchedena anupalambhāt avyāpaka tvam evam śabdaḥ api ākāśam na vyāpnoti tatra eva asya deśa bhedena upalambha anupalambhābhyām yugapad bhāva abhāva sambhavāt buddhi ādayaḥ hi antar bahis ca upalambha anupalambhābhyām avyāpakāḥ katham tarhi dharma adharmābhyām agni ādiṣu kriyā tayoḥ tad deśe abhāvāt iti ced na tatra āsatoḥ api tayoḥ sva āśraya sannidhi mātreṇa nimitta tvāt yathā vastrasya ekānte cāṇḍāla sparśaḥ apara anta saṃyuktasya traivarṇikasya pratyavāya hetuḥ tathā idam api draṣṭavyam 
NK_109.1–109.7	 śeṣāṇām āśraya vyāoi tvam apākaja rūpa rasa gandha sparśa parimāṇa eka pṛthaktvasāṃsiddhi kadrava tva guru tva snehānām yāvat dravya bhāvi tvam śeṣāṇām ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvam rūpa ādīnām sarveṣām guṇānām pratyekam apara sāmānya sambandhāt rūpa ādi sajñāḥ bhavanti śeṣāṇām āśraya vyāpi tvam uktebhyaḥ ye anye te śeṣāḥ teṣām āśraya vyāpi tvam saṃyoga ādi vat avyāpakam na bhavati iti arthaḥ apākaja rūpa ādīnām yāvat dravya bhāvi tvam yāvat āśraya dravyam tāvat rūpa ādayaḥ vidyante pākaja rūpa ādayaḥ satyā iva āśraye na santi iti apākaja grahaṇam śeṣāṇām ayāvat dravya bhāvi tvam apākaja rūpa ādi vyatiriktāḥ guṇāḥ yāvat dravyam na bhavanti satyā iva āśraye naśyanti iti arthaḥ 
NK_109.8	 samprati pratyekam guṇānām paraspara vaidharmya pratipādana artham āha rūpa ādīnām iti rūpam ādiḥ yeṣām guṇānām teṣām ekaikam pratyapara jāte rūpa tva ādikāyāḥ sambandhāt rūpa ādi saṃjñā rūpam iti rasaḥ iti apdi saṃjñāḥ bhavanti rūpa tva ādi apara sāmānya kṛtā rūpa ādi sajñā rūpa ādīnām pratyekam vaidharmyam rūpa tva ādi sāmānyam na asti iti kecid tat ayukram nīla pīta ādi bhedeṣu rūpam rūpam iti pratyaya anuvṛtteḥ cakṣuḥ grāhyatā upādhi kṛtā tad anuvṛttiḥ iti ced na teṣām rūpam iti evam cakṣuṣā agrahaṇāt tad grāhya tā nimitta tve hi grahaṇāt anantaram tathā pratyayaḥ syāt cakṣuḥ grāhyatā tad grahaṇa yogya tā sā ca nīla ādiṣu tri kāla avasthāyoni iti ced astu kāmam kintu eṣā yadi pratirūpam vyāvṛttāḥ pratyaya anuganaḥ na syāt eka nimitta abhāvāt atha anuvṛttāḥ saṃjñā bheda mātram evam rasa ādayaḥ api vyākhyātāḥ 
NK_110.1–110.2^1	 tatra rūpam cakṣuḥ grāhyam pṛthivī udaka jvalana vṛtti dravya ādi upalambhakam nayana sahakāri śukla ādi aneka prakāram salila ādi paramāṇuṣu nityam pārthiva paramāṇuṣu agri saṃga virodhi sarva kāryeṣu kāraṇa guṇa rūpvakam āśraya vināśāt eva vinaśyati iti sarva padārthānām abhivyakti nimitta tvāt ādau rūpam nirūpayati tatra rūpam cakṣuḥ grāhyam iti teṣām guṇānām madhye rūpam cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate na indriya antareṇa nanu rūpa tvam api cakṣuṣā eva gṛhyate katham idam vaidharmyam rūpasya na guṇebhyaḥ vaidharmyasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā ca prakṛtebhyaḥ nirddhāraṇa artham tatra iti uktam sāmānyāt asya vaidharmyam tu sāmānyavat tvam eva pṛthivī udaka jvalana vṛtti pṛthivī udaka jvalaneṣu eva varttate dravya ādi upalambhakam yasmin= āśraye varttate tasya dravyasya tad gatānām ca guṇa karma sāmānyānām upalambhakam 
NK_110.2^2	 nayana sahakāri sva gatam rūpam cakṣuṣaḥ viṣaya grahaṇe sahakāri śukla ādi aneka prakāram śukla ādayaḥ aneke prakārāḥ yasya tat tathāvidham salila ādi paramāṇuṣu nityam salila paramāṇuṣu tejaḥ paramāṇuṣu ca nityam pārthiva paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyoga virodhi agni saṃyogaḥ virodhī vināśakaḥ pārthiva paramāṇu rūpasya iti ca vakṣu pāmaḥ sarva kāryeṣu kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam kārya dravya gatam rūpam sva āśraya samavāyi kāraṇa rūpa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt eva vinaśyati kārya rūpa vināśasya āśraya vināśaḥ eva hetuḥ 
NK_111.1	 āśraya vināśāt rūpasya vinapvpaḥ iti na mṛṣyāmahe saha eva rūpa dravyayoḥ vināśa pratīteḥ iti ced na kādgara abhighātāt tāvat vayava kriyā vibhāga ādi krameṇa dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga nivṛttau tad ā ārabdhasya dravyasya vināśaḥ kāraṇa vināśāt tad gata rūpa vināśe tu kim kāraṇam yadi hi akāraṇasya api avayava saṃyogasya vināśāt rūpa vināśaḥ kapāla rūpāṇi api tatas vinaśyeyuḥ aviśeṣāt tasmāt pūrvam dravyasya vināśaḥ tadanu rūpasya āśu bhāvāt kramasya agrahaṇam iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ 
NK_111.2	 yaḥ tu rūpa dravyayoḥ tādātmyam icchantaḥ dravya kāraṇam eva rūpasya kāraṇam āhuḥ te idam praṣṭavyāḥ kim paramāṇu rūpam rūpantaram ārabhate na vā ārabhamāṇam api kim sva ātmani ārabhate kim vā su a āśraye paramāṇau yadi na ārabhate yadi vā sva ātmani sva āśraye ca ārabhate dvi aṇuke rūpa ādi anutpattau tat pūvam gaja da rūpam syāt atha tat dvi aṇuke āravat yamānasya sva āśraya tva ayogādurpanne dvi aṇuke paścāt tatra rūpa utpattiḥ iti avaśyam abhyupetavyam nirāśrayasya kāryasya anutpādāt tathā sati tādātmyam kutas pūrva apara kāla bhāvāt kiñca āsthitaḥ eva ghaṭe rūpa ādayaḥ vahni saṃyogāt vinaśyanti tathā sati jāyante ca iti bhavatām abhyupagamaḥ yasya ca utpattau yasya anutpattiḥ yat nivṛttau ca anivṛttiḥ na tayoḥ tādātmyam iti prakriyā iyam na ca atyanta bhede pṛthak upalambha prasaṅgaḥ sarvadā rūpasya dravya āśrita tvāt etat eva katham vastu svābhāvyāt iti kṛtam guruṣu pratikūla vādena 
NK_112.1–112.2^1	 rasaḥ rasana grahyaḥ pṛthivī udaka vṛttiḥ jīva vana puṣṭi bala ārogya nimittam rasana sahakārī madhura amla lavaṇa tikta kaṭu kaṣāya bheda bhinnaḥ asya api nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ rūpavat samprati bāhya ekaika indriya grāhyasya pratyakṣa dravya vṛtteḥ viśeṣa guṇasya nirūpaṇa saṅgena rasa gandhayoḥ vyākhyāta vyaya uru bhaya dravya vṛtti tva viśeṣeṇa ādau rūpam vyākhyāya rasam vyācaṣṭe rasaḥ rasana grāhyaḥ iti guṇeṣu madhye rasaḥ eva rasana grāhyaḥ rasana grāhyaḥ eva rasaḥ pṛthivī udaka vṛttiḥ pṛthivī udakayoḥ eva varttate jīvana puṣṭi bala ārogya nimittam 
NK_112.1–112.2^2	 jīvanam prāṇa dhāraṇam puṣṭiḥ avayava upacayaḥ balam utsāha viśeṣaḥ ārogyam roga abhāvaḥ eṣām rasaḥ nimittam etat ca sarvam vaidya śāstrāt avagantavyam rasana sahakārī svagataḥ rasaḥ rasanasya bāhya rasa upalambhe sahakārī madhura amla lavaṇa tikta kaṭu kaṣāya bheda bhinnaḥ madhura ādi bhedena bhinnaḥ ṣaṣ prakāraḥ iti arthaḥ tasya ca nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ rūpavat yathā rūpam pārthiva paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogādurpatti vināśa vat salila paramāṇuṣu nityam kārye kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati tatha rasaḥ api 
NK_113.1–113.2	 gandhaḥ ghrāṇa grāhyaḥ pṛthivī vṛttiḥ ghraṇa sahakārī surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ ca asya api pūrvavat utpatti ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ gandhaḥ ghrāṇa grahyaḥ gandhaḥ eva ghrāṇa grāhyaḥ ghrāṇa grāhyaḥ eva gandhaḥ nanu katham ayam niyamaḥ svabhāva niyamāt īdṛśaḥ gandhasya svabhāvaḥ yat ayam eva ghrāṇena ekena gṛhyate na anyaḥ dṛṣṭa anumitānām niyoga pratiṣedha abhāvāt pṛthivī vṛttiḥ pṛthivyām eva varttate na anyatra ghrāṇa sahakārī svagataḥ gandhaḥ ghrāṇasya sahakārī surabhiḥ asurabhiḥ ca iti bhedaḥ asya api pūrvavat utpatti ādayaḥ vyākhyātāḥ yathā rasaḥ pārthiva paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogāt utpatti vināśavān kārye kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakaḥ āśraya vināśāt ca vinaśyati tathā gandhaḥ api nitya tvam punar asya na asti eva 
NK_114.1–114.2	 sparśaḥ tvac indriya grāhyaḥ kṣiti udaka jvalana pavanavrpttiḥ tvac sahakārī rūpa anuvidhāyī śīta uṣṇa anuṣṇa aśīta bhedāt trividhaḥ asya api nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ pūrvavat sparśaḥ tvac indriya grāhyaḥ tvaci sthitam indriyam tena eva spārśaḥ gṛhyate na anyena kṣiti udaka jvalana pava vṛttiḥ eteṣu eva vṛttiḥ eva tvac sahakārī sva gata sparśaḥ tvac indriyasya viṣaya grahaṇa sahakārī rūpa anuvudhāyī rūpam anuvidhātum anugantum śīlam asya yatra rūpam tatra niyamena tatra sadbhāvāt śīta uśṇa anuśīta bhedāt trividhaḥ kāṭhinya praśithilāt aḥ tu saṃyoga viśeṣāḥ na sparśa antaram ubhaya indriya grāhya tvāt asya api nitya anitya tvaṣpattayaḥ pūrvavat iti vyavahitasya rasasya grahaṇam na gandhasya tasya nitya tva abhāvāt 
NK_115.1–115.3^1	 pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādīnā pākajoḥ patti vidhānam ghaṭa ādeḥ āma dravyasya agninā sambaddha gebhyaḥ saṃyoga vināśaḥ saṃyoga vināśebhyaḥ ca kārya dravyam vinaśyati tasmin vinaṣṭe svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogāt auṣṇya apekṣāt śyāmā ādīnām vināśaḥ punar anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt auṣṇya apekṣāt pāka jāḥ jāyante pārthiva pramāṇu rūpa ādīnām urpatti vināśa nirūpaṇām āha pārthiva paramāṇu rūpa ādinām iti ysdi api paramāṇavaḥ eva pṛthivī tathā api te kārya rūpa pṛthivī apekṣayā pārthivāḥ ucyante pṛthivyāḥ ime kāraṇam paramāṇavaḥ pārthiva paramāṇavaḥ teṣām ye rūpa ādayaḥ teṣām pāka jānām utpatteḥ vidhānam prakāraḥ kathyate nanu evam sati śyāma ādi vināśa nirūpaṇam na pratijñātam syāt na evam prakāra śabdena tasya avabodhāt evam hi rūpa ādīnām pākāt utpatti prakāraḥ yatra pūrveṣām vināśāt apareṣām utpādaḥ tam eva prakāram darśayati ghaṭa ādeḥ āma dravyasya ityādinā ādi śabdena śarāva ādayaḥ gṛhyante āma dravyasya iti apakva dravyasya iti arthaḥ 
NK_115.3^2–115.4	 pāka artham agninā sambaddhasya paramāṇuṣu karmāṇi upadyante āma dravyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ saṃyoginaḥ api udaka paramāṇavaḥ santi tad nivṛtti artham āha tad ārambhakeṣu iti tasya ghaṭa ādeḥ ārambhakeṣu iti arthaḥ ghaṭa ādi ārambhakāḥ ca paramāṇuvaḥ pāramparyeṇa karmaṇām kāraṇam iti āha agni abhighātāt nodanāt vā iti pārthivasya paramāṇoḥ agninā abhighātaḥ nodanam vā saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ sa ca karma adhikāre vakṣyate tebhyaḥ vibhāgāḥ tebhyaḥ karmabhyaḥ paramāṇūnām vibhāgāḥ vibhāgebhyaḥ dvi aṇuka ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāḥ saṃga vināśebhyaḥ ca kārya dravyam vinaśyati vibhāgebhyaḥ dvi aṇuka lakṣaṇam kārya dravyam vinaśyati tasmin vinaṣṭe svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogāt agni gata auśṇya apekṣāt śyāmā ādīnām pūrvarūpa rasa gandha sparśānām vināśaḥ punar anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt pāka jāḥ jāyante 
NK_115.5	 svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu pākaja utpattau kārya anavaruddhaḥ eva dravye sarvatra rūpa ādi utpatti darśanam pramāṇam paramāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ kārya anavaruddheṣu eva dravyeṣu bhavanti ārabhyamāṇa rūpa ādi tvāt tantu ādi rūpa ādi vat pūrvarūpa ādi vināśe api rūpa ādi antara utpattiḥ pramāṇam rūpa ādimati rūpa ādi antarātambhā sambhavāt rakta ādi rūpa ādayaḥ rūpa ādimatsu na ārabhyante rūpa ādi tvāt tantu ādi rūpa ādi vat evam paramāṇuṣu pūrvarūpa ādi vināśe siddhe vahni saṃyogaḥ eva vināśa hetuḥ avatiṣṭhate tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt anyasya asambhavāt na ca yat eva rūpa ādīnām vināśa kāraṇam tet eva teṣām utpatti kāraṇam iti avagantavyam tantu rūpa ādīnām anyatas utpatteḥ anyatas ca vināśa darśanāt tena paramāṇuṣu rūpa ādīnām anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt utpattiḥ anyasmāt agni saṃyogāt ca vināśaḥ iti avasīyate paramāṇu rūpa ādi vināśa utpādau= eka kāraṇakau na bhavataḥ rūpa ādi vināśa utpāda tvāt tantu rūpa ādi nāśa utpāda vat 
NK_116.1–116.2^1	 tad anantaram bhoginām adṛṣṭa apekṣā dārmā aṇu saṃyogāt utpanna pāka jeṣu aṇuṣu karma utpattau teṣām paraspara saṃyogāt dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa kārya dravyam utpadyate tatra ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ tad anantaram bhoginām adṛṣṭa apekṣāt ātma aṇu saṃyogāt upanna pāka jeṣu karma utpattau teṣām paraspara saṃyogāt dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kārya dravyam utpadyate iti utpanneṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu yeṣām tad sādhyayoḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ anubhavaḥ bhogaḥ bhaviṣyati te bhoginaḥ teṣām adṛṣṭamm dharma adharma lakṣaṇam tebhyaḥ teṣām paramāṇūnām paraspara saṃyogāḥ tatas ca dvābhyām paramāṇubhyām dvi aṇukam tribhiḥ dvi aṇukaiḥ tri aṇukam iti anena trameṇa kārya dravyam ghaṭa ādikam utpadyate iti tatra ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādi urpattiḥ 
NK_116.2^2	 paramāṇu dvaya rūpābhyām dvi aṇuke rūpam dvi aṇuka rūpebhyaḥ ca tri aṇuka rūpam iti anena krameṇa ghaṭa ādau rūpa rasa gandha sparśa utpattiḥ saṅkhī ā ādīnām na pākaja tvam teṣām avikṣaṇa tvāt nanu sparśasya api vailakṣaṇyam na dṛśyate satyam tathā api tasya pākaja tvam anumānāt tat ca pṛthivī adhikāre deśitam pākaja utpatti anantaram parama aṇuṣu kriyā na tu śyāma ādi nivṛtti sama kālam eva iti rūpa ādimati eva dravye rūpa ādimad kārya dravya ārambha hetu bhūta kriyā darśanāt kalpyate paramāṇu kriyā rūpa ādimati eva jāyate rūpa ādimad kārī a ārambha hetu bhūta kriyā tvāt paṭa ārambhaka saṃyoga utpādaka tantu kriyā vat 
NK_116.3	 atha katham kārya dravye eva rūpa ādīnām agni saṃyogāt utpāda vināśau na kalpyete pratīyante hi pāka artham upakṣiptā ghaṭa ādayaḥ sarva avasthāsu pratyakṣataḥ chidra viniveśita cakṣuṣā pratyabhijñāyante ca pāka uttara kālam api te eva amī ghaṭa ādayaḥ iti tatra āha na ca iti upapattim āha sarva aviyaveṣu iti antar bahis ca sarveṣu avayaveṣu varttamānasya samavetasya avayavinaḥ bāhye varttamānena vahninā avyāpteḥ vyāpakasya saṃyogasya abhāvāt kārya rūpa ādīnām utpatti vināśayoḥ akptiḥ antar varttinām apāka prasaṅgāt iti bhāvaḥ sa= chidrāṇi eva avayavi dravyāṇi tatra yadi nāma mahataḥ tejaḥ avayavinaḥ na antar praveśaḥ asti tad paramāṇūnām tu asti eva tatas vyāptiḥ bhaviṣyati 
NK_117.1–117.2^1	 na ca kārya dravye rūpa ādi utpattiḥ vināśaḥ vā sambhavati sarva avayava īśu antar bahis ca varttamānasya agninā vyāpti abhāvāt aṇu praveśāt epi ca vyāptiḥ na sambhavati kārya dravya vināśāt iti tatra āha aṇu praveśā api iti na tāvat paramāṇavaḥ sa antarāḥ nirbhāga tvāt dvi aṇukasya sāntara tve ca anupapattiḥ eva tasya paramāṇvoḥ a saṃyogāt saṃyuktau ced imau nirantarau= eva sabhāgayoḥ hi vastunoḥ kenacid aṃśena saṃyogāt sa antaraḥ saṃyogaḥ nirbhāgayoḥ tu na ayam vidhiḥ avakalpate sthūla dravyeṣu ca pratīyamāneṣu antaram na pratibhāti eva tri aṇukeṣu eva antaram tat ca anupalabdhi yogya tvāt na pratīyate iti gurvī iyam kalpanā 
NK_117.1–117.2^2	 tasmāt nirantarāḥ eva ghaṭa ādayaḥ teṣām antar tāvat agni paramāṇūnām praveśaḥ bhavati yāvat pārthiva avayavānām vyatibhedaḥ na syāt sparśavati dravye tathābhūtasya dravya antarasya pratīghātāt vyatibhidyamāneṣu ca avayaveṣu kriyā vibhāga ādi nyāyena dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt avaśyam dravya vināśaḥ iti kutas tasya aṇu praveśāt api vyāptiḥ na ca kārya dravyeṣu āśraya vināśāt anyatas rūpa ādīnām vināśaḥ kāraṇa guṇebhyaḥ ca anyatas utpādaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tena api ghaṭa vahni saṃyogāt rūpa ādīnām utpatti vināśau na kalpyete 
NK_117.3^1	 ghaṭa rūpa ādayaḥ āśraya vināśāt eva naśyanti kārya dravya gata rūpa rasa gandha sparśa tvāt mudgara abhihata naṣṭa ghaṭa rūpa ādi vat tathā ghaṭa rūpāt atas kāraṇa guṇebhyaḥ eva jāyante kārya dravya gata rūpa ādi tvāt paṭa gata rūpa ādi vat kiñca pūrvam avayavānām praśithilaḥ saṃyogaḥ āsīt idānīm kāṭhinyam upalabhyate na ca nodana abhighātayoḥ iva śaithilya kāṭhinyayoḥ ekatra samāveśaḥ yuktaḥ paraspara virodhāt tasmāt pūrva vyūha nivṛttau vyūha antaram etat upajātam tathā sati ca prāktana dravya vināśaḥ kāraṇa vināśaḥ dravya antarasya utpādaḥ kāraṇa antara sadbhāvāt eva iti avatiṣṭhate pratyabhijñānam ca jvālā ādi vat sāmānya viṣayam sarva avasthā upalabdhiḥ api kāryasya vinaśyataḥ api krameṇa vināśāt 
NK_117.3^2	 na hi ghaṭaḥ paramāṇu sañcaya ārabdhaḥ yena vibhakteṣu paramāṇuṣu sahasā eva vinaśyet kintu dvi aṇuka ādi praprameṇa ārabdhaḥ tasya svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu dvi aṇuka tri aṇuka ādi asaṅkhyeya dravya vināśa paramparayā cireṇa vinaśyataḥ yā= at na vināśaḥ tāvat upalabdhiḥ asti eva ekatas ca pūrve avayavāḥ vinaśyanti anyatas ca utpanna pāka jaiḥ aṇubhiḥ apūrve tad sthāne eva dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabhyante tena pakva apakva avayava darśanam yadā ca antya avayavānām nāśāt pūrva avayavinaḥ vinaśyattā tadā eva apūrva avayavānām urpādāt avayavi antarasya utpadyam ānata kṣaṇa antare pūrva avayavi vināśaḥ avaya vi antarasya ca utpādaḥ iti ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ avadhāraṇam ca syāt yāvantaḥ pūrvasya avayavāḥ tāvantaḥ eva uttarasya ārambhakāḥ iti tad parimāṇa tvam tad saṅkhyā tvam ca upapadyate 
NK_118.1^1	 prakriyā tu dvi aṇukasya vināśāḥ tri aṇukasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādīnām vinaśyattā sa kriye paramāṇau vibhāga ja vibhāgasya utpadyamāna tā rakta ādi utpādakasya agni saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tri aṇuka vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā śyāma ādīnām vināśaḥ vibhāga ja vibhāgasya utpādaḥ saṃyogasya vinaśyattā rakta ādi utpādaka agni saṃyoga utpādaḥ rakta ādīnām utpadyamāna tā śyāma ādi nivarttaka agni saṃyogasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tri aṇuka kārya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā vibhāga ja vibhāgāt saṃyogasya vināśaḥ uttarasya saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā rakta ādīnām utpādaḥ śyāma ādi ucchedaka agni saṃyogasya vināśaḥ dvitīya paramāṇau dravya ārambhaka kriyāyāḥ utpadyam ānatā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kāryasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vināśyattā uttara saṃyogasya utpādaḥ kriyā vibhāga vibhāga javi bhāgānām vinaśyattā dvitīya paramāṇau kriyāyāḥ utpādaḥ vibhāgasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
NK_118.1^2	 tatas tad kāryasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā kriyā vibhāga vibhāga ja vi bhāgānām vināśaḥ dvitīya paramāṇu ākāśa vibhāgasya utpādaḥ tad saṃyogasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kāryasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā paramāṇu ākāśa saṃyoga vināśaḥ uttara saṃyogasya utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kāryasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā paramāṇoḥ paramāṇu antareṇa saha uttara saṃyoga utpādaḥ dvi aṇukasya utpadyamāna tā vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vinaśyat tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad kāryasya vināśaḥ tad kāryasya vinaśyattā dvi aṇukasya utpādaḥ tad gatānām rūpa ādīnām utpadyamāna tā vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vināśaḥ tatas kṣaṇa antare kāraṇa guṇa prakrameṇa dvi aṇuke guṇa antara utpādaḥ iti evam sarvatra dvi aṇukeṣu kalpanā 
NK_118.2	 tri aṇuka ādi urpattau tu karma na cintanīyam yugapad bahūnām paramāṇūnām saṃyogāt utpanneṣu dvi aṇuka antara kāraṇasya paramāṇoḥ dvi aṇuka antara kāraṇena paramāṇunā saha saṃyogāt dvi aṇukasya dvi aṇuka antara kāraṇa paramāṇunā saṃyogaḥ tatas api dvi aṇukayoḥ saṃyogaḥ iti anena krameṇa dvi aṇuke saṃyoga ja saṃyogebhyaḥ eva eteṣām utpādāt evam yathopadeśam yathāprajñām ca vyākhyātam asmābhiḥ 
NK_119.1–119.2	 eka ādivyadahāra hetuḥ saṃkhyā sarva loka prasiddhe api saṅkhyā svarūpe ye kecid atyanta durdarśana abhyāsa tirohita buddhayaḥ vipratipadyante tān pratīdam āha eka ādi vyavahāra hetuḥ saṅkhyā iti vyavahṛtiḥ vyavahāraḥ jñeya jñānam vyavahriyate anena iti byavahāraḥ śabdaḥ ekaḥ ityādi vyavahāraḥ eka ādi vyavahāraḥ ekam dve trīṇi ityādi pratyayaḥ śabdaḥ ca tayoḥ hetuḥ saṅkhyā iti evam dve trīṇi ityādi pratyayaḥ viśeṣaṇa kṛtaḥ viśiṣṭa pratyaya tvāt daṇḍī iti pratyaya vat evam śabdam api pakṣīkṛtya viśiṣṭa śabda tvāt iti prayogaḥ darśayitavyaḥ 
NK_119.3^1	 nanu ayam pratyayaḥ rūpa ādi viṣayaḥ na tad pratyaya vilakṣaṇa tvāt rūpa nimittaḥ hi pratyayaḥ nīlam pītam iti evam syāt na tu ekam dve ityādi astu tarhi nirviṣayā rūpa ādi vyatiriktasya arthasya abhāvāt kutas asmin= eka dvi tri ādi ākāraḥ jātaḥ ālaya jñāna pratibaddha vāsanā paripākāt iti ced nīla ādi ākāraḥ api tatas eva astu na hi jñāna ārūḍasya tasya saṅkhyā ākārasya ca kaścait anubhava krptaḥ viśeṣaḥ yena ekaḥ artha jaḥ anartha jaḥ ca aparaḥ iti pratipadyāmahe atha ayam viśeṣaḥ ayam abhra antaḥ nīlākāraḥ saṅkhyāraḥ tu viplutaḥ iti tad asāram nīla ākārasya api atra abhra anta tve pramāṇa abhāvāt na tāvat kvacid asya asti saṃvādaḥ tad eka jñāna niyata tvāt kṣaṇika tvāt ca atas eva na artha kriyā api na ca pratyekam sarva jñāneṣu su a ākāra mātra samāhiteṣu pūrvāra jñāna vartti nām ākārāṇām sādṛśya pratipattiḥ asti yena tad sadṛśa ākāra pravāha upalabdhi nibandhanaḥ saṃvādaḥ vyavasthāpyeta na api sadṛśa ākāra upalambhe eva sarvatra vilakṣaṇa ākāra upalambhasya api kvacid bhāvāt 
NK_119.3^2–119.4^1	 na ca artha ja tvāt eva nīla ākārasya abhrānta tva siddhiḥ arthasya apratītau tad janya tva viniścaya ayogāt anyatas ca pramāṇa ādarśa pratīta ākāra kalpanā vaiyarthyāt ākāra saṃvedanāt eva artha siddhi abhyupagameca abhrānta ākāra saṃvedana artha siddhiḥ siddhe ca arthe tad janya tva viniścayāt ākārasya abhrānta tva siddhiḥ iti anyonya apekṣa tvam abādhita tvam ca nīla ākāra vat jñāna ārūḍasya saṅkhyā ākārasya api asti artha gata tvena ca bādhāyāḥ asambhavaḥ nīla ādiṣu api duradhi gataḥ teṣām sva rūpa viprakṛṣṭa tvāt tasmāt ākāra mātra saṃvedanam eva sarvatra sa ced ekatrā anartha jaḥ anyatra api tathā eva iti na nīla ādi siddhiḥ 
NK_119.3^2–119.4^2	 asati bāhye vastuni sva santāna mātra adhīna janmanaḥ vāsanā paripākasya kādācid katva anupapattau tanmātra hetoḥ nīla ādi ākārasya kādācid katva asambhavān nīla ādi kalpanā iti ced eka dvi tri ādi ākārasya api bāhya vaḥ tu ananurodhitaḥ na kādācid ka tvam upapadyate iti saṅkhyā api kalpanīyāḥ upapatteḥ ubhayatra api aviśeṣāt yat api dravya vyatiriktā saṅkhyā na vidyate bhedena agrahaṇāt iti uktam tat api ayuktam paraspara pratyāsannānām vṛkṣāṇām dūrāt eka tva ādi agrahaṇe api svarūpa grahaṇasya sambhavāt evam rūpa ādi vyatirekaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ dūre rūpasya agrahaṇe api dravya pratyaya darśanāt 
NK_120.1–120.3	 sā punar eka dravyā ca aneka dravyā ca tatra eka dravyāyāḥ salila ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām iva nitya anitya tvaṣpattayaḥ aneka dravyā tu dvi tva ādikā parārddhāntāḥ evam saddhe saṅkhyā svarūpe tasyāḥ bhedam pratipādayati sā punar eka dravyā ca aneka dravyā ca iti ekam dravyam āśrayaḥ yasyāḥ sā eka dravyā anekam dravyam āśrayaḥ yasyāḥ sā aneka dravyā aca a śabdau= eka dravya an eka dravyayoḥ anyonya samuccayam pradarśayantau prakāra antara abhāvam kathayataḥ tatra eka dravya aneka dravyayoḥ madhye eka dravyāyāḥ salila ādi paramāṇu rūpa ādīnām iva nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ yathā salila paramāṇau rūpa rasa sparśāḥ nityāḥ tathā ekatva saṅkhyā api yathā ca kārya salilasya rūpa ādayaḥ anityāḥ āśraya vināśāt vinaśyanti kāraṇa guṇa prakrameṇa ca niṣpadyante tathā ekatva saṅkhyā api aneka dravyā tu dvi tva ādikā parārddhāntāḥ dvi tvam ādiḥ yasyāḥ sā dvi tva ādikāḥ parārdha antaḥ yasyāḥ sā parārdha antāḥ yasmin niyatta vyavahāraḥ samāpyate sa parārdhaḥ eka dravya varttinyāḥ eka tva saṅkhyāyāḥ sakāśāt dvi tva ādeḥ aneka vṛtti tva viśeṣa pratipādana arthaḥ atu a ca abdaḥ 
NK_121.1	 tasyāḥ khalu ekatvebhyaḥ aneka viṣaya buddhi sahibhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt vināśaḥ iti katham yadā boddhuḥ cakṣuṣā samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ dravyatoḥ sannikarṣe sati tad saṃyukta samaveta samaveta eka tva sāmānya jñāna utpattau= eka tva sāmānya sat sambandha jñānebhya eka guṇayoḥ aneka viṣayikā buddhiḥ utpadyate tadā tām apekṣya eka tvābhyām sva āśrayayoḥ dvi tvam ārabhyate tatas punar tasmāt dvi tva sāmānya jñānam utpadyate 
NK_121.2–121.3	 tasmāt dvi tva sāmānya jñāmāt apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā dvi tva sāmānya tad sambandha tad jñānebhyaḥ dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyam ānatā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas idānīm apekṣā buddhi vināśāt dvi tva guṇasya vinaśyattā dvi tva guṇa buddhitaḥ sāmānya buddheḥ api vinaśyattā dvi tva guṇa jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ dve dravye iti dravya buddheḥ utpadyam ānatā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
NK_121.4^1	 tasyāḥ khalu ekatvebhyaḥ aneka viṣaya buddhi sahitebhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ apekṣā buddhi vanāśāt ca vināśaḥ khalu iti avadhāraṇe tasyāḥ eka tvebhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ eva na tu ekaika guṇa samuccaya mātra tvam iti arthaḥ eka tve ca eka tvāni ca iti samāsa āśrayaṇam anyathā dvi tva utpatti kāraṇam na kathitam syāt aneka viṣaya buddhi sahitebhyaḥ iti aneka śabdaḥ ekaḥ na bhavati iti vyutpattyā dvayoḥ buhuṣu ca draṣṭavyaḥ anekeṣu viṣayeṣu yā buddhiḥ tathitebhyaḥ iti etat eva praśna pūrvakam pratipādayati katham ityādinā yadā yasmin kāle boddhuḥ ātmanaḥ cakṣuṣā samāna jātīyayoḥ ghaṭayoḥ asamāna jātīyayoḥ ghaṭa paṭayoḥ vā sannikarṣe saṃyoge bhūte sati cakṣuḥ saṃyuktayoḥ dravyayoḥ pratyekam samavetau yau= eka eka guṇau tayoḥ samavetam yat ekatvam sāmānyam tasmin jñānam utpadyate viśeṣaṇa jñānam viśeṣya jñānasya kāraṇam eka guṇayoḥ ca viśeṣyayoḥ eka tva sāmānyam viśeṣaṇam tena ādau tatra eva jñānam cintyate 
NK_121.4^2	 na ca pratti āsattim antareṇa cākṣuṣam jñānam jāyate iti eka tva sāmānyasya indriyeṇa saṃyukta samaveta samavāya lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ darśitaḥ evam jñāna utpattau bhūtāyām eka tva sāmānyāt tasya ekatvasya eka guṇābhyām sambandhāt jñānāt ca eka guṇayoḥ aneka viṣayiṇī ubhaya eka guṇa ālambinī ekā buddhiḥ utpadyate iti ekam cakṣuḥ indriyam antaḥkaraṇena yugapad ubhayoḥ adhiṣṭhāna āsambhavāt ekasya eva sarvadā viṣaya grāhaka tve dvitīyasya kalpanā vaiyarthyāt tasya ubhābhyām golakābhyām raśmayaḥ nissaranti viṣayaiḥ ca saha sambadhyante pradīpasya iva gṛha antargatasya gavākṣa vivarābhyām tatra antaḥkaraṇam sākṣāt cakṣuḥ adhitiṣṭhati na viṣaya sambandhāt bahis nirgamana abhāvāt cakṣuḥ adhiṣṭhānāt eva ca tasya sambandhāḥ jñāna utpatti hetavaḥ evam ca sati yigapad anekeṣu viṣayeṣu jñānam bhavati eva kāraṇa sāmarthyāt tat ca bhavat ekam eva prabhavati ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogasya ekasya eka jñāna utpattau= eva sāmarthyāt
