NK_121.5^1	 atas eva sa vikalpaka utpattiḥ api yugapad abhi vyakteṣu aneka saṅketa viṣayeṣu saṃdkāreṣu smṛti hetuṣu ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogasya sāmarthyāt ekasya aneka viṣaya smaraṇasya utpādāt yadi nāma aneka guṇa ālambanā ekā buddhiḥ upajātā tatas kim iti atas āha tadā tām buddhim apekṣya eka tvābhyām eka guṇābhyām sva āśrayayoḥ dravyayoḥ dvi vyayoḥ dvi tvam ārabhyate sva āśrayayoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvam eka guṇayoḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam aneka viṣayāyāḥ buddheḥ nimitta kāraṇa tvam yadā eka guṇayoḥ ekā buddhiḥ utpadyate tadā eka tvābhyām dvi tvam ātabhyata iti eka kāla tā nirdeṣaḥ kṣaṇa dvaya ātma kalava ākhya kāla abhiprāyeṇa kṣaṇa abhiprāyeṇa tu kāla bhedaḥ eva kārya kāraṇayoḥ pūrva apara kāla bhāvāt 
NK_121.5^2	 jñānāt arthasya utpādaḥ iti na alaukikam idam sukha ādīnām tasmāt upatti darśanāt bāhya arthasya utpādaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ iti na vaidharmya mātram tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvasya ubhayatra api aviśeṣāt ubhaya guṇa jñāna ālambanasya dvi tva abhivyajjaka tve siddhe dve iti jñānasya tadā na anantaryya niyama upapattiḥ iti ced na aniyama prasaṅgāt yadi hi dvi tvam abuddhi jam syāt rūpa ādi vat puruṣa antareṇa api pratīyeta niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt buddhi ja tve tu yasya buddhyā yat janyate tat tena eva upalabhyate iti niyama upapattiḥ prayogaḥ tu dvi tvam buddhi jam niyamena eka pratipattṛ vedya tvāt yat niyamena eka pratipattṛ vesyam tat buddhi jam yathā sukha ādikam niyamena eka pratittṛ vedyam ca dvi tvam tasmāt idam api buddhi jam 
NK_121.6	 evam dvi tvasya utpannasya pratīti kāraṇam nirūpayati tatas punar iti tatas dvi tva utpādāt anantaram dvi tva sāmānye tasmin jñānam utpadyate atra api saṃyukta samavāyaḥ eva hetuḥ eka tva sāmānya apekṣayā punar iti vācoyuktiḥ dvi tva guṇasya viśeṣaṇam na ca agṛhīte viśeṣaṇe viśeṣye buddhiḥ udeti atas viśeṣya jñāna kāraṇa tvena ādau sāmānya jñānam nirūpitam asya sadbhāve api dvi tva sāmānya viśeṣṭāḥ dvi tva buddhiḥ eva pramāṇam tasyāḥ sadbhāve api dve dravye iti jñānam pramāṇam dve dravye iti jñānam viśeṣaṇa ajñāna pūrvakam viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt daṇḍī iti jñāna vat iti anumite guṇa jñāne tasya api viśiṣṭa jñāna tvena viśeṣaṇa jñāna pūrvaka tvam anumeyam 
NK_122.1	 ye tu viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ eka jñāna ālambana tvam āhuḥ teṣām surabhi candanam iti atra kā vārttā na hi vakṣuḥ gandha viṣayam na ca ghrāṇam dravyam ādatte atas eva na tābhyām sambandha grahaṇam ibhaya sambandhi grahaṇa adhīna tvāt sambandha grahaṇasya yathā saṃskāra indriya janyam pratyabhijñā pratyakṣam ubha kāraṇa sāmarthyāt pūrva apara kāla viṣayam evam cakṣuḥ ghrāṇābhyām sambhūya janyamānam idam kāraṇa dvaya sāmarthyāt ubhaya viṣayam syāt iti eke samarthayanti 
NK_122.2^1	 tat api na sādhīyaḥ nirbhāga tvāt yadi jñānam sa bhāgam syāt tadā kaścid asyāṃcaḥ ghrāṇena janyate kaścid cakṣuṣā iti upapadyate vyavasthā kintu idam ekam akhaṇḍam ubhāmyām janitam yadi gandham dravyam ca gṛhṇāti tadā gandhaḥ api cākṣuṣaḥ dravyam api ghrāṇa gamyam prasaktam tad janita jñāna viṣaya tva lakṣaṇa tvāt tad indriya grāhya tāyāḥ na ca aṇu tvāt manasaḥ yugapad ubhaya indriya indriya adhiṣṭhāna sambhavaḥ tasmāt ghrāṇena gandhe gṛhīte paścāt tad grahaṇa sahakāriṇā cakṣuṣā kevala viśeṣya ālambanam eva idam viśeṣya jñānam janyate iti akāmena api abhyupagantavyam 
NK_122.2^2	 tathā ca sati anyeṣām api viśeṣya jñānānām ayam nyāya upatiṣṭhate vivāda adhyāsitam veśeṣya jñānam kevala viśeṣya ālambanam pratyakṣa tve sati viśeṣya jñāna tvāt surabhi candanam iti jñāma vat pratyakṣa tve sati iti laiṅgika jñāna vyavaccheda artham nanu yadi dravya svarūpa mātram eva viśeṣya jñānasya ālambanam asati api viśeṣaṇe tathā pratyayaḥ syāt atha viśeṣaṇasya janaka tvāt na tad abhave viśeṣya jñāna udayaḥ tathā api dravya rūpa pratyayāt asya na viśeṣaḥ viṣaya viśeṣam antareṇa jñānasya viśeṣa antara abhāvāt na anabhyupagamāt 
NK_122.2^3	 na viśiṣṭa jñānasya dravya svarūpa mātram ālambanam brūmaḥ kintu viśiṣṭam viśeṣṭa tā ca svarūpa ati rekiṇī ā iva yā daṇḍī iti jñāne pratibhāsate na khalu tatra puruṣa mātrasya pratītiḥ na api daṇḍa saṃyogitā mātrasya tathā ca daṇḍī iti pratītau= itara vilakṣaṇaḥ eva puruṣaḥ saṃvedyate vailakṣaṇyam ca asya daṇḍīpasarjana tvam eva atas eva viśeṣaṇam vyavacchedakam iti gīyate daṇḍaḥ hi sva upasarjana tā pratipattim puruṣe kurvan puruṣam itarasmāt dyavacchinatti ayam eva ca asya upalakṣaṇāt viśeṣaḥ upalakṣaṇam api vyavacchinatti na tu sva upasarjanatā pratīti hetuḥ na hi yathā daṇḍī iti daṇḍī pasarjana tā puruṣe pratīyate tathā jaṭābhiḥ tāpasaḥ iti tāpase jaṭā upasarjana tā daṇḍī pasarjana tā puruṣasya prādhānyam ca artha kriyāyām upabhoga atiśayā atiśayapekṣayā nanu evam tarhi āpekṣikaḥ ayam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na vāstavaḥ kim na dṛṣṭaḥ bhavadbhiḥ kartṛ karaṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ āpekṣikaḥ vāstavaḥ ca iti kṛtam vistareṇa saṃgrahaṭīkāyām 
NK_122.3	 dvi tva sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyatā ubhaya eka guṇa ālambanā buddhiḥ apekṣā buddhiḥ iti ucyate tasyāḥ dvi tva sāmānya jñānāt vinaśyatā vināśa kāraṇa sānnidhyam dvi tva sāmānyāt tasya dvi tva guṇena saha sambandhāt jñānāt ca dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyam ānātāḥ utpatti kāraṇa sānnidhyam dvi tva sāmānya jñānam apekṣā buddheḥ vināśakam guṇa buddheḥ ca utpādakam tena tad utpattiḥ eva ekasya vinaśyatā parasya ca utpadyam ānatā iti upapadyate vinaśyat ta utpadyamāna tayoḥ eka kāla tvam tatas idānīm apekṣā buddhi nāśāt dvi tvasya vinaśyatta ityādi apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ dvi tva nāśasya kāraṇam tad abhāve tasya anupalambhāt atas apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ dvi tvasya vinaśyattā dṛṣṭaḥ guṇānām nimitta kāraṇā vināśāt api vināśaḥ yathā mokṣa prāpti avasthāyām antya tattva jñānasya śarīra vināśāt 
NK_123.1–124.1–124.4^1	 dvi tva guṇa jñānam dvi tva sāmānyajñā kāraṇam buddheḥ buddhi antara virodhāt tathā dravya jñānasya api kāraṇam atas guṇa buddhi utpādaḥ eva ekasya utpadyamāna tā aparasya vinaśyatā syāt dvi tva guṇa jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ iti dvi tva guṇaḥ ca tasya jñānam ca sambandhaḥ ca iti yojanā tad anantaram dve dravye iti dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ dvi tvasya vināśaḥ dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ vinaśyattā dravya jñānāt saṃskārasya utpadyam āna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tad anantaram dravya jñānāt dvi tva guṇa buddheḥ vināśaḥ dravya buddheḥ api saṃskārāt iti tad anantaram dve dravye iti dravya jñānasya utpādaḥ dvi tvasya vināśaḥ guṇa buddheḥ vināśyattā saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā dvi tva sāmānya jñānasya vināśaḥ guṇa buddheḥ vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ yadi api dve dravye iti jñāna utpatti kāle dvi tvam na asti tathā api tat asya kāraṇam kārya utpatti kāle kāraṇa sthiteḥ anupayogāt kārya utpatti anuguṇa vyāpāra janaka tvam hi kāraṇasya kāraṇa tvam 
NK_124.1–124.4^2	 sa ced anena kṛtaḥ kim asya kārya utpatti kāle sthityā vyāpārāt eva kārya utpatti siddheḥ na tu evam sati tasya akāraka tvam vyāpāra dvāreṇa tasya eva hetu tvāt na ca evam sati bhāktam kāra karvam sva vyāpāreṇa vyavadhāna abhāvāt anyathā śara mukti sama kālam niṣṭhura pṛṣṭha abhighātāt abhipatitasya dhanvinaḥ kṣaṇa antara bhāvani lakṣya vyatibhede kartṛ tvam na syāt tad anantaram dravya jñānāt guṇa buddheḥ vināśaḥ saṃskārasya utpadyamāna tā tatas saṃskārasya utpādaḥ dravya buddheḥ vinaśyattā kṣaṇa antara saṃskārāt dravya buddheḥ vināśaḥ dravya buddhi vināśa kāraṇa tvam ca saṃskārasya tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt anyasyāḥ asambhavāt ca 
NK_125.1–125.2	 etena tri tva ādi utpattiḥ vyākhyātāḥ eka tvebhyaḥ aneka viṣaya buddhi sahibhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ apekṣā buddhi vanāśāt ca vināśaḥ iti etena tri tva ādi utpattiḥ vyākhyātāḥ etena dvi tva utpatti vināśa nirūpaṇa prakrameṇa tritva ādīnām utpattiḥ vyākhyātāḥ tam eva prakāram darśayati eka tvebhyaḥ aneka viṣaya buddhi sahitebhyaḥ niṣpattiḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt ca vināśaḥ iti 
NK_125.3^1	 etena śata saṅkhyā ādi utpattiḥ api samarthitā pratyekam anubhūteṣu ekaika guṇeṣu krama bhāvinām saṃskārāṇām antya guṇa anubhava anantaram śata vyavahāra saṃvartaka adṛṣṭa āt yugapad abhi vyaktau saṃyoga eka tvāt aneka viṣaya eka smaraṇa utpāde satya yubhava smaraṇābhyām apekṣā buddhibhyām sva āśrayeṣu śata saṅkhyā janyate sā ca pūrva dravya saṃskāra sacivāḥ antya dravya saṃyukta indriya jñāna viṣaya tvāt pratyakṣā eva yatra vinaṣṭeṣu saṅkheyeṣu ante saṅkana ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ jāyate śatam pipīlikānām mayā nihatam iti tatra katham śata saṅkhyāyāḥ utpatti āśraya abhāvāt na utpadyate eva tatra sā kāraṇa abhāvāt śata vyavahāraḥ tu rūpa ādiṣu iva gauṇaḥ iti eke samarthayanti apare tu pratīteḥ tulya tvāt upacāra kalpa nāmanādṛtya atītānām eva dravyāṇām saṃskāra upanīta tvāt āśrayatām icchanti yat atyantam asat kha puṣpa ādi tat akāraṇam niḥsvabhāva tvāt 
NK_125.3^2–125.4^1	 atītānām tu vartamāna kāla sambandhaḥ na asti na tu svarūpam teṣām smṛti sannihitānām tad kārya anuguṇa sahakāri lābhāt samavāyi kāraṇa tvam aviruddham na ca evam sati sarvatra tathā abhāvaḥ yathādarśanam vyavasthāpanāt atītasya janaka tve anubhavasya eva smṛti hetu tva sambhave saṃskāra kalpanā vaiyarthyam iti ced na niranvaya pradhvastasya anupasthitasya api kāraka tvāt tad upasthāpaka anvaya kalpanāyām tu saṃskāra siddhiḥ tathā ca antya varṇa pratīti kāle pūrva varṇānām vinaṣṭānām api smṛti upanīta tvāt artha pratītau nimitta kāraṇa tvam asti eva 
NK_125.3^2–125.4^2	 yathā idam tathā samavāyikāraṇa tvam api keṣāñcid bhaviṣyati yathā ca saṃskāra sacivasya manasaḥ bāhye smṛti utpādana sāmarthyam evam pratyakṣa anubhava janana sāmarthyam api dṛṣṭa tvāt eṣitavyam evam ca sati na andha badhira ādi abhāvaḥ bāhya indriya pravṛtti anuvidhāyi tvāt yatra vinaṣṭaḥ eva āśraye smṛti upanīte dvi tvam utpadyate tatra smṛti lakṣaṇa apekṣā buddhi vināśāt eva asya vināśaḥ yatra tu āśraye vidyamāne tad utpannam tatra na kevalam apekṣā buddhi vināśāt asya vināśaḥ kvacid āśraya vināśāt api syāt 
NK_126.1–126.2	 kvacid ca āśraya vināśāt api katham yadā ekatva ādhāra avayave karma utpadyate tadā eva eka tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate karmaṇā ca avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate apekṣā buddheḥ ca utpattiḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle dvi tvam utpadyate saṃyoga vināśāt dravya vināśaḥ sāmānya buddheḥ ca utpattiḥ 
NK_126.3–126.4	 tatas yasmin eva kāle sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle āśraya vināśāt dvi tva vināśaḥ iti śobhanam etat vidhānam vadhya ghātaka pakṣe saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇe tu virodhe dravya jñāna anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ katham guṇa buddhi sama kālam apekṣā buddhi vināśāt dvi tva vināśe tad apekṣasya dve dravye iti dravya jñānasya anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti 
NK_126.5	 ekasya dravyasya dvayoḥ vā dravyayoḥ abhāvāt dve iti pratyaya abhāvāt iti āha kvacid ca āśraya vināśāt api iti katham iti ajñena pṛṣṭaḥ tad upapādayan āha yadā iti yasmin kāle eka guṇa āśrayasya dravyasya avayave kriyā utpadyate tasmin kāle eka guṇa varttinī eka tva sāmānye jñānam utpadyate kṣaṇa antare karmaṇā ca avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate eka tva sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ ca utpattiḥ yasmin eva kāle avaya vi vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tadā apekṣā buddheḥ dvi tvam utpadyate tatas saṃyoga vināśāt dravyasya vināśaḥ dvi tva sāmānya buddheḥ ca utpādaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
NK_126.6	 tatas yasmin kāle dvi tva sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ tadā eva avayavi vināśāt dvi tvasya vināśaḥ na tu apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ tasya kāraṇam sahabhāvi tvāt atra yadi api dve dravye iti jñānam akṛtvā eva praṇaṣṭasya dvi tvasya utpattyā na kiñcid prayojanam tathā api kāraṇa sāmarthya bhāvī kārya utpādaḥ na prayojana apekṣaḥ iti tad utpatti cintā kṛtā 
NK_126.7	 iha khalu dvi tva utpatti prakramepūrva pūrva jñānasya uttarottara jñānāt vināśaḥ darśitaḥ sa ca ayam jñānānām virodhe sati upapadyate virodham ca teṣām vadhya ghātaka svabhāvam kecid icchanti saha anavasthānam ca apare tatra ācāryaḥ vadhya ghāta kapekṣa parigraham kurvan= āha śobhanam etat vidhānam iti etat vidhānam eṣa dvi tva utpatti prakāraḥ vadhya ghātaka pakṣe dvitīyam jñānam utpadya kṣaṇa antare pūrva vijñānam nāśayati iti pakṣe śobhnam yuktam iti arthaḥ saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇe virodhe tu ekasya jñānasya utpādaḥ aparasya vināśaḥ iti pakṣe dve dravye iti jñāna anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ na yuktaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ etat eva upapādayati katham ityādinā saha anavasthā anapekṣe hi dvi tva sāmānya jñāna utpatti kāle eva apekṣā buddheḥ vināśāt dvi tvasya vinaśyattā guṇa buddhi sama kālam ca dvi tvasya vināśaḥ iti kṣaṇa antare dvi tvapekṣasya dve dravye iti jñānasya utpattiḥ na bhavet kāraṇa abhāvāt 
NK_127.1–127.2	 laiṅgika vat jñna mātrāt iti ced syāt matam yathā abhūtam bhūtasya iti atra liṅga abhāve api jñāna mātrāt anumānam tathā guṇa vināśe api guṇa buddhi mātrāt dravya prayayaḥ syāt iti na viśeṣya jñāna tvāt na hi viśeṣya jñānam sārūpyāt viśeṣaṇa sambandha mantreṇa bhavitum arhati tathā ca āha sūtrakāraḥ samavāyinaḥ śvaityāt śvaitya buddheḥ śvete buddhiḥ te kārya kāraṇa bhūte iti 
NK_127.3	 atra aśaṅkate laiṅgika vat iti etat vispaṣṭayati syāt matam ityādinā evam te matam syāt idam abhipretam bhavet yathā dhvani viśeṣeṇa puruṣa anumāne jjātam jñāna anantaram eva dhvani lakṣaṇam liṅgam abhūtam avidyamānam vinaṣṭam eva bhūtasya vidyamānasya puruṣa viśeṣasya liṅgam bhavati iti liṅgasya abhāve api tad jñāna mātrāt eva laiṅgikam jñānam jāyate tathā guṇa buddhi sama kālam dvi tve vinaṣṭe api tad jñāna mātrāt eva dve dravye iti jñānam syāt iti anyaḥ tu abhūtam varṣa karma bhūtasya vāyu abhra saṃyogasya liṅgam iti atra varṣa karmaṇoḥ yathā liṅgasya abhāve api tad jñāna mātrāt eva anumānam iti vyācaṣṭe tad asaṅgatam na hi atra varṣa karma liṅgam api tu tasya abhāvaḥ sa ca tadānīm asti eva sva rūpeṇa vastu anutpāde prāc abhāvasya avināśāt tasmāt asmad uktā eva rītiḥ anusaraṇīyā 
NK_127.4	 parihāram āha na viśeṣya jñāna tvāt iti jñāna mātrāt eva dve dravye iti jñāna utpattiḥ iti etat na kasmāt viśeṣya jñāna tvāt bhavatu viśeṣya jñānam tathā api kutas jñāna mātrāt na bhavati tatra āha na hi iti viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyasya sarūpam viśeṣyasya anurañjakam viśeṣye sva upasarjana tā pratīti hetuḥ iti yāvat na ca avidyamānasya anurañjaka tvam sva upasarjana tā pratīti hetu tvam yuktam atas na viśeṣya jñānam viśeṣaṇa sambandham antareṇa bhavitum arhati iti viśeṣya jñānam sārūpyāt viśeṣaṇa anukta tvāt viśeṣaṇa sambandham antareṇa bhavitum na arhati iti atra arthe sūtrakāra anumatim darśayati tathā ca aha iti samavāyinaḥ samavetāt śvaityāt śveta guṇāt śvaitya buddheḥ śveta guṇa buddheḥ śvete dravye buddhiḥ bhavati śvetam dravyam iti te viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya buddhī kārya kāraṇa bhūte kārya kāraṇa svabhāve iti sūtreṇa viśeṣaṇasya anutañjaka tvam uktam tat ca avidyamānasya na asti iti bhāvaḥ 
NK_128.1–128.2	 na tu laiṅgikam jñānam abhedena utpadyate tasmāt viṣamaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ na āśu utpatteḥ yathā śabdavat ākāśam iti atra trīṇi jñānāni āśu utpadyante tathā dvi tva ādi jñāna utpattauvityadoṣaḥ samprati laiṅgika jñānasya viśeṣya jñānāt atu aśabdena viśeṣam sūcayan= āha na tu iti laiṅgikam jñānam liṅga abhedena liṅginaḥ liṅga upasarjana tā grāhi tayā na utpadyata tasmāt viṣamaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ laiṅgika vat iti upanyāsaḥ viṣamaḥ dve dravye iti jñānena saha tulyaḥ na bhavati iti arthaḥ dve dravye iti jñāna kāle dvi tvam api na asti katham tat viśiṣṭam eva grahaṇam na jñāna utpatteḥ pūrvasmin kṣaṇe yasya sadbhāvāt sarvatra hi pratyakṣa jñānasya pūrvakṣaṇa varti eva arthoḥ viṣayaḥ asti ca dve dravye iti jñāna utpādāt pūrvasmin kṣaṇe dvi tvam iti tad upasarjana tā pratyayaḥ bhavati eva 
NK_128.3	 idam tu iha vaktavyam dve dravye iti jñāne yathā dravyam pratibhāti tathā upasarjanībhūtam dvi tvam api na ca avidyamānasya dvi tvasya pratibhāsaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt etat avinaṣṭam eva tadānīm viśeṣya jñānasya ālambanam syāt tad abhā samāna tā lakṣaṇa tvāt tad ālambanatāyāḥ iti atas āha na aśu utpatteḥ iti dravya jñāna kāle dvi tvam na vinaṣṭam iti etat na āśu utpattet vi tva guṇa jñānasya dravya jñānasya ca śīghram utpādāt kramasya agrahaṇe dvi tva dravyayoḥ ekasmin= eva jñāne pratibhāsaḥ iti abhimānaḥ vastu vṛttyā tu pūrvam dvi tvasya pratibhāsaḥ tad anudravyasya iti arthaḥ atra prakṛta anurūpam dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā iti śabda vat ākāśam iti atra śabda jñānam ākāśa jñānam śabda viśiṣṭa ākāśa jñānam ca trīṇi jñānāni āśu utpadyante yathā tathā dve ityādi vijñāna utpattau= api kim uktam syāt yathā śabda ādi jñāneṣu āśu bhāvitayā kramasya agrahaṇe yugapad pratibhāsā abhimānaḥ tathā dvi tva dravya jñānayoḥ api iti 
NK_129.1–129.3	 vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api samānaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam nanu vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api tarhi dravya jñāna anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ katham sāmānya buddhi sama kālam saṃskāra apekṣā buddhi vināśāt iti na samūha jñānasya saṃskāra hetu tvāt samūha jñānam eva saṃskāra kāraṇam na ālocana jñānam iti adoṣaḥ jñāna yaigapadya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced syāt matam nanu jñānānām vadhya ghātaka vi rodhe jñāna yaiga padya prasaṅgaḥ iti na avinaśyatoḥ avasthāna pratiṣedhāt jñāna ayaugapadya vacanena jñānayoḥ yugapad utpattiḥ avinaśyatoḥ ca yugapad ava sthānam pratiṣidhyate na hi vadhya ghātaka vi rodhe jñānayoḥ yugapad utpattiḥ avinaśyatoḥ ca yugapad ava sthānam asti iti 
NK_129.4^1	 vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api dravya jñāna anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti kenacid uktam tadāśaṅkate vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api iti asya artham vivṛṇoti syāt matam ityādinā yadi guṇa buddhi sama kālam dvi tva vināśe dravya jñānam na utpadyate tarhi vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api tad anutpattiḥ atra upapattim āha sāmānya buddhi sama kālam saṃskārāt apekṣā buddhi vināśāt iti yathā apekṣā buddhiḥ utpannā dvi tvam janayati tathā saṃskāram api sa ca tasyāḥ vināśakaḥ tena saṃskārasya dvi tvasya ca utpāde dvi tva sāmānya jñānasya ca utpadyamāna tapa īkṣā buddheḥ vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dvi tva sāmānya jñānasya ca utpādaḥ guṇa buddheḥ ca utpadyamāna tāpekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ dvi tvasya vinaśyatta iti ekaḥ kālaḥ 
NK_129.4^2	 tatas guṇa buddheḥ utpādaḥ dvi tvasya vināśaḥ iti kṣaṇa antare tad apekṣasya dve iti jñānasya anutpādaḥ iti vadhya ghātaka pakṣe api tulyaḥ doṣaḥ samādhatte na samūha jñānasya saṃskāra hetu tvāt iti saṃskārāt apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti etat na kṛtaḥ samūha jñānasya saṃskāra hetu tvāt etat eva vivṛṇoti samūhaḥ ityādinā samūha jñānam dvi tva guṇa viśiṣṭa dravya jñānam eva saṃskāram karoti na ālocana jñānam na nirvikalpam apekṣā jñānam atas na asya saṃskārāt vināśaḥ iti arthaḥ apekṣā jñānasya saṃskāra ahetu tve dravya vivekena eka guṇayoḥ smaraṇam pramāṇam guṇa viśiṣṭa dravya jñānasya tad hetu tve ca viśiṣṭa dravya smaraṇam pramāṇam 
NK_129.5	 yadi jñānam utpadya pūrva utpannam jñānam vināśayati tadā ekasmin kṣaṇe tayoḥ saha avasthānam prāpnoti tatas ca jñāna ayaugapadyāt iti sūtra virodhaḥ iti kenacid uktam tadāśaṅkate jñāna yaugapadya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced syāt matam ityādinā asya vivaraṇam karoti nanu ityādinā samādhatte na iti ekasmin kṣaṇe vināśya vināśaka jñānayoḥ saha avasthānam na doṣāya jñāna ayaugapadyāt iti sūtreṇa avinaśyatoravasthāna pratiṣedhāt etat eva darśayati jñāna ayaugapadya vacanena yugapad utpattiḥ avinaśyatoḥ ca yugapad ava sthānam pratiṣidhyate iti vadhya ghātaka pakṣam ca na jñānayoḥ yugapad utpādaḥ asti na api avinaśyatoḥ saha avasthānam ekasya utpāde dvitīyasya vinaśyat rūpa tvāt iti āha na hi iti aiti aśabdaḥ samāptim kathayati 
NK_130.1^1	 ayi bhoḥ sarvam idam utpatti ādi nirūpaṇam dvi tvasya anupapannam tad sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt dve iti jñānam pramāṇa eti ced na grāhya lakṣaṇa abhāvāt tathā hi arthaḥ jñāna granyaḥ bhavat = utpannaḥ anutpannaḥ vaḥ ubhayathā api anupapattiḥ anutpannasya asatvāt utpannasya ca sthiti abhāvāt atītaḥ eva arthaḥ jñāna grāhyaḥ tad janaka tvāt iti ced na vartamāna tā avabhāsa virodhāt indriyasya api grāhya tva prasaṅgāt ca īdṛśaḥ eva arthasya sva kāraṇa sāmagrīkṛtaḥ svabhāvaḥ yena janakatvā aviśeṣe api ayam eva grāhyaḥ na indriya ādikam tad ananta rakṣaṇa viṣayaḥ ca vartamāna tā avabhāsaḥ iti ced kim punar idam asya grāhya tvam jñānam prati hetu tvam iti ced punar api indriyasya grāhya tvam āpatitam hetu tva mātrasya tatra api aviśeṣāt jñānasya sva saṃvedanam eva artha asya grāhyatā iti ced anyasya svarūpa saṃvedanam anyasya grāhyatā iti ati citram etat na citram svabhāvasya aparyanuyojya tvāt artha avagraha svabhāvam hi vijñānam 
NK_130.1^2	 tena asya svarūpa saṃvedanam eva arthasya grahaṇam bhavati yad artha jam ca idam tasya eva ayam avagrahaḥ na sarvasya iti na ati prasaktiḥ na eka tvāt arthaja tvam nāma jñānasya arthāt utpattiḥ sā ca ekā na jñāna arthayoḥ ubhayoḥ dharmaḥ bhavatum arhati aneka vṛtti tvena nānātva āpātāt yadi tu jñānasya dharmaḥ na artham niyamayet atha arthasya na jñānam anya dharma tvāt ubhaya niyamāt ca tayoḥ paraspara grāhya grāhaka bhāva vyavasthā na eka sambandhi niyamāt na ca atīta anāgatayoḥ arthayoḥ jñānam pratyasti kāraka tvam asattvāt viṣaya viṣayi bhāva niyamāt grāhya grāhaka bhāva niyamaḥ iti ced na abhedāt grāhya tvam eva viṣaya tvam grāhaka tvam ca viṣayi tvam tayoḥ pratiniyame eva kāraṇe pṛṣṭe tat eva uttaram ucyate iti sarva uttara dhiyām idam parisphupati niyata artha grāhitā api jñānasya svabhāvaḥ iti ced sa punar asya svabhāvaḥ yadi nirhetukaḥ niyamaḥ na prāpnoti atha kāraṇa vaśāt tat evaḥ cyatām kim svabhāva parighoṣaṇayā na ca tad tad utpatteḥ anyat paśyāmaḥ 
NK_130.2–130.3	 atha ucyate yat utpādayati sarūpayati ca jñānam tat asya grāhyam na itarat avaśyam ca arthāraḥ jñāne aparyoṣitavyaḥ anyathā nirākārasya bodha mātrasya sarva artham pratyaviśeṣāt nīlasya idam pītasya idam iti vyavasthā anupaptau tatas artha viśeṣa prati iti abhāvāt atas eva viṣaya ākāram pramāṇam āhuḥ sa ca asādhāraṇaḥ jñānam artha viśeṣeṇa saha ghaṭayati na sādhāraṇam indriya ādikam tat uktam arthena ghaṭayati enām na hi muktvā artha rūpa tām tasmāt prameya adhigateḥ pramāṇam meya rūpa tā 
NK_131.1^1	 aparatra ca uktam na hi vitti sattā eva tad vedanā yuktāḥ tasyāḥ sarvatra aviśeṣāt tām tu sārūpyam āviśat sarūpayantam ghaṭayet ita atra ucyate sa ākāreṇa jñānena kim arthaḥ anubhūyate kim va su ākāraḥ kim uta ubhayam na tāvat ubhayam nīlam etat iti ekasya eva ākārasya sarvadā saṃvedanāt arthasya ca jñānena anubhavaḥ na yuktaḥ tasya svarūpa sattā kāle jñāna anutpādāt jñāna kāle ca atītasya vartamāna tayā avabhāsā yogāt jñāna sahabhāvinaḥ kṣaṇasya ayam varttamāna tā avabhāsaḥ iti sva siddhānta śraddhālutā iyam tasya tat agrāhya tvāt kaḥ ca atra hetuḥ yat vijñānam niyatam artham bodhayati na sarvam na hi tayoḥ asti tādātmyam tad utpattiḥ ca na vyavasthā hetuḥ iti iktam tad ākāra tā niyam ahetuḥ iti ced kim iti ekaḥ nīlakṣaṇaḥ samāna ākāram nīla antaram na gṛhṇāti grāhaka tvam jñānasya eva svabhāvaḥ na arthasya iti ced 
NK_131.1^2	 tathā api ekam nīla vijñānam sarveṣām nīlakṣaṇānām grāhakam syāt tad ākāra tva aviśeṣāt tad utpatti sārūpyābhyām sva utpādakasya eva artha kṣaṇasya grāhyatā na sarveṣām iti ced indriya samanantara pratyayayoḥ api grāhyatā āpattiḥ tābhyām api hi jñānam utpadyate bibharti ca tayoḥ yathāsvam viṣaya grahaṇa pratiniyamam bodha ātmaka tvam ca sārūpyam atha matam yat etat viṣaya grahaṇa pratiniyata tvam indriya sārūpyam vijñānasya yat api samanantara pratyaya sārūpyam bodha ātmaka tvam tat ubhayam api sarva jñāna sādhāraṇam asādhāraṇam tu viṣaya sārūpyam vijñānasya nīla je eva nīla jñāne nīla ākārasya saṃbhavāt yaḥ ca asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ saḥ eva niyāmakaḥ iti etāvatā viśeṣeṇa jñānam artham gṛhṇāti na indriya samanantara pratyayau iti tat api asāram samāna viṣayasya samanantara pratyayasya grahaṇa prasaṅgāt 
NK_131.2	 yaḥ vijñāne nīla ādi ākāram arpayati saḥ eva tasya grāhyaḥ na ca dhārāvāhika vijñāne samanantara pratyayāt nīla ādi ākārasya utpattiḥ kintu arthāt arthasya eva tad utpattau= anvaya vyatirekābhyām sarvatra sāmarthya upalabdheḥ bodha ākāra utpattau eva bodhasya sāmarthya avagamāt iti ced nila ādya ākāra samarpakaḥ grāhyaḥ iti kasya iyam ājñā na anyasya kasyacid tasya eva tu grāhya tva svabhāva niyamaḥ niyāmakaḥ evam svabhāva niyamāt eva niyamaḥ astu jñānam hi sva sām agrī pratiniyamāt pratiniyata artha saṃvedana ātmakam eva upajāyate arthaḥ api saṃvedya svabhāva niyamāt eva saṃvedyate na indriya ādikam iti akāraṇam ākāraḥ na hi chidi kriyā vṛkṣa ākāravatī yena iyam vṛkṣeṇa saha sambaddhyate na kuṭhāreṇa kintu asyāḥ vṛkṣasya ca tādṛśaḥ svabhāvaḥ yat iyam atra eva niyamyata na anyatra asya idam saṃvedanam iti ca vyavasthā tatra asya tad avabhāsa mātra nibandhana eva iti tad artham api ākāraḥ na mṛgyaḥ 
NK_131.3	 atha sa ākāreṇa jñānena arthaḥ na saṃvedyate eva kintu su a ākāra mātram tad artha sadbhāvaḥ niṣpramāṇakaḥ na tāvat arthasya grahaṇam na ca adhyavasāyaḥ vikalpaḥ hi adhyavasyati sa ca utprekṣā mātra vyāpāraḥ bhavan= api pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvi tvāt yatra pratyakṣam pravṛttam tatra sva vyāpāram parityajya kāraṇa vyāpāram upādadānaḥ vastu sākṣa ātmaroti yatra tu pratyakṣam eva apravṛttam tatra vikalpaḥ api asamartham eva kāraṇa abhāvāt jñāna ākāraḥ sva sadṛśam kāraṇam vyavasthāpayan= artha siddhau pramāṇam iti ced tat kim idānīm sthūla ākārasya samarpakārasya samarpakaḥ api arthaḥ bahis asti kā gatiḥ asya vacanasya 
NK_131.4–131.5	 tasmāt na arthena vijñāne sthūla ābhāsaḥ tad ātmanaḥ ekatra pratiṣiddha tvāt bahuṣu api na sambhavaḥ iti atha ayam anartha jaḥ kutaścid nimittāt kadācid bhavati asannava vā pratīyate tadvat itara ākāraḥ api bhaviṣyati asan eva vā pratyeṣyate na ca ākāra vāde jñāna ākārāṇām bhrānta abhra anta tva vivekaḥ sugamaḥ iti nirūpita prāyam 
NK_131.6	 kiñca tadānīm bodha ākāraḥ sadṛśam artham kāraṇam kalpayati yadi yādṛśaḥ bodhākāraḥ tādṛśaḥ eva arthāḥ tasya kāraṇam iti avagatam na ca arthasya asaṃvedya tve tathā pratītiḥ saṃbhavati hetu tva sā adṛśyayoḥ viniścayasya ubhaya grahaṇa adhīna tvāt iti na ākārāt artha saddhiḥ tat evam na hetu tvam grāhya lakṣaṇam na api ākāra arpaṇa kṣamasya hetu tvam tasmāt grāhya lakṣaṇa abhāvāt buddheḥ anyaḥ anubhāvyaḥ na asti iti sādhu uktam 
NK_131.7^1	 itas api buddhi vyatiriktaḥ arthaḥ na asti yadi asau jaḍaḥ na svayam prakāśeta na ca tasya prakāśaka antaram upalabhāmahe sarvadā eva ekasya eva ākārasya upalambhāt atha asti prakāśam na tad svayam aprakāśa mānam aprakāśa svabhāvam viṣayam api prakāśayet yat avyakta prakāśam tat avyaktam yathā kuḍya ādi vyavahitam vastu avyakta prakāśaḥ ca parasya bāhyaḥ arthaḥ tathā yat parasya prakāśakam tad sva prakāśe sajātīya para anapekṣam yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśakam ca parasya jñānam iti atas prakāśamānasya eva bodhasya viṣaya prakāśaka tvam iti nyāyāt anapetam tathā sati saha upalambha niyamāt sat candra asat candrayoḥ iva vedya vedakayoḥ abhedaḥ bhedasya hi saha upalambha aniyamaḥ vyāpakaḥ nīla pīryugapad upalanbha niyama abhāvāt saha upalambhān iyama viruddhaḥ ca saha upalambha niyamaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhyā bhedāt aniyama vyāptyā vyāvartamānaḥ niyamaḥ abhede vyavatiṣṭhate iti pratibandha siddhiḥ 
NK_131.7^2	 na ca asaha aśabdasya sāhāyyam yaugapadyam vā arthaḥ tayoḥ ca bhedena vyāpta tvāt viruddhaḥ iti vācyam ābhimānikasya sahabhāvasya hetu viśeṣaṇa tvena upādānāt dṛṣṭānte dvi candre ābhimānikaḥ sahabhāvaḥ na tāttvikaḥ candrasya eka tvāt sārvajñya vid takṣaṇaḥ svena ātmānā saha sarvān prāṇinaḥ yugapad upalabhate na ca teṣām sarva jñāt abhedaḥ iti anaikāntika tvam iti ced na aniyamāt kṣaṇa abhiprāyeṇa tāvat yayoḥ saha upalambhaḥ tayoḥ asau niyataḥ eva kṣaṇikayoḥ pratyekaḥ punar anupalambhāt kintu sa na vivakṣitaḥ santāna abhiprāyeṇa saha upalambha niyamaḥ hetu arthaḥ na ca sarvajña santānasya citta antara santānena saha yugapad upalambhaḥ asti sarvajñsya kadācid sva ātma mātra pratiṣṭhasya api sambhavāt na ca tadānīm ayama sarvajñaḥ sarva jñāna sāmarthaya sambhavāt 
NK_131.8	 apacan= api pācakaḥ yathā tathā yat vedyate yena vedanena tat tatas na bhidyate yathā ātmā jñānasya vedyante ca nīla ādayaḥ bhede hi jñānena asya vedya tvam na syāt tādātmyasya niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt tad utpatteḥ aniyāka tvāt anyena anyasya asambaddhasya vedya tve ca ati praṅgāt iti bhede niyama hetoḥ sambandhasya vyāpakasya anupalabdhyā bhedāt vipakṣāt vyāvartamānam vedya tvam abhedena vyāpyate iti hetoḥ pratibandha siddhiḥ iti etena aham iti ākārasya api jñānāt abhedaḥ samarthitaḥ yaḥ ca ayam grāhya grāhaka saṃvittīnām pṛthak avabhāsaḥ saḥ ekasmin= candramasi dvi tva bhāsaḥ iva bhramaḥ tatra api anādiḥ avicchinna pravāha abheda vāsanā eva nimittam yathā uktam 
NK_131.9–131.12	 bhedeḥ ca bhrānta vijñāne dṛśyeta indau= iva advaye iti nanu bāhya abhāve yryam nīla ādi ākārā buddhiḥ udeti tasyāḥ kim kāraṇam yathā uktam arthabhddhiḥ tad ākārā sā tu ākāra viśeṣaṇā sā bāhyāt anyatas vā iti vicāram imam arhati atra api vadanti bāhya sadbhāve tasyām kim kāraṇam nīlādiḥ arthaḥ iti ced na tāvat ayam dṛśyate arthasya sadā atīndriya tvāt kārya vaicitryeṇa kalpanīyaḥ ced dṛśyasya samanantara pratyayasya eva śakti vaicitryam kalpyatām yena sva prajñāne api āra vaicitryam ghaṭate na hi tatra deśa kāla vyavahitānām arthānām sāmarthyam avidyamāna tvāt nanu evam citra pratyayaḥ api na syāt jñānasya ekatve tat avyatirekiṇām api ekatva prasaṅgāt pratyākāram ca jñāna bhede jñānānām pratyekam su a ākāra mātra niyata tvāt tebhyaḥ vyatiriktasya ca sarva ākāra grāhakasya abhāvāt 
NK_132.1	 atra brūmaḥ tāvat citram rūpam na prakāśate saṃvitti virodhāt jaḍasya ca prakāśa ayogaḥ tena idam jñāna ātmakam ekam eva rūpam na ca ākāra bhedāt jñāna bhedaḥ citra rūpasya ekasya ākāra bheda abhāvāt yathā nīlasya ekasya ekaḥ nīla svabhāvaḥ ākāraḥ tathā citrasya ekasya citra svabhāvaḥ ākāraḥ tasmin= ca ātma bhūte jñānam pravartamānam kṛtsnaḥ eva pravartate yadi vā na pravartate eva na tu bhāgena pravartate tasya nirbhāga tvāt ye tu amī bhāgāḥ paraspara viviktāḥ pratibhānti na te citram rūpam iti na kācid anupapattiḥ sthūla ākāraḥ api anayā eva diśā samarthanīyaḥ avayavaḥ tu ekaḥ sthūlaḥ vā na upapadyate nānā avayava vṛtti tvena tasya nānā tva āpātāt jñāna ākāraḥ tu ekasmin jñāne vartamānaḥ ekaḥ sthūlaḥ bhavati eva kampā kampa ādi virodhaḥ tu saṃvid virodhāt paryudasanīyaḥ iti kecid 
NK_132.2	 apare tu jñāna ākārasya api anādi vāsanā vaśena pratibhāsamānasya vicāra akṣam atvam alīka tvam eva tattvam āhuḥ tathā ca yaḥ pratyayaḥ sa bāhya anālambanaḥ yathā svapna ādi pratyayaḥ pratyayaḥ ca ayam jāgrataḥ stambha ādi pratyayaḥ nirālambanatā hi pratyayasya tanmātra anubandhinī svapna ādiṣu dṛṣṭāḥ jāgrataḥ pratyayasya api pratyaya tvam eva svabhāvaḥ sa yadi nirālambana tvam parityajati tadā svabhāvam eva parityajet nanu sarva pratyayānām anālambana tve dharmi hetu dṛṣṭānta ādi pratyayānām anālambana tvam tatas ca dharmi hetu tva ādi abhāvāt na anumāna pravṛttiḥ atha te sa ālambanāḥ taiḥ eva asya hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ na evam teṣām paramārthataḥ bahis anālambanānām saṃvṛtti mātreṇa anumāna pravṛtti hetu tvāt dṛṣṭā hi avidyātaḥ api vidyā prāptiḥ yathā lipi akṣarebhyaḥ varṇa pratītiḥ varṇa pratipādaka rekhā ādayaḥ api sva rūpeṇa satyāḥ satyam satyāḥ na tu te sva rūpeṇa pratipādakāḥ kakāra ādi rūpa adhyāropeṇa pratipādakāḥ tat eṣām kāryaḥ payogi rūpam asatyam eva iti pūrvakṣa saṃkṣepaḥ 
NK_133.1^1	 yat tāvat uktam grāhya lakṣaṇa ayogāt iti na tad artha abhāva sādhanam asāmarthyāt grāhya lakṣaṇa abhāve hi arthaḥ grāhyaḥ na bhavet na tu tasya asadbhāvaḥ grahaṇa abhāvasya piśāca ādi vat sva rūpa viprakarṣeṇa api upapateḥ grahaṇa yogya tve satya grahaṇāt abhāva siddhiḥ iti ced katham punar asya yogyatā saṃpradhāritā na hi tasya grahaṇam kvacid avagatam avagatam ced na grāhya lakṣaṇa ayogaḥ kiñca grāhaka adhīnam grahaṇam grāhakam ca jñānam sva ātma mātra niyatam iti etāvatā eva tad anyasya agrāhyatā grāhya abhāvāt eva ca idam agrahaṇam iti sādhya aviśiṣṭam api ca idam bhavān pṛṣṭaḥ vyācaṣṭā kā jñāna ākārasya grāhyatā na hi tasya asti jñāna hetu tvam tat avyatirekāt 
NK_133.1^2	 na api ākāra ādhāyaka tvam ākāra dvayān anubhavāt na ca jñāna ātma tvam eva grāhya tvam suṣupta avasthāyām jñāna ātma vat anubhūtasya avaśyam jñāna santāna vat anuvartamānasya api grahaṇa abhāvāt avabhāsamāna tvam eva tasya grāhya tvam iti ced kaḥ ayam ākārasya avabhāsaḥ jñāna pratibaddha hāna ādi vyavahāra yogya tā āpattiḥ ced bāhyasya api sā eva yogya tā tathā hinīlam pītam etat iti saṃvidānāḥ bāhyam eva upādadate jahati upekṣante vā na antaram ākāram iti asiddhaḥ grāhya lakṣaṇa ayogaḥ katham anyasya utpattyā anyasya vyavahāra yogya tā iti ced tasya sva kāraṇa sāmagrī niyamena tad viṣaya vyavahāra anuguṇa svabhāvasya utpādanāt iti yat kiñcid etat 
NK_134.1^1	 etena vedya tvam api pratyuktam bhede api jñānasya sva kāraṇa niyamāt eva tasya upapatteḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt yat api jaḍasya prakāśa ayogaḥ iti tat api prakāśa ātmaka tva abhāva abhiprāyeṇa siddha sādhanam saṃsarga abhiprapyeṇa nirupapattikam na hi jaḍasya prakāśa saṃsargeṇa na bhavitavyam iti asti rājā ājñā yathā chidi kriyā chedyena sambadhyate bhidyate ca tathā jñāna kriyā api jñeyena saha saṃbhantsyate bhetsyate ca sahopala niyamasya api vipakṣāt vyāvṛttiḥ sandigdhā jñānasya sva pata saṃvedana tā mātreṇa eva nīla tad dhiyoḥ yugapad grahaṇa niyamasya upapatteḥ bāhya abhāvāt jñānam parasya saṃvedakam na bhavati iti ced bāhya abhāva siddhau hetiḥ vipakṣāt vyāvṛtti siddhiḥ tad siddhau ca asya vipakṣa abhāvam prati hetu tvam iti anyonya pekṣitā 
NK_134.1^2	 anyatas bāhya abhāva siddhau= asya hetu tvam iti ced tat eva astu kim anena asiddhaḥ ca saha upalambha niyamaḥ nīlam etat iti bahirmukha tayā arthe anubhūyamāne tadānīm eva antarasya tad anubhavasya anubhavāt jñāsya sva saṃvedanatā siddhau saha upalambha niyama siddhiḥ iti ced sva saṃvedana siddhau kim pramāṇam yat prakāśakam tad sva prakāśe para anapekṣam yathā pradīpaḥ iti ced pradīpasya tad deśa varti tama upanayane vyāpāraḥ sa ca anena svayam eva kṛtaḥ iti tad artham pradīpa antaram na apekṣate vaiyarthyāt sva pratītau tu cakṣuḥ ādikam apekṣate eva iti sādhya vikalatā dṛṣṭāntasya atha prakāśaka tvam jñāna tvam abhipretam tasmāt para anapekṣā tadānīmasādhāraṇaḥ hetuḥ 
NK_134.2^1	 yat ca uktam yasya avyaktaḥ prakāśaḥ tat svayam avyaktam tathā pihitam vastu iti tatra api pihitasya avyakta tā aprakāśaḥ tad svayam avyakta tvāt kintu a bhāvāt eva iti vyāpti asiddhiḥ yat ca pratyaya tvāt iti tat api adhānam dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ svapna ādi pratyayāḥ api samāropita bāhya ālambanā na sva ātma mātra paryavasāyinaḥ jāgrat avastha upayuktānām eva arthānām saṃskāra vaśena tathā pratibhāsanāt anyathā dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu artheṣu tad utpatti niyama ayogāt kiñca yadi bāhyam na asti kim idānīm niyata ākāram pratīyate nīlam etat iti vijñāna ālāraḥ ayam iti ced na vijñānāt vahiḥ bhūtasya saṃvedanāt 
NK_134.2^2–134.3	 jñāna ākāra tve tu aham nīlam iti pratītiḥ syāt na tu idam nīlam iti jñānānām pratyekam ākāra bhedāt kasyacid aham iti pratībhāsaḥ kasyacid idam nīlam etat iti ced na nīladyākāra vat aham iti ākātasya vyavasthita tva abhāvāt tathā ca yat ekena aham iti pratīyate tad apareṇa tvam iti pratīyate svayam svasya saṃvedane aham iti pratibhāsate iti ced kim vai parasya api saṃvedanam asti svarūpasya api bhrāntyā bheda pratītiḥ iti ced pratyakṣeṇa pratītaḥ bhedaḥ vāstavaḥ na kasmāt bhrāntam pratyakṣam iti ced yathā uktam pariccheda antaram yaḥ ayam bhāgaḥ bahis avasthitaḥ jñānasya abhedinaḥ bheda pratibhāsaḥ hi upaplavaḥ iti 
NK_134.4^1	 kutas etat anumānena abheda prasādhanāt iti ced pratyakṣasya bhrānta tvena ābādhita viṣaya tvāt anumānasya ātma lābhaḥ labdha ātmake ca anumāne pratyakṣasya bhrānta tvam iti anyonya apekṣitā doṣaḥ astu vā bheda viplavaḥ niyata deśa adhikaraṇa pratītiḥ kutas na hi tatra ayam āropayitavyaḥ na anyatra iti asti prati niyama hetuḥ vāsanā niyamāt āropite niyamaḥ iti ced na tasyāḥ api tad deśa niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt sati hi artha sambhave yat deśaḥ arthaḥ tad deśa anubhavaḥ tad deśā ca tad pūrvikā vāsanā bāhya abhāve tu tasyāḥ kiṃkṛtaḥ deśa niyamaḥ asti tāvat ārope niyamaḥ na ca kāraṇa viśeṣam antareṇa kārya viśeṣaḥ ghaṭate bāhyaḥ ca arthaḥ na asti tena vāsanānām eva vaicitryam tad vaicitryasya arthavat tad kāraṇānām vaicitryāt iti anādiḥ iti ced 
NK_134.4^2	 vāsanā vaicitryam yadi bodha ākārāt ananyat kaḥ tāsām parasparataḥ viśeṣaḥ atha anyat arthe kaḥ pradveṣaḥ yena sarva loka pratītiḥ apahnūyate kena ca ayam ākāraḥ bahis āropyate jñānena iti ced kim tasya sva ātmani ākāra saṃvittiḥ eva bahis āra upasradanyaḥ vā ādye kalpe sā eva tasya samyak pratītiḥ sā eva ca mithyā iti āpatitam jñāna gata tvena ākāra grahaṇasya satya tvāt bāhya tā saṃvitteḥ ca ayathārtha tvāt anya tve ca tayoḥ na krameṇa bhāvaḥ tad kāraṇasya jñānasya kṣaṇika tvāt na ca ekasya yugapad satya tvena mithyā arvena ca pratīti sambhavaḥ na ca krama yaugadyābhyām anyaḥ prakāraḥ asti yatra vartamānam jñānam sva ātmani ākāram gṛhṇīyāt bahis ca tam āropayet 
NK_134.5–134.7	 api ca yadi jñāna ākāraḥ nīlādiḥ arthaḥ yasya eva ayam ākāraḥ saḥ eva tam pratīyāt na puruṣa antaram pratīyāt pratīyate ca ayam bahubhiḥ ekaḥ sarveṣām tad ābhimukhyena yugapad pravṛtteḥ yaḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ sa mayā api iti pratisamdhānāt tasmāt arthaḥ ayam na jñāna kāraḥ ye tu jñāna ākāram api apahnavānāḥ alīkāḥ eva nīla ādayaḥ pratibhāsante iti āhuḥ teṣām kāraṇa niyamāt utpatti niyamaḥ artha kriyā niyamaḥ ca na prāpnoti artha abhāvena kiñcat kasyacid kāraṇam sarvam vā sarvasya na artha kriyā saṃvādaḥ na vā visaṃvādaḥ iti viśeṣa abhāvāt yathā uktam gurubhiḥ āśāmodaka tṛptāḥ ye ye ca upārjita modakāḥ rasa vīrya vipāka ādi teṣām tulyam prasajyate iti 
NK_134.8	 vāsanā viśeṣāt tad viśeṣa siddhiḥ iti ced sā yadi bāhya artha kriyā aśeṣa hetuḥ saṃjjā bheda mātram arthaḥ vā āsanā iti atha jjāna ātmikā artha abhāve hi tasyāḥ viśeṣaḥ nirnibandhanaḥ bodha mātrasya upādānasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt bodha ākāra avyatiriktasya ca viśeṣasya abhyupagame artha sadbhāva abhyupagama prasaṅgāt iti uktam na ca asmin pakṣe nīla ādi pratyayasya kādācid ka tvam syāt tad janana samartha kṣaṇa santānasya sarvadā anuvṛtteḥ ananuvṛttau vā kāla antara api tatra tratyayā anupapattiḥ sva vyatiriktasya ācāpekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt kāraṇa paripākasya kādācid ka tvāt tad kāryasya kādācid ka tvam iti ced kāraṇasya paripākaḥ kārya jananam pratyābhimukhyam saḥ api sva saṃvedana mātra adhīnaḥ na kādācid kaḥ bhavitum arhati asti ca ayam kādācid kaḥ pratyakṣa pratibhāsaḥ saḥ eva pratīti viṣayam deśa kāla kāraṇa svabhāva niyatam bāhyam vastu vyavasthāpayan= tad abhāva sādhanam bādhate iti kāla atyayāt iṣṭa tvam api hetūnām iti uparamyata samadhigatā saṃkhyā 
NK_135.1–135.2	 parimāṇam māna vyavahāra kāraṇam tat caturvidham aṇu mahat dīrgham hrasvam ca iti tatra mahat dvividham nityam anityam ca nityam ākāśa kāla gātmasu parama mahat tvam anityam tri aṇuka ādau eva samprati parimāṇa nirūpaṇa artham āha parimāṇam māna vyavahāra kāraṇam iti māna vyavahāraḥ ṇu mahat dīrgham hrasvam ityādi jñānam śabdaḥ ca tasya kāraṇam parimāṇam iti anena pratyakṣa siddhasi api parimāṇasya vipratipannam prati kāryeṇa sattām darśayati yathā tāvat jñānasya jñeya prasādhaka tvam tathā uktam 
NK_135.3–135.4	 śabdasya tu katham na haysau= artha ātmā anna agni asi śabda uccāraṇe mukhasya pūraṇa dāha pāṭana prasaṅgāt na api artha jaḥ kauṣṭhya vāyu kaṇṭha ādi abhighāta ja tvāt atada ātmanaḥ atad utpannasya pratipādaka tve ati prasaṅgāt atra ucyate yadi kaṇṭha ādi abhighāta mātrajaḥ eva śabdaḥ na vaktuḥ vivakṣām api pratipādayet tad utpatti abhāvāt tathā ca vaktuḥ vivakṣām api na sūcayeyuḥ śabdāḥ iti pramatta gītam syāt pāramparyeṇa vivakṣā pūvaka tvāt śabdasya vivakṣā pratipādaka tvam iti ced evam artha anubhava pratipādaka tvam api vivakṣāyāḥ artha abhava pūrvaka tvāt asati api artha anubhave vipralambhakasya tad artha vivakṣā pratītiḥ iti ced asatyām api tad artha vivakṣāyām bhrāntasya tad artha viṣayam vākyam upalabdham tathā āhuḥ ācāryāḥ bhrāntasya anya vivakṣāyām anyat vākyam hi dṛśyate iti 
NK_135.5	 na anya vivakṣātaḥ anya abhidhānasya sambhavaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām yadi asya kāraṇam avagatam tasya tat vyabhicāre viśvasya ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt atas bhrāntasya apratīyamānā api tad artha vivakṣā sahasā upajātā gacchat tṛṇa saṃsparśa jñām a vada spaṣṭa rūpā kāryeṇa kalpanīyā iti ced vipralambhakasya api vivakṣā viśeṣaṇa tad artha anubhavaḥ kalpyatām asaṃvidite arthe tad viṣayasya vivakṣa viśeṣasya ayogāt tadānīm vipralambhakasya tad artha anubhavaḥ na asti iti ced mā sma bhūt smaraṇam tāvat vidyate vipralambhakaḥ hi pūrva anutam eva artham anyathābhūtam anyathā kathayati tatra asya tad artha vivakṣā sākṣāt smaraṇa kāraṇikā bhavantī pāramparyeṇa tad anubhava kāraṇikā iti na asti vyabhicāraḥ mithyā anubhava pūtvikāyāḥ api vivakṣāyāḥ pārampararyeṇa satya anubhava pūrvaka tvāt anubhavaḥ ca artha avyabhicāri iti śabdāt artha siddhiḥ anyathā vākya śrutau śrotuḥ artha pratīti abhāvāt vivakṣā mātra pratīteḥ ca apuruṣa artha tvāt śābadaḥ vyavahāraḥ ucchidyeta vādi prativādinoḥ ca jaya parājaya vyavasthā anupapattiḥ vivakṣā mātram pratyubhayoḥ api bhūta artha vādi tvāt 
NK_135.6–135.7^1	 yat ca uktam dravyāt avyatiriktam parimāṇam dravya agrahe tad buddhi abhāvāt iti tat asiddham dūrāt dravya grahaṇe api tad parimāṇa viśeṣasya agrahaṇāt atas eva mahān api aṇuḥ iva bhrāntyā dṛśyate evam vyavasthite parimāṇe tasya bhedam kathayati tat caturvidham iti yana rūpeṇa cāturvidhyam tat darśayati aṇu mahat dīrgham hrasvam ca iti caturasta ādikam tu avayavānām saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ na parimāṇa antaram dīrgha tva ādayaḥ api tathā bhavantu na avayava saṃsthāna anupalambhe api dūrāt dīrgha ādi pratyayasya darśanāt api ca bhoḥ ! dvi aṇuka parimānām tāvat aṇu mahat parimāṇa utpattau kāraṇa abhāvāt 
NK_135.6–135.7^2	 tasmāt ca paramāt ca para māṇu parimāṇam apakṛṣtam kārya parimāṇāt kāraṇa parimāṇasya hīna tva darśanāt tatas ca paramāṇoḥ parimāṇam dvi aṇuka parimāṇāt bhinnam evam ghaṭa ādīnām parimāṇāt anyat eva prakarṣa paryanta prāptam ākāśa ādi parimāṇam tathā dīrgham hrasvam ca iti parimāṇam aṣṭavidham eva kutas ca aturvidhyam iti āha tatra iti teṣu caturvidheṣu parimāṇeṣu madhye mahat dvividham nityam anityam ca iti keṣu nityam iti āśaṅkya āha nityam ākāśa kāla diś ātmasu tat ca parama mahat tvam iti ucyate anityam mahat parimāṇam tri aṇuka ādau= eva na ākāśa ādiṣu iti arthaḥ 
NK_136.1–136.2	 tathā ca aṇu api dvividham nityam anityam ca nityam paramāṇu manassu tat pārimāṇḍalyam anityam dvi aṇukaḥ eva kuvala āmalaka bilva ādiṣu mahatsu api tad prakarṣa bhāva abhāvam apekṣya bhāktaḥ aṇu vyavahāraḥ dīrgha tva hrasva tve ca utpādya mahat aṇutva eka artha samavete samidh ikṣu vaṃśa ādiṣu añjasā dīrgheṣu api tad prakarṣa bhāva abhāvam apekṣya bhāktaḥ hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ 
NK_136.3–136.5	 anityam caturvidham api saṃkhyā parimāṇa pracaya yoni tatra īśvara buddhim apekṣya utpannā paramāṇu dvi aṇukeṣu bahu tva saṃkhyā taiḥ ārabdhe kārya dravye tri aṇuka ādi lakṣaṇe rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam mahat tvam dīrgha tvam ca karoti dvi bahubhiḥ mahadbhiḥ ca ārabdhe kārya dravye kāraṇa mahat tvāni eva mahat tvam ārabhante na bahu tvam samāna saṃkhyaiḥ ca ārabdhe atiśaya darśanāt 
NK_136.6	 yathā mahat dvvidham tathā aṇu api dvividham nityam anityam ca ubhayatra api cakāraḥ prakāra antara vyavaccheda arthaḥ nityam aṇu parimāṇam paramāṇaumanaḥsu utpatti vināśa kāraṇa abhāvāt pārimāṇaṇḍalyam iti sarva apakṛṣṭam parimāṇam anityam aṇu parimāṇam dvi aṇukaḥ eva na anyatra ityarthaḥ etena etat uktam bhavati aṇu parimāṇa prabhedaḥ eva paramāṇu parimāṇam mahat parimāṇa prabhedaḥ ca parama mahat parimāṇam anyathā parama śabdena viśeṣaṇa ayogāt yat khalu parimāṇam rūpa sahāyam svākśrayam pratyakṣayati tatra mahat iti vyapadeśaḥ yat ca no pratyakṣayati tatra aṇu iti vyavahāraḥ na ca evam sati tri aṇukasya api aṇu tva prasaktiḥ tasya api pratyakṣa tvāt tri aṇukam asmad ādi pratyakṣam bahubhiḥ samavāyi kāraṇaiḥ ārabdha tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat yasya ca pratyakṣasya dravyasya avayavāḥ na pratyakṣāḥ tat eva tri aṇukam ākāśa parimāṇasya tu pratyakṣa hetu tva abhāve api mahat tvam eva tad āśrayasya dvi aṇuka vyāptitaḥ adhika vyāptika tvāt ghaṭa aparimāṇa vat 
NK_136.7	 anityam aṇu parimāṇam dvi aṇukam eva iti ayuktam kuvala āmalaka bilva ādiṣu paraspara apekṣayā aṇu vyavahāra darśanāt atas āha kuvala āmalaka bilva ādiṣu iti bilve yaḥ prakarṣa bhāvaḥ mahat parimāṇa atiśaya yogi tvam tasya āmalake abhāvam apekṣya aṇu vyavahāraḥ bhāktaḥ ubhābhyām bhajyate iti bhaktiḥ sādṛśyam tasya ayam iti bhāktaḥ sādṛśya mātra nibandhanaḥ gauṇaḥ iti arthaḥ evam āmalaka parimāṇa atiśaya abhāvam kuvale apekṣya aṇu vyavahāraḥ yatra hi mikhyam aṇu tvam dvi aṇuke tatra mahat parimāṇasya abhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ āmalake api yādṛśam bilve mahat parimāṇam tādṛśam na asti iti etāvatā sādharmyeṇa upacāra pravṛttiḥ 
NK_136.8	 dīrgha tva hrasva tvayoḥ viṣayam darśayati dīrgha tva hrasva tve ca iti mahatvam ca aṇu tvam ca mahat aṇu tve utpādye ca te mahat aṇu tve ca iti utpādya mahat aṇu tve rābhyām ekasmin= arthe samavete dīrgha hrasva tve yatra utpādyam mahat tvam tri aṇuka ādau tatra utpādyam dīrgha tvam yatra ca utpādyam aṇu tvam dvi aṇuke tatra utpādyam hrasva tvam iti arthaḥ tatra paramāṇoḥ parimaṇḍala tvāt hrasva tva abhāvaḥ vyāpāka tvāt ca ākāśasya dīrgha tva abhāvaḥ iti eke anye tu paramāṇu parama mahat vyavahāra vat parama hrasva parama dīrgha vyavahārasya api loke darśanāt paramāṇuṣu parama hrasva tvam parama dīrgha tvam ca ākāśe iti āhuḥ dirgha parimāṇa adhikaraṇam ākāśam mahat parimāṇa āśraya tvāt stambha ādi vat evam hrasva parimāṇa āśrayaḥ paramāṇuḥ aṇu parimāṇa āśraya tvāt dvi aṇuka vat 
NK_136.9	 yadi hrasva tvam utpādyena aṇu tvena eka artha samavetam katham anyatra hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ tatra āha samidh ikṣu vaṃśa ādiṣu iti samit ca ikṣuḥ ca vaṃśāḥ ca samidh ikṣu vaṃśāḥ eteṣu añjasā paramārthataḥ dīrgheṣu api vaṃśe yaḥ parimāṇa prakarṣa bhāvaḥ dīrgha atiśaya yogi tvam tasya abhāvam ikṣau= apekṣya pratītya bhāktaḥ gauṇaḥ vyavahāraḥ evam ikṣoḥ prakarṣa bhāvaḥ tasya abhāvam samidhi apekṣya hrasva vyavahāraḥ yat khalu paramārthataḥ hrasvam dvi aṇukam tatra dairghya abhāvaḥ ikṣau= api vaṃśasya yādṛśam dairghyam tādṛśam na asti iti upacāraḥ nanu eteṣu vāstavaḥ eva hrasva tva vyavahāraḥ kim na iṣyate na iṣyate teṣu eva para apekṣayā dīrgha vyavahāra darśanāt na ca ekasya dīrgha tvam hrasva tvam ca ubhayam api vāstavam yuktam virodhāt atha kasmāt dīrgha vyavahāraḥ eva gauṇaḥ na bhavati na tasya utpatti kāraṇa sambhavāt sarvatra eva bhāktaḥ hrasva vyavahāraḥ bhavatu na evam mukhya bhāve gauṇasya asambhavāt 
NK_136.10^1	 atha idānīm utpādyasya parimāṇasya kāraṇa nirūpaṇa artham āha anityam caturvidham api iti anityam caturnidham api dīrgham mahat aṇu ca iti caturvidham parimāṇam saṃkhyā parimāṇa pracaya yoni saṃkhyā parimāṇa pracaya kāraṇakam saṃkhyāyāḥ tāvat kāraṇa tvam āha tatra iti paramāṇubhyām ārabdham dvi aṇukam paramāṇu dvi aṇukam iti ucyate teṣu triṣu ekaika guṇa ālambanāmīśvara buddhim apekṣya utpannā yā tritva saṃkhyā sā taiḥ tribhiḥ dvi aṇukaiḥ ārabdhe kārya dravye tri aṇuka lakṣaṇe rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam eva mahat tvam dīrgha tvam ca karoti tatra iti padam mahat parimāṇa kāraṇa nitddhāraṇa artham tri aṇuka ādi ityādi padam caturaṇuka ādi parigraha artham katham punar eṣa niścayaḥ tri aṇuka ādi parimāṇasyat vyaṇuka gatāḥ bahu tva saṃkhyā eva asamavāyi kāraṇam iti anyasya asambhavāt na tāvat dvi aṇuka vṛttyaḥ rūpa rasa gandha sparśa eka tva eka pṛthaktva guru tva drava tva snehāḥ tasya asamavāyi kāraṇam teṣām kāraṇa vṛttīnām kārye guṇam ārabhamāṇānām samāna jātīya guṇa antara ārambhe eva sāmarthya darśanāt 
NK_136.10^2	 dvi aṇu kāṇu parimāṇānām ca ārambhaka tve tri aṇukasya aṇu tvam eva syāt na mahat tvam parimāṇāt samāna jātīyasya eva parimāṇasya utpatti avagamāt asti ca atra mahat tvam bhūyas avayava ārabdha tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat na ca asamavāyi kāraṇam vinā kāryam utpadyate dṛṣṭaḥ ca anyatra avayava saṃkhyā bāhulyāt samāna parimāṇa ārabdhayoḥ kāryayoḥ ekatra mahattva atiśayaḥ tena atra saṃkhyāyāḥ eva kāraṇa tvam kalpyate dvi aṇuka saṃyogābhyām tri aṇuke mahat tva utpattiḥ iti ced na saṃyogasya mahat tva ārambhaka tve dvi aṇuke api mahat tva upapattiḥ syāt yadi tu bhūyasām avayavānām saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam iti ucyate prāpta aprāpta vivekāt avayavānām bhūyaḥ tvam eva kāraṇam samarthitam syāt īśvara buddhi apekṣasya tritvasya sthiti hetu adṛṣṭa kṣaya ādi nāśaḥ na tu kadācid āśraya vināśāt api vināśaḥ na tu apekṣā buddhi vināśāt vināśaḥ īśvara buddheḥ nitya tvāt 
NK_136.11^1	 samprati mahat tvāt mahat tva utpattim āha dvi bahubhiḥ madbhiḥ iti dvau ca bahuvaḥ ca dvi bahuvaḥ taiḥ ārabdhe kārya dravye kāraṇa mahat tvāni eva mahat tvam ārabhante yatra dvābhyām mahadbhyām apracitābhyām ārabhyate dravyam tatra avayava mahat tvābhyām eva mahattvasya utpādaḥ bahu tva saṃkhyā pracayayoḥ abhāvāt yatra ca bahubhiḥ mahadbhiḥ ava yavaiḥ kāryam ārabhyate tatra avayava mahat tvebhyaḥ avayavini mahat tvasya utpādaḥ na bahu tva saṃkhyāyāḥ samāna saṃkhyaiḥ sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ ca ārabdhayoḥ dravyayoḥ sthūla ārabdhe mahattva atiśaya darśanāt 
NK_136.11^2	 saṃkhyāyāḥ kāraṇa tve hi kārya viśeṣaḥ na syāt tasyāḥ aviśeṣāt yatra tu samāna parimāṇaiḥ avayavaiḥ ārabdhayoḥ avayava saṃkhyā bāhulyāt ekatra parimāṇa atiśayaḥ dṛśyate tatra avayava saṃkhyā api kāraṇam eṣṭavyāḥ anyathā kārya viśeṣa ayogaḥ yatra samāna sākhyaiḥ samāna parimāṇaiḥ ca kāryam ārabdham tatra mahat tva utpattau= ubhayoḥ api kāraṇa tvam pratyekam ubhayoḥ api sāmarthya darśanāt tatra anyatara viśeṣa adarśanāt iti eke apare tu parimāṇa tām āhuḥ samāna jātīyāt kārya utpatti sambhave vijātīya kāraṇa kalpa nāna vakāśāt 
NK_137.1–137.2^1	 pracayasya tūla piṇḍayoḥ vartamānaḥ piṇḍa ārambhaka avayava praśithila saṃyoga anapekṣamāṇa itaretara piṇḍa avayava saṃyoga apekṣaḥ vā dvi tūlake mahat tvam ārabhate na bahu tva mahat tvāni samāna saṃkhyā pala parimāṇaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya darśanāt pracayasya kāraṇa tvam āha pracayaḥ ca iti pracayaḥ iti dyavya ārambhakaḥ praśithilaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ sa tu dvi tūla kavyārambhakayoḥ tūṇḍayoḥ vartamānaḥ pratyekam piṇḍayoḥ ārambhakāt praśithila an avayava saṃyoga anapekṣamāṇa itaretara piṇḍayoḥ avayavānām paraspara saṃyoga anapekṣamāṇaḥ vā dvi tūlake mahat tvām ārabhate 
NK_137.1–137.2^2	 yatra piṇḍayoḥ saṃyogaḥ svayam praśithilaḥ tayoḥ ārambhakāḥ ca avayava saṃyogogāḥ api praśithilāḥ tatra piṇḍābhyām ātabdhe dravye nibiḍa avayava saṃyoga ārabdha piṇḍa dvaya nibiḍa saṃyoga janita dravya pekṣayā mahattva atiśaya darśanāt piṇḍayoḥ praśithilaḥ saṃyogaḥ piṇḍa ārambhaka praśithila saṃyoga apekṣaḥ mahattvasya kāraṇam yatra tu piṇḍayoḥ saṃyogaḥ praśithilaḥ itaretara piṇḍa avayavānām itaretara avayavaiḥ saṃyogāḥ api praśithilāḥ piṇḍayoḥ ārambhakāḥ ca na praśithilāḥ tatra piṇḍābhyām ārabdhe dravye atyanta nibiḍa paraspara avayava saṃyoga piṇḍa dvaya ārabdha dravya apekṣayā mahattva atiśaya darśanāt piṇḍayoḥ praśithilaḥ saṃyogaḥ itaretara piṇḍa avayava saṃyoga apekṣaḥ mahattvasya kāraṇam iti vivekaḥ 
NK_137.3^1	 atha katham tatra bahu tva mahat tvayoḥ eva kpta sāmarthyayoḥ kāraṃatvam na iṣyate tatra āha na bahu tva mahat tvāni iti bahu tva mahat tvāni iti viṣya bheda apekṣayā bahuvacanam yatra yatra pravaya viśeṣāt parimāṇa viśeṣa pratītiḥ asti na tatra tatra bahu tvam mahat tvam ca kāraṇam iti arthaḥ atra ttiḥ samāna saṃkhyā pala parimāṇaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya darśanāt saṃkhyā ca palam ca parimāṇam ca saṃkhyā pala parimāṇāni samānāni saṃkhyā pala parimāṇāni yeṣām taiḥ ārabdhe kārye atiśaya darśanāt yadi hi saṃkhyā eva kāraṇam samāna saṃkhyaiḥ tribhiḥ caturbhiḥ vā praśithila saṃyogaiḥ nibiḍa saṃyogaiḥ ca ārabdhayoḥ dravyayoḥ praśithila saṃyoga ārabdhe nibiḍa saṃyoga ārabdha apekṣayā mahattva atiśayaḥ na syāt kāraṇa saṃkhyāyāḥ ubhayatra api tulya tvāt 
NK_137.3^2	 tathā yadi mahat tvam api kāraṇam samāna mahat tvaiḥ pracitaiḥ apracitaiḥ ca ārabdhayoḥ dravyayoḥ apracita ārabdha apekṣayā pracita ārabdhe parimāṇa atiśayaḥ na bhavet asti ca viśeṣaḥ tena evam tarkayāmaḥ na saṃkhyā kāraṇam na api mahat tvam iti yatra tu apracitaiḥ aṇubhiḥ mahadbhiḥ ca pracitaiḥ ārabdhayoḥ dravyayoḥ pracitaiḥ mahadbhiḥ ārabdhe mahattva atiśaya darśanam tatra mahattva pracayayoḥ kāraṇa tvam yatra pracitaiḥ samāna parimāṇaiḥ bahutara saṃkhyākaiḥ apracitaiḥ caḥ ca alpa saṃkhyākaiḥ rabdhayoḥ vyayoḥ bahutara saṃkhyākaiḥ pracitaiḥ ārabdhe atiśaya darśanam tatra saṃkhyā pracayayoḥ kāraṇa tvam yatra apracitaiḥ aṇubhiḥ alpa saṃkhyaiḥ ārabdhāt pracita bahutara sthūla ārabdhe viśeṣa darśanam tatra trayāṇām eva boddhavyam yaḥ tu manyate tulya parimeyeṣu dravyeṣu dravyeṣu kāraṇa gatāni palāni parimāṇa utpattau kāraṇam na mahat parimāṇāni tad mate palasya kāraṇa tvam abhyupagamya pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ sva mate tu palasya akāraṇa tvāt 
NK_138.1–138.3	 dvi tva saṃkhyā ca aṇvoḥ vartamānāḥ dvi aṇuke aṇu tvam ārabhate mahat tva vat tri aṇuka ādau kāraṇa bahu tva mahatva samāna jātīya pracayebhyaḥ dīrgha tvasya utpattiḥ aṇu tva vat dvi aṇuke dvi tva saṃkhyātaḥ hrasva tvasya utpattiḥ atha tri aṇuka ādiṣu varttamānayoḥ mahatva dīrgha tvayoḥ parasparataḥ kaḥ viśeṣaḥ dvi aṇukeṣu ca aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ iti tatra asti mahat tva dīrgha tvayoḥ parasparataḥ viśeṣaḥ mahatsu dīrgham ānīyatām dīrgheṣu ca mahat ānīyatām iti viśiṣṭa vyavahāra darśanāt iti aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ tu parasparataḥ viśeṣaḥ tad darśinām pratyakṣaḥ iti etat caturvidham api parimāṇam utpādyam āśravi nāśāt eva vinaśyati iti 
NK_138.4	 dvi tva saṃkhyā ca aṇvoḥ vartamānāḥ dvi aṇuke aṇu tvam ārabhate yaḥ tu paramāṇu parimāṇābhyām eva dvi aṇuke parimāṇa utpattim iccati tam prati dvi aṇukasya api aṇutama tva prasaktiḥ iti pūrvikā eva yuktiḥ āvartanīyāḥ adhikam ca etat yat nitya dravya parimāṇasya anārambhaka tvam paramāṇu parimāṇam na kasyacid ārambhakam nitya dravya parimāṇa tvāt ākāśa ādi parimāṇa vat paramāṇu parimāṇa tvāt vā manaḥ parimāṇa vat 
NK_138.5	 dīrgha tvasya utpattim āha mahat tva vat iti yathā mahattvasya kāraṇa bahu tvāt samāna jātīyāt kāraṇa mahat tvāt pracayāt ca utpattiḥ evam dīrgha tvasya api kāraṇa bahu tvāt pracaya utpattiḥ iti sarvam asya mahat tvena saha tulyam dvi aṇuke hrasva tvasya api dvi tva saṃkhyā eva asamavāyikāraṇam iti āha aṇu tva vat iti katham ekasmāt kāraṇāt kārya bhedaḥ adṛṣṭa viśeṣasya sahakāriṇaḥ bhedāt mahat tva viśeṣaḥ eva dīrgha tvam aṇu tva viśeṣaḥ eva hrasva tvam iti manyamānaḥ āha atha iti samādhatte tatra asti iti yadi dīrgha mahat tvayoḥ abhedaḥ dīrgheṣu mahat ānīyatām iti nirdhāraṇam na syāt abhedāt na hi bhavati rūpavatsu rūpavat ānīyatām iti asti ca idam nirdhāraṇam tena dīrgha tva mahat tvayoḥ bhedaḥ kalpyate parimāṇasya vyāpya vṛtti tvāt ekasmin dravye parimāṇa dvaya anupapattiḥ iti ced na vijātīyayoḥ ekatra vṛtti avirodhāt avāntara jāti bhede api nīla rītayoḥ ekatra samāveśaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ iti ced yayoḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ tayoḥ mā bhūt dīrgha tva mahat tvayoḥ tu sahabhāvaḥ sarva loka pratoti siddha tvāt aśakyatiḥ ākaraṇaḥ 
NK_138.6	 dvi aṇuka vartinoḥ aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ tu bhedaḥ yoginām pratyakṣaḥ iti āha aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ tu iti asmad ādīnām tu bhāktayoḥ aṇu tva hrasva tvayoḥ bhede na tad mukhyayoḥ api bheda anumānam etat caturvidham api parimāṇam āśraya vināśāt eva vinaśyati na anyasmāt iti niyamaḥ utpādya grahaṇena paramāṇu parama hrasva parama mahat parama dīrgha vyavacchedaḥ aṇu tva mahat tvayoḥ dīrgha tva hrasva tvayoḥ ca paraspara pekṣā kṛta tvam na tu svābhāvika tvam iti ced tatra kevala avasthāyām hasta vitasti ādi parimitasya parimāṇasya sa apekṣā avasthāyām api bheda anupalabdheḥ ubhaya abhāva prasaṅgāt ca kim artham tarhi apekṣā pratyekam āśraya grahaṇe gṛhītayoḥ eva parimāṇayoḥ prakarṣa bhāva abhāva prati iti arthāḥ yayoḥ adhigamāt idam asmāt dīrghamdam hrasvam iti vyavahāraḥ syāt 
NK_139.1–139.5	 pṛthaktu apa uddhāra vyavahāra kāraṇam tat punar eka dravyam aneka dravyam ca tasya tu nitya tva anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ saṃkhyayā vyākhyātāḥ etāvān tu viśeṣaḥ eka tva ādi vat eka pṛthaktva ādi a para sāmānya abhāvaḥ saṃkhyayā tu viśeṣyate tad viśiṣṭa vyavahāra darśanāt iti pṛthaktvam apoddhāra vyavahāra kāraṇam apa uddhāra vyavahāraḥ idam asmāt pṛthak iti jñānam vyapadeśaḥ ca tasya kāraṇam pṛthaktvam iti vyākhyānam pūrvavat itaretara abhāva nimittaḥ ayam vyavahāraḥ iti ced na pratiṣedhasya vidhi pratyaya viṣaya tva ayogāt tat punar eka dravyam aneka dravyam ca ekam dravyam āśrayaḥ yasya tat eka dravyam anekam dravyam āśrayaḥ yasya tad aneka dravyam punar śabdaḥ eka dravya vṛtteḥ parimāṇāt pṛthaktu asya eka aneka dravya vṛtti tva viśeṣa avat yotana arthaḥ parimāṇam eka dravyam eva pṛthaktvam punar eka dravyam aneka dravyam ca iti viśeṣaḥ 
NK_139.6	 tasya tu nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ saṃkhyayā vyākhyātāḥ tasya dvividhasya api pṛthaktvasya nitya tvam ca anitya tvam ca niṣpattiḥ ca saṃkhyayā vyākhyātāḥ yathā eka dravya eka tva saṃkhyā paramāṇuṣu nityā kārye kāraṇa guṇa pūrvikā āśraya vināśāt ca naśyati tathā eka dravyam eka pṛthaktvam yathā aneka dravyavya dvi tva ādikā saṃkhyā aneka guṇa ālambanāyāḥ apekṣā buddheḥ utpadyate tad vināśāt ca vinaśyati kvacid ca āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati tathā aneka dravya dvi pṛthaktva ādikam api iti atideśa arthaḥ nityam ca anityam ca nitya anitye tayoḥ bhāvaḥ nitya anitya tvam iti dvandvāt param śravaṇāt tu apratyayasya pratyekam abhisambandhaḥ atra api vākye tuśadaḥ viśeṣa avat yotana arthaḥ tasya nitya tva ādayaḥ saṃkhyayā vyākhyātāḥ na parimāṇasya iti arthaḥ 
NK_139.7^1	 evam saṃkhyā saha pṛthaktvasya sādharmyam pratipādya vaidharmyam pratipādayati etāvān= tu iti saṃkhyāyāḥ sakāśāt pṛthaktvasya etāvān bhedaḥ yathā saṃkhyā tu a para sāmānya apekṣayā eka tva dvi tva ādikam apara sāmānyam asti tathā pṛthaktva para sāmānya apekṣayā eka pṛthaktva t vi tvā ādikam apara sāmānyam na asti iti katham tarhi anekeṣu eka pṛthaktva ādiṣu avāntara pratyaya viśeṣaḥ tatra āha saṃkhyayā tu viśiṣyate iti ayam ekaḥ pṛthak dvau= imau pṛthak iti eka tva ādi saṃkhyā viśiṣṭaḥ vyavahāraḥ pṛthaktve dṛśyate 
NK_139.7^2	 tena ekatra dravye vartamānam pṛthaktvam ekārtha samavetayā eka tva saṃkhyayā viśiṣyate dvayoḥ vartamānam dvi tva saṅkhyayā smṛti upanītayā viśiṣyate tad viśeṣāt ca avāntara vyavahāra viśeṣaḥ anuvṛtti pratyayaḥ ca pṛthaktva sāmānya kṛtaḥ eva iti abhiprāyaḥ etena paramāṇu parimāṇa iṣtu api parama aṇu tvam saṃmānyam pratyākhyeyam parama śabda viśeṣitāt eva aṇutva sāmānyāt vyavahāra anugama upapatteḥ atha kasmāt sarva dravya anugatam ekam eva pṛthaktvam ekatva ādi saṃkhyā viśeṣaṇa bhedāt pratyaya bheda hetuḥ iti na iṣyate na iṣyate krameṇa upajāyamāneṣu dravyeṣu sāmānya vat guṇasya samavāya adarśanāt attha idam sāmānyam eva bhaviṣyati na piṇḍa antara ananu samdhāne sāmānya buddhi vat pṛthaktva buddheḥ abhāvāt 
NK_140.1–140.5^1	 saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta pratyaya nimittam sa ca dravya guṇa karma hetuḥ dravya ārambhe nirapekṣaḥ tathā bhavati iti sa apekṣebhyaḥ nirapekṣebhyaḥ ca iti vacanāt guṇa karma ārambhe tu sa apekṣaḥ saṃyukta samavāyāt agneḥ vaiśeṣikam iti vacanāt saṃyoga sadbhāva nirūpaṇa artham āha saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta pratyaya nimittam iti asti tāvat idamanena saṃyuktam iti pratyayaḥ laukikānām na ca asya rūpa ādayaḥ nimittam tad pratyaya vilakṣaṇa tvāt atas yat asya nimittam sa saṃyogaḥ naitantarya nibandhanaḥ ayam pratyayaḥ iti ced kim dravyayoḥ paraspara saṃśleṣaḥ nairantaryam antara abhāvaḥ vā tatra ādye kalpe na kiñcid atiriktam uktam syāt dravyayoḥ paraspara upasaṃśleṣaḥ eva hi naḥ saṃyogaḥ 
NK_140.1–140.5^2	 dvitīye kalpe sa antarayoḥ antara abhāve saṃyogāt anyaḥ kaḥ hetuḥ iti vācyam yat eva bhavatām asaṃyuktayoḥ saṃyoge kāraṇam tat eva naḥ sa antarayorayoḥ antara abhāve kāraṇam iti ced astu kāmam kintu idam sva āśrayam deśa antaram prāpayat tad antara abhāvam karoti aprāpayat vā aprāpti pakṣe tāvat antara abhāvaḥ durlabhaḥ rūrvā avaṣṭabdhe eva deśe avasthānāt deśa antara prāpti pakṣe tu tasyāḥ kaḥ nāma anyaḥ saṃyogaḥ yaḥ pratiṣidhyate avirala deśe dravyayoḥ utpāde saṃyoga vyavahāraḥ iti ced na utpāda mātre saṃyoga vyavahāraḥ kintvirala deśa utpāde yā eva iyam utpādyamānayoḥ avirala deśa tā saḥ eva saṃyogaḥ 
NK_140.6–140.7^1	 sa ca dravya guṇa karma hetuḥ tantu saṃyogaḥ dravyasya hetuḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ buddhi ādīnām guṇānām hetuḥ evam bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ śabdasya guṇasya hetuḥ prayatna vat ātma hasta saṃyogaḥ hasta karmaṇaḥ hetuḥ tathā vegavat vāyu saṃyogaḥ tṛṇa karmaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti ādikam ūhyam yathā ayam dravyam ārabhate yathā ca guṇa karmaṇī tam prakāram darśayati dravya ārambhaḥ ityādinā dravyasya ārambhe kartavye saṃyogaḥ sva āśrayam svasya nimitta kāraṇam antareṇa na anyat apekṣate na tu ayam anapekṣā arthaḥ paścāt bhāvi nimitta antaram na apekṣate iti śyāma ādi vināśa anantara bhāvinaḥ antyasya paramāṇu agni saṃyogasya pāka jānām guṇānām api ārambhe nirapekṣa kāraṇa tva prasaṅgāt katham etat avagatam tvayā yat ayam dravya ārambhe nirapekṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti tatra āha tathā bhavati iti asa apekṣebhyaḥ nirapekṣebhyaḥ ca a iti vacanāt paṭa artham upakriyamāṇebhyaḥ tantubhyaḥ abhaviṣyati paṭaḥ a iti pratyayaḥ jāyate iti pūrvam pratipādya sūtra kāreṇa etat uktam tathā bhavati iti sa apekṣebhyaḥ nirapekṣebhyaḥ ca iti 
NK_140.7^2	 asya ayam arthaḥ yathā upakriyamāṇebhyaḥ bhaviṣyati paṭaḥ iti pratyayaḥ tathā sa apekṣebhyaḥ nirapekṣebhyaḥ ca iti bhati iti vartamāna pratyayaḥ anyathā sa apekṣebhyaḥ nirapekṣebhyaḥ ca iti bhavati iti vartamāna pratyayaḥ na syāt yadā katicid tantavaḥ saṃyuktāḥ vartante katicid ca asaṃyuktāḥ tadā tebhyaḥ bhavati prṭaḥ iti pratyayaḥ syāt iti arthaḥ atra sūtre vārtamānika pratīti hetu tvena abhidhīyamāneṣu tantuṣu saṃyukteṣu eva anapekṣa śabda prayogāt saṃyogaḥ dravya ārambhe nirapekṣaḥ iti pratīyate iti tātparyam 
NK_140.8	 tuśabdena rūru asmāt viśeṣam pratipādayan= āha guṇa karma ārambhe tu sa apekṣaḥ kutas jñātam iti atas āha saṃyukta samavāyāt iti agneḥ vaiśeṣikam iti agni gatam uṣṇa tvam vivakṣatam tad pārthiva paramāṇu saṃyukte vahnau samavāyāt paramāṇau rūpa ādi utpattikāraṃam iti amāt vacaṇad guṇa ārambhe paramāṇu agni saṃyogasya uṣṇa sparśa sāpekṣa tvam pratīyate anyathā vahni saṃyoga jeṣu rūpa ādiṣu vahni sparśasya kāraṇa tva abhidhāna ayogāt buddhi ārambhe ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya sva āśraya sva nimitta kāraṇa vyatirekeṇa api dharma ādi apekṣa tvam iti yathāsaṃbhavam api ūhyam karma ārambhe api saṃyogasya sa apekṣa tvam vāyu gata vega apekṣasya tṛṇa vāyu saṃyogasya tṛṇe karma ārambhaka tvāt bīja vināśa anantaram aṅkurasya utpatteḥ mṛd puṇḍa dhvaṃsā anantaram ghaṭasya utpādādabhāvāt eva dravyasya utpādaḥ na saṃyogāt iti ced tat ayuktam avayava saṃyoga viśeṣebhyaḥ dravyasya utpatti darśanāt abhāvasya niratiśaya tve kārya viśeṣasya ākasmika tva prasaṅgāt ca 
NK_141.1	 edam tu iha nirūpyate kim satkriyate asat eva vā satkriyate iti sāṃkhyāḥ asat akaraṇāt na hi asataḥ gagama kusumasya sattvam kenacid śakyam karttum saraḥ ca satkāraṇam yuktam eva tad dharma tvāt dṛṣṭam hi tileṣu sataḥ eva tailasya niṣpīḍanena karaṇam asataḥ tu karaṇe na nidarśanam asti itas ca satkāryam upādāna grahaṇāt upādānāni kāraṇāni teṣām kāryeṇa grahaṇam kāryasya taiḥ saha sambandhaḥ tasmāt kāryam sat eva avidyamānasya sambandha abhāvāt asambaddham eva kāryam kāraṇaiḥ kriyate iti ced na sarva sambhava abhāvāt asambaddha tva aviśeṣe sarvam sarvasmāt bhavet na ca evam tasmāt kāryam prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha sambaddham yathā āhuḥ 
NK_141.2–141.4	 asattvāt na asti sambandhaḥ kāraṇaiḥ sattva saṅgibhiḥ asambaddhasya ca utpattim icchataḥ na vyavasthitiḥ iti api ca śaktasya janaka tvam aśaktasi vā aśaktasya janaka tve tāvat atiprasaktiḥ śaktasya janaka tve tu kim asya śaktiḥ sarvatra kvacid eva vaḥ sarvatra ced sā eva ati vyāptiḥ atha kvacid eva katham asati tasman kāraṇasya tatra śaktiḥ niyata iti vaktavyam asataḥ viṣaya tva ayogāt tasmāt śaktasya yat śakyam śakti viṣayaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ tasya karaṇāt prāk api śakyam sat eva itas api satkāryam kāraṇa bhāvāt kāraṇa svabhāvam kāryam iti na anyaḥ avayavī avayavebhyaḥ tad deśa tvāt yat tu yasmāt anyat na tat tasya deśaḥ yathā gauraśvasya ityādibhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ pratipāditam kāraṇam ca sat atas tat avyatireki kāryam api sat eva iti tat etat uktam asat akaraṇāt upādāna grahaṇāt sarva sambhava abhāvāt śaktasya śakya karaṇāt kāraṇa bhāvāt ca satkāryam iti 
NK_141.5	 atra ucyate yadi karaṇa vyāpārāt prāk api paṭaḥ tantuṣu san= ā iva kim iti upalabdhi kāraṇeṣu satsu satyām api jijñāsāyām na upalabhyate anabhivyakta tvāt iti ced kā iyam anabhivyaktiḥ yadi upalabdheḥ abhāḥ tasya eva anupapatti śaoditā katham tat eva uttaram atha upalabdha yogyasya artha kriyā nivartana kṣamasya rūpasya virahaḥ anabhivyaktiḥ tadānīm asat kārya vādaḥ tathābhūtasya rūpasya prāc asataḥ paścāt bhāvāt atha matam paṭasya cakṣuḥ ādi vat kuvinda ādi kāraṇa vyāpāraḥ api upalabdhi kāraṇam tasya abhāvāt sataḥ api anupalabdhiḥ iti ced na kāraṇa vyāpārasya api sarvadā tatra sambhavāt vyāpāraḥ api pūrvam anabhivyaktaḥ samprati kāraṇaiḥ abhivyajyamānaḥ bhāvam upalambhayati iti ced abhivyaktiḥ api yadi asatī katham tasyāḥ kāraṇam sati iti ced bhāva upalambha prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ eva iti kasyacid apūrvasya viśeṣasya upajananam antareṇa prāc anupalabdhasya paścāt upalambhaḥ durghaṭaḥ 
NK_141.6^1	 yat ca uktam asat aśakya karaṇam vyoma kusuma vat iti tatra svabhāva bhedāt asat eka svabhāvam gagana kusumam sat asat svabhāvam tu ghaṭa ādikam tat pūrvam asat paścāt sat bhavati katham sat asatoḥ ekatra na virodhaḥ iti ced kāla bhedena samāveśāt prāk utpatteḥ paṭasya dharmiṇaḥ abhāvāt katham asattvam tasya dharmaḥ iti ced yādṛśaḥ yakṣaḥ tādṛśaḥ bakiḥ sattvam asataḥ dharmaḥ na syāt asattvam tu asataḥ eva yuktam yat asat pūrvam āsīt tasya katham sattvam iti ced kāraṇa sāmarthyāt asti sa kaḥ api mahimā turya ādīnām yat eteṣu sambhūya vyāpriyamāṇeṣu asan= eva paṭaḥ saṃbhavati 
NK_141.6^2	 asataḥ asambaddhasya janya tve ati prasaktiḥ iti ced na tantu jātīyasya paṭa jātīyaḥ eva sāmarthyāt kutas etat tvad pakṣe api kutas etat tantuṣu eva paṭa ātma tā na sarvatra iti vastu svābhāvyāt iti ced sā eva atra api bhaviṣyati atas eva ca upādāna niyamaḥ api anvaya vyatireka abhtām tad jātīya niyamena tad jātīyasya śakti avadhāraṇāt yat punar etat kārya kāraṇayoḥ avyatirekāt kāraṇa avasthānāt eva kāryasya api avasthānam iti tat asiddham asiddhena sādhitam kārya kāraṇayoḥ sva rūpa śakti saṃsthāna bhedasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt pradhāna ātmaka viśvasya atīndriya tva prasaṅgāt ca tad deśa tvam tu tad āśrita tva mātra nibandhanam eva iti alam vṛddheṣu ati nirbandhena 
NK_141.7^1	 etat tu vimṛśyatām kā iyam śaktiḥ iti atīndriyā kācid iti āryāḥ tat ayuktam tasyāḥ sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt atha manyase yathābhūtāt eva vahneḥ dāha utpattiḥ avagatā tathābhūtāt eva mantra eṣadhi sannidhāne sati na dṛśyate yadi dṛṣṭam eva rūpam dāhasya kāraṇam tasya samagrasya sambhavāt dāha an utpādaḥ na syāt asti ca tad anutpattiḥ sā iyam dṛṣṭa rūpasya vaiguṇyam gamayantī hutabhuji śakteḥ atīndriyāyāḥ sattvam kalpayati yasyāḥ mantra ādinā abhibhavaḥ vināśaḥ vā kriyate tatra pratīkāra vaśena punar kārya udayaḥ tatra abhibhavaḥ yatra tu sarvathā eva anutpattiḥ kāryasya tatra vināśaḥ na ca etat vācyam na mantraḥ vahni saṃyuktaḥ na api tad samavetaḥ katham vyadhikaraṇām śaktim vināśayet vināśayati ced ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt iti tad uddeśena prāpta tvāt 
NK_141.7^2	 yathā eva asambaddhaḥ api abhicāraḥ yam uddiśya kriyate tam eva hinasti na puruṣa antaram evam yām eva vyaktim abhisamdhāya mantraḥ prayujyate tasyāḥ eva śaktm niruṇaddhi na sarvāsām na api etat udghoṣaṇīyam yadi śaktiḥ dravya ātmikā samavāyi asamavāyi kāraṇayoḥ anyatara vināśāt vinaśyet atha guṇān atirekiṇī tad āśraya vināśāt virodhi gunā prādurbhāvāt vā vinaśyet iti samavāyasya anabhyupagamāt yasya yatas vināśam pratīmasrasya tam eva vināśa hetum brūmaḥ na punar amum tvad kṛtam samayam abhyupagacchāmaḥ pratīti parāhata tvāt yadi ca avaśyam abhyupeyaḥ tadā dravya guṇayoḥ eva vināśam pratyabhupagamyatām yatra paridṛṣṭaḥ śaktiḥ punar iyam sādṛśya vat padārtha antaram prakāra antareṇa api vinaṃkṣyati kārya utpāda anutpādābhyām vahnau= adhigatā śaktiḥ kutas iyam sarva bhāveṣu kalpyate iti ced yat kiñcid etat ekatra tasyāḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇa tvena kalpitāyāḥ sarvatra tad utpattyā eva atra anumānāt 
NK_141.8^1	 atra usyate na mantra ādi sannidhau kārya anutpattiḥ adṛṣṭam rūpam ākṣipati yathā anvaya vyatirekābhyām avadhṛta sāmarthyaḥ vahniḥ dāsya kāraṇam tathā pratibandhaka mantra ādi prāgabhāvaḥ api kāraṇam sa ca mantra ādi prayoge sati nivṛttaḥ iti sāmagrī vaiguṇyāt eva dāhasya anutpattiḥ na tu śakti vaikalyāt bhāvasya bhāva rūpa kāraṇa niyata tva darśanāt abhāva kārya tvam na asti iti ced na nityānām karmaṇāka karaṇāt pratyavāyasya utpādāt anyathā nitya akaraṇe prāyaścitta anuṣṭhānam na syāt vaiyarthyāt nityānām akaraṇe anya karaṇāt pratyavāyaḥ na tu nityākaraṇasya karaṇa prāgabhāvasya hetu tvam iti ced na nityākaraṇasya api tad bhāva bhāvi tva niyatasya sahāya tvena vyāpārāt 
NK_141.8^2	 nanu yadi pratibandhakasya prayoge tad abhāvaḥ nivṛttaḥ iti dāhasya anutpattiḥ tadā pratibandhaka pratibandhake api dāhaḥ na syāt tad kāraṇasya prāgabhāvasya nivṛtta tvāt dṛśyate ca pratibandhakasya apareṇa mantra ādinā pratibandhe sati sā ahaḥ tena na abhāvaḥ kāraṇam iti avasthite ca śaktiḥ kāraṇam sā ca praktanena pratibaddhā dvi tiyena uttambhitā iti kalpanāḥ avakāśam labhate tat api apeśalam dṛṣṭe sambhavati adṛṣṭa kalpa nāna vakāśāt kadācid pratibandhaka mantra ādya bhāva sahitā sāmagrī kāraṇam kadācid dvitīya mantra ādi sahitā kāraṇam iti asyām kalpanāyām kaḥ virodhaḥ yat anurodhāt adṛṣṭam āśrīyate dṛṣṭaḥ hi eka rūpasya api kāryasya sāmagrī bhedaḥ yathā dāru nirmathana prabhavaḥ vahniḥ sūryakānta prabhavaḥ ca iti tarka siddhāntarahasyam mīmāṃsā siddhāntarahasyam tu tattva prabodhe kathitam asmābhiḥ 
NK_142.1–142.3	 atha katham lakṣaṇaḥ katividhaḥ ca iti aprāptayoḥ prāptiḥ saṃyogaḥ sa ca trividhaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ iti tatra anyatara karma jaḥ kriyāvatā niṣkriyasya yathā sthāṇoḥ śyenena vibhūnām ca mūrttaiḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ viruddha dikkriyayoḥ saṃnipātaḥ yathā mallayoḥ meṣayoḥ vā 
NK_142.4–142.7	 saṃyoga jaḥ tu utpanna mātrasya cira utpannasya vā niṣkriyasya kāraṇa saṃyogibhiḥ akāraṇaiḥ kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyoga pūrvakaḥ kārya akārya gataḥ saṃyogaḥ sa ca ekasmāt dvābhyām bahubhyaḥ ca bhavati ekasmāt tāvat tantu vīraṇa saṃyogāt dvi tantuka vīraṇa saṃyogaḥ dvābhyām tantu ākāśa saṃyogābhyām ekaḥ dvi tantuka ākāśa saṃyogaḥ bahubhyaḥ ca tantu turī saṃyogebhyaḥ ekaḥ paṭa turī saṃyogaḥ 
NK_142.8	 saṃyogaḥ saṃyukta pratyaya nimittam iti avagatam tāvat kintvasya svarūpam bhedaḥ ca na jñāyate tad artham paripṛcchati atha katham lakṣaṇaḥ katividhaḥ ca iti atha iti praśna upakṣepe kathaṃcabdaḥ kiṃśabda arthe yathā kaḥ dharmaḥ katham lakṣaṇaḥ iti lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ ca svarūpa vacanaḥ iti kiṃsvarūpaḥ saṃyogaḥ katividhaḥ ca iti kati prakāraḥ iti arthaḥ lakṣaṇam kathayati aprāptayoḥ prāptiḥ saṃyogaḥ rūpvam aprāptayoḥ dravyayoḥ paśca āt yā prāptiḥ paraspara saṃśleṣaḥ sa saṃyogaḥ aprāptayoḥ iti samavāya vyavaccheda artham idānīm tasya bhedam pratipādayati sa ca trividhaḥ iti 
NK_142.9	 caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇe saṃyogaḥ trividhaḥ eva traividhyam eva darśayati anyatara karma jaḥ ityādinā dvayoḥ saṃyoginoḥ madhye yat anyatarat dravyam tatra yat karma tad anyatara karma rasmāt jātaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ ubhayoḥ dravyayoḥ karmaṇī ubhaya karmaṇī tābhyām jātaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyogāt api saṃyogaḥ jāyate 
NK_142.10	 tatra anyatara karma jaḥ tatra teṣām trayāṇām madhye kriyāvatā dravyeṇa niṣkriyasya dravyasya saṃyogaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ asya udāharaṃam yathā sthāṇoḥ śyenena vibhūnām ca mūrtaiḥ niṣkriyasya sthāṇoḥ kriyāvatā śyenena saha saṃyogaḥ śyema karma jaḥ evam ākāśa ādīnām vibhūtām niṣkriyāṇām kriyāvadbhiḥ mūrtaiḥ asarva gata dravya parimāṇaiḥ mūrta dravya karma jaḥ nanu ekasya mandam gacchataḥ apareṇa tad pṛṣṭham anudhāvatā anyatara karma jaḥ saṃyogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kathanuktam kriyāvatā niṣkriyasya iti satyam niṣkriya tva vācoyuktiḥ tu vivakṣita saṃyoga hetu bhūta karma abhiprāyeṇa iti mantavyam 
NK_142.11	 prathamam śyena caraṇa sthāṇu śirasoḥ saṃyogaḥ tadanu sthāṇu śyena avayavinoḥ tatra avayavayoḥ saṃyogaḥ karma jaḥ avayavinoḥ tu saṃyoga jaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti kecid tat api asāram sa kriyasya api avayavinaḥ kriyāt eva avayavi antareṇa saṃyogāt yadi ca evam na iṣyate avayavānām api sva avayava apekṣayā avayavi tvena sarvatra avayaviṣu karma jasya saṃyogogasya ucchedaḥ syāt tathā sati ca avayavini karma abhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ tyaktavyam vā avayavi karmaṇaḥ saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapekṣa kāraṇam karma iti karma lakṣaṇam iti durakṣara durvidagdhānām yuktim ācārya vacanam ca utsṛjatām andhānām iva pade pade kiyat skhalitam upadarśayiṣyāmaḥ 
NK_142.12–142.13	 ubhaya karma jaḥ viruddha dikkriyayoḥ sannipātaḥ yābhyām digbhyām dvayoḥ paraspara deśam āgacchatoḥ anyonya pratīghātaḥ bhavati te viruddhe diśau yathā prācī prātīcyau dakṣiṇa udīcyau= iti viruddhayoḥ diśoḥ kriyā yayoḥ dravyayoḥ te viruddha dikkriye tayoḥ sannipātaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyogaḥ pratyekam anyatra dvayoḥ api sāmarthayā avadhāraṇāt yathā mallayoḥ meṣayoḥ vā iti udāharaṇam saṃyoga jaḥ tu saṃyogaḥ utpanna mātrasya cira utpannasya vā niṣkriyasya kāraṇa saṃyogibhiḥ akāraṇaiḥ kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyoga pūrvakaḥ kārya akārya gataḥ kāraṇa śabdena atra samavāyi kāraṇam abhimatam akāraṇa śabdena ca samavāyi kāraṇāt anyat ucyate śeṣam udāharaṇe vyaktīkariṣyāmaḥ 
NK_142.14^1	 sa ca ekasmāt dvābhyām bahubhyaḥ ca bhavati ekasmāt tāvat tantu vīraṇa saṃyogāt dvi tantuka vīraṇa saṃyogaḥ vīraṇa saṃyuktasya tantoḥ tamtvatareṇa saṃyogāt utpanna mātrasya dvi tantuka dravyasya niṣkriyasya samavāyi kāraṇa bhūta eka tantu saṃyoginā vīraṇena saṃyogaḥ prāktanāt tantu vīraṇa saṃyogāt ekasmāt bhavati sa ca ayam kāraṇa kāraṇa saṃyoga pūrvakaḥ kathyate dvi tantukasya samavāyi kāraṇam tantuḥ akāraṇam vīraṇam tayoḥ saṃyogena janita tvāt kārya akārya gataḥ ca ayam tantu kārye dvi tantuke tad akārye ca vīraṇe samaveta tvāt saṃyogasya saṃyoga hetu tvam anyasya asambhavāt pariśeṣa siddham 
NK_142.14^2–142.15	 pratyāsattiḥ ca atra kārya eka artha samavāyaḥ tantu vīraṇa saṃyogasya dvi tantuka vīraṇa saṃyogena kāryeṇa saha ekasmin= arthe vīraṇe samavāyāt saṃyogasya ekasya saṃyoga janaka tve guṇāḥ ca guṇa antaram ārabhante iti sūtra virodhaḥ na sūtra artha aparijñānāt guṇānām api guṇam prati kāraṇa tvam iti anena kathyate na punar asya ayam arthaḥ bahuvaḥ eva guṇāḥ ārabhante na ekaḥ na dvau= iti avadhāraṇasya aśravaṇāt yat punar atra guṇāḥ ca guṇa antaram ārabhante iti kāraṇa vṛttīnām samāna jātu ārambhakāṇām guṇān ām ayam niyamaḥ na sarveṣām iti samādhānam tad aśruta vyākhyātṝṇām prakṣṣṭa dhiyām eva nirvahati na asmākam dvābhyām tantu ākāśa saṃyogābhyām dvi tantuka ākāśa saṃyogaḥ iti ākāśam tāvat utpanna mātreṇa dvi tantukena samam saṃyujyate tad kāraṇa saṃyogi tvāt dvi tantuka kāraṇa saṃyukta vīraṇa vat na ca tasya saṃyogasya kāraṇa antaram asti atas dvi tantuka kāraṇayoḥ tantva uḥ a kāśa saṃyogābhyām eva tat ya utpattiḥ 
NK_142.16	 bahubhyaḥ ca tantu turī saṃyogebhyaḥ ekaḥ paṭa turī saṃyogaḥ paṭa kāraṇānām tantūnām pratyekam turyā saha ye saṃyogāḥ tebhyaḥ bahubhyaḥ ekaḥ paṭaturyoḥ saṃyogaḥ jāyate paṭa ārambhaka tvam ca tantūnām khṇḍa avaya vi dravya ārambha paramparayā na ca mūrtānām samāna deśa tā doṣaḥ yāvatsu tantuṣu ekaḥ avayavī varttate tāvatsu eva anyūnān atiriḥ teṣu aparasya samavāya anabhyupagamāt dvi tantukam dvayoḥ tantvoḥ samavaiti tri tantukam tu tayoḥ tantu antare ca tat adhikam dravyam teṣu ca iti uttarottareṣu kalpanāyām kutas samāna deśa tvam atas eva ca paṭa pāṭite tiṣṭhati ca alpataratama ādi bhāva bhedena khaṇḍa avayavi grahaṇam teṣu vinaṣṭeṣu tu yadi ārabhyate paṭaḥ durghaṭam idam 
NK_142.17	 nanu evam bāla śarīra avayavāḥ avinaṣṭe eva tasmin= āhāra avayava sahitāḥ śarīra antaram ārabheran ārabhantām yadi paṭaḥ iva khaṇḍa avayavinām vṛddha śarīre tiṣṭhati vināśite vā pūrva śarīrāṇām upalambhaḥ sambhavati atha na asti na tatra ayam vidhiḥ yathādarśanam vyavasthāpanāt etena ārabhya ārambhaka vāda pakṣe paramāṇu avasthitasya jagataḥ grahaṇam na syāt iti api pratyuktam paramāṇunām tri aṇuka ādi kāraṇa tva abhāvasya pṛthivī adhikāre darśita tvāt athavā yadi paramāṇavaḥ dvi aṇukam ārabhya tad sahitāḥ tri aṇukam ārabhante tri aṇuka sahitāḥ ca dravya antaram tathā api kutas viśvasya agrahaṇam mahattva aneka dravyavat tva rūpa viśeṣāṇām upalabdhi kāraṇānām sambhavāt atha satsu api teṣu ati indriya āśraya tvāt atīndriya tvam evam tvad pakṣe api durnivāram tasmāt na iyam atra anupapattiḥ paramāṇūnām tri aṇuka anārambhaka tve pṛthivī adhikāra uktā eva yuktiḥ anugantavyā 
NK_143.1–143.2	 ekasmāt ca dvayoḥ utpattiḥ katham yadā pārthiva apyayoḥ aṇvoḥ saṃyoge sati anyena pārthivena pārthivasya āpyena ca api ena ca api asya yugapad saṃyogau bhavataḥ tadā tābhyām saṃyogābhyām pārthivāpye dvi aṇuke yugapadārabhyete tatas yasmin eva kāle dvi aṇukayoḥ kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ tasmin= eva kāle itaretara kāraṇā karaṇa saṃyogāt itaretara kārya akāryatau saṃyogau yugapad utpadyete 
NK_143.3–143.4	 kim kāraṇam kāraṇa saṃyoginā hi akāraṇena kāryam avaśyam saṃyujyate iti nyāyaḥ atas pārthivam dvi aṇukam kāraṇa saṃyoginā apyena aṇunā sambaddhyate āpyam api dvi aṇukam kāraṇa saṃyoginā pārthivrna iti atha dvi aṇukayoḥ ita retara kāraṇā kāraṇa sambaddhayoḥ katham parasparataḥ sambandhaḥ tayoḥ api saṃyoga jābhyām saṃyogābhyām sambandhaḥ iti 
NK_143.5–143.7	 na asti ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ nitya parimaṇḍala vat pṛthak anabhidhānāt yathā caturvidham parimāṇam utpādyam uktvā āha nityam parimaṇḍalam iti evam anyatara karma ja ādi saṃyogam utpādyam uktvā pṛthak nityam brūyāt na tu evam abravīt tasmāt na astyajaḥ saṃyogaḥ paramāṇubhiḥ ākāśa ādīnām pradeśa vṛttiḥ anyatara karma jaḥ saṃyogaḥ vibhūnām tu parasparataḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti yuta siddhi abhāvāt sā punar dvayoḥ anyatarasya va pṛthak gatimat tvam pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam ca iti 
NK_143.8^1	 ekasmāt ca saṃyogāt dvayoḥ saṃyogayoḥ utpattiḥ katham iti ajñena pṛṣṭaḥ sannāhāḥ yadā iti pārthivā api ayoḥ paramāṇvoḥ saṃyoge sati anyena pārthivena paramāṇunā pārthivasya paramāṇoḥ anyena apyena ca api asya paramāṇoḥ yugapad saṃyogau bhavataḥ tadā tābhyayām saṃyogābhyām pārthivāpye dvi aṇuke yugapadārabhyete samāna jātīya saṃyogasya dravya antara utpatti hetu tvāt tatas yasmin eva kāle pārthiva apya dvi aṇukayoḥ kāraṇa pūrva krameṇa rūpa ādi utpattiḥ tasmin eva kāle itaretara kāraṇā kāraṇa gatāt saṃyogāt itaretara kārya akārya gatau saṃyogau yugapad utpadtete 
NK_143.8^2	 itaretare pārthivāpye dvi aḥuke tayoḥ kāraṇa araṇe paraspara saṃyuktau pārthiva apya paramāṇū pārthivaḥ paramāṇuḥ itarasya pārthiva t vi aṇukasya kāraṇam itarasya api asya dvi aṇukasya akāraṇam evam āpya paramāṇuḥ itarasya api advyaṇukasya kāraṇam itarasya pārthiva t vi aṇukasya akāraṇam tayoḥ saṃyogāt itarasya pārthiva paramāṇoḥ yat kāryam pārthivam dvi aṇukam akāryaḥ ca apyaḥ paramāṇuḥ tayoḥ saṃyogaḥ bhavati evam itarasya api aparamāṇoḥ yat kāryam āpyam dvi aṇukam akāryaḥ tu pārthivaḥ paramāṇuḥ tayoḥ api saṃyogaḥ bhavati iti ekasmāt dvyoḥ utpattiḥ 
NK_143.9	 kim kāraṇam pārthiva apyayoḥ dvi aṇukayoḥ vijātīya paramāṇu saṃyoge kim pramāṇam iti pṛṣṭaḥ san pramāṇam āha kāraṇa saṃyoginā iti pārthiva paramāṇuḥ āpya dvi aṇukena saha sambaddhyate tad kāraṇa saṃyogi tvāt paṭa saṃyukta turīvat evam āpyam paramāṇum api pakṣīkṛtya vaktavyam yatas kāraṇa saṃyoginā kāryam saṃyujyate atas pārthivam dvi aṇukam kāraṇa saṃyogi nāpyena paramāṇunā sambadhyate āpyam ca dvi aṇukam tasya kāraṇa saṃyoginā pārthiva paramāṇunā iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
NK_143.10	 atha pāthi va apyadvi aṇukayoḥ ita retara kāraṇambaddhayoḥ katham sambandhaḥ pārthiva t vi aṇukasya svakīya kāraṇena api advi aṇuka kāraṇena api aparamāṇunā sambaddhasya dvi aṇukasya ca svakīya akāraṇena pārthiva t vi aṇuka kāraṇena pārthiva paramāṇunā sambaddhasya katham sambandhaḥ iti pṛcchati uttaram āha tayoḥ api iti pārthiva t vi aṇukasya apyena paramāṇunā yaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ saṃyogaḥ yaḥ ca api advi aṇukasya pārthiva paramāṇunā saṃyoga jaḥ saṃyogaḥ tābhyām pārthi va ārya paramāṇu dvya saṃyogābhyām dvi aṇukayoḥ paraspara saṃyogaḥ atra api pūrva uktaḥ eva syāyaḥ kāraṇa saṃyoginā akāraṇena saṃyogi kāryam iti 
NK_143.11	 trividhaḥ eva saṃyogaḥ iti uktam nityasya api saṃyogasya sambhavāt iti kecid tad pratiṣedha artham āha na asti ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ parimaṇḍala vat pṛthak anabhidhānāt sarvajñena mahā ṛṣiṇā sarva artha upadeśāya pravṛttena pṛthak ata bhidhānāt ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti khpuṣpa vat etat eva vivṛṇoti yathā ityādinā saṃyogaḥ ajaḥ na bhavati iti pratijñā arthaḥ na punar ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti iti āśraya asiddha tvāt nanu paramāṇu ākāśayoḥ saṃyogaḥ nityaḥ eva tayoḥ nitya tvāt aprāpti abhāvāt ca 
NK_143.12^1	 yat punar ayam kaṇā ādena na uktaḥ tat bhrānteḥ puruṣa dharma tvāt atas āha paramāṇubhiḥ ākāśa ādīnām iti yathā mahataḥ nyagrodhasya mūla grāva yava vyapine ekasya mūlāt agram agrān mūlam gacchatā puruṣeṇa saṃyoga vibhāgau= anyatara karma jau yugapad pratīyete tathā vyāpinaḥ api ākāśasya paramāṇunā saha saṃyoga vibhāgau paramāṇu karma jau bhavataḥ tayoḥ avyāpya vṛtti tvāt iti na paramāṇu ākāśa saṃyogasya nitya tā idam tāvat ittham parihrptam vibhūnām parasparataḥ saṃyoge kā pratikriyā na hi asau= anyatara karma jaḥ na api ubhaya karma jaḥ teṣām niṣkriya tvāt na api saṃyoga jaḥ kāryasya hi kāraṇa saṃyoginā akāraṇena saṃyoga jaḥ saṃyogaḥ bhavati na ca ayam vibhūnām upapadyate nitya tvāt
