NK_143.12^2–143.13	 asti ca teṣām saṃyogaḥ ākāśam amūrtena api dravyeṇa samam saṃyujyate mūrta dravya saṃyogi tvāt paṭa ādi vat iti anumānāt pratīteḥ sat ākāraṇa vat nityam tasmāt anupapannam idam ajaḥ saṃyogaḥ na asti iti tatra āha vibhūnām iti yatra yuta siddhiḥ tatra eva saṃyogaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yuta siddhiḥ ca ākāśa ādiṣu na asti atas vyāpaka abhāvāt saṃyogaḥ api teṣu na bhavati yat ca saṃyoga pratipādakam anumān a nuktam tat asādhanam ubhaya pakṣa sama tvāt yathā idam vibhūnām saṃyogam praśasti tathā tābhyām eva hetu dṛṣṭāntābhyām vibhāgam api astu dvyoḥ api upapattiḥ pramāṇena tathā abhāva pratīteḥ iti ced na saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ ekasya nitya tve anyatarasya asambhavāt iti dvayoḥ api asiddhiḥ paraspara pratibandhāt atha kā iyam yuta siddhiḥ yasyāḥ abhāvāt vibhūnām saṃyogaḥ na siddhyati atra āha sā punar iti dvayoḥ anyarasya vā pṛthak gamanam yuta siddhiḥ nityānām dvyoḥ anyatarasya vā paraspara parihāreṇa pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam yuta siddhiḥ anityānām iyam dvividhā api ākāśa ādiṣu na asti iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NK_143.14	 vināśaḥ tu sarvasya saṃyogasya eka artha samavetāt vibhāgāt anyatara karma jasya ubhaya karma jasya saṃyoga jasya eka artha samavetāt vibhāgāt yayoḥ dravyayoḥ saṃyogaḥ vartate tayoḥ parasparam vibhāgāt sa yogasya vināśaḥ yadi api vibhāga kāle saṃyogaḥ vidyate eva tathā api tayoḥ sahabhāvaḥ na lakṣyate vināśasya aśubha avāt vibhāgena vā tad upalambha pratibandhāt kvacid āśraya vināśāt api saṃyogasya vināśaḥ katham tantvoḥ saṃyoge sati anyatarasya tantu ārambhakem aśau karma utpadyate kutaścid kāraṇāt tena karmaṇā aṃśvantarāt vibhāgāḥ kriyate vibhāgāt aṃśvoḥ saṃyoga vināśāt tantu vināśa tad āśritasya saṃyogasya vināśaḥ ubhaya āśrayasya tasya eka āśrayāyāvastḥane anupalambhāt iti 
NK_144.1–144.5	 vibhāgaḥ vibhakta pratyaya nimittam śabda vibhāga hetuḥ ca prāpti pūrvikā aprāptiḥ vibhāgaḥ sa ca trividhaḥ anya tararma jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ vibhāga jaḥ ca vibhāgaḥ iti tatra anyatara karma ja ubhaya karma jau saṃyoga vat vibhāgaḥ tu dvividhaḥ kāraṇa vibhāgāt kāraṇa kāraṇa vibhāgāt ca saṃyoga pūrvaka tvāt vibhāgasya tad anantaram nirūpaṇa artham āha vibhāgaḥ vibhakta pratyaya nimittam iti atra api vyākhyānam pūrvavat saṃyoga abhāve vibhakta pratyayaḥ iti ced asati vibhāge saṃyoga abhāvasya kasmāt utpādaḥ karmaṇā kriyate iti ced na karmaṇaḥ guṇa vināśe sāmarthya adarśanāt dṛṣṭam cā guṇa vināśe guṇānām hetu tvam tena atra api guṇa antara kalpanā kiñca saṃyoga abhāve asaṃyuktau= imau= iti pratyayaḥ syāt na vibhaktau= iti abhāvasya vidhi mukhena grahaṇa abhāvāt bhāktaḥ pratyayaḥ ayam iti ced tarhi vibhāgasya apratyākhyānam niṣpradhānasya bhāktasya abhāvāt 
NK_144.6	 tasya kāryam darśayati śabda vibhāga hetuḥ ca iti na kevalam vibhakta pratyaya nimittam śabda vibhāga hetuḥ ca iti ca arthaḥ vaṃśa dale pārṭyamāne yaḥ ayam ādyaḥ śabdaḥ sa tāvat guṇa antara nimittaḥ śabda tvāt bherī daṇḍa saṃyoga ja śabda vat na ca ayam saṃyogañḥ tasya abhāvāt tasmāt vaṃśa dala vibhāga jaḥ eva ayam tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt vibhāgasya vibhāga hetu tvam ca anantaram vakṣyāmaḥ 
NK_144.7	 prāptiḥ vikā aprāptiḥ iti tasya lakṣaṇa kathanam adharmaḥ iti nan yathā dharma virodhini guṇa antare na tu dharma abhāve tathā aprāptiḥ iti nan prāpti virodhini guṇa antare na tu prāpteḥ abhāve prāptau pūrva sthitāyām yā aprāptiḥ prāpti virodhī guṇa viśeṣāḥ sa vibhāgaḥ iti vākya arthaḥ kim prapteḥ pūrva avasthāna mātram kim vā vibhāgam prati hetu tvam api asti avasthiti mātram iti brūmahe saṃyogasya vibhāga hetu tve avayava saṃyoga anantaram eva tad vibhāgasya utpattau dravya anutpatti prasaṅgāt karma sahakārī saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam iti ced anvaya vyatireka avadhṛta sāmarthyam karma eva kāraṇam astu na saṃyogaḥ tasmin sati api abhāvāt pradhvaṃsa utpatta = iva bhāvasya vibhāga utpattau saṃyogasya pūrva kālatā niyamaḥ vibhāgasya tad virodhi svabhāva tvāt 
NK_144.8–144.9	 sa ca trividhaḥ iti bheda kathanam atra api caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇe trividhaḥ eva anyatara karma jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ vibhāga jaḥ ca vibhāgaḥ iti tatra teṣu madhye anyatara karma ja ubhaya karma jau saṃyoga vat yathā kriyāvatā niṣkriyasya saṃyogaḥ anyatara karma ja srathāḥ vibhāgaḥ api yathā ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyogaḥ mallayoḥ meṣayoḥ vā tathā vibhāgaḥ api vibhāga jaḥ tu dvividhaḥ iti tuśabena asya pūrvābhyām viśeṣa kathanam kāraṇayoḥ vibhāgāt ekaḥ vibhāgaḥ bhavati aparaḥ tu kāraṇa akāraṇayoḥ vibhāgāt iti dvaividhyam 
NK_145.1–145.2	 tatra kāraṇa vibhāgāt tāvat kārya āviṣṭe kāraṇe karma utpannam yadā tasya avayava antarāt vibhāgam karoti na tad ākāśa ādi deśāt yadā tu ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam karoti na tadā avayava antarāt iti sthitiḥ atas avayava karma avayava antarāt eva vibhāgam ārabhate vibhāgāt ca dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vinācaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ iti avayavi vināśaḥ tadā kāraṇayoḥ vartamānaḥ vibhāgaḥ kārya vināśa viśiṣṭam kālam svatantram vā avayavam apekṣya sa kriyasya eva avayasya kārya saṃyuktāt ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam ārabhate na niṣkriyasya kāraṇa abhāvāt uttara saṃyoga anutpattau= anupabhogya tva prasaṅgaḥ 
NK_145.3–145.4	 na tu tad avayava karma ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam karoti tad ārambhaka kāla atīta tvāt pradeśa antara saṃyogam tu karoti eva akṛta saṃyogasya karmaṇaḥ kāla atyaya abhāvāt iti kāraṇa vibhāgāt ca vibhāgaḥ kathyate kārya āviṣṭaḥ ityādinā kāryeṇa āviṣṭe vyāpte avaruddhe kāraṇe karma utpannam yadā tasya avayavasya avayava antarāt dravya ārmbhaka saṃyoga vināśakam vibhāgam karoti na tadā dravya avaruddhāt ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam karoti yadā ca ākāśa ādideśāt na tadā avayava antarāt iti sthitiḥ niyamaḥ atas avayava karma avayava antarāt eva vibhāgam ārabhate yatas ākāśa vibhāga kāraṇam karma avayava antarāt vibhāgam na karoti iti niyamaḥ atas avayava antara vibhāga ārambhakam karma avayava antarāt eva vibhāgam karoti na ākāśa ādideśāt 
NK_145.5	 ayam abhisamdhiḥ ākāśa vibhāga kartṛ tvam karmaṇaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga anārambhaka tvena vyāptam dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga anārambhaka tva viruddham ca dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga utpādaka tvam atas yatra idam upalabhyate tatra dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga anutpādaka tve nivartamāne tad vyāptam ākāśa vibhāga kartṛ tvam api nivartate yathā vahni vyāvṛttau dhūma vyāvṛttiḥ 
NK_145.6–145.7	 ākāśa vibhāga kartṛ tvasya dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga anārambhaka tvasya ca sahabhāva mātram na vyāptiḥ iti ced na vyabhicāra anupalabdheḥ yayoḥ kvacid vyabhicāraḥ dṛśyate tayoḥ sahabhāva mātram yathā vajre pārthiva tva loha lekhya tvayoḥ sati api pārthiva tve kāṣṭha ādiṣu loha lekhya tvāt na tu vyoma vibhāga kartṛ tvasya viśiṣṭa vibhānutpādaka tvasya ca vyabhicāraḥ dṛṣyate adṛśyamānaḥ api kadācid ayam bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkyeta yadi anayoḥ śiṣya ācāryayoḥ iva upādhi kṛtaḥ sahabhāvaḥ pratīyeta na ca evam api asti upādhīnām anupalambhāt yadi apratīta vyabhicāraḥ nirupādhikaḥ sahabhāvaḥ na vyāpti hetuḥ iti agni dhūmayoḥ api vyāptiḥ na syāt iti ucchinnā idānīm jagati anumāna vārtā yadi avayava karmaṇā avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate na ākāśa ādideśāt tatas kim siddham tatra āha vibhāgāt ca dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ ākāśa vibhāga kartṛ tve viśiṣṭa vibhāga anutpādāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ na bhavet iti arthaḥ 
NK_145.8^1	 saṃyoga vināśe kim syāt atas āha tasmin iti saṃyoge asamavāyi kāraṇe tasmin= aṣṭe kāraṇasya abhāvāt kārya abhavaḥ iti nyāyāt avayavinaḥ vināśaḥ avayavi dravye naṣṭe kim syāt atas āha tadā iti dravye vinaṣṭe tad kāraṇayoḥ avayavayoḥ vartamānaḥ vibhāgaḥ kārya vināśena viśiṣṭam kālam svatantram vā avayavam apekṣya makriyasya eva avayavasya kārya saṃyuktāt ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam ārabhate yāvat kārya dravyam na vinaśyati tāvat avayavasya svātantryam pṛthak deśa gamana yogya tā na asti iti avayavi deśāt tat vibhāgaḥ na ghaṭate tad artham uktam kārya vināśa viśiṣṭam kālam svatantram vā avayavam apekṣya iti kāraṇayoḥ vartamānaḥ vibhāgaḥ saktiyasya eva vibhāgam karoti iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ iti ced 
NK_145.8^2	 atas āha na niṣkriyasya kāraṇa abhāvāt iti vibhāgāt vibhāga utpattau karma api nimitta kāraṇam tasya abhāvāt na niṣkriyasya vibhāgaḥ ata eva arthe yukti antaram āha uttara saṃyoga anutpattau= anupabhogya tva prasaṅgaḥ iti kriyā hi prādhānyena uttara saṃyoga artham upajātāḥ deśa antara prāptena dravyeṇa kasyacid puruṣa arthasya sampādanāt tatra yadi sa kriyasya avayavasya kārya saṃyuktāt ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgaḥ na bhavati tadā pūrva daṇī ogasya pratibandhakasya anivṛtteḥ uttara saṃyoga anutpattau sa anupabhogyā niṣprayojanā syāt na ca eyat yuktam tasmāt sa kriyasya eva vibhāgaḥ iti tātparyam avayava kriyayoḥ avayava vibhāga sama kālam ākāśa ādi vibhāga kartṛ tvam na upapadyate iti 
NK_145.9	 mā kārṣīt iyam yugapad vibhāga dvayam krama karaṇe tu kaḥ virodhaḥ yana vibhāga janane dṛṣṭa sāmarthyām imām parityajya adṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya vibhāgasya vibhāga hetu tvam āśrīyate iti atra āha na tu tad avayava karma ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam karoti tad ārambhakaka atīta tvāt evam hi karmaṇaḥ svabhāvaḥ yat tad asamavāyokāraṇa tayā vibhāgam ārabhamāṇam sva utpatti ananta rakṣaṇaḥ eva ārabhate na kṣaṇa antare sa ca tasya vibhāga ārambha kālaḥ dvitīya bhāga utpatti kāle atītaḥ iti na tasmāt asya utpattḥ 
NK_145.10	 nanu eśā antara saṃyogam api kutas karoti aneka kṣaṇa vyavadhānāt atas āha pradeśa anta saṃyogam kayoti iti yathā karmaṇaḥ sva utpāda ananta rakṣaṇaḥ vibhāga ārambha kālaḥ tathā pūrva saṃyoga nivṛtti ananta rakṣaṇaḥ pradeśa antara saṃyoga ārambha kālaḥ pūrva deśa avasthitasya dravyasya deśa antara prāpteḥ asambhavāt tasya ca saṃyoga ārambha kālasya atyayaḥ atikramaḥ na bhūtaḥ tadānīm hi kālaḥ ayam atikrāntaḥ syāt yadi karmaṇā pradeśa antara saṃyogaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavet na tu evam tasmāt akṛta saṃyogasya karmaṇaḥ yaḥ saṃyoga ārabha kālaḥ tasya atyaya abhāvāt karma saṃyogam karoti na vibhāgam tana ced ayam na kṛtaḥ anyasya asambhavāt asamavāyi kāraṇena vinā ca vastunaḥ anutpādāt eka artha samavetaḥ vibāgosya kāraṇam iti avatiṣṭhate iti śabdaḥ prakrama samāptau 
NK_146.1–146.2	 kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāt api katham yadā haste karma utpannam avayava antarāt bhāgam akurvat ākāśa ādi deśebhyaḥ vibhāgān ārabhya pradeśa antare saṃyogān ārabhate tadā te kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgaḥ karma yā diśam prati kārya ambha abhimukham tām apekṣya kārya akārya vibhāgān ārabhante tad anantaram kāraṇa akāraṇa saṃyogāt ca kārya akārya saṃyogān iti yadi kāraṇa vibhāga anantaram kārya vibhāga utpattiḥ kāraṇa saṃyoga anantaram kārya saṃyoga utpattiḥ 
NK_146.3	 evam kāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakam vibhāgam pratītya kāraṃā kāraṇa vibhāga pūrvakam vibhāgam pratyetum icchan pṛcchati kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāt api katham iti uttaram āha yadā ityādinā haste kutas cit kāraṇāt karma utpannam tasya hastasya avayava antarāt vibhāgam akurvat ākāśa ādi deśebhyaḥ vibhāgān ārabhya pradeśa antaraiḥ saha yadā saṃyogān ārabhate tadā te kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgāḥ śarīta kāraṇasya hastasya akāraṇām ākāśa ādi deśānām vibhāgāḥ karma yasyām diśi kārya ārambha abhimukham karmaṇā yatra uttara saṃyogaḥ janayitavyaḥ tām diśam apekṣya kārya akārya vibhāgān hasta kāryasya śarīrasya akāryāṇām ākāśa ādi deśānām vibhāgān ārabhante yatas kuḍya ādi deśāt hasta na vibhāgaḥ tatas śarīrasya api vibhāgaḥ dṛśyate na ca ayam śarīra kriyā kāryaḥ tadānīm śarīrasya niṣkriya tvāt na api hasta kriyā kāryaḥ bhavitum arhati vyadhikaraṇasya karmaṇaḥ vibhāga hetu tva adarśanāt atas kāraṇa akāraṇa vibhāgaḥ tasya kāraṇam iti kalpyate ākāśa ādau= ityādi padam samasta vibhudravya avarodha artham atas eva vibhāgān iti bahuvacanam tad vibhāgānām bahu tvāt 
NK_146.4–146.5	 atra āhuḥ eke kuḍya ādi deśāt hasta śarīra vibhāgayoḥ yugapad bhāva pratīteḥ tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhidhānam pratyakṣa viruddham iti tad asaṅgatam hasta vibhāga kāle śarīra vibhāga utpatti kāraṇa abhāvāt na ca asati kāraṇe kārya utpattiḥ asti hasta kriyā ca na kāraṇam iti uktam tasmāt tayoḥ yugapad abhimānaḥ bhrāntaḥ anumānaganyaḥ krama bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa siddham ca yaugapadyam pratyakṣe ca paripanthini anumānasya utpattiḥ eva na asti abādhita viṣaya tva abhāvāt katham tad anumāna virodhāt pratyakṣasya bhrānta tvam iti ced utpala patra śata vyatibhede api kutas anumāna pravṛttiḥ pratyakṣa virodhāt atha manyase tatra pratyakṣa virodhāt anumānam na udeti yatra anena viṣayasya bādhaḥ niścitaḥ syāt iha tu asau sandigdhaḥ patra śata vyatibhedasya aśubhau= i tvena api nimittena yaugapadya grāhakasya pratyakṣasya pravṛtteḥ sambhavāt asti ca sarva loka prasiddham aati dṛḍham avyavahitā sūci bhinatti na vyavahitam a iti vyāpti grāhakam pramāṇam atas tad sāmarthyāt pratyakṣe saṃbhavati api bhavati anumānasya udayaḥ iti 
NK_146.6^1	 evam ced atra api vyadhikaraṇā kriyā vibhāgam na karoti iti vyāpti grāhakasya pramāṇasya ati dṛṅha tvāt pratyakṣasya ca anyathā api upapatteḥ su sthitam krama anumānam atas eva ca anumānena pratyakṣasya bādhaḥ idam hi sa viṣayam nirviṣayam ca pratyakṣam āśu bhāvi tva mātreṇa pravṛtteḥ yat ca sa viṣayam tat tathā tvena avasthatasya viṣayasya sāhāyya prāptyā balavat durbalam ca nirviṣa yam asahāya tvāt vyāpti grāhakeṇa eva pratyakṣeṇa hi tat bādha udayāt anumānena pratyakṣasya bādhaḥ 
NK_146.6^2	 tathā ca diś moha ādiṣu anumānam eva balavat iti manyante vṛddhā abhavati vai pratyakṣāt api anumānam balīyaḥ a iti vadantaḥ vahnau= uṣṇātva grāhiṇaḥ pratyakṣasya tu na anyathā upapattiḥ asti iti tena avadhārite viṣayasya bādhe na asti anumānasya pravṛttiḥ kimartham punar jñānayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ kalpyate samāne viṣaye tayoḥ virodhāt ekam eva tat vastu kiñcid rajatam iti evam bodhayati śuktikā iyam iti ca aparam śuktikā tva rajata tvayoḥ ca na ekatra saṃbhavaḥ sarvadā tayoḥ paraspara parihāreṇa avasthāna upalambhāt atas viṣaya virodhāt tad vijñānayoḥ api virodhe sati bādhya bādhaka bhāva kalpanam 
NK_146.7	 kaḥ bādhaḥ viṣaya apahāraḥ nanu rajata jñāna avabhāsitaḥ dharmī tāvat utpanne api jñāna antare tad avaḥ tḥ eva pratibhāti rajata tvam tu na asti eva kim apahriyate sambandha viyojanasya apahāra artha tvāt vijñāne pratibhātam tat iti ced satyam pratibhātam na tu pratibhātam śakya apahāram bhūta tvāt eva na hi pratibhāsitaḥ arthaḥ apratibhāsitaḥ bhavati vastu vṛttyā rajatam avidyamānam api jñānena tatra vidyamāna vat upadarśitam tasya jñāna prasañjitasya sākṣāt virodhi pratipādana dvāreṇa ca abhāva pratipādanam eva viyojanam iti ced rajata abhāve pratipādite rajata jñānasya kā kṣatiḥ abhūt na hi asya rajara sthiti karaṇe vyāpāraḥ api tu asya prakāśane tat ca anena jāyamānena iva kṛtam iti paryavasitam idam kim bādhyate rajata abhāva pratītau pūrva upajātasya rajata jñānasya ayathārtha tā svarūpam pratīyate iti eṣā kṣatiḥ abhūt 
NK_146.8	 nanu evam phala apahāraḥ eva bādhaḥ ayathārtha tā avagame sati jñānasya vyavahāra anaṅga tvāt mā evam phala apahārasya viṣaya apahārana āntarīyaka tvāt na tāvat jñānasya sarvatra phala niṣṭhatā tasya puruṣa icchā adhīnasya anupajanane ayupekṣā saṃvitteḥ paryavasānāt yatra api phala arthitāḥ patrā api phalasya viṣaya pratibaddha tvāt viṣayasya ca jñāna pratibaddha tvāt viṣaya apahāraḥ eva jñānasya bādhaḥ na phala apahāraḥ tasya viṣaya apahārana antarīyaka tvāt iti kṛtam grantha vistareṇa saṃgrahaṭīkārām 
NK_146.9–146.10	 vibhāga ja vibhāga anantara bhāvi tvāt pūrvam pratijñātasya cira utpannasya ca saṃyoga ja saṃyogam pratipādayati tad anantaram iti tasmāt vibhāga ja vibhāgāt anantaram śarīra kāraṇasya hastasya akāraṇānām ākāśa ādi deśānām saṃyogāḥ karma jāḥ hasta kāryasya śarīrasya niṣkriyasya akāryāṇām āśādi deśānām saṃyogān ārabhante na hasta kriyā tasyāḥ sva śrayasya deśa antara prāpti hetu tvāt iti śabdaḥ prakrama samāptau atra codayati yadi iti kāraṇasya hastasya vibhāga anantaram yadi kāryasya śarīrasya vibhāgaḥ tathā kāraṇasya saṃyoga anantaram kāryasya saṃyogaḥ na tad sama kālam 
NK_147.1–147.3	 nanu evam avayava avayavinoḥ yuta siddhi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti na yuta siddhi aparijñānāt sā punar dvyoḥ anyatarasya vā pṛthak gatimat tvam iyantu nityānām anityānām tu yuteṣu āśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ yuta siddhiḥ iti tvac indriya śarīrayoḥ pṛthak gatimat tvam na asti yuteṣu āśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ asti iti paraspareṇa saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ aṇu ākāśayoḥ tu āśraya antara abhāve anyatarasya pṛggatimat tvāt saṃyoga vibhāgau siddhau tantu paṭayoḥ anityayoḥ āśraya antara abhāvāt parasparataḥ saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvaḥ iti diś ādīnām tu pṛthak gatimat tva abhāvāt iti paraspareṇa saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvaḥ iti 
NK_147.4	 nanu evam satya vayava avayavinoḥ yuta siddhiḥ pṛthak siddhiḥ paraspara svātantryam syāt etat uktam bhavati yadi hasta āśritam śarīram tadā haste gacchati tat api saha eva gacchet tathā sati ca saṃyoga vibhāga kramaḥ na syāt krameṇa ced anayoḥ saṃyoga vibhāgau na tadā hastasya gamane śarīrasya gamanam iti tasya svātantrya prasaktiḥ 
NK_147.5	 pariharati na iti yuta siddhi prasaṅgaḥ iti na kutas yuta siddheḥ aparijñānāt yādṛśam yuta siddheḥ lakṣaṇam tādṛśam tvayā na jñātam iti arthaḥ kīdṛśam tasyāḥ lakṣaṇam tatra āha sā punar dvayoḥ iti dvayoḥ ekasya vā paraspara saṃyoga vibhāga hetu bhūta karma samavāya yogya tā yuta siddhiḥ dvayoḥ paramāṇvoḥ pṛthak gamanam ākāśa paramāṇvoḥ ca anyatarasya pṛthak gamanam iyam tu nityānām tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇe nityānām iti asmāt paraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ nityānām eva iyam yuta siddhiḥ iti arthaḥ anityānām tu yuteṣu āśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ yuta siddhiḥ dvayoḥ anyatarasya vā paraspara parihāreṇa anyatra āśraye samavāyaḥ yuta siddhiḥ anityānām dvayoḥ pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam ghaṭa paṭayoḥ śakuni ākāśayoḥ ca anyatarasya śakuneḥ pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam yadi api anyatarasya pṛthak gamanam api asti tathā api tasya pṛthak gamanasya na grahaṇam tasya nitya viṣaya tvena vyākhyānāt 
NK_147.6	 anityānām api pṛthak gamanam eva yuta siddhiḥ kim na ucyate tatra āha tvac indriya śarīrayoḥ pṛthak gmanam na asti yuteṣu āśrayeṣu samavāyaḥ asti iti paraspareṇa saṃyogaḥ siddhaḥ yadi tu anityānām api pṛthak gamanam yuta siddhiḥ ucyate tvac indriya śarīrayoḥ pṛthak gamana abhāvāt ayutasiddha tā syāt tatas ca tayoḥ paraspara saṃyogaḥ na prāpnoti tasya yuta siddhyā eva vyāpta tvāt saṃyogaḥ ca tayoḥ sambandhaḥ na samavāyaḥ tad vilakṣaṇa tvāt tasmāt anityānām na pṛthak gamanam yuta siddhiḥ iti arthaḥ āśraya abhāvāt eva pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam nityeṣu na asti teṣām ca pṛthak gatimat tvāt paraspara saṃyoga vibhāgau siddhau tena eṣām pṛthak gamanam eva yuta siddhiḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa āha aṇu ākāśayoḥ tu āśraya antara abhāve api anyatarasya pṛthak gatimat tvāt saṃyoga vibhāgau siddhau iti pūrvam asati api pṛthak gati nattve tvac indriya śarīrayoḥ pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tve sati saṃyoga vibhāga saṃbhavāt anityānām pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam yuta siddhiḥ na pṛthak gamanam iti uktam 
NK_147.7	 samprati enam eva artham samarthayitum tantu paṭayoḥ anyatarasya pṛthak gatimat tva asaṃbhave api pṛthak āśraya tva abhāvāt saṃyoga vibhāga abhāvam darśayati tantu paṭayoḥ ityādinā vibhūnām tu dvayoḥ anyatarasya vā pṛthak gamana abhāvāt na paraspareṇa saṃyogaḥ na api vibhāgaḥ tasya saṃyoga pūrvaka tvāt kim tu svarūpa sthiti mātram iti āha diś ādīnām iti etāvatā sandartheṇa etat upapāditam haste gacchati śarīram na gacchati iti etāvatā na yuta siddhiḥ yadi tu hasta śarīrayoḥ pṛthak āśraya āśrayi tvam syāt tadā bhavet anayoḥ yuta siddhiḥ tat tu na asti śarīrasya haste samaveta tvāt 
NK_148.1–148.3	 vināśaḥ tu sarvasya vibhāgasya kṣaṇika tvāt uttara saṃyoga avadhi sadbhāvāt kṣaṇikaḥ iti na tu saṃyoga vat yayoḥ eva vibhāgaḥ tayoḥ eva saṃyogāt vināśaḥ bhavati kasmāt saṃyukta pratyaya vat vibhakta pratyaya anuvṛtti abhāvāt tasmāt uttara saṃyoga avadhi sadbhāvāt kṣaṇikaḥ iti kvacid ca āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati iti katham yadā dvi tantuka kāraṇa avayave aṃśau sarma utpannam aṃśu antarāt vibhāgam ārabhate tadā eva tantu antare api karma utpadyate vibhāgāt ca tantu ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tantu karṃṇā tantu antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt tantu saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin= eva kāle saṃyoga vināśāt tantu vināśaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe tad āśritasya tantu antara vibhāgasya vināśaḥ iti 
NK_148.4^1	 vināśaḥ tu sarvasya vibhāgasya kṣaṇika tvāt karma jasya vibhāga jasya ca kāraṇa vṛtteḥ kāraṇa akāraṇa vṛtteḥ ca vibhagasya sarvasya kṣaṇika tvam āśutara vināśi tvam kutas siddham iti atra āha uttara saṃyoga avadhi sadbhāvāt iti uttara saṃyogaḥ avadhiḥ sīmā tasya sadbhāvāt kṣaṇikaḥ vibhāgaḥ kim uktam syāt na vibhāgaḥ niravadhiḥ kim tu asya uttara saṃyogaḥ avadhiḥ asti uttara saṃyogaḥ ca anantaram eva jāyate tasmāt āśu vināśi uttara saṃyogaḥ vibhāgasya avadhiḥ iti etat eva kutas tatra āha na tu saṃyoga vat iti yathā saṃyogaḥ sva āśrayayoḥ eva paraspara vibhāgāt vinaśyati na evam vibhāgaḥ sva āśrayayoḥ eva paraspara saṃyogāt vinaśyati kim tu sva āśrayasya anyena api saṃyogāt 
NK_148.4^2	 tathā hi vṛkṣasya mūle puruṣeṇa vibhāgaḥ tayoḥ eva paraspara saṃyogāt vinaśyati puruṣasya pradeśa antara saṃyogāt vā evam ced siddham uttara saṃyogau= adhi tvam vibhāgasya tad ārambakasya karmaṇaḥ sva āśrayasya deśa antara prāptim akṛtvā paryavasāna abhāvāt nanu etat api sādhya samam yat saṃyoga mātreṇa vibhāga nivṛttiḥ iti tatra āha saṃyukta pratyaya vat iti yathā saṃyukta pratyayaḥ ciram anuvartate na evam sva āśrayasya deśa antara saṃyoge bhūte vibhakta pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ asti atas tasya saṃyoga mātreṇa eva nivṛttiḥ iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti 
NK_148.5–148.6	 kvacid ca āśraya vināśāt api vināśaḥ katham iti ajñasya praśnaḥ uttaram yadā iti dvi tantuka kāraṇasya tantoḥ avayave aṃśau karmaā utpannam aṃśvantara antasyaṃśoḥ vibhāgam ārabhate yadā tadā eva tantu antare api karma vibhāgāt ca aṃśoḥ tantu ārambhaka sṃyoga vinācaḥ yadā tadā tantu karmanā tantu antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin kāle vibhāgāt tantvoḥ saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin= eva kālem aśvoḥ saṃyoga vināśāt tad ā ārabdhasya tantoḥ vināśaḥ tasmin= tantau vinaṣṭe tad āśritasya tantu antara vibhāgasya vināśaḥ tatrā aśraya vināśaḥ kāraṇam anyasya vināśa hetoḥ abhāvāt 
NK_149.1–149.2	 evam tarhi uttara vibhāga anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ kāraṇa vibhāga abhāvāt tatas pradeśa antara saṃyogavati saṃyoga abhāvaḥ iti atas virodhi guṇa asambhavāt karmaṇaḥ kāla antara avasthāyi tvam nitya dravya samavetasya ca nitya tvam iti doṣaḥ katham yat ā api advyaṇuka ārambhake paramāṇau karna utpannam aṇu anyarāt vibhāgam karoti tadā eva aṇu antare api karma tatas yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tadā eva aṇu antara karmaṇā dvi aṇukāṇvoḥ vibhāgaḥ kriyate tatas yasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt dvi aṇuka anusaṃyogasya vināśaḥ tasmin= eva kāle saṃoga vināśāt dvi aṇukasya vināśaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe tad āśritasya dvi aṇuka aṇu vibhāgasya vināśaḥ tatas ca virodhi guṇa asambhavān nitya dravya samaveta karmaṇaḥ nitya tvam iti 
NK_149.3–149.4	 tantu aṃśu antara vibhāgāt vibhāgaḥ iti adoṣaḥ āśraya vināśāt tantvoḥ eva vibhāgaḥ vinā aṣṭaḥ na tantu aṃśu antara vibhāgaḥ iti etasmāt uttaraḥ vibhāgaḥ jāyate aṅguli ākāśa vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa vibhāga vat tasmin nu karma saṃyogam kṛtvā vinaśyati iti adoṣaḥ athavā aṃśvantara vibhāga utpatti sama kālam tasmin eva tantau karma utpadyate tatas m aśvantara vibhāgāt tantu ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tantu karmaṇā ca tantu antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas saṃyoga vināśāt tantu vināśaḥ tad vināśāt ca tad āśritayoḥ vibhāga karmaṇoḥ yugapad vināśaḥ 
NK_149.5–149.6	 tantu vīraṇayoḥ vā saṃyoge sati dravya an utpatau pūrva uktena vidhānena āśraya vināśa saṃyogābhyām tantu vīraṇa vibhāga vināśaḥ iti atra punar vibhāgaḥ sa kriyasya tantra ākāśa ādi deśena samam vibhāga ja vibhāgaḥ na utpadyate kāraṇasya tantvoḥ vibhāgasya abhāvāt yadi uttaraḥ vibhāgaḥ na saṃvṛttaḥ tatas kim tatra āha tatas iti tatas uttara vibhāga anutpādāt prāktanasya tantu ākāśa saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya anivṛtteḥ sa kriyasya tanyoḥ pradeśa antareṇa saha saṃyogaḥ na bhavati atas kāraṇāt virodhinaḥ guṇasya uttara saṃyogasya abhāvāt karmaṇaḥ kāla antara avasthāti tvam syāt yāvat āśraya vināśaḥ vināśa hetuḥ na upanipatati nitya dravya samavetasya ca nitya tvam iti doṣaḥ 
NK_149.7	 katham iti praśnaḥ uttaram āha yadā iti āpya dvi aṇukasya ārambhake paramāṇau karma utpannamaṇu antarāt vibhāgam karoti yadā tadā eva dvi aṇuka saṃyoginī ana ārambhaka paramāṇu antare api karma tatas yasmin kāle paramāṇvoḥ vibhāgāḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tadā eva aṇu karmaṇā dvi aṇukāṇvaḥ vubhāgaḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle dvi aṇu kāṇvoḥ vibhāgāt dvi aṇukāṇvoḥ saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle paramāṇvoḥ saṃyoga nivāśāt tad ā ārabdhasya dvi aṇukasya vināśaḥ tasmin dvi aṇuke vinaṣṭe tad āśritasya dvi aṇuka aṇu vibhāgasya vināśaḥ tatas vibhāgasya kāraṇasya abhāvāt paramāṇoḥ ākāśa deśa vibhāgām utpāde pūrva saṃyoga anivṛttau= uttara saṃyogasya virodhi guṇasya vināśa hetoḥ asambhavān nitya paramāṇu samavetasya karmaṇaḥ nitya tvam syāt 
NK_149.8–149.9	 pūrva uktam tāvat pariharati tantu aṃśu antara vibhāgāt vibhāgaḥ iti adoṣaḥ kārya āviṣṭe kāraṇe karma utpannam avayava antareṇa samam svāśrasya vibhāgam kurvat ākāśa ādi deśāt vibhāgam na karoti iti nityamaḥ ākāśa ādi deśa vibhāga kartṛ tvasya viśiṣṭa vibhāga anārambhaka tvena vyāpta tvāt avayava antarasya avayavena sva āśraya saṃyoginā samam tu karoti eva virodha abhāvāt atas dvi tantuka kāraṇe tanttau karma utpannam tantu antarāt vibhāda sama kālam tad aṃśunā api tantu saṃyuktena samam vibhāgam ārabhate sa ca vibhāgaḥ tantoḥ aṃśoḥ ca avasthaa ūnādavasthitaḥ iti āha āśraya vināśāt tantvoḥ eva vibhāgaḥ vinaṣṭaḥ tantu aṃśu antara vibhāgaḥ tu avasthitaḥ iti 
NK_149.10	 kim atas yadi evam iti atas āha etasmāt iti aṅguli ākāśa vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa vibhāga vat yathā karma jāt aṅguluyākāśa vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa vibhāgaḥ evam karma jāt aṃśu tantu vibhāgāt tantu ākāśa vibhāgaḥ iti udāharaṇa arthaḥ hasta ākāśa vibhāgāt śarīra ākāśa vibhāgaḥ yuktaḥ na tu aṅguli ākāśa vibhāgāt aṅguleḥ śarīram pratyakāraṇa tvāt iti ced hastaḥ api bāhoḥ āśrayaḥ na śarīrasya kutas tad vibhāgāt api śarīra vibhāgaḥ atha samasta avayava vyāpi tvāt śarīrasya hastaḥ api āśrayaḥ evam aṅgulī api aśrayaḥ hasta aṅgulī ādi avayava samudāye śarīra pratyabhijñānāt tasmin= tantu ākāśa vibhāge jāte pūrva saṃyogasya pratibandhakasya nivṛttau tantu samavetam karma uttara saṃyogam kṛtvā tatas vinaśyati iti āha tasmin iti 
NK_149.11	 prakāra antareṇa api āśraya vināśāt vināśam kathayati athavā iti saṃśvantara vibhāga utpatti sama kālam tasmin= eva tantau vibhajyamāna avayave karma utpadyate tatas vibhāgāt tantu ārambhakasya aṃśu saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tantu karmaṇā ca tasya tastoḥ tantu antarāt vibhāgaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas tad anantaram saṃyogasya vināśāt tadā ātabdhasya tantoḥ vināśaḥ tad vināśāt ca tad āśritayoḥ vibhāga karmaṇoḥ yugapad vināśaḥ yat ca nitya samavetasya nitya tvam iti coditam tatra pratisamādhānam na uktam tasyāt yat tam asaṅga tā artha tvāt kārya āviṣṭe hi kāraṇe karma utpannam avayava antara vibhāga sama kālam ākāśa ādi deśena samam vibhāgam na karoti iti ākāśa ādi vibhāga kartṛ tvasya dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga virodhi vibhāga utpādaka tvasya ca virodhāt anārambhake tu dvi aṇuka saṃyogini paramāṇau karma dvi aṇuka vibhāga sama kālam tasya ākāśa deśena samam cibhāgam karoti eva tatas vibhāgāt ca paramāṇoḥ ākāśa saṃyoga nivṛttau= uttara saṃyoge sati tad āśritasya karmaṇaḥ vināśaḥ bhavati eva 
NK_149.12	 samāna jātīya saṃyoge sati dravya utpattau= āśraya vināśāt vibhāga karmaṇoḥ vināśaḥ kathitaḥ samprati vijātīya saṃyoge dravya anutpattau saṃyoga āśraya vināśābhyām vibhāga vinācam kathayati tantu vīraṇayoḥ vā saṃyoge sati dravya anutpattau pūrva uktena vidhānena iti tantu ārambhaka aṃśau karma utpatti sama kālam vīraṇe api karma tatas m aśukriyayā aṃśvantarāt vibhāgaḥ vīraṇa karmaṇā ca tasya vibhajyamāna avayavena tantunā ākāśa deśena ca samam vibhagaḥ kriyate tatomaḥ aśu vibhāgāt aṃśu saṃyoga vināśaḥ vīraṇa vibhāgāt ca tantu vīraṇa saṃyogasya ākāśa vīraṇa saṃyogasya ca vināśaḥ tatas m aśu saṃyoga viṇaśāt tantu vināśaḥ vīraṇasya ca uttara saṃyogaḥ tata uttara saṃyoga āśraya vināśābhyām tantu vīraṇa vibhāgasya vināśaḥ iti prakriyā 
NK_150.1–150.3	 paratvam aparatvam ca para apara abhidhāna pratyaya nimittam tat dvividham diś kṛtam kāla kṛtam ca tatra diś kṛtam diś viśeṣa pratyāyakam kāla kṛtam ca vayaḥ bheda pratyāyakam tatra dikkṛtasya utpattiḥ abhidhīyate katham ekasyām diśi avasthitayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ saṃyukta saṃyoga bahu alpa bhāve sati ekasya draṣṭuḥ sannikṛṣṭam avadhim kṛtvā etasmāt viprakṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti paratva ādhāre asannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas tām apekṣya pareṇa diś pradeśena saṃyogāt pratvaya utpattiḥ viprakṛṣṭam ca avardhim kṛtvā itarasmin sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas tām apekṣya apareṇa diś pradeṣena saṃyogāt aparatvasya utpattiḥ 
NK_150.4–150.5	 paratvam aparatvam ca para apara abhidhāna pratyaya nimittam iti param iti abhidhānasya pratyayasya ca nimittam paratvam aparam iti abhidhāna pratyayayoḥ nimittam aparatvam iti kāryeṇa sattām pratipādayati yadi api ākāśam kaṇṭha ādi ākāśa saṃyoga ādikam ca parāpara abhidhānayoḥ kāraṇam bhavati yadi api ātma manaḥ saṃyoga dikam ca parāpara pratīti kāraṇā syāt tathā api nimitta antara siddhiḥ viśiṣṭa pratyayasya asādhāraṇa kāraṇam antareṇa utpatti abhāvāt ekatra dvyoḥ upanyāsaḥ tayoḥ itaretara sāpekṣa tvāt 
NK_150.6	 atat dvividham a atat a paratvam aparatvam ca advividham a dvi prakāram iti bheda nirūpaṇam kiṃkṛtaḥ tayoḥ bhedaḥ iti āśaṅkya kāraṇa bhedāt bhedam āha diś kṛtam kāla kṛtam ca iti diś piṇḍa saṃyoga kṛtam dikkṛtam kāla piṇḍa saṃyoga kṛtam kāla kṛtam anayoḥ bhedaḥ kutas pratyetavyaḥ kārya bhedāt iti āha diś kṛtam diś viśeṣa pratyāyakam kāla kṛtam tu vayaḥ bheda pratyayāyakam diś kṛtam paratvam deśa viprakṛṣṭa tvam pratyāyati iti aparatvam ca deśa sannikṛṣṭa tvam kāla kṛtam tu paratvam piṇḍasya kāla viprakṛṣṭa tvam pratipādayati aparatvam ca kāla sannikṛṣṭtvam iti viśeṣaḥ 
NK_150.7^1	 tatra tayoḥ dikkṛta kāla kṛtayoḥ madhye dikkṛtasya utpattiḥ abhidhīyate katham iti praśne sati uttaram āha ekasyām iti pūrva apara diśi avasthitayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ parāpara pratyayau na sambhavataḥ tad artham ekasyām diśi avasthitayoḥ iti uktam ekasyām diśi prācyām vā pratīcyām vā vasthitayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ madhye ekasya draṣṭuḥ saṃyuktena bhūdeśena samāparasya pradeśasya saṃyogaḥ tena api samam aparasya iti saṃyukta saṃyogānām bahu tve alpa tve ca sati alpa saṃyogavantam piṇḍam sannikṛṣṭam avadhim kṛtvā etasmāt piṇḍāt viprakṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti saṃyoga bhūyaḥ tu avati bhaviṣyataḥ paratvasya ādhāre piṇḍe viprakṛṣṭā buddhiḥ udeti 
NK_150.7^2	 tatas viprakṛṣṭa buddhi utpatti anantaram tām viprakṛṣṭām buddhim apekṣya pareṇa saṃyoga bhūyaḥ tvavatā diś pradeśena saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt viprakṛṣṭe piṇḍe samavāyi kāraṇa bhūte paratvasya utpattiḥ draṣṭuḥ sva śarīra apekṣayā saṃyukta saṃyoga bhūyaḥ tvavantam viprakṛṣṭam ca avadhim kṛtvā itarasmin saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu avati sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ udeti tām sannikṛṣṭām buddhim nimitta kāraṇīkṛtya apareṇa saṃyukta saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu aviśiṣṭena diś pradeśena saha saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt sannikṛṣṭe piṇḍe samavāyi kāraṇe paratvasya utpattiḥ 
NK_150.8	 sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa buddhyoḥ paraspara pekṣa tvāt ubhaya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na anabhyupagamāt na sannikṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti evam pratītya eva tad apekṣayā viprakṛṣṭa buddhiḥ na api viprakṛṣṭaḥ ayam iti pratītya eva tad apekṣayā sannikṛṣṭa buddhi udayaḥ kintu saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu asahacaritam piṇḍam pratītya eva tad apekṣayā saṃyoga bhūyaḥ tu avati viprakṛṣṭa buddhiḥ evam saṃyoga bhūyaḥ tu asahacaritam piṇḍam pratītya eva tad apekṣayā saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu avati sannikṛṣṭa buddhi utpattiḥ iti na paraspara apekṣa tvam anayoḥ 
NK_151.1–151.2	 kāla kṛtayoḥ api katham vartamāna kālayoḥ aniyata diggeśa saṃyuktayoḥ yuvastha virayaḥ rūḍha śmaśru kārkaśyavali palita ādi sānnidhye sati ekasya draṣṭuḥ yuvānam avadhim kṛtvā sthavire viprakṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas tām apekṣya pareṇa kāla pradeśena saṃyogāt paratvasya utpattiḥ sthaviram ca avadhim kṛtvā yūni sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas tām apekṣya apareṇa kāla pradeśena saṃyogāt aparatvasya utpattiḥ iti vināśaḥ tu apekṣā buddhi saṃyoga dravya vināśāt 
NK_151.3	 apekṣā buddhi vināśāt tāvat utpanne paratve yasmin eva kāle sāmānya buddhiḥ utpannā bhavati tatas apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā sāmānya jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ paratva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyam āna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ guṇa buddheḥ ca utpattiḥ tatas apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vinaśyattā guṇa jñāna tad sambandhebhyaḥ dravya buddheḥ utpadyam āna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya buddheḥ utpattiḥ guṇasya vināśaḥ iti 
NK_151.4	 saṃyoga vināśāt api katham apekṣā buddhi sama kālam eva paratva ādhāre karma utpadyate tena karmaṇā diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate apekṣā buddhitaḥ paratvasya utpattiḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas sāmānya buddheḥ utpattiḥ diś piṇḍa saṃyogasya ca vināśaḥ tatas yasmin kāle paratva guṇa buddhiḥ utpadyate tasmin= eva kāle diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśāt guṇasya vināśaḥ 
NK_151.5–151.6^1	 drayva vināśāt api katham paratva ādhāra avayave karma utpannam yasmin kāle avayava antarāt vibhāgam karoti tasmin eva kāle apekṣā buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas vibhāgāt yasmin eva kāle saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin eva kale paratvam utpadyate tatas saṃyoga nivāśāt dravya vināśaḥ dravya nāśāt ca tad āśritasya guṇasya vināśaḥ kāla kratayoḥ api katham dikkṛtayoḥ tāvat paratva aparatvayoḥ utpattiḥ kathitāḥ kāla kṛtayoḥ api tayoḥ utpattiḥ katham iti praśnaḥ samādhānam vartamāna kālayoḥ iti dvayoḥ ekasmin vā piṇḍe avidyamāne paratva aparatve na bhavataḥ tad artham vartamāna kālayoḥ iti uktam 
NK_151.6^2	 aniyata diś deśayoḥ iti eka diśi avadiśi avasthitayaḥ anya diś ava sthitayoḥ vā yuvastha virayaḥ rūḍha śmaśyu ca valiḥ ca paliḥ ca palitam ca teṣām kāla viprakarṣa liṅgānām sānnidhye sati ekasya draṣṭuḥ yuvānam rūḍha śamaśru kārka śyā ādya bhāva anumitam alpa utpatti kālam arva adham kṛtvā rūḍha śmaśru vali palita ādimati sthavire viprakṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tām apekṣya pareṇa āditya parivartana bhūyaḥ tvavatā kāla pradeśena sa ayogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt tasmin eva sthavire paratvasya utpattiḥ sthaviram ca arvādham kṛtvā yūni sannikṛṣṭā buddhiḥ utpadyate tām buddhim apekṣya apareṇa alpa āditya parivartana upalakṣitena kāla pradeśena saṃyogāt aparatvasya utpattiḥ yuvasthavira śarīrayoḥ kāla saṃyoga alpīyaḥ tu abhūyaḥ tve śarīra santāna apekṣayā na tu vyakti viṣaya tvena tayoḥ pratikṣaṇam vināśāt 
NK_151.7	 kṛtakasya avaśyam vināśaḥ sa ca nirhetukaḥ na bhavati iti paratva aparatvayoḥ vināśa hetum āha vināśaḥ tu iti paratva aparatvayoḥ vināśaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśāt saṃyoga vināśāt dravya vināśāt dravya pekṣā buddhyoḥ vināśāt dravya saṃyogayoḥ vināśāt saṃyoga apekṣā buddhyoḥ vināśāt apekṣā buddhi saṃyoga dravyāṇām vināśāt iti saptavidhaḥ vinā śakram 
NK_151.8^1	 apekṣā buddhi vināśāt tāvat vināśaḥ kathyate utpanne paratve yasmin= eva kāle paratva sāmānye buddhiḥ utpannā bhavati tatas iti saptamī arthe sārvavibhaktikaḥ tasiliti tasit etasmin eva kāle apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyattā vināśa kāraṇa sānnidhyam syāt sāmānya jñāna tad sambandhemyaḥ paratva sāmānyam ca paratva sāmānya jñānam ca pararva guṇa sambandhaḥ ca tebhyaḥ paratva guṇa buddheḥ utpadyamāna tā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ paratva sāmān yat jānam eva apekṣā buddhi vināśa kāraṇam guṇa buddheḥ ca utpatti kāraṇam atas tad utpādaḥ eva apekṣā buddheḥ vinaśyatā guṇa buddheḥ ca utpadyamāna tā syāt 
NK_151.8^2	 tatas kṣaṇa antare apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ paratva guṇa buddheḥ ca utpādaḥ tatas tasmāt apekṣā buddhi vināśāt guṇasya vinaśyatā guṇaḥ ca guṇa jñānam ca tad sambandhaḥ ca tebhyaḥ dravya buddheḥ utpadyam ānatā iti ekaḥ kālaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ guṇa vināśasya kāraṇam guṇa buddhiḥ ca dravya buddheḥ kāraṇam apekṣā buddhi vināśa guṇa buddhi utpādau ca yugapad syātām atas guṇasya vinaśyattā dravya buddheḥ ca utpadyamāna tā api yugapad syāt tatas paratva viśiṣṭa dravya buddheḥ utpādaḥ paratva guṇasya ca vināśaḥ 
NK_151.9	 saṃyoga vināśāt api katham paratva aparatvayoḥ vināśaḥ iti praśne kṛte satyāha apekṣā buddhi sama kālam eva paratvasya ādhāre piṇḍe karma utpadyate kṣaṇa antare tena karmaṇā diśaḥ paratva ādhārasya ca piṇḍasya vibhāgaḥ kriyate apekṣā buddheḥ ca paratvasya utpattiḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas utpanne paratve paratva sāmānya buddheḥ utpatiḥ diś piṇḍa saṃyogasya ca vibhāgāt vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin kāle sāmānya jñānāt guṇa buddhiḥ utpadyate tasmin eva kāle diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ na apekṣā buddhi vināśāt apekṣā biddhiḥ api tadā animeva vināśāt 
NK_151.10	 dravya vināśāt api katham vināśaḥ iti āha paratva ādhāra avayavaḥ iti bhaviṣyataḥ paratvasya ādhāraḥ dravyam tasya avayave karma utpannam yadā avayava antarāt vibhāgam karoti tasmin eva kāle apekṣā buddhiḥ utpadyate tatas vibhāgāt yasmin eva kāle dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle apekṣā buddheḥ paratvam utpadyate tatas saṃyoga vināśāt dravya vināśaḥ tatas dravya vināśāt tad āśritasya guṇasya vināśa āha tadānīm eva paratva sāmānyat jānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ āśraya vināśāt ca diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ iti anayoḥ na hetu tvam sahabhāvi tvāt 
NK_152.1	 dravya apekṣā buddhyoḥ yugapad vināśāt api katham yadā pratva ādhāra avayave karma utpadyate tadā eva apekṣā buddhiḥ utpadyate karmaṇā ca avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate paratvasya utpattiḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin= eva kāle avayava vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin= eva kāle sāmānya buddhiḥ utpadyate tad anantaram saṃyoga vināśāt dravya vināśaḥ sāmānya buddheḥ ca apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya apekṣā buddhyoḥ vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ 
NK_152.2	 dravya apekṣā buddhyoḥ yugapad vināśāt api katham yadā eva paratva ādhāra avayave karma utpadyate tadā eva apekṣā buddhiḥ utpadyate karmaṇā ca avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate paratvasya utpattiḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin kāle avayava vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin eva kāle paratva sāmānya jñānam utpadyate tad anantaram saṃyoga vināśāt dravya vināśaḥ sāmānya buddheḥ ca apekṣā buddheḥ api iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas dravya apekṣā buddhyoḥ vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ pratyekam anyatra ubhayoḥ api vināśam prati kāraṇatva prati iti iha ca anyatara viśeṣa an avadhāraṇāt ubhayoḥ api vināśam prati kāraṇa tvam 
NK_153.1	 dravya saṃyoga vināśāt api katham yadā paratva ādhāra avayave karma utpannam avayava antarāt vibhāgam karoti tasmin eva kāle piṇḍa karma apekṣā buddhyoḥ yugapad utpattiḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle paratvasya utpattiḥ tasmin eva kāle vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ piṇḍa karmaṇā ca diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle sāmānya buddhiḥ utpadyate tasmin eva kāle dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt piṇḍa vināśaḥ vināśāt ca piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ tatas guṇa buddhi sama kālam piṇḍa saṃyogayoḥ vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ 
NK_153.2	 saṃyoga apekṣā buddhyoḥ yugapad vināśāt api katham yadā paratvam utpadyate tadā eva paratva ādhāre karma tatas yasmin eva kāle paratva sāmānya jñānam utpadyate tasmin eva kāle piṇḍa karmaṇā diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate tatas sāmānya buddhitaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ vibhāgāt ca diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas saṃyoga apekṣā buddhi vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ 
NK_153.3	 trayāṇām samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta kāraṇānām yugapad vināśāt api katham yadā apekṣā buddhiḥ utpadyate tadā eva piṇḍa avayave api karma tatas yasmin eva kāle karmaṇā avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate paratvasya ca utpattiḥ tasmin eva kāle piṇḍe api karma tatas avayava vibhāgāt piṇḍa ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ piṇḍa karmaṇā ca diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate sāmānya buddhiḥ ca utpattiḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas saṃyoga vināśāt piṇḍa vināśaḥ vibhāgāt ca diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti etat sarvam yugapad trayāṇām samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta kāraṇānām vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ iti 
NK_153.4	 dravya saṃyoga vināśāt api ityādi dravya saṃyoga vināśāt api katham vināśaḥ yadā paratva ādhāra avayave karma utpannam avayava antarāt vibhāgam karoti tasmin= eva kāle piṇḍa karma apekṣā buddhyoḥ yugapad utpattiḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle paratvasya utpattiḥ tasmin eva kāle avayava vibhāgāt dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ piṇḍa karmaṇā ca diśaḥ piṇḍasya ca vibhāgaḥ kriyate iti ekaḥ kālāḥ tatas yasmin eva kāle sāmānya buddhiḥ utpadyate tasmin eva kāle dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt piṇḍa vināśaḥ diś piṇḍa vibhāgāt ca diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ tatas guṇa buddhi sama kālam piṇḍa dikpiṇḍa saṃyoga vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ tu na kāraṇam tadānīm eva sāmānya buddheḥ tasya bhāvāt 
NK_153.5	 saṃyoga apekṣā buddhyoḥ yugapad vināśāt api katham yadā paratvam utpadyate tadā eva paratvasya ādhāre dravye karma tatas yasmin kāle para sva sāmānya jñānam utpadyate paratvasya ādhāre tasmin eva kāle piṇḍa karmaṇā diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate tatas sāmānya jñānāt apekṣā buddhi vināśaḥ diś piṇḍa vibhāgāt ca diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tatas saṃyoga apekṣā buddhi vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ dravya vināśaḥ tu tadānīm na asti eva iti na tasya hetu tvam 
NK_153.6	 trayāṇām samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta kāraṇānām yugapad vināśāt api katham samavāyi cāsamavāyi ca nimittam ca samavāyi asamavāyi nimittāni tāni ca kāraṇāni ca iti saṃvāyya samavāyi nimitta kāraṇāni dravya saṃyoga apekṣā jñānāni teṣām trayāṇām yugapad vināśāt katham paratvasya vināśaḥ iti praśne kṛte sati uttaram āha yadā iti yadā apekṣā buddhiḥ utpadyate tadā eva piṇḍa avayave api karma tatas yasmin= eva kāle karmaṇā avayava antarāt vibhāgaḥ kriyate apekṣā buddheḥ ca paratvasya utpattiḥ tasmin eva kāle piṇḍepi karma tatas avayava vibhāgāt piṇḍa ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśaḥ piṇḍa karmaṇā ca diś piṇḍa vibhāgaḥ kriyate sāmānya buddheḥ ca utpattiḥ iti ekaḥ kālaḥ tadā arambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt piṇḍa vināśaḥ vibhāgāt ca diś piṇḍa saṃyoga vināśaḥ sāmānya jñānāt ca apekṣā buddheḥ vināśaḥ iti etat sarvam yugapad bhavati kāraṇa yaugapadyāt tatas ca trayāṇām samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta kāraṇānām vināśāt paratvasya vināśaḥ iti paratvasya vināśaḥ iti upalakṣaṇam idam aparatvasya api ayam eva vināśa kramaḥ darśayitavyaḥ 
NK_154.1–154.4^1	 buddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ jñānam pratyayaḥ iti paryāyāḥ sā ca aneka prakārāḥ artha anantyāt prati artha niyata tvāt ca buddhi je paratva aparatve iti samarthite atha kā iyam buddhiḥ iti āha buddhiḥ ityādi pradhānasya vikāraḥ mahat ākhyam antaḥkaraṇam citta apara pararyāyam buddhiḥ buddheḥ indriya praṇālikayā bāhya viṣaya uparaktāyāḥ tad ākāra upasaṃgrahavatī sattva guṇa āśrayā vṛtti jñānam prāpta viṣaya ākāra upagrahāyām buddhau pratibimbitāyāḥ cetanā śakteḥ tad vṛtti anukāraḥ upalabdhaḥ 
NK_154.1–154.4^2	 tathā ca āha sma bhagavān patañjaliḥ apariṇāminī hi bhoktṛ śaktiḥ apratisaṅkramā ca pariṇāminī arthe pratisaṃkrāntā iva tad vṛttim anubhavati iti iti bhoktṛ śaktiḥ iti citi śaktiḥ ucyate sā ca ātmā eva pariṇāminī arthaḥ iti buddhi tattve pratisaṅkrāntā iva iti pratibimtā iva iti arthaḥ tad vṛttim anubhavati buddhau pratibimbitā satī buddhi= chāyā āpattyā buddhi vṛtti anukāriṇībhavati iti arthaḥ buddheḥ viṣayaḥ sukha ādi ākāraḥ pratyayaḥ tathā ca āha saḥ eva bhagavān śuddhe api puruṣaḥ pratyayam bauddham anupaśyati anupaśyan= atadātmā api tad ātmakaḥ iva pratyavabhāsate iti 
NK_154.5–154.6	 etat sāṃkhya matam nirākartum āha buddhiḥ ityādi yasyāḥ amī paryāya śabdāḥ sā buddhiḥ yā punar iyam prakriyā upadarśitā sā prati iti abhāvāt eva parāṇudyate viṣaya hāna upādāna anuguṇam utpāda vyaya dharmakam ekam tat adhikaraṇam ca aparam yasya tad utpādāt pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām iti ubhayam pratyātmam anubhūyate na prakārāni aram yā ca asyāḥ buddheḥ vṛttiḥ sā kim buddheḥ anyāḥ ananyā vaḥ na tau adanyā vṛtti vṛtti matoḥ aikāntika tāda ātmya abhyupagamāt atha ananyā tadā buddheḥ eka tve viṣaya ākāravatīnām tad vṛttīnām api eka tvāt tri catur ādi pratyayaḥ durlabhaḥ paraspara vilakṣaṇa ākāra saṃvedana abhāvāt buddhi ārūḍha ākāra mātra vedi tvāt ca puruṣasya yathā uktam abuddheḥ pratisaṃvīdī puruṣaḥ a iti vṛttīnām vā nānātve buddheḥ api nānātvāt ekatva vyāghātaḥ iti ādikam dūṣaṇa m ūhyam 
NK_154.7	 buddheḥ bhedam nirūpayati sā ca aneka prakāra iti atra kāraṇam āha artha ānantyāt iti yadi nāma arthasya viṣayasya ananta tvam buddheḥ anekavidha tve kim āyātam tatra āha pratyartha niyata tvāt ca iti pratyartham prativiṣayam asmad ādi buddhayaḥ niyatāḥ arthāḥ ca anantā iti pratyekam tatra niyatāḥ buddhayaḥ api anantāḥ yat api kvacid aneka artha viṣayam ekam vijñānam tat api tāvat artha viyata tvāt tad arthāt vijñāna antarāt vilakṣaṇam eva iti adoṣaḥ 
NK_155.1–155.3	 tasyāḥ sati api anekavidha tve samāsayaḥ dve vidhe vidyā ca avidyā ca iti tatra avidyā caturvidhāḥ saṃśaya viparyaya anadhyavasāya svapna lakṣaṇā buddheḥ viṣaya bhedena sati api bhede saṃkṣepataḥ dvaividhyam āha tasyāḥ iti niḥsandigdha ābādhita adhyavasāya ātmikā pratītiḥ vidyā tad viparītā ca avidyā iti artha pratipādana mātrasya vivakṣita tvāt paścāt uddiṣṭām api avidyām prathamam kathayati tatra iti tayoḥ vidyā vidyayoḥ madhye avidyā caturvidhā catuṣprakārā saṃśaya viparyaya anadhyavasāya svapna lakṣaṇā 
NK_155.4	 nanu avidyā caturvidhā iti parisaṃkhyāna anupapattiḥ rūḍhasya tarka jñānasya api sambhavāt anubhūyate hi antarā saṃśayam nirṇayam ca tarkaḥ tathā hi utpatti dharmakaḥ ātmā iti eke anutpatti dharmakaḥ iti apare tatas vipratipatteḥ kiṃsvidayam utpatti dharmā āhosvit evam na bhavati iti saṃśaye vicāra ātmakaḥ tarkaḥ pravartate yadi ayam utpatti dharmakaḥ tadā ekasya aneka śarīra ādi saṃyoga lakṣaṇaḥ saṃsāraḥ tad atyanta vimokṣaṇaḥ ca apavargaḥ na upapadyate anutpatti dharmake tu jñātari syātām saṃsāra apavargau iti anutpatti dharmakeṇa anena bhavitavyam iti 
NK_155.5–155.9^1	 kim asya sambhāvanā pratyayasya prayojanam tattva jñānam eva pratipakṣa niścaya vat pratipakṣa saṃśaye api hi hetoḥ apravṛttiḥ eva vastunaḥ dvairūpya abhāvāt yathā āhuḥ bhaṭṭa miśrāḥ yāvat ca avyatireki tvam śataṃśena api śaṅkyate vipakṣasya kutas tāvat hetoḥ gamanikā balam iti anena tu utpatti dharmaka tvam vyudasya anutpatti dharmaka tvam sambhāvayatā viṣaye vivecite satya sat pratipakṣa tvāt anumānam pravartate iti viṣaya vivecana dvāreṇa pramā anugrāhaka tayā tarkaḥ tattva jñānāya ghaṭate pramāṇasya karaṇasya karaṇa tvena iti kartavyatā sthānīya tarka sahāyasya eva sva kārye paryavasānāt 
NK_155.5–155.9^2	 na hi anapekṣita dṛḍha muṣṭi pīḍitaḥ jālmakara pañjara udare viluṭhan= api kaṭhora dhāraḥ kuṭhāraḥ pratitiṣṭhati aniṣṭhurasya api kāṣṭhasya chedāya tathā ca uktam na hi tad karaṇam loke vede vā kiñcid at īdṛśam itikartavya tā sādhye tasya na anugraherthitāḥ iti yadi punar evam tarkaḥ na iṣyate parasya āviṣṭa āpādana rūpaḥ prasaṅgaḥ api na abhyupagantavyaḥ syāt sa hi tarkān atiricyamāna ātmā asti ca vaiśeṣikāṇām api prasaṅgaḥ na prasaṅgaḥ hetuḥ āśraya asiddha tā ādi doṣāt 
NK_156.1	 atra ucyate kim para pakṣa abhāva pratītiḥ tarkaḥ kim vā sva pakṣa sambhāvanā ādye pakṣe pramāṇam eva idam jñātuḥ a nitya tve saṃsāra apavargayoḥ asaṃbhavaḥ iti jñānam yadi apramāṇam na asmāt vipakṣa abhāva siddiḥ apramāṇena kasyacid arthasya siddheḥ ayogāt iti atra anumānasya apravrptiḥ eva viṣaya viveka abhāvāt atha siddhi ati asmāt vipakṣa abhāvaḥ tadā pramāṇam idam pratyakṣa ādiṣu kasmiṃścid antar bhaviṣyati tad vyatirekeṇa anyasya pratīti sādhana abhāva āditya kāmena abhyupagantavyam prasaṅgaḥ api virodha udbhāvanam tat ca kasyacid balīyasaḥ viparīta pramāṇasyo padarśanam kaḥ tatra viparītāt pramāṇāt tad upadarśakāt ca vacanāt anyaḥ tarkaḥ 
NK_156.2–156.3	 atha sva pakṣa sambhāvana ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ tarkaḥ asya utpattau kim kāraṇam na tāvat sva pakṣa sādhakam pramāṇam tasya apravṛtteḥ tarkeṇa vivecite viṣaye sva pakṣa sādhakam pravartate tat eva yadi tasya kāraṇam su vyaktam anyonya āśraya tvam vipakṣa abhāve pratīte sva pakṣa sambhāvanā upajāyate iti vipakṣa abhāva pratītiḥ asya kāraṇam iti ced 
NK_156.4	 tarhi vipakṣa abhāva pratīti liṅgakam anumānam eva etat paraspara viruddhayoḥ eka pratiṣedhasya itara vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt bhavati evam yadi viṣayam avadhārayati evam eva idam iti anujānātyayam ekatara dharmam na tu avadhārayati na ca ayam saṃśayaḥ api ubhaya koṭi saṃsparśa abhāvāt kintu saṃśayāt pracyuti nirṇayam ca aprāptaḥ sambhāvanā pratyayaḥ anyaḥ eva tathā ca loke vaktaraḥ bhavanti evam aham tarkayāmi iti na yogyatā avadhāraṇāt yatra vipakṣa abhāvaḥ tatra anyatara pakṣa upapattiḥ yatra tu tasya sambhavaḥ tatra anupapattiḥ iti anvaya vyatireka darśī vipakṣa abhāvam pratipadyamānaḥ sambhāvayati ayam anutpatti dharma ko bhaviṣyati iti asmin arthe pramāṇam etat pratipādanāya yogyaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti pramāṇa yogya tām viṣayasya adhyavasyati iti anumānam eva ittham eva ca pramāṇam anugṛhṇāti yogya tā pratīteḥ pramāṇa pravṛtti hetu tvāt anyathā punar idam sambhāvanā mātram anarthakam eva svayam apramāṇasya siddhi upalambhayoḥ anaṅga tvāt viṣaya vivekasya api vipakṣa abhāvam pratipādayatā bādhaka pramāṇena eva kṛta tvāt 
NK_157.1–157.3	 saṃśayaḥ tāvat prasiddha aneka viśeṣayoḥ sādṛśya mātra darśanāt ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt adharmāt ca kiṃsvid iti ubhaya avalambī vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ anye tu saṃśaya prabhedaḥ eva tarkaḥ anavadhāraṇa ātmaka tvāt iti āhuḥ saṃśayaḥ tāvat tāvat śabdaḥ krama arthaḥ saṃśayaḥ tāvat kathyte ithyate iti arthaḥ prasiddha aneka viśeṣayoḥ iti prasiddhāḥ pūrvam pratītāḥ aneka viśeṣāḥ asādhāraṇa dharmāḥ vakra koṭara ādayaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādayaḥ ca yatoḥ sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ tayoḥ sādṛśya mātrasya sādhāraṇa dharma mātrasya kvacid ekatra dharmiṇi darśanāt ubhayoḥ sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ viśeṣāṇām vakra koṭara ādīnām śiraḥ pāṇi ādīnām ca pūrva pratītānām smaraṇāt adharmāt ca kiṃsvid iti ubhaya avalambī vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ kim sthāṇuḥ kim vā puruṣaḥ iti anavasthita ubhaya rūpeṇa ubhaya viśeṣa saṃsparśī viruddha artha avamarthaḥ jñāna viśeṣaḥ saṃśayaḥ 
NK_157.4	 sādṛśya mātra darśanāt iti mātra grahaṇa sāmarthyāt viśeṣāṇām anupalambhaḥ gamyate darśana śabdaḥ upalabdhi vacanaḥ na pratyakṣa pratīti vacanaḥ anumeyasya api sāmānyasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt sādṛśya upalambha abhidhānāt dharmī upalambhaḥ api labhyate tasya anupalambhe tad dharmasya sādṛśyasya upalambha abhāvāt saṃśayaḥ api ca dharmiṇī eva na sādṛśyā iva na sādṛśye tasya niścita tvāt sādṛśyam iti ca sādhāraṇa dharma mātram kathyate na aneka artha samavetam sādṛśyam asparśavat tvasya sparśa abhāvasya ākāśa antaḥkaraṇa sādhāraṇasya pratīti ātmani aṇu tva mahat tva saṃśaya darśanāt 
NK_157.5	 tat ayam saṃkṣepa arthaḥ yadā ayam pratipatta ubhaya sādhāraṇam dharmam kvacid ekatra dharmiṇī upalabhate kutaścid nimittāt tasya dharmiṇaḥ viśeṣam na upalabhate pūrva pratītayoḥ smarati viruddha viśeṣayoḥ na ca ubhayoḥ ekatra sambhāvayati sadbhāvam viruddha tvāt na api abhāvam tad avinābhūtasya sādhāraṇa dharmasya darśanāt tadā asya sādhāraṇa dharma viṣaya tvena avadhārite dharmiṇi viśeṣa viṣaya tvena anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ saṃśayaḥ bhavati 
NK_157.6	 nanu anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham idam hi pratyayasya pratyaya tvam yat viṣayam avadhārayati na ubhayasya api sambhavāt ayam hi sāmānya viśiṣṭa dhārmi upalambhena dharma viśeṣa anupalambha viruddha ubhaya viśeṣa smaraṇa sahakāriṇā janyamānaḥ ayam iti sāmānya viśiṣṭam dharmiṇam avadhārayan sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti viśeṣam anavadhārayan= anavadhāraṇa ātmakaḥ pratyayaḥ ca syāt dṛṣṭam hi yatra vilakṣaṇā sāmagrī tatra kāryam api vilakṣaṇam eva yathā pratyabhijñānam 
NK_157.7	 saṃśayaḥ api avidyā sā ca aniṣṭā puruṣasya iti adharma kārya tvam tasya darśitam adharmāt ca iti sāmānyam dṛṣṛvā yat ekam viśeṣam anusmṛtya viśeṣa antaram anusmarati tadā sāmānya darśanasya vinaṣṭa tvāt saṃśaya hetutva anupapattiḥ iti ced na ubhaya viśeṣa viṣayābhyām saṃskārābhyām yugapad prabuddhābhyām ubhaya viśeṣa viṣaya eka smaraṇa jananāt tad kāle ca vinaśyat avasthasya sāmānya jñānasya sambhavāt 
NK_158.1–158.4	 sa ca dvividhaḥ antar bahis ca antar tāvat ādeśikasya samyak mithyā ca uddiśya punar ādiśataḥ triṣu kāleṣu saṃśayaḥ bhavati akinnu samyak mithyā va a iti bahis dvividhaḥ pratyakṣa viṣaye ca apratyakṣa viṣaye ca tatra apratyakṣa viṣye tāvat sādhāraṇa liṅga darśanāt ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt adharmāt ca saṃśayaḥ bhavati yathā aṭavyām viṣāṇa mātra darśanāt gauḥ gavayaḥ vā iti 
NK_158.5–158.6	 pratyakṣa viṣaye api sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ ūrdhva tā mātra sādṛśya darśanāt vakra ādi viśeṣa anupalabdhitaḥ sthāṇu tva ādi sāmānya viśeṣa anabhivyaktau= ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt ubhayatra ākṛṣyamāṇasya ātmanaḥ pratyayaḥ dolāyate kim nu khlvayam sthāṇuḥ syāt puruṣaḥ vā iti sa ca dvividhaḥ iti bheda kathanam kena rūpeṇa iti atas āha antar bahis ca iti yaḥ samāna dharma upapatteḥ aneka dharma upapatteḥ vipratipatteḥ upalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ anupalabdhi avyavasthātaḥ ca samāna tāntrikaiḥ pañcavidhaḥ saṃśayaḥ darśitaḥ sa sarvaḥ dvaividhyena eva saṃgṛhītaḥ 
NK_158.7	 antar tāvat ādeśakasya iti ādeśakaḥ jyotiḥ vit tena ekadā kiñcid graha sañcāra ādi nimittam upalabhya ādiṣṭam evam amuketra abhūt varttate bhaviṣyati ca iti tat tathā eva tadā saṃvṛttam anyat ādiṣṭam tat vitatham abhūt punar idārīm tasya utpannam tathābhūtam eva nimittam dṛṣṭvā ādiśatas antar sva jñāne saṃśayaḥ bhavati yat etat mama naimittikam jñānam abhūta tat kim satyam asatyam ca iti 
NK_158.8–158.9	 bahis dvividhaḥ pratyakṣa viṣaye ca apratyakṣa viṣaye ca iti tatra tatoḥ madhye apratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat sādhāraṇa liṅga darśanāt ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt adharmāt ca saṃśayaḥ bhavati yathā aṭavyām viṣāṇa mātra darśanāt gauḥ gavayaḥ vā iti jñāṭa antaritasya piṇḍasya apratyakṣasya sāmānyena viṣāṇa mātra darśana anumitasya saṃśaya viṣaya tvāt apratyakṣa viṣayaḥ ayam saṃśayaḥ 
NK_158.10^1	 pratyakṣa viṣaye api kathayati sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ ityādinā sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ sambandhinī yā ūrdhva tā tanmātrasya pratyakṣa viṣaye puras vartiti dharmiṇi darśanāt vakra ādi viśeṣa anupalabdhitaḥ ityādi padena śiraḥ pāṇi ādi para grahaḥ vakra koṭara ādeḥ sthāṇu dharmasya śiraḥ pāṇi ādeḥ ca viśeṣasya puruṣa dharmasya anupalabdhitaḥ sthāṇu tva ādi sāmānya viśeṣa anabhivyaktau ityādi padena puruṣa tvāt yavarodhaḥ vakra koṭara ādayaḥ sthāṇu tva abhivyakti hetavaḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādayaḥ puruṣa tva abhivyakti hetavaḥ teṣām anupalambhāt 
NK_158.10^2	 sthāṇu tva puruṣa tvayoḥ anabhivyaktau satyām ubhayoḥ sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ pratyekam upalabdhānām viśeṣāṇām aṇu smaraṇāt ubhaya tra ākṛṣyamāṇasya ubhayatra sthāṇau puruṣe vā ākṛṣyamāṇasya pratipattuḥ yadā ūrdhvatā darśanāt sthāṇuḥ ayam iti niścetum icchati tadā puruṣa viśeṣa anusmaraṇena puruṣe samākṛṣyata yadā puruṣaḥ a yam iti niścetum icchati tadā sthāṇu viśeṣa anusmaraṇena sthāṇākṛṣyate iti ubhayatra ākṛṣyamāṇaḥ atas eva asya pratyayaḥ dolāyate na ekatra niyamena avatiṣṭhate dolā sādharmyam anavasthita rūpa tvam eva pratyayasya darśayati kinnu khalu ayam sthāṇuḥ syāt puruṣaḥ vā iti 
NK_159.1–159.3	 viparyayaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣyaḥ eva bhavati pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat prasiddha aneka viśeṣayoḥ pitta kapha anila upahata indriyasya ayatha artha ālocanāt asat nihita viṣaya jñāna ja saṃskāra apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt adharmāt ca ātasmin= tat iti pratyayaḥ viparyayaḥ yathā gavyevāḥ ca iti asati api pratyakṣe pratyakṣa abhimānaḥ bhavati yathā vyapagata ghana paṭalam acala jalanidhi sadṛśam ambaram añjana cūrṇa puñja śāmam śārvaram tamaḥ iti 
NK_159.4	 saṃśaya anantaram viparyayam nirūpayati viparyayaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva bhavati iti saṃśayaḥ tāvat pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva bhavati iti viparyayaḥ api tad viṣaye bhavati iti api śabda arthaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva bhavati iti pratyakṣa anumāna vyatirekeṇa pramāṇa antara abhāvāt pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat prasiddha aneka viśeṣayoḥ iti prasiddhāḥ pūrvam pratītāḥ aneke viśeṣāḥ sāsna ādayaḥ kesara ādayaḥ ca yayoḥ tau prasiddha aneka viśeṣau gavāśvau tayoḥ madhye yaḥ atasmin= anaśve gavi tat iti pratyayaḥ aśvaḥ iti pratyayaḥ sa viparyayaḥ 
NK_159.5	 nanu yadā gavi go tva sāsna ādayaḥ ca viśeṣāḥ parigṛhyante tadā viparyayaḥ na bhavati bhavati ced asya anuparama prasaṅgaḥ tatra āha ayathā artha ālocanāt iti ayathārtha ālocanam yathā artha ālocanasya abhāvaḥ yathāsau= arthaḥ gauḥ sāsnādimān= tathāgrahaṇa abhāvaḥ iti yāvat tasmāt atasmin tat iti pratyayaḥ bhavati iti anena viśeṣa anupalambhasya kāraṇa tvam uktam 
NK_159.6	 sannihite piṇḍe go tvasya agrahaṇe kaḥ hetuḥ kaḥ vā hetuḥ asannihitasya aśva tvasya pratītau= iti āha pitta kapha anila upahata indriyasya iti pittam ca kaphaḥ ca anilaḥ ca taiḥ upahatam dūṣitam indriyam yasya tasyām viparyayaḥ iti vāta pitta śloṣma ādi doṣāṇām asat nihita pratibhāse sannihita artha apratibhase ca sāmarthyam samarthitam yadi doṣa sāmarthyāt eva asat nihitam pratibhāti sarvam sarvatra avabhādeta niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt atas āha asat nihita viṣaya jñāna ja saṃskāra apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt iti 
NK_159.7^1	 asannihitaḥ viṣayaḥ aśvādiḥ tatas pūrvam utpannāt jñānāt jataḥ yaḥ saṃskāraḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt viparyayaḥ iti ayam asya arthaḥ gopiṇḍa saṃyuktam indriyam go tvam agṛhṇat api tam piṇḍam sādṛśya viśiṣṭam gṛhṇāti sa aṃśa tvāt vastunaḥ tena ca sādṛśya grahaṇena aśva viṣayaḥ saṃskāraḥ prabodhyate sa ca prabuddhaḥ aśva smṛti janane prāpte manaḥ doṣāt indriya saṃyukte gavya navaḥ eva sādṛśya anurodhāt anubhava ākārām aśva pratītim karoti atas na sarvasya sarvatra avabhāsaḥ sādṛśya saṃskārayoḥ pratiniyama hetvāt atas eva ca iyam gurubhiḥ indriya jā bhrāntiḥ ucyate evam hi indriya jāḥ na syāt yadi iyam saṃskāra eka sāmarthyāt asat nihitam anadhikaraṇam aśva tva mātram eva gṛhṇīyāt niruddha indriya vyāpārasya ca bhavet vyāpriyamāṇe cakṣuṣi tad saṃyuktam eva tu gopiṇḍam aśva ātmanā gṛhṇatī yadi iyam na indriya jāḥ kā tarhi indriya jā bhaviṣyati viparīta khyātiḥ api atas eva anyasya anya kāreṇa pratibhāsanāt 
NK_159.7^2	 yaḥ api viradhiṣṭhānaḥ viparyayaḥ tatra api avartamānaḥ arthaḥ sva rūpa viparītena vartamāna ākāreṇa pratīyate iti viparīta khyātiḥ eva na tu asat khyātiḥ svarūpataḥ arthasya sambhavāt asataḥ ca avabhāsana ayogāt yatra sadṛśam artham adhiṣṭhāya viparyayaḥ pravartate tatra sādṛśyam kāraṇam niradhiṣṭhāne tu vibhrame manaḥ doṣa mātra anubandhini na asya sambhavaḥ yathā hi kāmātuḥ asya itas tatas bhāvini strī nirbhāse vijñāne saṃskāra upi tatra eva kāraṇam yatra sa vikalpakaḥ bhramaḥ nirvikalpake tu indriya doṣasya eva sāmarthyam tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt yathā śaṅkhe pīta jñāna utpattau 
NK_159.8	 viparyayasya udāharaṇa antaram āha asati api pratyakṣe pratyakṣa abhimānaḥ ityādinā gagana avalokana kutūhalāt ūrdhvam anupreṣitāḥ nayana raśmayaḥ dūra gamanāt manda vegāḥ pratimukhaiḥ sūrya raśmibhiḥ ati prabala vegaiḥ āhatāḥ pratinivartamānāḥ sva golakasya guṇam deśa antare nirālambam nīli mānam ābhāsayantaḥ jaladhara paraṭala nirmukta nistaraṅga mahā udadhi kalpam ambaram iti pratyakṣam iva rūpa jñānam apratyakṣe nabhasi janayanti sva golaka guṇam vyoma adhikaraṇa tvena indriyam ābhāsayati iti atra tad guṇa anuvidhānena pratīti niyamaḥ pramāṇam tathā hi kāmalā adhiṣṭhita indriya adhiṣṭhānaḥ vidruta kala dhauta rasa viliptam iva antarikṣam īkṣate kapha adhika tayā dhavalagolakaḥ rajata sacchāyam paśyati śarvaryām bhavam śārvaram tamaḥ añjana cūrṇa puñjaḥ iva śyāmam iti kevala jñānam atyanta tejaḥ abhave sati sarvatra āraḥ apita rūpa mātra viṣayam apratyakṣam api pratyakṣam iva paśyati 
NK_160.1–160.3	 anumāna viṣaye api bāṣpa ādi bhiedhūma abhimataiḥ vahni anumānam gavaya viṣāṇa darśanāt ca gauḥ iti trayī darśana viparīteṣu śākya ādi darśaneṣu idam śreyaḥ iti mithyā pratyayaḥ viparyayaḥ viparyayaḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ sva ātma abhimānaḥ kṛtakeṣu nitya tva darśanam kāraṇa vaikalye kārya utpatti jñānam hitam upadiśatsu ahitam iti jñānam ahitam ipadiśatsu hitam iti jñānam anumāna viṣaye api bāṣpa ādibhiḥ bāṣpa dhūli patākā ādibhiḥ dhūma abhimataiḥ dhūmaḥ iti jñātaiḥ anagnike deśe agni anumānam tathā gavaya viṣāṇa darśanāt gauḥ iti jñānam anumāna viparyayaḥ 
NK_160.4^1	 atyanta durdaśana abhyāsāt ca viparyayaḥ bhavati iti āha trayī darśana viparīteṣu iti trayāṇām vedānām ṛc yajuḥ sāmnām samāhāraḥ trayī atharvavedaḥ tu trayī eka deśaḥ eva dṛśyate svarga apavarga sādhana bhūtaḥ arthaḥ anayoti darśanam trayī ā iva darśanam trayī darśanam tad viparīteṣu śākya ādi darśaneṣu śākya bhinnaka nirgranthaka saṃsāra mocaka ādi śāstreṣu idam śreyaḥ iti idam yat upadiśanti tad pramāṇam iti jñānam mithyā pratyayaḥ teṣu kaiścid eva upagṛhīteṣu sarmeṣām varṇa āśramiṇām vigānāt pramāṇa virodhāt ca 
NK_160.4^2	 tathā śarīra indriya manaḥsva ātma abhimanaḥ viparyayaḥ tebhyaḥ vyatiriktasya jñātuḥ pratipādanāt kṛtakeṣu vedeṣu nitya tva abhimānaḥ viparyayaḥ mīmāṃsakānām kāraṇa vaikalye dharma adharmayoḥ abhāve kārya utpatti jñānam sukha duḥkha ādi vaicitrya jñānam viparyayaḥ lokāyatikānām prāṇinaḥ na hiṃsitavyāḥ mala paṅka ādikam aśuci na dhārayitavyam iti ādikam hitam upadiśatsu veda vṛddheṣu ahitam iti vijñānam prāṇi hiṃsā paraḥ dharmaḥ mala paṅka ādi dhāraṇam eva śreyaḥ iti ahitam upadiśatsu kṣapaṇaka saṃsāra mocaka ādiṣu hitam iti jñānam tad śiṣyāṇām viparyayaḥ 
NK_161.1	 atra eke vadanti viparyayaḥ na asti kāraṇa abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca indriyāṇām yathā artha jñāna janana svabhāva tvāt doṣa vaśāt ayathārtham api jñānam indriyāṇi janayanti iti ced na śakti mātra vighāta hetu tvāt doṣāṇām śukti saṃyuktam indriyam doṣa upahata śaktikam śuktikā tvam na gṛhṇāti na tu asannihitam rajatam prakāśayati doṣāṇām saṃskāraka tva prasaṅgāt yadi ca apratyakṣam api cakṣuḥ adhyakṣayati sarvasya sarva vid tvam kena vāryate idam rajatam iti jñānasya śuktikā ālambanam iti ca saṃvid viruddham yasyām hi saṃvidi yaḥ arthaḥ avabhāsate sa tasyāḥ ālambanam rajata jñāne ca rajatam pratibhāti na śuktikā na ca agṛhīta rajatasya śuktau tad bhramaḥ tasmāt idam iti śukrikā viṣayaḥ anubhavaḥ rajatam iti ca sadṛśa avabodha prabodhita saṃskāra mātra jam doṣa kṛtam tat iti aṃśa pramoṣam rajara smaraṇam iti dve ime saṃvittī bhinna viṣaye 
NK_161.2^1	 atra icyate yadi rajata jñānam naśuktikā viṣayam tu eṣā rajata smṛtiḥ tadā tasmin jñāne rajata arthī pūrva anubhūte eva rajate pravarteta na śuktikāyām smṛteḥ anubhava deśe pravartaka tvāt atha manyase indriyeṇa rajatasya sādhāraṇam rūpam śuktikāyām gṛhītam na śuktikā tvam viśeṣaḥ rajata smaraṇana ca tat iti ullekha śūnyegṛ hīti rūpa tā mātram bibhratā anirdhārita diś deśam rajata mātram upasthāpitam tatra anayoḥ gṛhyamāṇa smaryamāṇayoḥ grahaṇa smaraṇayoḥ ca sādṛśyāt viśeṣa agrahaṇāt ca vivekam anavadhārayan śuktikā deśe pravartate sāmānādhikaraṇyam śuktikā ra jatayoḥ adhyavasyati rajatam etat iti 
NK_161.2^2	 tat api ayuktam avivekasya api agrahaṇāt rajata abheda grahaḥ hi rajata arthinaḥ śuktikāyām pravṛtti kāraṇam na sādṛśyam bheda grahaṇam ca tatas nivṛtti kāraṇam tad ubhayoḥ abhāvāt na pravarttate na nivarttate iti syāt na tu niyamena pravarttate viśeṣa abhāvāt evam sāmāna adhikaraṇī aṃpi na syāt abheda agrahaṇasya api vaiyadhi karaṇya hetoḥ sambhavāt tathā ca pravṛtti uttara kālīnaḥ na idam rajatam iti bādhaka pratyayaḥ api na ghaṭate śuktikā rajatayoḥ bhedaḥ na gṛhītaḥ na tu tādātmya madhyavasitam yena idam pratiṣidhyate 
NK_161.3	 bheda agrahaṇa prasañjitasya śuktikāyām rajatavyavahārasya ayam pratiṣedhaḥ iti ced na abheda agrahaṇāt atad vyavahāra pravṛtteḥ api sambhavāt asti ca śuktikā deśe rajata arthinaḥ pravṛttiḥ asti ca sāmānādhikaraṇya pratyayaḥ rajatam rtat iti asti ca bādhaka pratyayaḥ idanta adhikaraṇasya rajata ātma tā niṣedha paraḥ tena avagacchāmaḥ śukti saṃyuktena indriyeṇa doṣa sahakāriṇā rajata saṃskāra sacivena sādṛśyam anurundhatā śuktikā viṣayaḥ rajata adhyavasāyaḥ kṛtaḥ 
NK_161.4	 yat ca idam uktam śuktikā ālambana tvam banu bhava viruddham iti tad asāram idantayā niyata deśa adhikaraṇasya cākacikya viśiṣṭasya śukti kā śa kalasya api pratibhasanāt hāna ādi vyavahāra yogya tā ca ālambana arthaḥ sa ca atra eva sambhavati yaḥ api bheda agrahāt śuktau rajata vyavahāra pravṛttim icchati tena api viparyayaḥ aṅgīkṛtaḥ atasmin tat iti vyavahāra pravṛtteḥ eva viparyaya tvāt yat ca śakti vyāghāta nātra hetu tvam doṣāṇām iti tat api na kiñcid vāta ādi doṣa duṣṭānām dhātūnām roga antara janana upalambhāt sarvasya sarva vid tvam ca doṣāṇām śakti niyamāt eva parāhatam na ca jñānasya artha vyabhicāre sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ yatnena anviṣyamāṇānām bādhaka kāraṇa doṣāṇām anupalambhāt abhāva siddhau tad vyāptasya viparyayasya abhāva avagamāt eva viśvāsa upapatteḥ 
NK_161.5–161.6	 viparyaya anabhyupagame ca dvi candra jñānasya kā gatiḥ doṣa vyatibhinnānām cakṣū raśmi avayavānām ca pṛthak nirgatya patitānā candramasi janitasya jñāna dvayasya ayam dvi tva avabhāsaḥ iti ced na jñāna dharmasya cakṣuṣā grahaṇa abhāvāt jñāna dharmaḥ jñeya gata tvena gṛhyamāṇaḥ jñeya grāhakeṇa eva indriyeṇa gṛhyate iti abhyupagame tu bhrāntiḥ samarthitā syāt anya dharmasya anyatra grahaṇāt iti alam ati prakopitaiḥ śrotriya dvijanmabhiḥ iti uparamyate ye tu śuktikāyām rajata pratītau= alaukikam rajatam vastu bhūtam eva pratīyate iti vadantaḥ viparyaya abhāvam samarthayanti teṣām asmin jñāne pravṛttiḥ na syāt alaukikasya artha kriyā hetu tva anavagamāt 
NK_162.1–162.2	 anadhyavasāyaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣayaḥ eva san jāyate tatra pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat prasiddha artheṣu aprasiddha artheṣu vā vyāsaṅgāt anarthi tvāt vā kim iti ālocana mātram anadhyavasāyaḥ yathā vāhīkasya panasa ādiṣu anadhyavasāyaḥ bhavati tatra sattā dravya tva pṛthivī tva vṛkṣa tva rūpavat tva ādi śākhā ādi apekṣaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ eva panasa tvam api panaseṣu anuvṛttam āmra ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛttam pratyakṣam eva kevalam tu upadeśa abhāvāt viśeṣa saṃjñā pratipattiḥ na bhavati anumāna viṣaye api nārikela dvīpa vāsinaḥ sāsnā mātra darśanāt kaḥ nu khlu ayam prāṇī syāt iti anadhyavasāyaḥ bhavati 
NK_162.3^1	 anadhyavasāyaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaye san jāyate pratyakṣa anumāna viṣaye viparyayaḥ tāvat bhavati anadhyavasāyaḥ api bhavati iti api cabda arthaḥ pratyakṣa viṣaye tāvat anumāna viṣaye krameṇa anadhyavasāyaḥ vakravyaḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa krama vācinam tāvat śabdam āha prasiddha artheṣu aprasiddha artheṣu va vyāsaṅgāt anarthi tvāt vā kim iti ālocana mātram anadhyavasāyaḥ prasiddhāḥ ca te arthāḥ ca prasiddhārthāḥ ye arthāḥ pūrvam jñāta āsyeṣu vyāsaṅgāt anyatra āsakta citta tvāt viśeṣa prati iti anarthi tvāt vā kim iti ālocana mātram gate api prasiddhe rājani kopī anena pathā gataḥ iti jñāna mātram anavadhārita viśeṣam anadhyavasāyaḥ 
NK_162.3^2	 aprasiddheṣu aparijñānāt eva anadhyavasāyaḥ yathā vāhīkasya panasa ādiṣu anadhyavasāyaḥ bhavati ṭakka deśa udbhavasya panasa ādiṣu anadhyavasāyaḥ iti arthaḥ tatra api panase sattva dravya tva pṛthivī tva vṛkṣa tva rūpattva ādi śākhā ādi apekṣaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ eva dravyam etat pārthivaḥ ayam vṛkṣoyam rūpa ādimān śākhādimān= ca iti avadhāraṇāt panasa tvam api panaseṣu anuvṛttam āmra ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛttam nirvikalpaka pratyakṣam eva kevalam tu asya panasa śabdaḥ nāmadheyam iti upadeśa abhāvāt viśeṣa saṃjñā pratipattiḥ na bhavati panasa śabda vācyaḥ ayam iti pratipattiḥ na bhavati kintu kim api asya nāmadheyam bhaviṣyati iti etāvat mātra pratītiḥ syāt sā iyam sañjñā viśeṣa anavadhāraṇa ātmikā pratītiḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ 
NK_162.4	 anumāna viṣaye api nālikera dvīpa vāsinaḥ sāsnā mātra darśanāt kaḥ nu khlu atra pradeśe prāṇī syāt iti anadhyavasāyaḥ nālikera dvīpe gavām abhāvāt tatratyaḥ lokaḥ aprasiddha go jātīyaḥ tasya deṣa antaram āgatasya vane sāsnā mātra darśanāt sāmānyena piṇḍa mātram anumāya tatra jāti viśeṣa viṣaya tvena kaḥ nu khlu atra prāṇī syāt iti anavadhāraṇa ātmakam jñānam anadhyavasāyaḥ adhyavasāyāt aviśeṣa avadhāraṇa jñānāt anyat iti vyutpattyā nanu ayam saṃśayaḥ eva anavadhāraṇa ātmaka tvāt na kāraṇa bhedāt svarūpa bhedāt ca kiñca ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt saṃśayaḥ na tu anadhyavasāyaḥ pratīti viśeṣayatvena api asya sambhavāt tathā anavasthita ubhaya koṭi saṃsparśī saṃśayaḥ na tu ayam iti bhedaḥ vidyā tu ayam na bhavati vyavahāra anaṅga tvāt iti 
NK_163.1–163.2	 uparata indriya grāmasya pralīmanaskasya indriya dvāreṇa eva yat anubhavanam mānasam tat svapna jñānam katham yadā buddhi pūrvāt ātmanaḥ śarīta vyāpārāt ahani khinnā asya prāṇinaḥ niśi viśrāma artham āhāra pariṇāma artham vā adṛṣṭa kārita prayatna apekṣāt ātma antar karaṇa saṃyogāt manasi kriyā prabandhāt antar hṛdaye nirindriye ātma pradeśe ātma pradeśe yadā niścalam manaḥ tiṣṭhati tadā pralīna manaskaḥ iti ākhyāyate pralīne ca tasmin uparata indriya grāmaḥ bhavati tasyām avasthāyām prabandhena prāṇa apāna santana pravṛttau= ātma manaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt svāpa ākhyāt saṃskārāt ca indriya dvāreṇa eva asatsu viṣayeṣu pratyakṣa ākāram svapna jñānam utpadyate 
NK_163.3	 svapni rūpaṇa artham āha uparata indriya grāmasya ityādi uparataḥ sva viṣaya grahaṇāt virataḥ indriya grāmaḥ yasya asau= uparata indriya grāmaḥ prakarṣeṇa sarva ātmanā līnam manaḥ yasya asau pralīna manaskaḥ iti tasya uparata indriya grāmasya pralīna manaskasya indriya dvāreṇa yat anubhavanam pūrva adhigama anapekṣam pariccheda svabhāvam mānasam manaḥ mātra prabhavam tat svapna jñānam 
NK_163.4	 yadā yathā puruṣasya manaḥ pralīyate indriyāṇi ca viramanti tat darśayati katham ityādinā ātmanaḥ śarīra vyāpārāt gamana āgamana ādi lakṣaṇāt buddhi pūrvāt ahani khinnasya pariśrāntasya prāṇinaḥ niśi rātrau viśrāma artham śrama upaśama artham bhukta pītasya āhārasya rasa ādi bhāvena pariṇāma artham ca adṛṣṭena kāritam prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt ātma antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogāt manasi yaḥ kriyā prabandhaḥ kriyā santānaḥ jāta s tasmāt antar hṛdaye nirindriye bāhya indriya sambandha śūnye ātma pradeśe niścalam manaḥ tiṣṭhati yadā tadā puruṣaḥ pralīna manaskaḥ iti ākhyāyate pralīne ca tasmin manasi uparata indriya grāmaḥ bhavati antaḥkaraṇa an adhiṣṭhitānām indriyāṇām viṣaya grahaṇa abhāvāt tasyām pralīna manaskā avasthāyām prabandhena bāhulyena prāṇa apāna vāyu santānasya nirgama praveśa lakṣaṇāyām pravṛttau sambhavantyām ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt svāpa ākhkhyāt svāpaḥ iti nāmadheyāt saṃskārāt ca pūrva anubhūta viṣayāt asatsu deśa kāla vyavahiteṣu viṣayeṣu pratyakṣa ākāram aparokṣa saṃvedana ākāram svapna jñānam utpadyate 
NK_164.1–164.3	 tat tu trividham saṃskāra pāṭavāt dhātu doṣāt adṛṣṭāt ca tatra saṃskāra pāṭavāt tāvat kāmī kruddhaḥ vā yadā yam artham ādṛtaḥ cintayan svapiti tadā sā eva cintā santatiḥ pratyakṣa ākārā san jāyate dhātu doṣāt vāta prakṛti vā adūṣitaḥ vā ākāśa gamana ādīni paśyati pitta prakṛtiḥ pitta dūṣitaḥ vādni praveśa kanaka parvata ādīni paśyati śleṣma prakṛtiḥ śleṣma dūṣitaḥ vā sarit samudra prataraṇa hima parvata ādīn paśyati 
NK_164.4–164.5	 yat svayam anubhūteṣu ananubhūteṣu vā prasiddha artheṣu aprasiddha aetheṣu vā yat śubha avedakam gaja ārohaṇa= chatra lābha ādi tat sarvam saṃskāra dharmābhyām bhavati viparītam ca taila abhyañjana khra uṣṭra ārohaṇa ādi tat sarvam adharma saṃskārābhyām bhavati atyanta aprasiddhā artheṣu adṛṣṭāt eva iti svapna antikam yadi api uparata indriya grāmasya bhavati tathā api atītasya jñāna prabandhasya pratyavekṣaṇāt smṛtiḥ eva iti bhavati eṣā caturvidhā avidyā iti 
NK_164.6–164.8	 tat tu trividham kutas iti atra āha saṃskāra pāṭavāt dhātu doṣāt adṛṣṭāt ca iti saṃskāra pāṭavāt tāvat kāmī kruddhaḥ vā yadā yam artham priyatamām śatrum vā ādṛtaḥ ananya manāḥ cintayan svapiti tadā sā eva cintā santatiḥ saṃskāra atiśayāt pratyakṣa ākārā sākṣāt artha avabhāsinī san jāyate śarīta dhāraṇāt dhātavaḥ vasā asṛj māṃsa medaḥ majja asthi śukra ātmānaḥ teṣām doṣāt vāta ādi dūṣita tvāt viparyayaḥ bhavati iti āha vāta prakṛtiḥ yadi vā kutaścid nimittāt upacitena vātena dūṣitaḥ sva ātmanaḥ ākāśa gamanam itas tatas dhāvanam iti ādikam paśyati pitta prakṛtiḥ pitta dūṣitaḥ vai agni praveśa kanaka parvata abhyudita arka maṇḍala ādikam paśyati śleṣma prakṛtiḥ śleṣma dūṣitaḥ vā sarit samudra prataraṇa hima parvata ādīn paśyati 
NK_164.9^1	 svayam anubhūteṣu paratra aprasiddheṣu svapam ananu bhūteṣu paratra prasiddheṣu svayam anubhūteṣu vā paratra aprasiddheṣu satsu yat gaja ārohaṇa= chatra lābha ādikam śubha avedakam svapne dṛśyate tat sarvam saṃskāra dharmābhyām bhavati śubha āvedaka viparītam taila abhyañjala khayā uṣṭra ārohaṇa ādi a dharma saṃskārābhyām bhavati atyanta aprasiddheṣu svatas paratas ca apratīteṣu candrāt iti abhakṣaṇa ādiṣu jñānam tat adṛṣṭāt eva ananubhūtaṣu saṃskāra abhāvāt yadi api saṃskāra pāṭavāt dhātu doṣāt adṛṣṭāt vā samāropita bāhya svarūpaḥ svapna pratyayaḥ bhavan atasmin tat iti bhāvāt viparyayaḥ tathā api avasthā viśeṣa bhāvi tvāt pṛthak uktaḥ 
NK_164.9^2	 kadācid svapna dṛṣṭasya arthasya svapna avasthāyām eva pratisamdhānam bhavati ayam mayā dṛṣṭaḥ iti tat ca pūrva anubhūtasya svapnasya ante avasāne bhavati iti svapna antikam ucyate tat api uparata indriya grāmasya bhāvāt svapna jñānam iti kasyacid āśaṅkām apanetum āha svapna antikam yadi api uparata indriya grāmasya bhavati tathā api atītasya pūrva anubhūtasya svapna jñāna prabandhasya pratyavekṣaṇāt anusandhānāt smṛtiḥ eva iti upasaṃharati bhavati eṣā caturvidhā avidyā iti 
NK_165.1–165.4	 vidyā api caturvidhāḥ pratyakṣa laiṅgika smṛti ārṣa lakṣaṇāḥ tatra akṣam akṣam pratītya utpadyate iti pratyakṣam akṣāṇi indriyāṇi ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotra manāṃsi ṣaṭ tat hi dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu utpadyate samprati vidyām vibhajate vidyā api caturvidhā iti na kevalam avidyā caturvidhāḥ vidyā api caturvidhā iti pratyakṣe laiṅgika smṛti ārṣa lakṣaṇā pratyakṣa smṛti ārṣa svabhāvāḥ ādau pratyakṣasya nirdeśaḥ kāraṇa tvāt tad anantaram anumānasya tad pūrvaka tvāt tad anamtaram smṛteḥ pratyakṣa anumitrṣu artheṣu bhāvāt lokika pramāṇa ante saṃkīrtanam ārṣasya loka uttarāṇām puruṣāṇām tad bhāvāt 
NK_165.5	 pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇam tāvat kathayati tatra akṣam akṣam pratītya utpadyate iti pratyakṣam iti akṣam akṣam pratītya yat utpadyate tat pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti kāraṇa viśeṣa ja tvam api kāryasya samāna asamāna jātīya vyavaccheda samartha tvāt lakṣaṇam bhavati yathā yava bīja prabhava tvam yava aṅkurasya atas eva yava aṅkuraḥ iti vyapadiśyate sukha duḥkha saṃskārāṇām api indriya ja tvāt pratyakṣa pramāṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ iti ced na buddhi adhikāreṇa viśeṣita tvāt akṣam akṣam pratītya yā buddhiḥ utpadyate tat pratyakṣam sukha ādayaḥ ca na buddhi svabhāvāḥ kutas teṣu prasaktiḥ yadi evam sannikarṣasya prāmāṇyam na labhyate satyam itas vākyāt na labhyate yadi tu karaṇa vyutpattyā tasya api prāmāṇyam abhimatam pariccheda hetu tvāt saṃśaya viparyaya vyudāsaḥ vidyā virūpaṇasya prakṛta tvāt 
NK_165.6	 akṣam pratītya yat utpadyate tat pratyakṣam iti ukte ati prasiddha tvāt vāhya indriya jam eva pratyakṣam iti kasyacid bhrāntiḥ syāt tad nivṛtti artham akṣam akṣam iti vīpsā sakala indriya avabodha arthā kṛtā kugati prādayaḥ iti prādi samāsaḥ pratigatam akṣam pratyakṣam iti anena asya abhidheya liṅgatā pratyakṣam jñānam pratyakṣam buddhiḥ pratyakṣaḥ pratyayaḥ iti ca akṣa śabdasya bahuṣu artheṣu nirūḍha tvāt viśinaṣṭi akṣāṇi indriyāṇi tāni ca sāṃkhya ekādaśavidhāni uktāni tad nivṛtti artham parisakhyām karoti ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvac śrotra manāṃsi iti 
NK_165.7^1	 akṣa jam vijñānam pratyakṣam iti ukte smṛtiḥ api pratyakṣā syāt atas tām asat viṣayām vyudasitum pratyakṣasya viṣayam nirdiśati tat hi dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu utpadyate iti hi śabdaḥ avadhāraṇe tat pratyakṣm kravyādiṣu eva dravya guṇa karmasānānyeṣu eva utpadyate na viśeṣa samavāyayoḥ iti arthaḥ dravyasya prādhānyāt prathamam tatra pratyakṣa utpattim āha dravye tāvat iti tāvat śabdaḥ krama arthaḥ mahati dravye trividhe pṛthivī ap tejaḥ lakṣaṇe pratyakṣam bhavati kutas kāraṇāt iti atra āha aneka dravyavat tvāt iti aneka dravyavat tvam bhūyas avayava āśrita tvam rūpasya prakāśaḥ udbhava samākhyātaḥ rūpasya dharmaḥ yad abhāvāt vāri sthe tejasi pratyakṣa abhāvaḥ 
NK_165.7^2	 catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt ātmanaḥ manasā saṃyogaḥ manasaḥ indriyeṇa indriyasya arthena etasmāt kāraṇa kalāpāt dhama ādi sāmagrye ca pratyakṣa abhāvāt mahati iti uktam avayava bhūyaḥ tva prakarṣa aprakarṣābhyām avayavini sphuṭa tva asphuṭa tva atiśayān atiśaya darśanāt aneka dravyavat tvam kāraṇam sati api mahat tve aneka dravyavat tve ca vāyoḥ anupalambhāt rūpa prakāśaḥ hetuḥ sarvasya eva jñānasya sukha duḥkha ādi hetu tvāt deśa kāla aniyamena utpādāt ca dharma adharma dikkāla janya tvam antareṇa ātma manaḥ saṃyogam manaḥ indriya saṃyogam indriya artha saṃyoga gam ca pratyakṣa abhāvāt caruṣṭaya sannikarṣaḥ kāraṇam 
NK_166.1–166.2	 dravye tāvat dvividhe mahati aneka dravyavattva udbhūta rūpa prakāśa catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt dharma ādi sāmagrye ca svarūpa ālocana mātram sāmānya viśeṣa dravya guṇa karma viśeṣaṇa apekṣāt ātma manaḥ sannikarṣāt pratyakṣmutpadyate sat dravyam pṛthivī viṣāṇī śuklau gauḥ gacchati iti indriya artha sannikarṣasya hetu tve sāmānya upalambha vat viśeṣa upalambhasya avaśyaṃbhāvitayā saṃśaya viparyaya anutpattiḥ iti ced na aniyamāt sāmānyam hi bahu viṣaya tvāt sva āśrayasya cakṣiḥ sannikarṣa mātreṇa upalabhyate viśeṣaḥ tu su alpa viṣaya tvāt sva āśrayasya tad avayavānām ca bhūyasām cakṣuḥ avayavānā bhūyobhiḥ ca tad avayavaiḥ saha sannikarṣam apekṣate iti na saha upalambha niyamaḥ sāmagrī bhedāt atas eva dūrāt avyakta grahaṇam gacchataḥ cakṣūraśmeḥ antarāle viśīrṇānām avayava antarāṇām artha prāpti abhāvāt 
NK_167.1^1	 kecid sa vikalpakam eva ekam pratyakṣam ācakṣate vyavasāya ātmaka tvena sarmasya vyavahāra yogya tvāt śabda vyutpattiḥ ahitānām api tiraścām artha vikalpāt pravṛtteḥ tān pratyāha svarūpa ālocana mātram iti svarūpasya ālocana mātram vikalpa rahitam grahaṇa mātram iti yāvat pratyakṣam pratyaksa yadi hi vastu svarūpasya nirvikalpakena grahaṇam na iṣyate tadā tad vācaka śabdasya smṛti abhāvāt sa vikalpakam api na syāt atas sa vikalpakam icchatā nirvikalpakam api eṣitavyam tat ca na sāmānya mātram gṛhṇāti bhedasya api pratibhāsanāt na api sva lakṣaṇa mātram sāmānya ākārasya saṃvedanāt vyakti antara darśane pratisandhānāt ca kintu sāmānyam viśeṣam ca ubhayam api gṛhṇāti yadi param idam sāmānya mayam viśeṣaḥ iti evam vivicya na pratyeti vastu antara anusamdhāna virahāt 
NK_167.1^2	 piṇḍa antara anuvṛtti grahaṇāt hi sāmānyam vivicyate vyāvṛtti grahaṇāt viśeṣaḥ ayam iti vivekaḥ nirvikalpakadaśāyām ca piṇḍa antara anusamdhāna abhāvāt sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī dharmau na gṛhyete tayoḥ agrahaṇāt na vivicya grahaṇam svarūpa grahaṇam tu bhavati eva tasya anya anapekṣa tvāt atas eva nirvikalpena sāmānya viśeṣa sva lakṣaṇānām na viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva avagamaḥ tasya bheda avagati pūrvaka tvāt nirvikalpakam ca sāmānya ādīnām paraspara bhedān adhyavasāyāt tatas param tu sa vikalpakam sāmānya viśeṣa rūpa tām pratyeti piṇḍa antaram anusanda dhānasya ātmanaḥ anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī dharmau pratipadyamānasya indriya dvāreṇa tathābhūta prati iti upapateḥ 
NK_168.1	 saugatāḥ punar evam āhuḥ sva lakṣaṇa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi pratibhāsam nirvikalpakam vastuni abhra antam atas tat eva pratyakṣam na sa vikalpakam tasya vāsanā adhīna janmanaḥ vastu ananurodhi pratibhāsasya keśa ādi jñāna vat vastuni bhrānta tvāt iti teṣām matam nirākurvan sa vikalpakasya api pratyakṣatām āha sāmānya viśeṣa dravya guṇa karma viśeṣaṇa apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣāt iti sāmānyam ca viśeṣaḥ ca dravyam ca guṇaḥ ca karma ca sāmānya viśeṣa dravya guṇa karmāṇi sāmānya viśeṣa dravya guṇa karmāṇi eva viśeṣaṇāni sāmānya viśeṣa dravya guṇa karma viśeṣaṇāni tāni apekṣate yaḥ ātma manaḥ sannikarṣaḥ tasmāt sat dravyam iti sāmānya viśiṣṭam pṛthivī iti pṛthivī tva viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭam viṣāṇi iti dravya viśṣṭam śuklaḥ gauḥ iti guṇa viśiṣṭam gacchti iti karma viśiṣṭam pratyakṣam syāt catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt iti anena eva ātma manaḥ saṃyoge labdhe punar asya upādānam pūrvasmāt nirvikalpaka prakramāt idam prakrama antaram iti avadyotana artham 
NK_168.2–168.4	 sa vikalpa kalarthe na pramāṇam iti katham ucyate pratīyate hi ghaṭaḥ ayam iti vijñāne vicchinnaḥ kambu grīva ātmā sarvatas vyāvṛttaḥ padārthaḥ anartha ja pratibhāsaḥ vikalpaḥ tasmāt artha adhyavasāyaḥ bhrāntaḥ iti ced yathā uktam vikalpaḥ vastu nirbhāsāt visaṃvādāt upaplavaḥ iti na pravṛttau saṃvādāt artha anubhava janmā vikalpaḥ artha ātma tayā āropita sva pratibhāsaḥ sva lakṣaṇa sva pratibhāsayoḥ bhedam tirodhāya sva lakṣaṇa deśe puruṣam pravartayati saṃvādayati ca maṇi prabhāyām maṇi buddhi vat pāramparyeṇa artha pratibandhāt artha prāpteḥ iti ced yadi vikalpaḥ vastu na saṃspṛśati katham tad ātma tayā sva pratibhāsam āropayet na hi apratīte maru marīci nicaye tad adhikaraṇaḥ jala samāropaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
NK_168.5	 atha pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhavī vikalpaḥ kāraṇa vyāpāram upādadānaḥ artha kriyā samartham vastu sākṣātkaroti anyathā artha kriyā arthinaḥ vikalpataḥ pravṛtti ayogāt yathā āha tatas api vikalpāt vastuni eva pravṛttiḥ iti evam tarhi vastuni pramāṇam tatra avisaṃvādi pratīti hetu tvāt atha manyase yaḥ kṣaṇaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate na asau vikalpena adhyavasīyate yaḥ ca vikalpena adhyavasiyate na sa pravṛttyā labhyate iti kṣaṇa apekṣayā na saṃvādaḥ teṣām kṣaṇika tvāt kintu yādṛśaḥ kṣaṇaḥ pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate tādṛśaḥ vikalpena adhyavasīyate yādṛśaḥ ca vikalpena adhyavasīyate tādṛśaḥ ca pravṛttyā labhyate iti anākali ta kṣaṇa bhedasya atad vyāvṛtta vastu mātra apekṣayā saṃvādaḥ tatra ca vikalpaḥ gṛhīta grāhi tvāda pramāṇam tathābhūtasya arthasya pratyakṣeṇa eva gṛhīta tvāt liṅgajaḥ tu vikalpaḥ pramāṇa antara aprāpta sva lakṣaṇa prāpaka tayā pramāṇam iti
