NK_168.6	 tat api asāram na hi kṣaṇasya anya vyāvṛttiḥ abhāva rūpāni avyāvṛtti apekṣayā vā tasya āropitam sādhāraṇam rūpam avastu bhūtam pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyate hetu tvasya grāhya lakṣaṇa tvāt avastunaḥ ca samasta artha kriyā virahāt kṣaṇaḥ tu parama arthaḥ sannartha kriyā samartha tvāt pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ sa ca vikalpa kālān anupāti iti uktam kutas viṣaya eka tā astu vā vikalpa pratyakṣayoḥ anirūpita rūpaḥ kaścid ekaḥ pravṛtti saṃvāda yogyaḥ viṣayaḥ tathā api vic slpaḥ pramāṇa tvam na ativarttate dhārāvāhika buddhi vat artha paricchede pūrva anapekṣa tvāt adhyavasita prāpaṇa yogya tvāt ca pramāṇa tve ca avasthite pratyakṣam eva syāt liṅga ādi abhāvāt artha indriya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvāt ca 
NK_168.7	 yat punar ayam artha jaḥ bhavan api nirvikalpaka vat indriya āpāta mātreṇa na bhavati tad indriya artha sahakāriṇaḥ vācaka śabda smaraṇasya abhāvāt smṛti anantara bhāvī vikalpaḥ smṛti jaḥ eva na indriya artha jaḥ tayoḥ smṛtyā vyavahita tvāt iti ced kim bhoḥ sahakārī bhāvasya svarūpa śaktim tirodhatte kṣiti udaka tirohitasya bījasya aṅkura jananam prati kā vārttā śabda smaraṇa indriya arthayoḥ kaḥ upakāraḥ yena idam tayoḥ sahakāri bhavati iti ced yathā vikalpaḥ sva utpattau= artha indriyayoḥ anvayavi atirekau= anukaroti tathā smṛteḥ api tatra indriya arthayoḥ ayam eva smaraṇena upakāraḥ yat etau kevalau kāryam akurvantau smṛti sahakāri lābhā kurutaḥ svarūpa atiśayānādhāyinaḥ na sahakāriṇaḥ iti kṣaṇa bhaṅga pratiḍedha avasare pratiṣiddham 
NK_169.1–169.3	 syāt etat kalpanā rahitam pratyakṣam kalpanā jñānam tu sa vikalpakam tasmāt arthe na pramāṇam iti atha kā iyam kalpanā śabda saṃyojana ātmikā pratītiḥ ekā artha saṃyojana ātmikā ca aparā viśiṣṭa grāhiṇī artha pratītiḥ kalpanā tat ayuktam vikalpa anupapatteḥ śabda saṃyojana ātmikā pratītiḥ kimarthe saṃyojayati kim vā svayam śabdena saṃyujyate yadi tāvat arthe śabdam saṃyojayati tatra api kim śabda ātmakam artham karoti kim vā śabda ākāra uparaktam gṛhṇāti āhosvit śabdena vyapadiśati na tāvat pratītiḥ artham śabda ātmakam karoti arthasya nirvikalpaka gṛhītena eva svarūpeṇa vikalpa jñāne api pratibhāsanāt artha kriyā karaṇāt ca anyathā vyutpanna avyutpannayoḥ yugapad eka ārta vyavasāya ayogāt 
NK_169.4	 atha śabda ākāra uparaktam artham gṛhṇāti tat api ayuktam apratīteḥ nirvikalpaka jñānena arthe gṛhīte prāk anubhūtaḥ tad vācakaḥ śabdaḥ smaryate pratiyogi darśanāt smṛtyā rūḍhaḥ ca asau taṭa sthaḥ eva artha paricchinatti na tu sphaṭikaḥ iva nīla uparaktaḥ śabda ākāra uparaktaḥ arthaḥ gṛhyate śabdasya ācākṣuṣa tvāt kevalasya eva arthasya īdantayā nirvikalpaka vat pratibhāsanāt ca na ca vācake smaryamāṇe vācyasya kācid sva rūpa kṣatiḥ asti yena ayam sati api indriya saṃyoge pratyakṣatām na labhate yathā uktam 
NK_169.5–169.6	 saṃjñā hi smaryaṃmāṇā api pratyakṣa tvam na bādhate saṃjñānaḥ sā taṭa sthāḥ hi na rūpa ācchādana kṣamā iti pratītiḥ śabdena saṃsṛṣṭa artham vyapadiśati iti api na su pratītam ātmā hi cetanaḥ pratisamdhāna ādi sāmarthyāt saṅketa kāla anubhūtam vācaka śabdam smṛtvā tena artham vyapadiśati ghaṭaḥ ayam iti na pratītiḥ tasyāḥ pratisandhāna ādi sāmarthya abhāvāt evam tāvat pratītiḥ na cabdam saṃyojayati 
NK_169.7–169.8	 na api svayam śabdena saṃyujyate jñānasya tat avyatiriktasya ca ākārasya kṣaṇika tvena asādhāraṇa tayā ca aśakya saṅketayoḥ śabdena san= taṣṭum ayogya tvāt viṣaya vācinā śabdena viṣayiṇaḥ vijñānasya vyapadeśa abhāvāt ca atha manyase vikalpaḥ śabda saṃsṛṣṭa artha viṣayaḥ sa ca arthaḥ saṃsṛjya śabdena saṃsṛjyate vyapadiśyate ca yatra śabdasya saṅketaḥ tatra ca śabdasya saṅkataḥ yat akṣaṇikam sādhāraṇam ca na ca sva lakṣaṇam sva lakṣaṇa viṣayaḥ vā bodhaḥ bodha viṣayaḥ ca ākāraḥ sādhāraṇaḥ akṣaṇikaḥ ca bhavati bodha ākārasya bāhya tvam api bodha ākārāt ananyat asā dhāraṇam eva sāmānyam ca vastu bhūtam na asti vicāra asaha tvāt tasmāt pratyekam vikalpaiḥ bāhya tveropiteṣu su a ākāreṣu paraspara bheda anadhyavasāyāt anya vyāvṛtta tayā ekatve samāropite śabdasya saṅketa iti pramāṇa balāt āyātam avarjanīyam tatra ca alīke śabda saṃsargavati vikalpaḥ pravartamānaḥ asantam artham vikalpayati iti kalpanā jñānam iti yathā uktam tasyām yat rūpam ābhāti bādyam ekam iva anyatas vyāvṛttam iva nistattvam parīkṣanaṅga bhāvataḥ iti 
NK_170.1^1	 atra ucyate yadi sāmānyasya vastu bhūtasya abhāvāt tad viśiṣṭa grāhitā kalpanā tvam tarhi asat artha tā eva kalpanā tvam na śabda saṃsṛṣṭa grāhitā tatra yadi śakṣyāmaḥ pramāṇena sāmānyam upapādayitum tadā sati api śabda saṃsṛṣṭa grāhaka tve tad viṣayam vikalpa jñānam indriya artha ja tvāt pratyakṣam eva syāt yat aparokṣa avabhāsi tad pratyakṣam yathā nirvika lokam aparokṣa avabhāsi ca vikalpa jñānam iha jñānānām parokṣa tvam anindriya artha ja tvena vyāptam yathā anumāne anindriya ja tu aviruddham ca indriya artha jatu mā tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt nirvikalpaka jñāne pratīyate iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ 
NK_170.1^2	 vipakṣe yat smṛti pūtvakam tat apratyakṣam yathā anumāna jñānam smṛti pūrvakam ca sa vikalpaka jñānam iti pratipakṣa anumānam api asti iti cetaḥ pratyakṣa tvam yadi na kvacid avagatam tadā sa vikalpake tasya na pratiṣedhaḥ prāpti pūrvaka tvāt pratiṣedhasya atha nirvikalpake pratītam tat katham pratītam indriya artha tad bhāva bhāvitva anuṃanena iti ced tarhi pratyakṣa tva prasādhakasya tad bhāva bhāvitva anumānasya prāmāṇya abhyupagame sati pratyakṣa tva pratiṣedhaka anumānam pravṛttam tad viparīta vṛtti aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ itivarttena eva bādhyate evam tāvat śabda saṃyojana ātmikā pratītiḥ kalpanā na bhavati iti 
NK_170.2^1	 artha saṃyojana ātmikā api viśiṣṭa grāhiṇī na kalpanā viśeṣaṇasya ca tayoḥ sambandhasya ca vyavacchedya vyavacchedaka bhāvasya vāstava tvāt artha avagrahaḥ vijñānam tad artha indriya sannikarṣāt yathābhūtaḥ arthaḥ tathā upajāyate na tu arthe vicārya pravarttate viśiṣṭa jñānam tu vicāraḥ iti idam viśeṣaṇam idam viśeṣya mayam anayoḥ sambandhaḥ esā ca loka sthitiḥ daṇḍī puruṣaḥ na tu paruṣī daṇḍaḥ iti vicārya ca pratyekam etāni paścāt ekīkṛtya gṛhṇāti daṇḍī paruṣaḥ iti yadi arthasya viśiṣṭa tā vāstavī prathamam eva viśiṣṭa jñānam jāyeta na bhavati ced 
NK_170.2^2	 na asya svarūpataḥ viśiṣṭa tā kim tu upādhi kṛtā iti viśiṣṭa tā jñānam kalpanā iti ced durūham idam āyuṣmatā ātmā hi pratyekam viśeṣaṇa ādīn gṛhītvā tān anusandhānaḥ indriyeṇa arthasya viśiṣṭa tām pratyeti na jñānam acetanam tasya pratisamdhāna aśakteḥ viramya vyāpāra abhāvāt ca arthaḥ viśeṣaṇa sambandhāt viśiṣṭaḥ eva viśeṣaṇa ādi grahaṇasya sahakāriṇaḥ abhāvāt prathamam indriyeṇa na tathā gṛhyate gṛhīteṣu viśeṣaṇa ādiṣu gṛhyate iti artha indriya jam tāvat viśiṣṭa jñānam yadi viśiṣṭa jñāna tvāt eva aparādhāt pratyakṣam na bhavati duḥsamādheyam iti uparamyate 
NK_171.1–171.5	 rūpa rasa gandha sparśeṣu aneka dravya samavāyāt sva gata viśeṣāt sva āśraya sannikarṣāt niyata indriya nimittam utpadyate śabdasya traya sannikarṣāt śrotra samavetasya tena eva upalabdhiḥ saṃkhyā parimāṇa pṛthaktva saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva sneha drava tva vega karmaṇām pratyakṣa dravya samavāyāt cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām grahaṇam buddhi sakha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnānām dvayoḥ ātma manasoḥ sannikarṣāt upalabdhiḥ bhāva dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādīnām upalabhya ādhāra samavetānām āśraya grāhakaiḥ indriyaiḥ grahaṇam iti etat asmad ādīnām pratyakṣam 
NK_171.6–171.7	 rūpa ādiṣu pratyakṣa utpatti kāraṇam āha rūpa rasa gandha sparśeṣu iti anekeṣu avayaveṣu samavetam dravyam aneka dravyam tatra samavāyāt svagataḥ viśeṣaḥ rupe rupatvem rase rasa tvam gandhe gandha tvam sparśe tasmāt sva āśraya sannikarṣāt rūpa ādīnām yaḥ āśrayaḥ tasya grāhakaiḥ indriyaiḥ sannikarṣāt niyata indriya nimittam cakṣuḥ nimittam rūpe rasana nimittam rase ghrāṇa nimittam gandhe tvac indriya nimittam sparśe jñānam uptadyate sva gata viśeṣāṇām hetu tvāt rūpa ādiṣu indriya vyavasthā anyathā pariplavaḥ syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt śabdasya traya sannikarṣāt śrotra samavetasya tena eva upalabdhiḥ traya sannikarṣāt iti ātma manaḥ indriyāṇām sannikarṣaḥ darśitaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ śrotra samavetasya iti anena uktaḥ tena eva upalabdhiḥ iti śrotreṇa eva upalabdhiḥ iti arthaḥ 
NK_171.8^1	 saṃkhyā ādīnām karmāntānām pratyakṣa dravya samavetānām āśraya vat cakṣuḥ sparśanābhyām grahaṇam karma pratyakṣam iti na mṛṣyāmahe gacchati dravye saṃyoga vibhāga atirikta padārtha antara anupalabdheḥ yaḥ tu ayam calati iti pratyayaḥ sa saṃyoga vibhāga anumita kriyā ālambanaḥ iti tad asāram yadi karma apratyakṣam vibhāga saṃyogābhyām anumīyate tadā vibhāga saṃyogayoḥ ubhaya vṛtti tva āśraya antare api karma anumīyeta na ca mūlāt agram agrāt ca mūlam gacchati śākhāmṛge tarau= api anyata saṃyoga vibhāga adhikaraṇe calati iti pratyayaḥ udayate yadi matam yaḥ ayam taru mṛgasya ākāśa ādinā api saṃyogaḥ tasya taru samavetāt karmaṇaḥ niṣpatti anavakalpanāt na tarau karma anumānam iti kalpyatām tarhi deśa antara saṃyoga artham taru mṛge api karma antaram tarau tu karma kalpanā na nivarttate eva yat adhikaraṇam kāryam tad adhikaraṇam kāraṇam iti utsargaḥ tasya ekatra vyabhicāre anyatra kaḥ āśvāsaḥ 
NK_171.8^2	 śākhāmṛga samavetena karmaṇā kalpitena śākhāmṛgasya taruṇā deśa antaraṇā api samam saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ utpatteḥ ubhaya karma kalpanā anupayogaḥ iti ced na evam pratibaddham hi liṅgam yatra upalabhyate tatra pratibandhakam upasthāpayati iti etāvatī eva anumānasya sāmagrī tasya arthāpatti vat anyathā upapattyā kaḥ paribhavaḥ na ca idam puruṣaḥ iva cetanam yasprayojana anurodhāt pravartare yadi tu ekasya vyoma pradeśasya saṃyoga vibhāgāḥ kriyā anumiti hetavaḥ kalpyante na śakyam kalpatitum atīndriya vyoma āśrayāṇām vibhāga saṃyogānām apratyakṣa tvāt bhū golaka pradeśa vibhāga saṃyoga santāna anumeya tve gacchataḥ viyati vihaṅgamasya karma duradhigamam syāt viyat vitata āloka nivaha vibhāga saṃyoga pravāhaḥ yadi tasya liṅgam iṣyate anicchataḥ api andhakāre vāyu doṣāt ekasmāt upajāta avayava kampasya bhuja agram me kampate bhrūḥ calati iti adṛṣṭa antaḥkaraṇa adhiṣṭhita tvac indriya jā karma buddhiḥ anibandhanā syāt rātrau mahā megha andhakāre kṣaṇa mātra sthāyinyām vidyuti calati iti pratyayasya kā gatiḥ 
NK_171.9–171.10	 buddhi sakha duḥkha icchā dveṣa prayatnānām dvayoḥ ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt upalabdhiḥ buddhi ityādi ātma samavetānām tad saṃyukta samavāyāt grahaṇam bhāva dravya guṇa karma tva ādīnām upalabhya ādhāra samavetānām āśraya grāhakaiḥ indriyaiḥ grahaṇam sattā dravya tva ādīnām sāmānyānām āśrayaḥ yena indriyeṇa gṛhyate tena eva tāni gṛhyante tatra saṃyogāt dravya grahaṇam saṃyukta samavāyāt guṇa ādi pratītiḥ saṃyikta samaveta samavāyāt guṇa tva ādi jñānam samavāyāt śabda grahaṇam samaveta samavāyāt śabda tva grahaṇam sambaddha viśeṣaṇa tayā ca abhāva grahaṇam iti ṣoḍhā sannikarṣaḥ yad saṃyukra samaveta viśeṣaṇa tvena rūpe rasa ādi abhāva grahaṇam yā ca saṃyukta samaveta viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaṇa tvena rūpa tve rasa tva ādi abhāva pratītiḥ yaḥ ca samaveta viśeṣaṇa tayā kakāre khakāra ādya bhāva avagamaḥ yat ca samaveta samaveta viśeṣaṇa tayā gatve khtu ā ādya bhāva saṃvedanam tat sarvam sambaddha viśeṣaṇa bhāvena saṃgṛhītam 
NK_171.11–171.12	 apare tu sarvatra yathā sambhāvam saṃyoga samavāyayoḥ eva hetu tvāt avāntara sambandha kalpanām na icchanti īdṛśaḥ hi teṣām bhāvānām svabhāvaḥ yat eṣām anya sannikarṣāt eva grahaṇam atiprasaṅgaḥ ca na asti sva āśraya pratyāsatteḥ niyāmaka tvāt upasaṃharati etat asmad ādīnām pratyakṣam iti asmad ādīnām ayoginām iti arthaḥ 
NK_172.1	 asmad viśiṣṭānām tu yoginām yuktānām yoga ja dharma anugṛhītena manasā sva ātma antara ākāśa diś kāla paramāṇu vāyu manassu tad samaveta guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣeṣu samavāye ca avitatham sva rūpa darśanam utpadyate viyuktānām punar cayuṣṭaya sat nikarṣāt yoga ja dharma anugraha sāmarthyāt sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭeṣu pratyakṣam utpadyate 
NK_172.2	 yogi pratyakṣam āha asmad viśiṣṭānām tu iti yogaḥ samādhi sa dvividhaḥ samprajñātaḥ asamprajñātaḥ ca samprajñātaḥ dhārakeṇa prayatnena kvacid ātma pradeśe vaśīkṛtasya manasaḥ tattva bubhutmā viśiṣṭena ātmanā saṃyogaḥ asamprajñātaḥ ca vaśīkṛtasya manasaḥ nirabhisandhi nirabhyutthānaḥ kvacid ātma pradeśe saṃyogaḥ tatra ayam uttaraḥ mumukṣūṇām avidyā saṃskāra vilaya artham antye janmani paripacyate na dharmam upacinoti abhisamdhi sahakāri virahāt na api bāhyam viṣayam abhimukhīkaroti ātmani eva pariṇāmāt pūrvaḥ tu yogaḥ abhisandhi sahāyaḥ pratanoti dharmam yad artham tattva bubhutsā viśiṣṭaḥ ca tad artha ddyotayati iti tena yogena yoginaḥ cyuta yogāḥ api yogya tayā yoginaḥ ucyante na ca teṣām aprakṣīṇaṃla āvaraṇānām tadānīm atīndriya artha darśa nam asti atas āha yuktānām iti 
NK_172.3^1	 tuktānām samādhi avasthitānām yoga ja dharma anugṛhītena manasā sva ātmani sva ātma antareṣu sva ātmanaḥ ātma antareṣu para kīreṣu parakīyeṣu ākāśe diśi kāle vāyau parama aṇuṣu manassu tad samaveteṣu guṇa ādiṣu samavāye ca aviyatham aviparyastam sva rūpa darśanam bhavati asmad ādibhiḥ ātmā sarva daiva aham mama iti kartṛ tva svāmi tva rūpa saṃbhinnaḥ pratīyate ubhayam ca etat śarīra ādi upādhi kṛtam rūpam na svābhāvikam atas eva aham amam a iti pratyayaḥ mithyādṛṣṭiḥ iti gīyate sarva pravādeṣu viparīta rūpa grāhaka tvāt a svābhāvikam tu yat asya svarūpam tat yogibhiḥ ālocyate yadā hi yogī vedān tat praveditam ātma svarūpam aham tattvataḥ ajānīyām iti abhisamdhānāt vahiḥ indriyebhyaḥ manaḥ pratyāhṛtya kvacid ātma deśe niyamya ekāgra tayā ātma anucintana pravāham abhyasyati tadā asya tattva jñāna saṃvartaka dharma ādhāna krameṇa ahaṅkāram amakāra vinirmuktam ātma tattvam sphuṭībhavati 
NK_172.3^2	 yadā tu parātma ākāśa kāla ādi bubhutsayā tad anucintana pravāham abhyasyati tadā asya para ātma ādi tattva jñāna anuguṇaḥ acintya prabhāvaḥ dharmaḥ pracīyate tad balāt ca antaḥkaraṇam bahis śarīrāt nirgatya para ātma ādibhiḥ saṃyujyate teṣu saṃyogāt saṃyukta samavāyāt tad guṇa ādiṣu saṃyukra samaveta samavāya aguṇa tva ādiṣu sambaddha viśeṣaṇa bhāvena samavāya abhāvayoḥ jñānam janayati dṛṣṭam tāvat samāhitena manasā abhyayamānasya vidyā śilpa ādeḥ ajñātasya api jñānam tad itaratra anumānam ātma ākāśa ādiṣu abhyāsa pracayaḥ tattva jñāna hetuḥ viśiṣṭa abhyāsa tvāt vidyā śilpa ādi abhyāsa vat tathā buddheḥ tāratamyam kvacid niratiṣayam sa atiśaya tvāt parimāṇa tāratamya vat 
NK_172.4^1	 nanu santāpyamānasya udakasya auṣṇye tāratamyam asti na ca tasya sarva atiśāyī vahni rūpa tā patti lakṣaṇaḥ prakarṣaḥ dṛśyate na api laṅghana abhyāsasya kvacid viśrāntiḥ avagatā na saḥ asti paruṣaḥ yaḥ samutplavena bhuvanatrayam laṅghayati ucyate yaḥ sthira āśrayaḥ dharmaḥ sva āśraye ca viśeṣam ārabhate sobhyāsa krameṇa prakarṣa paryantam āsādayati yathā kaladhautasya puṭapāka prabandha āhitā viśuddhiḥ parām paktasāra tām na ca udaka tāpasya sthiraḥ āśrayaḥ yatra ayam abhyasyamānaḥ parām kāṣṭhām gacchet atyanta tāpe sati udaka parikṣayāt 
NK_172.4^2	 na api laṅghana abhyāsya sva āśraye viśeṣa ādhāye viśeṣa ādhāyaka tvam asti niranvaya vinaṣṭe pūrva laṅghane laṅghana antarasya bala antarāt prayatna antarāt apūrvavat utpatteḥ atas eva kricatura utplava pariśrāntasya laṅghanam pūrvasmāt apacīyate sāma arthya parikṣayāt buddhiḥ tu sthira āśrayā sva āśraye viśeṣam ādhatte prathamam agṛhīta arthasya punar punar abhyasyamānasya grahaṇa darśanāt tasyāḥ pūrva pūrva abhyāsa āhita adhika adhika uttara uttara viśeṣa ādhāna krameṇa dīrgha kāla ādara nairantaryeṇa sevitāyāḥ yoga ja dharma anugraha samāsādita śakteḥ prakarṣa paryanta prāptiḥ na anupapattimatī 
NK_172.5–172.6	 yat punar atra uktam yoginaḥ asmad ādi ati indriya artha draṣṭāraḥ na bhavanti prāṇi tvāt asmad ādi vat tat yadi puruṣa mātram pakṣīkṛtya uktam tadā siddha sādhanam puruṣa viśeṣaḥ ca parasya asiddhaḥ siddhaḥ ced dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa viruddham anumānam atha ucyate prasaṅga sādhanam idam prasaṅga sādhanam ca na sva pakṣa sādhanāya upādīyate kintu parasya aniṣṭa āpādana artham para aniṣṭam ca tad abhyupagama siddhā etā iva dharmya ādibhiḥ śakyam āpādayitum tatra pramāṇena sva pratītiḥ anapekṣaṇīyāḥ na hi evam paraḥ pratyavasthātum arhati ata va asiddhāḥ dharmya ādayaḥ na aham sva siddheṣu api teṣu pratipadye a iti 
NK_172.7^1	 atra brūmaḥ kim prasaṅga sādhanam anumānam tat anyat vā yadi anyat kva api ukta lakṣaṇeṣu pramāṇeṣu antarbhāvaḥ varṇanīyaḥ vaktavyam vā lakṣaṇa antaram yadi tu anumānam eva tadā svāratīti pūrvakam eva pravarttate sva niścaya vat anyeṣām niścaya utpipādayiṣayā sarvasya para artha anumānasya pravṛtteḥ anyathā gagana kamalam surabhi kamala tvāt krīḍā saraḥ kamala vat iti asya api pratipādaka abhyupagamāt asiddha āśrayasya prāmāṇya upapattiḥ sandigdha vyāptayaḥ ca prāṇi tva ādayaḥ yadi hi vivāda adhyāsitasya puruṣa dhaureyasya prāṇi tva ādikam api bhavet sarvajña tvamāi syāt kaivātra anupapattiḥ 
NK_172.7^2	 na hi tayoḥ kaścid virodhaḥ pratīkṣitaḥ sarvajñātāyāḥ pramāṇa antara agocara tvāt prāṇi tva ādeḥ asarva jñtayā sahabhavaḥ tu sandigdhaḥ kim asmad ādīnām prāṇi tva ādi anubandhinīyam asarva jñtāḥ kim va sarva jñāna kāraṇa tvena avagatasya yoga ja dharmasya abhāva kṛtā iti na śakyate nirdhārayitum atas anavadhārita vyāptikam prāṇi tva ādikam na tad anumāna samartham atīndriya jñāna kāraṇam yoga jaḥ dharmaḥ iti na siddham kutas tad abhāvāt asmad ādīnām asarva jñtā śaṅkyeta asmākam tāvat siddham tena idam āśaṅkyate tatas ca na ubhaya siddhā vyāptiḥ kutas anumānam 
NK_172.8	 yuktānām pratyakṣam vyākhyāya viyuktānām vyācaṣṭe viyuktānām punar iti atyanta yoga abhyāsa upacita dharma atiśaya asamādhi avasthitāḥ api ye atīndriyam paśyanti te viyuktāḥ teṣām abhimukhībhūta nikhila viṣaya grāmāṇām apratihata karaṇa gaṇānām catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt ātma manaḥ indriya artha sannikarṣāt yoga ja dharma anugrahaḥ sahakāritā tad sāmarthyāt sūkṣmeṣu manaḥ paramāṇu prabhṛtiṣu vyavahiteṣu nāga bhuvana ādiṣu viprakṛṣṭeṣu brahma bhuvana ādiṣu pratyakṣam utpadyate jñānam 
NK_173.1–173.3	 tatra sāmānya viśeṣeṣu svarūpa ālocana mātram pratyakṣam pramānyam prameyāḥ dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāta ātmā pramitiḥ dravya ādi viṣayam jñānam sāmānya viśeṣa jñāna utpattau= avibhaktam ālocana mātram pratyakṣam pramāṇam na tasmin pramāṇa antaram asti aphala rūpa tvāt athavā sarveṣu catuṣṭaya sannikarśāt avitatham avyapadeśyam yat jñānam utpadyate tat pratyakṣam pramāṇam prameyāḥ dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāta ātmā pramitiḥ guṇa doṣa mādhyasthya darśanam iti 
NK_173.4	 evam tāvat vyākhyātam pratyakṣam samprati pramāṇa phalam vibhajate tatra sāmānya viśeṣeṣu svarūpa loca mātram pratyakṣam iti sāmānyam sattā dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādikam viśeṣāḥ vyaktayaḥ teṣu svarūpa locana mātram svarūpa grahaṇa mātram vikalpa rahitam pramāṇam pramāyām sādhakatama tvāt sādhakatama tvam ca tasmin sati pramitsoḥ pramā bhavati eva iti atiśayaḥ pramātari prameye ca sati pramā bhavati na tu bhavati eva pramāṇe tu nirvikalpake viśeṣaṇa jñāna ādi lakṣaṇe viśeṣya jñāna ādi lakṣaṇā pramā bhavati eva iti atiśayaḥ prameyāḥ dravya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ dravya ādayaḥ catvāraḥ padārthāḥ prameyāḥ pramiti viṣayāḥ pramitau jātāyām teṣu hāna ādi vyavahāraḥ pravarttate iti arthaḥ pramātāḥ ātmā bodha āśraya tvāt praminiḥ dravya ādi viṣayam jñānam yadā nirvikalpakam sāmānya viśeṣa jñānam pramāṇam tadā dravya ādi viṣayam viśeṣṭam jñānam pramitiḥ iti arthaḥ 
NK_173.5^1	 nanu nirvikalpakam sāmānya viśeṣa jñānam api pramā rūpam artha pratīti rūpa tvāt tadā tad utpattau kim pramāṇam iti atas āha sāmānya viśeṣa jñāna utpattā avibhaktam ālocana mātram pratyakṣam ālocyate anena iti ālocanam indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ tanmātram avibhaktam kevalam jñāna anapekṣam iti yāvat sāmānya viśeṣa jñāna utpattau pramāṇam viśeṣya jñāna utpattau= api indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pramāṇam bhavati eva pramāhetu tvāt kintu viśeṣaṇa jñāna sahakāri tayā na kevalaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa jñāna utpattau tu jñāna anapekṣaḥ kevalaḥ eva iti abhiprātaḥ 
NK_173.5^2	 sannikarṣa mātram iha pramāṇam na jñānam iti atra upapattim āha na tasmin iti sāmānya viśeṣa jñāne na anyat pramānam jñāna rūpam asti sāmānya viśeṣa jñānasya aphala rūpa tvāt jñāna phala tva abhāvāt viśeṣya jñānam hi viśeṣaṇa jñānasya phalam viśeṣaṇa jñānam na jñānantara phalam anavasthā prasaṅgāt atas viśeṣaṇa jñāne indriya artha sannikarṣa mātram eva pramāṇam iti arthaḥ yadā nirvikalpakam sāmānya viśeṣa jñānam phalam tadā indriya artha sannikarṣaḥ pramāṇaḥ tadā viśeṣya jñānam phalam tadā sāmānya viśeṣa ālocanam pramāṇam iti uktam tāvat 
NK_173.6	 samprati hāna ādi buddhīnām phalatve viśeṣya jñānam pramāṇam iti āha athavā iti sarveṣu padārtheṣu catuṣṭaya sannikarṣāt catuṣṭaya grahaṇam udāharaṇa artham dvaya sat nikarṣāt traya sannikarṣāt vitatham saṃśaya viparyaya rahitam avyapadeśyam vyapadeśe bhavam vyapadeśyam na vyapadeśyam avyapadeśyam śabda ajanyam yat vijñānam jāyate tat pratyakṣam pramāṇam saṃśayaḥ hi anavasthita ubhaya dharma tayā padārtham upadarśya avasthita eka dharmāṇam dharmiṇam prāpayat yathā adhyavasāyam vitathaḥ eva iti avitatha padena vyudasyate avyutpannasya sannihite arthe vyāpriyamāṇe cakṣuṣi śabda śravaṇa anantaram yat gauḥ iti jñānam jāyate tatra akṣam api kāraṇam anyathā rekhā uparekhā ādi viśeṣa pratīti ayogāt na ca tat pratyakṣam anantara bhāvinaḥ śabdasya eva tad utpattau sādhakatama tvāt indriyasya api tad sahakāritā mātra tvāt tathā api pṛṣṭaḥ vyapadiśati anena samākhyātam na punar evam abhidhatte pratyakṣaḥ mayā pratītam gauḥ ayam iti tasya vyavaccheda artham uktam avyapadeśyam iti 
NK_173.7–173.8	 pramitiḥ guṇa doṣa mādhyasthya darśanam guṇa darśanam upādeya tva jñānam doṣa darśanam heya tva jñānam mādhyasthya darśanam na heyam na upādeyam iti jñānam pramitiḥ padārtha svarūpa bodhe sati upakāra ādi smaraṇāt sukha sādhana tva ādi viniścaye sati upādeya ādi jñānam bhavat padārtha svarūpa bodhasya eva phalam bhavati sukha smaraṇa ādīnām avāntara vyāpāra tvāt yathā uktam antarāle tu yaḥ tatra vyāpāraḥ kārakasya saḥ iti 
NK_173.9	 anye tu evam āhuḥ yadarśasya sukha sādhana tva jñānam tat guṇa darśanam upādeya tva jñānam api tat eva yat duḥkha sādhana tva jñānam tad doṣa darśanam heya tva jñānam api tat eva yat ca na sukha sādhanam na ca duḥkha sādhanam etat iti jñānam tad mādhyasthya darśanam upekṣā jñānam api tat eva sarvam ca etat abhyāsa pāṭava upetasya vyāpti smaraṇam anapekṣamāṇasya vastu svarūpa grahaṇa mātrāt eva ananu saṃhita liṅgasya aparokṣa avabhāsitayoḥ pādāt abhyāsa pāṭava sahakāriṇaḥ pratyakṣasya phalam iti 
NK_174.1–174.2	 liṅga darśanāt sañjāyamānam laiṅgikam liṅga darśanāt sañjāyamānam laiṅgikam darśana śabdaḥ upalabdhi vacanaḥ na cākṣuṣa pratīti vacanaḥ anumita anumānasya api sambhavāt liṅga darśanāt liṅga viṣayaḥ saṃskāraḥ jāyate kintvasya na parigrahaḥ buddhi adhikāreṇa viśeṣita tvāt saṃśabdena samyak artha vācinā saṃśaya viparyaya smṛtīnām vyudāsaḥ liṅgasya darśanāt jñānāt samyak jāyamānam laiṅgikam iti vākya arthaḥ tasya ca jñānasya samyak jātīyasya yathā artha paricchedaka tayā utpāgaḥ sarva dhiyām yathā artha parisshedaka tvasya kula dharma tvāt saṃśaya viparyayau tāvat yathā asau= arthaḥ na tathā tad paricchintaḥ smṛtiḥ api artha paricchedikā na bhavati anubhava pāratantryāt iti vakṣyāmaḥ anye tu vidyā adhikāreṇa saṃśaya viparyayau vyudasyanti anartha jāyāḥ ca smṛteḥ vyudāsa artham atat hi dravya ādiṣu padārtheṣu utpadyate a iti āvarttayanti tat ayuktam vākya labhye arthe prakaraṇasya anapekṣaṇāt anartha ja tvāt smṛti vyudāde ca atīta āgata viṣayasya laiṅgika jñānasya api vyudāsa prasaṅgāt 
NK_175.1–175.3^1	 liṅgam punar yat anumeyena sambaddham prasiddham ca tad anvite tat abhave ca na asti eva tat liṅgam anumāpakam liṅgasya lakṣaṇam āha liṅgam punar iti anumeyaḥ pratipipādayiṣita dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī tena yat sambaddham tasmin vartate iti arthaḥ yathā vipaṣa eka deśe vartamānam api liṅgam vipakṣa vṛtti bhavati evam pakṣa eka deśe vartamānam anumeyena sambaddham eva tatas caturvidhāḥ paramāṇavaḥ anityāḥ gandhat tvāt iti asya api bhaga asiddhasya hetu tvam prāpnoti iti ced na vaidharmyāt yaḥ sādhya sādhana vyāvṛtti viṣayaḥ arthaḥ sa vipakṣaḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāvṛttiḥ na samuditebhyaḥ kintu pratyekam eva sambhavati iti pratyekam eva vipakṣatā pakṣaḥ tu sa bhavati yatra vādinā sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ pratipādayitum iṣyate 
NK_175.3^2	 na ca vādinā pārthiva paramāṇau ekasmin anitya tvam pratipādayitum iṣyate kintu catuṣru api paramāṇuṣu iti samuditānām eva pakṣa tve sthite asiddha vat bhāga asiddhasya api vyudāsaḥ anumeya sambandha abhāvāt prasiddham ca tad anvitaḥ iti tat iti yogya tvāt sādhya tvāt sādhya dharmaḥ parāmṛśyate tad anvite sādhya dharma anvite sa pakṣe prasiddham parijñātam iti viruddha asā dhāraṇayoḥ vyavacchedaḥ tad abhave ca na asti eva iti atra api tat iti sādhya dharmasya eva parāmarśaḥ tasya sādhya dharmasya abhāve na asti eva na punar eka deśe asti api iti anaikāntika vyavacchedaḥ tad liṅgam anumāpakam anumeyasya jñāpakam 
NK_176.1–176.2	 viparītam atas yat syāt ekena dvitayena vā viruddha asiddha sandigdhamaliṅgam kāśyapaḥ abravīt yat anumeyena arthena deśa viśeṣe kāla viṣeṣe vā sahacaritam anumeya dharma anvite ca anyatra sarvasmin eka deśe vā prasiddham anumeya viparīte ca sarvasmin pramāṇataḥ asat eva tat aprasiddhārthasya anumāpakam liṅgam bhavati iti 
NK_176.3	 liṅgam vyākhyāya liṅga ābhāsam vyācaṣṭe viparītam atas yat syāt iti atas ukta lakṣaṇat liṅgāt yat ekena dvitayena vā liṅga lakṣaṇena viparītam rahitam viruddham asiddham sandigdham tat kaśyapa ātmajaḥ aliṅgam anumeyā pratipādakam abravīt asiddham anumeye na asti anaikāntakam vipakṣāt avyāvṛttam iti anayoḥ ekena liṅga lakṣaṇena viparīta tvam viruddham sa palṣe na asti vipakṣāt avyāvṛttam iti tasya dvitayena liṅga lakṣaṇena rahita tvam 
NK_176.4	 yat anumeyena sambaddham iti śloka artham vivṛṇoti yat anumeyena iti anumeyena arthena sādhya dharmiṇā saha yad deśa viśeṣe kāla viśeṣe vā sahacaritam sambaddham anumeya dharma anvite ca anyatra sa pakṣe sarvasmin eka deśe vā prasiddham pramāṇena pratītam anumeya viparīte ca sādhya vyāvṛtti viṣaye ca arthe sarvasmin pramāṇataḥ asat eva tad aprasiddhārthasya sādhya dharmiṇya pratītasya arthasya sādhya dharmasya anumāpakam liṅgam bhavati yāvati deśe kāle vā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi liṅgasya sādhya dharmeṇa āvinābhāvaḥ nidarśitaḥ tāvatī eva deśe kāle vā sādhya dharmiṇi pratīyamānasya gamaka tvam iti pratipādana artham uktam deśa viśeṣe kāla viśeṣe va sahacaritam iti sarva sapakṣa vyāpaka vat sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ api hetu tva artham sarvasmin eka deśe va prasiddham iti uktam samasta vipakṣa vyāpaka vat vipakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ api ahetu tva avat yotana artham sarvasmin= asat eva iti padam 
NK_176.5–176.7	 kecid pravādukāḥ evam vadanti na avaśyam pramāṇa siddhaḥ vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ eva eṣṭavyaḥ ayatra idam na asti tatra idam api na asti a iti vacanāt api sādhya vyāvṛttyā sādhana vyāvṛtti pratīti sambhavāt tathā ca teṣām grantham tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte aneṣṭaḥ avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ tad abhave api tat na iti vacanāt api tad gateḥ iti tad nivṛtti artham pramāṇataḥ iti sādhya viparīte yat pramāṇataḥ asat tat liṅgam na tu vāc mātreṇa iti arthaḥ pramāṇa śūnyasya vacana mātrasya sarvatra sambhave hetu hetvābhāsa vyavasthā anupapatti prasaṅgaḥ ati vyāpakam idam liṅga lakṣaṇam prakaraṇa same kāla atyaya apadiṣṭe ca bhāvāt iti ced 
NK_176.8^1	 atra āha kaścid prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭau= anaikāntikaḥ eva antarbhavataḥ saṃdigdha vipakṣe sādhya dharmiṇi prakaraṇa samasya bhāvān niścita vipakṣe ca kāla atyaya apadiṣṭasya pravṛtteḥ tathā ca prakaraṇa samaḥ ayataḥ prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ a prakriyete prastūyeta iti prakaraṇe pakṣa pratipakṣau tayoḥ cintā vicāraḥ sā yad kṛtā sa nirṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ ubhaya pakṣa sāmyāt na prakaraṇa samaḥ anyatara pakṣa nirṇayāya kalpate 
NK_176.8^2	 yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ anitya dharma anupalabdheḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ nitya dharma anulabdheḥ iti śabde nitya anitya dharmayoḥ anupalambhāt nitya anitya tva saṃśaye sati tidvicāraḥ abhūt antyatara dharma grahaṇe tattva niścayāt vicārasya apravṛtteḥ tatra anitya dharma anupalambhaḥ nitya tva viniścaya artham upadiṣṭaḥ nitya dharma anupalambhaḥ anitya tva viniścaya artham upadiṣṭaḥ nitya dharma anupalambham pratipakṣam anativartamānaḥ na nirṇayāya kalpate tad pratibandhāt sa ca ayam saṃbhavat pratipakṣe dharmiṇi vartamānaḥ ekasmin= ante niyataḥ na bhavati iti anaikāntikaḥ evam kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ api anaikāntikaḥ pratyakṣa niścita uṣṇa tve vahnau vipakṣe kṛtaka tvasya bhavāt 
NK_176.9^1	 etat ayuktam yadi pakṣa vyāpaka tve sati sa pakṣe sadbhāvaḥ vipakṣāt ca tasya vyāvṛttiḥ iti etāvatā eva hetoḥ gamaka tvam tadā astu nāma sādhya dharmiṇi pratipakṣa sambhāvanā tathā api prakaraṇa samena sva sāmarthyāt sādhyam sādhayitavyam eva atha na śaknoti sādhayitum pratipakṣa saṃśaya ākrānta tvāt na tarhi trairūpya mātreṇa gamaka tvam iti asat pratipakṣa tvam api rūpa antaram āstheyam sati pratipakṣe hetu tva abhāvāt asati tad bhāvāt evam kāla atyaya apadiṣṭe api vācyam yadi trairūpya mātreṇa liṅga tvam kṛtaka tvāt vahnau= anuṣṇa tvam asti eva iti katham anaikāntika tvam 
NK_176.9^2	 atha sati api kṛtaka tve vahnau= anuṣṇa tvam na bhavati pratyakṣeṇa eva uṣṇatā pratītiḥ tadā pratyakṣa avirodhe sati pratipādanam na tad virodhaḥ iti abādhita viṣaya tvam api rūpa antaram anusaraṇīyam tasmāt anyathā ucyate pakṣaḥ nāma sādhya paryāyaḥ sādhyam ca tat bhavati yat sādhanam arhati sambhāvyamāna pratipakṣaḥ ca arthaḥ na sādhanam arhati vastunaḥ dvairūpya abhāvāt iti ayama pakṣa dharmaḥ eva tathā pratyakṣa ādi viruddhaḥ api pakṣaḥ na bhavati rūpa antareṇa siddhasya rūpa antareṇa sādhanān arha tvāt atas prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa avapakṣa dharmau= ubhau ayat anumeyena sambaddham a iti anena eva parāhatau anumeya ābhāsa āśraya tvāt 
NK_177.1^1	 nanu evam api alakṣaṇam idam avyāpaka tvāt trividhaḥ hi hetuḥ anvayī vyatirekī anvaya vyatirekī ca iti tatra anvayī viśeṣaḥ abhidheyaḥ prameya tvāt sāmānya vat asya hi pakṣāt anyaḥ sarve eva sat asat prabhedaḥ sa pakṣaḥ pramātṛ mātrasya pramāṇa mātra apekṣayā anabhidheyasya aprameyasya abhāvāt yaḥ ca puruṣa mātrasya anabhidheyaḥ aprameyaḥ ca sa vāji viṣāṇa vat asan eva na vā asan sa pakṣaḥ vipakṣaḥ vā sa syāt niḥsvabhāva tvāt yaḥ ca san sa sarvaḥ sa pakṣaḥ eva iti tad abhave ca na asti eva iti avyāpakam lakṣaṇam vyatireka abhāvāt ca āgamakam eva tat iti ced na anvaya avi abhicārāt anyasya sadbhāvāt anyasya siddhiḥ iti atra anvayaḥ kāraṇam tasya tu vyabhicāra pratītiḥ apavādikā 
NK_177.1^2	 asti tāvat prameya tva abhidheya tvayoḥ anvayaḥ sarvatra prameye abhidheya tvasya darśanāt na ca vyabhicāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na api śaṅkām ārohati yam yam vyatireka viṣayam buddhi gocarīkaroti parasya ca vaktum icchati tasya sarvasya prameya tva abhidheya tva prāpteḥ na ca asti viśeṣaḥ vipakṣe satya vyabhicāraḥ kāraṇam na vipakṣa abhāvāt iti tena prameya tvam abhidheya tvam gamayati vyatirekī ca sātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvāt iti asya pakṣāt anyaḥ sarmaḥ eva vipakṣaḥ tathā api hetu tvam viparyaya sambandha avi abhicārāt ghaṭa ādiṣu aprāṇa ādimattvena nirātmaka tvasya vyāptiḥ apagatāḥ aprāṇa ādimattvasya ca jīvat śarīre nivṛttiḥ pratīyate tad pratītyā tat vyāptasya nirātmaka tvasya nivṛtti anumānam 
NK_177.2^1	 atha manyase yaḥ arthaḥ na avagataḥ tad vyatirekaḥ api na śakyate pratyetum pratiṣedhasya vidhi viṣaya tvāt ātmā ca na kvacid avagataḥ katham tasya ghaṭa ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛtti pratītiḥ iti tat ayuktam parasya tāvat samasta vastu viṣayam nairātmyamisshataḥ ghaṭa ādibhyaḥ siddhā eva ātma vyāvṛttiḥ svasya api jīvat śarīteṣu eva ātmanaḥ buddhi ādibhiḥ kāryaiḥ saha kārya kāraṇa bhave siddhe ghaṭa ādibhyaḥ buddhi ādi vyāvṛttyā tad utpādana samarthasya viśiṣṭa ātma sambandhasya abhāva siddhiḥ yathā dhūma abhāve kvacid tad utpādam ayogyasya vahneḥ abhava siddhiḥ yadi evam ātmā api jīvat śarīreṣu siddhaḥ eva sambandhi pratītim antareṇa sambandha pratīteḥ asambhāvāt tatas ca vyatireki anumāna vaiyarthyam niṣpādi kriye karmaṇi sādhanasya sādhana nyāya atipātāt 
NK_177.2^2	 na evam sva siddhasya ātmanaḥ param pratyasiddhasya sādhya tvāt na ca anvaya avi abhicāraḥ pratipādakaḥ na vyatireka avyabhicāraḥ iti asti niyama hetuḥ tasmāt vyatirekiṇaḥ api hetu tvāt tena prasiddham ca tad anvite iti avyāpakam atra eke samāna tantra prasiddhyā kevala anvayinaḥ kevala vyatirekiṇaḥ ca parigrahaḥ iti vadanti apare tu vyasta samastam lakṣanam varṇayanti anumeyena sambaddham prasiddham ca tad anvitaḥ iti anvayinaḥ lakṣaṇam anumeyena sambaddham tad viparīte ca na asti eva iti vyatirekiṇaḥ iti samastam lakṣaṇam anvaya vyatirekiṇaḥ iti sādhya sādhana tvam sāmānya lakṣaṇam trayāṇam yathā pramāṇānām yathā artha paricchedaka tvam sāmānya lakṣaṇam 
NK_178.1–178.2	 yat tu yathā uktāt tri rūpāt liṅgāt ekena dharmeṇa dvābhyām vā viparītam tat anumeyasya adhigame liṅgam na bhavati iti etat eva āha sūtrakāraḥ aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ asan sandigdhaḥ ca anapadeṣaḥ iti viparītam atas yat syāt iti dvitīya ślokasya artham vivṛṇoti yat tu yathā uktāt tri rūpāt liṅgāt ekena dharmeṇa dvābhyām va dharmābhyām viparītam tat anumeyasyāt digame liṅgam na bhavati iti etat eva āha sūtrakāraḥ aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ asata sandigdhaḥ ca anapad eṣaḥ iti apadeśaḥ hetuḥ na bhavati iti apadeśaḥ ati anapadeśaḥ ahetuḥ iti arthaḥ aprasiddhaḥ iti viruddha asā dhāraṇayoḥ parigrahaḥ tayoḥ sādhya dharmeṇa saha prasiddhi abhāvāt ahetutvam asan iti asiddhasya avarodhaḥ sa hi sa pakṣe sādhya dharmeṇa saha prasiddhaḥ api dharmiṇi vṛtti abhāvāt ahetuḥ sandigdhaḥ ca iti anaikāntika abhidhānam sa hi dharmiṇi dṛśyamānaḥ kim sādhya dharma sahacaritaḥ kim vā tat rahitaḥ iti samdigdhaḥ bhavati na punar ekam dharmam upasthāpayitum śaknoti ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt ahetuḥ 
NK_179.1–179.2	 vidhiḥ tu yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ agni abhave dhūmaḥ api na bhavati iti evam prasiddha samayasya asandigdha dhūma darśanāt sāhacarya anusmaraṇāt tad anantaram agni adhyavasāyaḥ bhavati iti idam anena avinābhūtam iti jñānam yasya na adti tam dharmiṇi dharmasya anvaya vyatirekavataḥ api liṅga tvam na vidyate tad artham avinā abhāva smaraṇam anumeya pratītau= upāyaḥ iti darśayati vidhiḥ tu iti 
NK_179.3	 vidhiḥ tu anumeya pratīti prakāraḥ tu yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ agni abhāve dhūmaḥ na bhavati iti evam prasiddha samayasya prasiddha avinā bhāvasya puruṣasya asandigdha dhūma darśanāt dhūmaḥ eva ayam na bāṣpa ādikam iti jñānāt sāhacarya anusmaraṇādyatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti evam anusmaraṇāt agni adhyavasāyaḥ bhavati tad anantaram agni anumānam bhavati nanu evam dvitīyaḥ liṅga parām arthaḥ na labhyate mā alambhi na hi naḥ tena prayojanam liṅga darśana vyāpti smaraṇābhyām eva anumeya pratīti upapatteḥ na ca smṛti anantara bhāvi tvāt anumeya pratītiḥ aniyata diś deśā syāt liṅga darśanasya niyāmaka tvāt na api upanaya vaiyarthyam avayava antaraiḥ apratipāditasya pakṣa dharma tvasya pratipādana artham para artha anumāne tasya upanyāsāt 
NK_180.1–180.2	 api bhoḥ ! kaḥ ayam avinābhāvaḥ nāma avyabhicāraḥ sa kasmāt bhavati tādātmya tad utpattibhyām iti saugatāḥ yādṛcchikaḥ sambandhaḥ yathā eva bhavati na bhavati api tathā ca niyama hetoḥ abhāvaḥ tatra yadi nāma sa pakṣe darśanam adarśanam ca vipakṣe tathā api avyabhicāraḥ na śakyate jñātum vipakṣa vṛtti śaṅkāyāḥ anivāraṇāt tad utpatti viniścaye tu śaṅkā nivāryate kāraṇena vinā kāryasya ātma lābha asaṃbhavāt tad utpatti vinaḥ cayaḥ api kārya hetiḥ pañca pratyakṣa upalambhānupalambha sādhanaḥ kāryasya utpatteḥ prāc anupalambhaḥ kāraṇa upalambhe sati upalambhaḥ upalabdhasya paścāt kāraṇa anupalambhāt anupalambhaḥ iti kāryasya dvau anupalambhau ekaḥ upalambhaḥ kāraṇasya ca upalambhānupalambhau iti evam upalambha anupalambhaiḥ pañcabhiḥ sati eva agnau dhūmasya bhāvaḥ asati abhāvaḥ iti niścīyate kāryasya etat eva kāryatvam yat tasmin sati eva bhāvaḥ asati abhāvaḥ iti tādātmya pratītyā api avinā abhāvaḥ niścīyate bhāvasya svabhāva vyabhicāre niḥsvabhāva tva prasaṅgāt 
NK_180.3–180.6	 tādātmya niścayaḥ vipakṣe bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttyā siddhyati apravṛtte tu bādhake śataśas saha bhāva darśane api kadācid etat vipakṣe syāt iti śaṅkāyāḥ kaḥ nivārayitā tat uktam kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhāva nimaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt niyāmakāt svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinābhāvasya niyamaḥ na sa pakṣe darśanāt vipakṣe ca adarśanāt iti 
NK_180.7	 atra ucyate kim yatra tādāymi atat utpattī tatra avyabhicāraḥ kim vā yatra avyabhicāraḥ tatra tādātmya tad utpattī na tāvat ādyaḥ kalpaḥ sati api tad utpāde dhūma dharmasya pārthiva tva ādeḥ agni vyabhicārāt sati api tādātmye vṛkṣa tvasya śiṃśapā vyabhicārāt atha yatra avyabhicāraḥ tatra tādātmya tad utpattī tarhi avyabhicāre siddhe tayoḥ gamaka tvam evam ced avyabhicāraḥ eva astu gamakaḥ kim tādātmya tad utpattibhyām kāryam api hi na kāryam iti eva gamayati iti na api svabhāvaḥ svabhāvaḥ iti kintu tat avyabhicāri iti avyabhicāraḥ eva gamaka tve kāraṇam na tādātmya tad utpattī vyabhicārāt na ca evam upapattim ārohati dhūmaḥ vahninā kriyate na pārthiva tva ādayaḥ tad dharmā iti vastunaḥ nirbhāga tvāt na api etat upalabdham śiṃśapā vṛkṣa ātmikā na vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapa ātmakaḥ dhava khadira ādi dhāraṇa tvāt iti tayoḥ abhedāt 
NK_180.8–180.10	 yadi ca dhava ādi sādhāraṇī vṛkṣa tā na śiṃśapā tvam tadā na anayoḥ eka tvam svabhāva bhedasya bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt abhede tu yathā vṛkṣa tvam sarva vṛkṣa sādhāraṇam tathā śiṃśapā tvam api syāt na ca tādātmye gamya gamaka bhāve vyavasthā yuktāḥ tasya abheda āśraya tvāt yadi śiṃśapā tve gṛhyamāṇe vṛkṣa tvam agṛhītam kva tādātmyam gṛhītam ced tat kva anumānam atha ucyate yathā avasthitaḥ dharmī śiṃśapā tvam vṛkṣa tvam ca trayam eka ātmakam eva tatra dharmiṇi gṛhyamāṇe śiṃśapātva vat vṛkṣa tvam api gṛhītam eva yathā uktam tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ bhāgaḥ kaḥ anyaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate iti 
NK_180.11^1	 yadi param śiṃśapā vikalpaḥ jātaḥ na vṛkṣa vikalpaḥ sa vṛkṣa śabda smṛti abhāva aparādhāt śiṃśapā śabda saṃskāra prabodha janmanā śiṃśapā vikalpena ca aśiṃśapā vyāvṛtti paryavasitena na avṛkṣa vyāvṛttiḥ upanīyate sarva vikalpānām paryāyatva prasaṅgāt gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ ca vyāvṛttyoḥ anayoḥ na bhedāt atas yathā ukta doṣa anupapattiḥ iti aho pūrva apara anusandhāne param kauśalam paṇḍitānām tādātmyam anumāna bījam sādhya sādhana bhūtayoḥ vyāvṛttyoḥ parasparam bhedaḥ iti kim idam indrajālam vṛkṣa śiṃśapāyoḥ tādātmyam tad ātmatayā ca adhyavasthitayoḥ avṛkṣa vyāvṛttya śiṃśapā vyāvṛttyoḥ sati api bhede yathā adhyavasāyam tādātmyam iti ced 
NK_180.11^2	 siddhe tādātmye satya śiṃśapā vyāvṛttyā dharmiṇya vṛkṣa vyāvṛttiḥ adhyavaseyāḥ tatra adhyavasitāyām ca avṛkṣa vyāvṛttau yathā adhyavasāyam tādātmya siddhiḥ iti anyonya āśraya doṣaḥ vyāpti grahaṇa velāyām eka ātma tayā adhya vasitayoḥ vyāvṛttyoḥ tādātmya siddham iti ced tathā api anayoḥ abhedaḥ kālpanikaḥ yadi anumānam kalpanā samāropeṇa api pravartteta na kaścid ahetuḥ nāma prameya tva anitya tvayoḥ api eka ātma tayā adhyavasitayoḥ yathā adhyavasāyam tādātmya saṃbhavāt vipakṣa vyāvṛtti abhāvāt prameya tvasya anitya tvena saha tādātmya abhāvaḥ iti ced satyam vāstavam tādātmyam na asti kalpanā samāropitam tāvat asti eva tat eva anumāna udaya bāndhavam samarthitavantaḥ yūyam iti vipakṣāt avyāvṛttiḥ asat samā 
NK_180.12	 api ca tādātmyasya tad utpādasya ca yasya pratītiḥ vipakṣe hetu abhāva pratītyai tad abhāva pratītiḥ api dṛśya anupalabdheḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca anumāna antarbhūta tvāt sva sādhyena vipakṣe hetu abhāvena saha tādātmya pratītyā tad utpāda pratītyā vā pravartate tasyāḥ api sva sādhyena tādātmya tad utpāda niścayaḥ vipakṣe vṛtti abhāva pratītyai tad abhāva pratītiḥ ca anupalabdhi antara sā apekṣā yāvān pratiṣedhaḥ sa sarvaḥ api anupalabdhi viṣayaḥ iti abhyupagamāt tatas ca anavasthāpātāt vyatireka asiddhau tādātmya tad utpāda asiddheḥ na svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā hetuḥ kiñca tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ abhāve api kṛttikā udaya rohiṇī a staṅgamanayoḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ pratīyate tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā niyamaḥ svabhāvāt vā iti anāla ucita abhidhānam 
NK_181.1^1	 svabhāvena hi kasyacid kenacid saha sambandhaḥ niyataḥ nirupādhika tvāt upādhikṛtaḥ hi sambandhaḥ tad apagamāt nivartate na svābhāvikaḥ yadi dhūmasya upādhikṛtaḥ vahni sambandhaḥ upādhayaḥ upalabdhāḥ syuḥ śiṣya ācāryayoḥ iva pratyāsattau= adhyayanam na hi vahni dhūmayoḥ asakṛt upalabhyamānayoḥ tad upādhinām anupalambhe kiñcid bījam asti na ca upalabhyamānasya niyamena anupalabhyāḥ bhavanti upādhayaḥ te hi yadi sva rūpa mātra anubandhinaḥ tathā api avyabhicāra siddhiḥ tad kṛtasya api sambandhasya yāvat dravya bhāvi tvāt atha āgantukāḥ tad kāraṇāni api pratīyeran upādhayaḥ tad kāraṇāni ca sarvāṇi atīndriyāṇi iti gurvī iyam kalpanā 
NK_181.1^2	 yasya ca upādhayaḥ na santi sa dhūmaḥ kadācid svatantraḥ api upalabhyeta yathā ārdra indhana upādhi kṛta dhūma sambandhaḥ vahniḥ śuṣka indhana kṛta ādhipatyaḥ vidhūmaḥ pratyavamṛśyate na ca tathā sa vid antare dhūmaḥ kadācid niragniḥ ābhāti tasmāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānām upādhīnām anupalambhāt abhāva pratītau upalabdhānām deśa kāla indhana avasthā viśeṣāṇām punar punar darśaneṣu vyabhicārāt ahetu tva niścaye sati nikhila deśa kāla ādi viśeṣa ādi prahāṇena upādhi abhāva upalabdhi bhūyas sahabhāva darśana ja saṃskāra sahakāriṇā nirasta pratipakṣa āśaṅkena carama pratyakṣeṇa dhūma sāmānyasya agni sāmānyena svabhāva mātra adhinam sahabhāvam niścinvānaḥ idam anena niyatam iti niyamam niścinoti 
NK_181.2	 yadi api prathama darśane api sahabhāvaḥ gṛhītaḥ tathā api na niyama grahaṇam na hi sahabhāva mātram niyamaḥ api tu nirupādhikam sahabhāvaḥ nirupādhika tvam ca tasya bhūyas darśana abhyāsauvaseyam iti antena bhūyas sahabhāva grahaṇa bala bhuvā sa vikalpaka pratyakṣeṇa saḥ adhyavasīyate iti etena pratyakṣasya vidyamāna viṣaya tvāt atīta anāgatāsu vyaktiṣu katham niyama grahaṇam iti pratyuktam na hi viśeṣa niṣṭham vyāpti grahaṇam ācakṣmahe viśeṣa hānyā sāmānyena vyāpti grahaṇe tu sarvatra eva nirviśaṅkaḥ pratyayaḥ tasya sarvata eka rūpa tvāt kim vyaktayaḥ vyāptau= apraviṣṭāḥ eva kaḥ vai brūte na praviṣṭāḥ iti kintu sāmānya rūpa tayā na viśeṣa rūpeṇa atas eva dhūna saṃvittyā vahni mātram eva anusandadhānaḥ tam anudhāvati na viśeṣam ādriyate yadi tu sāmānyena sarvatra niścite api niyame niṣprāmāṇikā eva āśaṅkā kriyate tadā tvad pakṣe api pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭāsu vahni dhūma vyaktiṣu gṛhīte api kārya kāraṇa bhāve deśa kāla vyavahitāsu tad bhāva sandehāt anumāna pravṛttim kaḥ nivārayati 
NK_181.3^1	 atha ucyate bhūyas darśanena kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ nirddhāryate sakṛt darśanena tad upādhi jatva śaṅkāyāḥ anivartanāt bhuyaḥ darśanam ca sāmānya viṣayam kṣaṇikānām vyaktīnām punar punar darśana abhāvāt tena anagni vyāvṛttasya adhūma vyāvṛttasya ca sāmānya viṣayaḥ kārtakāraṇa bhāvaḥ ekatra niścīyamānaḥ sarvatra viniścitaḥ bhavati sāmānyasya eka tvāt iti ced asmābhiḥ api ittham eva sarvatra niścīyamānaḥ niyamaḥ kim bhavadbhyaḥ na rocate kiñca bhavatī pratyakṣa agocaraḥ sāmānyena kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ anubhavataḥ avastu tvāt vyaktayaḥ tādṛśyaḥ 
NK_181.3^2	 tāḥ tu sarvān apratyakṣeṇa gṛhyante na ca atīta anāgatānām vyaktīnām manasā saṃkalanam iti nyāyyam manasaḥ bahis artheṣu svātantrye andha badhira ādya bhāva prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭāsu vyaktiṣu kārya kāraṇa bhāva adhyavasāye ca dṛāṭāsu na anumāna udayaḥ tad anya tvāt na api vyaktīnām sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ parasparam ananvita tvāt na ca tāsām ekena sāmānyena upagrahaḥ vastu avastunoḥ samvandha abhāvāt asambaddhasya upagrahaka tve ca atiprasaṅgāt tat kiṃviṣayaḥ pratyakṣa sādhanaḥ tad utpāda viniścayaḥ yasmāt anumāna pravṛttiḥ iti na vidmaḥ 
NK_182.1–182.2	 evam sarvatra deśa kāla avinābhūtam itarasya liṅgam śāstre ca kātyādi grahaṇam vidarśana artham kṛtam na avadhāraṇa artham kasmāt vyatireka darśanāt tat yathā adhvaryurom śrāvayan vyavahitasya hotuḥ liṅgam candra udayaḥ samudra vṛddheḥ kumuda vikāsasya ca śaradi jala prasādaḥ agastya udayasya iti evamādi tat sarvam asya idam iti sambandha mātra vacanāt siddham 
NK_182.3	 evam sarvatra deśa kāla avinābhūtam itarasya liṅgam yathā dhūmaḥ vahniḥ liṅgam evam deśāvinābhūtam kālāvinābhūtam ca itarasya sādhya dharmasya liṅgam yathā kāśmīreṣu suvarṇa bhāṇḍa agārika puruṣaiḥ yava vāṭikā saṃrakṣaṇam yava nāleṣu kema aṅkura udbhedasya liṅgam kālāvinābhūtam yathā prāgjyotiṣa adhipateḥ veśmani jayanāndīninādaḥ nṛpati prabodhasya liṅgam 
NK_182.4	 yadi deśa kāla avinā bhāva mātreṇa gamaka tvam nanu sutra virodhaḥ asya idam kāryam kāraṇam saṃyogi virodhi samavāyi ca iti laiṅgikam iti tatra āha śāstre kārya ādi grahaṇam nidarśana artham kṛtam na avadhāraṇa artham iti asya idam iti sūrya ādīnām upādānam liṅga nidarśana artham kṛtam na tu etāvanti eva liṅgāni iti avadhāraṇa artham katham etat iti āha kasmāt iti uttaram āha vyatireka darśanāt iti kārya adi vyatirekeṇa api anumāna darśanāt na avadhāraṇa artham sūtram yatra kārya ādīnām vyatirekaḥ tat darśayati yathā adhvari urom śrāvayan vyavahitasya hotuḥ liṅgam iti adhvaryuḥ hotā aramom iti evam śrāvayati na anyam iti evam yasya pūrvam avagatiḥ abhūt tasya om iti śrāvayantam adhvaryum pratītya kuḍya ādi vyavahite hotari anumānam hotā api atra asti iti na ca adhvaryuḥ hotuḥ kāryam na kāraṇam na saṃyogī na ca virodhī na samavāyī ca iti vyatirekaḥ 
NK_182.5	 udāharaṇa antaram āha candra udayaḥ samudra vṛddheḥ ityādi yadā candraḥ udeti tadā samudraḥ varddhate kumudāni ca vikasanti iti niyamaḥ yena avagataḥ tasya candra udayaḥ samudra vṛddheḥ kumuda vikāsasya ca liṅgam syāt na ca candra udayaḥ samudra vṛddhi kumuda vikāsayoḥ kāryam udayaḥ hi candrasya viśiṣṭa deśa saṃyogaḥ sa ca candra kriyā kāryaḥ na samudra vṛtti ādi nimittaḥ na ca ayam samudra vṛddheḥ kāraṇam na api kumuda vikāsasya utkallola lakṣaṇāyāḥ vṛddheḥ patrāṇām paraspara vibhāga lakṣaṇasya ca vikāsasya tad kāla sannihita kāraṇa adhīna karma janya tvāt ityādi vācyam śaradi jala prasādaḥ agastya udayasya jalasya prasādaḥ vaimalyam tat śaradi pratīyamānam agastya udayasya liṅgam na kāla antare vyabhicārāt 
NK_182.6	 kārya ādi vyatiriktam api yadi liṅgam asti tarhi nyūnam sūtram sarva liṅgānām anavarodhāt atas āha evamādi tat sarvam asya idam iti sambandha mātra vacanāt siddham iti adhryuḥ oṃśrāvayan evam ādi yat avinābhūtam liṅgam tat sarvam asya idam iti padena sambandha mātra vacanāt siddham parīgṛhītam artha antaram artha antarasya liṅgam iti na yujyate bhavati ced ati prasaktiḥ syāt iti paryanuyogam āśaṅkyā it am uktam sūtrakāreṇa asya idam iti liṅgam iti anyatva aviśeṣe api asya sādhyasya idam sambandhi iti kṛtvā asya idam liṅgam na sarvasya iti sāmānyena sambandhi mātrasya liṅga tva pratipādanāt yat dyasya deśa kāla ādi avinābhūtam tat tasya liṅgam iti uktam tat eva hi tasyavyat yasya avyabhicāri yat yena vyabhicāri na tat tasya anyatra api bhāvāt api bhoḥ ! kim asya idam kāryam iti na sambandhaḥ na iti brūmahe kārya ādi grahaṇam tarhi kimartham nidarśana artham iti uktam avaśyam hi śiṣyasya udāharaṇa niṣṭham kṛtvā kim api avyabhicāri liṅgam darśanīyam iti sūtre kārya ādikam udāhṛtam na tu etāvanti eva liṅgāni iti arthaḥ 
NK_183.1–183.3	 tat tu dvividham dṛṣṭam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca tatra dṛṣṭam prasiddha sādhyayoḥ jātyabhede anumānam yathā gavi eva sāsnām upalabhya deśa antare api sāsnā mātra darśanāt gavi pratipattiḥ prasiddha sādhyayoḥ atyanta jāti bhede liṅga anumeya dharma sāmānya anuvṛttitaḥ anumānam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam yathā karṣaka vaṇigrāja putuṣāṇām pravṛtteḥ phalavat tvam upalabhya varṇa āśramiṇām api dṛṣṭam prayojanam anuddiśya pravartamānānām phala anumānam iti 
NK_183.4–183.5	 bhedam kathayati tat tu dvividham dṛṣṭam sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam ca iti nu śabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ tad anumānam dvividham eva dṛṣṭam ekam aparam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam tatra tayoḥ madhye dṛṣṭam prasiddha sādhyayoḥ jātya bhede anumānam prasiddham yat pūrvam liṅgena saha dṛṣṭam sādhyam yat samprati anumeyam tayoḥ atyanta jāti abhede sati yat anumānam tat dṛṣṭam yathā gavyā iva sa asnā mātram upalabhya deśa antare gavi pratipattiḥ pūrvam go tva jāti viśiṣṭāyām eva go vyaktau sāsnā upalabdhyā samprati api go tva jāti viśiṣṭāyāḥ eva go vyakteḥ anumānam atyanta jāti abhede idam ca dṛṣṭam iti ākhyāyate 
NK_183.6^1	 sāsnā mātra darśanāt vana antare yat anumīyate go tva sāmānyam tasya sva lakṣaṇam pūrvam nagare dṛṣṭam iti kṛtvā prasiddha sādhyayoḥ atyanta jāti bhede liṅga anumeya dharma sāmānya anuvṛttitaḥ anumānam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam prasiddham liṅgena saha pratītam sādhyam anumeyam tayoḥ atyanta jāti bhede sati liṅgam ca anumeya dharmaḥ ca liṅga anumeya dharmau yatoḥ sāmānye liṅga anumeya dharma sāmānye tayoḥ anuvṛttiḥ liṅga anumeya sāmāni anuvṛttiḥ tatas liṅga sāmānyasya sādhya sāmānyena saha āvinā abhāvāt yat anumānam tat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam 
NK_183.6^2	 yathā karṣaka vaṇi grāja puruṣāṇām pravṛtteḥ phalatvam upalabhya varṇa āśramiṇām api dṛṣṭam prayojanam anuddiśya pravartamānānām phala anumānam karṣaka ādi pravṛtteḥ phalam dṛṣṭvā varṇa āśramiṇām pravṛtteḥ api phala anumānam karṣakasya pravṛtteḥ phalam śasya ādikam vaṇijaḥ rāja puruṣasya ca pravṛtteḥ phalam kāñcana maṇi muktā vāji vāraṇa ādikam varṇa āśramiṇām ca pravrptteḥ phalam svarga ādikam iti anayoḥ atyanta jāti bhedaḥ anumāna udayaḥ tu pravṛtti tva sāmānyasya phalavat tva sāmānyena āvinā abhāvāt atas eva ca idam sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ucyate sāmānyena niyama darśanāt 
NK_183.7	 yaḥ punar atra anumeyaḥ svarga ādi lakṣaṇaḥ phala viśeṣaḥ na etat jātīyasya phalasya niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ varṇa āśramiṇām pravṛtteḥ api jīvikā mātram eva prayojanam iti bārhaspatyāḥ tad artham āha dṛṣṭam prayojanam anuddiśya iti santi eva tathāvidhāḥ puruṣāḥ ye khalu dṛṣṭa nispṛhāḥ vānaprastha ādikam vratam ācarantih teṣām pravṛtteḥ idam phala anumānam iti na siddha sādhyatā iti arthaḥ 
NK_184.1–184.3	 tatra liṅga darśanam pramāṇam pramitiḥ agni jñānam athavā agni jñānam eva pramāṇam pramitiḥ agnau guṇa doṣa mādhyasthya darśanam iti etat sva niścita artham anumānam prāmāṇa śabdaḥ karaṇa vyutpatti siddhaḥ na phalam vinā paryavasyati atas pramāṇa phala vibhāgam darśayati tatra liṅga darśanam pramāṇam iti tatra āmāne liṅga jñānam pramāṇam pramīyate anena iti vyutpattyā pramitiḥ pramāṇasya phalam agni jñānam yadi api liṅga liṅgi jñānayoḥ utpatti apekṣayā viṣaya bhedaḥ tathā api liṅga jñānasya api liṅgini jñāna utpattau vyāpārāt liṅgi viṣaya tvam tatas ca pramāṇa phalayoḥ na vyadhikaraṇa tvam prakāra antaram āha athavā iti agni jñānam pramāṇam pramitiḥ pramāṇasya phalam agnau guṇa doṣa mādhyasthya darśanam guṇa darśanam sukha sādhanam etat iti jñānam doṣa darśanam duḥkha sādhana tva jñānam mādhyasthya darśanam sukhduḥkha sādhana tva abhāva jñānam agni jñāne sati tathā aprati iti utpādāt etat sva niścita artham anupānam niścitam iti bhāve niṣṭhā sva niścita artham sva niścaya artham etat anumānam iti arthaḥ 
NK_185.1–185.2	 śabda ādīnām api anumāne antarbhāvaḥ samāna vidhi tvāt yathā prasiddha samayasya liṅga darśana prasiddhi anusmaraṇābhyām atīndriye arthe bhavati anumānam evam śabda ādibhyaḥ api iti śabda ādīni api pramāṇa antarāṇi saṅgirante pravādinaḥ tāni kasmāt iha na uktāni iti paryanuyogam āśaṅkya teṣām atra eva antarbhāvāt pṛthak anabhidhānam iti āha śabda ādīnām api iti śabda ādīnām anumāne antarbhāvaḥ anumāna avyatireki tvam samāna vidhi tvāt samāna pravṛtti prakāra tvāt yathā vyāpti grahaṇa balena anumānam pravartate tathā śabda ādayaḥ api iti arthaḥ śabdaḥ anumānam vyāpti balena artha pratipādaka tvāt dhūma vat samāna vidhi tvam eva darśayati yathā iti prasiddhaḥ samayaḥ avinā abhāvaḥ yasya puruṣasya tasya liṅga darśana prasiddhi anusmaraṇābhyām liṅga darśanam ca yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti evam bhūtāyāḥ prasiddheḥ anusmaraṇam ca tābhyām yathā atīndriye arthe bhavati anumānam tathā śabda ādibhyaḥ api iti tāvat hi śabdaḥ na artham pratipādayati yāvat ayasya avyabhicārī iti evam na avagamyate jñāne tu avyabhicāre pratipādayan dhūmaḥ iva liṅgam syāt 
NK_185.3	 atra āha kaścid anumāne sādhya dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī pratīyate śabdāt artha anumāne kaḥ dharmī na tāvat arthaḥ tasya tadānīm apratīyamāna tvāt śabdaḥ dharmī iti ced kim asya sādhyam arthavat tvam ced na parvata ādeḥ eva vahni ādinā śabdasya arthena saha saṃyoga samavāya ādi lakṣaṇaḥ kaścid sambandhaḥ nirūpyate yena ayam artha viśiṣṭaḥ sādhanīyaḥ pratipādya pratipādaka bhāvaḥ eva hi tayoḥ sambandhaḥ saḥ artha pratīti uttara kālīnaḥ na artha pratipādanāt pūrvam sambhavati naca agni dhūmayoḥ eva śabda arthayoḥ asti avinābhāva niyamaḥ deśa kāla vyabhicārāt tad vyabhicāraḥ ca asati api yudhiṣṭhire kalau yudhiṣṭhira śabda prayogāt asat yām api laṅkāyām jambudvīpe laṅkā śabda śravaṇāt tasmāt anumāna sāmagrī vailakṣaṇyāt śabdaḥ na anumānam itas api śabdaḥ na anumānam deśa viśeṣe sva artha vyabhicārāt na dhūmaḥ vahnim kvacid vyabhicarati śabdaḥ tu sva artham vyabhicarati tathā hi cauraḥ iti bhakta abhidhānam dākṣiṇātyānām āryāvarta nivāsinām tu taskara abhidhānam 
NK_185.4–185.5^1	 yadi ca śabdaḥ anumānam trairūpya pratītyāḥ asya prāmāṇya niścayaḥ syāt na āpta ukta tva pratītyai tad pratītyā tu niścīyamāne prāmāṇye anumānāt vyatiricyate eva vaidharmyāt atra ucyate yat ūrdhvīkṛtāyām tarjanyām deśa kāla vyavahiteṣu artheṣu daśa saṃkhyā anumānam na tatra daśa saṃkhyā dharmiṇī apratīyamāna tvāt na api tarjanī vinyāsaḥ dharmī tasya pratipādyamānayā daśa saṃkhyayā sambandha antara abhāvena tad viśiṣṭa pratipādana ayogāt na api anayoḥ eka deśa tā na api eka kāla tvam katham anumāna pravṛttiḥ kraya vikraya vyavahāre vaṇijām tathāvidha tarjanī vinyāsasya daśa saṃkhyā pratipādana abhiprāya avi abhicāra upalambhāt karttuḥ tad pratipādana abhiprāya avagati mukhena asya daśesaṃkhyā pratīti hetu tvam iti ced śabdasya api evam eva 
NK_185.5^2	 prathamam go śabdāt uccāritāt vaktuḥ kakudādi mad artha vivakṣā gamyate sva santāne go śabda uccāraṇasya padārtha vivakṣā pūrvaka tva upalambhāt tad artha vivakṣayā ca artha anumānam ayam ca atra prayogaḥ puruṣaḥ dharmī kakudādi mad artha vivakṣāvān go śabda uccāraṇa karttṛ tvāt aham iva iti artha abhāve api anāptānām vivakṣā upalabdheḥ na vivakṣātaḥ artha siddhiḥ iti ced śabdāt api katham tad siddhiḥ bhrāntyā vipralambha dhiyā vā artha śūnyasya śabdasya prayogāt āpta uktāt śabdāt artha pratītiḥ iti ced āpta abhiprāyāt eva arthasya adhigatiḥ iti samānam 
NK_185.6	 yaḥ tu sati api liṅga tve deśa viśeṣe śabdasya arthasya vyabhicāraḥ na dhūmasya tatra eṣa nyāyaḥ dhūmaḥ svābhāvikena sambandhena agneḥ liṅgam śabdaḥ tu ceṣṭā vat puruṣa icchā kṛtena saṅketena pravartamānaḥ yatra yatra arthe puruṣeṇa saṅketyate tasya tasya eva arthasya vivakṣā adhigati dvāreṇa liṅgam atas eva asmāt āpta prayukta tva anusāreṇa ceṣṭātaḥ iva artha niścayaḥ sātatya ūrdhva gati ādi dharma viśiṣṭasya iva dhūmasya āpta uktasya eva śabdasya artha avi abhicāra sambhavāt 
NK_185.7^1	 śabdasya artha pratipādaka tvam eva mukhyayā vṛttyā kim na kalpyate sambandha abhāvāt asambaddhasya gamaka tve ca atiprasaṅgāt śabda arthayoḥ asti svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ iti ced na śabdasya ekasya deśa bhedena nānā artheṣu prayogāt yatra āyama arthaiḥ prayujyate tatra asya vācaka tvam itaratra saṅketa anurodhāt pravṛttasya liṅga tvam iti ced na tulyaḥ eva tāvat caura śabdaḥ taskare bhakte ca pratīti karaḥ tatra asya taskare vācaka tvam bhakte ca liṅga tvam iti na asti viśeṣa hetuḥ 
NK_185.7^2–185.8	 āryāṇām api caura śabdāt artha pratītiḥ liṅga pūrvikā caura śbda janita pratipatti tvāt ubhaya abhimata dākṣiṇātya prayujyamāna caura śabda janita pratipatti vat na ca svābhāvika sambandha sadbhāve pramāṇam asti śabdasya vācyaniṣṭhā svābhāvikī vācikā śaktiḥ eva ubhayatra datta pada tvāt sambandhaḥ iti ucyate bhavadbhiḥ yathā uktam śaktiḥ eva hi sambandhaḥ iti śabda śakteḥ ca svabhāvāt eva vācya niṣṭha tve vyutpanna vat avyutpannaḥ api śabdāt artham pratīyāt śabdasya arthasya tayoḥ sambandhasya ca saṃbhavāt jñātaḥ sambandhaḥ artha pratyaya hetuḥ na sattā mātreṇa iti ced yathā uktam jñāpaka tvāt hi sambasdhaḥ sva ātma jñānam apekṣate tena asau vidyamānaḥ api na agṛhītaḥ prakāśakaḥ iti 
NK_185.9	 kīdṛśam tasya sambandhasya jñānam asya śabdasya ayam arthaḥ vācyaḥ iti evaṃbhūtam iti ced tat kasmāt bhavati vṛddha vyavahārāt iti ced etat eva abhidhāna abhidheya ālambana jñānam parasparam vyavaharadbhiḥ vṛddhaiḥ pārśva sthasya bālakasya kriyamāṇam saṅketaḥ vyutpattiḥ iti ca abhidhīyamānam saṃskāra dvāreṇa artha pratīti kāraṇam astu kim sambandha antareṇa śabdasya hi nijam sāmarthyam śabda tvam āgantukam nu sāmarthyam saṅketaḥ viśiṣṭā ca ānupūrvī tasmāt eva ca sāmarthya dvitayāt tad artha pratyaya upapatteḥ sambandha antara kalpanā vaiyarthyam dṛṣṭāt kārya upapattau= adṛṣṭa kalpa nāna vakāśāt 
NK_186.1–186.2	 aśruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ api āmnāyaḥ vaktṛ prāmāṇya apekṣaḥ tad vacanāt āmnāya prāmāṇyam a liṅgāt ca anityaḥ buddhi pūrvā vākya kṛtiḥ vede buddhi pūrvaḥ dadātiḥ iti ukta tvāt nanu yadi vaktṛ dvāreṇa śabdaḥ artha avabodhakaḥ tadā veda vākyāt artha pratyayaḥ na ghaṭate vaktuḥ abhāvāt atas āha śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ api āmnāyaḥ vaktṛ prāmāṇya apekṣaḥ iti na kevalam laukikaḥ āmnāyaḥ śruti smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ api āmnāyaḥ vaktuḥ prāmāṇyam apekṣya pratyāyakaḥ śabdaḥ vaktra dhīna doṣaḥ na tu ayam asurabhi gandha vat svabhāvataḥ eva duṣṭaḥ yathā uktam 
NK_186.3–186.4	 śabde kāraṇa varṇa ādeḥ doṣāḥ vaktṛ narāśrayāḥ na hi svabhāvataḥ śabdaḥ duṣṭaḥ asuḥ abhigandha vat nitya tve vedasya vaktuḥ abhāvāt doṣāṇām anavakāśe sati nirāśaṅkam prāmāṇyam siddhyati pauruṣeya tve tu nirvicikitsam prāmāṇyam na labhyate kadācid puruṣāṇām rāga dveṣa ādibhiḥ ayathārthasya api vākyasya darśanāt tatra āha tad vacanāt āmnāyasya prāmāṇyam iti tat iti anāgata avekṣaṇa nyāyena na ca asmad buddhibhyaḥ liṅgam ṛṣeḥ iti sūtre pratipāditasya asmad viśiṣṭasya vaktuḥ parāmarśaḥ tad vacanāt tena viśiṣṭena puruṣeṇa praṇayanāt āmnāyasya vedasya prāmāṇyam 
NK_186.5	 ayam abhisandhiḥ doṣa abhāva prayuktam prāmāṇyam na nitya tva prayuktam sati api nitya tve śrotra manasoḥ āgantuka soṣaiḥ kvacid aprāmāṇyāt asati api nitya tve pramṛṣṭa doṣāṇām cakṣuḥ ādīnām prāmāṇyāt doṣāḥ ca puruṣa viśeṣe na eva santi iti upapāditam tena tad prayuktasya āmnāyasya sati api pauruṣeya tve prāmāṇyam na hi yathārtha draṣṭā prakṣīṇa rāga dveṣaḥ kṛpāvān upadeśāya pravṛttaḥ ayathārtham upadiśati iti śaṅkām ārohati 
NK_186.6	 puruṣa viśeṣa praṇītaḥ vedaḥ iti kutas eṣā pratītiḥ iti sarvaiḥ varṇa aśramibhiḥ avigānena tad artha parigrahāt yad kiñcana puruṣa praṇīta tve tu vedasya buddha ādi vākya vat na sarveṣām parīkṣakāṇām avigānena tad artha anuṣṭhānam syāt kasyacid aprāmāṇya avabodhena visaṃvāda pratīteḥ api sambhavāt yatra ca sarveṣām saṃvāda niyamaḥ tad pramāṇam eva yathā pratyakṣa ādikam pramāṇam vedaḥ sarveṣām avisaṃvādi jñāna janaka tvāt pratyakṣa vat yat tu dṛṣṭa artheṣu karmasu anuṣṭhānāt kvacid phala adarśanam na tat asya prāmāṇyam pratikṣipari sāmagrī vaiguṇya nibandhana tvāt tad nibandhana tvam ca yathāvat sāmagrī sambhave sati phala darśanāt 
NK_186.7–186.8	 āpta ukta tvam āmnāyasya iti na yuktam tad artha anuṣṭhāna kāle abhiyuktaiḥ anuṣṭhātṛbhiḥ smṛtya yogyasya kartuḥ asmaraṇāt abhāva siddheḥ atas āha liṅgāt ca anityaḥ iti tad vacanāt āmnāya prāmāṇyam iti atra uktam āmnāya padam prakṛta tvāt iha sambadhyate liṅgāt āmnāyaḥ anityaḥ gamyate iti arthaḥ liṅgam upanyasyati buddhi pūrvā vākya kṛtiḥ vedaḥ iti vede vākya kṛtiḥ vākya racanā buddhi pūrvikā vākya racanā tvāt laukika vākya racanā vat liṅga antaram āha buddhi pūrvaḥ dadātiḥ iti ukta tvāt vede dadāti śabdaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ dadātiḥ iti ukta tvāt laukika dadā ati śabda vat 
NK_186.9	 yat ca idam asmaryamāṇa kartṛka tvāt iti tat asiddham prajāpatiḥ vā idam ekaḥ āsīt na aharāsīt na rātriḥ āsīt sa tapaḥ atapyata tasmāt tapaḥ tapanāt catvāraḥ vedāḥ ajāyante iti āmnāyena eva kartṛ smaraṇāt jīrṇa kūpa ādibhiḥ vyabhicārāt ca tat evam anitya tve vedasya siddhe puruṣa vacasām dvaita upalambhāt prāmāṇya sandehe sati dṛṣṭe viṣaye kadācid artha sandehāt pravrpttiḥ bhavati api adṛṣṭe tu viṣaye pacuḥ avitta vyaya śarīra āyāsa sādhye tāvat prekṣāvān na pravartate yāvat tad viṣayasya vākyasya prāmāṇyam na avadhārayati dṛṣṭam ca loke vacasaḥ prāmāṇyam vaktṛ guṇa avagati pūrvakam tena vede api tathā eva prāmāṇyāt nirvicikit samanuṣṭhānam syāt 
NK_187.1	 straike vadanti na āpta ukta tva nibandhanam vacasaḥ pramāṇyam sarva pramāṇānām svatas eva prāmāṇyāt iti te idam praṣṭavyāḥ prāmāṇyam eva tāvat kim ucyate kimartha avyabhicāraḥ kim vā yathā artha paricchedaka tvam na tāvat artha avyabhicāraḥ sati api vahni niyata tve dhūmasya kutaścid nimittāt anutpādita agni jñānasya prāmāṇya abhāvāt nīla pīta ādiṣu pratyekam vyabhicāre api cakṣuṣaḥ yathā artha jñāna janaka tvena eva prāmāṇyāt 
NK_187.2^1	 atha yathā artha paricchedaka tvam prāmāṇyam tat kim svatas jñāyate svatas vā jāyate kim vā svatas vyāpriyate yadi tāvat jñānena sva prāmāṇyam svayam eva jñāyeta yathā artharicchedakam aham asmi iti na pramāṇe yathārtham idam ayathārtham vā iti saṃśayaḥ kadācid api syāt viparyaya jñāne ca pravṛttiḥ na bhavet atha sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt ātma ām agṛhṇa dvijñānam ātmanaḥ yathā artha paricchedaka tvam na gṛhṇāti tarhi tad paricchedāya param apekṣitavyam pramāṇena vinā prameya pratīteḥ abhāvāt pramāṇasya api pramīyamāna daśāyām prameya tvāt iti paratas prāmāṇyam eva pareṇa prāṃāṇye jñāmāṇye tasya api prāmāṇyam apareṇa jñeyam tasya api anyena iti anavasthā iti ced na anavasthā sarvatra prāmāṇye jijñāsā abhāvāt 
NK_187.2^2–187.3	 pramāṇam hi sva utpattyā eva artham paricchinatti na jñāta prāmāṇyam tena tu arthe paricchinne api yatra kutaścid nimittāt pramāṇam idam apramāṇam vā iti saṃśaye jāte viṣaya sandehāt puruṣasya apravṛttiḥ tatra asya pravṛtti artham kāraṇa antarāt pramāṇi ajijñāsā bhavati anavadhārite prāmāṇye saṃśaya anucchedāt yatra punar atyanta abhyāsa pāṭavāt akhila viśeṣa grahaṇāt vā pramṛṣṭa sandeha kalaṅka lekham eva pramāṇam udeti tatra tad utpatti avārtha niścaye pramātuḥ nirākāṅkṣa tvāt prāmāṇya pratipitsā eva na asti iti na pramāṇa antara anusaraṇam yaḥ tu tatra api jñānasya ubhayathā darśanena sandeham āropayati sa na śaknoti āropayitum tad artha niścayena eva parāhata tvāt yathā āha maṇḍanaḥ brahma siddhau anāśvāsaḥ hi vijñāne jñānena eva apabādhyate iti 
NK_187.4	 yadi pravṛtti artham prāmāṇyam jijñāsyate yatra anavadhārita prāmāṇyasya eva artha saṃśayāt pravṛttiḥ abhūt tatra artha prāpti parituṣṭasya prāmāṇye jijñāsā na asti katham pravṛtti sāmarthyāt pramāṇasya arthavat tva avadhāraṇam na tatra api karṣakasya iva bīja parīkṣā artham prāmāṇya parīkṣā artham eva pravṛttasya asti evam tad arthitāḥ jñāne yasya tu prāmāṇya sandehāt arthe sanda hānasya artha grahaṇa artham eva pravṛttiḥ jātā tasya artha prāpti carita arthasya anabhisaṃhitam api prāmāṇya avadhāraṇam vastu sāmarthyāt bhavati pravṛtti sāmarthyasya prāmāṇya avi abhicārāt tat evam tāvat prāmāṇyam svatas na jñāyate na api svatas jāyate yadi jñānam utpadya paścāt sva ātmani yathā artha paricchedaka tvam janayati pratipadyemahi tasya svatas pramāṇa tām yathā artha avabodha svabhāvasya eva tasya svīya kāraṇāt utpattim paśyantaḥ para apekṣam eva tasya prāmāṇyam manyāmahe 
NK_187.5^1	 atha manyase pramāṇam svayam eva svasya prāmāṇyam janayati iti svatas pramāṇa tvam na brūmaḥ api tu jñānam prāmāṇya utpādāya sva utpādaka kāraṇa kalāpāt anyat na apekṣate iti svatas prāmāṇyam etat api asat yadi hi anyūna anatirikta jñāna utpādikā eva sāmagrī prāmāṇye kāraṇam viparyajñānam kutas yathā artha jñāna jananam kāraṇānām svabhāvaḥ sa yadā doṣaiḥ pracyāvyate tadā tāni ayathārtha jñānam janayanti yadā tu svabhāva pracyuti hetavaḥ doṣāḥ na bhavanti tadā teṣām yathārtha jñāna jananam eva svabhāvaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate iti ced 
NK_187.5^2	 tat kim vaktṛ jñāna mātrāt eva tad pūrvake vākye yathārtha tā utpādaḥ nanu evam sati sarvam eva vākyam avitatham syāt atha pramāṇa jñānāt vākye yathārtha tā utpādaḥ na tarhi kāraṇa svarūpa mātrāt prāmāyam api tu tad guṇāt śabdasya kārāam artha jñānam tasya guṇaḥ yathārtha tvam ayathārtha tvam ca doṣaḥ tatra yathārtha tāyāḥ vākya prāmāṇya hetu tve kāraṇa guṇāt eva tasya prāmāṇyam na sva rūpa mātrāt śabdasya ca guṇāt prāmāṇye jñāna antarāṇām api tathā eva syāt vivāda adhyāsitāni vijñānāni kāraṇa guṇa adhīna pramāṇyāni pramāṇa jñāna tvāt śabda adhīna pramāṇa jñāna vat 
NK_187.6^1	 śabde api kāraṇa guṇasya doṣa abhāve vyāpāraḥ na prāmāṇya utpattau= iti ced na guṇḥ na doṣa pratibandhāt doṣa kāryasya ayathārtha tvat pattiḥ mā bhūt yathārtha tva utpādaḥ tu kutas kāraṇa abhāve hi kārya abhāvaḥ na tu viparītasya kāryasya bhāvaḥ jñāna svarūpa mātrāt iti ced na tasya aviśeṣāt artha sambandhaḥ hi jñānasya viśeṣaḥ sa ced doṣa pratibandha mātra upakṣīṇa tvāt yathārtha tā utpattau= anaṅgam svarūpasya aviśeṣāt na artha viśeṣa niyatam vākyam syāt aviśeṣa dviśeṣa siddheḥ abhāvāt atha yad artha viṣayam jñānam tad artha viṣayam eva tat vākyam janayati iti tadā jñānasya yathārtha tā eva vākyasya yathārtha tā hetuḥ na bodha rūpa tā mātram iti āyātam tasya guṇāt eva prāmāṇyam 
NK_187.6^2–187.7	 astu vā guṇasya doṣa abhāve vyāpāraḥ tathā api paratas prāmāṇyam na hīyate tad utpattau sarvatra kāraṇa svabhāva vyatiriktasya doṣa abhāvasya api anvaya vyatirekābhyām sāmarthya ādhāraṇāt doṣa abhāvāt viparyaya abhāvaḥ prāmāṇyam tu indriya ādi svarūpa mātra adhinam iti ced deṣaḥ prāmāṇya utpattiḥ pratibadhyate viparyayaḥ punar indriya ādi svarūpa adhīnaḥ eva iti kasmāt na kalpyate doṣa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvāt viparyayasya na evam kalpanā iti ced prāmāṇyasya api doṣa abhāva anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tva darśanāt na tad kalpanā iti samānam na hi tat asti prāmāṇam yad doṣāṇām prāgabhāvam pradhvaṃsa abhāvam na apekṣate evam pravṛtti ādi kārya janana vyāpāraḥ api pramāṇasya paratas eva na sva rūpa mātra adhīnaḥ upakāra apakāra ādi sāpekṣasya pravṛtti ādi karya janaka tvāt iti eṣā diś 
NK_188.1–188.2	 prasiddha abhinayasya ceṣṭayā pratipatti darśanāt tat api anumānam eva hastasya avāṅmukha ākuñcana āhvānam pratīyate parāṅmukha utkṣepaṇāt ca visarjana pratītiḥ bhavati etad pramāṇa antaram icchanti kecid tān pratyāha prasiddha abhinayasya iti kara ākuñcana ādi lakṣaṇaḥ abhinayaḥ anena abhiprāyeṇa kriyata ti evam yat puruṣasya prasiddhaḥ abhinayaḥ tasya ceṣṭayā karavinyāsena āhvāna visarjana ādi pratītiḥ dṛśyate na anyasya atas tat api ceṣṭayā jñānam anumānam eva 
NK_189.1–189.2	 āptena aprasiddhasya gavayasya gavā gavaya pratipādanāt upamānam āpta vacanam eva upamānasya anumāne antarbhāvam kurvan= āha āptena aprasiddhasya gavayasya gavā gavaya pratipādanāt upamānam āpta vacanam eva āptiḥ sākṣa ādarśasya prāptiḥ yathārtha upalambhaḥ tayā varttate iti āptaḥ sākṣātkṛta dharmāḥ yathādṛṣṭasya arthasya cikhyā apayiṣayā prayukta upadeṣṭā tena āptena vanecareṇa vidita gavayena aprasiddha gavayasya ajñāta gavayasya nāgarikasya kīdṛś gavayaḥ iti pṛcchataḥ gavā go sārūpyeṇa gavayasya pratipādanāt upamānam yathā gauḥ gavayaḥ tathā iti vākyam āpta vacanam eva vaktṛ prāmāṇyāt eva tatra artha pratīteḥ āpta vacanam ca anumānam tasmāt upamānam api anumāna avyatiriktam iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NK_189.3–189.4	 ye tāvat pūrvam īmāṃsakāḥ vanecara vacanam eva upamānam āhuḥ teṣām idam anumānam eva ye api śabara svāmi śiṣyāḥ anubhūtasya gopiṇḍasya vane gavaya darśanāt smṛti ārūḍhāyām gavi amadīyā gauranena sadṛśī a iti sārūpya jñānam upamānam ācakṣate tat api smaraṇam eva sādṛśyam hi sāmānya vat pratyekam vyakti samāptam na saṃyoga vat ubhayatra vyāsajya vartate gopiṇḍasya adarśane api vane gavaya vyaktau go sadṛśaḥ ayam iti prati iti utpādāt yathā uktam mīmāṃsā gurubhiḥ 
NK_189.5–189.6	 sāmānya vat ca sādṛśyam eka ekatra samāpyate pratiyogini adṛṣṭe api yasmāt tat upalabhyate iti pratyekam parisamāpta tve api sādṛśyasya yadi api gavaya grahaṇa abhāvāt gavaya sadṛśaḥ ayam iti gavi pūrvam pratītiḥ na āsīt tathā api sva āśraya sannikarṣa mātra bhāvinī sādṛśya pratītiḥ uditā eva yathā pratiyogi antara agrahaṇāt tasmāt idam dīrgham idam hrasvam iti pratyaya abhāve api sva āśraya pratyāsatti mātreṇa parimāṇasya svarūpataḥ grahaṇam katham anyathā deśa antara gataḥ pratiyoginam gṛhītvā asmāt tat dīrgham hrasvam iti ca adhyavasyati 
NK_189.7	 yadi gavi purā sādṛśyam indriya āpāta mātreṇa na gṛhītam samprati api gavaye na gṛhyate gavaya darśanāt eva gavyā iva ca smaraṇam iti ubhaya niyamaḥ na syāt aviśeṣāt yāvatām khura lāṅgūli tva ādi sāmānyānām gavi grahaṇam tāvatām eva gavaya api grahaṇāt smaraṇa niyamaḥ iti ced bhūyas avayava sāmānyāni eva ubhaya vṛtti tvāt sādṛśyam tāni ced pratyekam āśraya grahaṇena gṛhītāni gṛhyante gṛhītam eva sādṛśyam tasmāt gavaya grahaṇe satya sannihita go piṇḍa avalambinī sādṛśya pratītiḥ sadṛśa darśana abhivyakta saṃskāra janyā smṛtiḥ eva na pramāṇa antaram dṛṣṭā ca nirvikalpaka gṛhītasya api smṛti viṣaya tā avyutpanneka piṇḍa grahaṇe prathamam avikalpitasya sāmānyasya piṇḍa antara grahaṇe pratyabhijñānāt 
NK_189.8^1	 ye api śruta atideśa vākyasya gavaya darśinaḥ go sādṛśya pratītyāḥ aasya gavaya śabdaḥ nāmadheyam a iti saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha pratītim upamānam icchanti teṣām api yathā gauḥ gavayaḥ tathā iti vākyam tad janatā ca aloke yaḥ khalu iti śrūyate sa go sadṛśaḥa iti buddhiḥ āgamaḥ eva yat api go sadṛśasya gavaya śabda vācya tva jñānam tat api anumānam tatra tad śabda prayogāt yaḥ khalu śabdaḥ yatra abhiyuktaiḥ avigānena prayujyate sa tasya vācakaḥ prayujyate ca āraṇyakaiḥ avigānena go sadṛśe gavaya śabdaḥ iti 
NK_189.8^2	 tasmāt saḥ api gavaya śabda vācyaḥ eva iti sāmānyena jñānam anumānam eva pratyakṣe gavaye sādṛśya jñānam trailokya vyāvṛtta piṇḍa buddhar api pratyakṣa phalam yat ca tad gata tvena saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha anusandhānam tat api s ā d ṛ ś y a g r a h a ṇ ā b h i v y a k t a p ū r v ī p a j ā t a s ā m ā n y a p r a v ṛ t t a g o s a d ṛ ś a g a v a y a ś a b d a v ā c y a t v a j ñāna janita saṃskāra ja tvāt ekatra upajāta sāmānya viṣaya saṅketa jñāna saṃskāra kṛta tad jātīya piṇḍa antara viṣaya rat śabda vācya tva anusandhāna vat smaraṇam eva evam hi tadā ayam anusandhatte aasya eva tat mayā pūrvam etat śabda vācya tvam avagatam a iti upamāna abhāvaḥ 
NK_190.1–190.3^1	 darśana arthāt arthapattiḥ virodhyeva śravaṇāt anumita anumānam dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā arthaḥ anyathā na upapadyate iti artha antara kalpanā iti arthāpattiḥ śruta grahaṇasya pṛthak abhidhāna sāphali anupapādayatā pareṇa artha āpattiḥ ubhayathā upapāditā dṛṣṭa artha āpattiḥ śruta arthāpattiḥ ca yatra arthaḥ anyathā anupapadyamānaḥ artha antaram gamayati sā dṛṣṭa artha āpattiḥ yathā jīvati caitraḥ gṛhe na asti iti atra abhāva pramāṇena gṛhe caitrasya abhāvaḥ pratītaḥ jīvati iti śruteḥ ca tatra sambhavaḥ api pratīyate jīvataḥ gṛha avasthāna upalambhāt na ca ekasya caitra ādeḥ yugapad ekatra bhāva abhāva sambhavaḥ tayoḥ saha anavasthāna virodhāt 
NK_190.1–190.3^2	 tat ayam abhāvaḥ pratīyamānaḥ jīvati iti śravaṇāt na upapadyate anupapadyamānaḥ ca yasmin sati upapadyate tata kalpayati jīvataḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ anyathā na upapadyate yadi ayam bahis na bhavati iti jīvati iti anena saha virodhaḥ eva tasya anupapattiḥ sā caitrasya bahirbhāve pratīte nivartate caitraḥ jīvati gṛhe ca na asti bahis sadbhāvāt iti sāvakāśa niravakāśayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ virodhe sati niravakāśasya anupapatti mukhena sa avakāśasya viṣaya antara upapādanāt tayoḥ avirodha āpādanam arthāpattiḥ yā punar deśa ādi niyatasya sambandhinaḥ darśanāt sambandha smaraṇa dvāraṇa sambandhi antara pratītiḥ sa anumānam iti anayoḥ bhedaḥ jñāna udaya prakāra bhedāt 
NK_190.4–190.7	 yathā uktam anvaya adhīna janma tvam anumāne vyavasthitham arthāpattiḥ iyam tu anyā vyatireka pravartinī iti tathā śruta arthāpattiḥ api yatra anupapadyamānaḥ śabdaḥ śabda antaram kalpayati yathā apīnaḥ divā na bhuṅkte a iti vākyāt rātrau bhuṅkte iti vākya kalpanā tatra dṛṣṭa arthāpattim tāvat anumāne antar bhāvayati darśana arthāt arthāpatti virodhye avā iti dṛśyate iti darśanam darśanam ca tad artthaḥ ca iti darśana arthaḥ pañcabhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ eva avagataḥ arthaḥ tasmāt darśana artha dartha antarasya āpattiḥ artha antarasya avagatiḥ virodhi anumānam eva yasya yathā niyamaḥ tasya tathā eva liṅga tvam iha tu pramāṇa antara viruddhaḥ eva arthaḥ artha antarāvinābhūtaḥ iti virodhyeva liṅgam 
NK_190.8	 ayam abhiprāyaḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ yadi anupapatti mātreṇa bahirbhāvam kalpayati niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt artha antaram api kalpayet sva upapattye gṛha abhāvaḥ artha antaram kalpayati anyasmin kalpite ca na tasya upapattiḥ iti ced bahirbhāve sati tasya upapattiḥ iti api kena kathitam vayam tu brūmaḥ bahirbhāve api sati gṛha abhāvasya anupapattiḥ eva dṛṣṭam etat yat avyāpakam dravyam ekatra asti tat avyatra na asti iti yathā prācī pratīcyoḥ ekatra upalabhyamānaḥ savitā anyatra na bhavati iti idam darśana balena eva avadhāryate jīvataḥ gṛha abhāvaḥ gahirbhāve sati upapadyate na anyathā iti yadi evam anvayāvak ati pūrvikā eva tathā upapatti avagatiḥ tathā sati ca arthāpattiḥ anumānam eva anvaya adhīna janma tvāt yat tu virodhe sati pravartate iti tad vaidharmya mātram tathā ca atra prayogaḥ devadattaḥ bahis asti jīvana sambandhi tve sati gehe anupalabhyamāna tvāt aham iva iti 
NK_190.9	 śruta arthāpattim antar bhāvayati śravaṇāt anumita anumānam iti pīnaḥ divā na bhuṅkte iti vākya śravaṇāt rātri bhojana kalpanā aanumita anumānam a liṅga bhūtena vākyena anumitāt pīna tvāt tad kāraṇasya rātri bhojanasya anumānāt pīna tvam bhojana kāryam divā bhojane sati tat na upapadyate kāraṇa abhāvāt tad anupapattau ca vākyam api anupapannam ananvita artha tvāt iti ced tarhi artha anupapattiḥ vākyasya anupapanna tvam artha upapattiḥ ca upapanna tvam na tu asya sva rūpeṇa upapatti anupapattī divā na bhuñjānasya pīna tva lakṣaṇaḥ ca arthaḥ bhojana lātya tvāt rātri bhojana rūpeṇa arthena upapadyate na rātri bhojana vākyena iti arthasya anupapattyā tasya tad vākyasya ca upapatti hetuḥ arthaḥ eva arthanīyaḥ na vākyam anupapādaka tvāt arthyamānaḥ ca arthaḥ arthena eva avagamyate divā bhojanar ahitasya pīna tvasya rātri bhojana kārya tva avyabhicārāt iti na asti arthāpattiḥ śabda gocarā 
NK_190.10^1	 atha matam arthaḥ arthena eva upapadyate iti tad upapatya eva tad śabdasya api upapannatā kintu śābdaḥ arthaḥ śābdena eva arthena upapadyate pramāṇa antara avagatasya tena saha anvaya abhāvāt na hi pacati iti ukte kriyāyāḥ karmaṇā vinā anupapattiḥ pacyamānasya kalāyasya pratyakṣeṇa darśanāt upaśāmyati tasmin sati api kim pacati iti ākāṅkṣāyāḥ anivṛtteḥ śabda upanīte tu karmaṇi nirvicikitsaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati aśākam pacati kalāyam pacati a iti 
NK_190.10^2–190.13	 apīnaḥ divā na bhuṅkte a iti api vākya ārya anupapattiḥ iyam tasmāt asyāḥ śābdena eva arthena upaśāntiḥ bhaviṣyati iti prathamam arthāpattyā rātri bhojana pratipādakam vākyam eva prārthanīyam anyathā divā vākya padārthaiḥ saha rātri bhojanasya anvaya abhāvāt vākya viṣaye ca arthāpatti paryavasāne rātri bhojanam arthaḥ na arthāpatti viṣaya tām eti tasya vākyāt eva avagamāt na ca etat vācyam divā vākyasya tad arthasya vā rātri vākyena saha pratyasatti abhāvāt na tābhyām tad upasthāpanam iti artha pratyāsatti dvāreṇa vākyasya api pratyasanna tvāt na ca artha āpattau anumāna vat pratyāsattiḥ apekṣate tasyāḥ anupapatti mātreṇa eva pravṛttaḥ tat uktam na ca arthena arthaḥ eva ayam dvitīyaḥ gamyate punar sa vikalpaka vi jñāna grāhya tvāt tat tirohitaḥ śabda antarāṇi abuddhvā sā na artham eva avagacchati tena eṣā prathamam tāvat niyatam vākya gocarā vākyam eva tu vākya artham gata tvāt gamayiṣyati iti 
NK_191.1^1	 atra ucyate padāni vākya artha pratipādanāya prayujyate tāni pratyekam padārtha saṃsarga ātmakam vākya artham pratipādayitum aśaknuvanti aparyavasita vyāpāra tvāt eka artha kārīṇi pada antarāṇi apekṣante yatra punar amībhiḥ vākya arthaḥ pratipāditaḥ tatra eṣām śabda antara apekṣā na asti eva sva vyāpārasya kṛta tvāt yaḥ taiḥ pratipāditaḥ arthaḥ sa na upapadyate iti ced mā upapādi na hi arthasya avirodha upapādanam api śabdasya vyāpāraḥ kintu pratipādanam tat ca anena āsat nihite api rātri vākye kṛtam eva pratīyate hi divā abhojana vākyāt pīnasya abhojanam niḥsandigdhā abhra antā ca iyam pratītiḥ anyathā artha āpatteḥ api pravṛtti abhāvāt 
NK_191.1^2	 niścitya eva hi pīnasya divā abhojana pramāṇa siddhasya anupapattiḥ na yuktā iti tad upapādana artham arthyate sandigdhe viparīta tvena ca avadhārite tu asmin kasya upapattayaḥ artha antara kalpanā syāt na ca arthayoḥ paraspara virodhaḥ iti tayoḥ pratītiḥ apratītiḥ bhavati tasmāt artha pratītyā eva upapannaḥ śabdaḥ na śabda antaram apekṣate kartanya antara abhāvāt arthaḥ eva tu tena abhihitaḥ artha antareṇa vinā anupapadyamānaḥ prati iti anusāreṇa sva upapattaye tat mṛgayati iti su vyāhṛtam śabda śravaṇāt anumita anumānam iti 
NK_192.1–193.2	 sambhavaḥ api avinā abhāvi tvāt anumānam eva śatam sahasre sambhavati iti sambhava ākhyāt pramāṇa antarāt sahasre śata jñānam iti kecid tad nirāsa artham āha sambhavaḥ api avinābhauvi tvāt anumānam eva sahasram śatena avinābhūtam tad pūrvaka tvāt tena sahadrāt śata jñānam anumānam eva abhāvaaḥ api anumānam eva yathā utpannam kāryam kāraṇa sadbhāve liṅgam evam anutpannam kāryam kāraṇa asadbhāve liṅgam prameya abhāva pratītau bhava grāhaka pratyakṣa ādi pañca pramāṇām uttira bhāva ākhyam pramāṇa antaram kaiścid iṣṭam tat vyudasyati abhāvaḥ api anumānam eva atham iti atra āha yathā utpannam kāryam kāraṇa sadbhāve liṅgam evam anutpannam kāryam kāraṇa asadbhāve liṅgam jñānam jñeyasya kāryam tasya abhāvaḥ jñeya abhāvasya liṅgam yathā kāraṇasya liṅgam 
NK_193.3	 yaḥ api abhāvam pramāṇam icchati tasya api na jñāna nuta pāda mātrāt prameya abhāva jñānam sva rūpa viprakṛṣṭasya api vastunaḥ abhāva pratīti prasaṅgāt kintu jñāna kāraṇeṣu satsu jñāna yogyasya vastunaḥ jñānāni tpādaḥ abhāva avagama nimittam na ca ayogya anupalambhāt yogya anupalambhasya laścit svarūpataḥ viśeṣaḥ abhāvasya niratiśaya tvāt tena na ayam sva śaktyā eva indriya vat bodhakaḥ kintu yogyā anupalambhaḥ jñeya abhāvam na vyabhicarati ayogya anupalambhaḥ tu vyabhicarati satapi jñeye tasya sambhavāt etāvatā viśeṣeṇa yogyā anupalambhaḥ pratipādakaḥ na aparaḥ evam satyabhavaḥ liṅgam eva syāt avinā abhāva grahaṇa sāpekṣa tvāt tad anapekṣa tve tu aviśeṣeṇa sarvasya eva abhāvasya ābodhaka tvam iti durnivāraḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
NK_193.4	 api ca indriya sannikarṣāt upalabhyamāne bhū tale abhāva jñānam api bhavati aaghaṭam bhū talam a iti tatra bhū talasya iva abhāvasya api pratyakṣatā kim na iṣyate bhāva aṃśena eva indriyasya sambadhaḥ yogya tvāt iti ced na idam anupapāditam sidhyati kārya gamyā hi yogyatā yathā indriya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi kāryam bhāve dṛśyate tadvat abhāve api iti bhāvavat abhāvaḥ api indriya grahaṇa yogyaḥ eva kārya darśanāt eva ca asya indriya sambandhaḥ api kaścid kalpayiṣyate 
NK_193.5^1	 atha matam niradhikaraṇaḥ na kasyacid abhāvaḥ pratīyate deśa ādi niyamena pravṛtti nivṛtti darśanāt yat adhikaraṇaḥ ca ayam pratīyate tasya pratītau= indriya vyāpāraḥ na abhāva grahaṇe indriya vyāpāra uparame api abhāva pratīti darśanāt tathā āha kaścid svarūpeṇa devakula ādikam pratītya sthāna antaram gataḥ devakule devadattaḥ asti na asti iti kenacid pṛṣṭaḥ tadānīm eva jñāna jijñāsaḥ na asti iti pratyeti pratītya ca vyāharati na asti iti na ca pūrvam eva devakula grahaṇa samaye devadatta abhāvaḥ nirvikalpena gṛhītaḥ samprati smaryate iti vācyam yuktam ghaṭa ādīnām indriya sannikarṣāt nirvikalpena grahaṇam teṣām svarūpasya para anapekṣa tvāt 
NK_193.5^2	 abhāvasya tu pratiṣedha svabhāvasya svarūpam eva yasya ayam pratiṣedhaḥ tad adhīnam atas tad pratiṣedha tām antareṇa tad abhāvasya svarūpa antara abhāvāt tatra asya pratiyogi svarūpa nirūpaṇaṃntareṇa nirūpaṇam aśakyam ayam eva hi bhāva abhāvayoḥ viśeṣaḥ yat ekasya vidhi rūpa tayā grahaṇam aparasya tu anya praṣedha mukhena yat āha nyāya vārttikakārāḥ svatantra paratantra upalabdhi anupalabdhi kāraṇa bhāvāt ca viśeṣaḥ sat khalu pramāṇasya ālambanam svatantram asat tu paratantram anya pratiṣedha mukhena iti a yadi tu abhāvasya api svātantryeṇa grahaṇam tadā bhāvāt aviśeṣaḥ syāt atas na asti abhāvasya nirvikalpakena grahaṇam 
NK_193.6–193.7	 yat api vikalpitam kim devatta saṃkīrṇasya devakulasya pūrvam pratīra āsīt tad viviktasya vā saṃkīrṇa grahaṇe tāvat kevalasya na smaraṇam vivikta grahaṇe ca abhāvaḥ gṛhītaḥ eva paścāt smaryate iti prāptam tat api asāram devadatta bhāva abhāvayoḥ agrahaṇe api devakulasya sva rūpeṇa grahaṇāt tasmāt na pūrvam abhāva grahaṇam tad abhāvāt na smṛtiḥ na ca tadānīm pramāṇa antaram upalabhyate tasmāt vyavahite pratiyogini smṛrūḍhe abhāva grahaṇāya pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa pañcaka vyāvṛttiḥ eva pramāṇam ekatra ca abhāvasya abhāva paricchedya tve siddhe anyatra api tena eva setsyati iti siddham abhāvasya pramāṇa antara tvam 
NK_193.8–193.9	 atra ucyate deśa antaram gatam kenacid pṛṣṭaḥ devakule devadattatyedāni intana anupalambhena ida ani intana abhāvam pratyeti aidānīm na asti a iti kim vā prāktana anupalambhena prāktana abhāvam devakula grahaṇa samaye na āsīt iti idānīntana anupalabdhiḥ tāvat yogya anupalabdhiḥ na bhavati deśa vyavadhānāt samprati abhavaḥ api tatra devadattasya sandigdhaḥ āgamanasya api sambhavāt prāktana abhāva pariccheda yogyā tu prāktana anupalabdhiḥ na īdānīm anuvartate avasthā antara prāpteḥ na ca avidyamānā pratīti kāraṇam bhavitum arhati na api smṛti ārūḍhā vyāpriyate pūrvam asaṃvidita tvāt na hi anupalabdhiḥ pramāna antara saṃvedyā abhāva rūpa tvāt anupalabdhi antara apekṣāyām ca anavasthā syāt tasmāt iyam agṛhītā eva indriya vat artha paricchedikā iti rāddha antaḥ tathā sati kutas tayāḥ smaraṇam anubhava abhāvāt
