NK_193.10^1	 atha matam devakule devadatta anupalambhaḥ devadatta upalambhena nivartyate na ca deśa antara gatasya tad upalambhaḥ jātaḥ tasmāt asti eva tad anupalambhaḥ yadi tu avasthā antaram āpannaḥ na ca avasthā bhede vastu bhedaḥ iti astu tarhi tāvat iha evam yatra tu pūrvam pratiyogi smaraṇa abhāvāt vastu abhāvaḥ na gṛhītaḥ paścāt kāla antare vastu grahaṇa ādi ha idānīm na āsīt iti prāktana abhāva jñānam tatra kaḥ pratīkāraḥ nivṛttaḥ hi tad vastu anupalambhaḥ tasya upalambhena na ca anupalambhaḥ pūrvam āsīt iti samprati avidyamānaḥ api pratīti hetuḥ pranaṣṭa indriyasya api viṣaya grahaṇa prasaṅgāt 
NK_193.10^2	 adyatanena va tu upalambhena ca ādyatana anupalambhaḥ tasya nivartitaḥ prāktana anupalambhaḥ tu asti eva tena prāk kālīnābhāva pariccheda yogyena prāktana abhāvaḥ paricchidyate iti ced aho pāṇḍityam aho naipuṇyam anupalambhaḥ upalambha prāgabhāvaḥ sa ca vastu utpatti avadhiḥ ekaḥ eva na prāktanāt yatana kāla bhedena bhidyate tatra ādyatana anupalambhaḥ nivṛttaḥ prāktanaḥ na nivṛttaḥ iti kaḥ kuśa agrīya buddheḥ anyaḥ imam ati sūkṣma viveka lava gāhate tasmāt abhāvaḥ aparicchidyate iti na buddhyāmahe 
NK_193.11	 katham tarhi sva rūpa mātram gṛhītvā sthāna antaram gatasya smaryamāṇe pratiyoginyabhāva pratītiḥ anumānāt yaḥ hi yasmin pratiyogini smaryamāṇe smṛti yogyaḥ satyām api su smūrṣāyām na smaryate sa grahaṇa kāle na āsīt iti yathā kevale pradeśe smaryamāṇe tatra prāc pratītaḥ ghaṭaḥ asmaryamāṇaḥ na ca smaryate devakule smaryamāṇe satyām api susmūrṣāyām smṛti yogyaḥ api devadattaḥ tasmāt saḥ api devakula grahaṇa samaye na āsīt iti smṛti abhāvāt anumānam saha upalabdhayoḥ api vastunoḥ saṃskāra pāṭava ādi virahāt ekasya asmaraṇa parasya smaraṇam dṛṣṭam yathā adhītasya ślokasya ekasya pada antara asmaraṇe api pada antara smaraṇam tatra katham ekasya smaraṇe parasya asmaraṇāt abhāva anumānam anaikāntika tvāt iti ced saha sthitayoḥ api padārthayoḥ kadācid kāraṇa anurodhāt ekaḥ upalabhyate na aparaḥ tatra api katham bhū tala upalambhāt anupalabhyamānasya ghaṭasya abhāva siddhiḥ 
NK_194.1	 atha matam raj jñāna saṃsargiṇoḥ eka upalambhe aparasya anupalambhaḥ abhāva sādhanam na sarvaḥ yena vijñānena pradeśaḥ gṛhyate tena eva tad saṃyogī ghaṭaḥ api gṛhyate yā ca pradeśa grahaṇe sāmagrī sā eva ghaṭasya api sāmagrī yadi pradeśe ghaṭaḥ abhiviṣyat saḥ api pradeśe jñāyamāne vyajñāsyat tad tulya sāmagrīka tvāt na jñāyate ca tasmāt na asti eva tad anupalambhasya prakāra antareṇa asambhavāt iti yadi evam asmākam api eka jñāna saṃsatgiṇoḥ eka smaraṇam abhāva sādhanam yā devakula grahaṇa sāmagrī sā devadattasya api tad saṃyuktasya grahaṇa sāmagrī yā ca daiva kulasya smaraṇa sāmagrī sā devadattasya api smṛti sāmagrī tad eka jñāna saṃsargi tvāt yadi devakula grahaṇa kāle devadattaḥ abhaviṣyat saḥ api devakule smaryamāṇe asmariṣyat tad tulya sāmagrī tvāt na ca smaryate tasmāt na āsīt eva tat asmaraṇasya prakāra antareṇa asambhavāt iti samānam ślokasya tu padāni uccāraṇa anurodhāt krameṇa paṭhyante na eka jñāna saṃsargīṇi teṣu yatra tu paṭutaraḥ saṃskāraḥ jātaḥ tat smaryate na aparam iti na asti anupapattiḥ 
NK_194.2–194.3	 evam upalabhyamānasya api vastunaḥ yat prāktana abhāva jñānam prāk idam iha na āsīt iti jñānam tat api pratiyoginaḥ prāktana astitve smaryamāṇe tata sattā smṛti abhāvāt anumānam ye tu smṛti abhāvam api abhāvam pramāṇam ācakṣate teṣām abhāvaḥ api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ iti bhāṣya virodhaḥ pramāṇa pañcakam yatra vastu rūpe na jāyate iti ādi vārttika virodhaḥ ca iti alam bahunā 
NK_195.1	 ye panarevam āhuḥ abhāva rūpasya prameyasya abhāva anna sādhvī tasya prāmāṇa cintā iti te idam praṣṭavyāḥ na asti iti saṃvidaḥ kim ālambanam yadi na kiñjit dattaḥ sva hastaḥ nirālambanam vijñānam icchatām mahā yānikānām atha bhū talam ālambanam kaṇṭakādimatī api bhū tale kaṇṭakaḥ na asti iti saṃvittiḥ tad pūrvakaḥ ca niḥśaṅkam gamana āgamana lakṣaṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ durnivāraḥ kevala bhū tala viṣayam anāsti iti a saṃvedanam kaṇṭaka sadbhāve ca kaivalyam nivṛttam iti pratipatti pravṛttyoḥ abhāvaḥ iti ced kim kaivalyam bhū talasya svarūpam eva kim uta dharma antaram svarūpam tāvat kaṇṭaka ādi saṃvedane api aparāvṛttam iti saḥ eva pratipatti pravṛttyoḥ avirāmaḥ doṣaḥ dharma antara pakṣe ca tattva antara siddhiḥ 
NK_195.2–195.3	 atha manyase bhāvaḥ eva ekākī sa dvitīyaḥ ca iti dvayīm avasthām anubhavati tatra ekākī bhavaḥ svarūpa mātram iti kevalaḥ iti ca ucyate tādṛśasya tasya dṛśye pratiyogini ghaṭa ādau jighṛkṣite sati upalabdhiḥ ghaṭa ādi abhāva vyavahāram pravartayati iti atra api brūmaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ abhāvam bhū talam ca vyatirekya ekāki śabdasya arthaḥ kaḥ samarthitaḥ bhavadbhiḥ yaḥ hi na asti iti pratiṣedha dhiyaḥ ālambanam na hi viṣaya vailakṣaṇyam antaraṇa vilakṣaṇāyāḥ buddheḥ asti udayaḥ na api vyavahāra bhedasya saṃbhavaḥ avabhāvikam yat ekatvam bhāvasya tat eva ekāki tvam iti ced kim eka tvam pratiyogi rahita tvam eka tva saṃkhyā vā ekatva saṃkhyā tāvat yāvat āśraya bhāvinī bhāvasya sa dvitīya avasthāyām api anuvartate atha pratiyogi rahita tvam svābhāvikam eka tvam ucyate siddham prameya antaram 
NK_195.4	 nanu abhāva vādinaḥ api bhū tala grahaṇam abhāva pratīti kāraṇam apratīte bhū tale tatra abhāva pratīteḥ ayogāt tatra na tāvat kaṇṭaka ādi sahita bhūtala upalambhāt laṇṭakaḥ na asti iti pratītiḥ abhāva viśiṣṭa bhū tala grahaṇasya abhāva pratīti hetu tve ca abhāva grahaṇāt tad abhāva viśiṣṭa bhū tala grahaṇam abhāva viśiṣṭa bhū tala grahaṇāt ca abhāva grahaṇam iti svayam eva svasya kāraṇam abhyupagatam syāt tasmāt abhāva vyatiriktā pratiyogi saṃsarga vyatirekiṇī bhū talasya tvayā api kācid ekāki tva astha anupagantavyā yasyāḥ pratīta avabhāva pratītiḥ syāt sā eva asmākam na asti iti vyavahāram pravartayati iti tat api ayuktam bhū tala svarūpa grahaṇasya eva abhāva pratīti hetu tvāt na ca sa dvitīya grahaṇe apyet pratīti prasaṅgaḥ bhū tala grahaṇa vat abhāva indriya sannikarṣa upyabhāva grahaṇa sāmagrī kaṇṭaka ādi sadbhāve tad abhāvaḥ na asti iti viṣaya indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt sati api bhū tala grahaṇe na abhāva pratītiḥ na hi cakṣuḥ āloka ādikam upalambha kāraṇam asti iti yadi atra na asti tat api tatra pratīyate tat evam siddhaḥ abhāvaḥ 
NK_196.1–196.2	 sa ca caturdhā rūḍhaḥ prāc abhāvaḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ itaretarābhāvaḥ atyanta abhāvaḥ ca iti prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇeṣu kāryasya abhāvaḥ prāc abhāvaḥ tatra prāk kārya utpatteḥ pūrvam abhāvaḥ viśeṣasya prāc abhāvaḥ sa ca anādiḥ api anityaḥ kārya utpādena tasya vināśāt avināśe ca kāryasya utpatti abhāvāt kaḥ prāgabhāvasya vināśaḥ vastu utpādaḥ eva nivṛtte vastuni prāc abhāva upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ iti ced vastu vat vastu avayavānām api ārabdha kāryāṇām prāc abhāva vināśa lakṣaṇa tvāt 
NK_196.3	 utpannasya svarūpa pracyutiḥ pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ sa ca utpattimān api avināśī bhāvasya punar anupalambhāt prāc abhūtasya paścāt bhāvaḥ utpādaḥ pradhvaṃsasya kaḥ prāc abhāvaḥ yasya arthasya yaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ tasya arthasya svarūpa sthitiḥ eva tad pradhvaṃsasya prāc abhāvaḥ yathā vastu utpattiḥ eva tad prāgabhāvasya vināśaḥ tathā pradhvaṃsa utpattiḥ eva tad prāgabhāvasya vināśaḥ yat asat bhūtam tasya katham sadbhāvaḥ yat ca sadbhūtam tasya katham abhāvaḥ iti aparicodyam kāraṇa sāmarthyasya aparyanuyojya tvāt 
NK_196.4	 gavya śva abhāvaḥ aśve ca gora bhāvaḥ itaretarābhāvaḥ sa ca sarvatra ekaḥ nityaḥ eka piṇḍa vināśe api sāmānya vat piṇḍa antare pratyabhijñānāt yathā ca sāmānyam adṛṣṭa vaśāt upajāyamānena eva piṇḍena saha sambaddhyate nitye ca svabhāva siddham tathā itaretarābhāvaḥ api iyān tu viśeṣaḥ piṇḍa grahaṇa mātreṇa sāmānya grahaṇam itaretarābhāva grahaṇam tu pratiyogi sapa īkṣam para tūpa nirūpaṇīya tvāt 
NK_196.5	 atyanta abhāvaḥ yat asataḥ pratiṣedhaḥ iti itaretarābhāvaḥ eva atyanta abhāvaḥ iti ced aho rājamārgaḥ eva bhramaḥ itaretarābhāvaḥ hi svarūpa siddhayoḥ eva gavāśvayoḥ itaretara ātma tā pratiṣedhaḥ atyanta abhāve tu sarvathā asat bhūtasya eva buddha avaropitasya deśa kālān avacchinnaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yathā ṣaṣ padārthebhyaḥ na anyat prameyam asti iti yadi ca atyanta abhāvaḥ na iṣyate ṣaṭ eva padārthāḥ iti ayam niyamaḥ durghaṭaḥ syāt 
NK_197.1–197.2	 tathā eva aitihyam api avitatham āpta upadeśaḥ eva iti aitihyam api avitatham āpta upadeśaḥ eva aiti ha a iti nipāta samudāya upadeśa pāramparye vartate tatra ayam svārthikaḥ ṣyan pratyayaḥ aitihyam iti vitatham aitihyam tāvat pramāṇam eva na bhavati avitatham āpta vacanam eva āpta upaḍeśaḥ ca anumānam tasmāt avitatham aitihyam anumānāt na vyatiticyate iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NK_198.1–198.2	 pañca avayavena vākyena sva niścita artha pratipādanam para artha anumānam pañca avayavena eva vākyena saṃśayita viparīta avyutpannānām pareṣām sva niścita artha pratipādanam para artha anumānam vijñeyam para artha anumāna vyutpādana artham āha pañca avayavena vākyena sva niścita artha pratipādanam para artha anumānam iti pratipādanīyasya prthasya yāvati śabda samūhe pratītiḥ paryasyati tasya pañca bhāgāḥ samūha apekṣayā avayavāḥ iti ucyante svayam sādhya anantarīyaka tvena niścitaḥ arthaḥ sva niścita arthaḥ sādhyāvinābhūtam liṅgam tasya pañca avayavena vākyena pratipādanam tad pratipatti janana samartha pañca avayava vākya prayogaḥ para artha anumānam pañca avayavam hi vākyam yapvatsu rūpeṣu liṅgasya sādhya avinābhāvaḥ parisamāpyate tāvat rūpam liṅgam pratipādayati tad pratipāditāt ca liṅgāt sādhya siddhiḥ na tu vākyam eva sādhyam bodhayati tasya śābda tva prasaṅgāt tasmāt avinābhūta liṅga abhidhāyaka vākya prayogaḥ eva para artha anumānam ucyate 
NK_198.3	 apare tu yat paraḥ śabdaḥ sa śabdāthaḥ vākyam ca sādhya param tad pratipādana artham asya prayogāt liṅga pratipādanam tu avāntara vyāpāraḥ vacana mātreṇa vipratipannasya sādhya pratīteḥ abhāvāt iti vadante evam vyācakṣate sva niścitorthaḥ sādhyaḥ tasya liṅga pratipādanam eva avāntara vyāpārīkṛtya pajśa avayavena vākyena pratipādanam tad pratipādaka vākya prayogaḥ para artha anumānam iti 
NK_198.4	 sva uktam vivṛṇoti pañca avayavena eva ityādinā dvi avayavam eva vākyam iti eke tri avayavam iti apare tad pratiṣedha artham evakāra karaṇam pañca avayavena eva iti pratipādye arthe yasya saṃśayaḥ asti sa saṃśayitaḥ yasya viparyaya jñānam sa viparītaḥ yasya na saṃśayaḥ na viparyayaḥ kintu a jñāna mātram saḥ avyutpannaḥ trayaḥ api pratipādana arhāḥ tattva pratīti virahāt 
NK_199.1	 yaḥ yāni padāni samuditāni prayuṅkte sa tad padārtha saṃsarga pratipādana abhiprāyavān iti sāmānyena sva ātmani niyame pratīte paścāt pada samūha prayogāt vaktuḥ tad padārtha saṃsarga pratipādana abhiprāya avagati dvāreṇa padebhyaḥ vākya artha anumānam na tu padārthebhyaḥ tad pratītiḥ na hi padārthaḥ nāma pramāṇam asti mīmāṃsakānām na api vākya artha pratipādanāya padaiḥ pratyekam abhidhīyamānānām padārthānām vākya artha pratipāda śaktiḥ āviḥ bhavati prameya pratīti mātra vyāpārasya pramāṇasya prameya śakti ādhāyaka tva abhāvāt tasmāt padārthāḥ vākya artham pratipādayantaḥ liṅga tvena vā pratipādayeyuḥ anyathā anupapattyā vā ubhaya bhā api aśābdaḥ vākya arthaḥ syāt 
NK_199.2	 nanu kim padāni pratyekam ekaikam artham pratipādayanti vākya arthasya liṅgam kim vā paraspara anvitam sva artham bodhayanti atra eke tāvat āhuḥ vyutpatti apekṣayā padānām artha pratipādanam vyutpattiḥ ca gām ānaya gām badhāna ityādiṣu vṛddha vyavahāreṣu kriyā anvite kārake kāraka anvitāyām ca kriyāyām na sva rūpa mātre atas paraspara anvitāḥ eva padārthāḥ padaiḥ pratipādyante iti 
NK_199.3^1	 atra nirūpyate yadi gāmānaya ityādi vākye gām iti padena eva anayā iti artha anvitaḥ sva arthaḥ abhihitaḥ tadānayā iti padam vyartham ukta artha tvāt ānayeti padena ānayana arthe abhihite asti ānayā iti artha anvitaḥ sva arthaḥ gopadena abhidhīyate tena ānayā iti padasya na vaiyarthyam iti ced tarhi ānayā iti padam kevalam sva artha mātram ācakṣāṇam ananvitā abhidhāyi prāptam yathā ca idam ananvitā artham tathā pada antaram api syāt iti datta jala añjaliḥ anvita abhidhāna vādaḥ atha ānayā iti padena api pūrva pada abhihitena arthena anvitaḥ sva arthaḥ abhidhīyate tadā yāvat pūrva padam sva artham na abhidhatte tāvat uttara padasya pūrva padārtha anvita sva artha abhidhānam na asti 
NK_199.3^2	 yāvat ca uttara padam sva artham na abhidhatte tāvat pūrva padasya uttara padārtha anvita sva artha pratipādanam na bhavati iti anyonya āśraya tvam atha manyase prathamam padāni kevalam padārtham smārayanti paścāt itara itara smāritena arthena anvitam sva artham abhidadhati iti tatas na itaretara āśraya tvam tat api asāram sarvadā eva hi padāni anvitena sva arthena saha gṛhīta sāhacaryāṇi na ananvitam kevalam padārtha mātram smārayitum īśate yathā anubhavam smaraṇasya pravṛtteḥ 
NK_199.3^3	 vṛddha vyavahāreṣu anvaya vyatirekābhyām go śabdasya kakudādimad arthe niyamaḥ gṛhītaḥ na kriyākaranādiṣu iti teṣām pratyekam vyabhicāre api go śabdasya prayoga darśanāt tena ayam go śabdaḥ śrūyamāṇaḥ abhyāsa paṭavāt avyabhicarira sāhacaryam kakudādi mad artha mātram smārayati na kriyā karaṇa ādīni iti ced evam tarhi yasya śabdasya yatra arhe sāhacarya niyamaḥ gṛhyate tatra eva tasya abhidhāyaka tvam na anyatra iti ananvita artha abhidhāne api samānam na ca smaraṇam anumāna vat sāhacarya niyamam apekṣya pravartate iti api su pratītam tarhi saṃskāra mātra nibandhanam pratiyogi mātra darśanāt api bhavati 
NK_199.3^4	 tathā āha dhūma darśanāt agniḥ iva rasavati adi pradeśaḥ api smaryate tat yadi go śabdaḥ sahabhāva pratīti mātreṇa eva gopiṇḍam smārayati gopiṇḍa pratiyoginaḥ api padārthān kadācid smārayet niyamena tu gopiṇḍam eva smārayan= taḥ tad viṣayam vācaka tvam eva avalambate tathā asati eva niyama sambhavāt kiñca yathā vākye padānām anvita abhidhānam tathā pade api prakṛti pratyayayoḥ anvita abhidhānam icchanti bhavantaḥ tābhyām ced paraspara anvitaḥ sva arthaḥ abhihitaḥ kaḥ tad anyaḥ padārthaḥ yaḥ paścāt smaryate tat etat āstām nagnāṭaka pakṣa patitam vacaḥ 
NK_200.1	 prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ astu avam padānām artha pratipādanam idam tu na saṅgacchate para artham anumānam iti liṅgam tat janitam vā jñānam anumānam na ca liṅgasya jñānasya ca parārtha tvam anumāna vācakasya śabdasya para artha tvāt anumānam para arthamucyeta ced pratyakṣa vācakasya api śabdasya para artha tvāt pratyakṣam api para arthamucyeta tat uktam 
NK_200.2–200.4	 jñānāt vā jñāna hetoḥ vā na anyasya asti anumāna tā tayoḥ ca na parārtha tvam prasiddham loka vedayoḥ vacanasya para artha tvāt anumāna parārtha tā pratyakṣasya api pārārthyam tad dvāram kim na kalpyate iti atra samābhiḥ na śabdasya para artha tvāt tad vācyam anumāna prārtham iti vadāmaḥ api tu yat para artham pañca avayavam vākyam tad liṅga pratīti dvāraṇa anumiti hetutvāt anumānam iti brūmaḥ nanu evam api liṅga pratipādaksya pratyakṣasya anumānatā upacāra prasaṅgaḥ na prasaṅgaḥ tatra laukika śabda prayoga abhāvāt 
NK_201.1–201.3	 avayavāḥ punar pratijñā apadeśa nidarśana anusamdhāna pratyāmnāyāḥ tatra anumeya uddeśaḥ avirodhī pratijñā pratipipāt ayiṣita dharma viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇā upadeśa viṣayam āpādana artham uddeśa mātram pratijñā yathā dravyam vāyuḥ iti pañca avayavam vākyam iti uktam ke punar te pañca avayavāḥ tatra āha avayavāḥ punar pratijñā apadeśa nidarśana anusandhāna pratyāmnāyāḥ punar śabdaḥ vākya alaṅkāre 
NK_201.4–201.7	 tatra teṣām madhye anumeya uddeśaḥ avirodhī pratijñā etat svayam eva vivṛṇoti pratipipādayiṣita ityādinā pratipādayitum iṣṭaḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ tena viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī anumeyaḥ pakṣaḥ iti kathyate tasya yat uddeśa mātram saṅkīrtana mātram sādhana rahitam sā pratijñā iti yathā upadiśanti santaḥ vacanasya pratijñātvam tad arthasya ca pakṣatā iti yadi hetuḥ ahitam uddeśa mātram pratijñā na etasyāḥ sādhya siddhiḥ asti iti asādhana aṅga tvāt na prayogam arhati yathā vadanti tathāgatāḥ śaktasya sūcakam hetuḥ vacaḥ aśaktam api svayam sādhya abhidhānāt pakṣektiḥ pāramparyeṇa na api alam iti 
NK_201.8^1	 atra āha apadeśa viṣayam āpadana artham iti apadeśaḥ hetuḥ tasya viṣayam āśrama āpādayitum pratipādayitum pratijñā khalu yatra kvacana sādhya sādhanāya hetuḥ prayujyate tasya siddha tvāt api tarhi kasmiṃścid dharmiṇi pratiniyate tasmin= = anupanyasyamāne nirāśrayaḥ hetuḥ na pravarteta tasya apravṛttau na sādhya siddhiḥ atas pratijñāyāḥ dharmi grāhakam pramāṇam apadarśayantyāḥ hetoḥ āśrayaḥ dharmī sannidhāpyate iti āśraya upadarśana dvāreṇa hetum pravartayantī pratijñā sādhya siddheḥ aṅgam 
NK_201.8^2	 tathā ca nyāya bhāṣyam asatyām pratijñāyām anāśrayāḥ hetu ādayaḥ na pravarteran iti upanayāt eva hetoḥ aśrayaḥ pratīyate iti ced na asati pratijñā vacane tasya api apravṛtteḥ upanayaḥ hi sādhanasya pakṣa dharma tā lakṣaṇam sāmarthyam upadarthayati na ca pratyetuḥ prathamam eva sādhanam pratyakāṅkṣāḥ kintu sādhye tasya pradhāna tvāt ākāṅkṣite sādhye tad siddhi aṅgam sādhanam paścāt ākāṃkṣyate tadanu sādhana sāmarthyam iti prathamam sādhya vacanam eva upatiṣṭhate na punar agratas eva sādhana sāmarthyam ucyate tasya tadānīm anapekṣita tvāt 
NK_201.9	 pratipipā dayiṣitena dharmeṇa viśiṣṭaḥ dharmī iti vipratiṣiddham idam apratītasya aviśeṣaka tvāt iti ced satyam apratītam viśeṣaṇam na bhavati pratītaḥ tu sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ saḥ idānīm pakṣe vipratipannam prati jñāpanāya dharmi viśeṣaṇa tayā pratijñāyate atas eva ca dharmiṇaḥ pakṣatā vāstavī tasya svarūpeṇa siddhasya api pratipādya dharma viśiṣṭa tvena aprasiddhasya tena rūpeṇa āpādyamāna tva sambhavāt pakṣa dharma tā api hetoḥ ittham eva yadi kevalam eva anitya tvam sādhyate bhavet śabda dharmasya kṛtaka tvasya apakṣa dharma tā śabde eva tu anitye sādhye na ayam doṣaḥ yathā āhuḥ ācāryāḥ  
NK_201.10–201.11	 saḥ eva ca ubhaya ātmā ayam gamyaḥ gamakaḥ eva ca asiddhena eka deśena gamyaḥ siddhena bodhakaḥ iti pratijñāyai udāharaṇam āha dravyam vāyuḥ iti yaḥ vāyum pratipadyamānaḥ api tasya dravya tvam na pratipadyate tam prati sādhayitum iṣṭena dravya tvena viśiṣṭasya vāyoḥ abhidhānam pratijñā kriyate dravyam vāyuḥ iti 
NK_202.1	 avirodhi grahaṇāt pratyakṣa anumāna abhyupagata sva śāstra sva vacana virodhinaḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti yathā anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ iti pratyakṣa virodhī ghaṭam ambaram iti anumāna rodhī brāhmaṇena surā peyā iti āgama virodhī vaiśeṣikasya prāk utpatteḥ satkāryam iti bruvataḥ sva śāstra virodhī na śabdaḥ artha pratyāyakaḥ iti sva vacana virodhī 
NK_202.2	 avirodhi grahaṇasya tātparyam kathayati avirodhi grahaṇāt pratyakṣa anumāna abhyupagata sva śāstra sva vacana virodhinaḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti iti vādinā sādhayitunabhipretaḥ arthaḥ sādhyaḥ iti ucyate pratijñā iti etāvat mātram ucyate pratyakṣa ādi viruddham api vacanam pratijñā syāt na ca iyam pratijñā tad arthasya sādhayitum aśakyatvāt atas avirodhi grahaṇam kṛtam na vidyate pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ yasya anumeya uddeśasya asau= apratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ tasya vacanam pratijñā yasya tu tad virodhaḥ asti na sā pratijñā iti arthaḥ kim anena uktam bhavati na vādi abhiprāya vyāpti mātreṇa sādhya tā kim tu yat sādhanam arhati tat sādhyam saḥ eva ca pakṣaḥ tad itaraḥ pakṣa ābhāsaḥ iti 
NK_202.3	 pratyakṣa ādi virodha udāharaṇam yathā anuṣṇaḥ agrniḥ iti anuṣṇaḥ iti uṣṇa sparśa pratiṣedhaḥ ayam avagatam ca pratiṣidhyate na anavagatam na ca uṣṇa tvasya vahniḥ anyatraa upalambha sambhavaḥ vahnā api tasya pratītiḥ na anumānikī pratyakṣa abhāve anumānasya apravṛtteḥ pratyakṣa pratītasya ca pratiṣedhe pratyakṣa prāmāṇya abhyupagamena pravartamānam pratiṣedha anumānam tad viparīta vṛtti tena eva bādhyate viṣaya apahārāt kaḥ viṣayasya apahāraḥ tad viparīta artha pravedanam tasmin satya numānasya kim bhavati utpatti abhāvaḥ prathama pravṛttena ābādhita viṣaya pratyakṣeṇa vahneḥ uṣṇa tve pratipādite tad prati iti avaruddhe ca tasya anuṣṇa tva pratītiḥ na bhavati hetoḥ api ayam eva bādhaḥ yat ayam anuṣṇat pratipādanāya prayuktaḥ tad pratītim na karoti pratyakṣa virodhāt yathā uktam 
NK_202.4–202.5	 vaiparītya paricchede na avakāśaḥ parasya tu mūle tasya hi anutpanne pūrveṇa viṣayaḥ hṛtaḥ iti bādhā vinā bhāvayoḥ virodhāt avinābhūtasya bādha anupapattiḥ iti ced yadi trairūpyam avinā abhāvaḥ abhimataḥ tadā asti evāvinābhūtasya bādhaḥ yathā anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ kṛtaka tva ādityasya eva atha ābādhita viṣaya tve sati trairūpyam avinā abhāvaḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa ucyatte avinābhūtasya na asti bādhā iti tadom iti ucyate kintva bādhita vita viṣaya tvam eva rūpam kathayitum pratyakṣa ādi avirodhi grahaṇam kṛtam 
NK_202.6–202.7	 pratyakṣa virodhaḥ kim prakṣasya doṣaḥ kim vā hetoḥ na pakṣasya dharmiṇaḥ tādavasthyāt na api hetoḥ sva viṣaye tasya sānarthyāt viṣaya antare sarvasya eva āsāmārthyāt kintu pratipādayituḥ idam dūṣaṇam yaḥ aviṣaye sādhanam prayuṅkte yadi pratijñāta artha pratīti yogya tā virahaḥ tad pratipādana yogya tā virahaḥ ca dūṣaṇam abhimatam tadā karma karaṇayoḥ api asti doṣaḥ ghanam ambaram iti anumāna virodhī yena pramāṇena akāṣam avagatam tena eva ākāśasya nitya tvam niravayava tvam ca pratipāditam atas nibiḍa avayavam ambaram iti pratijñā dharmi grāhaka anumāna viruddhāḥ 
NK_202.8	 brāhmaṇena surā peyā iti āgama virodhī brāhmaṇasya pāna arhā surā pītā pāpa sādhanam na bhavati iti pratijñā arthaḥ atra kṣīram udāharaṇam kṣīrasya ca pāpa sādhana tva abhāvaḥ śruti smṛti āgama eka samadhigamyaḥ yena eva āgamena kṣīra pānasya pāpa sādhana tva abhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ tena eva su pāpānasya pāpa sādhana tvam pratipāditam iti brāhmaṇena surā peyā iti pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭānta grāhaka pramāṇa virodhaḥ 
NK_202.9–202.10	 vaiśeṣikasya prāk utpatteḥ satkāryam iti bruvataḥ sva śāstra virodhī vaiśeṣikaḥ hi vaiśeṣika śāstra prāmāṇya abhyupagamena vāda ādiṣu pravartate tasya aprāc utpādāt sat kāryam a iti bruvataḥ pratijñāyāḥ sva śāstreṇa virodhaḥ vaiśeṣika śāstre aasat utpadyate a iti pratipādanāt śabdaḥ na artha pratyāyakaḥ iti sva vacana virodhī yadi śabdasya artha pratyāyaka tvam na asti tadā aśabdaḥ na artham pratipādayati a iti asya arthasya pratipādanāya śabda prayogaḥ anupapannaḥ atha etad artham śabdaḥ prayujyate tatabhyupagatam śabdasya artha pratyāyaka tvam iti pratijñāyāḥ sva vacanam irodhaḥ 
NK_202.11	 pratyakṣa anumāna avagata vastu tattva ākhyānam śāstram tad virodhaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna virodhaḥ eva tathā tad bhāva bhāvitva anumāna samadhigamyam śabdasya artha pratyāyaka tvam pratiṣedhayataḥ anumāna viruddhā eva pratijñā kasmāt sva śāstra sva vacana virodhayoḥ pṛthak abhidhānam atra ucyate pramāṇa ābhāsa mūlam api śastram bhavati yathā śākya ādīnām atra bauddhasya asarvam akṣaṇikam a iti pratijānataḥ sva ca astra virodhaḥ eva na pramāṇa virodhaḥ sva vacanam api kadācid apramāṇa mūlam api syāt atas tat virodhāḥ na pramāṇa virodhaḥ kintu sva vacana virodhaḥ eva 
NK_203.1	 liṅga vacanam apadeśaḥ yat anumeyena sahacaritam tad samāna jātīye ca sarvatra sāmānyena prasiddham tad viparīte ca sarvasmin asat eva tat liṅgam uktam tasya vacanam apadeśaḥ yathā kriyāvat tvāt guṇavat tva at aca a iti tathā ca tad anumeye asti tad samāna jātīye ca sarvasmin guṇavat tvam asarvasmin kriyāvat tvam asti ubhayam api etat adravye na asti eva tasmāt tasya vacanam apadeśaḥ iti siddham 
NK_203.2	 liṅga vacanam apedeśaḥ asya artham kathayati yat anumeyena ityādinā tad sugamam udāharaṇam āha akriyāvat tvāt guṇavat tvāt ca a iti dravyam vāyuḥ iti pratijñāyām kriyāvat tvāt iti kriyāvat tvasya liṅgasya vacanam apadeśaḥ tasyām eva pratijñāyām guṇavat tvasya liṅgasya guṇavat tvāt iti vacanam apadeśaḥ ubhayoḥ upanyāsaḥ sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ sa pakṣa vyāpakasya ca hetu tva pradarśana arthaḥ yat iktam liṅga lakṣaṇam tat kriyāvat tvasya guṇavat tvasya ca asti iti āha tathā ca tat iti tat guṇavat tvam anumeye asti tad samāna jātīye sa pakṣe dravye sarvasmin asti asarvasmin sa pakṣa eka deśe mūrta dravya mātre kriyāvat tvam asti ubhayam api etat kriyāvat tvam guṇavat tvam ca adravye vipakṣe na asya iva tasya ubhayasya vacanam kriyāvat tvāt guṇavat tvāt iti evam rūpam apadeśaḥ iti hetuḥ iti siddham vyavasthitam nirdoṣa tvāt 
NK_204.1–204.2	 etena asiddha viruddha sandigdha anadhya vasita vacanānām anapadeśa tvam uktam bhavati tatra asiddhaḥ caturvidhaḥ ubhaya asiddhaḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ tad bhāva asiddhaḥ anumeya asiddhaḥ ca iti tatra ubhaya asiddhaḥ ubhayoḥ vādi prativādinā uḥ asiddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sāvayava tvāt iti anyatara asiddhaḥ yathā anutyaḥ śabdaḥ kāryatvāt iti tad bhāva asiddhaḥ yathā dhūma bhāvena agni adhinatau karttavyāyām upanyasyamānaḥ bāṣpaḥ dhūma bhāvena asiddhaḥ iti anumeya asiddhaḥ yathā pārthivam tamaḥ kṛṣṇa rūpavat tvāt iti 
NK_204.3	 etena apadeśa lakṣaṇa kathanena arthāt asiddha viruddha sandigdha anadhya vasita vacanānām anapadeśa tvam uktam bhavati anumeyena sahacaritam iti anena asiddha vacanasya anapadeśa tvam uktam tad samāna jātīye ca prasiddham iti anena viruddha anadhya vasita vacanayoḥ anapadeśa tvam tad viparīte na asti eva iti anena sandigdha vacanasya anapadeśa tvam iti vivekaḥ 
NK_204.4–204.5	 eṣām asiddha viruddha sandigdha anadhyavasitānām madhye asiddham kathayati tatra asiddhaḥ caturvidhaḥ ubhaya asiddhaḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ tad bhāva asiddhaḥ anumeya asiddhaḥ iti tatra ubhaya asiddhaḥ ubhayoḥ vādi prativādinā uḥ asiddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sa avayava tvāt iti śabde sa avayava tvam na vādinaḥ na api prativādinaḥ siddham iti ubhaya asiddhaḥ 
NK_204.6–204.8	 anyatara asiddhaḥ kārya tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti yadi api śabde vastutas kāryatvam asti tathā api vipratipannasya mīmāṃsakasya asiddham iti anyatarā siddham sādhyam na sādhayati yāvat na prasādhyate tad bhāva asiddhaḥ yathā dhūma bhāvena agni adhigatau karttavyāyām upanyasyamānaḥ bāṣpaḥ dhūma bhāvena dhūma svarūpeṇa asiddhaḥ tad bhāva asiddhaḥ iti ucyate anumeya asiddhaḥ yathā pārthivam tamaḥ kṛṣṇa rūpavat tvāt tamaḥ nāma dravya antaram na asti āropitasya kārṣṇya mātrasya pratīteḥ atas tamaḥ dravyam pārthivam kṛṣṇa rūpavat tvāt iti anumeya asiddham āśraya asiddham anumeyam asiddham yasya iti asiddha anumeyam iti prāptau= āhitāgni ādi tvāt niṣṭhāyāḥ pūrva nipātaḥ 
NK_204.9	 yathā hetuḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ ubhaya asiddhaḥ vā bhavati evam āśraya asiddhiḥ api ubhayathā yathā ca hetuḥ vādi prativādinoḥ pratyekam samuditayoḥ vā ajñānāt sandehāt viparyayāt vā asiddhaḥ bhavati tathā āśrayaḥ api yathā ca hetuḥ kaścid vādinaḥ ajñānāṃsiddhaḥ prativādinaḥ sandigdhā asiddhaḥ iti yat vā vādinaḥ ajñāna asiddhaḥ yadi vā prativādinaḥ viparyaya asiddhaḥ yat vā vādinaḥ sandeha asiddhaḥ prativādinaḥ ajñāna asiddhaḥ yat vā viparyaya asiddhaḥ bhavati vādinaḥ prativādinaḥ sandeha asiddhaḥ evam āśrayaḥ api iti yojanīyam viśeṣaṇa asiddha ādayaḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ bhaya asiddheṣu eva antarbhavanti iti pṛthak na uktāḥ 
NK_205.1–205.2	 yaḥ hi anumeye avidyamānaḥ api tad samāna jātīye ca sarvasmin āsti tad viparīte ca asti sa viparīta sādhanāt viruddhaḥ yathā yasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt aśvaḥ iti viruddham hetvābhāvam kathayati yaḥ hi anumeye vidyamānaḥ api tad samāna jātīye ca sarvasmin na asti tad viparīte ca asti sa viparīta sādhana tvāt viruddhaḥ iti yadā kaścid vana antarite gopiṇḍe viṣāṇam upalabhya aayam piṇḍaḥ aśvaḥ viṣāṇi tvāt a iti sādhayati tadā viṣāṇi tvam aśva jātīye piṇḍa antare avidyamānam aśva viparīte gavi mahiṣa ādau ca vipakṣe vidyamānam vyāpti balena aśva tva viruddham anaśva tvam sādhayat abhimata sādhya viparīta prasādhanāt viruddham iti uvyate idam vipakṣa eka deśa vṛtteḥ viruddhasya udāharaṇam viṣāṇi tvasya sarvatra anaśve stambha ādau= asambhavāt samasta vipakṣa vyāpakasya viruddhasya udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti draṣṭavyam 
NK_206.1–206.4	 yaḥ tu san anumeye tad samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ san eva sa sandeha janaka tvāt sandigdhaḥ yathā yasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt gauḥ iti ekasmin ca dvayoḥ hetvoḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ viruddhayoḥ sannipāte sati saṃśaya darśanāt ayam anyaḥ sandigdhaḥ iti kecid yathā mūrta tva amūrta tvam prati namasaḥ kriyāvat tva asparśavat tvayoḥ iti nanu ayam asādhāraṇaḥ eva ācākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tva vat saṃhatayoḥ anyatara pakṣa asambhavāt tatas ca anadhyavasitaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ 
NK_206.5	 yaḥ tu san anumeye dharmiṇi tad samāna jātīyayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ sa sandeha janaka tvāt sandigdhaḥ yathā yasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt gauḥ iti yadā ayam piṇḍaḥ gauḥ viṣāṇi tvāt iti sādhyate tadā viṣāṇi tvam gavi mahiṣe ca darśanāt sandeham āpādayan sandigdhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ syāt ayam sa pakṣa vyāpakaḥ vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ anaikāntikaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ vyāpakaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ prameya tvāt iti sa pakṣa vipakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ nityam ākāśam amūrta tvāt iti sa pakṣa eka deśa vṛttiḥ vipakṣa vyāpakaḥ dravyam śabdaḥ niravayava tvāt iti samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ sādhāraṇaḥ iti yat sādhāraṇa padam tasya vivaraṇam san eva iti 
NK_206.6^1	 yathā ekaḥ dharmaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ darśanāt dharmiṇi sandeham kurvan sandigdhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ syāt evam ekasmin dharmiṇi dvayoḥ hetu osyulya balayoḥ viruddha artha prasādhakayoḥ sannipāte sati saṃśaya darśanāt ayam viruddha dvaya sannipātaḥ anyaḥ sandigdhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ iti kaiścid uktam tat dūṣayitum upanyasyati ekasmin= ca iti tasya udāharaṇam āha yathā mūrta tva amūrta tvam prati manasaḥ kriyāvat tva asparśat tvayoḥ iti mūrtam manaḥ kriyāva tvāt śara ādi vat amūrtam manaḥ asparśavat tvāt ākāśa vat iti viruddha artha prasādhakayoḥ kriyāvat tva asparśavat tvayoḥ hetvoḥ sannipāte manasaḥ mūrtta tva amūrtta tvam prati saṃśayaḥ na hi atra ubhayoḥ api sādhaka tvam vasyunaḥ dvaya ātmaka tva asambhavāt 
NK_206.6^2	 na api paraspara virodhāt ubhayoḥ api asādhaka tvam mūrta amūrta tva vyatirekeṇa prakāra antara abhāvāt na ca anyatarasya hetoḥ viśeṣaḥ avagamyate yena eka pakṣa avadhāraṇam syāt atas kriyāvat tva asparśavat tvābhyām manasi saṃśayaḥ bhavati kim mūrtam kim vā amūrtam iti ayam eva ca viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ prakaraṇa samāt bhedaḥ yat ayam saṃśayam karoti prakaraṇa samaḥ tu sandigdhe arthe prayujyamānaḥ saṃśayam na nivartayati 
NK_206.7	 nanu ayam asādhāraṇaḥ eva acākṣuṣa pratyakṣa tva vat saṃhatayoḥ anyatara pakṣā sambhavāt iti kriyāvat tva asparśavat tve pratyekam na tāvat saṃśayam janayataḥ nirṇaya hetu tvāt sannipātaḥ ca tayoḥ ayam asādhāraṇaḥ eva saṃhatayoḥ tayoḥ manaḥ vyatirekeṇa anyatara pakṣe sa pakṣe vipakṣe vā asambhavāt yathā acākṣuṣa tva pratyakṣa tvayoḥ pratyekam guṇa vyabhicāre api samuditayoḥ guṇa vyatirekeṇa anyatra asambhavaḥ yadi api viruddha avyabhicāri dharma dvaya upanipātaḥ asādhāṇaḥ dharmaḥ tathā api saṃśaya hetu tvam eva vyatirekiṇaḥ hi vipakṣāt eva ekasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ niyatā tena pakṣe nirṇaya hetu tvam asādhāraṇasya tu vyāvṛttiḥ anaikāntikī vipakṣāt iva sa pakṣāt api tasyāḥ sambhavāt tatra yadi gandhavat tvam anitya vyāvṛtta tvāt nitya tvam sādhāyati nityāt api gaganāt vyāvṛtteḥ anitya tvam api sādhayet na ca asti ubhayoḥ siddhiḥ vastunaḥ dvairūpya abhāvāt na api ubhayoḥ asiddhiḥ prakāra antara abhāvāt atas gandhavat tvāt pṛthivyām saṃśayaḥ bhavati kim iyam nityāḥ kim vā anityai iti yathā āhuḥ bhaṭṭa miśrāḥ 
NK_206.8–206.10	 yatra asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ tad abhāva mukhena tu dvaya asattva virodhāt ca sa naḥ saṃśaya kāraṇam yat ca āha nyāya vārttikakāraḥ vibhāga ja tvam vibhāga ja vibhāgā samavāyikāraṇaka tvam na ṛte śabdāt sambhavati iti sarvatas vyāvṛtteḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ iti atra āha tatas cāna dhvasitaḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ iti viruddhayoḥ sannipātaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ asādhāraṇa tvāt ca anadhyavasiyaḥ ayam iti vakṣyāmaḥ kim uktam syāt asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ adhyavasāyam na karoti na punar saṃśayam karoti iti vakṣyāma tyarthaḥ 
NK_207.1	 nanu śāstre tatra tatra ubhayathā darśanam saṃśaya kāraṇam apadiśyate iti na saṃśayaḥ viṣaya dvaita darśanāt saṃśaya utpattau viṣaya dvaita darśanam eva nimittam tulya bala tve ca tayoḥ parasparam virodhāt nirṇaya anutpādaka tvam syāt na tu saṃśaya hetu tvam na ca tayoḥ tulya balavat tvam asti anyatarasya anumeya uddeśasya āgama bādhita tvāt ayam tu viruddha bhedaḥ eva 
NK_207.2^1	 viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ saṃśaya hetu tva abhāve pratipādite śāstra virodham codayati nanu ca śāstre tatra tatra ubhayathā darśanam saṃśaya kāraṇam ādiśyate iti ubhayathā darśanam ubhābhyām viruddha dharmābhyām saha ekasya dharniṇaḥ darśanam saṃśaya kāraṇam iti śāstre tatra tatra sthāne kathitam adṛṣṭam ca dṛṣṭa vat dṛṣṭvā a saṃśayaḥ bhavati amūrta tvena saha ātmani dṛṣṭam asparśavat tvam yathā manasi dṛśyate tathā mūrta tvena saha paramāṇau dṛṣṭam kriyāvat tvam api dṛśyate atas amūrta tvena saha dṛṣṭam asparśavat tvam iva mūrta tvena saha dṛṣṭam kriyāvat tvavam api dṛṣṭvā saṃśayaḥ bhavati kim manaḥ mūrttam 
NK_207.2^2	 kim uta amūrttam iti ayathādṛṣṭam ayathā dṛṣṭam ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt saṃśayaḥa yathā yena dharmeṇa mūrta tva avyabhicāriṇā kriyāvat tvena samam adṛṣṭam a manaḥ tasmāt aayathādṛṣṭam a amūrta tva avyabhicāriṇā sparśavat tvena samam dṛṣṭam atas aubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt a saṃśayaḥ kim kriyāvat tvāt mūrttam manaḥ uta asparśavat tvāt amūrttam iti sūtrarthaḥ tena viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ saṃśaya hetu tvam nirākurvataḥ śāstra virodhaḥ 
NK_207.3	 etat pariharati na saṃśayaḥ viṣaya dvaita darśanāt iti yat tvayā uktam śāstra virodhaḥ iti tat na yasmāt saṃśayaḥ viṣaya dvaita darśanāt bhavati etat eva vivṛṇoti saṃśaya utpattau viṣaya dvaita darśanam kāraṇam iti yādṛśe dharmiṇī ūrdhva svabhāve saṃśayaḥ jāyate asthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā a iti tādṛśasya viṣayasya pūrvam dvaita darśanam ubhayathā darśanam sthāṇu tva puruṣa tvābhyām saha darśanam saṃśaya kāraṇam na tu ekasya dharmiṇaḥ viruddha dharma dvaya sannipātasyasya kāraṇam tasmāt na ayam sūtra arthaḥ yat viruddha avi abhicāri dharma dvaya upanipātāt saṃśayaḥ iti abhiprayaḥ 
NK_207.4	 tathā ca dṛṣṭam ca dṛṣṭa vat dṛṣṭvā iti asya ayam arthaḥ dṛṣṭam eva padārtham sthāṇum vā puruṣam vā adṛṣṭa vat a dṛṣṭābhyām sthāṇu puruṣa antarābhyām tukyam varttamānam dṛṣṭam sthāṇu puruṣa antara samānam iti yāvat deśa antare kāla antare vā punar dṛṣṭvā kutaścid nittāt viśeṣa anupalambhe sati saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti dṛṣṭam ca iti caśabdena pūrvam adṛṣṭam api padārtham dṛṣṭa vat dṛṣṭābhyām sthāṇu puruṣa antarābhyām samānam dṛṣṭvā saṃśayaḥ iti arthaḥ 
NK_207.5	 sūtra antaram ca yathādṛṣṭam ayathādṛṣṭam ubhayathā dṛṣṭam iti eka dharmi viśeṣa anusmaraṇa kṛtam saṃśayam darśayati pūrva dṛṣṭam eva puruṣam ayathādṛṣṭam a yena yena avasthā viśeṣeṇa dṛṣṭam muṇḍam jaṭilam vā tasmāt ayathā dṛṣṭam anyena anyena avasthā bhedena dṛṣṭam kāla antare dṛṣṭvaḥ avasthā viśeṣam apaśyataḥ smarataḥ ca evam tasya eva prāktanīm anavasthitām ubhayīmana sthām kim ayam idānīm muṇḍaḥ kim vā jaṭilaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ syāt iti sūtra arthaḥ 
NK_207.6	 na tu viruddha avyabhicārī saṃśaya hetuḥ prayoga abhāvāt yadi tāvat ādi asya hetoḥ yathā ukta lakṣaṇa tvam anagatam tadā tasmāt yaḥ arthaḥ avadhāritaḥ sa tathā eva iti na dvitīyasya prayogaḥ pratipatti bādhita tvāt atha ayam yathā ukta lakṣaṇaḥ na bhavati tadānīm ayam eva doṣaḥ vācyaḥ kim pratyanumānena viruddham pratyanumānam na vyabhicarati na ativartate iti viruddha avyabhicārī prathamaḥ hetuḥ tasya ayam eva doṣaḥ yad viparīta anumāna sambhavaḥ dvitīyena pratipakṣe sthāpyamāne prathamasya sādhya sādhaka tva abhāvāt iti ced yadi dvitīya vat prathamam api anumāna lakṣaṇa upapannam na prathamasya asādhaka tvam tat asādhaka tve anyatra api anumāne kaḥ āśvāsaḥ vastunaḥ dvairūpya abhāvāt asādhaka tvam iti det vastu dvi rūpam na bhavati iti kena etat uktam yathā hi pramāṇam artham gamayati tat eva hi tasya tattvam 
NK_207.7	 atha ekam vastu ubhaya ātmakam na bhavati iti su dṛḍha pramāṇau= asitaḥ ayam arthaḥ na śakyate anyathā kartum tarhi tayoḥ tulya balavattā na asti eva ekasya yathārtha tvāt iti kutas saṃśayaḥ yadi api vastu vṛttyā dvayoḥ yathārtha tā na asti tathā api anyatarasya viśeṣānupalambhena bhavet tulya balatva abhimānaḥ iti cedaḥ tu evam tathā api tulya bala tvāt yathottareṇa ādyam pratibadhyate tathā ādyena api uttaram pratibadhyate iti paraspara pratibandhāt ubhayoḥ sva sādhya sādhaka tvam na syāt na tu saṃśaya kartṛ tvam viśeṣa anupambha mātreṇa viruddha ubhaya viśeṣa upasthāna abhāvāt iti āha tulya bala tve ca tayoḥ parasparam virodhāt nirṇaya anutpādaka tvam syāt na tu saṃśaya hetu tvam iti 
NK_207.8	 nanu yat caḥ tu tat mūrtam bhavati amūrtam vā na mūrta amūrtābhyām prakāra antaram upalabdham atas manasi mūrtta tva amūrtta tvayoḥ anupalambhe api dvayoḥ abhāvam dvayoḥ api bhāvam asambhāvayataḥ bhavati eva anyatara pakṣe saṃśayaḥ satyam bhavati eva na tu viruddha avyabhicāri dharma dvaya sannipātāt kintu vastu tvāt yat mūrta tva amūrta tvābhyām dṛṣṭa āsāha caryam manasi pratīyamānam smṛti dvāreṇa tayoḥ upasthāpanam karoti 
NK_207.9–207.10	 tulya bala tvam abhyupagamya viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ saṃśaya hetu tvam nirastam na tu anayoḥ tulya bala tvam asti anyatarasya anumeya uddeśasya aamūrtam manaḥa iti asya āgamena tad abhāvāt aṇu manaḥ iti sūtreṇa bādhita tvāt atha idam sūtram apramāṇam vyāpakam eva manaḥ tadā manaḥ sadbhāve na kiñcid pramāṇam asti iti amūrttam manaḥ asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ atha yugapad jñāna anutpattyā siddham manasi ādāḥ dharmi grāhaka pramāṇa bādhitaḥ yugapad jñāna anutpatteḥ manasaḥ a ṇu parimāṇa tve sati sambhavāt vyāpaka tve manasaḥ yuga parsamaḥ ta indriya sambandhāt yugapad eva jñānāni prasajyante anumeya uddeśasya āgama virodhaḥ kim dūṣaṇam atas āha ayam tu viruddha bhedaḥ eva ayam āgama viruddhaḥ anumeya uddeśaḥ avirodhī pratijñā iti avirodhi grahaṇena nivartitānām pratyakṣa ādi viruddhānām pratijña ābhāsānām prabhedaḥ eva na ayam samdigdhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ kintu viruddha prabhedaḥ eva iti tuśabda arthaḥ 
NK_208.1	 yaḥ ca anumeye vidyamānaḥ tad samāna asamāna jātīyotasan= eva saḥ anyatara asiddhaḥ anadhyavasāya hetutvāt anadhta vasitaḥ yathā satkāryam utpatteḥ iti ayam aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ iti vacanāt avaruddhaḥ nanu ca ayam viśeṣaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ abhihitaḥ śāstre tulya jīyeṣu artha antara bhūteṣu viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iti na anya artha tvāt śabde viśeṣa darśanāt saṃśayān utpattiḥ iti ukte na ayam dravya ādīnām anyatamasya viśeṣaḥ syāt śrāvaṇa tvam kintu sāmānyam eva sampadyate kasmāt tulya jātīyeṣu artha antara bhūteṣu dravya ādi bhedānām ekaikaśas viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iti ukte na saṃśaya kāraṇam anyathā ṣaṭsu api padārtheṣu saṃśaya prasaṅgāt tasmāt sāmānya pratyakṣāt eva saṃśayaḥ iti 
NK_208.2	 anadhyavasitaḥ iti asādhāraṇaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ kathyate tam vyutpādayati yaḥ ca anumeye vidyamānaḥ tad samāna asamāna jātīyayoḥ asan= eva saḥ anyataratra asiddhaḥ anadhyavasāya hetu tvāt anadhyavasitaḥ yathā satkāryam utpatteḥ iti sarvam kāryam utpādāt pūrvam api sat iti sādhye utpatteḥ iti hetuḥ sāṃkhyānām sati sa pakṣe vyomāt ā= asati vipakṣe gagana kusuma ādā= abhāva at na ekatara pakṣa adhyavasāyam karoti viśiṣṭa artha kriyā janana yogyena rūpeṇa pūrvam anabhibyaktasya paścāt abhivyaktiḥ eva utpattiḥ iti sāṃkhyāḥ tena teṣām utpatteḥ iti hetoḥ na svatas asiddha tā 
NK_208.3^1	 ayam anadhyavasitaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ kena vacanena sūtra kṛtā saṃgṛhītaḥ iti āha ayam aprasiddhaḥ anapadeśaḥ iti vacanāt avaruddhaḥ iti anaikāntika vat asā dhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ saṃśayam karoti tena asya asandigdhaḥ ca anapadeṣaḥ a iti anena saṃgrahaḥ yuktaḥ na punar aprasiddha vacanena iti abhiprāyeṇa āha nanu ca ayam saṃśaya hetuḥ abhihitaḥ śāstre tulya jātīyeṣu artha antara bhūteṣu viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iti tulya jātīyeṣu artha antara bhūteṣu iti pañcamī arthe saptamī padārthānam viśeṣaḥ tulya jātīyebhyaḥ artha antara bhūtebhyaḥ bhavati yathā pṛthivyām gandhavat tvam viśeṣaḥ dravya antarebhyaḥ api syāt guṇa karmabhyaḥ ca bhavati 
NK_208.3^2	 śabde ca śrāvaṇa tvam viśeṣaḥ dṛśyate tat kim śabdasya rūpa ādibhyaḥ sajātīyebhyaḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ kim vā vijātīyebhyaḥ yadi śabdaḥ guṇaḥ tadā rūpa ādibhyaḥ sajātīyebhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ ayam atha dravyam karma vaḥ tadā vijātīyebhyaḥ iti śabde śrāvaṇa tvāt dravyam guṇaḥ karma iti saṃśayaḥ iti pūrva pakṣa vādinā sūtra virodhe darśite satyāha na anyārtha tvāt iti na ayam sūtra arthaḥ yat asādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ iti kintvasya anyaḥ eva arthaḥ tam eva artham darśayati śabde viśeṣa darśanāt ityādinā śrotra grahaṇaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ sa cabdaḥ iti pratipādya tasmin dravyam guṇaḥ karma iti saṃśaya iti abhihitam sūtrakāreṇa tasya ayam arthaḥ tasmin śrotra haṇe arthe saṃśayaḥ kim dravyam kim vā guṇaḥ kim uta karma iti 
NK_208.4^1	 atra pareṇa uktam śrotra grahaṇe śabde saṃśayam vadatā tvayā śrotra grāhya tvam eva saṃśaya kāraṇa tvam uktam śrotra grāhya tvam ca viśesaḥ tasya darśanāt saṃśaya anupapattiḥ viruddha ubhaya smṛti pūrvakaḥ hi saṃśayaḥ smṛtiḥ ca nāsā dhāraṇa dharma darśanāt bhavati tasya kenacid viśeṣeṇa saha anupalambhāt iti pareṇa ukte sati sūtrakāreṇa prativihitam etat na ayam dravya ādīnām anyatamasya viśaṣaḥ śrāvaṇa tvam dravya guṇa krmaṇām madhye anyatam asya dravyasya guṇasya karmaṇaḥ vā śrāvaṇa tvam viśeṣaḥ na bhavati kintu teṣām sāmānyam eva idam sampadyate kasmāt 
NK_208.4^2	 tulya jātīteṣu artha antara bhūteṣu ca dravya ādi bhedānāme kaikaśaḥ viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iti uktam bhidyante iti bhedāḥ dravya ādayaḥ eva bhedāḥ dravya ādi bhedāḥ dravya guṇa karmāṇi teṣām madhye ekaikasya dravyasya guṇasya karmaṇaḥ vā tulya jātīyebhyaḥ artha antara bhūtebhyaḥ viśeṣa aubhayathāḥ dṛṣṭaḥ a pṛthivyāḥ para jātīyebhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ pṛthivī tvam dravya tvena saha dṛṣṭam rūpasya viśeṣaḥ rūpa tvam guṇa tvena saha dṛṣṭam upkṣepaṇasya viśeṣaḥ utkṣepaṇa tvam karma tvena saha dṛṣṭam 
NK_208.4^3	 śabdasya api śrāvaṇa tvam viśeṣaḥ guṇa tvena saha dṛṣṭam tasmāt etat api viśeṣa tvena rūpeṇa dravya ādīnām sāmānyam eva tatas ca asya tena rūpeṇa saṃśaya hetu tvam yuktam yat punar asādhāraṇam rūpam na tat saṃśaya kāraṇam viśeṣa smāraka tvāvāt iti āha na saṃśaya kāraṇam iti tulya jātīyebhyaḥ artha antara bhūtebhyaḥ ca iti vaktavye sūtre saptamī abhidhānāt eṣaḥ api arthaḥ gamyate śabde śrāvaṇa tva viśeṣa darśanāt dravyam guṇaḥ karma iti saṃśayaḥ dravya ādi bhedānām ekaikaśas viśeṣasya tulya jātīyeṣu sa pakṣeṣu artha antara bhūteṣu vipakṣeṣu darśanāt iti kim uktam syāt 
NK_208.4^4	 viśeṣaḥ dravye guṇe karmāṇi ca dṛṣṭaḥ śabde ca śravaṇa tvam viśeṣaḥ dṛśyate tasmāt viśeṣa tvāt dravya ādi viṣayaḥ saṃśayaḥ yadi ca asādhāraṇam api rūpam saṃśaya kāraṇam tadā ṣaṭsu api padārtheṣu saṃśaya prasaṅgaḥ sarveṣām eva teṣām eva teṣām asādhāraṇa dharma yogi tvāt tatas ca saṃśayasya avirāma prama prasaṅgaḥ iti āha anyathā ṣaṭsu api padārtheṣu saṃśaya prasaṅgāt iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti sādhāraṇaḥ dharmaḥ viruddha viśeṣābhyām saha dṛṣṭa sāhacaryaḥ tayoḥ smaraṇam śaknoti kārayitum arasyat darśanāt eva saṃśayaḥ bhavati nāsā dhāraṇa dharma dharśanāt iti upasaṃhāra arthaḥ 
NK_209.1	 dvividham nidarśanam sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca tatra anumeya sāmānyena liṅga sāmānyasya anuvidhāna darśanam sādharmya nirśanam tat yathā yat kriyāvat tat dravyam dṛṣṭam yathā śaraḥ iti anumeya viryaye ca liṅgasya abhāva darśanam vaidharmya nidarśanam tasyathā yat adravyam tat kriyāvat na bhavati yathā sattā iti 
NK_209.2	 nidarśana svarūpa nirūpaṇa artham āha dvividham nidarśanam sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca iti sādhya sādhanayoḥ anugamaḥ nidarśyate yena vacanena tat vacanam sādharmya nidarśanam sādhya vyāvṛttyā sādhana vyāvṛttiḥ yena vacanena nidarśyate tad vaidharmya nidarśanam iti bhedaḥ tatra tayoḥ madhyesādharmi anidarśanam kathayati tatra anumeya ityādinā tad vyaktam eva vaidharmya nidarśanam kathayati anumeya viparyayaḥ ityādinā tat api vyaktam eva 
NK_210.1–210.2^1^1	 anena nidarśana ābhāsāḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti tat yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrtta tvāt yat amūrttam dṛṣṭam tat nityam yathā paramāṇuḥ yathā karma yathā sthālī yathā tamaḥ ambara vid iti yat dravyam tat kriyāvat dṛṣṭam iti ca liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśraya asiddhān anugata viparīta anugatāḥ sādharmya nidarśana ābhāsāḥ anena nidarśana ābhāsāḥ nirastāḥ bhavanti anidarśanāni api kenacid sādharmyeṇa nidarśana vat ābhāsantaḥ iti nidarśana ābhāsāḥ nidarśana sadṛśāḥ anena nidarśana lakṣaṇa kathanena arthān nirastāḥ bhavanti tad lakṣaṇa rahita tvāt 
NK_210.1–210.2^1^2	 yāvat nidarśana ābhāsānām svarūpam na jñāyate tāvat teṣām sva vākye varjanam para vākye ca upālambhaḥ na śakyate kartum atas teṣām svarūpam kathayati yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrta tvāt yat amūrtam tat nityam dṛṣṭam yathā paramāṇuḥ yathā karma yathā sthālī yathā tamaḥ ambara vat yat dravyam tat kriyāvat dṛṣṭam iti ca liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśraya asiddhān anugata viparīta anugatāḥ sādharmya niśana ābhāsāḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrta tvāt yathā paramāṇuḥ iti liṅga asiddhaḥ nidarśana ābhāsaḥ paramāṇoḥ amūrta tva abhāvāt yathā karma iti anumeya asiddhaḥ karmaṇaḥ nitya tva abhāvāt yathā sthālī iti ubhaya asiddhaḥ na sthālyām sādhyam nitya tvam asti na api sādhanam amūrta tvam 
NK_210.2^2	 yathā tamaḥ iti āśraya asiddhaḥ paramārthataḥ tamaḥ nāma na kiñcid asti kva sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāptiḥ kathyate ambara vat iti ananugataḥ ayam na darśana ābhāsaḥ yadi api ambare nitya tvam amūrtta tvam ubhayam api asti tathā api yat amūrtam tat nityam evam na brūte kintu ambara vat iti etāvat mātram āha na ca etasmāt vacanāt aprapannasya sādhya sādhanayoḥ ambare sadbhāva pratītiḥ asti tasmāt ananugataḥ ayam nidarśana ābhāsaḥ yat dravyam tat kriyāvat dṛṣṭam iti viparīta anugataḥ dravyam vāyuḥ kriyāvat tvāt iti atra api vyāpyam kriyāvat tvam vyāpakam ca dravya tvam yat ca vyāpyam tad eka niyatā vyāptiḥ na saṃyoga vat ubhayatra vyāsajyate vyāpakasya vyāpya vyabhicārāt yatra api samavyāptike kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādau vyāpyasya api vyāpaka tvam asti tatra api vyāpya tva rūpam samāśritā eva vyāptiḥ na vyāpaka tva rūpa āśrayā vyabhicāriṇī api tad rūpasya sambhavāt 
NK_210.3–210.5	 yathā upadiśanti guravaḥ vyāpaka tva gṛhītaḥ tu vyāpyaḥ yadi api vastutas ādhikye api aviruddha tvāt vyāpyam na pratipādayet iti atas vyāptiḥ vyāpya gata tvena darśanīyāḥ yat kriyāvat tat dravyam iti na vyāpaka gata tvena tatra tasyāḥ abhāvāt atas viparīta anugataḥ ayam liṅgam ca anumeyam ca ubhayam ca āśrayaḥ ca liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśrayāḥ te asiddhāḥ yeṣām te liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśraya asiddhāḥ liṅga anumeya ubhaya āśraya asiddhāḥ ca ananugatāḥ ca viparīta anugatāḥ ca iti yojanā 
NK_211.1–211.2^1	 yat anityam tat mūrtam dṛṣṭam yathā karma yathā paramāṇuḥ yathā ākāśam yathā tamaḥ ghaṭa vat yat niṣkriyam tat adravyañca iti liṅga anumeya ubhaya avi āvṛtta āśraya asiddha avi āvṛtta viparīta vyāvṛttāḥ vaidharmya vidarśana ābhāsāḥ iti vaidharmya nidarśana ābhāsān kathayati yat anityam ityādinā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrtta tvāt yat anityam tat mūrttam yathā karma iti liṅga avyāvṛttaḥ vaidharmya nidarśana ābhāsaḥ karmaṇaḥ mūrta tva abhāvāt yathā paramāṇuḥ iti anumeya avyāvṛttaḥ anumeyam nitya tvam paramāṇoḥ na vyāvṛttam yathā ākāśam iti ubhaya vyāvṛttaḥ na ākāśāt amūrta tvam na api natya tvam vyāvṛttam 
NK_211.1–211.2^2	 yathā tamaḥ iti āśraya asiddhaḥ paramārthataḥ tu tamaḥ eva na asti kim āśrayā sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāvṛttiḥ syāt ghaṭa vat iti avyāvṛttaḥ yadi api ghaṭe sādhya sādhanayoḥ asti vyāvṛttiḥ tathā api yat anityam tat mūrtam iti evam na vadati na ca tathā anabhidhāne sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāvṛtti pratipattiḥ vipratipannasya bhavati atas ayam avyāvṛttaḥ yat niṣkriyam tat adravyam iti viparīta vyāvṛttaḥ yathā sādhyam vyāpakam sādhanam vyāpyam tathā sādhya abhāvaḥ vyāpyaḥ sādhana abhāvaḥ ca vyāpakaḥ 
NK_211.3–211.5	 yathā uktam niyamya tva niyantṛ tve bhāvayoḥ yādṛśe mate viparīte pratīyete te eva tad abhāvayoḥ iti tatra dravyam vāyuḥ kriyāvat tvāt iti atra viparyaya vyāpti pradarśana artham tat akriyam iti vācyam ayam tu na tathā brūte kintu evam āha yat niṣkriyam tat adravyam iti evam ca na vyāptiḥ asti ākāśasya kriyā rahita tve api dravya tvāt tasmāt dvi parīta vyāvṛttaḥ ayam vaidharmya nidarśana ābhāsaḥ liṅgam ca anumeyam ca ubhayam ca liṅga anumeya ubhayāni tāni avyāvṛttāni yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ āśrayaḥ asiddhaḥ yasya saḥ āśraya asiddhaḥ liṅga anumeya ubhaya avyāvṛttaḥ ca āśraya asiddhaḥ ca avyāvṛttaḥ ca viparīta vyāvṛttaḥ ca iti vyākhyā 
NK_212.1	 nidarśane anumeya sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭasya liṅga sāmānyam anumeye anvānayanam anusandhānam anumeya dharma mātra tvena abhihitam liṅga sāmānyam anupalabdha śaktikam nirdarśane sādhya dharma sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭam anuyameye yena vacanena anusandhīyate tad anusandhānam tathā ca vāyuḥ kriya pvapniti anumeya abhāve ca tasya asattvam upalabhya na ca tathā vāyuḥ niṣkriyaḥ iti 
NK_212.2	 nidarśane anumeya sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭasya liṅga sāmānya spānu meye anvāvayanam anusandhānam nidarśyate niścitā sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāptiḥ asmin= iti nidarśanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ tasmin= anumeya sāmānyena sādhya sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭasya pratītasya liṅga sāmānyasya anumeye sādhya dharmiṇī anvānayanam sat bhāva upadarthanam yena vacanena kriyate tad anusandhānam dṛṣṭānte sādhyāvinābhūta tvena darśitam liṅgam pakṣe anusandhīyate pratipādyate anena iti vyutpattyā etat eva sva uktam vivṛṇoti anumeya dharma mātra tvena abhihitam liṅga sāmānyam iti pratijñā anantaram hetu vacanena liṅgam vastu vyāvṛttyā anumeye asti iti etāvān mātra tayā hetu tvena abhihitaḥ na tu dharmiṇi tasya sadbhāvaḥ kathitaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ liṅgasya sādhya pratipādane śaktiḥ anvaya vyatirekau pakṣa dharma tā ca sā pūrvam pratijñā hetu vacanābhyām tasya na avagatā iti anupalabdha śaktikam nidāśane sādhya dharma sāmānyena saha dṛṣṭa meye yena vacanena anusandhīyate tad anusandhānam iti 
NK_212.3^1	 ayam atra abhisandhiḥ para arthaḥ śabdaḥ yathā yathā parasya jijñāsā udayate tathā tathā prayujyate pratyetuḥ ca sādhye abhihite sādhane bhavati ākāṅkṣāḥ kutas idam siddhi ati iti na tu sādhanasya sāmarthye sva rūpa vagati pūrvaka tvāt sāmarthya jijñāsāyāḥ sādhane ca ākāṅkṣite pratyujyamānam hetu vacanam hetu svarūpa mātram kathayati na tasya pakṣa dharma tām ekasya śabdasya ubhaya artha vacaka tva abhāvāt vijñāte hetau katham asya hetu tvam iti sāmarthya jijñāsāyām sādhya pratīteḥ avinā abhāva pratītinā āntarīyaka tvāt vyāpti vacanena āvinā abhāve kathite sati avadhārita sāmarthyasya hetoḥ pakṣe paścāt sambhavaḥ jijñāsyata iti udāharaṇa anantaram pakṣa dharma tā avagama artham upagantavyaḥ upanayaḥ hetu tva abhidhāna sāmarthyāt eva pakṣa dharma tvam pratīyate vyadhikaraṇasya asādhaka tvāt iti ced tad abhidhāna sāmarthyāt vyāptiḥ api lapsyate ananvitasya hetu tva abhāvāt iti udāharaṇam api na vācyam 
NK_212.3^2–212.4^1	 asādhāraṇasya api bhrāntyā hetu tva abhidhāna upapatteḥ na tasmāt ekāntena anvaya pratītiḥ asti iti udāharaṇena vyāptiḥ upadarśyate iti ced dharmiṇī a vidyamānasya api bhrameṇa hetu tva abhidhāna upalambhāt naḥ tatas pakṣa dharmatā siddhiḥ asti iti udāharaṇa sthasya liṅgasya pakṣe astitatva niścaya artham upanayaḥ vācyaḥ asiddhasya bhramāt upanayaḥ api dṛśyate katham tasmāt api pakṣa dharmatā siddhiḥ iti ced asiddhāvinā bhāvasya api bhrāntyā vyāpti vacanam dṛśyate katham tasmāt anvaya siddhiḥ udāharaṇe vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa anusāreṇa anvaya niścayaḥ na vāc mātreṇa tasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt iti ced 
NK_212.3^2–212.4^2	 upanaye api pakṣa dharmatā grāhi pramāṇa anusārāt eva tad dharma tāniḥ cayaḥ na vacana mātrāt hetu abhidhānāni atha anupapattyā eva pakṣa dharma tā agra ahi pramāṇa anusāraḥ bhavati iti ced tat anyathā anupapattyā eva vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa anusāraḥ bhaviṣyati hetu vacanasya anya artha tvāt na tad upanayana sāmarthyam asti iti tad upasthāpanam udāharaṇena kriyate iti ced iha api sā eva rītiḥ anugamyatām alam anyathā sambhāvitena astu tarhi upanayaḥ vyartham hetu vacanam na asti hetu vacane sādhana svarūpa anavabodhāt tad sāmarthya jijñāsāyāḥ anupapatau udāharaṇa ādi vacanānām pravṛtti abhāvāt tathā ca nyāya bhāṣyam aasati hetau kasya sādhana bhāvaḥ pradarśyate a iti 
NK_213.1–213.2	 anumeya tvena uddiṣṭe ca aniścite ca pareṣām niścaya āpādana artham pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam pratyāmnāyaḥ pratipādya tvena uddiṣṭe ca aniścite ca pareṣām hetu ādibhiḥ ava yavaiḥ āhita śaktīnām parisamāptena vākyena vākyena niścaya āpādana artham pratijñāyāḥ panarvacanam pratyāmnāyaḥ tasmāt dravyam eva iti na hi etasmin na sati pūrveṣām avayavānām samastānām vyastānām vā tad artha vācaka tvam asti gamyamāna artha tvāt iti ced na atiprasaṅgāt tathā hi pratijñā anantaram hetu mātra abhidhānam kartavyam viduṣām anvaya vyatireka smaraṇāt tad artha avagatiḥ bhaviṣyati iti tasmāt atra eva artha parisamāptiḥ anusandhānasya ākāram darśayati tathā ca vāyuḥ kriyāvān iti vaidharmya anusandhānam āha anumeya abhāve anyatarasya asattvam upalabhya abhidhatte na ca tathā vāyuḥ niṣkriyaḥ iti 
NK_213.3	 pratyāmnāyam vyācaṣṭe anumeya tvena uddiṣṭe ca aniścite ca pareṣam punar niścaya āpādana artham pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam pratyāmnāya iti pratijñā vacanena pakṣe anumeya tvena pratipādya tvena uddiṣṭe sādhya dharme aniścite tasya eva sādhya dharmiṇi pratyāmnāyam pratyāvṛttyā abhidhānam yena vacanena kriyate tad pratyāmnāyaḥ abhihitasya punar abhidhānam kim artham atas āha pareṣām niścaya āpādana artham iti prathamam sādhyam abhihitam na tu tat niścitam pratijñā mātreṇa sādhya siddheḥ abhāvāt tasya upadarśite hetau kathite ca hetoḥ sāmarthye niścayaḥ pratyāmnāyena kriyate iti asya sāphalyam etat eva darśayati pratipādya tvena uddiṣṭaḥ ityādinā prathamam vacana mātreṇa pareṣam sādhya niścayaḥ na bhūtaḥ teṣām hetu udāharaṇa upanayaiḥ avayavaiḥ hetoḥ trairūpye darśite sañjāta anumeya pratipatti sāmarthyānām pratyāmnāye kṛte aparisamāptena a vākyena paripūrṇena avākyena a niścayaḥ jāyate iti etad artham pratijñāyāḥ panarvacanam pratyāmnāyaḥ pravarttate tasya udāharaṇam tasmāt dravyam eva iti 
NK_213.4–213.5	 hetta ādibhiḥ avayavaiḥ eva sādhyam niścīyate kim pratyāmnāyena iti atas āha na hi etasmin= asati iti pratijña ādayaḥ avayavāḥ pratyekam sva artha mātreṇa paryavasāyinaḥ asati pratyāmnāye na ekam artham pratipādayitum īśate svatantra tvāt sati tu etasmin= etat artha ākāṅkṣa upagṛhītāḥ aṅgāṅgi bhāvam upagacchantaḥ śaknuvanti iti yuktaḥ pratyāmnāyaḥ punar codayati gamyamāna artha tvāt iti 
NK_214.1^1	 ayam abhiprāyaḥ sva artha anumāne yā eva pratipatti sāmagrī sā eva para artha anumāne api iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ sva pratītau= iyam svayam anusandhīyate para pratītau ca pareṇa bodhyate svayam ca liṅga sāmarthyāt arthaḥ avagamyate parasya api tat eva gamakam vākyam tu liṅga upakṣepa mātre caritārtham pratipāditam ca hetu ādibhiḥ avayavaiḥ pakṣa dharma tā anvaya vyatireka upapannam liṅgam tāvatā eva ca tasmāt artha avagati sambhavāt kṛtam nigamanena iti samādhatte na ati prasaṅgāt iti vākyam liṅga sāmarthyam eva bodhayati na sādham kim tu tasya sāmarthyam bahis vyāpti pakṣa dharmatā mātram sati api tasmin prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭayoḥ asādhaka tvāt api tu abādhita viṣaya tvam asat pratipakṣa tvam api sāmarthyam 
NK_214.1^2	 tat ubhayam yāvat pramāṇena na pratipādyate tāvat pratipakṣa sambhava āśaṅkāyāḥ anivartanāt dharmiṇī u saṃhṛte api sādhane sādhya pratīteḥ ayogaḥ iti viparīta pramāṇa abhāva pratipādana artham nigamanam anena viparīta pramāṇa abhāva grāhakam pramāṇam upadarśyate tad abhāve pratipādite prakaraṇa sama kālatyaya apadiṣṭa tva abhāve niścite prakhyāpita sāmarthyam sādhanam sādhyam samarthayati iti pratyāmnāya upayogaḥ tatra yadi anuktam api sāmarthyam arthāt gamyate iti asya pratikṣepaḥ kriyate tadā udāharaṇa ādikam api pratikṣeptavyam pratijñā anantaram hetu abhidhāne viduṣām svayam eva anvaya vyatireka smaraṇāt artha avagati sambhavāt 
NK_214.2	 etat uktam bhavati na pratipannam prati para artha anumānam vaiyarthyāt na ca pratipādyasya kiyati aśe pratipattiḥ asti kiyati na asti iti śakyam avagantum para citta vṛtteḥ durunneya tvāt na api tad śakti anurodhāt vākya kalpanā yuktāḥ pratipattṝṇām vicitra śakti kattvāt tasmāt param bodhayatā yāvatā hetoḥ sādhaka tvam vastu vṛttyā upapadyate tāvān arthaḥ vacanena pratipādanīyaḥ na pratipattṛ viśeṣa anurodhena vartitavyam 
NK_214.3–214.7	 yathā uktam vastu pratyabhidhātavyam siddhārthaḥ na narān prati kaḥ hi vipratipanna arthāḥ tad buddhīḥ anudhāvati upasaṃharati tasmāt atra eva artha parisamāptiḥ iti yasmāt nigamane sati hetoḥ samagram sāmartham pratīyate tasmāt atra eva nigamane arthasya sādhyasya parisamāptiḥ pratīti paryavasānam yat vā evam yojanā yasmāt nigamanam antareṇa viparīta pramāṇa abhāvaḥ na avaganyate tasmāt etasmin eva arthasya samyak etu sāmarthyasya parisamāptiḥ paryavasānam iti pratyekam uktam eva avayavānām rūpam ekatra saṃhṛtya praśna pūrvakam kathayati katham ityādinā kim śabdaḥ nityaḥ kim vā anityaḥ iti anyatara dharma jijñāsāyām pratijñā vacanena aniścitena anitya tva mātreṇa viśiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ kathyate aanityaḥ śabdaḥ a iti 
NK_215.1–215.2	 katham anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti anena aniścita anitya tva mātra viśiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ kathyate prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti anena anitya tva sādhana dharma mātram abhidhīyate aiha yat prayatna ānantarīyakam tat anityam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭa a iti anena sādhya sāmānyena sādhana sāmānyasya anugama mātram ucyate nityam aprayatna ānantarīyakam dṛṣṭam yathā ākāśam iti anena sādhya abhāvena sādhanasya asattvam pradarśyate tathā ca prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca tathā ākāśa vat aprayatna ānantarīyakaḥ śabda iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām dṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya sa adhama sāmānyasya śabde anusamdhānam gamyate tasmāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti anena anityaḥ eva śabdaḥ iti pratipipādayiṣita artha parisamāptiḥ gamyate tasmāt pañca avayavena eva vākyena pareṣām svaḥ citā artha pratipādanam kriyate iti etad para artha anumānam siddham iti 
NK_215.3^1	 tatra kaḥ hetuḥ iti apekṣāyām prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt pūrvam asataḥ prayatna anantaram upalabhyamāna tvāt iti hetu vacanena anitya tvasya sādhana dharma mātram abhidhīyate mātra grahaṇena pakṣa dharma tāyāḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ ca anabhidhānam darśayati avagata sādhanasya katham idam sādhyam gamayati iti sādhana sāmarthya apekṣāyām iha jagati yat prayatna ānantarīyakam tat anityam dṛṣṭam iti udāharaṇena sādhya sāmānyena sādhana sāmānyasya anugama mātram karoti na tu svarūpa antaram iti mātra śabda arthaḥ nityam aprayatna ānantarīyakam iti vaidharmya nidarśanena sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāvaḥ pradarśyate yat prayatna āntarīyakam tat anityam iti dṛṣṭam etat kim tu śabde tat asti navā iti jijñāsāyām tathā ca prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ iti yathā ghaṭaḥ prayatna ānantarīyakaḥ yathā śabdaḥ api prayatna āntarīyakaḥ na ca tathā ākāśa vat aprayatnantarīyak iti anusandhānena anvaya vyatirekābhyām dṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya dṛṣṭa avinābhāvasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya śabde dharmiṇī anusandhānam avasthānam gamyate 
NK_215.3^2	 yathā yat kṛtakam tat anuṣṇam dṛṣṭam ghaṭaḥ iti sati api bahis vyāpti sambhave api kadācid kṛtakaḥ tejaḥ avayavī anuṣṇaḥ na bhavati pramāṇa virodhāt tathā yat ptayatna āntarīyakam tat anityam iti bahis vyāpti sambhave kadācid prayatna anantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ na bhavet iti vipakṣa āśaṅkāyām hetoḥ asādhaka tve tasmāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratyāmnāyaḥ yasmāt nitya tva pratipādakam pramāṇam mā asti tasmāt śabdaḥ anityaḥ nityaḥ na bhavati iti arthaḥ anena anya vyāvṛtti vācinā viparīta pramāṇa abhāva grāhakam pramāṇam upasthāpya tad abhāve pratipādite viparyaya śaṅkā nivṛttau darśita avinā abhāvāt hetoḥ dharmiṇī upasaṃhṛtāt vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa balena nirvicikitsaḥ sādhyam pratyeti na aparam kiñcid apekṣate iti anena pratyāmnāyena anityaḥ eva śabdaḥ iti pratipipādayiṣitasya arthasya parisamāptiḥ niścayaḥ gamyate 
NK_215.4	 sādhya vākya artha vādinaḥ tu nigamanasya ittham arthavat tvam samarthayanti anyat eva ghaṭasya kṛtaka tvam anyat śabdasya tatra yadi nāma ghaṭasya kṛtaka tvam anitya tvena vyāptam kim etāvatā śabda gatena api tathā bhavitavyam iti vyāmuhyataḥ darśitayoḥ api liṅgasya pakṣa dharma tva avina abhāvayoḥ sādhya pratīti abhave sati nigamanena tasmāt iti sarva nāmnā sāmānyena pravṛtta vyāpti grāhakam pramāṇam anusmārya śabde anitya tvam pratipādyate yasmāt yat kṛtakam tat anityam iti sāmānyena pratītam na viśeṣataḥ tasmāt kṛtaka tvena anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti etasmin pakṣe ca prakaraṇa sama kāla atyaya apadiṣṭa tva abhāvaḥ pakṣa vacanena eva upadarśyate asat pratipakṣa tva ābādhita viṣaya tvayoḥ pakṣa lakṣaṇa tvāt 
NK_215.5–215.6	 apare tu tasmāt iti trairūpyam eva parāmṛśanti ayasmāt yat kṛtakam tat anityam dṛṣṭam yasmāt kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ yasmāt ca pratipakṣa bādhayoḥ asambhavaḥ tasmāt kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ a iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti yasmāt pañcasu eva avayaveṣu samagrasya sādhana sāmarthyasya pratītau sādhya pratītiḥ paryavasyati na aparam kiñcid apekṣate tasmāt pañca avayavena eva anyūna adhikena vākyena sva niścitasya arthasya pratipādanam kriyate iti kṛtvā etat pañca avayavam vākyam para artha anumānam iti siddham vyavasthitam 
NK_216.1	 ye tu pratyakṣam eva ekam pramāṇam icchantaḥ na anumānam pramāṇam iti vadanti te idam praṣṭavyāḥ kim ekam eva pratyakṣam sva lakṣaṇam pramāṇam yat svarūpam pratīyate kim vā sarvam eva na tāvat ekam eva pramāṇam aparasya tad tulya sāmagrīkasya aprāmāṇya kāraṇa abhāvāt atha atītam anāgatam ca puruṣa antara varti sarvam eva pratyakṣam sva lakṣaṇam pramāṇam katham idam niścīyate pratīyamāna pramāṃa vyakti sajātīya tvāt iti ced aṅgīkṛtam svabhāva anumānasya prāmāṇyam 
NK_216.2	 evam anumāna pramāṇa tvam api vikalpya vācyam kaḥ ca pratyakṣam eva ekam pramāṇam iti pratipādyate na tāvat sva ātmā eva pratipādaka tvāt paraḥ ced sa kim pratipannaḥ pratipādyate vipratipannaḥ vā na tāvat pratipannaḥ pratipādyaḥ pratipannasya pratipādana vaiyarthyāt vipratipannaḥ ced paruṣa antara gatā vipratipattiḥ ca na pratyakṣeṇa gamyate vacana liṅgena anumīyate ced siddham kārya anumānasya prāmāṇyam 
NK_216.3–216.5	 anumānam apramāṇam iti kena pramāṇena sādhyate pratyakṣam vidhi viṣayam na kasyacid pratiṣedhe prabhavati anupalabdhyā tad avagamyate ced tarhi anupalabdhi liṅgakam anumānam syāt tathā ca uktam saugataiḥ pramāṇa itara sāmānya sthiteḥ anyadhiyaḥ gateḥ pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ pratiṣedhāt ca kasyacid iti pramāṇa tad abhāva sāmānya vyavasthāpanāt para buddheḥ abhigamāt kasyacid arthasya pratiṣedhāt ca pratyakṣāt pramāṇa antarasya svabhāva kārya anupalabdhi liṅgasya anumānasya sadbhāvaḥ iti vārttika arthaḥ iti 
NK_217.1–217.3	 viśeṣa darśana jam avadhāraṇa jñānam saṃśaya virodhī nirṇayaḥ etat eva pratyakṣam anumānam vā tat viśeṣa darśanāt saṃśaya virodhi utpadyate sa pratyakṣa nirṇayaḥ yathā sthāṇu puruṣayoḥ ūrdhva tā mātra sādṛśya ālocanāt viśeṣeṣu apratyakṣeṣu ubhaya viśeṣa anusmaraṇāt kim ayam sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā iti saṃśaya utpattau śiraḥ pāṇi ādi darśanāt puruṣaḥ eva ayam iti avadhāraṇa jñānam pratyakṣa nirṇayaḥ viṣāṇa mātra darśanāt gauḥ gavayaḥ vā iti saṃśaya utpattau sāsnā mātra darśanāt gaure vā ayam iti avadhāraṇa jñānam anumāna nirṇayaḥ iti nirṇayam kecid pratyakṣa anumānābhyām pramāṇa antaram icchanti tān pratyāha viśeṣa darśana jam ityādi yatra viśeṣa anupalambhāt saṃśayaḥ saṃjātaḥ tatra viśeṣa darśanāt jāyamānam avadhāraṇa jñānam nirṇayaḥ sa ca saṃśaya virodhī tasmin upajāyamāne saṃśayasya ucchedāt yathā āha maṇḍanaḥ vibhrama viveke 
NK_217.4	 niścite na khalu sthāṇau= ūrdhva tvena viśerate viśerate iti saṃśerataḥ iti arthaḥ yadi api sarvam eva niścaya ātmakam jñānam nirṇayaḥ tathā āya uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ nirṇaya tvena prasiddhi prābalyāt saṃśaya virodhi iti uktam sva uktam saṃgraha vākyam vivṛṇvan nirṇayasya pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ antarbhāvam darśayati etat eva pratyakṣam anumānam yat viśeṣa darśanāt saṃśaya virodhi utpadyate sa nirṇayaḥ iti pratyakṣa viṣaye yad avadhāraṇa ātmakam jñānam sa pratyakṣa nirṇayaḥ yat ca anumāna viṣaye avadhāraṇa jñānam saḥ anumāna nirṇayaḥ iti uparitanena grantha sandartheṇa kathayati 
NK_218.1–218.2^1	 liṅga darśana icchā anusmaraṇa ādi apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt paṭvā abhyāsa ādara pratyaya janitāt ca saṃskārāt dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu artheṣu śeṣa anuvyavasāya icchā anusmaraṇa dveṣa hetuḥ ahīta viṣayā smṛtiḥ iti smṛtaḥ lakṣaṇām vidyām ācaṣṭe liṅga darśana icchā ityādinā liṅga darśanam ca icchā ca anusmaraṇam ca ādi śabdena nyāya sūtra uktāni praṇidhāna ādīni gṛhyante tāni apekṣamāṇāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt iti smṛti kāraṇa kathanam ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya va liṅga darśana ādi sahakāritā eva viśeṣaḥ kevalāt asmāt smaraṇa anutpatteḥ 
NK_218.1–218.2^2	 liṅga darśana ādi vat saṃskāraḥ api smṛteḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti āha paṭvā abhyāsa ādara pratyaya janitāt ca saṃskārāt iti paṭu pratyayaḥ sphuṭatara pratyayaḥ tasmāt saṃskāraḥ jāyate tena gacchat tṛṇa saṃsparśa jñānāt kvacid paṭu pratyayayotpāde api grahaṇa yogyaḥ saṃskāraḥ na bhavati yathā sakṛt paṭhite anuvāke tena gṛhītasya āvṛttyā punar punar grahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ abhyāsaḥ saṃdkāra kāraṇam tasmin satya nuvākasya grahaṇa darśanāt kvacid atyanta āścarya kare vastuni sakṛt upalabdhe api kāla antare smṛti darśanāt ādara grahaṇam api saṃskāra nimittam dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu iti viṣaya saṅkīrtanam 
NK_218.3	 dṛṣṭeṣu iti pratyakṣa pratīteṣu śruteṣu iti śabda avagateṣu anubhūteṣu iti anumiteṣu iti arthaḥ śeṣa anuvyavasāya icchā smaraṇa dveṣa hetuḥ iti kārya nirūpaṇam śiṣyata pariśiṣyate iti aśeṣaḥ a aanu a paścāt vyavasitiḥ anuvyavasāyaḥ śeṣaḥ ca asau= anuvyavasāyaḥ ca śeṣa anuvyavasāyaḥ prathama upajāta liṅga jñāna apekṣayā tad anantar bhāvi anumeya jñānam tasya hetuḥ vyāpti smaraṇam sakha sādhana tva smṛtiḥ icchā hetuḥ prathama padasmṛtiḥ dvitīya pada anusmaraṇa hetuḥ duḥkha sādhaka smaraṇam dveṣa hetuḥ tat iti evam smṛteḥ ākāraḥ tatra ca arthasya atītattvam pūrva anubhū tvam pratīyate iti atīta viṣayā smṛtiḥ atas eva na pramāṇam tasyāḥ pūrva anubhava viṣaya tva upadarśanena artham niścinvatyāḥ artha paricchede pūrva anubhava pāratantryāt anumāna jñānam tu utpattau para apekṣam sva viṣaya paricchede svatantram eva smṛtiḥ iva tasmāt pūrvām ubhava anusandhānena artha pratīti abhāvāt yathā āhuḥ tantra ṭīkāyām sarva uttaradhiyaḥ guravaḥ 
NK_218.4–218.7	 pūrva vijñāna viṣayam vijñānam smṛtiḥ iṣyate pūrva jñānāt vinā tasyāḥ prāmāṇyam na avaganyate iti yathā ca idam āhuḥ kārikāyām tatra yat pūrva vijñānam tasya prāmāṇyam iṣyate tad upasthāna mātreṇa smṛteḥ syāt caritārtha tā iti ye tu anartha ja tvāt smṛteḥ aprāmāṇyam āhuḥ teṣām atīta anāgata viṣayasya anumānasya aprāmāṇyam syāt iti dūṣaṇam 
NK_219.1	 āmnāya vidhātṝṇām ṛṣīm atīta anāgata vartamāneṣu atīndriyeṣu artheṣu dharma ādiṣu grantha upanibaddheṣu anupanibaddheṣu ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt dharma viśeṣāt ca yat prātibham yathārtha nivedanam jñānam utpadyate tat ārṣam iti ācakṣate tat tu prastāreṇa deva ṛṣīṇām kadācid eva laukikānām yathā kanyakā bravīti aśvaḥ me bhrātā agantā iti hṛdayam me kathayati a iti 
NK_219.2	 siddha darśanam na jñāna antaram kasmāt añjana pāda lepa khaṅga gulikā ādi siddhānām dṛśya draṣṭṝṇām sūkṣma vyavahita viprakṛṣṭeṣu artheṣu pad darśanam tat pratyakṣam eva atha divya antarikṣa bhaumānām prāṇinām graha nakṣatra sañcāra ādi nimittam dharma adharma vipāka darśanam iṣṭam tat api anumānam eva atha liṅga anapekṣam dharma ādiṣu darśanam iṣṭam tat api pratyakṣa ārṣayoḥ anyatarasmin antarbhūtam iti evam buddhiḥ iti 
NK_219.3	 ārṣam vyācaṣṭe āmnāya vidhātṝṇām iti āmnāyaḥ vedaḥ tasya vidhātāraḥ kartāraḥ ye ṛṣayaḥ teṣām atīteṣu anāgateṣu vartamāneṣu atīndriyeṣu indriya patha atīteṣu dharma adharma diś kāla prabhṛtiṣu grantha upanibaddheṣu āgama pratipāditeṣu anupanibaddheṣu āgama apratipāditeṣu ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt yat prātibham jñānam yathā ātma nivedanam yathā anya svarūpa saṃvedanam saṃśaya viparyaya rahitam jñānam utpadyate tat ārṣam iti ācakṣate vidvāṃsaḥ indriya liṅga ādi abhāve yad artha pratibhānam sā pratibhā pratibhā eva prātibham iti ucyate vidvadbhiḥ tasya utpattiḥ anupapannā kāraṇa abhāvāt iti anuyoge sati idam uktam dharma viśeṣāt iti viśiṣyate iti viśeṣaḥ dharmaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ dharma viśeṣaḥ tapaḥ samādhi jaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ tasmāt pratibhā udayaḥ tat tu prātibham prastāreṇa bāhulyena deva ṛṣīṇām bhavati kadācid eva laukikānām yathā kanyakā bravīti śvas me bhrātā agantā iti hṛdayam me kathayati iti na ca idam saṃśayaḥ ubhaya koṭi saṃsparśa abhāvāt na ca viparyayaḥ saṃvādāt atas pramāṇam eva 
NK_219.4	 siddha darśanam api vidyā antaram iti kecid icchanti tad nivṛtti artham āha siddha darśanam na jñāna antaram etat eva upapādayati kasmāt ityādinā praśna pūrvaka mañjama pāda lepa ādi siddhānām dṛśyānām darśana yogyānām svarūpavatām padārthānām draṣṭāraḥ ye te asiddhāḥ a ucyante teṣām dṛśya draṣṭṝṇām añjana ādi siddhānām sūkṣmeṣu vyavahiteṣu viprakṛṣṭeṣu ca artheṣu yad darśanam indriya adhona anubhavaḥ tad pratyakṣam eva atha divya antarikṣa bhaumānām prāṇinā graha nakṣatra sañcāra nimittam dharma adharma vipāka darśanam siddha darśanam iṣṭam tat api anumānam eva graha sañcāra ādīnām liṅga tvāt atha liṅga anapekṣam dharma ādiṣu darśanam iṣṭam siddhānām tad pratyakṣa ārṣayoḥ anyatarasmin antarbhūtam yadi dharma ādi darśanam indriya jam tadā pratyakṣam atha indriya anapekṣam tadā ārṣam iti arthaḥ upasaṃharati evam buddhiḥ iti evam anantara ukta grantha krameṇa buddhiḥ vyākhyātā iti arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ pratisamāptim sūcayati 
NK_220.1	 anugraha lakṣaṇam sukham sraj ādi abhipreta viṣaya sānnidhye satīṣṭa upalabdhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt dharma ādi apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt anugraha abhiṣvaṅga nayana ādi prasāda janakam utpadyate tat sukham atīteṣu viṣyeṣu smṛti jam anāgateṣu saṅkalpa jam yat tu viduṣām asatsu viṣaya anusmaraṇa icchā saṅkalpeṣu āvirbhavati tad vidyā śama samtoṣa dharma viśeṣa nimittam iti 
NK_220.2^1	 buddhi kārya tvāt sukham buddhi anantaram vyācaṣṭe anugraha lakṣaṇam sukham iti anugṛhyate anena iti anugrahaḥ anugraha lakṣaṇam anugraha svabhāvam iti arthaḥ sukham hi anukūla svabhāva tayā svaviṣaya manu bhavam kurvan puruṣam anugṛhṇāti etat eva vyācaṣṭe sraj ādi iti sraj candana vanitā ādayaḥ ye abhipretāḥ viṣayāḥ teṣām sānnidhye sannikarṣe sati iṣṭī pa labdhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt dharma ādi apekṣāt yat utpadyate tat sukham indriya sannihite api abhite api abhimate arthe viṣaya antara vyāsaktasya sukha anutpāda ādiṣṭa upalabdheḥ kāraṇa tvam gamyate viyuktasya sukha abhāvāt viṣaya sannikarṣasya api kāraṇatva avagamaḥ dharma ādi ityādi padena svastha tā ādi parigrahaḥ anugraha abhiṣvaṅga nayana ādi prasāda janakam iti kārya upavarṇanam anugrahaḥ sukha viṣayam saṃvedanam 
NK_220.2^2–220.3	 abhiṣvaṅgaḥ anurāgaḥ nayana ādi prasādaḥ vaimalyam ādi śabdāt mukhprasādasya grahaṇam eteṣām sukham janakam sekhena utpannena sva anubhavaḥ janyate saḥ eva ātmanaḥ anugrahaḥ sukhe ca upajāte mukha ādīnām prasanna tā syāt sukha sādhaneṣu anurāgaḥ sukhāt bhavati atīteṣu smṛti jam atīteṣu sukha sādhaneṣu anubhūteṣu sukham pūrva anusmaraṇāt bhavati anāgata ūṣu idam me bhaviṣyati iti saṅkalpāt jāyate yat tu viduṣām ātma jñānavatām asatsu viṣaya anusmaraṇa saṅkalpeṣu asati viṣaye asati ca anusmaraṇe asati ca saṅkalpe ca āvirbhavati tad vidyā śama santoṣa dharma viśeṣa nimittam iti vidyā ātma jñānam śamaḥ jita indriya tvam santoṣaḥ deha sthiti hetu mātra atiriktān abhikāṅkṣi tvam dharma viśeṣaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ nivartaka lakṣaṇaḥ etat catuṣṭaya nimittam ye tu duḥkha abhāvam eva sukham āhuḥ teṣām ānanda ātma tā anubhava virodhaḥ hitam āpsyāmi ahitam hāsyāmi iti pravṛtti dvaividhya anupapattiḥ ca 
NK_221.1–221.2	 upaghāta lakṣaṇam duḥkham viṣa ādi anabhipreta viṣaya sānnidhye satya niṣṭa upalabdhi indriya artha sannikarṣāt arma ādi apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt yat amarṣa upaghāta dainya nimittam utpadyate tat duḥkham atīteṣu sarpa vyāghra caura ādiṣu smṛti jam anāgateṣu saṅkalpa jam iti sukha pratyanīka tayā tad anantaram duḥkham vyācaṣṭe upaghāta lakṣaṇam duḥkham upahanyate anena iti upaghātaḥ upaghāta lakṣaṇam upaghāta svabhāvam duḥkham upajātam pratikūla svabhāva tayā sva ātma viṣayam anubhavam kurvat ātmānam upahanti etāt vivṛṇoti aniṣṭa upalabdhī iti ādinā amaeṣaḥ asahiṣṇu tā dveṣaḥ iti yāvat upaghātaḥ duḥkha anubhavaḥ dainyam vicchāyatā teṣām nimittam duḥkhe sati tad anubhava lakṣaṇaḥ ātma upaghātaḥ syāt atīteṣu sarpa ādiṣu smṛti jam anāgateṣu saṅkalpajam iti sukha vat vyākhyānam 
NK_222.1–222.2	 sva artham para artham vā aprāpta prārthanā icchā sā ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt sukha ādi apekṣāt smṛti apekṣāt votpadyate prayatna smṛti dharma adharma hetuḥ kāmaḥ abhilāṣaḥ rāgaḥ saṅkalpaḥ kāruṇyam vairāgyam upadhāḥ bhāvaḥ iti evam ādaye icchā bhedāḥ maithuna icchā kāmaḥ abhyavahāra icchā abhilāṣaḥ punar punar viṣaya anurañjana icchā rāgaḥ anāsanna kriyā icchā saṅkalpaḥ sva artham anapekṣya para duḥkha prahāṇa icchā kāruṇyam doṣa darśanāt viṣayati āga icchā vairāgyam para vañcana icchā upadhā antar nigūḍha icchā bhāvaḥ cikīrṣā aji hīrṣā iti ādi kriā bhedāt icchā bhedāḥ bhavanti 
NK_222.3	 sva artham para artham vā aprāpta prārthanā icchā aprāptasya vastunaḥ sva artham prati yā prārthanā idam me bhūyāt iti para artham vā yā prārthanā asya idam bhavatu iti sā icchā sā ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt sukha ādi apekṣāt smṛti apekṣāt votpadyate anāgate sukha sādhane vastuni icchā upajāyate tad utpattau ca tad viṣaya sādhyam sukham anāgatam api buddhi siddha tvāt nimitta kāraṇam yathāḥ nyāya vārttikakāraḥ phalasya prayojaka tvāt iti atikrānte sukha hetau= icchā utpatteḥ smṛtiḥ kāraṇam prayatna smṛti dharma ādhārma hetuḥ upādāna icchātaḥ tad anuguṇaḥ prayatnaḥ bhavati smaraṇa icchātar smaraṇam vihiteṣu jyotiṣṭoma ādiṣu phala icchayā pravṛttasya dharmaḥ jāyate pratiṣiddheṣu rāgāt pravṛttasya adharmaḥ kāma ādayaḥ api santi te kasmāt na uktāḥ atas āha kāmaḥ ityādi 
NK_222.4	 kāma ādayaḥ icchā prabhedāḥ na tattva antaram iti yat uktam tat eva darśayati maithuna icchā kāmaḥ iti nirupapadaḥ kāma śabdaḥ maithuna icchāyam eva pravartate anyatra tasya pada antara samabhivyāhārāt pravṛttiḥ yathā svarga kāmaḥ yajeta iti abhyavahāra icchāḥ abhilāṣāḥ abhyavahāraḥ bhojanam tatra icchā abhilāṣaḥ punar punar viṣaya anurañjana icchā rāgaḥ punar viṣayāṇām bhoga icchā rāgaḥ iti arthaḥ anāsanna kriyā icchā saṅkalpaḥ anāgatasya arthasya karaṇa icchā saṅkalpaḥ sva artham anapekṣya para dūkha prahāṇa icchā kāruṇyam sva artham sva prayojanam kim api anabhisamdhāya yā para duḥkha prahāṇe apanayane icchā sā kāruṇyam doṣa darśanāt duḥkha hetutva avagamāt viṣayāṇām parityāga icchā vairāgyam para vañcana icchā para pratāraṇa icchā upadhā antar nigūḍha icchā liṅgaiḥ āvirbhāvitā yā icchā sā bhāvaḥ cikīrṣā jihīrṣāḥ iti ādi kriyā bhedāt icchā bhedāḥ bhavanti karaṇa icchā cikīrṣā haraṇa icchā jihīrṣā gamana icchāḥ jigamiṣā iti evamādayaḥ icchā bhedāḥ kriyā bhedāt bhavanti 
NK_223.1–223.2	 prajvalana ātmakaḥ dveṣāḥ yasmin sati prajvalitam iva ātmānam manyate sa dveṣāḥ sa ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt duḥkha apekṣāt smṛtyāā īkṣāt vā utpadyate yatna smṛti dharma adharma smṛti hetuḥ krodhaḥ drohaḥ manyuḥ akṣamāḥ amarṣaḥ iti dveṣa bhedāḥ prajvalana ātmakaḥ dveṣaḥ etat vivṛṇoti yasmin sati ityādinā tad vyaktam sa ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt duḥkha apekṣāt smṛti apekṣāt vā utpadyate sannihite duḥkha hetau= anubhūyamāne tad sādhye duḥkhe dveṣaḥ duḥkhāt utpadyate atīte duḥkha hetau tad ja duḥkha smṛti jaḥ dveṣaḥ prayatna dharma smṛti hetuḥ enam aham manmi iti prayatnaḥ dveṣāt veda artha viplava kāriṣu dveṣāt dharmaḥ tad artha paripālana pareṣu dveṣāt adharmaḥ smṛtiḥ api dveṣāt upajāyate yaḥ yam dveṣṭi sa tam satatam smarati krodhaḥ drodhaḥ manyuḥ akṣamāḥ amarṣaḥ iti dveṣa bhedāḥ śarīra indriya ādi vikāra hetuḥ kṣaṇa mātra bhāvī dveṣaḥ krodhaḥ alakṣita vikāraḥ cira anubaddha apakāra avasānaḥ dveṣaḥ drohaḥ apakṛtasya pratyapakāra asamarthasya antar nigūḍhaḥ dveṣaḥ manyuḥ para guṇa dveṣaḥ akṣamā sva guṇa paribhava samutthaḥ dveṣaḥ amarṣaḥ 
NK_224.1–224.4	 prayatnaḥ saṃrambhaḥ utsāhaḥ iti paryāyāḥ sa dvividhaḥ jīvana pūrvakaḥ icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ ca tatra jīvana pūrvakaḥ suptasya prāṇa apāna santāna prerakaḥ prabodha kāle ca antaḥkaraṇasya indriya antara prāpti hetuḥ asya jīvana pūrvakasya ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt dharma adharma apekṣāt utpattiḥ itaraḥ tu hita ahita prāpti parihāra samarthasya vyāpārasya hetuḥ śarīra vidhārakaḥ ca sa ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt icchā pekṣāt dveṣa apekṣāt votpadyate prayatnaḥ saṃrambhaḥ utsāhaḥ iti paryāyāḥ sa dvividhaḥ jīvana pūrvakaḥ icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ ca iti sa dehasya ātmanaḥ vipacyamāna karma āśaya sahitasya manasā saha saṃyogaḥ sambandhaḥ jīvanam tad pūrvakaḥ prayatmaḥ kāmartha kriyām karoti iti atas āha 
NK_224.5	 tatra jīvana pūrvakaḥ iti suptasya prāṇa apāna kriyā prayatna kāryā prāṇa apāna kriyā tvāt jāgrataḥ pāṇa apāna kriyāvat kriyā tvāt na ca tadānīm icchā dveṣau prayatna hetū sambhavataḥ tasmāt jīvana pūrvakaḥ eva prayatnaḥ prāṇa apāna prekaḥ gamyate na kevalam jīvana pūrvakaḥ prayatnaḥ prāṇa apāna prerakaḥ kintu pta bodha kāle antaḥkaraṇasya indriya antara prāpti hetuḥ ca viṣaya upalambha anumita antaḥkaraṇa indriya saṃyogaḥ prayatna pūrvaka antaḥkaraṇa kriyā janyaḥ antaḥkaraṇa indriya saṃyoga tvāt jāgara antaḥkaraṇa indriya saṃyoga vat iti prayatna pūrvaka tā siddhiḥ asya jīvana pūrvakasya ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt dharma adharma apekṣat utpattiḥ dharma adharma apekṣaḥ ātma manasoḥ saṃyogaḥ jīvanam tasmāt asya utpattiḥ iti arthaḥ 
NK_224.6	 itaraḥ tu icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ tu hita ahita prāpti pati hāra samarthasya vyāpārasya hetuḥ śarīra vidhārakaḥ ca guru tve satya patataḥ śarīrasya icchā pūrvakaḥ prayatnaḥ vidhārakaḥ sa ca ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt icchā dveṣa apekṣāt utpadyate hita sādhana upādāne prayatnaḥ icchā pūrvakaḥ duḥkha sādhana parityāge prayatnaḥ dveṣa pūrvakaḥ 
NK_225.1–225.2	 guru tvam jala bhūmyoḥ patana karma kāraṇam apratyakṣam patana karma ānuneyam saṃyoga prayatna saṃskāra virodhi tasya ca ābādi paramāṇu rūpa ādi vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ guru tvam jala bhūnyoḥ iti āśraya kathanam patana karmāraṇam iti tasya kārya nirūpaṇam apratyakṣam iti svabhāva upavarṇanam na kenacid indriyeṇa guru tvam gṛhyate iti arthaḥ 
NK_225.3^1	 ye tu tvac indriya grāhyam guru tvam āhuḥ teṣām adhas sthitasya dravyasya sparśa upalambha vat guru tva upalambha prasaṅgaḥ tvac indriyasya artha upalambhe sva sannikarṣa vyatirekeṇa anya apekṣā sambhavāt yat tu uparisthitasya guru tvam pratīyate tad hasta ādīnām adhas gamana anumānāt atīndriyam ced katham asya pratītiḥ iti atas āha patana karma anumeyam iti yat avayavi dravyasya patanam tena yat eka artha samavetā samavāyika arṇam anamīyate tat eva hi naḥ guru tvam etena etat pratyuktam yat uktam aparaiḥ avayavi guru tva kāryasya avanati viśeṣasya anupalambhāt avayau iti guru tva abhāvaḥ iti avayavinaḥ patana abhāva prasaṅgāt 
NK_225.3^2	 atha avayavānām guru tvāt eva tasya patanam tadā avayavānām api svāvayāva apekṣayā avayavi tvāt patanam iti sarvatra kārye tad ucchedaḥ atha vyadhikaraṇebhyaḥ sva avayava guru tvebhyaḥ avayavānām patana asambhavāt teṣu guru tvam kalpyate tadā avayavivī api kalpanīyam nyāyasya samāna tvāt yat punar avayavi guru tvasya kārya atirekaḥ na gṛhyate tad avayava avayavi guru tva bhedasya alpa antara tvāt yathā mahati dravye unmīyamāne tata parita sūkṣma dravya antara guru tva kārya antara agrahaṇam 
NK_225.4–225.5	 saṃyoga prayatna saṃskāra virodhi guru tvasya saṃyogena prayatnena vega ākhyena ca saṃskāreṇa saha virodhaḥ vidyate taiḥ pratibaddhasya sva kārya akaraṇāt tathā ca dolā ārūḍhasya saṃyogena pratibandhāt apatanam prayatnena pratibandhāt aparanam ca śarīrasya vegena pratibandhāt apatanam bahis kṣiptasya śara śalāka ādeḥ tasya ca ābādi paramāṇu rūpa ādi vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ yathā api aparamāṇu rūpa ādayaḥ nityāḥ tathā pārthiva apya paramāṇuṣu api guru tvam yathā ca ābādi kārya dravye kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa rūpa ādayaḥ jāyante āśraya vināśāt ca vinaśyanti tathā guru tvam api 
NK_226.1–226.2	 dravyam syandana karma kāraṇam tri dravya vṛtti tat tu dvividham sāṃsiddhikam naimittikam ca saṃsiddhi kamapām viśeṣa guṇaḥ naimittikam pṛthivī tejasoḥ sāmānya guṇaḥ sāṃsiddhikasya guru tva vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ saṅghāta darśanāt sāṃsiddhi ka drava tvana yuktam iti ced na divyena tejasā saṃyuktānām āpyānām paramāṇūnām parasparam saṃyogaḥ dravya ārambhakaḥ saṅghāta ākhyaḥ tena paramāṇu drava tva pratibandhāt kārye hima karakā t audrava tva anutpattiḥ 
NK_226.3	 naimittikam ca pṛthivī tejasoḥ agni saṃyoga jam katham sarpiḥ jatu madhūcchiṣṭa ādīnām kāraṇeṣu paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogāt vega apekṣāt karma utpattau tad jebhyaḥ vibhāgebhyaḥ dravya ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt kārya drvi a nivṛttau= agni saṃyogāt auṣṇya apekṣāt svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu dravya tvam utpdyate tatas teṣu bhoginām adṛṣṭa apekṣāt ātma aṇu saṃyogāt karma utpattau tad jebhyaḥ saṃyogebhyaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kārya dravyam utpadyate tasmin ca rūpa ādi utpatti sama kālam kāraṇa guṇa prakrameṇa drava tvam utpadyate iti 
NK_226.4–226.5	 drava tvam syandana karma kāraṇam yat syandana karma kāraṇam tat drava tvam iti arthaḥ tri dravya vṛtti pṛthivī udaka jvalana vṛtti iti arthaḥ tat tu dvividham iti guru tvam ekavidham drava tvam tu dvividham iti tuśabda arthaḥ naimittikam sāṃsiddhikam ca nimittam vahni saṃyogaḥ tasya idam kāryam iti naimittikam sāṃsiddhikam svabhāva siddham vahni saṃyoga anapekṣam iti yāvat sāṃsiddhikam apām viśeṣa guṇaḥ anyatra abhāvāt naimittikam pṛthivī tejasoḥ sāmānya guṇaḥ sādhāraṇa guṇa tvāt sāṃsiddhikasya dravya tvasya guru tva vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ yathā nitya dravya samavetam guru tvam nityam anitya dravya samavetam ca kārya kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt vinaśyati iti tathā sāṃsiddhikam dravya tvam api
