NK_226.6	 atra codayati saṅghāta darśanāt sāṃsiddhi ka dravyavatvam ayuktam iti ced āpyasya himakaraka ādeḥ dravyasya saṅghāta darśanāt kāṭhinya darśanāt apām svabhāva siddham dravya tvam iti ayuktam samādhatte divyena iti sarvatra udake svabhāva siddhasya drava tu asya upalambhāt apām svabhāva siddham eva drava tvam tāvat niścitam yatra tu himakaraka ādau kārye drava tva anutpattiḥ tatra divyena tejasā saṃyuktānām ā api a paramāṇūnām paraspara saṃyogaḥ dravya ārambhakaḥ saṅghāta ākhyaḥ tena himakaraka ārambhakāṇām paramāṇūnām drava tva pratibandhāt tejaḥ saṃyogena paraṃaṇūnām drava tvam pratibaddham iti anyatra api adravyasya lavaṇasya vahni saṃyogena drava tva pratibandha darśanāt anumitam lavaṇasya api atvam api hima karaka ādi vat kāla antareṇa dravībhāva darśanāt avagatam vilayanam tu himakaraka ādeḥ bhauma agni saṃyogāt yat vilayanam laṭhina dravyasya tad vahni saṃyogāt avagatam yathā suvarṇa ādīnām himakaraka ādi vilayanam api vilayanam eva tasyāt iha api dṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ vahnismāyogaḥ eva nimittam āśrīyate 
NK_226.7	 sāṃsiddhikam dravya tvam vyākhyāya naimittikam drava tvam vyācaṣṭe naimittikam pṛthivī tejasoḥ agni saṃyoga jam iti katham iti ajñena pṛṣṭaḥ san= upapādayati sarpiḥ iti ādinā sarpiḥ jatu madhūcchiṣṭānām pārthivānām kāraṇeṣu paramāṇuṣu agni saṃyogāt karma utpattau satyām karma jebhyaḥ vibhāgebhyaḥ sarpiḥ ādi a ārambhaka saṃyoga vināśāt sarpiḥ ādi dravya nivṛttau satyām svatantreṣu paramāṇuṣu vahni saṃyogāt drava tvam utpadyate tad anantaram utpanna drava tveṣu paramāṇuṣu bhoginām a gṛṣṭa apekṣāt ātma paramāṇu saṃyogāt kriyā utpattau satyām karma jebhyaḥ paramāṇūnam paraspara saṃyogebhyaḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa kārya dravye jāte rūpa ādi utpatti kāle eva kāraṇa drava tvebhyaḥ drava tvam utpadyate himakaraka ādi vilayane a pi evam eva kramaḥ 
NK_227.1–227.2	 sneha haḥ apām viśeṣa guṇaḥ saṃgraha mṛjā ādi hetuḥ asya api guru tva vat nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ snehaḥ aviśeṣa guṇaḥ saṃgraha mṛjā ādi hetuḥ saṃygrahaḥ parasparam asmāyuktānām saktvādīnām piṇḍībhāva prāpti hetuh sma ayoga viśeḍaḥ mṛjā kāyasya udvartana ādi kṛtā viśuddhiḥ ādi śabdāt mṛdu tvam ca teṣām hetuḥ snehaḥ asya api guru tva vat nitya anitya tva viṣpattayaḥ guru tvam ca paramāṇuṣu nityam kārye ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam āśraya vināśāt vināśi tathā sneha upi iti 
NK_228.1–228.2^1	 saṃskāraḥ trividhaḥ vegaḥ bhāvanā sthiti sthāpakaḥ ca tatra vegaḥ mūrtimatsu pañcasu dravyeṣu nimitta viśeṣa apekṣāt karmaṇaḥ jāyate niyata dikkriyā prabandha hetuḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga viśeṣa virodhī kvacid kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa utpadyate saṃskāraḥ trividhaḥ vegaḥ bhāvanā sthāpakaḥ ca iti tatra vegaḥ mūrtimatsu pañca dravyeṣu nimitta viśeṣa apekṣāt karmaṇaḥ jāyate pañcasu dravyeṣu pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vovāyu manassu karma vegam karoti na anyatra svayam abhāvāt nodana abhighāta ādi nimmitta viśeṣa apekṣam na kevalam manda gatau vega abhāvāt 
NK_228.1–228.2^2	 niyati dikkriyā prabandha hetuḥ yat diś ābhi mukhyena kriyayā vegaḥ janyate tad diś abhimukha tayā eva kriyā santānasya hetuḥ iti arthaḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga viśeṣa virodhī viśiṣṭena sparśavat dravya saṃyogena atyanta nibaḍa avayava vṛttinā vegaḥ vināśyate yaḥ svayaṃviśiṣṭaḥ mandaḥ tu vegaḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyoga mātreṇa vinaśyati yathā ati dūram gatasya iṣaḥ stimita vāyu pratibaddhasya kvacid kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa utpadyate bāhulyena tāvat vegaḥ karma jaḥ kvacid vegavat avayava ārabdhe jala avayavini kāraṇa vegebhyaḥ a pi jāyate 
NK_229.1–229.2	 bhāvanā saṃjñakaḥ tu ātma guṇaḥ dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūtesu artheṣu smṛti pratyabhijñāna hetuḥ bhavati jñāna mada duḥkha ādi virodhī paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyaya jaḥ paṭu pratyaya apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt āścarye arthe paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ jāyate yathā dākṣiṇāti asya uṣṭra darśanāt iti vidyā śilpa vyāyāma ādiṣu abhyāsyamāneṣu tasmin= eva arthe pūrva pūrva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇāt uttara uttarasmāt pratyayāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskāra atiṣayaḥ jāyate 
NK_229.3^1	 bhāvanā sañjñakaḥ tu ātma guṇaḥ bhāvanā saṃjñakaḥ tu sma āskāraḥ ātma guṇaḥ dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu iti dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu artheṣu smṛteḥ pratyabhijñānasya ca hetuḥ iti tasya kārya kathanam dṛṣṭa śruta anubhūteṣu iti viparyaya avagataḥ ari arthaḥ boddhavyaḥ tatra api smṛti darśanāt jñāna mada duḥkha ādi virodhī pratipakṣa jñānena saṃskāraḥ vināśyate dyūta ādi vyasana āpannasya pūrva adhīta vismaraṇāt medena api saṃskārasya vināśaḥ surā mattasya pūrva smṛti vilopāt maraṇa ādi duḥkhāt api saṃskāraḥ vinaśyati janma antara anubhūta smaraṇa abhāvāt ādi śabdena sukha ādi parigrahaḥ bhoga āsaktasya kupitasya vā pūrva vṛtta smṛti abhāvāt paṭu abhyāsa ādara pratyayanaḥ paṭu pratyayāt abhyāsa pratyayāt ādara pratyayāt ca saṃskāraḥ jāyate paṭu pratyaya apekṣāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt āścarye arthe paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ jāyate 
NK_229.3^2	 yathā dākṣiṇāti asya uṣṭra darśanāt iti uṣṭraḥ ḍakṣiṇātyasya atyantān anubhūta ākāra tvāt āścarya bhūtaḥ arthaḥ tad darśanāt tasya paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ jāyate kāla antare api uṣṭra anubhava smṛti jananāt abhyāsa pratyaya jam saṃskāram daṛśayati vidyā śilpa vyāyāma ādiṣu ityādinā vidyā śāstra āgama ādikāḥ śilpam pattra bhaṅga ādi kriyā vyāyāmaḥ āyudha ādi śramaḥ teṣu abhyasyamāneṣu tasmin eva arthe pūrva gṛhīte pūrva pūrva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskāra atiśāyaḥ jāyate yaḥ su ciram anuvartate sphuṭataram ca smaraṇam karoti na hi ādya anubhavaḥ eva sma āskāra viśeṣam ādhatte prathamam kadartha smaraṇa abhāvāt na api uttaraḥ eva tasya hetuḥ pūrva abhyāsa vaiyarthyāt tasmāt pūrva saṃskāra apekṣā uttara uttara anubhava ahita adhika adhika saṃskāra utpatti krameṇa upāntya saṃskāra apekṣā dantya anubhavāt tad utpattiḥ 
NK_230.1	 idam tu iha nirūtyate vidyāyām abhyasyamānāyām kim tad arthaḥ vākyena pratipādyate kim vā sphoṭena kutas saṃśayaḥ vipratipatteḥ eke vadanti sphoṭaḥ artham pratipādayati iti apare tu āhuḥ yakam iti atas yuktaḥ kim tāvat prāptam sphoṭaḥ artha pratyāyakaḥ iti yadi hi varṇān atiiriktam padam pada anatiriktam ca vākyam tadā artha pratyayaḥ eva na syāt iti tathā hi na varṇāḥ pratyekam artha viṣayām dhiyam āvirbhāvayanti śeṣa varṇa vaiyarthyāt samudāyaḥ ca teṣām na sambhavati antya varṇa grahaṇa samaye pūrveṣām asambhavāt nitya tvāt varṇānām asti samudāyaḥ iti ced tathā api na teṣām pratītiḥ anuvartate apratīyamānānām ca pratyāyaka tve sarvadā artha pratīti prasaṅgaḥ na hi pratītya apratīyamānānām sarvathā apratīyamānānām ca kaścid viśeṣaḥ pūrva avagatāḥ varṇāḥ smṛti ārūḍhāḥ pratīti hetavaḥ iti ced yadi hi smṛtiḥ api krama bhāvinī tadā na asti varṇa vat sāhityam tṛtīya varṇa grahaṇa kāle prathama varṇa smṛti vilopāt yugapad utpādaḥ tu smṛtī nāmanā śaṅkanīyaḥ eva jñāna yauga padya pratiṣedhāt 
NK_230.2	 atha prathamam ādye varṇe jñānam tena sma āskāraḥ tadanu dvitīya varṇa jñānam tena prāktanena saṃskāreṇa antaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ saṃskāraḥ janyate iti anena krameṇa antye nikhila varṇa viṣayaḥ saṃskāraḥ jātaḥ nikhila varṇa viṣayām ekām eva smṛtim yugapad karoti iti āśrīyate tadākramaḥ hīyate kramaḥ hi paurvāparyam tat ca deśa nibandhanam kāla nibandhanam vā syāt ubhayam api tad varṇeṣu na avakāśam labhate teṣām sarva gata tvāt nitya tvāt ca buddhi krama nibandhanaḥ tu varṇānām kramaḥ bhavet sa ca ekasyām smṛti buddhau viparivartamānānām pratyasta mite iti akramāṇām eva pratipādaka tvam tat śca saraḥ rasaḥ vanam navam nadī dina ityādiṣu artha bheda pratyayaḥ na syāt varṇānām abhedāt kramasya prati iti anaṅga tvāt ca asti ca ayam pratīti bhedaḥ savarṇeṣu anupapadyamānaḥ tarhi atiriktam nimitta antaram ākṣipati iti sphoṭa siddhiḥ 
NK_230.3–230.4	 nanu sphoṭaḥ api na anabhivyaktaḥ artham pratipādayati sarvadā artha upalabdhi prasaṅgāt abhivyaktiḥ ca na tasya varṇebhyaḥ sambhavati uktena nyāyena teṣām ekaikaśas kamuditānām api asāmarthyāt tasmāt sphoṭāt api durlabhā artha pratītiḥ atra vadanti prayatna bheda anupātinaḥ vāyavīyā dhvanayaḥ pratyekam eva tad tad varṇa ātmaka tayā sphoṭam asphuṭam abhivyañjayantaḥ pūrva pūrva viṣaya saṃskāra sāci vī alābha āt antye sphoṭam ābhāsayanti tathā ca ante pratyastamita nikhilava varṇa vibhāga ullekham akramam anavayavam ekam vispaṣṭam artha tattvam anubhūyate yadi hi varṇāḥ eva padam na tad ekabuddhi nirgrāhyam iti anālambanā buddhiḥ paryavasyati aśabdāt artham pratipadyāmahe a iti ca vyapadeśaḥ na ghaṭate tasmāt varṇa vyatriktaḥ kaḥ api sambhavati ekaḥ yasmāt arthaḥ sphuṭībhavati iti 
NK_230.5	 evam prāpte abhidhīyate guṇa ratna ābharaṇaḥ kāyastha kula tilakaḥ pāṇḍhu dāsaḥ ityādiṣu padesu uccārya maṇeṣu krama bhāvinaḥ varṇāḥ param pratīyante na tu ante varṇa vyatiriktasya kasyacid arthasya saṃvedanam asti yadi hi tasya pūrvam varṇa ātmaka tayā saṃviditasya ante svarūpa saṃvedanam pūrva jñānasya mithyātvam avasīyate rajata jñānasya iva śuktikā saṃvitau na ca evam pratipattiḥ asti anāyam varṇaḥ kim tu sphoṭaḥa iti yā ca iyam ekārtha avamarśinī buddhiḥ sā api na artha antaram avabhāsayati kintu vana pratyaya vat varṇa samudāya mātram ālambate aśabdāt arthama pratipadyāmahe a iti varṇa samudāyam eva uorīkṛtya lokaḥ prayuṅkte 
NK_230.6	 na ca pratyakṣeṇa apratīyamānaḥ pramāṇa antarataḥ śakyaḥ nirūpayitum upāya abhāvāt artha prati iti anyathā anupapattiḥ tad upāyaḥ iti ced kim apratīyamānaḥ sphoṭaḥ artha adhigama hetuḥ samarthitaḥ bhavadbhiḥ pratīyamānaḥ vā apratīyamānasya hetu tve sarvadā artha pratīti prasaṅgaḥ pratītiḥ ca tasya na asti iti uktam artha pratyayaḥ api ca varṇānām eva tad bhāva bhāvitām anugacchati tena eṣām eva varam vyutpatti anusāreṇa artha pratipādane kaścid upāya āśrīyatām na punar apratīyamānasya gagana kusumasya iva kalpanā yuktāḥ na ca idam vā ayam varṇānām pratipādaka tve krama bhede karttṛ bhede vyavadhāne ca pratīti prasaṅgaḥ iti na hi viparīta kramāḥ karttṛ bheda anupātinaḥ deśa kāla vyavahitāḥ tad artha dhiyaḥ kāraṇam kārya unneyāḥ hi śaktayaḥ bhāvānābh yathā tebhyaḥ kāryam dṛśyate tathā eva teṣām śaktayaḥ kalpyante yathā upadiśanti santaḥ 
NK_230.7–230.8	 yāvantaḥ yādṛśāḥ ye ca yad artha pratipādane varṇāḥ prajñāta sāmarthyāḥ te tathā eva avabodhakāḥ iti atas eva nadī dīna ityādiṣu artha bhedaḥ krama bhedāt varṇeṣu kramaḥ na asti sa katham eṣām aṅgam syāt iti ced na teṣām utpatti bhājām avyāpya vṛttīnām deśa kṛtasya kāla kṛtasya ca paurvāparyasya sambhavāt yat ca idam uktam pratyekaśaḥ samuditānām ca na sāmarthyam iti tat api na parasya matam ālocitam yadi api varṇāḥ anavasthāyinaḥ tathā api tad viṣayāḥ krama bhāvinaḥ saṃskārāḥ saṃbhūya padārtha dhiyamātanvate yat vā pūrva varṇa saṃskāra maraṇayoḥ anyatara apekṣaḥ antyaḥ varṇaḥ pratyāyakaḥ yathā ca aneka saṃskārāḥ saṃbhūya smaraṇam janayanti tathā upapāditam dvi tve atha manyase varṇa viṣayāt saṃskāra ādarśa pratītiḥ ayuktāḥ saṃskārāḥ hi yad viṣaya upalambha sambhāvita janmānaḥ tad viṣayām eva smṛtim ādhātum ūśate na kārya antaram yathā āha maṇḍanaḥ sphoṭa siddhau 
NK_230.9–230.12	 saṃskārāḥ khalu yat vastu rūpa prakhyā vibhāvitāḥ phalam tatra eva janayanti atas arthe dhīḥ na kalpyate iti tat api asamīcīnam yatas padārtha prati iti anuguṇa tayā pratyekam anubhavaiḥ ādhīyamānā varṇa viṣayāḥ saṃskārāḥ smṛti hetu saṃskāra vilakṣaṇa śaktayaḥ eva ādhīyante tathābhūtānām eva teṣām kāryeṇa adhigamāt santu vā bhāvanā rūpāḥ saṃskārāḥ tathā api teṣām artha pratipādana sāmarthyam upapadyate tad bhāva bhāvi tvāt yaḥ hi sphoṭam kalpayati tena sphoṭasya artha pratyāyana śaktiḥ api kalpanīyā iti kalpanā gauravam ubhaya siddhasya saṃskārasya sāmartha mātra kalpanāyām lāghavam asti iti etat eva kalpayitum ucitam yathā uktam nyāya vādibhiḥ yadi api smṛti hetu tvam saṃskārasya vyavasthitam kārya antare api sāmarthyam na tasya pratihanyate iti tat evam varṇabhyaḥ eva saṃskāra dvāreṇa artha pratyaya sambhavāt ayuktā sphoṭa kalpanā iti 
NK_231.1–231.2	 prayatnena manaḥ cakṣuṣi sthāpayitvā apūrvam artham didṛkṣamāṇasya vidyut sampāta darśana vat ādara pratyayaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma manadoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskāra atiśayaḥ jāyate yathā devahrade rājata sauvarṇa padma darśanāt iti ādara pratyaya jam saṃskāram darśayati prayatnena ityādinā ādaraḥ prayatna atiśayaḥ tasmāt āūrvam artham draṣṭum icchataḥ yad vidyut sampāta darśana vartha darśanam tad ādara pratyayaḥ tam eva apekṣamāṇāt ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt saṃskāra atiśayaḥ jāyate cira kāla atikrame api tasya anucchedāt atra udāharaṇam yathā devahrade rājata sauvarṇa padma darśanāt iti devahrade caitra māsasya citrā nakṣatra saṃyuktāyām paurṇasyām ardharātre rājatāni sauvarṇāni ca padmāni dṛśyante iti vārtām avagamya tasyām tithau didṛkṣayā militānām sannidhīyamāne ardharātre prayatna atiśayāt cakṣuṣi manaḥ sthāpayitvā sthitānām utthiteṣu padmeṣu kṣaṇa mātra darśanāt ādara pratyayāt saṃskāra atiśayaḥ kāla antare api sphuṭatara smṛti hetuḥ upajāyate 
NK_232.1	 sthiti sthāpakaḥ tu sparśa vat dravyeṣu vartamānaḥ ghana avayava sanniveśa viśiṣṭeṣu kāla antara avasthāyiṣu sva āśrayam anyathā akṛtam yathā avasthitam sthāpayati sthāvara jaṅgama vikāreṣu dhanuḥ śākhā śṛṅga danta sthi sūtra vastra ādiṣu bhugna saṃvartiteṣu sthiti sthāpakasya kāryam saṃlakṣyate nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ asya api guru tva vat 
NK_232.2^1	 sthita sthāpakam kathayati sthita sthāpakaḥ tu iti asparśa vat dravvya vṛtteḥ bhāvanā ākhyāt saṃskārāt sparśavat dravya vṛtti tvena sthita sthāpakasya viśeṣam ākhyātum tuśabdaḥ ghanāḥ nibiḍāḥ ye avayava sanniveśāḥ taiḥ viśiṣṭeṣu sparśavatsu dravyeṣu vartamānaḥ sthita sthāpakaḥ sva āśrayam anyathākṛtam avanāmitam yathāvat sthāpayati pūrvavat ṛjūkaroti ye pratyakṣayaḥ anupalambhāt sthiti sthāpakasya abhāvam icchanti tān prati tasya kāryeṇa sadbhāvam darśayan= āha sthāvara jaṅgama vikāreṣu iti 
NK_232.2^2	 bhugnāḥ kubjīkṛtāḥ saṃvirtatāḥ pūrva avasthām prāpitāḥ bhugnāḥ ca te saṃvartitāḥ ca iti bhugna saṃvirtatāḥ teṣu sthiti sthāpakasya kāryam lakṣyate kim uktam syāt dhanuḥ śākhā ādiṣu avana amita vimukteṣu yat pūrva avasthā prāpti hetoḥ ādya asya karmaṇaḥ eka artha samavetam asamavāyi kāraṇam sa sthiti sthāpakaḥ saṃskāraḥ anyasya asambhāvāt anye tu bhugna saṃvartiteṣu iti sūkṣma stra ādiṣu iti asya idam viśeṣaṇam iti manyamānāḥ bhugnāni yāni sūtra ādīni saṃvartitāni teṣu iti vyācakṣate tasya nitya anitya tva niṣpattayaḥ guru tva vat yathā guru tvam paramāṇuṣu nityam kāryeṣu anityam kāraṇa guṇa pūrvakam ca tathā sthiti sthāpakaḥ api iti arthaḥ 
NK_233.1–233.3	 dharmaḥ puruṣa guṇaḥ kartuḥ priya hita mokṣa hetuḥ atīndriyaḥ antya sukha saṃvijñāna virodhī puruṣa antaḥkaraṇa saṃyoga viśuddha abhisamdhi jaḥ varṇa āśramiṇām pratiniyata sādhana nimittaḥ tasya tu sādhanāni śruti smṛti vihitāni varṇa āśramiṇām sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvena avasthita anidravya guṇa karmāṇi dharmaḥ puruṣa guṇaḥ yaḥ dharmaḥ sa puruṣasya guṇaḥ na karma sāmarthyam iti arthaḥ kartuḥ priya hita mokṣa hetuḥ kartuḥ priyam sukham hitam sukha sādhanam mokṣaḥ navānām ātma viśesa guṇānām atyanta ucchedḥ teṣām hetuḥ karttuḥ priya ādīnām eva yaḥ hetuḥ sa dharmaḥ iti vyākhyyam na tu karttuḥ eva yaḥ priya ādi hetuḥ sa dharmaḥ iti vyākhyā putreṇa kṛtasya śrāddha asya pitṛ gāmi tṛpti phala śravaṇāt vṛṣṭi kāmena kārīryām kṛtāyām tad anyasya api samīpa deśa vartinaḥ vṛṣṭi phala sambandha darśanāt 
NK_233.4–233.6	 svarga kāmaḥ yajeta ityādi vākye yāgena svargam kuryāt iti karmaṇaḥ śroyaḥ sādhana tvam śrūyate yaḥ ca niḥśrayasena puruṣam saṃyunakti sa dharmaḥ sasmāt yāga ādikam eva dharmaḥ na puruṣa guṇaḥ tathā hi yaḥ yāgam anutiṣṭhati tam dhārmikam iti ācakṣate etat ayuktam kṣaṇikasya karmaṇaḥ kāla antara bhāvi phala sādhanatva asambandhāt atha ucyate kṣaṇikam karma kāla anta bhāvi ca svargphalam vinaṣṭāt ca kāraṇāt kāryasya anutpattiḥ śrutam ca yāga ādeḥ kāraṇa tvam tat etat anyathā anupapattyā pala utpatti anuguṇam kim api kalā antara avasthāyi karma sāmarthyam kalpyate yad dvāreṇa karmaṇām śrutā phala sādhana tā nirvahati tat ca pramāṇa antara agocara tvāt apūrvam iti vyapadiśyate yathā uktam phalāya vihitam karma kṣaṇikam cira bhāvine tad siddhiḥ na anyathā iti etat apūrvam api karpyate 
NK_233.7	 atra ucyate na karma sāmarthyam kṣaṇike karmaṇi samavaiti śaktimati vinaṣṭe nirāśrayasya sāmarthyasya avasthāna asaṃbhavāt svarga ādikam ca phalam tadānīm anāgatam eva na śakteḥ āśrayaḥ bhavitum arhati yadi tu anuṣṭhāna anantaram eva svargaḥ bhavati apūrva kalpanā vaiyarthyam tad upabhogaḥ ca durnivāraḥ viśiṣṭa śarīra indriya ādi virahāt ananubhavaḥ ca iti tarhi aham tadānīm anupajātaḥ eva svargasya upabogyakasya svabhāva tvāt anupabhogyam api sukha svarūpam asti iti adṛṣṭa kalpanā iyam tasmāt na phala āśrayam apūrvam na ca ākāśa ādi samavetāt apūrvāt ātma gāmi phala sambhavaḥ vastu bhūtam ca kāryam anādhāram na upapadyate tasmāt ātma samavetasya eva tasya utpattiḥ abhyanujñeyāḥ tathā sati na tad karma samarthyam syāt anya sāmarthyasya anyatra asamavāyāt atha anyasya api anya samavetā śaktiḥ iṣyate tasyāḥ kārya anumeya tvāt iti ca iti 
NK_233.8–233.10^1	 atha uktam śaktiḥ kārya anumeyāḥ hi yat gatā eva upalabhyate tad gata eva abhyuetavyā sva āśrayāni āśrayā api ca iti tat ayuktam vinaṣṭe śaktimati tad nirapekṣasya śakti mātrasya kārya janaka tva anupalambha āde etena etat api pratyuktam yat uktam maṇḍanena vidhi vid eke tad ā āhta tvāt tasya śaktiḥ iti yāgena āhita tvāt arūrvam yāgasya kāryam syāt na tu śaktiḥ apūrva upakṛtāt karmaṇaḥ phala anutpatteḥ tasmāt cita nivṛtte karmaṇi deśa kāla avasthā ādi sahakāriṇaḥ apūrvāt eva phalasya utpattiḥ iti apūrvam eva śreyaḥ sādhanam karaṇa tva śrutiḥ tu yāga ādara pūtva janana dvāreṇa na sākṣāt iti pramāṇa anurodhāt āśrayaṇīyam tathā sati yuktam dharmaḥ puruṣa guṇaḥ iti 
NK_233.10^2	 yaḥ api yāga ādau dharma vyapadeśaḥ saḥ api apūrva sādhana tayā prīti sādhanaḥ iva svarga śabda prayogaḥ svarga sādhane hi caḥ ditasya jyotiṣṭomasya nirantaram prīti sādhana tayā artha vādena stuteḥ candana ādau ca prīti yoge sati prayogāt tad abhāve ca aprayogāt prīti nibandhanaḥ svarga śabdaḥ tasya yathālakṣaṇayā prīti sādhane prayogaḥ prīti mātra abhidhāne api tasmāt prīti sādhana pratīti upapatteḥ ubhaya abhidhāna śakti kalpanā vaiyarthyāt evam dharma śabdasya api lakṣaṇayā tad sādhane prayotaḥ eka abhidhānāt eva ubhaya pratīti siddheḥ ubhaya abhidhāna śakti kalpanā anavakāśāt iti tārkikāṇām prakriyā 
NK_233.11	 atīndriyaḥ kenacid indiḥ iyeṇa ayogibhiḥ na gṛhyate iti atīndriyaḥ dharmaḥ antya sukha saṃvijñāna virodhī dharmaḥ tāvat kārya tvāt avaśyam vināśī na ca nirhetukaḥ vināśaḥ kasyacid vidyate anyatas tatas vināśe ca asya niyamena phala utpatti kālam yāvat avasthānam na syāt phalam ca dharmasya kasyacid aneka saṃvatsara sahatra upabhogyam tasya yadi prathama upabhogāt eva nāśaḥ kāla antare phala anutpādaḥ naca elasya nirbhāgasya bhāgaśas nāśaḥ sambhāvyate tasmāt antyasya eva sukhasya samyak vijñānena dharmaḥ vināśyate ye tu nityam dharmām āhuḥ teṣām prāyaṇa anupapattiḥ dharma adharma kṣaya abhāvāt puruṣa antar karaṇa saṃyogaḥ ātma viśeṣa guṇa tvāt sukha ādi vat viśuddhaḥ abhisandhinaḥ viśuddhaḥ abhisamdhiḥ dambha ādi rahitaḥ saṃkalpa viśeṣaḥ tasmāt dharmaḥ jāyate varṇa āśramiṇām pratiniyata sādhana nimittaḥ varṇāḥ brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viś śūdrāḥ āśramiṇaḥ brahmacāri gṛhastha vān aprasthatayaḥ teṣām dharmaḥ prativarṇām pratyāśramam ca adhikṛtya vihitaiḥ sādhanaiḥ janyate iti arthaḥ 
NK_234.1–234.3	 tatra sāmānyāni dharme śradhā ahiṃsā bhūta hita tvam satya vacanm asteyam brahmacaryam anupadhā krodha varjanam abhiṣecanam śuci dravya sevanam viśiṣṭa detā bhakti tarupavāsaḥ apramādaḥ ca brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām sāmānyāni dharma sādhanāni ijyā adhyayana dānāni brāhmaṇasya viśiṣṭāni pratigraha adhyāpana yājanāni sva varṇa vihitāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ 
NK_234.4–234.7	 kṣatriyasya samyak prajāpāla nam asādhu nigrahaḥ yuddheṣu anivarttanam svakīyāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ vaiśyasya kraya vikraya kṛṣi paśu pālanāni svakīyāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ śūdrasya pūrva varṇa pāratantryam amantrikāḥ ca kriyāḥ āśramiṇām tu brahmacāriṇaḥ guru kula nivāsinaḥ sva śāstra vihitāni guru śuśrūṣā agni indhana bhaikṣya ācaraṇāni madhimāṃdivāsvapna añjana abhyañjana ādi varjanam ca 
NK_234.8^1	 atīndriyasya dharmasya sādhanāni kutā prayetavyāni tatra āha tasya tu iti viśiṣṭena anuṣṭhānena ācārya mukhāt śrūyataḥ eva na likhitvā gṛhyate iti śrutiḥ vedaḥ smṛtiḥ manu ādi vākyam kābhyām vihitāni pratipāditāni sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvena avasthitāni dravya gunā karmāṇi sāmānyani dharma sādhanāni tatra sarveṣām varṇānām āśramiṇām ca sāmānya rūpa tayā dharma sādhanāni kathyante dharme śraddhā dharme manaḥ prasādaḥ ahiṃsā bhūtānām anabhidroha saṃkalpaḥ pratiṣiddhasya abhidrohasya nivṛtteradharmaḥ na bhavati na dharmaḥ jāyate anabhidroha saṃkalpasya vihita tvāt syāt eva dharma sādhanam bhūta hitam bhūtānām anugrahaḥ satya vacanam yathārtha vacanam asteyam aśāstra pūrvakam para sva grahaṇam mayā na kartavyam iti saṃkalpaḥ na tu para sva ādāna nivṛtti mātram abhāva rūpam brahmacaryam strī seva parivarjanam 
NK_234.8^2	 etat api saṃkalpa rūpam anupadhā bhāve viśuddhiḥ viśuddhena abhiprāyeṇa kṛtānām karmaṇām dharma sādhana tvāt krodha varjanam krodha parityāgaḥ saḥ api saṃkalpa ātmakaḥ eva abhiṣecanam snānam śuci dravya sevanam śucīnām tila ādi dravyāṇām kvacid parvaṇi niyamena sevanam dharma sādhanam viśiṣṭa devatā bhaktiḥ trayī saṃmatāyām devatāyām bhaktiḥ iti arthaḥ upavāsaḥ ekādaśyāt aubhojana nivṛtti saṃkalpaḥ apramādaḥ nitya naimittikānām karmaṇām avaśyambhāvena karaṇam etāni sarveṣām eva samānāni dharma sādhanāni brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām sāmānyāni dharma sādhanāni ijyā adhyayana dānāni ijyā yāga homa anuṣṭhānam adhyayanam veda pāṭhaḥ dānam sva dravyasya para svatāpatti phalaḥ saṃkalpa viśeṣaḥ śūdrasya api dānam asti eva tena yajña ādiṣu yat dānam tad abhiprāyeṇa idam traivarṇikānām viśiṣṭam dharma sādhana mukram 
NK_234.9	 brāhmaṇasya viśiṣṭāni asādhāraṇāni dharma sādhanāni pratipādayati pratigraha adhyāpana yājanāni pratigrahaḥ viśiṣṭāt dravya grahaṇam adhyāpanam tu prasiddham eva yājanam ārtvijyam etāni brāhmaṇasya dharma sādhanāni tasya amībhiḥ eva upāyaiḥ arjitānām dravyāṇām dharma adhikārāt sva varṇa vihitāḥ ca aṣṭacatvāriṃśat saṃskārāḥ vaidika karma aniṣṭhāna yogya tā āpādana dvāreṇa brāhmaṇasya dharma sādhanam 
NK_234.10–234.12	 kṣatriyasya viśiṣṭāni dharma sāmanāni samyak prajā pālanam nyāya vṛttīnām prajānām parirakṣaṇam asādhu nigrahaḥ duṣṭānām yathāśāstram śāsanam yuddheṣu anivarttanam yuddheṣu vijaya avadhiḥ prāṇauvadhiḥ vā āyudha vyāpāraḥ svakīyāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ vaiśyasya kraya vikraya kṛṣi paśu pālanāni mūlyam dattvā parasmāt dravya grahaṇam krayaḥ mūlyam ādāya parasya sva dravya dānam vikrayaḥ  kṛṣiḥ parikarmitāyām bhūmau bījasya vapanam ropaṇam ca paśepa alanam gojāvika ādi paripakṣaṇam etāni vaiśyasya dharma sādhanāni tasya amībhiḥ eva upāyaiḥ arjitānām dhanānām dharma aṅga tvāt śūdrasya pūrveṣu varṇeṣu pāratantryam amantrikāḥ ca kriyā dharma sādhanam 
NK_235.1–235.2	 vidyā vrata snātaksya kṛta vārasya gṛhasthasya śālīnayāya avara vṛtti upārjitaiḥ arthaiḥ bhūta manuṣya deva pitṛ brahma ākhyānām pañcānām mahā yajñānām sāyam prātar anuṣṭhānam eka agni vidhānena pākayajña saṃsthānām ca nityānām śaktau vidyamānāya anagni ādheya ādīnām ca haviḥ yajña saṃsthānām agniṣṭoma ādīnām soma yajña saṃsthānām tu antareṣu brahmacaryam apatya utpādanam ca brahmacāriṇaḥ gṛhasthasya vā vana vāsaḥ valkala ajina keśa śmaśru nakha roma dhāraṇam vanya huta atithi śeṣa bhojanāni vana sthasya 
NK_235.3	 āśramiṇām tu dharma sādhanam ucyate brahmacāriṇaḥ guru kula nivāsinaḥ iti upanīya yaḥ śiṣyam sāṅgam saram adhyāpayati sa guruḥ tasya kule gṛhe vasana śīlasya brahmacāriṇaḥ sva śāstra vihitāni brahmacāriṇam adhikṛtya śāstreṇa vihitāni vihitāni guru śuśrūṣā agni indhana bhaikṣya ācaraṇāni madhu māṃsa divāsvapna abhyañjana añjana varjanam ca vrata rūpa dharma sādhanam guru śuśrūṣā guroḥ paricaryā guru śuśrūṣā ca agniḥ ca indhanam ca bhaikṣyam ca teṣām ācaraṇāni guru śuśrū bhaikṣyayoḥ karaṇam eva caraṇam agneḥ ācaraṇam pratyaham agnau homaḥ indhanasya ācaraṇam agni artham vanāt indhanasya āharaṇam iti vivekaḥ 
NK_235.4^1	 gṛhasthasya dharma sādanam kathayati vidyā vrata snātakasya iti yaḥ veda adhyayana artham gṛhītam vratam adhīte vede visarjitavān sa vidyā vrata snātakaḥ tasya kṛta dārasya kṛta patnī parigrahasya gṛhasthasya śalīnayāyāvara vṛtti upārjitaiḥ arthaiḥ bhūta manuṣya deva pitṛ brahma ākhyānām pañcānām mahā yajñānām sāyam prātar anuṣṭhānam yāvatā dhānyena kuśūla mātram kumbhī pātram vā pripūryate tri aham eka aham vā vartanam bhavati tāvat mātrasya pareṇa svayam ānīyamānasya śraddhayā dīyamānasya yaḥ parigrahaḥ sā śālīnā vṛttiḥ parasmāt apratigṛhṇataḥ cakram ādāya yat pratyaṅganam bhikṣā aṭanam sā yāyāvara vṛttiḥ tābhyām upārjitaiḥ artheḥ pañcānām mahā yajñānām sāyam prātar aparāhṇe ca anuṣṭhānam gṛhasthasya dharma sādhanam bhūtebhyaḥ bali pradāna bhūta yajñaḥ atithi pūjanam manuṣya yajñaḥ homaḥ deva yajñāḥ śrāddham pitṛ yajñaḥ brahma yajñe veda pāṭhaḥ 
NK_235.4^2	 eka agni vidhānena pākayajña saṃsthānām nityānām śaktau vidyamānāyām anuṣṭhānam anuṣṭhānam eka agniḥ iti aupāsanikaḥ tasya vidhānam vivāha kāle parigrahaḥ tena pākayajña saṃsthānām pākayajña viśeṣāṇām aṣṭakā pārvaṇī caitrya āśvayujyā ādīnām nityānām avaśya karaṇīyānām sati sāmarthye anuṣṭhānam agni ādheya ādīnām haviḥ yajña saṃsthānām agniṣṭoma ādīnām soma yajña saṃsthānām ca anuṣṭhānam dharma sādhanam agni ādheya śabdena agni ādhānasya abhidhānam yat brāhmaṇena vasante kriyate haviḥ yajña saṃsthāḥ haviḥ yajña viśeṣāḥ darśa paurṇamāsa cāturmāsya agrahāyaṇa ādikāḥ iṣṭayaḥ kathyante agniṣṭoma ādi iti agniṣṭoma ukthi a ṣoḍaśī ivā japeya atirātra āptoḥ yāmāḥ sapta soma yajña viśeṣāḥ soma yajña saṃsthāḥ ucyante ṛtu antarā iti ṛtu kālāt anya kāleṣu brahmacarya vrata rūpeṇa strī sevā parivarjanam dharma sādhanam apatya utpādanam api dharma sādhanam putreṇa lokān jayati iti śruteḥ 
NK_235.5	 vana sthasya dharma sādhanam kathayati brahmacāriṇaḥ gṛhasthasya vā iti yat ahar eva asya śraddhā abhavati tat ahar eva ayam pravrajet iti śravaṇāt sati śraddhā upanaye brahmacātiṇaḥ vana vāsaḥ bhavati gṛhasthasya vā tasya vānaprastha vratam ācarataḥ valkala ajina keśa śmaśru nakha roma dhāraṇam vanyasya phala mūlasya bhojanam huta śeṣa bhojanam atithi śeṣa bhojanam ca dharma sādhanam yaḥ prājāpatyām iṣṭim nirūpa sarva svam dakṣiṇām dattvā ātmani agnim samādhāya putre bhāryām nikṣipya pravrajitaḥ na tasya homaḥ na api atithi parigrahaḥ yaḥ tu saha patnyā saha eva agninā vanam prasthitaḥ tasya huta śeṣa bhojanam atithi ceṣa bhojanam ca 
NK_236.1–236.3^1	 trayāṇām anyatamasya śraddhāvataḥ sarva bhūtebhyaḥ nityam abhayam dattvā saṃtyasya svāni karmāṇi yama nimeṣu apramattasya ṣaṭpadārtha prasaṃkhyānāt yoga prasādhanam pravrajitasya iti dṛṣṭam prayojanam anuddiśya etāni sādhanāni bhāva prasādam ca apekṣyātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt hārma utpattiḥ iti yati dharmam kathayati trayāṇām iti yati āśrama parigrahe api niyamaḥ na asti śraddhā upagame sati brahmacārī eva atiḥ bhavati gṛhasthaḥ vā bhavati vānaprasthaḥ vā iti anena abhiprāyeṇa uktam trayāṇām anyatam asya iti śraddhāvataḥ citta prasādavataḥ sarva bhūtebhyaḥ nityam abhayam dattvā bhūtāni mayā na jātu hiṃsitavyāni iti adro saṅkalpam gṛhītvā svāni karmāṇi kāmyāni saṃnyasya parityajya yama niyameṣu apramattasya ahiṃsā asatya ādayaḥ yamāḥ yathā āha bhagavān patañjaliḥ ahiṃkāsatyāsteya brahmacarya aparigrahāḥ yamāḥ iti tapaḥ śauca ādayaḥ tu niyamāḥ 
NK_236.3^2	 yathā āha saḥ eva bhagavān śauca santoṣa tapaḥ svādhyāya īśvara praṇidhānāni niyamāḥ iti nyāya bhāṣya kāraḥ tu pratyāśramam viśiṣṭam dharma sādhana niyamam āha teṣu apramattasya tānanatiktam atas ṣaṣ padārtha prasaṃkhyānāt ṣaṇṇām padārthānām tattva jñānāt yogasya ātma jñāt pādana samarthasya samādhi viśeṣasya prasādhanam utpādanam pravrajitasya dharma sādhanam yathā etāni dharmam sādhayanti tathā kathayati dṛṣṭam ca iti lābha pūjā ādi prayojanam anuddiśya anabhindhāya yadā etāni sādhanāni kriyante tadā etāni sādhanāni bhāva prasādam ca abhiprāya viśuddhim ca apekṣyātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt dharma utpattiḥ iti 
NK_236.4	 pratyaham duḥkhaiḥ abhihanyamānasya tattvataḥ vijñāteṣu uḥkha eka nidāneṣu viṣayeṣu viraktasya ātyantikam duḥkha viyogam icchataḥ ātma khyātiḥ aviplavāḥ hāna upāyaḥ atasyāḥ ca samādhi viśeṣaḥ nibandhanam a iti śrutavataḥ saṃnyasya sarva kāmya karmāṇi samādhim anutiṣṭhāsataḥ tad pratyanīka bhūyiṣṭham grāmam parityajya vanam āśritasya yama niyamābhyām kṛtātma saṃskātasya samādhi abhyāsāt nivarttakaḥ dharmaḥ jāyate tasmāt asya prakṛṣṭaḥ samādhiḥ tatas anyaḥ prakṛṣṭataraḥ dharmaḥ tasmāt api anyaḥ prakṛṣṭatamaḥ samādhiḥ iti anena krameṇa antye janmani sa tādṛśaḥ samādhi viśeṣaḥ pariṇamati yaḥ dvandvena api abhibhavitum na śakyate dṛṣṭaḥ hi kiñcid abhimatam viṣayam ādareṇa anucintayataḥ tad ekāgrībhūta cittasya sannihiteṣu prabaleṣu api viṣayeṣu asaṃbodhaḥ yathā iṣukāraḥ iṣaḥ labdha lakṣyaḥ abhyāse gacchantam api rājānam na buddhyate tathā ca bhagavān patañjaliḥ abhyāsa vairāgyābhyām tad nirodhaḥ iti evam pariṇate samādhau= ātma svarūpa sākṣāt kāri vijñānam udeti yathā āhuḥ kāpilāḥ 
NK_236.5–236.6	 evam tattva abhyāsāt na atī na me na aham iti apariśeṣam aviparyayāt viśuddham kevalam utpadyate jñānam iti atas ātma jñāna artham yatinā yoga sādhanam anuṣṭhīyate jñānam jñeya abhivyakti mātra phalam śrauta ātma jñānena api ātma svarūpam prāpyate kim asya dhyāna abhyāsāt pratyakṣīkaraṇena iti ced na parokṣasya pratyakṣa jñāna bādhane sāmarthayā abhāvāt svarūpataḥ tāvat ātmā na karttā na bhoktā kintu udāsīnaḥ eva tatra deha indriya sambandha upādhikṛtaḥ aham mama iti kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva pratyayaḥ mithyā atasmin= tat iti bhāvāt etad kṛtaḥ ca anukūleṣu rāgaḥ pratikūleṣu dveṣaḥ tābhyām pravṛtti nivṛttī tatas dharma adharme tatas ca saṃsāraḥ yotha uktam saugataiḥ 
NK_236.7–236.8	 ātmani sati para saṃjñā sva para vibhāgāt parigraha dveṣau anayoḥ saṃpratibaddhāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ prajāyante anādi vāsanā vāsitaḥ ati prabalaḥ nisarga siddhaḥ sarvaḥ sāṃvyavahārikaḥ pratyakṣeṇa eṣa pratyayaḥ śrautam ātma tattva jñānam kṣaṇikam anupalabdha saṃvādam parokṣam ca na ca dṛḍhataraḥ pratyakṣa avabhāsaḥ parokṣa avabhāsena śakyate niṣeddhum na hi śatacaḥ api pramāṇa antara avagate guḍasya mādhuryet uṣṭa indriya jaḥ tikta pratibhāsaḥ tad kṛtaḥ ca duḥkhāa gamaḥ nivartate tasmāt pratyakṣa jñāna artham samādhiḥ upāsitavyaḥ pracite samādhau tad sāmarthyāt karttṛ tva bhoktṛ tva pripanthini ātma tattve sphuṭībhūte samāne viṣaye vidyā vidyayoḥ virodhāt ahaṅkāram amakāra vāsana ucchede san= api prapañcaḥ na ātmānam spṛcati tathā ca kāpilaiḥ uktam 
NK_236.9–236.10	 tena nivṛtta prasavām artha vaśāt sapta rūpa vinivṛttau prakṛtim paśyati puruṣaḥ prekṣaka vat avasthitaḥ svasthaḥ tena tattva jñānena satā nivṛtta prasavām nivṛtta upabhoga jananasām athyā j jñāna dharma vairāgya aiśvarya adharma ajñāna avaitāgyān aiśvaryebhyaḥ sapta rūpebhyaḥ vinivṛttām prakṛtim puruṣaḥ prekṣaka vat udāsīnaḥ svasthaḥ rajaḥ tamaḥ vṛtti kaluṣa tayā buddhyā na sambhinnaḥ paśyati iti arthaḥ yadi api anādiḥ iyam moha vāsanā ādimān= ca tattva sākṣātkāraḥ tathā api anena sā niruddhyate tattva avagrahaḥ hi dhiyām paramam balam 
NK_237.1–237.2	 adharmaḥ api ātma guṇaḥ karttu ḥ ahita pratyavāya hetuḥ atīndriyaḥ antya duḥkha saṃvijñāna rodhī tasya tu sādhanāni śāstre pratiṣiddhāni dharma sādhana viparītāni hiṃsā anṛta steya ādīni vihita akaraṇam pramādaḥ ca etāni duṣṭa abhisandhem ca apekṣyātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt adharmasya utpattiḥ aviduṣaḥ rāga dveṣavataḥ pravarttakāt dharmāt prakṛṣṭāt su alpa adharma sahitāt brahma indra prajāpati pitṛ manuṣya lokeṣu āśaya anurūpaiḥ iṣṭa śarīra indriya viṣaya sukha ādibhiḥ yogaḥ bhavati tathā prakṛṣṭāt adharmāt su alpa dharma sahitāt preta tiryagyoni sthāneṣu aniṣṭa śarīra indriya viṣaya duḥkha ādibhiḥ yogaḥ bhavati evam pravṛtti lakṣaṇāt dharmāt adharma sahitāt deva manuṣya tiryak na arkeṣu punar punar saṃsāra prabandhaḥ bhavati 
NK_237.3	 adharmaḥ api ātma guṇaḥ na kevalam dharmaḥ adharma upya ātma guṇaḥ karttu ḥ ahita pratyavāya hetuḥ karttu ḥ ahitam duḥkha sādhanam pratyavāyaḥ duḥkham tayoḥ adharmaḥ hetuḥ atīndriyaḥ na kena api indriyeṇa gṛhyate iti arthaḥ antya duḥkha sṃvijñāna virodhī antyasya duḥkhasya samyak vijñānena vināśyate tasya sādhanāni śāstre pratiṣiddhāni dharma sādhana viparītāni hiṃsā anṛta steya ādīni hiṃsā para abhidrohaḥ anṛtam mithyā vacanam steyam aśāstra pūrvam para sva grahaṇam evamādīni dharma sādhana viparītāni śāstre pratiṣiddhāni yāni tāni adharma sādhanāni vihita akaraṇam pramādaḥ ca vihita ālaraṇam avaśya larta vyākaraṇam pramādaḥ abuddhi pūrvakaḥ atikramaḥ etat api dvayam adharma sādhanam yathā etebhyaḥ dharmasya utpatiḥ tat darśayati etāni ca duṣṭam ca abhisandhim apekṣya ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt adharma utpattiḥ iti yatra kāmanā pūrva kam adharma sādhana anuṣṭhānam tatra duṣṭaḥ abhisandhiḥ kāraṇam akāma kṛte tu pramādena asya hetu tvam 
NK_237.4^1	 evam adharmasya sādhanam abhidhāya saṃprati sādhyam kathayati aviduṣu ityādinā yaḥ karttā bhoktāsmi iti ātmānam abhimanyate paramārthataḥ duḥkha sādhanam ca bāhya ādhyātmika viṣayam sukha sādhanam iti abhimanyate saḥ avidvān sa ca sva upabhoga tṛṣṇā pariplutaḥ sukhsādhana tvena āropite viṣaye rajyate tad uparodhini ca dviṣṭaḥ bhavati tasya pravarttakāt dharmāt devaḥ vā syām gandharvaḥ vā syām iti punarbhava prārthanayā kṛtāt dharmāt prakṛṣṭāt phala atiśaya hetoḥ āśaya anurūpaiḥ karma anurūpaiḥ iṣṭa śarīra ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ bhavati brahma indra ādi sthāne api mātrayā duḥkha sambhedaḥ asti na ca adharmāt anyat duḥkha saṃvedaḥ asti 
NK_237.4^2	 na ca adharmāt anyat duḥkhasya karaṇam atas su alpa adharma sahitāt iti uktam yasya prakṛṣṭaḥ dharnaḥ tasya prakṛṣṭāni śarīra ādīni bhavanti yasya prakṛṣṭataraḥ dharmaḥ tasya prakṛṣṭatarāṇi bhavanti yasya prakṛṣṭatamaḥ dharmaḥ tasya prakṛṣṭatamāni iti pratipādayitum āśaya anurūpaiḥ iti uktam iṣṭa śabdaḥ pratyekam śarīra ādiṣu sambaddhyate dvandva anantaram prayogāt tathā prakṛṣṭāt adharmāt preta yonīnām tiryagyonīnām ca sthāneṣu aniṣṭaiḥ śarīra ādibhiḥ yogaḥ bhavati preta ādi sthāne api manāk sukham asti tat ca dharmasya kāryam atas svalpa dharma sahitāt iti uktam upasaṃharati evam iti 
NK_238.1	 jñāna pūrvakāt tu kṛtāt asaṃkalpita phalāt viśuddhe kule jātasya duḥkha vigama upāya jijñāsoḥ ācāryam upasaṅgamya utpanna ṣaṭpadārtha tattva jñānasya ajñāna nivṛtau viraktasya rāga dveṣa abhāvāt tad jayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ anutpattau pūrva sañcitayoḥ ca upabhogān nirodhe santoṣa sukham śarīta paricchedam ca utpādya rāga ādi nivṛttau nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ kevalaḥ dharmaḥ parama artha darśana jam sukham kṛtvā nivarttate tadā nirodhāt nirbījasya ātmanaḥ śarīra ādi nivṛttiḥ punar śarīra ādi anutpatau dagdha indhana anala vat upaśamaḥ mokṣaḥ iti 
NK_238.2^1	 evam dharmāt saṃsāram pratipādya apavargam pratipādayati jñāna pūrvakāt tu iti svarūpataḥ ca aham udāsīnaḥ bāhya ādhyātmikāḥ ca viṣayāḥ sarve eva ete duḥkha sādhanam iti yasya jñānam abhūt sa dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya sukha vitṛṣṇaḥ evam aham bhūyāsam iti me bhūyāsuḥ iti phala ākaṅkṣayā vinā nivṛtti sādhana tayā vihitam aparam ca avaśya karaṇīyam karma karoti tasmāt karmaṇaḥ jñāna pūrvakāt kṛtāt asya viśuddhe kule janma bhavati akulīnasya śraddhā na bhavati na ca aśraddadhānasya jijñāsā sampadyate na ca ajijñāsoḥ tas sva jñānam tad vikalasya ca na asti mokṣa prāptiḥ 
NK_238.2^2	 atas mokṣa anuguṇam asaṃkalpita phalam karma viśuddhe kule janma grāhayati viśuddhe kule jātasya pratyaham duḥkhaiḥ anuhanyamānasya duḥkha vigama upāye jijñāsā sampadyate kutonu khalu ayam mama duḥkha uparamaḥ syāt iti sa ca evam āvirbhūta jijñāse ācaryam upagacchati tasya ca ācārya upadeśāt ṣaṇṇām padārthānām śrautam tattva jñānam jāyate tadanu śravaṇa manana nididhya āsana ādi krameṇa pratyakṣam bhavati utpanna tattva jñānasya ajñānam sa vāsanam nivartate viparyaya jñānam tad nivṛttau viraktasya vicchinna rāga dveṣa saṃskārasya rādak veṣayoḥ abhāvāt tad jayoḥ dhama adharmayoḥ anutpādaḥ 
NK_238.2^3	 kleśa vāsana upanibaddhāḥ hi pravṛttayaḥ tuṣa avanaddhāḥ iva taṇḍulāḥ prarohanti kṣīṇeṣu kleśeṣu nistuṣāḥ iva taṇḍulāḥ kāryam na pratisanda dhate yathā āha bhagavān patñjaliḥ sati mūle tad vipākaḥ jāti āyuḥ bhogāḥ iti yathā āha bhagavān akṣapādaḥ na pravṛttiḥ pratisamdhānāya hīna kleśasya pūrva sañcitayoḥ ca dharma adharmayoḥ nirodhaḥ upabhogāt nivṛtti phala hetoḥ ca karma antarāt santoṣa sukham śarīra parikhedam ca utpādya rāga ādi nivṛttau nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ kevalaḥ dharmaḥ parama artha darśana jam sukham kṛtvā nivarttate 
NK_238.2^4	 nivarttyate saṃsāraḥ anayā iti nivṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ lakṣaṇam yasya asau nivṛtti lakṣaṇaḥ nivṛtti svabhāvaḥ dharma rāga ādi nivṛttau bhūtāyām kevalaḥ vyavasthitaḥ santoṣa sukham śarīra parikhedam ca utpādya parama artha darśana jam ātma darśana jam sukham karoti tat kṛtvā nivarttate āvamānika kārya vidhi tvāt tadā nirbījasya ātmanaḥ śarīra ādinittau punar śarīra ādi anutpattau dagdha indhana anala vat upaśamaḥ mokṣaḥ yadā parama artha darśanam kṛtvā nivṛttaḥ dharmaḥ tadā nirbījasya ātmanaḥ śarīra ādi bīja dharma adharma rahirasya ātmanaḥ utpannānām śarīra ādīnām karma kṣayāt nivṛttau bhūtāyām anāgatānām kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpattau yathā dagdha indhanasya analasya upaśamaḥ punar anutpādaḥ evam punar śarīrānutpādaḥ mokṣaḥ 
NK_239.1	 idam nirūpyate kim jñāna mātrāt muktiḥ uta jñāna karma samuccayāt jñāna karma samuccayāt iti vadāmaḥ nivṛtta itara abhilāṣasya kāmya karmabhyaḥ nivṛttasya api nitya naimittika karma adhikāraḥ na nivarttate tāni hi upanītam grāhmaṇa mātram adhikṛtya vihitāni mumukṣuḥ api brāhmaṇaḥ eva jāteḥ anucchedāt sa yadi adhikāri tve satya vaśya karaṇīyāni atikramet pratyavāyaḥ asya pratyaham upacīyeta tad upacayāt ca baddhaḥ na mucyate yathā uktam 
NK_239.2–239.5	 yāni kāmyāni karmāṇi pratiṣiddhāni yāni api tāni bandhanti akurvantam nitya naimittikāni api iti vihita akaraṇam abhāvaḥ na na ca abhāvasya bhāva hetu tvam asti atas na asmāt pratyavāya utpattiḥ iti ced na vihita akataṇe anya karaṇāt pratyavāyasya sambhavāt abhāvasya hi svātavtryeṇa hetu tvam na iṣyate na tu bhāva upasarjana tayā na ca śarīrī sandhi ādi kāle kāyena vācā manasā vā kiñjit na karoti śarīra dhāraṇa ādīnām api karaṇāt yathā uktam karmaṇām prāc abhāvaḥ yaḥ vihita akaraṇa ādiṣu na ca anartha kara tvena vastu tvāt na apanīyate sva kāle yat akurvaḥ tat karoti anyat acetanaḥ pratyavāyaḥ asya tena eva na abhāvena sa janyate iti 
NK_239.6^1	 abhāvena kevalena na asau janyate iti arthaḥ pratiṣiddha ācaraṇāt pratyavāyaḥ śarīra dhāraṇa ādikam ca na pratiṣiddham tat kurvan= api yadi sandhyāyām yogam abhyasyati kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced tat na tad kāle vihitasya avaśya vaśya kartavyatā vidheḥ arthāt kevalasya śarīra dhāraṇa ādeḥ karaṇam pratiṣiddham iti tat ācarataḥ bhavati eva pratiṣiddha ācaraṇa nimittaḥ pratyavāyaḥ atha ucyate dīrgha kāla ādara nairantarya sevita bhāvanā hita viśada bhāvam ātma jñānam eva rāga dveṣau moham ca sa mūla kāṣam kaṣat vihita akaraṇa nimittam pratyavāyam api kaṣati iti tat ayuktam 
NK_239.6^2–239.7	 yatra hi abhyāsaḥ prasīdati tatra tattva grahaḥ jātaḥ saṃśaya viparyayau vyudasyati na tu asya vastu antara nirvahaṇe sāmarthyam dṛṣṭa pūrvam yadi punar ātma jñānam karmāṇi niruṇaddhi upāruḍha phala bhogam api karma nirundhyāt tatas su dūram gatā jīvanmuktiḥ tattva darśana anantaram eva vilīna akhila karmaṇaḥ dehapātāt asti ca ayam parama artha dṛṣṭi niruddha akhila avidyaḥ api citralikhitam iva ābhāsa mātreṇa sarvam jagat paśyan= ekatra api anārūḍha abhiniveśaḥ prārabdha phalam karma viśeṣam upabhuñjānaḥ kulāla vyāpāra vigame cakra bhrānti vat saṃskāra vaśāt anuvarttamānasya dehapātam udīkṣamāṇaḥ tathā ca śrutiḥ jīvan= eva hi vidvān saṃharṣa āsābhyām vipramucyate iti tathā ca āhuḥ kāpilāḥ samyak jñāna adhigamāt dharma ādīnām akāraṇa prāptau tiṣṭhati saṃskāra vaśāt cakra bhrama vat dhṛta śarīraḥ iti 
NK_239.8	 dharma ādīnām akāraṇa prāptau iti tattva jñānena ucchinneṣu sa vāsana kleśeṣu dharma ādīnām sahakāri kāraṇa prāpti abhāve sati iti arthaḥ alabdha vṛttīni karmāṇi tattva jñānāt vilīyante iti ced na teṣām api karma tvāt ārabdha phala karma vat jñānena vināśa abhāvāt yaḥ api akṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare a iti upadeśaḥ tasya api ayam arthaḥ jñāne sati anāgatāni karmāṇi na kriyante iti na punar ayam asya arthaḥ utpannāni karmāṇi jñānena vināśyante iti tathā ca āgama antaram anābhuktam kṣīyate karma kalpa koṭi śataiḥ api a avaśyam eva bhoktavyam kṛtam karma śubha aśubham ityādi jñānam yadi na kṣiṇoti karmāṇi aneka janma sahastra sañcitānām karmaṇām kutas parikṣayaḥ bhogāt karmabhiḥ ca tad artham coditaiḥ anantānām katham ekasmin janmani parikṣayaḥ iti ced na kāla aniyamāt yathā eva tāvat pratijanma karmāṇi cīyante tathā eva bhogāt kṣīyante ca yāni tu aparikṣīṇāni tāni ātma jñena apūrvam asañcinvatā ca krameṇa upabhogāt karmabhiḥ ca nāśyante yathā uktam 
NK_239.9–239.10^1	 kurvan= ātma svarūpa jñaḥ bhogāt karma parikṣayam yuga koṭi sahasreṇa kaścid ekaḥ vimucyate iti tat evam vihitam akurvataḥ pratyavāya upapatteḥ tasya ca bandha hetu tvāt aanyatas virāma abhāvāt pratyavāya nirodha artham muktim icchatā yoga abhyāsa avirodhena bhikṣā bhojana ādi vat yathākālam vihitāni anuṣṭheyāni yāvat asya ātma tattvam na sphuṭībhavati sphuṭīkṛta ātma tattvasya api jīvanmuktasya tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat deha yātrā anuvartate ātma eka pratiṣṭhasya tu abhyarṇa mokṣasya parikṣīṇa prākarmaṇaḥ tāni naśyanti eva bahis saṃvitti virahāt 
NK_239.9–239.10^2	 p a r i ṇ a t a s a m ā d h i s ā m a r t h y a v i ś a d ī k ṛ t a mupacita vairāgya ahita paripāka paryantam āpādita viṣayāt vaitam unmūlita nikhila viparyaya vāsanam ekāgrīkṛta antaḥkaraṇa kāraṇam ātma jñānam eva kevalam tat dānīm san jāyate na bahis saṃvedanam bādya indriya vyāpāra uparamāt tatra kaḥ saṃbhavaḥ karmaṇām tathā ca śrutiḥ ana śṛṇoti iti āhuḥ ekībhavati na paśyati iti āhuḥ ekībhavati ityādi tadā ca akaraṇa nimittaḥ pratyavāyaḥ api na asti sandhyā iyam upasthitā iti ādikam ajānataḥ brāhmaṇosmi iti pratīti rahitasya karma adhikāra paribhraṃśāt yathā uktam 
NK_239.11–239.12^1	 brahmaṇa tva anahaṃmānī katham karmāṇi saṃsṛjet iti na ca asya uparata samasta vyāpārasya kāṣṭha vat avasthitasya api prāṇi hiṃsā api saṃbhavati yat punar asya dṛṣṭa drṣṭavyasya kṣīṇa kṣetavyasya vaśīkṛta manasaḥ viṣaya avabodha smaraṇa saṃkalpa sakha duḥkha ādi rahitasya brahma lagna samādheḥ api śarīram kiyantam cit tad śarīra sthiti mātra hetoḥ āyuḥ vipākasya karma grantheḥ anucchedāt yadā tu yāvantam kālam āyuḥ vipākena karmaṇā śarīram dhārayitavyam tāvat kāla prāptiḥ abhūt tadā sva kārya karaṇāt karma samucchede tad kāryasya śarīrasya nivṛttiḥ tad nivṛttau tad kāryasya tattva jñānasya api vināśāt ātmā kaivalyam āpadyate 
NK_239.12^2–239.16	 tatra ātma tattva jñānasya vihitānām ca karmaṇām bandha hetu karma pratibandhe vyāpārāt asti sambhūya kāritā śarīra ādi viviktam ātmānam jānataḥ ca tad upakāra apakārā= a ātmani apratisanda dhānasya ahaṅkāra mamakārayoḥ uparame sati upakāriṇī apakāriṇi ca rāga dveṣayoḥ abhāvāt udāsīnasya apravṛttau= anāgatayoḥ kuśala itara karmaṇoḥ asañcayāt sañcitayoḥ ca upabhogena karmabhiḥ ca parikṣayāt vihita akaraṇa nimittasya pratyavāyasya ca vihita anuṣṭhānena eva pratibandhāt kṣīṇe karmaṇi aihikasya dehasya nivṛttau kāraṇa antara abhāvāt āmuṣmikasya dehasya punar utpatti abhāve satya ātmanaḥ sva rūpeṇa avasthānam yathā uktam nitya naimittikaiḥ eva kurvāṇaḥ durita kṣayam jñānam ca vimalīkurvan= abhyāsena tu pācayena abhyāsāt pakva vijñānaḥ kaivalyam labhate naraḥ iti tathā paraiḥ api ayam gṛhītaḥ mārgaḥ karmaṇā sattva saṃśuddhiḥ jñānena ātma viniścayaḥ bhavet vimukti tabhyāsāt tayoḥ eva samuccayāt iti 
NK_240.1	 kim punar ātmanaḥ svarūpam yena avasthitiḥ muktiḥ ucyate ānanda ātma tā iti kecid tat ayuktam vikalpa asaha tvāt sa kim ānandaḥ muktau= anubhūyate vā na vā yadi na anubhūyate sthita upya sthitāt na viśeṣyate anupabhogya tvāt anubhūyate ced anubhavasya kāraṇam vācyam na ca kāya karaṇa ādi vigame tad utpatti kāraṇam paśyāmaḥ antaḥkaraṇa saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam iti ced na dharma adharma upagṛhītasya hi manasaḥ sahāya tvāt tad akhila śubha aśubha bīja nāśa uparībhūtam na ātma ānukūlyena varttate yoga ja dharma anugrahāt ātmānam anukūlayati ced yoga jaḥ api dharmaḥ kṛtaka tvāt avaśyam vināśī iti tad prakṣaye manasaḥ kaḥ anugrahītā atha matam acetanasya ātmanaḥ muktasya api pāṣāṇāt aviśeṣaḥ saḥ api hi na sukhāyate na ca duḥkhāyate muktaḥ api yadi tathā eva kaḥ anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ tasmāt asti ātmanaḥ svābhāvikī citiḥ sā yadā indriyaiḥ bahis ākṛṣyate tadā bahirmukhībhavati yadā tu indriyāṇi uparatāni bhavanti tadā sva ātmani eva ānanda svabhāve nimajjati 
NK_240.2	 ayam hi citeḥ ātmā yadi yam kañcid avabhāsayati yadi punar iyam mukta avasthāyām udāste tarhi sthitā api na sthitā eva varam ātmā jaḍaḥ eva kalpitaḥ iti ced atra ucyate kim citeḥ ānanda ātma tā svābhāvikī kāraṇa antara janyā vā na tāvat avabhāsa kāraṇam muktau= asti kāya karaṇa ādīnām tad kāraṇānām vilayāt iti uktam svābhāvikī ced saṃsāra avasthāyām api ānandaḥ anubhūyeta citi caittyayoḥ ubhayoḥ api sambhavāt avidyā pratibandhāt ananubhavaḥ iti ced na nityāḥ citeḥ ānanda anugraha svabhāvāyāḥ svarūpasya apracyuteḥ kaḥ pratibandha arthaḥ pracyutau vā svarūpasya kā nitya tā tasmāt nityaḥ ānandaḥ nityayā cityā ca ityamānaḥ dvayoḥ api avasthayoḥ aviśeṣeṇa cetyate na ca evam asti saṃsāra avasthāyām utpanna apavargiṇaḥ viṣaya indriya adhīna jñānasya sukhasya anubhavāt atas na asti ātmanaḥ nityam sukham tad abhāvāt na tad anubhava mayī mokṣa avasthā kintu samasta ātma viśeṣa guṇa uccheda upalakṣitā sva rūpa sthitiḥ eva yathā ca ayam puruṣa arthaḥ tathā upapāditam 
NK_241.1–241.2	 śabdaḥ ambara guṇaḥ śrotra grāhyaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ kārya kāraṇa ubhaya virodhī saṃyoga vibhāga śabda jaḥ pradeśa vṛttiḥ samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇaḥ sa dvividdhaḥ varṇa lakṣaṇaḥ dhvani lakṣaṇaḥ ca tatra akāra ādiḥ varṇa lakṣaṇaḥ śaṅkha ādi nimittaḥ dhvani lakṣaṇaḥ ca tatra varṇa lakṣaṇasya utpattiḥ ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt smṛti apekṣāt varṇa uccāraṇa icchā tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma vāyu saṃyogāt vāyau karma jāyate sa ca ūrdhvam gacchan kaṇṭha ādīn abhihanti tatas sthāna vāyu saṃyoga apekṣāt sthāna ākāśa saṃyogāt varṇa utpattiḥ 
NK_241.3–241.5	 avarṇa lakṣaṇaḥ api bherī daṇḍa saṃyoga ādi apekṣāt bherī ākāśa saṃyogāt utpadyate veṇu parva vibhāga apekṣāt veṇu ākāśa vibhāgāt ca śabdāt ca saṃyoga vibhāga niṣpannāt vīcī santāna vat śabda santānaḥ iti evam santānena śrotra pradeśana āgatasya grahaṇam śrotra śabdayoḥ gamana āgamana abhāvāt aprāptasya ca anupalabdheḥ pariśeṣāt santāna siddhiḥ iti iti praśasta pāda bhāṣye guṇa padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_241.6	 śabdaḥ ambara guṇaḥ ākāśa guṇaḥ nanu saṃkhyā ādayaḥ api ākāśa guṇaḥ sambhavanti katham idam śabdasya lakṣaṇam syāt atas āha śrotra grāhyaḥ iti śrotra grāhya tve sati ambara guṇaḥ yaḥ sa śabdaḥ itya arthaḥ parasya vipratipatti nirākaraṇa artham āha kṣaṇakaḥ iti āśutara vināśī śabdaḥ na tu nityaḥ uccāraṇāt ūrdhvam anupalambhāt sadbhāve pramāṇa abhāvena vyañja ka kṣaṇika tva kalpa nāna vakāśāt pratyabhijñānasya jvālā ādi vat sāmānya viṣaya tvena upapatteḥ tīvra manda tā ādi bhedasya ca vyaktita bheda prasādhaka tvāt kārya kāraṇa ubhaya vitodhī ādyaḥ śabdaḥ sva kāryeṇa virudhyate antyaḥ sva kāraṇena upāntya śabdena virudhyate anyasya vināśa kāraṇasya abhāvāt madhya vartinaḥ tu ubhayathā virudhyante saṃyoga nibhāga śabda jaḥ ādyaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyogāt vibhāgāt ca jāyate tata pūrvakaḥ tu śabdāt iti vivekaḥ 
NK_241.7–241.8	 pradeśa vṛttiḥ avyāpya vṛttiḥ ityārthaḥ etat ca upapāditam samāna asamāna jātīya kāraṇaḥ śabda jaḥ śabdaḥ samāna jātīya kāraṇaḥ saṃyoga ja vibhāga jaḥ ca asamāna jātīya kāraṇaḥ sa dvividhaḥ varṇa lakṣaṇaḥ dhvani lakṣaṇaḥ ca akāra ādiḥ varṇa lakṣaṇaḥ śaṅkha ādi mittaḥ dhvani lakṣaṇaḥ tatra tayoḥ madhye varṇa lakṣaṇasya utpattiḥ ucyate ātma manasoḥ saṃyogāt pūrva anubhūta varṇa smṛti apekṣāt tad sadṛśa varṇa uccāraṇe kartavye icchā bhavati tatas prayatnaḥ tam prayatnam nimitta kāraṇam apekṣamāṇāt ātma vāyu saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt kauṣṭhī avāyau karma jāyate sa ca vāyuḥ ūrdhvam gacchan kaṇṭha ādīn abhihanti hṛd kaṇṭha tālu ādīn pradeśān abhihanti tatas abhighātāt anantaram sthānasya kaṇṭha ādeḥ kauṣṭhī a vāyunā saha yaḥ saṃyogaḥ tad nimitta kāraṇa bhūtam apekṣamāṇāt sthāna ākāśa saṃyogāt samavāyi kāraṇāt varṇa utpattiḥ 
NK_241.9	 avarṇa lakṣaṇaḥ api bherī daṇḍa saṃyogāt daṇḍa gatam vegam apekṣamāṇāt bheri ākāśa saṃyogāt upajāyate bherī ākāśa saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam bherī daṇḍa saṃyogaḥ daṇḍa gataḥ ca vegaḥ nimitta kāraṇam veṇu parva bhāgāt veṇu ākāśa vibhāgāt ca śabdaḥ jāyate śabdāt ca śabda nirṣpāttam kathayati śabdāt saṃyoga vibhāga niṣpannāt vīcī santāna vat śabda santānaḥ yathā jala vīcyāḥ tad avyavahite deśe vīcī antaram upajāyate tatas api anyat tatas api anyat iti anena krameṇa vīcī santānaḥ bhavati tathā śabdāt utpannāt tad avyavahite deśe śabda antaram tatas api anayoḥ gamana āgamana abhāvāt prāptasya eva upalabdhiḥ iti tatas api anyat tatas api anyat iti anena krameṇa śabda santānaḥ bhavati evam santānena śrotra deśe samāgatasya antya śabdasya grahaṇam 
NK_241.10–241.12	 nanu eṣā kalpanā kutas siddhi ati iti atas āha śrotra śabdayoḥ iti na śrotram śabda deśam upagacchati na api śabdaḥ śrotra deśam tayoḥ niṣkriya tvāt aprāptasya grahaṇam na asti indriyāṇām prāpta kāri tvāt prakāra antareṇa ca upalabdhiḥ na ghaṭate dṛṣṭā ca vīcī santāne sva utpatti deśe vinaśyatām api sva pratyāsattim apekṣya tat avyavahite deśe sadṛśa kārya ārambha paramparayā deśa antara prāptiḥ tena śabda santānaḥ kalpyate na ca anavasthā yāvat dūram nimitta kāraṇa bhūtaḥ kauṣṭhya vāyuḥ anuvarttate tāvat dūram śabda santāna anuvṛtteḥ atas eva prativātam śabdānupalambhaḥ kauṣṭhya vāyu pratīghātāt atīva ayam mārgaḥ tārkikaiḥ kṣuṇṇaḥ tena asmābhiḥ iha bhāṣya tātparya mātraam vyākhyātam na aparā yuktiḥ uktāḥ guṇa upabaddha siddhāntaḥ yukti śukti prabhāvitaḥ mukta āhāraḥ iva svacchaḥ hṛdi vinyasyatām ayam iti bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhara kṛtāyām padārtha praveśa nyāya kanda līṭīkāyām guṇa padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_242.1–242.2	 utkṣepaṇa ādīnām pañcānām api karma tva sambandhaḥ eka dravyavat tvam kṣaṇika tvam mūrta dravya vṛtti tvam aguṇavat tvam guru tva drava tva prayatna saṃyogava tvam sva kārya saṃyoga virodhi tvam saṃyoga vibhāga nirapekṣa kāraṇa tvam asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam sva para āśraya samaveta kārya ārambhaka tvam samāna jātīya anārambhaka tvam dravya anārambhaka tvam ca pratiniyata jāti yogi tvam diś viśiṣṭa kārya rambhaka tvam ca viśeṣaḥ jagat aṅkura bījāya saṃsāra arṇava setave namaḥ jñāna amṛtasyandri candrāya ardha indu maulaye 
NK_242.3	 utkṣepaṇa ādīnām parasparam sādharmyam itara padārtha vaidharmyam ca pratipādayan= āha utkṣepaṇa ādīnām iti karma tvam nāma sāmānyam tena saha sambandhaḥ utkṣepaṇa ādīnām eva eka dravyavat tvam ekadā ekasmin dravye ekam eva karma vartate ekam karma ekatra eva dravye varttate iti eka dravyavat tvam yadi ekasmin dravye yugapad viruddha ubhaya karma samavāyaḥ syāt tadā tayoḥ paraspara pratibandhāt diś viśeṣa saṃyoga vibhāga anutpattau saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ anapekṣam kāraṇam karma iti lakṣaṇa hāniḥ syāt atha aviruddha karma dvaya samāveśaḥ tadā ekasmāt eva tad deśa dravya vya saṃyoga vibhāgayoḥ upapatteḥ dvitīya kalpanā vaiyarthyam evam ekam karma na anekatra varttate ekasya calane tasmāt karmaṇaḥ anyasya calana anupalambhāt kṣaṇika tvam āśutara vināśi tvam mūrta dravya vṛtti tvam avacchinna parimāṇa dravya vṛtti tvam aguṇavat tvam guṇa rahita tvam guru tva drava prayatna saṃyoga ja tvam sva kārya saṃyoga virodhi tvam sva kāryeṇa saṃyogena vināśya tva na vibhāga vināśya tvam uttara saṃyoga abhāva prasaṅgāt 
NK_242.4	 saṃyoga vibhāga nirapekṣa kāraṇam yathā vega ārambhe nodana abhighāta viśeṣa apekṣa tvam na evam saṃyoga vibhāga ārambhe nodana ādi apekṣa tvam iti arthaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam yathā gunānām nimitta kāraṇa tvam api na evam karmaṇām kim tu asamavāyi kāraṇa tvam eva iti arthaḥ sva para āśraya samaveta kārya ārambhaka tvam sva āśraye para āśraye ca vyāsajya samavetam yat kāryam saṃyoga vibhāga lakṣaṇam tadārambhaka tvam samāna jātīya anārambhaka tvam karmaṇaḥ karma antarātambhe gacchataḥ gati virāmaḥ na syāt icchā prayatna ādi virāmāt ante gati virāmaḥ iti ced tarhi icchā prayatna ādikam eva uttarottara karmaṇām api kāraṇam na tu karmam vivāda adhyāsitam karma karma kāraṇam na bhavati karma tvāt antyakarma vat athavā vivāda adhyāsitam karma karma sādhyam na bhavati karma tvāt ādi a karma vat dravya anārambhaka tvam uttara saṃyogāt nivṛtte karmaṇi dravyasya utpādāt pratiniyata jāti yogi tvam utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu pratyekam utkṣepaṇa tva ādi yogaḥ iti arthaḥ etat sarva pañcānām api sādharmyam digviśiṣṭa kārya karttṛ tvam eva kathayati tatra iti 
NK_243.1–243.3	 tatra utkṣepaṇam śarīra avayaveṣu tad sambaddheṣu ca yat ūrdhva bhāgbhiḥ pradeśaiḥ saṃyoga kāraṇam adhas bhā adbhiḥ ca vibhāga kāraṇam karma utpadyate guru tva prayatna saṃyogebhyaḥ tad utkṣepaṇam tad viparīta saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇam kārma avakṣepaṇam ṛjunaḥ dravyasya agra avayavānām tad deśaiḥ vibhāgaḥ saṃyogaḥ ca mūla pradeśaiḥ yena karmaṇā avayavī kuṭilaḥ san jāyate tad ākuñcanam 
NK_243.4–243.6	 tad viparyayeṇa sma ayoga vibhāga utpattau yena karmaṇā avayavī ṛjuḥ sampadyate tad prasāraṇam yat aniyata diś pradeśa saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇam tat gamanam iti etat pañcavidham api karma śarīra avayaveṣu tad sambaddheṣu ca sat pratyayam asat pratyayam ca yat anyat tat apratyayam eteṣu anyeṣu ca tad gamanam eva karmaṇām jāti pañcatvam ayuktam gamana aviśeṣāt 
NK_243.7–243.8	 śarīra avayaveṣu hasta ādiṣu tad sambadheṣu musala ādiṣu ca yadu prdhvabha adbhiḥ pradeśaiḥ saṃyoga kāraṇam adhobhāgbhiḥ ca vibhāga kāraṇam guru tva saṃyoga prayatnebhyaḥ jāyate tad utkṣepaṇam tad viparīta saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇam kārma avakṣepaṇam sdhaḥ deśesaṃyoga kāraṇam ūrdhva deśa vibhāga kāraṇam karma avakṣepaṇam iti arthaḥ 
NK_243.9–243.12	 ṛjunaḥ iti tad deśa etagrāvayava sambaddhaiḥ ākāśa ādi deśaiḥ san jāyate iti yena karmaṇā iti sambandhaḥ agra avayavānām mūla pradeśa vibhāgāt uttra deśa saṃyoga utpattau satyām iti arthaḥ sat pratyayam iti prayatna pūrvakam aprayatna pūrvakam ca bhavati iti arthaḥ yat anyat iti eteṣu śarīra avayaveṣu musala ādiṣu anyeṣu vā dravyeṣu yat tad apratyaya jam karma jāyate sat prapādanyat tad gamanam eva codayati karmaṇām iti utkṣepaṇa ādīnām karmaṇām jāti pañcatvam ayuktam gamanāt sarveṣām aviśeṣāt abhedāt iti codana arthaḥ 
NK_244.1–244.2	 sarvam hi kṣaṇikam karma gamana mātram utpannam sva āśrayasya ūrdhvam adhas tiryak vā paramāṇu vivara mātraiḥ pradeśaiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgān karoti sarvatra ca gamana pratyayaḥ aviśiṣṭaḥ tasmāt gamanam eva sarvam iti na vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt iha utkṣepaṇam para tra apakṣepaṇam iti evamādi sarvatra vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī dṛṣṭe tad hetuḥ sāmānya viśeṣa bhedaḥ avagamyate teṣām udādi upasarga viśeṣāt pratiniyata diś viśiṣṭa kārya ārambha tvāt upalakṣaṇa bhedaḥ api siddhaḥ 
NK_244.3–244.4	 sarveṣām gamanāt aviśeṣam eva kathayati sarvam hi ityādinā utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu ūrdhvam gacchati adhas gacchati iti pratyaya darśanāt sarvam eva idam utkṣepaṇa ādikam gamanam eva samādhate na iti yat tvayā uktam tat na utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu vargaśas prativargam pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttyoḥ darśanāt govarge aśva ādi varga vyāvṛttyā pratyaya anugama darśanāt go tvam kalpyate yathā tathā utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu prativargam itara vyāvṛttyā pratyaya anugama darśanāt utkṣepaṇa tva ādi sāmānya kalpanā iti abhiprāyaḥ asya vivaraṇam sugamam 
NK_244.5	 teṣām iti upalakṣaṇa bhedaḥ api iti api śabdaḥ kārya ārambhāt iti asmāt paraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ upalakṣyate anya vilakṣaṇa tayā pratipādyate vyaktiḥ anayā iti upalakṣaṇam jātiḥ tat ayam atra arthaḥ na kevalam anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti pratyaya daeśanāt utkṣepaṇa apakṣa īpṇa ādīnām jāti bhedaḥ siddhaḥ udādi upasarga bhedāt pratiniyata diś viśiṣṭa kārya ārambhāt api siddhaḥ apare tu teṣām utkṣepaṇa ādīnām udādi upasarga viśeṣāt diś viciṣṭa kārya ārambhāt upalakṣaṇa bhedaḥ api pratipatti bhedaḥ api siddhaḥ iti abhede hi yathā utkṣepaṇam ūrdhva saṃyoga vibhāga hetuḥ evam apakṣepaṇa ādikam api syāt 
NK_245.1	 evam api pañca eva iti avadhāraṇa anupapattiḥ niṣkramaṇa praveśana ādiṣu api vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt yadi utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu sarvatra vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt jāti bhedaḥ iṣyate evam ca niṣkramaṇa praveśana ādiṣu api kārya bhedāt teṣu pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī iti ced na utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu api kārya bhedāt eva pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti prasaṅgaḥ atha samāne vargaśas pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti sadbhāve utkṣepaṇa ādīnām eva jāti bhedaḥ na niṣkramaṇa ādīnām iti atra viśeṣe hetuḥ asti iti na jāti saṅkara prasaṅgāt niṣkramaṇa ādīnām jāti bhedāt pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttau jāti saṅkaraḥ prasajyate katham 
NK_245.2	 dvayoḥ draṣṭroḥ ekasmāt apavarakāt apavaraka antaram gacchataḥ yugapad niṣkramaṇa praveśana pratyayau dṛṣṭau tathā dvāra pradeśe praviśati niṣkrāmati iti ca yadā tu pratisīra ādi apanītam bhavati tadā na praveśana pratyayaḥ na api niṣkramaṇa pratyayaḥ kintu gamana pratyayaḥ eva bhavati tathā nālikāyām vaṃśa patra ādau patati bahūnām draṣṭṝṇām yugapad bhramaṇa patana praveśana pratyayāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ iti jāti saṅkara prasaṅgaḥ na ca evam utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu pratyaya saṅkaraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt utkṣepaṇa ādīnām eva jāti bhedāt pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛttī niṣkramaṇa ādīnām tu kārya bhedāt iti 
NK_245.3–245.4	 katham yugapad pratyaya bhedaḥ iti ced atha matam yathā jāti saṅkaraḥ na asti evam aneka karma saṅkaraḥ api na asti iti ekasmin karmaṇi yugapada draṣṭṝṇām bhramaṇa patana praveśana pratyayāḥ katham bhavanti iti atra brūmaḥ na avayava avayavinoḥ digviśiṣṭa saṃyoga vibhāgānām bhedāt yaḥ hi draṣṭā avayavānām pāśrvataḥ paryāyeṇa diś pradeśaiḥ saṃyoga vibhāgān paśyati tasya bhramaṇāratyayaḥ bhavati yaḥ tu avayavinaḥ ūrdhva pradeśāt vibhāgam adhas saṃyogam ca avekṣate tasya patana pratyayaḥ bhavati yaḥ punar nālika antar deśe saṃyogam bahis deśe ca vibhāgam paśyati tasya praveśana pratyayaḥ bhavati iti siddhaḥ kārya bhedāt niṣkramaṇa ādīnām pratyaya bhedaḥ iti bhavatu utkṣepaṇa ādīnām jāti bhedāt pratyaya bhedaḥ niṣkramaṇa ādīnām tu kārya bhedāt iti 
NK_245.5	 puvaḥ codayati evam api iti yadi prativargam pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu sāmānyam abhyupeyate tadā niṣkramaṇa ādiṣu api prativargam pratyaya anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti darśanāt niṣkramaṇa tva ādikam abhyupeyam tatas ca pañca eva iti avadhāraṇa anupapattiḥ atha niṣkramaṇa ādiṣu kārya bhedāt pratyaya bhedaḥ na jāti bhedāt tadā utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu api tathā syāt iti āha kārya bhedāt teṣu iti samādhatte na iti yadi niṣkramaṇa tva ādi jātayaḥ iṣyante tadā jāti saṅkara prasaṅgaḥ ekasyām vyāktau viruddha aneka jāti samavāyaḥ prasajyate iti arthaḥ 
NK_245.6	 katham iti pṛṣṭaḥ san= āha dvayoḥ draṣṭroḥ iti dvayoḥ draṣṭroḥ ekasmāt apavarakāt apavaraka antaram gacchataḥ puruṣasya yau draṣṭārau tayoḥ ekasyām karma vyaktau niṣkramaṇa praveśana pratyayau dṛṣṭau yatas apavarakāt puruṣaḥ nirgacchati tatra sthitasya nirgacchati iti pratyayaḥ yatra praviśati tatra sthitasya praviśati iti pratyayaḥ yadi jāti kṛtau= imau pratyayau dṛṣṭau tadā ekasyām vyaktau paraspara viruddha niṣkramaṇa tva praveśana tva jāti dvaya samāveśaḥ dūṣaṇam syāt tayā dvāra pradeśe praviśati niṣkrāmati iti yathā ekasmin eva bahu prakoṣṭhake gṛhe prakoṣṭhāt prakoṣṭha antaram gacchati puruṣe pūrva apara prakoṣṭha sthitayoḥ draṣṭroḥ dvāra pradeśe nirgacchati praviśati iti pratyayau bhavataḥ yadā tu pratisīra ādi apanītam madhya sthitam javanika ādi apanītam bhavati tadā na na praveśana pratyayaḥ na api niṣkramaṇa pratyayaḥ kintu gamana pratyayaḥ eva bhavati tasmāt gamanam eva tatra upādhi kṛtaḥ ca pratyaya bhedaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NK_245.7	 udāharaṇa atraram āha tathā nālikāyām iti nālikā iti garttasya abhidhānam sva pakṣe viśeṣam āha na ca evam iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti ekadailasmin dravye tāvat ekam eva karma bhavati tatra katham yugapad aneka karma pratyayaḥ iti āha katham iti tat vivṛṇoti atha matam ityādinā atra brūmaḥ iti siddhānta upakramaḥ yat tvayā uktam tat na avayavānām avayavinaḥ ca diśā viśiṣṭānām saṃyoga vibhāgānām bhedāt asya sugamam vivaraṇam avayava karmasu pārśvatas saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇeṣu bhramaṇa pratyayaḥ avayavi kriyāyām kārya bhedāt patana praveśana pratyayau= iti arthaḥ 
NK_246.1–246.3	 atha gamana tvam kim karma tva paryāyaḥ āhosvit aparam sāmānyam iti kutas te saṃśayaḥ samasyeṣu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu karma pratyaya vat gamana pratyaya aviśeṣāt karma tva paryāyaḥ iti gamyate yatas tu utkṣepaṇa ādi vat viśeṣa saṃjñayā abhihitam tasmāt aparam sāmānyam syāt iti na karma tva paryāya tvāt ātma tva puruṣa tva vat karma tva paryāyaḥ eva gamana tvam iti atha viśeṣa saṃjñayā kimartham gamana grahaṇam kṛtam iti na bhramaṇa ādi avarodha artha tvāt utkṣepaṇa ādi śabdaiḥ anavaruddhānām bhramaṇa patana spandana ādīnām avarodha artham gamana grahaṇam krātam iti anyathā hi yāni eva cātvāri viśeṣa saṃjña tā uktāni tāni eva sāmānya viśeṣa saṃjñā viṣayāṇi prasajyeran iti athavā astu aparam sāmānyam gamana tvam aniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga kāraṇeṣu bhramaṇa ādiṣu eva vartate gamana śabdaḥ ca utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu bhāktaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ sva āśraya saṃyoga vibhāga kartṛ tva sāmānyāt iti 
NK_246.4	 bhavatu utkṣepaṇa ādīnām jāti bhedāt pratyaya bhedaḥ atha gamana tvam kim karma tva paryāyaḥ āhosvit aparam sāmānyam iti siddhāntī pṛcchati kṛtaḥ te saṃśayaḥ saṃśayaḥ atra anupapannaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ paraḥ saṃśayam upapādayati samasteṣu iti utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu sarveṣu yathā karma pratyayaḥ calana ātmaka tā pratyayaḥ tathā teṣu gamana pratyayaḥ ūrdhvam gacchati adhas gacchati mūlapradeśam gacchati agra deśam gacchati iti pratyayaḥ bhavati iti tena gamana tvam karma tva paryāyaḥ iti gamyate samasta bheda vyāpaka tvāt yat tu uskṣepaṇa ādi vat gamanam api pṛthak abhihitam viśeṣa saṃjñayā tasmāt gamana tvam aparam sāmānyam syāt avāntara bheda nirūpaṇa avasare tasya saṃkīrtanāt 
NK_246.5	 evam upapādite pareṇa saṃśaye sati ācāryaḥ prāha na iti na kartavyaḥ saṃśayaḥ kutas gamana tvasya karma tva paryāya tvāt etat vivṛṇoti ātma tva puruṣa tva vat karma tva paryāyaḥ eva gamana tvam iti yathā ātma tvasya paryāyaḥ puruṣa tvam samasta bheda vyāpaka tvāt tathā gamana tvam karma tvasya paryāyaḥ atha kim artham viśeṣa saṃjñayā pṛthak gamana grahaṇam kratam iti codayati atha iti 
NK_246.6	 uttaram āha na iti utkṣepaṇa ādi śabdaiḥ anavaruddhāḥ na saṃgṛhītāḥ bhramaṇa ādayaḥ yadi gamana grahaṇam na kriyeta tadā teṣām karma tvena saṃgrahaḥ na syāt kintu viśeṣa saṃjñayā uddiṣṭānām utkṣepaṇa ādīnām eva param karma tva saṃjñā viṣaya tvam bhavet bhramaṇa ādayaḥ api ca loke karma tvena prasiddhāḥ atas teṣām parigraha artham pṛthak gamana grahaṇam kṛtam iti grantha arthaḥ 
NK_246.7	 athavā astu aparam sāmānyam gamana tvam tat keṣu varttate tatra āha aniyata diś deśe kutas tarhi utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu gamana pratyayaḥ atas āha gamana śabdaḥ tu iti gamana śabda grahaṇasya upalakṣaṇa artha tvāt gamana pratyayaḥ api utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu bhāktaḥ vyākhyeyaḥ upacārasya bījam āha sva āśraya saṃyoga vibhāga kartṛ tva sāmānyāt iti gamanam sva āśrayasya saṃyoga vibhāgau karoti utkṣepaṇa ādayaḥ api kurvanti etāvatā sādharmyeṇa utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu gamana vyavahāraḥ anena sādharmyeṇa gamane kasmāt utkṣepaṇa ādi vyavahāraḥ na bhavati paiṅgalya pāṭala tva ādi sādharmyeṇa vahnau api māṇavaka vyavakāraḥ kasmāt na bhavati atha ucyate na kāraṇa sadbhāve sati upacāra kalpanā kintu sthite vyavahāre kāraṇa kalpanā iti evam ced atra api saḥ eva parihāraḥ 
NK_247.1–247.2^1	 sat pratyaya karma vidhiḥ katham cikīrṣateṣu yajña adhyayana dāna kṛṣi ādiṣu yadā hastam utkṣeptum icchati akṣeptum vā tadā hastam atyātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ san jāyate tam prayatnam gurutam ca apekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt haste karma bhavati hasta vat sarva śarīra avayaveṣu pāda ādiṣu śarīre ca iti tad sambaddheṣu api katham yadā hastena musalam gṛhītvā icchām karoti autkṣipāmi hastena musalam a iti tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt yasmin eva kāle haste utkṣepaṇa karma utpadyate tasmin eva kāle tam eva prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt dhaḥ tam usala saṃyogāt musale api karma iti 
NK_247.1–247.2^2	 tatas dūram utkṣipte musale tad artha icchā nivartate punar api apakṣepaṇa icchā utpadyate tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇa ādi athā uktāt saṃyoga dvayāt hasta musalayoḥ yugapad apakṣepaṇa karmaṇī bhavataḥ tatas antyena musala karmaṇā ulūkhla musalayoḥ abhighāta ākhyāḥ saṃyogaḥ kriyate sa saṃyogaḥ musala gata vegam apekṣamāṇaḥ apratyayam musale utpatana karma karoti tad karma abhighāta apekṣam musale saṃskāram ārabhate tam apekṣya musala hasta saṃyogaḥ apratyayam haste ayutana karma karoti 
NK_247.3–247.4	 yadi api prāktanaḥ saṃskāraḥ vinaṣṭaḥ tathā api musalelūkhalayoḥ saṃyogaḥ paṭu karma utpādakaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣa bhāvāt tasya saṃskāra ārambhe sācivya samarthaḥ bhavati athavā prāktanaḥ eva paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ abhighātāt avinaśyan= avasthitaḥ iti atas saṃskāravati punar saṃskāra ārambhaḥ na asti atas yasmin kāle saṃskārāa īkṣāt abhighātāt apratyayam musale utpatana karma tasmin eva kāle tam eva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇān musala hasta saṃyogāt apratyayam haste api utpatana karma iti 
NK_247.5–247.6	 pāṇi mukteṣu gamana vidhiḥ katham yadā tomaram hastena gṛhītvā utkṣeptum icchā utpadyate hastena tomara nud kṣipāmi iti tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇa ādi athā uktāt saṃyoga dvayāt tomara hastayoḥ yugapad a ākarṣaṇa karmaṇī bhavataḥ prasārite ca haste tad ākarṣaṇa arthaḥ prayatnaḥ nivartate tad anantaram tiryak ūrdhvam dūram āsannam vā kṣipāmi iti icchāsan jāyate tad anantaram tad anurūpaḥ prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇaḥ tomara hasta saṃyogaḥ nodana ākhyaḥ tasmāt tomare karma utpannam nodana apekṣam tasmin saṃskāram ārabhate tatas saṃskāra nodanābhyām tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat hasta tomara vibhāgaḥ iti tatas vibhāgāt nodane nivṛtte saṃskārāt ūrdhvam tiryak dūram āsannam vā prayatna anurūpāṇi karmāṇi bhavanti āpatanāt iti 
NK_247.7	 tathā yantra mukteṣu api gamana vidhiḥ katham yaḥ balavān kṛta vyāyāmaḥ vāmena kareṇa dhanuḥ viṣṭabhya dakṣiṇena śaram sandhāya sa śarām jyām muṣṭinā gṛhītvā ākarṣaṇa icchām karoti sajyeṣu akarṣayāmi etat dhanuḥ iti tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta sma ayogāt ākarṣa karma haste yadā eva utpadyate tadā eva tam eva prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt hasta jyā śara saṃyogāt jyāyām śare ca karma prayatna viśiṣṭa hasta jyā śara saṃyogam apekṣamāṇābhyām jyā koṭi saṃyogābhyām karmaṇī bhavataḥ dhanuṣkoṭyoḥ iti etat sarvam yugapad 
NK_247.8	 evam ākarṇāt ākṛṣṭe dhanuṣi na atas paramanena gantavyam iti yat jñānam tat = tad ākarṣaṇa arthasya prayatnasya vināśaḥ tatas punar mokṣaṇa icchā san jāyate tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma aṅguli saṃyogāt aṅguli karma tasmāt jyā aṅguli vibhāgaḥ tatas vibhāgāt saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin vinaṣṭe pratibandhaka abhāvāt yadā dhanuṣi vartamānaḥ sthiti sthāpakaḥ saṃskāraḥ maṇḍalībhūtam dhanuḥ yathā avasthitam sthāpayati tadā tam eva saṃskāram apekṣāmāṇāt dhanuḥ jyā saṃyogāt jyāyām śare ca karma utpadyate tad sva kāraṇa apekṣam jyāyām saṃskāram karoti tam apekṣamāṇaḥ iṣu jyā saṃyogaḥ nodanam tasmāt iṣau= ādyam karma nodana apekṣa miṣau saṃskāram ārabhate tasmāt saṃskārān nodana sahāyāt tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat iṣujyā vibhāgaḥ vibhāgāt nivṛtte nodane karmāṇi uttarottarāṇi iṣu saṃskārāt eva aparanāt iti 
NK_247.9–247.10	 bahūni karmāṇi kranaśaḥ kasmāt saṃyoga bahu tvāt ekaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ antarālekarmaṇaḥ apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt iti evam ātma adhiṣṭhiteṣu sat pratyayam asat pratyayam ca karma uktam sat pratyaya karma vidhiḥ prayatna pūrvakaḥ karma prakāraḥ kathyate iti arthaḥ katham iti pṛṣṭaḥ san= āha cikīrṣiteṣu iti yajña ādiṣu kartum abhipreteṣu satsu yadā puruṣaḥ hastam utkṣeptum avakṣeptum vā icchati tadā gastavati ātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ jāyate tam prayatnam nimitta kāraṇa bhūtam apekṣamāṇāt ātma gasta saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt haste karma bhavati sati api prayatne guru tva rahitasya utkṣepaṇa apakṣepaṇayoḥ aśakya karaṇa tvāt guru tvasya api kāraṇa tvam hasta vat sarva śarīra avayaveṣu pāda diṣu śarīre ca iti pāde karma utpattau pādavatī ātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ nimitta kāraṇam pāda ātma saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam evam sarvatra śarīra avaya kriyā utpattau draṣṭavyam śarīra kriyā utpattau api śarīra ātma saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam śarīra vat ātma pradeśe prayatnaḥ nimitta kāraṇam 
NK_247.11^1	 tad sambaddheṣu api śarīra avayava sambaddheṣu api katham karma utpattiḥ iti praśna arthaḥ yadā hastena musalam gṛhītvā icchām karoti autkṣipāmi hastena musalam a iti tad anantaram tasyāḥ icchāyāḥ anantaram prayatnaḥ hastena musalam ūrdhvam utkṣipāmi iti hasta musalayoḥ yugapad utkṣepaṇa icchātaḥ prayatnaḥ jāyamānaḥ tayoḥ yugapad utkṣepaṇa samarthaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ eva jāyate tam prayatnam viśiṣṭam nimittama papekṣamāṇāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt samavāyi kāraṇāt yasmin eva kāle haste utkṣepaṇa karma utpadyate tasmin= eva kāle tam eva prayatnam ubhaya artham utpannam apekṣamāṇāt hasta musala saṃyogāt asamavāyi kāraṇāt musale api karma bhavati kāraṇa yaugapadyāt 
NK_247.11^2	 tatas dūram utkṣipte musale tad artha icchā nivartate utkṣepaṇa icchā nivartate punar api apakṣepaṇa icchā utpadyate hastena musakasya apakṣepaṇa icchā upajāyate iti arthaḥ tad anantaram prayatnaḥ saḥ api jāyamānaḥ utkṣepaṇa prayatna vat viśiṣṭaḥ eva jāyate tam prayatnam apekṣamāṇādi athā uktāt saṃyoga dvayāt ātma hasta saṃyogāt hasta musala saṃyogāt hasta musalayoḥ yuga padakṣepaṇa karmaṇī bhavataḥ tatas antyena musala karmaṇā ulūkhala musalayoḥ abhighāta ākhyaḥ saṃyogaḥ kriyate 
NK_247.11^3	 apakṣiptasya musalasya anyena karmaṇā ulūkhala musala samavetaḥ musalasya utpatana hetuḥ saṃyogaḥ kriyate iti arthaḥ sa saṃyogaḥ musala gata vegam apekṣamāṇaḥ apratyayam aprayatna pūrvakam musale utpatana karma karoti utpatana karma utpatau abhighātaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam musala gataḥ vegaḥ nimitta kāraṇam musalam samavāyi kāraṇam tad karma abhighāta apekṣam musale saṃskāram ārabhate utpatana karma sva kāraṇa abhighāta ākhyam saṃyogam apekṣamāṇam musale vegam ārabhate tam saṃskāram apekṣya hasta musala saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇa bhūtaḥ pratyayam aprayatna pūrvakam haste api utpatana karma karoti 
NK_247.11^4	 yaḥ asau prāktanaḥ apakṣepaṇa saṃskāraḥ musala gataḥ saḥ api abhighātāt vinaṣṭaḥ tad abhāve katham musale apratyayam utpatana karma utpatana saṃskāaram ārabhate apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt atas āha yadi api prāktanaḥ saṃskāraḥ vinaṣṭaḥ tathā api musala ulūkhala saṃyogaḥ paṭu karma utpādakaḥ saṃskāra janaka karma utpādakaḥ kutas saṃyoga viśeṣa bhāvāt saṃyoga viśeṣa tvāt kim atas yadi evam tatra āha tasya karmaṇaḥ saṃskāra ārambhe kartavye sācivya samarthaḥ bhavati sāhayye samarthaḥ bhavati asmin pakṣe hasta musalayoḥ utpatana karmaṇī krameṇa bhavataḥ āśu bhāvāt ca yaugapadya grahaṇam 
NK_247.12	 prakārantaram āha athavā prāktanaḥ eva paṭuḥ saṃskāraḥ abhighātāt avinaśyan= avasthitaḥ iti viśiṣṭa kāraṇa janya tvāt ati prabalaḥ saṃskāraḥ sparśavat dravya saṃyogena api na vinaśyati atas saṃskāravati saṃskāra antara ārambhaḥ na asti atas prāktana apakṣepaṇa saṃskāraḥ na vinaṣṭaḥ atas prāktana saṃskāravati musale saṃskāra antara ārambhaḥ na asti iti pratīyate yasmin kāle saṃskāra apekṣāt abhighātāt apratyayam musale utpatana karma tasmin= eva kāle tam eva saṃskāram apekṣamāṇāt dhasta musala saṃyogāt apratyayam haste api utpatana karma iti asmin pakṣe hasta musala utpatana karmaṇoḥ vāstavam eva yaugapadyam 
NK_247.13^1	 pāṇi mukteṣu gamana vidhiḥ katham pāṇi mukteṣu dravyeṣu gamana vidhiḥ gamana prakāraḥ katham utpadyate iti praśne kṛne satyāha yadā tomaram gṛhītvā utkṣeptum icchā utpadyate ahastena tomaram utkṣipāmi iti a tad anantaram prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt i athā ukta saṃyoga gvaya āda anya hasta saṃyoga hasta tomara saṃyogāt ca hasta tomarayoḥ yugapad a ākarṣaṇa karmaṇī bhavataḥ yugapad ākarṣaṇa iti anākṛṣya utkṣeptum aśakyatvāt prasārite haste tad ākarṣaṇa arthaḥ prayatnaḥ nivartate iti tayoḥ hata tomarayoḥ ākarṣaṇa prayojanaḥ prayatnaḥ nivartate tad virodhi prasāraṇa prayatna utpādāt iti arthaḥ tad anantaram prasāraṇa anantaram tiryak ūrdhvam vā dūram āsannam vā kṣipāmi iti iccha utpadyate tad anantaram tad anurūpaḥ prayatnaḥ tiryakkṣepaṇa icchāyām tiryak kṣepaṇa prayatnaḥ jāyate 
NK_247.13^2	 ūrdhva kṣepaṇa icchāyām ūrdhva kṣepaṇa prayatnaḥ jāyate dūra kṣepaṇa icchāyām mahan prayatnaḥ āsanna kṣepaṇa icchāyām ca śithilaḥ prayatnaḥ jāyate iti tad anurūpa śabda arthaḥ tam apekṣamāṇaḥ tomara hasta saṃyogaḥ nodana ākhyaḥ na udyasya tomarasya na udakasya ca hastasya saha gamana hetu tvāt tasmāt nodana ākhyāt i athā uktāt i= chā anurūpa prayatna apekṣāt tomare karmpa utpannam tat karma nokana apekṣam tasmin tomare saṃskāram ārabhate tatas saṃskāra nodanābhyām tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat hasta tomara vibhāgaḥ iti tatas vibhāgāt nivṛte nodane saṃskārāt ūrdhvam tiryak dūram āsannām vā tad anurūpāni kārmāṇi bhavanti āpātanāt iti tomarasya patanam yāvat saṃskāra anurūpāṇi karmāṇi bhavati iti arthaḥ 
NK_247.14	 yantra mukteṣu api gamana vidhiḥ katham yaḥ balavān kṛta vyāyāmaḥ kṛta āyudha abhyāsaḥ vāmena kareṇa dhanuḥ viṣṭabhya gāḍham gṛhītvā dakṣiṇena śaram sandhāya jyāyām śaram saṃyojya sa śarām jyām śareṇa saha vartamānām jyām muṣṭinā gṛhītvā icchām karoti sajyeṣu ākarṣayāmi etat dhanuḥ iti jyā iti dhanuḥ guṇasya ākhyā iṣuḥ iti śarasya abhidhānam jyā ca iṣuḥ ca jyeṣū saha jyeṣubhyām vartate iti sajyeṣū dhanuḥ etat ākarṣayāmi iti icchāyāḥ ākāraḥ darśitaḥ tad anantaram prayatnaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma gasta saṃyogāt ākarṣaṇa karma haste yadā eva utpadyate tadā eva tam eva prayatnam apekṣamāṇāt hasta jyā saṃyoga āt jyāyām karma śare ca karma hasta śara saṃyogāt prayatna viśiṣṭa jyā hasta saṃyogam apekṣamāṇābhyām jyā koṭi saṃyogābhyām karmaṇī dhanuṣkoṭyoḥ iti etat sarvam yugapad kāaraṇa yaugapadyāt evam ākarṇāt ākṛṣṭe dhanuṣi ṇataḥ paramanena hastena gantavyam iti yat jñānam tasmāt tad ākarṣaṇa arthasya iti dhanuḥ ākarṣaṇa arthasya prayatnasya vināśaḥ iti 
NK_247.15	 tatas śarasya guṇasya ca mokṣaṇa icchā tad anantaram prayatnaḥ mokṣaṇa arthaḥ tam apekṣamāṇāt ātma aṅguli saṃyogāt aṅguli karma tasmāt aṅguli vibhāgaḥ śara guṇābhyām tatas vibhāgāt śara guṇa aṅguli saṃyoga vināśaḥ tasmin saṃyoge vinaṣṭe pratibandhaka abhāvāt yadā dhanuṣi vartamānaḥ sthiti sthāpakaḥ saṃskāraḥ maṇḍalībhūtam dhanuḥ yathā avasthitam sthāpayati tadā tam saṃskāram apekṣamāṇāt dhanuḥ jyā saṃyogāt jyāyām śare ca karma utpadyate tat karma sva kāraṇa apekṣam dhanuḥ jyā saṃyoga apekṣam jyāyām saṃskāram vega ākhyam karoti tam saṃskāram apekṣamāṇaḥ iṣu jyā saṃyogaḥ nodanam na udyasya iṣā ūḥ na udakasya guṇasya saha gamana hetu tvāt tasmāt nodana ādiṣau= ādyam karma bhūtam nodana apekṣa miṣau saṃskāram ārabhate tasmāt saṃskārāt nodana sahāyāt tāvat karmāṇi bhavanti yāvat iṣujyā vibhāgaḥ vibhāgāt nivṛtte nodane karmāṇi uttarottarāṇi saṃskārāt eva vega ākhyāt bhadanti yāvat patanam iṣoḥ etasya ca pātaḥ guru tva pratibandhaka saṃskāra kṣayāt 
NK_247.16	 atra codayati bahūni karmāṇi kramaśas kasmāt iti jyā vibhaktasya iṣoḥ antarāle kramaśas bahūni karmāṇi bhavanti iti kasmāt kalpyate ekam eva karma kutas na kalpitam iti abhiprāyaḥ samādhatte saṃyoga bahu tvāt iti uttara saṃyoga antam karma iti avasthitam kṣiptaṣoḥ antarāle bahuvaḥ saṃyogāḥ dṛśyante tena bahūni karmāṇi bhavanti iti āśrīyate ekaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ antarāle karmaṇaḥ apekṣā kāraṇa abhāvāt nodana abhighātayoḥ anyatara apekṣam karma saṃskāram ārabhate na karma mātram vega abhāvāt na ca antarāle nodanam na api abhighātaḥ tasmāt ekaḥ eva śarajyaā saṃyoga apekṣeṇa śara karmaṇā kṛtaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ saṃskāraḥ yāvat patanam anuvartate yathā yathā ca asya kārya karaṇāt śaktiḥ kṣīyate tathā tathā kāryam mandataratamādi bheda bhinnam upajāyate yathā taroḥ taruṇasya phalam prakṛṣyateniḥkṛṣyate ca jīrṇasya 
NK_248.1–248.4	 anadhiṣṭhiteṣu bāhyeṣu caturṣu mahābhūteṣu apratyayam karma gamanam eva nogana ādibhyaḥ bhavati tatra noganam guru tva drava tva vega prayatnāt samasta vyasta anapekṣamāṇaḥ yaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ nodanam avibhāga hetoḥ karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam tasmāt caturṣu api mahābhūteṣu karma bhavati yathā paṅka ākhyāyām pṛthivyām vega apekṣaḥ yaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ vibhāga hetoḥ ekasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam saḥ abhighātaḥ tasmāt api caturṣu mahābhūteṣu karma bhavati yathā pāṣāṇa ādiṣu niṣṭhure vastuni abhipatiteṣu tathā pāda ādibhiḥ nudyamānāyām abhihanyamānāyām vā paṅka ākhyāyām yaḥ sma ayogaḥ nodana abhighātayoḥ anyatara apekṣaḥ ubhaya apekṣaḥ vā sa saṃyukta saṃyogaḥ tasmāt api ye pradeśāḥ na nudyante na api abhihanyante teṣu api karma jāyate 
NK_248.5	 upasaṃharati evam iti anadhiṣṭhiteṣu bāhyeṣu caturṣu mahābhūteṣu apratyayam gamanam eva nodana ādibhyaḥ bhavati ātmanā asādhāraṇena sambandhi nā anadhiṣṭhiteṣu bāhyeṣu aprayatna pūrvakam gamana ākhyam eva karma bhavati na utkṣepaṇa ādi rūpam iti arthaḥ mahābhūteṣu nodana ādibhyaḥ karma bhavati iti uktam atha kim idam nodanam atas āha tatra nodanam guru tva drava tva prayatna vegāna samasta vyasta anapekṣamāṇe yaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ katham ayam saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ nodanam ecyate tatra āha nodanam avibhāga hetoḥ karmaṇaḥ kāraṃam iti na udyana udakayoḥ paraspara vibhāgam na karoti yat karma tasya kāraṇam noganam 
NK_248.6	 kim uktam syāt anena saṃyogena saha na udakaḥ na udyam nodayati na anyathā tena ayam noganam ucyate nodanam tu kva karma kāraṇam atra āha yathā paṅka ākhyāyām pṛthityām iti yadā paṅkasya upari manda vyavasthāpitā prastara guṭikā kramaśas paṅkena samam adhas gacchati tadā guru tva apekṣaḥ prastara paṅka saṃyogaḥ nodanam yadā prayatnena dūram utthāpya prastareṇa abhihanyate paṅkaḥ tadā guru tva prayatna vega apekṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ nodanam yadā jalena āhanyate tadā samasta apekṣaḥ saṃyogaḥ nodanam iti yathāsambhava m ūhyam iti 
NK_248.7	 vega apekṣaḥ yaḥ saṃyogaḥ ekasya vibhāga kṛtaḥ karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam saḥ abhighātaḥ abhighātya abhighātakayoḥ paraspara vibhāgaḥ yatas karmaṇaḥ jāyate tasya eva ekasya hetuḥ yaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ saḥ abhighātaḥ tasmāt api caturṣu mahābhūteṣu karma bhavati yathā pāṣāṇa ādiṣu niṣṭhure vastuni abhipatiteṣu nodanam paraspara avibhāga hetoḥ eva ekasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam na paraspara vibhāga hetoḥ evam abhighātaḥ api paraspara vibhāga hetoḥ eva ekasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam na paraspara avibhāga hetoḥ idam uktam ekasya karmaṇaḥ kāraṇam 
NK_248.8	 saṃyukta saṃyogam vyācaṣṭe pāda ādibhiḥ nudyamānāyām abhihanyamānāyām vā paṅka ākhyāyām pṛthivyām yaḥ saṃyogaḥ nodana abhighātayoḥ anyatara apekṣa ubhaya apekṣaḥ vā saṃyukta saṃyogaḥ tasmāt api ye pradeśāḥ na nudyante na api abhihanyante teṣu api karma jāyate ekatra pṛthivyām pādena nudyamānāyām abhihanyamānāyām vā ye pradeśāḥ na nudyante na api abhihanyante teṣu api karma dṛśyate tatra calatām pradeśa antarāṇām nudyamāna abhihanyamāna bhū pradeśaiḥ saha saṃyukta pradeśa saṃyogaḥ kāraṇam yatra abhighātakam dravyam bhū pradeśam abhihatya kiñcid adhas nītvā utpatati tatra pradeśa antara kriyāyām ubhaya apekṣaḥ saṃyukta saṃyogaḥ tetuḥ 
NK_249.1–249.2	 pṛthivī udakayoḥ guru tva vidhāraka saṃyoga prayatna vega abhāve sati guru tvāt yat adhas gamanam tat patanam yathā musala śarīreṣu ādiṣu uktam tatra ādyam guru tvāt dvitīya ādīni tu guru tva saṃskārābhyām guru tvasya karma kāraṇa tvam āha pṛthivī udakayoḥ guru tva vidhāraka saṃyoga prayatna vega abhāve guru tvāt yat adhas gamanam tat patanam yathā musala śarīra ādiṣu uktam guru tva pratibandhakasya hasta saṃyogasya abhāve musalasya yat adhas gamanam tat patanam guru tvāt bhavati evam guru tva vidhāraka prayatna abhāveśarīrasya patanam kṣiptasya iṣoḥ antarāle vega abhāvāt patanam guru tvāt tatra ādyam karma guru tvāt dvitīya ādīni tu guru tva saṃskārābhyām teṣu musala ādiṣu ādyam karma guru tvāt bhavati tena karmaṇā saṃskāraḥ kriyate tad anuttarottara karmāṇi guru tva saṃskārābhyām jāyante dvayoḥ api pratyekam anyatra sāmarthya avadhāraṇāt 
NK_250.1–250.2	 srotaḥ bhuotānām apām sthalān nimna abhisarpaṇam yat tat drava tvāt syandanam katham samantāt rodhaḥsmāyogena avaya vi drava tvam pratibaddham avayava drava tvam api ekārtha samavetam tena eva pratibaddham uttara uttara avayava drava tvāni saṃyukta saṃyogaiḥ pratibaddhāni yadā tu mātrayā setu bhedaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati tadā samantāt pratibaddha tvāt avayavi drava tvasya karī ā ārambhaḥ na asti setu samīpa sthasya avayava drava tvasya uttayottreṣām avayava drava tvānām pratibamdhaka abhāvāt vṛtti lābhaḥ tatas kramaśas saṃyuktānām eva abhisarpaṇam tatas pūrva dravya vināśe sati prabandhena avasthitaiḥ avayavaiḥ dīrgham drama ārabhyate tatra ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrva krameṇa drava tvam utpadyate tatra ca kāraṇānām saṃyuktānām prabandhena gamane yad avayavini karma utpadyate tat syandana ākhyam iti 
NK_250.3^1	 drava tvasya kāraṇa tvam kathayati srotaḥ bhūtānām apām sthalān nimna abhisarpaṇam yat tat drava tvāt syandanam apām yat nimna abhi sarpaṇam tat syandanam drava tvāt upajāyate iti arthaḥ katham iti praśnaḥ samantāt iti uttaram samantāt sarvatas rodhaḥ saṃyoge kūla saṃyoge sati avayavinaḥ drava tvam pratibaddham syandanam na karoti avayava drava tvam api ekārtha samavesam tena eva pratibaddham yasmin= avayave sākṣāt rodhaḥ saṃyogaḥ asti tad avayava gatam drava tvam tena eva rodhaḥ saṃyogena pratibaddham uttarottarāṇi tu avayava drava tvāni saṃyukta saṃyogaiḥ pratibaddhāni rodhaḥ saṃyuktena avayavena saha saṃyogāt avayava antarasya drava tvam pratibaddham iti
