NK_250.3^2	 tad saṃyogāt aparasya pratibaddham iti enena eva nyāyena uttarottara drava tvāni pratibaddhāni pratibaddhāni yadi tu mātrayā setu bhedaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati tadā samantāt pratibaddhasya avayavi drava tvasya kārya ārambhaḥ na asti dīrghatareṇa setunā samantāt pratibaddhasya avayavinaḥ mahā parimāṇasya eka deśa kṛtena alpīyasā mārgeṇa nirgama abhāvāt setu samīpa sthasya tu avayava drava tvasya vṛtti lābhaḥ bhavati alpasya avayavasya tena mārgeṇa nirgati sambhavāt tasya vṛtti lābhe ca uttareṣām avayava drava tvānām api pratibandhaka abhāvāt vṛtti lābhaḥ sva kārya kartṛ tvam syāḥ 
NK_250.4	 tatas kramaśas saṃyuktānām evabhisarpaṇam setu samīpa sthaḥ avayavaḥ prathamam abhisarpati tadanu tad samīpa sthaḥ tatas tad samīpa sthaḥ iti anena krameṇa sarve avayavāḥ abhisarpanti te ca abhisarpantaḥ na paraspara bhinna deśāḥ abhisarpanti kim tu tathā abhisarpanti yathā paraspara saṃyuktāḥ bhavanti iti etat avat yotana artham uktam saṃyuktānām eva abhisarpaṇam na punar asya ayam arthaḥ apracyuta prācya saṃyogānām eva abhisarpaṇam iti saṃsthāna antara upalambhāt tatas prāktana saṃyoga vināśe pūrva dvavya vināśe prabandhena avasthitaiḥ avayavaiḥ saṃyuktībhāvena avasthītaiḥ avayavaiḥ dīrgham dravyam ārabhyate yatra ca kāraṇa guṇa pūrva prakrameṇa krava tvam utpadyate avayava drava tvebhyaḥ dīrghatare avayavini drava tvam utpadyate tatra ca kāraṇānām saṃyuktānām prabandhena gamane yad avayavini karma utpadyate drava tvāt tat syāndanam tatra tasmin drava tve utpanne sati kāraṇānām avayavānām prabandhena gamane paṅktībhāvena abhinna deśa tayā gamane yat avayavini drava tvāt karma utpadyate tat syandana ākhyam 
NK_251.1–251.2^1	 saṃskārāt karma iṣu ādiṣūvatam tathā cakra ādiṣu avayavānām pārśvatas pratiniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga utpattau yat avayavinaḥ saṃskārāt aniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga nimittam karma tat bhramaṇam iti evamādayāḥ gamana viśeṣāḥ saṃskārāt karmeṣu ādiṣu uktam tathā cakra ādiṣu tathā śabdaḥ yathāśabdam apekṣate yat tadoḥ nitya sambandhāt yathā iṣu ādiṣu saṃskārāt karma kathitam tathā cakra ādiṣu api bhavati iti arthaḥ etat eva darśayati avayavānām pārśvatas pratiniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga utpattau yat avayavinaḥ saṃskārāt aniyata diś deśa saṃyoga vibhāga nimittam karma tat bhramaṇam 
NK_251.1–251.2^2	 pārśvatas pratiniyatāḥ ye diś deśāḥ taiḥ saha avayavānām vibhāga saṃyogayārutpattau satyām yat avayavinaḥ saṃskārāt aniyata diś deśaiḥ sarvatodikkaiḥ vibhāga saṃyogayoḥ nimittam karma jāyate tad bhramaṇam prathamam cakra avayavini daṇḍa saṃyogāt karma utpadyate uttarottarāṇi karṃāṇi nodanāt abhighātāt karma jāt saṃskārāt ca bhavanti evam vegāda daṇḍa saṃyukte cakra avayave ādyam karma daṇḍa saṃyogāt avayava antareṣu ca saṃyukta saṃyogāt daṇḍa saṃyuktasya avayavasya uttarottara karmāṇi saṃskārān nodanāt ca apareṣām saṃskārāt saṃyukta saṃyogāt ca daṇḍa vigame tu cakre tad avayaveṣu ca saṃskārāt eva kevalāt upasaṃharati evamādayaḥ gamana viśeṣāḥ iti 
NK_252.1–252.2	 prāṇa ākhye tu vāyau karma ātma vāyu saṃyogāt icchā dveṣa prayatna apekṣāt jāgrate icchā anuvidhāna darśanāt suptasya tu jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt prāṇa ākhye vāyau karma ātma vāyu saṃyogāt icchā dveṣa prayatna apekṣāt jāgrataḥ puruṣasya prāṇa ākhye vāyau karma icchā du eṣa pūrvaka prayatnāt bhavati iti katham idam jñātamaraḥ āha icchā anuvidhāna darśanāt recaka pūraka ādi prayogeṣu icchā anudhāyinī prāṇa kriyā upalabhyate nāsā randhra praviṣṭe rajasi tad nirāsa artham prāṇa kriyā dveṣāt api bhavati atas prayatna pūrvikā iti avagamyate suptasya jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt ātma vāyu saṃyogāt prāṇa kriyā suptasya prāṇa kriyā prayatna kāryā prāṇa kriyā tvāt jāgrataḥ prāṇa kriyāvat sa vā icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ na bhavati suptasya icchā dveṣayoḥ abhāvāt tasmāt jīvana pūrvakaḥ eva niścīyate prāṇa dhāraṇasya tad pūrvaka tvāt 
NK_253.1–253.2	 ākāśa kāla diś ātmanām sati api dravya bhāve niṣkriya tvam sāmānya ādi vat amūrta tvāt mūrtiḥ asarva gata dravya parimāṇam tad anuvidhāyinī ca kriyā sā ca ākāśa ādiṣu na asti tasmāt na teṣām kriyā sambandhaḥ asti iti caturṣu mahābhūteṣu iva ākāśa ādiṣu kasmāt kriyā utpattiḥ na cintyate iti atas āha ākāśa kāla diś ātmanām sati api dravya bhāve niṣkriya tvam sāmānya ādi vat amūrta tvāt kriyāvat tvam mūrta tvena vyāptam mūrta tvam ca ākāśa ādiṣu na asti atas kriyāvat tvam api na vidyate iti arthaḥ etat eva vivṛṇoti mūrtiḥ ityādinā tad vyaktam 
NK_254.1–254.2	 sa vigrahe manasi indriyantara sambandha artham jāgrataḥ karma ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt icchā dveṣa pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt anvabhiprāyam indriya antareṇa viṣaya antara upalabdhi darśanāt suptasya prabodha kāle jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt apasarpaṇa karma upasarpaṇa karma ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt adṛṣṭa apekṣāt katham yadā jīvana sahakāriṇoḥ dharmayoḥ upabhogāt prakṣayaḥ anyonya abhibhavaḥ vā tadā jīvana sahāyayoḥ vaikalye tad pūrvaka prayatma vaikalyāt prāṇa nirodhe sati anyābhyām labdha vṛttibhyām dharma adharmābhyām ātma manaḥ saṃyoga sahāyābhyām mṛta śarīrāt vibhāga kāraṇam apasarpaṇa karma utpadyate 
NK_254.3–254.4	 tatas śarīrāt bahis apagatam tābhyām eva dharma adharmābhyām samutpannena ativāhika śarīreṇa sambadhyate tad saṃkrāntam ca svargam narakam vā gatvā āśaya anurūpeṇa śarīreṇa sambaddhyate tad saṃyoga artham karma upasarpaṇam iti yoginām ca bahis udrecitasya manasaḥ abhipreta deśa gamanam pratyāgamanam ca tathā sarga kāle pratyagreṇa śarīreṇa sambandha artham karma adṛṣṭa kāritam 
NK_254.5–254.6	 evam anyat api mahābhūteṣu yat pratyakṣa anumānābhyām anupalabhyamāna kāraṇam upakāra apakāra samartham tat api adṛṣṭa kāritam yathā sarga ādau= aṇu karma agni vāyvoḥ ūrdhva tiryak gamane mahābhūtānām prakṣobhaṇam abhiṣiktānām maṇīnām taskaram prati gamana ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhisarpaṇam ca iti iti praśasta pāda bhāṣye karma padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_254.7	 manasi karma kāraṇam āha sa vigrahaḥ iti jāgrataḥ paruṣasya sa vigrahe manasi sa śarīre manasi indriya antara sambandha artham karma ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt icchā dveṣa pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt bhavati icchā dveṣa pūrvakaḥ prayatnaḥ jāgrataḥ manaḥ kriyā hetuḥ iti katham etat avagatam tatra āha anvabhiprāyam indriya antareṇa viṣaya upalabdhi darśanāt jāgara avasthāyām abhiprāya anatikrameṇa indriya antareṇa cakṣuḥ ādinā viṣaya upalabdhiḥ dṛśyate yadā pūram jighṛkṣati puruṣaḥ tadā pūram paśyati yadā rasam jighṛkṣate tadā rasam rasayati na ca antaḥkaraṇa sambandham antareṇa bādya indriya viṣaya grahaka tvam asti tasmāt icchā dveṣa pūrvakāt prayatnāt manasi kriyā bhūta iti gamyate suptasya prabodha kāle jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt suptasya puruṣasya indriya antara sambandha artham prabodha kāle manasi kriyā jīvana pūrvaka prayatna apekṣāt ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt 
NK_254.8^1	 apasarpaṇa upasarpaṇa karma ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogāt adṛṣṭa apekṣāt upajāyate etat eva katham ityādinā praśna pūrvakam kathayati viśiṣṭa ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ jīvanam tasya sva kārya karaṇe dharma adharmau sahakāriṇau yadā tayoḥ upabhogāt praksāyaḥ vināśaḥ anyonya abhibhavaḥ vā paraspara pratibandhāt sva kārya akaraṇam vā tatas jīvana sahāyayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ vaikalye abhāve sati tad pūrvaka prayatna vaikalyāt jīvana pūrvakasya prayatnasya vaikalyāt abhāvāt prāṇa vāyoḥ nirodhe sati patitetasmin śarīre yābhyām dharma adharmābhyām deha antare phalam bhojayitavyam tau labdha vṛttikau bhūta avaihika śarīra upabhogya dharma adharma arati baddha tvāt deha antara bhogyābhyām dharma adharmābhyām kāryam na kṛtam 
NK_254.8^2	 yadā tu aihika śarīra upabhogyau dharma adharmau prakṣīṇau tadā deha antara upabhogyayoḥ dharma adharmayoḥ vṛtti lābhaḥ pratibandha abhāvaḥ jātaḥ tābhyām labdha vṛttibhyāmaihika deha upabhogyāt karmaṇaḥ a nyābhyām ātma manaḥ saṃyoga sahāyābhyāṃmṛta śarīrāt manasaḥ vibhāga kāraṇam apasarpaṇa karma utpadyate apasarpaṇa karma utpattau= ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ asamavāyi kāraṇam manaḥ samavāyi kāraṇam labdha vṛttī dharma adharmau nimitta kāraṇam tatas tad anantaram tat manaḥ mṛta śarītāt bahis nirgatam tābhyām eva labdha vṛttibhyām dharma adharmābhyām sakāśāt utpannena ativāhika śarīreṇa sambaddhyate 
NK_254.8^3	 tad saṃkrāntam tadā ativāhika śarīra saṃkrāntam manaḥ svargam narakam vā gacchati tatra gatvā āśya anurūpeṇa karma anurūpeṇa śarīreṇa sambaddhyate svarge narake vā yat upajātam śarīram tatra tāvat manaḥ sambandhena bhavitavyam anyathā tasmin deśe bhoga asambhavāt na ca ātma vat agatvā eva manasaḥ deha antara sambandhaḥ asti avyāpaka tvāt gamanam ca tasya etāvat dūram kevalasya na sambhavati mahāpralaya anantara avasthā vyatirekeṇa aśarīrasya manasaḥ karma abhāvāt tasmāt mṛta śarīra pratyāsannam adṛṣṭa vaśāt upajāta kriyaiḥ aṇubhiḥ dvi aṇuka ādi prakrameṇa ārabdham ati sūkṣmam anupalabdhi yogyam śarīram parikalpyate 
NK_254.8^4	 tat ca mṛta śarīram atikramya manasaḥ svarga naraka ādi deśaṃprativahana dharmaka tvāt ātivāhikam iti ucyate maraṇa janmanoḥ antarāle manasaḥ karma śarīra upagṛhītasya eva utpadyate mahāpralaya anantara avasthā bhā vi manaḥ karma vyatirikta tve sati manaḥ karma tvāt dṛśyamāna śarīra vṛtti manaḥ karma vat āgamaśaca atra saṃvādakaḥ dṛśyamāna śarīra vṛtti manaḥ karma vat āgamaḥ ca atra saṃvādakaḥ dṛśyate iti tad saṃyoga artham ca karma upasarpaṇam iti tena svarge narake vā pratyagra jātena śarīreṇa manaḥ saṃyoga artham karma upasarpaṇam iti 
NK_254.9–254.11	 yoginām ca bahis udrecitasya vahiḥ niḥsāritasya manasaḥ abhipreta deśa gamanam pratyaāgamanam ca tathā sarga kāle pratyagreṇa śarīreṇa sambandha artham samaḥ karma adṛṣṭa kāritam na kevalam etāvat sarvam anyat api mahābhūteṣu yat pratyakṣā mānābhyām anupalabhyamāna kāraṇam upakāra apakāra samartham tat api adṛṣṭa kāritam yathā sarga ādau= aṇu karma agni vāyvoḥ yathāsaṃkhyam ūrdhva tiryak gamane mahābhūtānām bhū golaka ādīnām ca prakṣobhaṇam calanam parīkṣā kāle abhiṣiktānām maṇīnām taskaram prati gamanam ayasaḥ ayaskānta abhisarpaṇam ca sarvam etat adṛṣṭa kāritam iti hita ahita phala upāya prāpti tyāga nibandhanam karma iti paramam tattvam yatnatas kriyatām hṛdi iti bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhara kṛtāyām padārtha praveśa nyāya kanda līṭīkāyām karma padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_255.1–255.3	 sāmānyam dvividham param aparam ca sva viṣaya sarva gatam abheda ātmakam aneka vṛtti eka dvi bahuṣu ātma svarūpa anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam svarūpa abhedena ādhāreṣu prabandhena vartamānam anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam katham pratipiṇḍam sāmānya apekṣam prabandhena jñāna utpattau= abhyāsa pratyaya jatitāt ca saṃskārāt atīta jñāna prabandha pratyavekṣaṇāt yat anugatam asti tad sāmānyam iti jayanti jagat utpatti sthiti saṃhṛti hetavaḥ viśvasya paramātmānaḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ 
NK_255.4^1	 sāmānyam vyācaṣṭe dvividham sāmānyam parama param ca iti kṛta vyākhyānam etat uddeśa avasare sarvam sarva gatam sāmānyam iti kecid tad niṣedha artham āha sva viṣaya sarva gatam iti yat sāmānyam yatra piṇḍe pratīyate sa tasya svaḥ viṣayaḥ tatra sarvasmin gatam samavetam sarvatra tad pratyayāt sarva sarva gata tva abhāve tu anupalabdhiḥ eva pramāṇam abheda ātmakam abhinna svabhāvam yena svabhāvena ekatra piṇḍe vartate sāmānyam tena eva svabhāvena piṇḍa antare api vartate tad pratyaya aviśeṣāt iti arthaḥ anekeṣu piṇḍeṣu vṛttiḥ yasya tad aneka vṛtti abhinna svabhāvam anekatra vartate iti ca pratīti sāmarthyāt samarthanīyam na hi pramāṇa avagate arthe kācid anupapattiḥ nāma 
NK_255.4^2	 dvi tva ādikam api abhinna svabhāvam anekatra vartate tasmāt sāmānyasya viśeṣaḥ na labhyate tatra āha eka dvi bahuṣu ātma svarūpa anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam iti sāmānyam ekasmin piṇḍe dvayoḥ piṇḍayoḥ bahuṣu vā piṇḍeṣu ātma svarūpa anugama pratyayam karoti ekasya piṇḍasya dvayoḥ bahūnām api upalambhe gauḥ iti pratyayasya bhāvāt dvi tva ādikam tu evam na bhavati iti viśeṣaḥ aneka vṛtti t tve sati yat eka dvi bahuṣu ātma svarūpa anugama pratyaya kāraṇam tat sāmānyam iti lakṣaṇa arthaḥ etat eva vivṛṇoti svarūpa abhedena iti ekasmin piṇḍe yat sva rūpam tad piṇḍa antare api tasmāt abhedena ādhāreṣu prabandhena anuparameṇa pūrva pūrva piṇḍa aparityāgena vartamānam yat anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam sva ātma svarūpa anugama pratīti kāraṇam sāmānyam 
NK_255.5	 katham iti parasya praśnaḥ katham anekeṣu piṇḍeṣu sāmānyasya vṛttiḥ avagamyate iti arthaḥ uttaram āha pratipiṇḍam iti piṇḍam piṇḍam prati sāmānya apekṣam yathā bhavati tathā jñāna utpattau satyām yaḥ abhyāsa pratyayaḥ tena yaḥ saṃskāraḥ janinaḥ yasmāt atītasya jñāna prabandhasya jñāna pravāhasya pratyavekṣaṇāt smaraṇāt yat anugatam asti tad sāmānyam kim uktam syāt ekasmin piṇḍe sāmānyam upalabhya piṇda antare tasya pratyabhijñānāt ekasya aneka vṛtti tvam avagamyate atas eva atra bādhaka hetavaḥ pratyakṣa virodhāt apāsyante 
NK_256.1	 tatra sattā sāmānyam param anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam eva yathā paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu carma vastra kambala ādiṣu ekasmāt nīla dravya abhisambandhāt nīlam nīlam iti pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ tathā paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu dravya guṇa karmasu aviśiṣṭā sat sat iti pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ sā ca artha antarāt sambandhāt bhavitum arhati iti yat tad artha antaram sā sattā iti siddhāḥ sattā anusambandhāt sat sat iti pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ tasmāt sā sāmānyam eva 
NK_256.2	 yat pūrvam uktam parama param ca dvividham sāmānyam iti tat idānīm vivicya kathayati tatra param sattā sāmānyam anuvṛtti pratyaya kāraṇam eva yadi api pratyakṣeṇa pratīyate sattā tathā api vipratipannam pratyanumānam āha yathā paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu iti tad vyaktam dravya ādiṣu sat saditi pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ vyatirikta pratyaya nibandhanā bhinneṣu pratyaya anuvṛtti tvāt carma vastra ādiṣu nīla pratyaya anuvṛtti vat yasmāt sattā triṣu dravya ādiṣu pratyaya anuvṛtim karoti na vyāvṛttim tasmānyam eva na viśeṣaḥ iti upasaṃhāra arthaḥ 
NK_257.1	 aparam dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādi anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca bhavati tatra dravya tvam paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetutvāt sāmānyam guṇa karmabhyaḥ vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetutvāt viśeṣaḥ tathā guṇa tvam paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu rūpa ādiṣu anuvṛtti hetu tvāt sāmānyam dravya karmabhyaḥ vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ tathā karma tvam paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam dravya guṇebhyaḥ vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ 
NK_257.2–257.3	 evam pṛthivī tva rūpatva utkṣepaṇa tva go tva ghaṭa tva paṭa tva ādīnām api prāṇi aprāṇi gatānām anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ etāni dravya tva ādīni prabhūta viṣaya tvāt prādhānyena sāmānyāni sva āśraya viśeṣaka tvāt bhaktyā viśeṣa ākhyāni iti aparam dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādi anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ ca bhavati dravya tva dravyeṣu anuvatti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam guṇa karmabhyaḥ vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ guṇa tvam guṇeṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam dravya karmabhyaḥ vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ tathā karma tvam paraspara viśiṣṭeṣu utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu anuvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānyam dravya guṇebhyaḥ vyāvṛtti hetu tvāt viśeṣaḥ 
NK_257.4	 dravya tva ādi vat pṛthivī tva ādīnām api anuvṛtti vyāvṛtti pratyaya hetu tvāt sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvaḥ asti iti āha evam iti prāṇi gatāni sāmānyāni go tva aśva tva ādīni prāṇi gatāni ghaṭa tva paṭa tva ādīni kim dravya tva ādīnām sāmānya rūpa tvam vāstavam kim vā viśeṣa rūpa tā āhosvit ubhaya rūpa tā atra āha etāni iti samānānām bhāvaḥ sāmānyam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇam dravya tva ādiṣu vidyate sva āśrayam sarvatas viśinaṣṭī iti viśeṣaḥ iti tu lakṣaṇam na asti atas etāni mukhyayā vṛttyā sāmānyāni eva na viśeṣāḥ viśeṣa saṃjñām tu upacāreṇa labhante viśeṣaḥ hi sva āśrayam sarvatas viśinaṣṭi dravya tva ādikam api vijātīyebhyaḥ sva āśrayasya viśeṣakam iti etāvatā sādharmyeṇa upacāra pravṛttiḥ 
NK_258.1–258.2	 lakṣaṇa bhedāt eṣām dravya guṇa karmabhyaḥ padārtha antara tvam siddham atas eva ca nitya yvam dravya tva ādīni dravya ādi vyatiriktāni na bhavanti atas teṣām pṛthakkārya nirūpaṇam anyāyyam iti atra āha lakṣaṇa bhedāt iti anugata ākāra buddhi vedyāni dravya tva ādīni vyāvṛtti buddhi vedyāḥ ca dravya ādi vyaktayaḥ tasmāt eṣām dravya tva ādīnām lakṣaṇa bhedāt pratīti bhedāt dravya guṇa karmabhyaḥ padārtha antara tvam atas eva ca nitya tvam yatas eva sāmānyasya dravya ādibhyaḥ bhedaḥ atas eva nitya tvam dravya ādi abhede sāmānyasya dravya ādi vināśe vināśaḥ tad utpāde ca utpādaḥ syāt bhede tu na ayam vidhiḥ avatiṣṭhate iti 
NK_259.1^1	 atra eke vadanti bhinneṣu anugatā buddhiḥ sāmānyam vyavasthāpayati sā ca pratipiṇḍam na svatantre sāa anya viśeṣa lakṣaṇe dve vastunī pratibhāsayati na api tayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ gotvavān iti evam anudayāt kim tu tādātmya grāhiṇī pratītiḥ iyam gauḥ ayam iti eka ātma tā aparāmarśāt ubhayoḥ anyonya prahāṇena svarūpa antara abhāvāt ca anuvṛtta tā hi go tvasya iva sāmānya antarasya api sva rūpam vyāvṛtta tā api go vyakteḥ iva vyakti antarāṇām api svabhāvaḥ sāmānya antara vyāvṛttam tu go tvasya sva rūpam vyakti antara vyāvṛttiḥ ca go vyakteḥ svabhāvaḥ paraspara ātma tām antareṇa anyonyam na śakyate nirdeṣṭum na ca tasya saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva ca sambandhi iti upapadyate niḥsvabhāvasya sambandha abhāvāt 
NK_259.1^2	 tasmāt jāti vyaktyoḥ paraspara ātma tā eva tattvam evam sati bheda abheda vādaḥ api siddhyati yathā hi śābaleyaḥ gauḥ iti evam pratīyate tathā bāhuleyaḥ api na ca asti kasyacid bādhaḥ śābaleyaḥ eva gauḥ na bāhuleyaḥ iti kintu sarveṣām ekam ati tvam eva asa gauḥ ayam api gauḥ iti a tatra pratīti balena śābaleya ātmakasya go tvasya bāhuleya ātmaka tve siddhe śābaleyāt bhedaḥ api siddhyati ayam eva hi sāmānyasya pūrva piṇḍāt bhedaḥ yat piṇḍa antarātmaka tvam idam eva ca sāmānya rūpa tvam yat ubhaya ātmaka tvam bheda abhedau= ekasya viruddhau iti ced na yukti jñasya bhavataḥ sāmpratam etat abhidhātum tad viruddham yatra buddhiḥ viparyasyati yat tu sarvadā pramāṇena tathā eva pratīyate tatra virodha abhidhānam eva viruddham 
NK_259.2	 anyatra evam na dṛṣṭam iti ced kim vai pratyakṣam api anumānam iva dṛṣṭam anusarati hatam tarhi idam anavasthayā atha idam sva sāmarthyāt pravartate tadā yathā yat vastu yat darśayati tathā eva tat na tu etat anyatra adarśanena pratyākhyānam arhati sarva bhāva pratyākhyāna prasaṅgāt tasmāt sāmānyam vyakti utpāda vināśayoḥ utpāda vināśavat tvāt vyakti antara avasthāne ca avasthānāt nityam anityam ca na punar nityam eva 
NK_259.3	 evam prāpte abhidhīyate kim jāti vyaktyoḥ avilakṣaṇam ākāram gṛhṇatī pratītiḥ tayoḥ abhedam gṛhṇāti āhosvit paraspara vilakṣaṇau= ākārau ādye kalpe tāvat ekam eva vastu syāt na ubhayoḥ eka ātmaka tvam avilakṣaṇākār abuddhi vedya tvasya abheda lakṣaṇa tvāt dvitīye tu kalpe vyāhatiḥ eva vilakṣaṇa ākāra saṃvittiḥ eva hi bheda saṃvittiḥ tasyāḥ sambhave sati tayoḥ abheda pratipattiḥ eva na asti katham bhinnayoḥ abhedaḥ vyavasthāpyate katham tarhi tādātmya pratītiḥ na kathañcid iti vadāmaḥ 
NK_259.4	 yadi tāvat ekaḥ ākāraḥ anubhūyate ekasya eva vastunaḥ pratītiḥ iyam na ubhayoḥ atha dvau= ākārau anubhūyete tadā asyāḥ pratīteḥ asambhavaḥ eva yat punar gauḥ iti ayam avibhāgena saṃvedanam tad samavāya sāmarthyāt saṃyoge hi dvayoḥ saṃsarga avabhāsaḥ samavāyasya punar eṣa mahimā yat atra sambandhinā āvayaḥ piṇḍa vahni vat piṇḍībhūtau eva pratīyete jātiḥ eva ca vyakteḥ sva rūpam tena sati api bhede badara ādi vat kuṇḍasya jātitaḥ vyakteḥ svarūpam pṛthak na niṣkṛṣyate paraspara parihāreṇa tu upalambhaḥ asti eva dūre go tva agrahaṇe api piṇḍasya grahaṇāt pūrva piṇḍa agrahaṇe api piṇḍa antare go tva grahaṇāt tasmāt vyakteḥ atyantam bhinnam eva sāmānyam iti tārkikāṇām praktiyā 
NK_260.1–260.4	 dravya ādiṣu vṛtti niyamāt pratyaya bhedāt ca parasparataḥ ca anya tvam pratyekam sva āśrayeṣu lakṣaṇa aviśeṣāt viśeṣa lakṣaṇa avāt ca eka tvam yadi api aparicchinna deśāni sāmānyāni tathā api upalakṣaṇa niyamāt kāraṇa sāmagrī niyamāt ca sva viṣaya sarva gatāni antarāle ca saṃyoga samavāya vṛtti abhāvāt avyapadeśyāni iti iti praśasta pāda bhāśye sāmānya padārthaḥ samāptaḥ dravya ādiṣu vṛtti niyamāt pratyaya bhedāt ca parasparataḥ ca anya tvam dravya tva ādayaḥ pratyekam dravya ādiṣu eva niyatāḥ pratyaya bhedāḥ ca eteṣu dṛśyante tasmāt dravya ādiṣu vṛtti niyamāt pratyaya bhedāt ca dravya tva ādīnām parasparataḥ bhedaḥ 
NK_260.5	 abheda ātmakam sāmānyam iti pūrvam pratijñā mātreṇa uktam tat idānīm pramāṇa siddham tasya karoti pratyekam sva āśrayeṣu lakṣaṇa aviśeṣāt viśeṣa lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ca eka tvam lakṣyate anena iti lakṣaṇam anugata ākāram jñānam pratyekam pratipiṇḍam aviśeṣāt vailakṣaṇya abhāvāt viśeṣe bhede lakṣaṇasya pramāṇasya abhāvāt ca sāmānyasya sva āśrayeṣu eka tvam abhinna svabhāva tvam iti arthaḥ 
NK_260.6	 sva viṣaye sarvatra sāmānyam samavaiti na anyatra iti yat pūrvam uktam tatra kāraṇam āha yadi api iti yadi api sāmānyāni yatra tatra upajāyamānena piṇḍena sambandhāt aparicchinna deśa ani a niyata deśāni tathā api upalakṣaṇasya abhivyañjakasya avayava saṃsthāna viśeṣasya niyamān niyata tvāt piṇḍa utpādaka kāraṇa sāmagrī niyamāt ca sva viṣaye sarvatra samavayanti na anyatra iti 
NK_261.1	 etat uktam bhavati sāsnādi saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ go tvasya vyañjakaḥ kesara ādi saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ aśva tvasya viśiṣṭa grīvā ādi saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ ghaṭa tvasya pratīti niyamāt ete ca saṃsthāna viśeṣāḥ na sarveṣu piṇḍeṣu sādhāraṇāḥ api tu pratiniyateṣu bhavanti tatra yadi api sarvam sāmānyam sarvatra upajāyamānena sva viṣayeṇa iva piṇḍa antareṇa api sambaddhum kṣamate tathā api yasya abhivyañjakam yatra piṇḍe sambhavati tasya tatra eva samavāyaḥ na anyatra evam sāmagrī niyamāt api sāmānya sambandha niyamaḥ eṣa hi tantu ādīnām kāraṇānām svabhāvaḥ yat etaiḥ utpādyamāṇe dravye paṭa tvam eva samavaiti na anyat eṣa hi mṛd piṇḍa ādīnām mahimā yattaiḥ kriyāmāṇe dravye ghaṭa tvam eva samavaiti na anyat 
NK_261.2	 na tāvat sāmānyam anyatas gatvā anyatra sambadhyate niṣkriya tvāt tatra api yadi pūrvam na āsīt tatra upajāyamānena piṇḍena asya sambandhaḥ na syāt dṛśyate ca sarvatra upajāyamānena piṇḍena sambandhaḥ tasmāt sarvam sarvatra asti iti kasyacid matam tat nirākurvan āha antarāle saṃyoga samavāya vṛtti abhāvāt avyapadeśyāni iti antarālam iti ākāśam vā diś dravyam vā stimita vāyuḥ vā mūrtta dravya abhāvaḥ vaḥ teṣu go tva ādi sāmānyānām na saṃyogaḥ na api samavāyaḥ na ca asambaddhānām eva teṣām avasthāne pramāṇam asti atas antarāle na sāmānyāni vyapadiśyante na santi iti arthaḥ katham tarhi tatra upajāyamānena piṇḍena sambadhyante kāraṇa sāmarthyāt saṃyogaḥ hi anyatas samāgatasya bhavati tatra eva avasthitasya vā bhavati tasmāt vilakṣaṇaḥ tu samavāyaḥ yatra yatra eva piṇḍa utpattau kāraṇāni vyāpriyante tatra tatra eva kāraṇānām sāmarthyāt piṇḍe anyatas anāgatasya tatra sthitasya api sāmānyasya bhavati vastu śakteḥ aparyanuyojya tvāt 
NK_262.1^1	 atra āhuḥ saugatāḥ pratīyamāneṣu bhedeṣu maṇi sūtra vat ekasya ākārasya anupalambhāt sāmānyam na asti eva iti tat ayuktam anekāsu go vyaktiṣu anubhūyamānāsu aśva ādi vyakti vilakṣaṇa tayā sāmānya ākāra pratīti sambhavāt yadi śābaleya ādiṣu paraspara bhinneṣu ekam anuvṛttam na kiñcid asti yathā gavāśu avyaktayaḥ paraspara vilakṣaṇāḥ saṃvedyante tathā go vyaktayaḥ api saṃvedyāḥ syuḥ yathā vā go vyaktayaḥ sarūpāḥ pratīyante tathā gavāśu avyaktayaḥ api pratīyeran viśeṣa abhāvāt niyamena tu go vyaktayaḥ pratīyamānāḥ sarūpāḥ sva varga sādhāraṇam aśva ādi vyāvṛttam kiñcid ekam rūpam āpakṣipanti eka artha kriyā kāri tvāt eka hetu tvāt vā 
NK_262.1^2	 go vyaktīnām eka tvam iti ced na asati sāmānye vyaktīnām iva vyakti hetūnām vyakti kāryāṇām api paraspara vyāvṛttānām eka tvāt kiñca yat eka hetu tvāt ekatvam bhinna kāraṇa prabhavāṇām vyaktīnām eka tvam na syāt dṛśyate ca abhinna svabhāvānām api kāraṇa bhedaḥ yathā vahneḥ dāru nirmathanāt vidyutaḥ āditya gabhasti kṣobhitāt sūryakāntāt api maṇeḥ utpattiḥ eka kārya tvāt ekatve ca vijātīyānām api ekatva āpattiḥ dṛṣṭāḥ hi vāha dohana ādi kriyā gavā ādi vyaktīnām iva mahiṣī ādi vyaktīnām api yā ca gauḥ na duhyate na ca vāhyate sā gauḥ na syāt 
NK_262.2^1	 api ca sāmānya abhāve kaḥ arthaḥ śabda saṃsarga viṣayaḥ na tāvat sva lakṣaṇam tasya kṣaṇikasya sarvatas vyāvṛttasya saṅketa viṣaya tva abhāvāt na api vikalpaḥ śabda arthaḥ tasya api kṣaṇika tvāt asā dhāraṇa tvāt ca vikalpa ākāraḥ śabda arthaḥ iti ced kim vikalpa ākāraḥ vikalpa vyatiriktaḥ avyatiriktaḥ vā yadi bhinnaḥ sa kim sarva vikalpa sādhāraṇaḥ kim vā prativikalpam bhidyate sādhāraṇa tve tāvat etasya sāmānyāt abhedaḥ yadi param tava jñāna dharmaḥ ayam asmākam ca arthaa dharma bahirmukha tayā pratīyamāna tvāt iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
NK_262.2^2	 yadi vyatiriktaḥ ayam ākāraḥ pratijñānam bhidyate athavā jñānāt avyatiriktaḥ eva ubhayathā api na śabda saṃsarga yogya tā jñāna vat aśakya saṅketa tvāt vikalpaḥ pāramparyeṇa tad utpatti pratibandhāt bāhya ātma tayā su a ākāram āropya vikalpayati tatra ayam śabda saṃsargaḥ iti ced bāhya tvena āropitaḥ vikalpa ākāra vikalpa eka adhīna svabhāva tvāt vikalpe jāyamāne jāyamānaḥ iva vinaśyati vinaśyan iva pratīyamānaḥ prativikalpam bhinnaḥ eva avatiṣṭhate na ca bheda anupātinī saṅketa pravṛttiḥ iti uktam 
NK_262.3	 atha ucyate yādṛśam ekaḥ go vikalpe bāhya ātma tayā sva pratibhāsam āropayati go vikalpa antaram api tādṛśam eva āropayati vikalpāḥ ca pratyekam su a ākāra mātra grāhiṇaḥ na paraspara āropitānām ākārāṇām bheda grahaṇāya paryāpnuvanti tasya ubhaya grahaṇa adhīna tvāt tad agrahaṇāt ca vikalpa āropitānām ākārāṇām eka tvam aropya vikalpānām ekaḥ viṣayaḥ iti ucyate tat eva ca sāmānyam bahis āropitebhyaḥ vikalpa ākārebhyaḥ atyanta bheda abhāvena abhāva rūpam sva lakṣaṇa jñāna tad ākāra āropita aiḥ caturbhiḥ sahābhiḥ samasya arddha pañcama ākāraḥ iti ucyamānam āropita bāhya tva śabda abhidheyam śabda saṃsarga viṣayaḥ tad adhyavasāyaḥ eva sva lakṣaṇa adhyavasāyaḥ tad ātma tayā tasya samāropāt anya vyāvṛtti svabhāvam bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇam ca idam gauḥ asti na asti iti prayogāt bhāva ātmaka tve hi asya gauḥ asti iti prayoga asambhavaḥ punar ukta tvāt na asti iti ca na prayujyate virodhāt evam tasya abhāva ātmaka tve na asti iti punar uktam asti iti virudhyate yathā uktam 
NK_262.4–262.6	 ghaṭaḥ asti iti na vaktavyam san eva hi yatas ghaṭaḥ na asti iti api na vaktavyam virodhāt sat asat tvayoḥ iti etasmāt eva ca bhinnānām api vyaktīnām eka tā avabhāsaḥ idam hi sarveṣām eva vikalpānām viṣayaḥ asya ca ekatvāt vikalpānām api eka tvam teṣām api ekatvāt ca tad kāraṇānām pratipiṇḍa bhāvinām nirvikalpakānām api eka tvam teṣām ekātvāt ca tad kāraṇānām vyaktīnām ekatva avagamaḥ yathā uktam eka pratyavamarṣasya hetu tvāt dhīra bhedinī ekadhi hetu bhāvena vyaktīnām api abhinnatā iti 
NK_262.7	 etat api ayuktam vikalpa anupapatteḥ vikalpa ākārāṇām bheda agra laṇāt āropitam aikyam sāmānyam ācakṣate bhikṣavaḥ atra brūmaḥ kim ākārāṇām bheda agrahaṇam eva abheda samāropaḥ āhosvit abheda grahaṇam abheda āropaḥ na tāvat ādyaḥ kalpaḥ bheda samāropasya api prasaṅgāt yathā vikalpa ākārāṇām bhedaḥ na gṛhyate tadvat abhedaḥ api na gṛhyate tatra bheda agrahaṇāt abhedāra upavada bheda agrahaṇāt bheda āropasya api prasakta avabheda ucita vyavahāra pravṛtti ayogaḥ abheda grahaṇam abheda āropaḥ iti api na yuktam ātma vāde ekaḥ hi aneka darśī teṣām bheda abhedau pratyeti nairātmya vāde na ekaḥ aneka artha draṣṭā na kaścid asti vikalpānām pratyekam su a ākāra mātra niyata tvāt astu vā aneka artha darśī kaścid ekaḥ tathā api ekam nimittam antareṇa bhinneṣu ākāreṣu nābheda grahaṇam asti bhavat vā gavāśvam ahiṣa ādi ākāreṣu api bhavet aviśeṣāt 
NK_263.1–263.3	 gavā ākāreṣu api ago vyāvṛttiḥ ekam nimittam asti iti ced ke punar agāvaḥ yat vyāvṛttyā gavā ākāreṣu eka tvam ārepyate ye gāvaḥ na bhavanti te agāvaḥ iti ced gāvaḥ ke te ye agāvaḥ na bhavanti te gāvaḥ iti ced gavām svarūpe nirūpite tad vyāvṛtta tvena āgavām svarūpam nirūpyate agavām ca svarūpe nipūpite tad vyāvṛttyā gavām svarūpa nirūpaṇam iti eka apratipattau= itara apratipatteḥ ubhaya apratipattiḥ yathā āha tatrabhavān siddhaḥ ca āgauḥ apohyeta go niṣedha ātmakaḥ ca saḥ tatra gauḥ eva vaktavyaḥ nañā yaḥ pratiṣidhyate gavya siddhe tu agauḥ na asti tad abhāve tu gauḥ kutas iti 
NK_263.4	 atha anya apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ anāropita bāhya tvam tatra api ucyate kaḥ ayam apohaḥ nāma kim agoḥ apohaḥ bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā yadi bhāvaḥ sa kim gopiṇḍa svabhāvaḥ atha agopiṇḍa ātmakaḥ gopiṇḍa ātmaka tve tāvat asya asādhāraṇa tā na ca asādhāraṇe arthe śabda pravṛttiḥ iti uktam agopiṇḍa ātmaka tve api ayam eva doṣaḥ dūṣaṇa antaram ca etat adhikam yat go śabdasya agauḥ iti ayam arthaḥ prāpnoti yadi tu piṇḍa vyatiriktam aneka sādhāraṇam vastu bhūram apoha tattvam iṣyate śabda mātra viṣayā vipratipattiḥ atha apohaḥ anya vyāvṛtti rūpa tvāt abhāva svabhāvaḥ iṣyate tadā asya pratyakṣeṇa grahaṇam na syāt jñāna janakasya eva grāhya lakṣaṇa tvāt abhāvasya ca samasta artha kriyā viraha lakṣaṇa tvāt na ca pratyakṣa agṛhīte arthe saṅketa grahaṇam asti iti abhāve śabdasya apravṛttiḥ eva na ca tasmin pratīyamāne śrotuḥ artha viṣayā pravṛttiḥ syāt bhāva abhāvayoḥ anya tvāt asambandhāt ca 
NK_263.5–263.7^1	 sva lakṣaṇa ātmaka tvena abhāva pratītau= avivekena sva lakṣaṇe pravṛttiḥ iti ced yathā uktam dṛśya vikalpyau= arthau= ekīkṛtya atad sanniveśinyā bhrāntyā pravṛttiḥ pratipattṝṇām iti tat ayuktam apratīte tad ātmaka tayā abhāva samāropa anupapatteḥ na ca śrotuḥ tadānīm artha pratipattiḥ asti śabdasya ārat viṣaya tvāt pramāṇa antarasya abhāvāt asti ca śabdāt artha pratipattiḥ tasmāt na abhāvaḥ api śabda arthaḥ na ca anyat ekam nimittam kiñcid asti sarvam idam artha jātam paraspara vyāvṛttam pratikṣaṇam apūrvam anubhūyamānam na śabdāt pratīyate 
NK_263.5–263.7^2	 na api pratyakṣa pratītam api hāna upādāna viṣayaḥ bhavet aparijñāta sāmarthya tvāt asti ca śabdaḥ vyavahāraḥ asti ca prāṇa bhṛt mātra anubandhinī pratyakṣa pūrvikā hita ahita prāpti parihāra arthā lokayātrā sā eva ca bhinnāsu vyaktiṣu sāmānyam ekam vyavasthāpayati tad viṣayā śabda pravṛttiḥ yat ca upalabhyate tad jātīya tvena tad artha kriyā yogya tām viniścitya apūrva avagate api arthe lokaḥ pravartate iti bhinneṣu anugata ākārā buddhiḥ jāteḥ nibandhanam asyai abhāve na eva iyam lokayātrā pravartate iti iti bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhara viracitāyām padārtha praveṣaka nyāya kanda līṭīkāyām sāmānya padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_264.1–264.2	 anteṣu bhavāḥ antyāḥ sva āśraya viśeṣaka tvāt viśeṣāḥ vināśa ārambha rahiteṣu nitya dravyeṣu aṇu ākāśa kāla diś ātma manassu pratidravyam ekaikaśas vartamānāḥ atyanta vyāvṛtti buddhi hetavaḥ yathā asmad ādīnām gavā ādiṣu aśva ādibhyaḥ tulya ākṛti guṇa kriyā avayava saṃyoga nimittā pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā gauḥ śuklaḥ śīghra gatiḥ pīnaḥ kakudmān mahā ghaṇṭaḥ iti tathā asmāt viśiṣṭānām yoginām nityeṣu tulya ākṛti guṇa kriyeṣu paramāṇuṣu mukta ātma manassu ca anya nimitta asambhavāt yebhyaḥ nimittebhyaḥ pratyādhāram vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam vilakṣaṇaḥ ayam iti pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ deśa kāla viprakarṣa dṛṣṭe ca paramāṇau saḥ eva ayam iti pratyabhijñānam ca bhavati te antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ 
NK_264.3	 yadi punar antya viśeṣam antareṇa yoginām yoga jāt dharmāt pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam ca syāt tatas kim syāt na evam bhavati yathā na yoga jāt dharmāt aśukle śukla pratyayaḥ san jāyate atyanta adṛṣṭe ca pratyabhijñānam yadi syāt mithyā bhavet tathā iha api antya śeṣam antareṇa yoginām na yoga jāt dharmāt pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam vā bhavitum arhati 
NK_264.4–264.6	 atha antya viśeṣeṣu iva paramāṇuṣu svatas pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ kalpyate iti ced na tādātmyāt iha atad ātmakeṣu anya nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādiṣu pradīpāt na tu pradīpe pradīpa antarāt yathā vā aśva māṃsa ādīnām svatas eva aśuci tvam tad yogāt anyeṣām tathā iha api tādātmyāt anya viśeṣeṣu svatas eva pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ tad yogāt paramāṇu ādiṣu iti iti praśasta pāda bhāṣye viśeṣa padārthaḥ samāptaḥ caturyuga catur vidyā caturvatṇa vidhāyine namaḥ pañcatva śūnyāya caturmukha bhṛte sadā 
NK_264.7	 viśeṣa vyākhyāna artham āha anteṣu bhavāḥ antyāḥ iti utpāda vināśayoḥ ante avasthita tvāt anta śabda vācyāni nitya dravyāṇi teṣu bhavāḥ sthitāḥ iti arthaḥ sva āśrayasya sarvatas viśeṣaka tvāt bhedaka tvāt viśeṣāḥ etat vivṛṇoti vināśa ārambha rahiteṣu iti ādinā vināśa ārambha rahiteṣu ati antya padasya vivaraṇam atyanta vyāvṛtti buddhi hetavaḥ iti ca sva āśrayasya viśeṣaka tvāt iti asya vivaraṇam pratidravyam ekaikaśas vartamānāḥ iti dravyam dravyam pratyeka ekaḥ viśeṣaḥ vartate iti arthaḥ ekena eva viśeṣeṇa sva āśrayasya vyāvṛtti siddheḥ aneka viśeṣa kalpanā vaiyarthyāt yathā ca idam viśeṣānām lakṣaṇam bhavati tathā pūrvam vyākhyātam 
NK_264.8	 siddhe viśeṣa sadbhāve teṣām lakṣaṇa abhidhānam yuktam na asiddhe iti āaṅkya ca viśeṣāṇām sadbhāvam pratipādayitum grantham avatārayati yathā ityādinā yathā gavā ādiṣu aśva ādibhyaḥ tulya ākṛti nimittāḥ gauḥ iti guṇa nimittā śuklaḥ iti kriyā nimittā śīghra gatiḥ iti avayava nimittā pīnaḥ iti kakudmān iti saṃyoga nimittā mahā ghaṇṭaḥ iti yathā asmad ādīnām pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā tathā asmad viṣṭānām yoginām tulya ākṛti guṇa kriyeṣu tulya ākṛtiṣu tulya guṇeṣu tulya kriyeṣu paramāṇuṣu mukta ātma manassu ca anya nimitta asambhava ādyebhyaḥ nimittebhyaḥ pratyādhāram ayam asmāt vilakṣaṇaḥ iti pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ bhavati te antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ 
NK_264.9	 yathā asmad ādīnām gavā ādi vyaktiṣu pratyaya bhedaḥ bhavati tathā paramāṇu ādiṣu api tad darśinām paraspara apekṣayā pratyaya bhedena bhavitavyam vyakti bhedasya sambhavāt na ca asya vyakti bhedaḥ eva nimittam tad upalambhe api sthāṇu ādiṣu saṃśaya darśanāt nimitta antaram ca na asti ākṛteḥ guṇasya kriyāyāḥ ca tulya tvāt na ca nirnimittaḥ pratyaya bhedaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt yat asya nimittam sa viśeṣaḥ iti deśa viprakarṣeṇa kāla vipra kaeṣeṇa ca dṛṣṭāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kasyacid pratyabhijñā viṣayāḥ sāmānya viśeṣavat tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat na ca pūrva dṛṣṭe arthe pratyabhijñānam viśeṣa a= agatim antareṇa bhavati atas asti tasya nimittam viśeṣaḥ 
NK_264.10–264.12	 atra codayati yadi punar iti yathā yoga ja dharma sāmarthyāt yoginām atīndriya artha darśanam bhavati tathā viśeṣam antareṇa eva pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam ca bhaviṣyati iti codanā arthaḥ samādhatte na evam iti yathā yogi nām aśukle śukla pratyayaḥ na bhavati atyanta adṛṣṭe ca pratyabhijñānam na syāt yadi syāt mithyā pratyayaḥ bhavet tathā antya viśeṣam antareṇa pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ pratyabhijñānam ca na bhavitum arhati yoga jāt dharmāt atīndriya artha darśanam na punar asmāt nirnimittaḥ eva pratyayaḥ bhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ punar codayati atha antya viśeṣeṣu iti na tāvat antya viśeṣeṣu api viśeṣa antara sambhavaḥ anavasthānāt yathā ca teṣu viśeṣa antaram antareṇa svatas eva pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ bhavati yoginām tathā paramāṇuṣu api bhaviṣyati kim viśeṣa kalpanayā iti atra uttaram āha na iti 
NK_264.13–264.15	 yat tvayā uktam tat na kutas tāt ātmyāt etat eva vivṛṇoti iha iti atada ātmakeṣu anya nimittaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati na tad ātmakeṣu yathā ghaṭa ādiṣu aprakāśasu abhāveṣu pradīpa ādeḥ prakāśa svabhāvāt prakāśaḥ bhavati na tu pradīpe pradīpa antarāt prakāśaḥ kintu svatas eva yathā vā aśva māṃsa ādīnām svatas eva aśuci tvam spraṣṭuḥ pratyavāya kara tvam tad yogāt tad sambandhāt anyeṣām aśuci tvam tathā iha api tādātmyāt atyanta vyāvṛtti svabhāva tvāt antya viśeṣeṣu svatas eva svarūpāt eva pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ na viśeṣa antara sambandhāt atad a ātmakeṣu tu paramāṇu ādiṣu sādhāraṇa dharmakeṣu viśeṣa yogāt eva pratyaya vyāvṛttiḥ yuktāḥ na sva rūpa mātrāt iti nitya dravyeṣu sarveṣu paraspara sadharmasu pratyekam anuvartante viśeṣāḥ bheda hetavaḥ iti bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhara kṛtāyām padārtha praveśa nyāya kanda līṭīkāyām viśeṣa padārthaḥ samāptaḥ 
NK_265.1	 ayutasiddhānām ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām yaḥ sambandhaḥ iha pratyaya hetuḥ sa samavāyaḥ dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣāṇām kārya kāraṇa bhūtānām akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām vā ayuta siddhānām ādhārya ādhāra bhāvena avasthitānām iha idam iti buddhiḥ yatas bhavati yatas ca asarva gatānām adhigata anyatvānām aviṣvagbhāvaḥ sa samavāya ākhyaḥ sambandhaḥ 
NK_265.2–265.3	 katham yathā iha kuṇḍe dadhi iti pratyayaḥ sambandhe sati dṛṣṭaḥ tathā iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ iha vīraṇeṣu kaṭaḥ iha dravye guṇa karmaṇī iha dravya guṇa karmasu sattā iha dravye dravya tvam iha guṇe guṇa tvam iha karmaṇi sarma tvam iha nitya dravye antyāḥ viśeṣāḥ id pratyaya darśanāt asti eṣām sambandhaḥ iti jñāyate tubhyam bhava bhide viśva saṃhāra utpatti hetave nirmala jñāna dehāya namaḥ somāya śambhave 
NK_265.4	 samavāya nirūpaṇa artham āha ayutasiddhānām ādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām yaḥ sambandhaḥ iha pratyaya hetuḥ sa samavāyaḥ tat etat kṛta vyākhyānam uddeśa avasare ke te ayutasiddhāḥ yeṣām sambandhaḥ samavāyaḥ bhavet atas āha dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣāṇām iti kārya kāraṇa bhūtānām akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām iti anityam akathanam avayava a= ayavinām anitya dravya tad guṇānām nitya dravya vyatat samavetānām nitya guṇānām karma tadvatām kārya kāraṇa bhūtānām samavāyaḥ nitya dravya tad guṇānām sāmānya tadvatām antya viśeṣa tadvatām ca akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām samavāyaḥ ayuta siddhānām iti niyamaḥ evam ādhārya ādhāra bhāvena avasthitānām iti api niyamaḥ eva iha idam iti buddhiḥ yatas kāraṇāt bhavati yatas ca asarva gatānām niyata deśa avasthitānām adhigata anyatvānām adhigata svarūpa bhedānām aviṣvagbhāvaḥ apṛthagbhāvaḥ asvātantryam sa samavāyaḥ bhinnayoḥ paraspara upaśleṣasya sambandha kṛta tva upalambhāt 
NK_265.5	 etat eva katham ityādinā praśna pūrvakam upapādayati yathā iha kuṇḍe dadhi iti pratyayaḥ keṇḍa dadhnoḥ sambandhe sati dṛṣṭaḥ tathā iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ ityādi pratyayānāṇ darśanāt asti eṣām tantu paṭa ādīnām sambandhaḥ iti jñāyate iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ ityādi pratyayāḥ sambandha nimittākāḥ abādhita iha pratyaya tvāt iha kūṇḍe dadhīti pratyaya vat 
NK_266.1–266.2	 na ca asau saṃyoghāḥ sambandhinām ayuta siddha tvāt anyatara karma ādi nimitta asambhavāt vibhāga anta tva adarśanāt adhikaraṇa adhikartavyayoḥ eva bhāvāt iti nanu ayam saṃyogaḥ bhaviṣyati iti atas āha na ca asau saṃyogaḥ iti asau tantu paṭa ādīnām sambandhaḥ na saṃyogaḥ bhavati kutas iti atra āha sambandhinām ayuta siddha tvāt iti saṃyogaḥ hi yuta siddhānām eva bhavati ayam tu ayuta siddhānām iti tathā saṃyogaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyoga jaḥ vā syāt iti iha tu anyatara karma ādīnām nimittānām abhāvaḥ bhāva utpādaka kāraṇa sāmarthya bhāvi tvāt saṃyogasya vibhāga anta tvam vibhāga vināśi tvam dṛśyate na samavāyasya saṃyogaḥ svatantrayoḥ api bhavati yathā ūrdhva avasthitayoḥ aṅgulyoḥ ayam tu adhikaraṇa adhikartavyayoḥ eva bhavati tasmāt na ayam saṃyogaḥ kintu tasmāt pṛthak eva 
NK_267.1–267.2^1	 sa ca dravya ādibhyaḥ padārthantaram bhāvavat lakṣaṇa bhedāt yathā bhāvasya dravya tva ādīnām sva ādhāreṣu ātma anurūpa pratyaya kartṛ tvāt sva āśraya ādibhyaḥ parasparataḥ ca artha antara bhāvaḥ tathā samavāyasya api pañcasu padārtheṣu iha iti pratyaya darśanāt tebhyaḥ padārtha antara tvam iti evam sthite samavāye tasya dravya ādibhyaḥ bhedam pratipādayati sa ca dravya ādibhyaḥ padārtha antaram iti kutas iti atas āha bhāvavat lakṣaṇa bhedāt iti etat vivṛṇoti yathā iti bhavaḥ iti sattāmahā sāmānyam ucyate dravya tva ādi ityādi padena guṇa tva ādi parigrahaḥ 
NK_267.1–267.2^2	 yathā bhāvasya sva ādhāreṣu dravya guna karmasu ātma anurūpaḥ pratyayaḥ sat saditi pratyayaḥ dravya tvasya sva āśrayeṣu dravyeṣu ātma anurūpaḥ pratyayaḥ dravyam dravya miti pratyayaḥ guṇa tvasya sva āśrayeṣu guṇeṣu ātma anurūpaḥ pratyayaḥ guṇaḥ iti pratyayaḥ karma tvasya sva āśrayeṣu karmasu ātma anurūpaḥ pratyayaḥ karma iti pratyayaḥ tasya kartṛ tvāt bhāva dravya tva ādīnām sva āśraya ādibhyaḥ parasparataḥ ca artha antara bhāvaḥ tathā samavāyasya api pañcasu padārtheṣu iha iti pratyaya darśanāt tebhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ padārtha antara tvam 
NK_268.1–268.3	 na ca saṃyoga vat nānātvam bhāvavat liṅga aviśeṣāt viśeṣa liṅga abhāvāt ca tasmāt bhāva vat sarvatra ekaḥ samavāyaḥ iti nanu yadi ekaḥ samavāyaḥ dravya guṇa karmaṇām dravya tva guṇa tva karma tvāt viśeṣaṇaiḥ saha sambandha eka tvāt padārtha saṅkara prasaṅgaḥ iti na ādhāra ādheya niyamāt yadi api ekaḥ samavāyaḥ sarvatra svatantraḥ tathā api ādhāra ādheya niyamaḥ asti katham dravyeṣu eva davya tvam guṇeṣu eva guṇa tva karmasu eva karma tvam iti 
NK_268.4–268.5	 evamādi kasmāt anvaya vyatireka darśanāt iha iti samavāya nimittasya jñānasya anvaya darśanāt sarvatra ekaḥ samavāyaḥ iti gamyate dravya tva ādi nimittānām vyatireka darśanāt pratiniyamaḥ jñāyate yathā kuṇḍa dadhnoḥ saṃyoga eka tve api bhavati āśraya āśrayi bhāva niyamaḥ tathā dravya tva ādīnām api samavāya eka tve api vyaṅgyañjaka śakti bhedāt ādhāra ādheya niyamaḥ iti 
NK_268.6	 kim ayam ekaḥ āhosvit anekaḥ iti atra āha na ca saṃyoga vat nānātvam iti yathā saṃyogaḥ nānā na evam samavāyaḥ kutas iti atra āha bhāvavat liṅga aviśeṣāt viśeṣa liṅga abhāvāt ca yathā sat sat iti jñānasya lakṣaṇasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt availakṣaṇyāt viśeṣe bhede lakṣaṇasya pramāṇasya abhāvāt ca sarvatra ekaḥ bhāvaḥ tat vat iheti pratyayasya lakṣaṇasya sarvatra availakṣaṇyāt bhede pramāṇa abhāvāt ca sarvatā ekaḥ samavāyaḥ iti upasaṃharati tasmāt iti 
NK_268.7	 cedayati yadi ekaḥ samavāyaḥ iti samavāyasya ekatve yaḥ eva dravya tvasya pṛthivī ādiṣu yogaḥ saḥ eva guṇa tvasya guṇeṣu karma tvasya ca karmasu tatra yathā dravya tvasya yogaḥ pṛthivī ādiṣu asti iti teṣām dravya tvam tathā tad yogasya guṇa ādiṣu api sambhavāt teṣām api dravya tvam yathā ca guṇa tvasya yogaḥ rūpa ādiṣu asti iti rūpa ādīnām tathā tad yogasya dravya karmaṇoḥ api bhāvāt tayoḥ api guṇa tvam syāt evam ca karmasu api padārthānām saṅkīrṇa tā darśayitavyā 
NK_268.8	 samādhatte na iti na ca padāthānām saṅkīrṇa tā kutas ādhāra ādheya niyamāt na samavāyasadbhāva mātreṇa dravya tvam kintu dravya tva samavāyāt dravya tvam tat samavāyaḥ ca dravyeṣu eva na guṇa karmasu atas na teṣām dravya tvam evam guṇa karmasu api vyākhyeyam etat saṅgraha vākyam vivṛṇoti yadi api ekaḥ samavāyaḥ ityādinā svatantraḥ iti saṃyoga vat sambandha antareṇa na vartate iti arthaḥ vyaktam aparam 
NK_268.9	 punar codayat evamādi kasmāt iti dravyeṣu eva dravya tvam vartate guṇeṣu eva guṇa tvam karmasu eva karma tvam iti evamādi kasmāt tvayā jñātam iti athaḥ uttaran āha anvaya vyatireka darśanāt iti dravya tva nimittasya pratyayasya dravyeṣu anvayaḥ guṇa karmabhyaḥ ca vyatirekaḥ guṇa tva nimittasya pratyayasya guṇeṣu anvayaḥ dravya karmabhyaḥ ca vyatirekaḥ tathā karma tva nimittasya pratyayasya karmasu anvayaḥ dravya guṇebhyaḥ ca vyatirekaḥ dṛśyate tasmāt anvaya vyatireka darśanāt dravya tva ādīnām niyamaḥ jñāyate asya vivaraṇam sugamam 
NK_268.10	 samavāya aviśeṣe kutas eva ayam niyamaḥ dravya tvasya pṛthivī ādiṣu eva samavāyaḥ guṇa tvasya rūpa ādiṣu eva karma tvasya utkṣepaṇa ādiṣu eva na anyatra iti atas āha yathā iti saṃyogasya eka tve api kuṇḍa dadhnoḥ āśraya āśrayi bhāvasya niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śakti niyamāt kuṇḍam eva āśrayaḥ dadhi eva ādheyam na tu kuṇḍam ādheyam dadhi vā aadhāraḥ tathā samavāya ekatva ipi dravya tva ādīnām ādhāra ādheya niyamaḥ vyaṅgya vyañjaka śakti bhedāt kim uktam syāt dravya tva abhivyañjikā śaktiḥ dravyāṇām eva tena dravyeṣu eva dravya tvam samavaiti na anyatra iti evam guṇa karmasu api vyākhyeyam 
NK_269.1–269.3	 sambandhya nitya tve api na saṃyoga vat anitya tvam bhāva vat akāraṇa tvāt yathā pramāṇataḥ kāraṇa anupālabdheḥ nityaḥ bhāvaḥ iti uktam tathā samavāyaḥ api iti na hi asya kiñcid kāraṇam pramāṇataḥ upalabhyate iti kim punar ayam anityaḥ āhosvit nityaḥ iti saṃśaye satyāha sambandhya nitya tve api iti yathā sambandhinoḥ anitya tve saṃyogasya anitya tvam na tathā samavāyinoḥ anitya tve samavāyasya anitya tvam bhāva vat akāraṇa tvāt iti etat vivṛṇoti yathā ityādinā yuktaḥ hi sambandhi vināśe saṃyogasya vināśaḥ tad utpāde sambandhinoḥ samavāyi kāraṇa tvāt samavāyasya tu sambandhinau na kāraṇam sambandhi mātra tvāt yathā ca etau na kāraṇam tathā upapāditam tasmāt etasya sambandhi vināśe api avināśaḥ sat tāvat āśraya antare api pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt 
NK_270.1–270.2	 kayā punar vṛttyā dravya ādiṣu samavāyaḥ vartate na saṃyogaḥ sambhavati tasya guṇa tvena dravya āśrita tvāt na api samavāyaḥ tasya eka tvāt na ca anyā vṛtti tasti iti na tādātmyāt yathā dravya vyaguṇa karmaṇām sat ātmakasya bhāvasya na anyaḥ sattā yogaḥ asti evam avibhāginaḥ vṛtti ātmakasya samavāyasya na anyā vṛttiḥ asti tasmāt sva ātma vṛttiḥ 
NK_270.3–270.8	 atas eva atīndriyaḥ sattā ādīnām iva pratyakṣeṣu vṛtti abhāvāt sva ātma gata saṃvedana abhāvāt ca tasmāt iha buddhi anumeyaḥ samavāyaḥ iti iti praśasta pāda bhāṣye samavāya padārthaḥ samāptaḥ yoga ācāra vibhūtyā yaḥ toṣayitvā maheśvaram cakre vaiśeṣikam śāstram tasmai kaṇabhuje namaḥ iti praśasta pāda viracitam dravya ādi ṣaṭpadārtha bhāṣyam samāptam kim asambaddhaḥ eva samavāyaḥ sambandhinau sambandhayati sambaddhaḥ vā na tāvat asambaddhaka tvam yuktam atiprasaṅgāt sambandhaḥ ca asya na saṃyoga rūpaḥ sambhavati tasya dravya āśrita tvāt na api samavāyaḥ eka tvāt na ca saṃyoga samavāyābhyām vṛtti antaram asti 
NK_270.9^1	 tat katham asya vṛttiḥ iti atas āha kayā punar vṛttyā dravya ādiṣu samavāyaḥ vartate iti vṛtti abhāvāt na vartate iti abhiprāyaḥ etat samādhate na iti vṛtti abhāvāt na vartate iti etat na tādātmyāt vṛtti ātmaka tvāt svatas eva ayam vṛttiḥ iti kṛtakaḥ hi saṃyogaḥ tasya vṛtti ātmakasya api vṛtti antaram asti kāraṇa samavāyasya kārya lakṣaṇa tvāt samavāyasya vṛtti antaram na asti tasmāt asya sva ātmanā sva rūpeṇa eva vṛttiḥ na vṛtti antareṇa iti arthaḥ atas eva atīndriyaḥ sattā ādīnām iva pratyakṣeṣu vṛtti abhāvāt 
NK_270.9^2	 yathā sattā ādīnām pratyakṣeṣu artheṣu vṛttiḥ asti tena te saṃyukta samavāyāt indriyeṣu gṛhyante na evam samavāyasya vṛtti sambhavaḥ atas atīndriyaḥ ayam saṃyoga sama bāya apekṣasya eva indriyasya bhāva grahaṇa sāmarthya upalambhāt yadi samavāya viṣayam aindriyakam saṃvedanam asti sambandha abhāva abhidhānam pralāpaḥ atha na asti tat eva vācyam iti atra āha sva ātma gata saṃvedana abhāvāt ca iti yathā indriyeṇa saṃyoga pratibhāsaḥ na evam samavāya pratibhāsaḥ sambandhinoḥ piṇḍībhāva upalambhāt atas ayam apratyakṣaḥ upasaṃharati tasmāt iti 
NK_270.10–270.14	 paraspara upasaṃśleṣaḥ bhinnānām yad kṛtaḥ bhavet samavāyaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ svātantrya prarodhakaḥ iti bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhara kṛtāyām padārtha praveśa nyāya kanda līṭīkāyām samavāyāada arthaḥ samāptaḥ suvarṇa maya saṃsthāna ramyā sarva uttara sthitiḥ sumeroḥ śṛṅgavīthī iva ṭīkā iyam nyāya kandalī akṣīṇa nija pakṣeṣu khyāpayantī guṇān asau para prasiddha siddhāntān dalati nyāya kandalī 
NK_270.15–270.17	 āsīt dakṣiṇa rāḍhāyām dvijānām puṇya karmaṇām bhūri sṛṣṭiḥ iti grāmaḥ bhūri śiṣṭa jana āśrayaḥ ambhaḥ rāśeḥ iva etasmāt babhūva kṣiti candramāḥ jagat ānanda kṛt handyaḥ bṛhaspatiḥ iti jvijaḥ tasmāt viśuddha guṇa ratna mahā samudraḥ vidyā latā samavalambana bhūruhaḥ abhūt svaccha āśayaḥ vividha kīrttana dīpravāha prasyanda sampada balaḥ baladeva nāmā 
NK_270.18–270.21	 tasya abhūt bhūri yaśasaḥ viśuddha kula sambhavāḥ ap boka iti arcita guṇāḥ guṇinaḥ gṛhamedhinī sa= chāyaḥ sthūla phala daḥ bahu śākhaḥ dvija āśrayaḥ tābhyām śrīdharaḥ iti uccais arthi kalpadrumaḥ abhavat asau vidyā vidagdhānām asūta śravaṇa ucitām ṣaṭpadārtha hitām etām rucirām nyāya kandalīm tri adhika daśa uttara nava śata śāka abde nyāya kandalī racitā śrī pāṇḍu dāsa yācita bhaṭṭa śrī śrīdhareṇa iyam
